MHB 1
1 . MEENYA ngyiramá apem matow ndwom
Meyi mo Pomfò ayɛw,
Makamfo me Hen N'enyimnyam,
N'adom no konyimdzi.

MHB 1
2 . Mo Wùra dɔyɛfo, me Nyankopon,
Boa m' ma mombɔ dawur,
Memfa Wo dzin n'enyidzi no
Mentahye mbea nyina.

MHB 1
3 . Jesus! dzin a otu hen suro,
Ͻma ’werɛhow b՝ᴐ adze;
Ͻyɛ sanku wo abᴐn asom’,
Ͻyε nkwa nye asomdwee.

MHB 1
4 . Ɔ kasa, na wotsie Ne ndze a,
Ewufo nya nkwa bio,
Akoma wѐrɛhonyi dzi dɛw,
Hianyi bùrobùro gye dzi.

MHB 1
5 . Odwuruw bᴐn no tum koraa,
Otu daduanyi duam';
No bᴐgyaa tum san fifo ho,
Odzii nyim maa mo so.

MHB 1
6 . Hom bᴐn nyina da Jesus do;
Wokum Nyame Eguambaa,
Wɔdze Ne kra so bɔɔ afɔr
Maa obiara ne kra.

MHB 10
1 . HƐN akoma, nsa nye ndze
Yɛdze da nyame ase;
Ɔayɛ anwanwadze,
Wiadze dzi ho ehurusi;
Ofi hɛn na ne yamu,
Ɔdze dɔ akyɛ dze
Ehyira hɛen kwan nyina m',
Na ɔda ho yɛ hɛndze.

MHB 10
2 . Ɔ kyɛso Nyankopɔn
Ɔnka hɛn ho daa nyina,
Ɔmfa ahotɔ krɔnn,
Ɔndom hɛn akoma daa,
Ɔnkora hɛn N'adom mu,
Ongya hɛn nkɔntɔnkye m',
Na ɔmpa hɛn mbusu,
Sesei na ndaamba so.

MHB 10
3 . Ayεyi nye ndaase
Ɔnkã Nyame sor Egya,
Nye Ne Ba Kortonoo,
Nye Nyame Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn:
Ɔkorsa Nyankopɔn
Sor nye asaase sɔr No;
Mbrɛ ahyɛse ɔtse n'.	
Ɔtse dɛm afebɔɔ.    Amen.

MHB 100
1 . OBI wɔ hɔ a ɔkyɛn obiara, 
Ɔsɛ dɛ yɛfrɛ N'nyɛnko;
No dɔ kyɛn onua mpo no dɔ, 
Aboɔdzen, wɔnntɔ, onnyi ewiei;
Hɔn a wɔsɔ No dɔ n' hwɛ n', 
Hu dɛ ɔyɛ onnyiewiei dɔ.

MHB 100
2 . Nyɛnko bɛn na ɔbɛgye hɛn a, 
Nkyɛ obotum ehue no bɔgyaa n'?
Naaso hɛn Jesus wui gyee hɛn; 
Ɔkaa hɛn nye Nyame bɔɔ m';
Iyi, dɔ a onnyi mbanano a;
Jesus yɛ nyɛnko mapa.

MHB 100
3 . Ber a ɔbaa adasa wiadze no,
Ne dzin nye Abɔn Damfoedu;
Afei ɔwɔ N'enyimnyam mu,
Odzi dɛw wɔ dzin yi mu;
Ɔfrɛ hɛn 'nuamom, ndamfo,
Na ɔhwɛ hɛn ehiadze nyina.

MHB 100
4 . Nkyɛ hɛn akoma aagow!
Ewuradze, kyerɛ hɛn, yɛndɔ;
Hɛndze, ao, hɛn werɛ fir ntsɛ! 
Nyɛnko bi a yɛwɔ n' sor hɔ a!
Sɛ wɔdze hɛn 'kra ba fie a,
Yɛbɔdɔ Wo dɛ mbrɛ ɔsɛ.

MHB 1000
1 . Mo, sunsum, kra, nye honam,
Jesus, medze ma Wo,
Afɔrbɔdzѐ a no ho tsew krɔnn,
Ɔnyɛ Wodze daa nyinaa.

      M'adze nyinaa gu pata no do,
      Morotweɔn ogya n' ma ɔaaba,
      Morotweɔn, morotweɔn, morotweɔn,
      Morotweɔn ogya n' mà ɔaaba.

MHB 1000
2 . Jesus, Agyenkwa tumfo,
Motwer Wo dzin kɛse n';
M'enyiwa da Wo nkwangye n' kwan
W'anohoba n' meregye.

MHB 1000
3 . Ao, ma ogya n' nsian sesei,
Ɔmbra mo sunsum do,
Ɔmbra mbɛhyew m' afɔrbɔdze,
Ɔmma mo ho ntsew krɔnn.

MHB 1000
4 . Jesus pa, meyɛ Wodze,
Eguar m' Wo bɔgyaa n' mu
Fa Wo Sunsum bɛgyɛ me nsew,
Ma menyɛ Nyame dze.

MHB 1001
1 . Ao o, m'afɛ! hom nhwɛ frankaa
Rinyam wɔ sor hɔ!
Afei nkyidɔm riyi hɔnho,
Konyim abɛm hɛn.

      Wontsim aban n', na mereba,
      Jesus rinyam nsa;
      Wɔnto ano nse n' sor hɔ dɛ,
      W'adaworom yetsim n'.

MHB 1001
2 . Hwɛ dɔmtutuw a wɔreba,
Abɔnsam dzi kan:
Akatakyi rohwe ase,
Mbanyinndam pέ etu!

MHB 1001
3 . Hwɛ, konyim frankaa no rinyam!
Tsie, abɛn rehɛn,
Yɛdze hɛn Hen dzin bedzi nyim
Wɔ adɔm nyina do.

MHB 1001
4 . Ɔko asaasaa do akyer
Na boafo bɛn hɛn:
Hɛn Sahen kɛse no reba,
Kofo, hyέ akoma.

MHB 1002
1 . Gyedzinyi, twer No, twer No,
Sɛ ko n' kyer do dɛn arà a;
Ɔyɛ dέn arà a ibedzi nyim,
Wo Nyame b]ko ama w'.

     Twer No, twer No,
     Sɛ sum n' yɛ hu dɛn ara a;
     Twer No, twer No,
     Na adzekyee no abɛn.

MHB 1002
2 . Twer No, na mbusu n' rebɛn,
Ngyigye dzendzen rebɛn;
Obokutow wo arta
Ɔbra n'awor huhu n'.

MHB 1002
3 . Ewuradze botum agye hɛn,
Ɔyɛ Nyɛnko arà ampa;
Gyedzinyi, twer No, twer No,
Twer N' ara ewiei.

MHB 1003
1 . Werɛhonyi, 'wɔ hen arà a,
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ kwan!
Kã dza ɔhow wo werɛ,
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ kwan!
Kã ma w' Agyenkwa no ntse,
Gyaa suro nyinaa mu mà ɔnkɔ,
Kasà ara na ɔbɛtse;
Mbeamudua n' ho wɔ kwan!

MHB 1003
2 . Kobɔfo, ka w' ho, mma nnkyim;
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ kwan!
Hwehwɛ beà a woehyira do n':
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ kwan!
'Wo a wo kɔn ebu, aberɛ,
Jesus tum deda adwen;
Jesus tum deda adwen;
Hom wɔ w'Agyenkwa no mu:
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ nkwan!

MHB 1003
3 . Bɔnyɛnyi a enndwen, ndɛ bra,
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ kwan!
Tsie! Sunsum n' nyѐ Asɔrmba se,
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ kwan!
Hwɛ nkwa nsubùra woebue n' hɔ,
Woebue ama me nye wo,
Ebirɛmpɔn nyѐ akɔhweaban
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ kwan!

MHB 1003
4 . Asɛmpa ny' 'i! Kwan wɔ hɔ
Ma nyimpa nyina!
Dɔ ayɛ mpata-dwuma n',
Mbeamudua n' ho wɔ kwan!
Adom esutsen repem,
Nyimpa nyinaa wɔ ho kwan;
O nkyέ adasa nyinà eehu dɛ
Mbeamùdua n' ho wɔ kwan!

MHB 1004
1 . Metse dɛ Gyefo n' se,
W' ahoɔdzen suar ampa;
Na dwen do weɔn na sɔr,
Fa Me yɛ w'adze nyina.

     Jesus tuaa ne nyina,
     Ne nyina fir Noara;
     Bɔn egu mo ho fi dɛnn,
     Ɔahor ma ayɛ fitaa.

MHB 1004
2 . Ewùradze, menyà ehu
Dɛ Wo nkotsee Wo tum
Na otu kwata bɔr,
Na ɔnam 'koma bo.

MHB 1004
3 . 'Midze, minnyi yie bi a
Medze bɛgye W'adom;
M'bɔhor me ntar fitaa
Wɔ Eguambaa bɔgyaa mu.

MHB 1004
4 . Da bi a me kra bɔsoɛr
Mo wumpa dὸ afow sor,
Jesus tuaa ne nyina!
Begyigye wim' hɔ nyina.

MHB 1004
5 . Na minya mudu sor
Ahengua n' enyim hɔ a,
Medze m'asadze nyina
Bogu N'anànadze hɔ.

MHB 1005
1 . Ao, dwen ofi a ɔwɔ hɔ ho,
Osi baka fɛɛfɛw n' ho hɔ,
Mbrέ apapafo a wonnkowu pɛn
Woewuna hɔn ntar efufuw . . . .
     
Ɔwɔ hɔ!. . . . Ɔwɔ hɔ! . . .

MHB 1005
2 . Ao, dwen w'afέ a wɔwɔ hɔ ho,
Hɔn a woedzi kan ewie akwantu n',
Dwen ndwom a wɔrotow n' hɔ no ho,
Wɔ Nyamѐ ahemfi no mu hɔ . . .

MHB 1005
3 . M'Agyenkwa no so ɔwɔ hɔ,
Hɔ na m'asɛfo akɔhom,
Da bi mo so m'befi yaw nsa
Makɔ ahomka man no mu . . .

MHB 1005
4 . Aka kùmaa ma meedu fie hɔ,
M'enyi tua m'akwantu n'ewiei,
M'adɔfo dodὸwara wɔ hɔ a
Hɔn enyiwa tua mo so kwan. . . .

MHB 1006
1 . Man bi wɔ hɔ a ɔhyerɛn sen wi mpo,
Na yɛdze gyedzi hu n' wɔ ekyir;
Na Egya n' rotweɔn wɔ kwan no do,
Oesiesie kobew ama hɛn hɔ.

      Da bi da . . . dɛɛdɛw n' mu
      Yebehyia wɔ mpoano fɛɛfɛw n' do.
      Da bi da . . . dɛɛdɛw n' mu,
      Yebehyia wɔ mpoano fɛɛfɛw n' do.

MHB 1006
2 . Yɛbɔtow wɔ mpoano fɛɛfɛw n' do
Esiarfo hɔn ndwom a ɔyɛ dɛw n';
Hɛn sunsum nnkedzi yaw ara pɛn,
Apempen nnkɔfὸra hɛn ahomgye.

MHB 1006
3 . Hɛn Egya dɔyɛfὸ a ɔwɔ sor hɔ,
Yɛdze hɛn ayɛyi bɛkɛma N'
Wɔ no dɔ ayamùyie no ne ntsi,
Wɔ nhyirà a ɔdze adom hɛn ha.

MHB 1007
1 . Ɔman bi wɔ hɔ, no mu hyerɛn,
No wim' tsew wann daa nyina
Hɔ sum nn-gye dabiara pɛn:
Agyenkwa hyerɛn hɔ daa.

      Sɛ yɛsoa. . . mbeamudua n' a. . .
      Nna ahenkyɛw n'. . . so yɛbɔsoa,. . .
      Na yɛnye . . . ahoɔfɛfo astena, . . .
      Wɔ ahomka no mu da nyina.

MHB 1007
2 . Beebi wɔ hɔ, asomdwee bea
Ɔbra po yi n' ekyir,
Hɔ ehum nn-kotu hɛn da:
Sie w'adze nyina wɔ hɔ.

MHB 1007
3 . Ofi bi wɔ hɔ, enyimnyam fi,
Sor ahemfi papa;
Na hɔn a yɛdɔ hɔn wɔ ha 'i
Bɛyɛ etuu wɔ hɔ.

MHB 1007
4 . Hɛn kɔn dɔ dɛ yegya bea yi a
Orutwam' hwew hwew yi;
Na yɛkɔfὸra dɔmtutuw n' a
Hɔn dɛw ɔmmbɔ adze da n'.

MHB 1008
1 . Ana yebehyia baka n' ho,
Mbrɛ ahohyѐrɛnfo edua n',
Dza no nsu gyenen-gyenen pem
Daa wɔ Nyame N'egua nkyɛn n'?

       Nyew, yebehyia baka no ho,
Baka fɛɛfɛw, baka fɛɛfɛw no ho;
Yɛnyѐ esiarfo n' behyia baka no ho;
Ofi Nyame N'eguam' pem n'.

MHB 1008
2 . Baka fɛɛfɛw n' nkɔnkɔnoa hɔ,
Yeboguar ne mpetsema n',
Yɛpasar na yeeyi ayɛw,
Ahomka da fɛɛfɛw n' nyina,

MHB 1008
3 . Yerubodu baka fɛɛfɛw n' ho a,
Yɛbɔto adzesoa nyina fam';
Adom bɛgye hɛn kra efim',
Na ɔama ntar nye ahenkyɛw.

MHB 1008
4 . Baka fɛɛfɛw no hyerɛn a,
Hɛn Agyenkwa N'enyim no a,
Esiarfo a wonnwu da no
Wotu nkwagye ndwom wɔtow.

MHB 1008
5 . 'Ka kùmaa ma yeedu baka n' ho,
Ma yeewie hɛn akwantu,
Ma yaakɛtse asomdwee ndwom a,
Onunu akoma nyina.

MHB 1009
1 . Bra Agyenkwa hɔ, mma nnyɛ ekyim:
Ɔakyѐrɛ hɛn finimfin ha n-dɛ,
Reka No mberɛwm'dɛ, Bra.

         N-hyiamu no bɛyɛ enigye
Ber-a hɛn akomam' astsew wɔ bɔn ho
Na yɛnye Ɔwὸ Agyenkwa atsena
Hɛn fi a onnyi ewiei n'mu.

MHB 1009
2 . Tsie, ɔse dɛ: Wɔmma mbofra kwan!
Wɔmma akoma nyina ndzi ehurusi;
Ma yɛmfa No nyɛ hɛn afamudze:
Mma nnyɛ ekyim, na bra.

MHB 1009
3 . Dwen prɛko bio dɛ ɔwɔ ha ndɛ;
Bu Ne siar frɛ no bi, na dzi do;
Tsie, N'awɔse ndze n'rowosow dɛ:
Ao, me mba, ao, hom mbra!

MHB 101
1 . ABRƐFO ahomgye,
'Werɛhofo dɛw,
Ehufo enyidar,
Ɔhɔho ne fie,
Daa ahoɔdzen,
Mbusu m' guandɔbea,
'Gyenkwa, Nyɛnko.

MHB 101
2 . Sundzi a ɔdɔ dze
Ne tsir to do,
Hɔn a woruwu asomdwee,
Ewufo nkwa,
'Hobrɛadzefo kwan,
Ewiei akatua,
'Hotsewfo ahom,
'Gyenkwa, Nyɛnko.

MHB 101
3 . Sɛ me nan fintsiw a, 
M'bosu afrɛ W';
Abrɛfo ahenkyɛw,
Ɔsor mbeamudua,
Sɛ me nan fom a,
Bɔ mo ho ban,
Nokwafo, dɔfo,
'Gyenkwa, Nyɛnko.

MHB 101
4 . M'bɔbɔ W' dzin akyerɛ,
M'bɛma Wo do,
M'behyira W' mahyɛ W' 'nyam,
M'beyi W' ayɛw;
Mo ndwuma nyina,
Wiadze a onnyi ewiei,
 Meyɛ Wodze daa,
'Gyenkwa, Nyɛnko.

MHB 1010
1 . ANÀ ɔwo rennyɛ hwee? Naasὸ edwuma wɔ hɔ,
Mo Wùra No turo mu, wo ho edwuma wɔ hɔ.
Yɛ abofra nokwafo gyina w’aweɔmber do;
Mbrɛ wo Wùra frɛ w’ biara tsen wo nsa suo mu bi.

   Suo mu bi, suo mu bi, tsen wo nsa suo mu bi;
   Afonafo retsew hwe; tsen wo nsa suo mu bi;
   Suo mu bi, suo mu bi, tsen wo nsa suo mu bi,
   Jesus da ho refrɛ; tsen wo nsa suo m’ bi.

MHB 1010
2 . Anà ayɛ komm tse hɔ ? Ndwom wɔ ha a wɔtow;
Bohur N’ayɛyi ndwom, bosuo mu ma yɛntow;
Gyedzi ndze nyina sesa, po nye aman do,
Ma ɔkɛpem sor do; tsen wo nsa suo mu bi.

MHB 1011
1 . NA wɔwoo m’ ma meewu,
Maato honam yi famù ?
Ana me kra wɔ dɛ otu,
Kɔ wiadze fofor bi m?
Man a sum agye do,
Nyimpa n’adwen hwira mu,
Asamankyir hɔ nwinwin na
Mbrɛ adze nyina wѐrɛ fir n’.

MHB 1011
2 . Minya fi asaase kɔ a,
M’ewie bowie me dɛn ?
Siar anaa mbusù a onnyi ewiei
Ɔbɛyɛ me kyɛpɛn;
Abɛn ne ndze n’ nyan mѐ a,
M’befi me nda mù masoɛr, ’
Mehu Enyimnyam Tsɛmbuafo n’
Nye wimù a ɔredzɛw n’.

MHB 1011
3 . M’befi me nda mu dɛn ?
Konyim anaa yaw mù a ?
M’behyia atsɛn hun anaà atsɛn pa ?
N-dom anaa nhyirà a ?
Ana engyirfo bɛfa,
Hɔn nuà akɔ asɛndzii ?
Ana mbɔnsam bɔwɔ m' kra ntaa,
Akɔ ma woeebu n' fɔ ?

MHB 1011
4 . Dza munnhu m’ yi woana
Bomm esi no pi ?
Dɛ m’bɔfora hɔn a wɔapaa hɔn n’
Anaa m’bɔforà esiarfo n’ ?
Woeyi m’ Nyame nkyɛn a,
Menye m’ Gyefo bɛsténa ?
Nyame bɛhyɛ dɛ monkɔ heaven
Anaa menkɛda hɛll?

MHB 1011
5 . Ao! Ɔwὸ a emmpɛ dɛ,
Bɔnyɛnyi biara wu !
Woara wui ma aagye me kra
Wɔ mbusù a onnyi ewiei mu !
Kyѐrɛ m’ mbrɛ menyɛ mimfi
W'ebufuwhyew no nsa,
Ama sɛ bɛtséna W'egua n' dὸ a,
Medze dɛw meepue hɔ.

MHB 1011
6 . Woarà ankasa nye kwan n’,
Kyérɛ Woho wɔ mo mu;
Ama maahwer me mher tsiabaa ’i,
Wɔ W'apɛdze ne yɛ m’;
Ama maadɔ m’ Nyame.
Osiandέ odzii kan dɔɔ m';
Na meeyi Wo ayɛw daa wɔ
W‘enyimnyam tsѐnabew hɔ.

MHB 1012
1 . HƐN Wùra kɛse rutu,
Asorɛkye rubu akɛse;
Wimu enyi ebir kebikebi,
Yennyi boafo anaa sumabcw.
Anà ɔnnyɛ wo asɛm dɛ yeruwu yi ?
Eyɛ dɛn tum da dɛm ?
Naaso aber nyina iriyi hɛn hu dɛ
Annyɛ a yɛbɔkɔ nsuadze.

Mframa nye asorɛkye
Betsie Me ndze: Dzinn, yɛ komm !
Sɛ po a oetutu ne tsir egu do o,
Mbɔnsam o, nyimpa o,
Anaadɛ ebɛnadze ara o,
Nsu biara nnkotum amen hɛn yi,
Epo nye asaase nye wimù hɔn Wùra da mu,
Hɔn a wɔdze dɛw betsie Ne ndze;
Dzinn, yɛ komm!
Dzinn, yɛ komm!
Hɔn a wɔdze dɛw betsie Ne ndze:
Dzinn, Dzinn, yɛ komm!.

MHB 1012
2 . Mo Wura, medze awerɛhow sunsum
Abɔ me tsir adze ndɛ,
Awerɛhow ahyɛ m’akoma n’ase:
Ao, meserɛ Wo, nyan na gye m' nkwa !
Mframa nye atseetsee na nsupram yi
Rohom me kra a ɔrodɔ no do,
Na m’ Ewuradze dɔfo, muruwu, muruwu;
Ao, meserɛ Wo yɛ ntsɛm na suo so me nsamu !

MHB 1013
1 . ANA rigya Jesus hɔ akɔ anafua yi,
Wo nko ara ako yaw na sum mu ?
Ana bɔpow Ne fafir nye No nkwa a ɔdze rema wo yi ?
’Yi nye asomdwee a ennhu bi pɛn ?
Ana rigya No hɔ akɔ, ana rigya no hɔ akɔ ?
Ana rigya Jesus hɔ akɔ anafua yi ?

MHB 1013
2 . Ana rigya Jesus a ɔyɛ wo nyɛnko no hɔ akɔ,
Nyɛnko a ɔkye yɛ nokwar daa ?
Ɔbɛkyekye wo werɛ, ɔakyerɛ wo kwan,
ɔakõ agye wo,
Ɔbɛyɛ ne nyina kwa ama wo.

MHB 1013
3 . Jesus dze ɔdɔ a wonnsusu no ho amandzɛ wui,
Da hi ɔbɔɔ werdam maa abɔn;
Ao! Hwɛ No bɔgyaa wɔ esutsen nwanwa no mu,
Ɔbahohor efifidze nyina.

MHB 1014
1 . TSIE Guanhwɛfo n’ Ne ndze nà ɔda m’
Wɔ sar do noho kɔnkɔn no m’,
Ɔrefrɛ No nguàn a wɔatɔ gon,
Efi nguambuw mu kɔ ekyirkyir.

   Fa hɔn bra, fa hɔn bra,
   Fa hɔn fi bɔn nhaban no m’ bra,
   Fa hɔn bra, fa hɔn bra,
   Fa hɔn a wɔatɔ gon n’ bra Jesus.

MHB 1014
2 . Woana bakaboa Guanhwefo yi.
Na aahwehwe nguan a waata gon?
Woana dze han beba buw no m’
Mbre wobefi awaw no mu ‘?

MHB 1014
3 . Tsie! Worusũ sar do noho,
Nkokwaa atsentsen etsifi;
Tsie ! Hɛn Wùra nà ɔrekã kyerɛ w’ dɛ
Kɔhwehwɛ Mo nguan fa hɔn bra.

MHB 1015
1 . DÀ a ɔbɛba, dà a ɔbɛba
Abɛkan N’edwindze,
N’edwindze a wɔsom bo nyina;
Nedze a ɔdɔ hɔn.

     Hyɛnhyɛn dɛ adzekyee nworaba
     Wɔfemfam N’ahenman m’;
     Wɔbɛhyerɛn hɔn ahoɔfɛw n ’ mu
     Ne kyɛw ho nworaba.

MHB 1015
2 . Ɔbɔboa, ɔbɔboa
Hɔn anὸ akɔ N’ahenman m’;
Hɔn a hɔn ho tsew, hɔn a wɔhyѐrɛn.
Nedze a ɔdɔ hɔn.

MHB 1015
3 . Mbofraba, mbofrabà a,
Wɔdɔ hɔn Pomfo no,
Hɔn nye N’ewindze a wɔsom bo n’,
Nedze a ɔdɔ hɔn.

MHB 1016
1 . MEYƐ hɔho wɔ ha,
Sor nye me fie;
Asaase yέ awerɛhow,
Sor nye me fie;
Mbusu nye awerɛhow,
Etwa mo ho ehyia;
Ɔsor nye m'Egya kùrowm',
Sor nye me fie.

MHB 1016
2 . Kaansa ehum rutù a,
Sor nye me fie;
M'akwantu ɔyɛ tsia,
Sor nye me fie;
Mber n'ehum nye me fie;
Ɔnnkyɛr na abɔ adze;
Na ewiei n' m'bokodu fie
Sor nye me fie.

MHB 1016
3 . M'Agyenkwa Ne nkyɛn hɔ-
Sor nye me fie-
Ɔbɛhyɛ m' enyimnyam,
Sor nye me fie;
Eyiefo nye esiarfὸ a
Modɔ hɔn nyina wɔ hɔ;
Hɔ na mo so m'bɔhom,
Sor nye me fie.

MHB 1016
4 . Dɛm ntsi minndzi nkɔmbɔ,
Sor nye me fie;
Me kyɛpɛn tse dɛn ara a,
Sor nye me fie;
Mo Wura abanyimfa
Na m'begyina ampa;
Ɔsor nye m'Egya kùrom',
Sor nye me fie.

MHB 1017
1 . Wiadze ruwu; daa nyinara
Mpempem mpempem na wɔsen kɔ!
Christianfo, hom m-per ngye hɔn;
Hom nka Jesus nkyѐrɛ hɔn ntsɛntsɛm.

MHB 1017
2 . Ahodze, ahoɔdzen, nyimdzee,
Nyew, hom n-kwa mpo hom mfa mma;
Hom Gyefo ayɛ bi ama hom!
Na 'bɛn na hom nnkɛyɛ ama N'?

MHB 1017
3 . Nyame No Sunsum, fi edzi,
Keka po mu, nunu kwaa mu.
Mbew nyina do, mbea nyinara,
Prapra Nyame Ne mba boà ano.

MHB 1018
1 . AWERƐKYEKYER Nyankopɔn,
Gye nyim no yɛ Wodze;
Woara Wodze na yɛdze ma W'
Wɔ daa ayɛyi mu.

MHB 1018
10 . Nna hom ma yɛnhom do nkodu
Edà a yebodu fie;
O bra, yɛ ntsɛm fi sor sian bra
Jesus, Pomfo Kɛse!

MHB 1018
2 . Yɛnam Woara Wo mu yɛbae,
Hɛn akoma yɛ kor;
O Jesus, yehyiaa Wo dzin mu,
Yɛpaam' so Wo dzin mu.

MHB 1018
3 . Yɛpaam' honamm', nnyɛ sunsum mu,
Na hɛn adwen si kor;
Hɛn nyina yɛfam Jesus hὸ a,
Hɛn nsa bɛda nsam' daa.

MHB 1018
4 . Hɛn sunsum nyinaa yέ adze kor,
Wɔpaa hɛnm' à ɔnnkɛyɛ;
Nkokwaa bɔsoɛr, epo bɛpram,
Worunntum mmpaa hɛn mu.

MHB 1018
5 . Hɛn nkwa wɔ Christ hɔ wɔ Nyamem';
Hɛn Nkwa befir edze ntsɛm,
Na oeyi N' enyimnyam akyѐrɛ
Wɔ Ne mfɛwbam' wɔ ha.

MHB 1018
6 . Hɛn sunsum wɔ No tum n-sam',
Ɔdze hɛn besie daa;
Na menye wo yɛnye N' begyina
zion koko no do.

MHB 1018
7 . Hɛn enyi bohu No wɔ hɔ,
Yɛbɛhyѐrɛn dɛ ꓛno:
Ahotsewfo nye abɔfo hyia a,
O 'bɛn enyimnyam nye 'i!

MHB 1018
8 . O, n-hyiamu no bɛyɛ dɛw!
Yɛbɛhyɛ ntar fitaa,
Yebenyinam menankɔnson
Na yɛasoa ahenkyɛw.

MHB 1018
9 . Nna hom mbɔ mbɔdzen ma yɛnko,
Yɛnko ntsew mu nkɔ sor;
Hɛn adwen ngyinà ewiei no do,
Hɛn enyi ntsim botae n'.

MHB 1019
10 NYAME, fa wo nhyira pon hɛn,
Ma yɛnkɔ asomdwee mu;
Yɛnda ho ndzi sor edziban;
Dɔr hɛn gyedzi nye hɛn dɔ:
Fa akomatɔmù hyɛ hɛn mu;
Yɛdze hɛn 'koma ma Wo;
Yenya du hɛn siar bea no dὸ a,
Yɛbɛma Wo ayɛyi pa!
Alleluia.      Amen.

MHB 102
1 . BƐKYEBO Dɔ a daa ayɛ ma,
Daa nyina ɔpem kwa,
Wɔkyɛ ma obiara nya bi,
Ɔwɔ hɔ daa, ɔnnsa.

MHB 102
2 . Hɛn anofamfa bɔ Dzin no,
Dzin no sen edzin nyina;
Ɔdɔ nko na onyim mbrɛ ofi,
Na ɔtse ɔdɔ ase.

MHB 102
3 . Bi a yɛnnkɔfow akɔ sor,
'Wuradze Christ aba famu;
Yɛhwehwɛ No wɔ bun mu kwa,
Bun biara nnkɛmen No.

MHB 102

Bɔn mu awerɛhow,
Odzi N'ankasa ho dase,
Ne dasee wɔ No mu.

MHB 102

Ɔyɛ Ɔboafo kɛse;
Gyedzi da ho wɔ N' Olivet, 
Ɔdɔ wɔ N' Galilee.

MHB 102
6 . N'atar a wɔammpam mu ayarsa n',
Ɔbɛn hɛn yaw mpa mpo;
Yɛper na yɛdze hɛn nsa ka N',
Na yenya ayarsa.

MHB 102
7 . Yedua No do dze hɛn mpaabɔ, 
Mbofra mpaabɔ mpo koraa;
Dza ewufo ka no berɛww mpo,
Ne dzin ahyɛ mu ma.

MHB 102
8 . Hɛn nyina hɛn Ewuradze na hɛn Wura,
Mbrɛ hɛn dzin tse biara,
Yedzi W'ekyir, yɛtse Wo frɛ,
Yɛdze W' sɔ hɛn bra hwɛ.

MHB 1020
1 . EWÙRADZE a meda ho twer Wo,
'Besie m' nokwarm' akɔ ewiei;
Wo nokwar, Wo dɔ, nye Wo tum
Bɛgye m' akɔ me mber ewiei;
Sɛ moto honam yi ase a
'Dze kyɛw a ɔnnsɛɛ botua m' kaw.

MHB 1020
2 . Jesus, Wo dzin kɛse no mu
Na mirikedzi owu do nym;
Migya dɛtse durdur yi hɔ
Na abɔfo soa m' atsaban do a,
Me kra botwà owu-mprɛnu mpὸ a,
Na oedzi hen daa daa wɔ wim'.

MHB 1020
3 . Enyi nnhunii, aso nn-tsee
Dza Christ ahyehyέ ama Ne mba a
Wɔnam Gyefo n' tum mu dzi nyim;

Wɔdze hɔn nan tsia owu do,
Wowu ahomkam' hyia hɔn Wùra.

MHB 1020
4 . Ana 'pɛ dɛ ehwehwɛ hu
Dzin fofor a wɔdze bɛma wo?
Dzi aper wɔ wo tamfo do nyim wɔ wum';
Ɔno 'reper hwehwɛ no gyan:
Konyim nko na otum kyerɛ.

MHB 1021
1 . YESÙ mfɛfὸ a wɔkɔ yɛ dɛn?

MHB 1021

Hɔn Tsir no Ne nkyɛn a?

MHB 1021

MHB 1021

MHB 1022
1 . Enye me ntsѐna! onwim ano rotɔ;

MHB 1023

MHB 1031

3 . Tsie, owu yɛ nda ma kwantunyi;
Ɔbra n’akotorka dzenndzen,
Ɔbra n’enyibɔ nyina twa m’ sen;
Tsie, owu yɛ nda ma kwantunyi.

MHB 1074
4 . Ao, owu yɛ dɛw ma Christ suanyi;
Bɛkyebo dɛw, bɛkyebo nkwa.
Na owu ma yenya no kwa;
Ao, owu yɛ dɛw ma Christ suanyi.

MHB 1074
5 . Sãa owu yɛ mfaso, mo dɔfo;
Alleluia, Alleluia,
Alleluia nkã Ɔkorsa,
Sãa owu yɛ mfaso, mo dɔfo.

MHB 1075
1 . AMANAMAN robɔ mbubuw,
Rekã mmɔn yi, asѐ ɛ ?

Ma enyidar nyina asa.

Ma woayε kyirpaafo,

MHB 1075

MHB 1076
1 .WIADZE mbusù a ! Enntsѐ ase?

Ma worutwà ewuo, atse ?

MHB 1076

MHB 1076

MHB 1076

MHB 1077

MHB 108
1 . Jesu, Wo ho adwen nko mpo 
Dze dɛw hyɛ mo mu ma;
Na meba m' bohu W' enyim dze a,
Edɛw no bɔbor do.

MHB 108
2 . O adasa hɛn Agyenkwa, 
Dzin biara nnto Wodze a
Yɛdze enyigye bɔtow ho ndwom,
Na yɛadwen ho dɔ mu.

MHB 108
3 . O 'koma bobɔe n' Enyidar, 
Abrɛfo Enyigye,
Iye ma asehwefo na
Hɔn a wɔhwehwɛ Wo.

MHB 108
4 . Na hɔn a wohu Wo nka dɛn? 
Wonnhu dza wɔnka mpo:
Hɔn a wɔtse Wo dɔ nko ara
Na wonyim ne dɛw no.

MHB 108
5 . Jesu, yɛ hɛn enyigye ndɛ, 
Hɛn ndaamba akatua;
Jesu, yɛ hɛn Enyimnyam ndɛ
Na mfesantsen nyina.    Amen.

MHB 109
1 . Jesu, 'koma dɔyɛfo hɔn Dɛw, 
Adasa Kan, nkwa Nsunyiwa,
Wiadze mu ndzepa nntum mmee hɛn,
Yɛdze kɔm yɛdan ba Wo hɔ.

MHB 109
2 . Wo nokwar si pi, ɔnnsakyer; 
Nyia ɔfrɛ Wo n' egye no nkwa;
Iye ma nyia ɔhwehwɛ Wo,
Nyia ohu Wo n' N' adze nyina.

MHB 109
3 . Yɛsɔ Wo hwɛ, n-kwa Edziban, 
Na hɛn kɔn dɔ yeedzi bi daa;
Yɛnom Wo, n-kwa Esutsen,
Na hɛn kra pɛ ma wɔaahyɛ n' ma.

MHB 109
4 . Hɛn sunsum haahaa hwehwɛ Wo, 
Mbrɛ ɔbra dze hɛn si biara,
Eyaa W' ano hɛn enyi gye,
Yesuo Wom' a siar aka hɛn.

MHB 109
5 . O Jesus, nye hɛn ntsena daa, 
Ma hɛn mber pa na asomdwee;
Yi bɔn no sum nyina wɔ hɔ,
Ma Wo kan no nhyerɛn wiadze.    Amen.

MHB 11
1 . YƐDZE enyigye sɔr, dzi dɛw, yɛtow ndwom,
Yɛdze hɛn siar akoma na hɛn ndze aba,
Ndaase asɛm dadaw no bodu Wo tsenabea,
Ɔwo a eyɛ enyimnyam Hɛn, Nyame yamuyiefo.

MHB 11
2 . Dza ɔfata W' yɛdze ma W', enyidzi mapa,
Yɛnye W'abɔdze nyina, sor, asaase na po,
Bɔ m' dze W'ayɛyi ma W' wɔ wiadze mbea nyina,
Yɛdze ɔnosɛɛ tonton, huhor Wo daa nyina.

MHB 11
3 . Wo Sunsum woo hɛn fofor, Wo Ba n' gyee hɛn,
Wo mba dzi Wo nyi wɔ dza ayɛ nyina ntsi,
Egya, Wo mba resan aba dɔ na kan m'.
Yɛreper atonton Wo dɛ mbrɛ ɔsɛ.

MHB 11
4 . Yɛka abɔfo ho na yɛtow Wo ndwom,
Alleluia! Amà asaase aagye do,
Amen! Enyimnyam nka Wo sor nye ase,
Domankoma dɔ a ɔpon hɛn, konyimdzifo!

MHB 110
1 . Jesu, me kra no Dɔfo, 
Ma munguan mbɛhyɛ Wo bom',
Ber a esu no repem yi,
Ber a ehum no rutu yi,
Me Gyefo, fa me hunta,
Ma ehum no mbɔ mbɛsen;
Gya me kodu berano,
Ao, ewiei no gye me kra.

MHB 110
2 . Minnyi sumabew biara, 
Me kra twer Wo nkotonoo;
Mma nndan mo nkotonoo nngya,
Suo mo mu, kyekye mo werɛ:
Mo werɛ gyina Wo do,
Mo mboa nyina fir wo hɔ;
Fa W' atsaban kɛse no
Kata m' etsikwa yi do.

MHB 110
3 . Christ, morohwehwɛ Wo nko, 
Minya W' a menya adze nyina,
Ma mo do si, hyɛ me dzen,
Yɛ m' edur na gye me nkwa:
'Wo na eyɛ tseneneenyi,
'Midze, meyɛ brakyewnyi;
Bɔn na ahyɛ emi ma,
Adom ahyɛ wo so ma.

MHB 110
4 . Adom pii wɔ Wo nsam' a 
Ɔkata mo bɔn nyina do;
Ma nkwa nsu no ɔmpem mbra,
San mo ho na fa me sie:
N-kwa Nsunyiwa nye Woara,
Ma membɛsaw bi monnom,
Bra bɛtaa mo 'koma mu,
Taa mu kɔ mfesantsen nyina.  Amen.

MHB 111
1 . JESUS, dɛm enyiwa yi nnhun

        nntse W' nka,

MHB 112

MHB 113

MHB 114

MHB 114

MHB 114

MHB 116

MHB 117

MHB 118

MHB 119

MHB 12
1 . Me kra, yi ɔsor hen ayɛw, 
Fa w' ayɛdze bra N' enyim;
Ɔapon wo, dze wo bɔn akyɛ w',
Woana mbɔ nyi No ayɛw?
Yi No ayɛw!
Yi bɛkyebo Hen ayɛw.

MHB 12
2 . Yi N' ayɛw, Nadom na enyimpa 
Hwɛɛ egyanom ahohiam';
Yi No ayɛw, ɔnnsakyer da,
Ɔka enyim nyaa, ohyira ntsɛm:
Yi No ayɛw!
Nyimnyamfo wɔ nokwardzim'.

MHB 12
3 . Ɔhwɛ hɛn, dze fir hɛn dɛ egya;

Ɔgye hɛn atamfo nyina nsam',
Yi No ayɛw!
Dɛ mbrɛ N' adom pem mber nyina.

MHB 12

Hom hu N' enyim na enyim;
Ewia, bosoom, hom nkotow, No,
Mber na mbea nyinam' abɔdze,
Hom nyi N' ayɛw!
Hom nye hɛn nyi Nyame ayɛw.    Amen.

MHB 120
1 . O Christianfo, hom nnyan na adze akye, 
Anapa yi na wɔwoo Agyenkwa;
Hom nsoɛr na hom ntonton Nyame dɔ,
Esumasɛm a abɔfo tow ho ndwom;
Hɔn na wodzii kan kaa n-sɛmpa no,
Mbrɛ Nyame bɛbrae ma ɔbaabun woo N'.

MHB 120
2 . N-guanhwɛfo a wɔroweɔn hɔn nguan no 
Tsee bɔfo huafo ne ndze dɛ ɔse:
Hwɛ, medze Agyenkwa N' awoo ho nsɛm
Bɔ hom na wiadze nyina amandzɛɛ;
N-dɛ Nyame apon N' anohoba,
Wɔawo Ewuradze Christ, hɛn Agyenkwa.

MHB 120
3 . Owiee kasaa n', nna sor adwontofo 
Dze enyigye toow ndwom fofor koraa,
Wɔkamfoo Nyame dɔ a ɔropon hɛn,
Na Alleluia gyigyee wim' nyina;
Hɔn ndwom nye dɛ, Enyimnyam nka Nyame,
Asomdwee na enyisɔ mbra nyimpam'.

MHB 120
4 . Hɔ ara na nguanhwɛfo n', kɔr Bethlehem 
Kɔhwɛɛ dza Nyame ayɛ ama adasa:
Wɔdze enyigye saan kɔhwɛɛ hɔn nguan,
Dɛ wɔda ho riyi Nyame ayɛw,
Yinom nye asomafo a wodzii kan
Wɔbɔɔ Abofra no ho nsɛm dawur.

MHB 120
5 . N-kyɛ  yaakaa Nyame N' anwanwa dɔ a 
Ogyaa N' ma ɔregye adasa nkwa;
Abofra a ɔama yeenya hɛn siar yi,
Yɛnhwɛ N' mbowadan mu nkɔ mbeamudua n' do:
Ɔmboa hɛn ma yentsia N' anamɔn mu
Nkodu adasa hɛn sor sibea hɔ.

MHB 120
6 . Dɛm na hɛn ho bɛtsew ma yaafora 
Abɔfodɔm yɛatow konyimdzi ndwom;
Nyia wɔawo N' n-dɛ enyigye da yi,
Ɔdze enyimnyam bɛhyerɛn hɛn ho nyina;
No dɔ bɛgye hɛn nkwa na yaatow ndwom
Afebɔɔ yɛakamfo sor Hen tumfo n'.

MHB 121
1 . M'AKOMA dzi ehurusi enago 'i
Ber a ekyirkyir metse
Abɔfo ndze dɛɛdɛw n';
'Dwontofo n' tow dɛ, Wɔawo Christ!
Na enyigye ndwom dɛɛdɛw n'
Gyegye wimu nyina.

MHB 121
2 . Tsie! Dzidzidaka n' mu ndze bi
Reserɛ bɔkɔɔ se dɛ:
Hom nguan mfi mbusu ho,
Nuanom, hom mbra, hom efi haw mu, 
Wɔagye hom; dza hom hia
Nyina mebɛma hom.

MHB 121
3 . Afei hom mma yɛnyɛ no ntsɛm, 
'Kɛse na nkuma nyina,
Nkotow suro nwanwa m'.
Yɛndɔ Nyia dɔ ahyɛ No ma n',
Nhua Woraba a ɔdze
Enyidar rehyerɛn no.

MHB 121
4 . O Ewuradze , m'betsie, adɔ W', 
Nye W' atsena, na sɛ 
Muwu mpo a, maannhera,
Na mbom menye W' atsena afebɔɔ
Wɔ sorsor wɔ dɛw a
Ɔnnkɛsakyer da n' mu.

MHB 122
1 . Adzekyee mba nyinara mu dansewa, 
Pa hɛn isum na fa wo mboa brɛ hɛn;
Boka nworaba a epue ma wim' atsew wann,
Gya hɛn kɔ mbrɛ wɔawo Gyefo ama hɛn.

MHB 122
2 . N' adasoe do na bɔw rososɔ hyɛnhyɛnn; 
Nantwibuwm' na ɔdze Ne tsir ato komm;
Ɔda hɔ n' abɔfo ruhuahua no dɛ,
Adasa Yɛfo, Ɔhen na Gyefo.

MHB 122
3 . Aso ampa dɛ hɛn so yɛbɛkyɛ No 
Edom nduhuam na asomfo akyɛdze,
Mbepɔw do mbobaa, po do nankyenema,
Kwaa mu wandze, daadzetsirmu sika?

MHB 122
4 . Hɛn ayɛyɛdze piigyan nyina nnsɛ hwee; 
Akyɛdze biara nntum nnya N' enyimpa;
Akomam' ndaase na abɔbɔfo mpaabɔ
Som bo kɛsekɛse ma Onyame.

MHB 122
5 . Adekyee mba nyinara mu dansewa, 
Pa hɛn isum na fa wo mboa brɛ hɛn;
Boka nworaba a epue ma wim' atsew wann,
Gya hɛn kɔ mbrɛ wɔawo Gyefo ama hɛn.

MHB 123
1 . 'NAGO sɔnn, anago krɔnn!
Wiadze ada, esuma,
Mary na Joseph wɔ mbowa dan mu 
Roweɔn Dɔba fɛɛfɛw no a 
Ɔada sor ahomgye mu n'.

MHB 123
2 . 'Nago sɔnn, anago krɔnn!
Nguanhwɛfo hun kan no,
Tsee abɔfo ndwom no ne ngyegyee,
Wɔ anoano nye ekyirekyir,
Christ hɛn Pomfo n' wɔ ha.

MHB 123
3 . 'Nago sɔnn, anago krɔnn!
Nyame Ba a ehyerɛn, 
Ɔdɔ reserew W'enyimdua mu!
Ma adom ber no mbra mbɔto hɛn, 
Agyenkwa a wɔawo W' ntsi!

MHB 124
1 . Hwɛ, wɔawo Nyame Eguambaa a 
Wɔdze N' bɔɔ anohoba n',
Oesian aba asaase
Rebɛkyerɛ hɛn ɔsor kwan. 

      Ao, hɛn siar da, aba yie! 
      Hwɛ hɛn nkwahosan aba! 
      Tow ndwom twa Jerusalem: 
      Wɔawo Christ wɔ Bethlehem!

MHB 124
2 . Hwɛ, nyia ɔtse ahengua do 
Wɔ sorsor abɔfo ntam'
Nyia ɔyɛɛ wim' nworaba n',
Da mbowa dzidzidaka mu.

MHB 124
3 . Hom n-guanhwɛfo krɔnkrɔn, 
Hom dze asɛmpa bɛn nam?
Wɔyɛ n' dɛn na hom egya
Hom nguan wɔ haban mu yi?

MHB 124
4 . Esuom a yɛroweɔn no, 
Hwɛ, yehun kan nwanwa bi:
Abɔfo dze adwontow
Kaa dɛ wɔawo Agyenkwa n'.

MHB 124
5 . O Akɔkowaba krɔnkrɔn, 
Wo dɔ yɛ nwanwa dodow!
Dɔ a ogyaa W' ma ifii sor
Baa wiadze a ɔtse dɛm yim'.

MHB 124
6 . O Nyame Ba, Kyerɛkyerɛ hɛn 
Wo suban a ɔdwe  no,
Ma yensua Wo mbrɛhoadze,
Na yɛnyɛ dɛ mbrɛ Ɔwo tse.

MHB 125
1 . O Bethlehem kurow kakraba,
Hwɛ mbrɛ esi ada dzinn!
Bea a ada hatsee n'etsifi
N-woraba rikyin komm:
W'abɔntsen no do anago n'
Bɛkyebo kan n' hyerɛn;
Mber nyina enyidar na suro 
Dzi ehia wɔ Wo mu.

MHB 125
2 . Anapa mworaba, hom mbɔ mu
M-bɔ awoo krɔnn n' dawur,
Na hom ntow ndwom mma Nyame Hen n',
Asomdwee nka asaase;
Na Mary awo ɔba Christ;
Nna abɔfo aboa ano wimu,
Roweɔn ɔdɔ nwanwa Ba no,
Ber a adasa so ada n'.

MHB 125
3 . Akyɛdze nwanwa no wɔdze
Maa wiadze dzinn na komm!
Dɛm na Nyakoɔn kyɛ nyimpa
Siar akyɛdze fi sor.
Asowa bi nnkɛtse Ne mbae,
Mbom bɔn wiadze yi mu,
Abrɛfo a wɔgye No n' na
Christ dɔyɛfo n' to hɔn.

MHB 125
4 . O Bethlehem Ɔba krɔnkrɔn,
Yeserɛ Wo, bra hɛn nkyɛn;
Pam hɛn bɔn na afei tsena hɛn mu;
Ma wɔnwo W' hɛn mu ndɛ.
Yɛtse Borɔnya abɔfo n'
Nka dɛ wɔrobɔ amandzɛɛ n';
O bra hɛn nkyɛn, nye hɛn ntsena,
Hɛn Wura Immuanuel.  Amen

MHB 126
1 . M'AKOMA, hwɛ, ma w'enyi do:
Woana da edzidzidaka n' m' hɔ?
Woana nye Akɔkowa fɛɛfɛw yi?
Akɔkowa Christ siarfo n' nye No.

MHB 126
2 . Ewuradze a ebɔɔ adze nyina,
Mbrɛ esi ayɛ Wo ho keteseaba,
Dɛ ebɛyɛ W' dabew wɔ bea a
Nsoaso na anantwi dzidzi.

MHB 126
3 . Sɛ wiadze ne fɛw yɛ mbordo,
Na sika na abopa anyɛ n' ma a,
Nkyɛ iyi mpo mmfata koraa dɛ 
Ɔwo Ewuradze bɛda hɔ.

MHB 126
4 . Ao, Jesus Akɔkowa krɔnkrɔn!
Bra bɛhyehyɛ Wo mpa a ho tsew n'
Wɔ m'akoma bɔbɔfo m' ma
Ɔaayɛ mpiatun dzinn ama Wo.

MHB 126
5 . M'akoma keka n' ho dɛw mu daa,
Na m'ano nnkɛyɛ komm bio da;
Medze dɛw m'bɔtow Wo ndwom daa,
Tsetse abagyegye ndwom dɛɛdɛw n'.

MHB 126
6 . Enyimnyam nka Nyame wɔ sor,
Ɔno a ɔdze Ne Ba ama nyimpa,
Ber a abɔfo dze dɛw ma hɛn
Afenhyia pa wɔ asaase do.

MHB 127
1 . NYIMPA Ba no dze Ne tsir too
Mbowa edzidzidaka n’ mu;
Ͻdaa wiadze ha Ne nda kan
Nguanhwɛfo no dze enyigye tsiee
‘Bͻfo krͻnkrͻn n’amandzɛɛ;
Hͻn a wͻwͻ nguambuw mu hͻ n’
Dze enyigye soom hͻn Wura.

MHB 127
2 . Hͻn a wͻtsee Ne famu ha mbae
Nka n’ nyina nyaa enyigye;
Na hͻn so a wohuaa Ne mbae no,
Kamfo No dͻ n’, nyaa dɛw pii.
Agyenkwa Siarfo, Christ krͻnkrͻn,
Edaa mbowa edzidzibea;
Innkotum abrɛ Woho adze
Abɛtsena m’akoma m’?

MHB 127
3 . Ndzebͻn edzi W’enyim kan kͻ;
Akoma a wͻtoo mu pon n’,
Ana bɛhɛn mu mbͻbͻr mu,
Nyimpa Ba,dze Wo tsir ato?
Afei hɛn mu, Jesus krͻnkrͻn,
Yɛ Borͻnya wͻ m’akomam’;
Ma mo mbowa edzidzibea ndan
Heaven a Ͻwo wͻ hͻ no.

MHB 127
4 . Ma hͻn a wͻanntse W’awoo ho
Nsɛmpa no nyinara no,
Wͻwͻmber dadaw m’ , nnyɛ Borͻnya m’,
Wͻmfa W’asomdwee mbrɛ hͻn,
Fa enyigye asɛmpa n’ brɛ hͻn,
Ma wͻntse Borͻnya ndwom no wͻ hͻ:
Yi Nyame ayɛw, Christ aba!

MHB 128
1 . DƐ mbrɛ nkɔnhyɛfo kae no, ɔbaabun bi 
Awo Akɔkowaba; dɛm na osii,
Dɛ ɔmbɔpon hɛn owu, hɛll na bɔn a 
Adam ne mbrato dze furaa hɛn no mu.
       Dɛm ntsi hom enyi ngye, ntow awerɛhow ngu;
       Wɔwoo hɛn Agyenkwa Jesus Christ ber yi.

MHB 128
2 . Na Jewfo kurow bi a wɔfrɛ n' Bethlehem,
Hɔ na Joseph na Mary nyina kɔsoɛe,
Ama wɔaakan hɔn na binom wɔ ɔtow ntsi,
Osiandɛ dɛm na Caesar hyɛɛ dɛ wɔnyɛ.

MHB 128
3 . Na wokodur kurow fɛɛfɛw no mu no,
Nna nyimpadodow ahyɛ hɔ nyina ma,
Ma Joseph nye Mary a wɔyɛ ehiafo n'
Ennya kwan biara wɔ ahɔhodan no mu.

MHB 128
4 . Na okehiaa dɛ wɔkɔsoɛ edzdzidaka m'
Beebi a daa wɔdze anantwu na nguan gui:
Na wɔammfɛr dɛm famu famu tsenabea hɔ koraa,
Na n'adzkyee n' ara na wɔwoo Agyenkwa.

MHB 128
5 . Adasa nyina ahenfo Hen n' aba wiadze
Ndwera kakraba na wonyaa kyekyeer N' ho;
Na Mary kyekyeer ne Ba no ho wiei no,
Ɔdze No too nantwi edzidzidaka mu.

MHB 128
6 . Na Nyame somaa ɔbɔfo fii sorsor
Kɔr nguanhwɛfo ehiafo bi nkyɛn, wɔ sar do,
Kɛsee hɔn dɛ mma wonndzi awerɛhow bio,
'Siandɛ wɔawo hɛn Agyenkwa ndɛ da yi.

MHB 128
7 . Amon mu hɔ ara na nguanhwɛfo no hun
Abɔfo dɔm kɛse dɛ wɔwɔ wimu;
Wɔdze dɛw kɛse kasae, toow ndwom dɛɛdɛw 
Dɛ enyimnyam nka Nyame hɛn sor Hen no.

MHB 129
1 . Anago bi na nguanhwɛfo 
Tsena fam' roweɔn hɔn nguan,
Ewuradze bɔfo fi sor bae,
Na kan hyerɛɛn hɔ nyina.

MHB 129
2 . Ihu kɛse kaa hɔn n-tsi 
Ɔsee dɛ, Mma hom nnsuro:
Mebrɛ hom na adasa nyina
Asɛmpa a ɔyɛ dɛw.

MHB 129
3 . Wɔawo Agyenkwa ama hom 
Wɔ David ahenkurowm',
Wɔawo Ewuradze Christ n-dɛ;
Yi na hom dze bohu N':

MHB 129
4 . Hom bohu dɛ Akɔkowaba n' 
Da mbowa dzidzidakam',
Hom bohu No nantwibuw mu,
Dɛ tam kyekye No ho.

MHB 129
5 . Nyame bɔfo n' wiee dɛm ka ara, 
Na sor dɔm pii bae a
Wɔdze ndwom yii Nyame ayɛw
Enyigye mu see dɛ:

MHB 129
6 . Enyimnyam nka Nyame wɔ sor, 
Asomdwee nka 'saase;
Nyame enyisɔ nhyɛ ase
Wɔ adasa mu ndɛ.   Amen.

MHB 13
1 . ƆSORSOR, hom nyi Ewuradze ayɛw; 
Ewia, bosoom, dzi N'enyim dɛw; 
Nworaba, kan, hom ntonton No.

MHB 13
2 . Yi Ewuradze ayɛw na ɔakasa a, 
Wiadze tsiee ne ndze kɛse n'; 
mbrasɛm a wonnkobu do da, 
Wɔ hɔ ma hɛn akwankyerɛ.

MHB 13
3 . Yi Ewuradze ayɛw, nyimnyamfo no a;
 N'anohoba nnyɛ gyan da; 
Ɔama N'ahotsewfo konyim; 
Bɔn na wu nnkedzi nyim da.

MHB 13
4 . Yi hɛn nkwagye Nyame ayɛw; 
Sor dɔm mpaa mu nka No tum; 
Sor na asaase nye abɔdze nyina
Ntonton No, nhuhor Ne dzin.   Amen.

MHB 130
1 . ƆBAA danafua kɔnnkɔnn bi
Abɔfo a woesian famu
Robɔ hɔn sika nsanku toow
Tsetse ndwom dɛɛdɛw n' dɛ 
'Somdwee na pɛpa nka adasa,
Omfi sor Hen hɔ mbra!
Na wiadze ntaa dzinn ara ntsie
Abɔfɔ hɔn ndwom no.

MHB 130
2 . Wɔkɔr do ara fi sor sianee,
Wɔdze asomdwee sianee,
Na wɔtsee hɔn sorsor ndwom no
Wɔ fona wiadze yi m',
N'awerɛhow paprata no mu;
Wotuu faa kyinkyinii,
Wɔtoow ndwom n' ma wɔtsee no wɔ
Babel nkwaado nyina.

MHB 130
3 . Wiadze ehu amandze akyɛr 
Wɔ bɔn na aperdzi ho;
Abɔfo ndwom dɛɛdɛw n' ekyir,
Bɔn etsim mfe mpenu;
Adasa roko ntsi wɔnntse
Dɔ ndwom a wɔdze ma, n';
O akofo, hom nyɛ komm ntsie
Sor abɔfo ndwom no.

MHB 130
4 . Hom a abrabɔ ahyɛ hom do
Ma ntsi hom kɔn ebu,
Hom a hom berɛ wɔ kwan do
Ma hom nntum nnantsew yie,
Hom nhwɛ! Engyigye na mber pa
Dze ntsaban reba ntsɛm:
O hom nhom wɔ ɔfona kwan n' nkyɛn 
Ntsie abɔfo ndwom yi.

MHB 130
5 . Hom nhwɛ! Nda n' reba ntsɛntsɛm a
Nkɔnyɛfo aka n' dada;
Ɔdze mber pa a akyɛr no 
Bɛba ber pa no mu.
Asomdwee bɛba wiadze nyina,
Tsetse ahoɔfɛw n' epue;
Na wiadze nyina agye ndwom a
Abɔfo rotow no.

MHB 131
1 . BORƆNYA a odzi kan a ɔbɔfo no kae n',
Ɔkaa kyerɛɛ nguanhwɛfo bi a wɔwɔ sar do,
Nna wɔwɔ sar n' do rohwɛ hɔn nguan
Ɔpɛber 'nafua bi a nna awɔw aba.
    Borɔnya afe pa! Borɔnya afe pa!
    Wɔawo Israelmba hɔn Hen.

MHB 131
2 . Wɔhwɛɛ sor na wohun woraba a
Ɔrehyerɛn boka ekyirekyire,
Na ɔrema asaase kan kɛse,
Na ɔyɛɛ dɛm adzekyee na adzesaa.

MHB 131
3 . Na enyansafo baasa bi nam
Woraba n' ne kan mu fi ekyirkyir bae;
Wɔbaa dɛ wɔrobɔhwɛ Ɔhen n'
Na woeetsin woraba n' do ekyinkyin.

MHB 131
4 . Woraba yi kɔr kwaamu-anee
Siankaa Bethlehem do kakra;
Na ekyir no ogyinaa koraa
Wɔ beebi a Jesus da no.

MHB 131
5 . Enyansafo baasa n' hɛɛn mu 
Buu nkotodwe enyidzi mu ara;
Na N'enyim hɔ ara yɛɛ N' ayɛ: 
Sika, krɔbɔɔ na akyenkyendur.

MHB 131
6 . Dɛm a wɔmma yɛmfa adwen kor
Ntow ayɛyi mma hɛn sor Hen no,
Ɔno na ɔmaa sor na asaase bae
Na ɔdze N' bɔgyaa tɔ adasa.

MHB 132
1 . DƐ mbrɛ tsetsemba no nam
Enyigye mu hwɛɛ woraba n'
Na wɔdze dɛw huaa ne kan a
Ɔhyerɛɛnee kyerɛɛ kwan n',
Ewuradze, dɛm na hɛn so
Wɔnkyerɛn hɛn kwan mbra Wo hɔ.

MHB 132
2 . Dɛ mbrɛ wɔdze dɛw tuu anan
Baa Agyenkwa Wo mpa ho ara
Bobuu ntwɛr wɔ Ɔwo a sor na
Asaase sɔr Wo W'enyim n',
Dɛmara na ma hɛn so
Nhwehwɛ mbɔbɔrhu egua n'.

MHB 132
3 . Dɛ mbrɛ wɔkyɛɛ W' dza ho hia
Wo wɔ ehiafo mpa no ho n',
Dɛmara pɛr na hɛn so
Mfa dwɛw krɔnn a bɔn nnyi mu
Mfua hɛn aboɔdzendze mu,
Mbrɛ Wo Christ hɛn sorsor Hen.

MHB 132
4 . Jesus krɔnkrɔn, fa hɛn si
Kwan tseabaa no mu daa daa, 
Na sɛ wiadze bɔ adze a,
Fa hɛn akra a woefi nsa n'
Kɔ bea a wonnhia wimu kwankyerɛ,
Bea a fua nnhyɛ W'enyimnyam do.

MHB 132
5 . Ɔsor man hyɛnhyɛnn no mu
Wonnhia abɔdze kan biara;
Ɔwo nye n' kan, dɛw, abɔtsir,
Ɔwo nye n'ewia a ɔnntɔ da;
Yɛntow W'ayɛyi wɔ hɔ, 
Hallelujah nka hɛn Hen.   Amen.

MHB 133
1 . ENYANSAFO bi fii
Hɔn nyimdzee mu twae
Fii boka mbepɔw do 
Kɔr 'bɔbɔfo fie.
Nyamesom pa gyaa hɔn
Ntsɛm fii ekyirkyir,
Towee kɔr kan daa daa,
Tsiin woraba bi do.

MHB 133
2 . Hɔ na hɔn Wura na
Gyefo brɛfo n' da,
Kan nwanwa a odzii hɔn kan
Wɔ hɔn akwantu mu n'
Bɔkɔ do ahyerɛn
Ekyirkyir aman do;
Ber a woraba no dze hɔn 
Resan akɔ hɔn nkyir.

MHB 133
3 . Ɔwo a da bi edaa
Mbowa edzidzidaka m',
Na sesei idzi hen
Nyimnyam m' aman do,
Boaboa wiadzefo a
Wɔwɔ ekyir n' ano,
Hɔn a wonnhun woraba n'
Kwankyerɛ kan no.

MHB 133
4 . Boaboa tokyemfo ano;
Dɔnsuartɔfo no,
Tow Wo kan n' gu hɔn do,
Gya hɔn abamba;
Hɔn a wonnhun Wo no,
Hɔn a wɔato gon n',
Fa Wo woraba ne hyerɛn 
Gya hɔn abamba.

MHB 133
5 . Gya hɔn fa sum kebii m',
Ber a obi nnkɔ mmba n',
Hyerɛn dzi hɔn enyim kan
Wɔ Wo dɔ kan n' mu;
Jewfo na Amamforafo,
Akobɔfo nyina,
Mbofra na mpanyin so,
Fa woraba n' gya hɔn.

MHB 134
1 . 'NYIMNYAM nka Nyame wɔ sor, 
Na asomdwee nsian asaase;
Nyankopɔn, dwir, konton wimu,
Na ɔkyerɛ dɛ ɔyɛ nyɛnko:
Nyame a yennhu No n'aba:
Nyame osiarfo, MARA
Aba nyinsu bɔnsa yi m'
Na Ne dzin nye Jesus.

Hom nhw sor na ase Wura a
Afei wɔyɛɛ No honam n'
Da mbowa edzidzibea.

MHB 134
2 . Abɔfo nyina tontoon
Hɔn Bɔfo na hɔn Hen;
Wɔdze hɔn Wura brɛfo n'
Ho nsɛm brɛɛ adasa.
Ɔtoo N'ahendzi no pan,
N'enyimnyam nwanwa n' hyerɛn, 
Nkwa farbaa no hyɛ ase;
Wɔawo Nyame ankasa!

MHB 134
3 . Hwɛ Nyame Ba bɛkyebo n',
Nyimpa Ba bɛkyebo n';
Nyia sor enntum annkora No n'
Aba honandua mu.
Ɔsor mba, hom mbɔ mbubuw;

MHB 134
4 . Hɛn nyimpa mba, yendzi dɛw, 
Mbɔ asomdwee Hen n' dawur,
Yɛnye sor dɔm mma ndze do
Mfa Immanuel dzin ntsea m':
Hɛn anan, hɛn akoma kotow N',
Jesus hɛn honam mu nyi n'
Yɛ hɛn Nua sesei ampa,
Na Nyame yɛ hɛndze.

MHB 135
1 . Ɔsor dɔ no ɔkrɔn dodow, 
Nyame Baatan N' ayamuhyehye;
Ɔdze Agyenkwa fi sor bae,
Ɔmaa da pa n' hyerɛɛn hɛn do,
Na tsenenee ewia no puei,
Bɛtseew hɛn sum wiadze enyi.

MHB 135
2 . Nyame daa edzi wɔ Christ mu, 
Dze Ne kan abɛpam hɛn sum,
Etu hɛn bɔn na enyifura,
Dze hɛn nan esi kwan pa mu;
Na hɛn akra a woenya fakyɛ,
Akɔ daa ahomgye man no '.

MHB 135
3 . Ewuradze, fa Wo kan bra, 
Gyedzi a otu hɛn suro no a;
Ma Wo dɔ nkitsa hɛn 'koma,
Gya hɛn kɔ W' asomdwee kwan mu;
Hɛn akra a wosuro wu dzen,
Gya hɔn twa no sunsuma mu.

MHB 135
4 . Ma W' adom ne nhyehyɛɛ nda edzi, 
Nyame a ɔbɛyɛɛ nyimpa maa m';
Mo sunsum nyɛ Wo fie krɔnkrɔn,
Yɛ me kan na mo nkwagye mu;
Gya me twa owu sum no mu
Kodu W' ahengua enyim hɔ.

MHB 136
1 . EWIA na bosoom Yɛfo no,
Hɛn asaase yi Yɛfo n',
Hwɛ! Akyɛdze pa a ɔammba ntsɛm, 
Ɔaba ma wɔawo No.

MHB 136
2 . Ber a Nyame maa yɛdɔree no,
Wiadze nyaa siar kɛse;
Christ dze tsenenee na asomdwee
Bɛsaa akoma yarba.

MHB 136
3 . Ɔsor nworaba nyinara
Hyerɛɛn dze gyaa No kwan;
Naaso adasa nko na wɔmaa
Wohum Ne nyimpa su.

MHB 136
4 . Adaasa poow Ne nyimpa su,
Naaso owui hɛn bɔn ntsi;
No dɔ a wɔnam gyedzi do hu n'
Da ho gye wiadze nkwa.

MHB 136
5 . O ɔdɔ mapa a yenntum nnhu,
Kan a ɔtra ntseasee,
Sian bra wiadze anago yi,
Bɛsa akoma yarba.

MHB 137
1 . AWƆW kɛse ber mu,
Mframa nwin bi bɔe;
Famu yɛɛ dɛ dadze,
N-su kyeen dɛ ɔbo;
Esukwankyɛba tɔɔ pii,
'Sukwankyɛba;
Awɔw kɛse ber mu,
Tsetseber mu.

MHB 137
2 . Hɛn Nyame, sor nntum nnkora W',
Asaase so nntum;
Sor na asaase boguan
Ber a obedzi adze;
Awɔw kɛse ber no mu ',
Mbowadan mpo ye;
Ewuradze Nyame Tumfo,
O Jesus Christ!

MHB 137
3 . Nna abɔfo ahorow
Pii etwa ehyia;
Cherubfo, Seraphfo
Wokyiin wɔ wimu;
Naaso Ne na nkotoo wɔ
Ne mbaabun ber m'
Dze ɔdwe mfewano sɔɔr
No Dɔba no.

MHB 137
4 . Ebɛn na m'bɛma Wo
Emi hianyi yi?
Sɛ meyɛ guanhwɛfo a,
Nkyɛ m'bɛma 'guambaa;
Sɛ meyɛ nyansafo dze a,
Nkyɛ m'bɛyɛ m'dze;
Ebɛn mpo na m'bɛma?
M'akoma nko.

MHB 138
1 . ƆDƆ siaan Borɔnya ber,
Sunsum dɔ a ɔyɛ fɛw;
Wɔwoo ɔdɔ wɔ Borɔnya,
Woraba na abɔfo kyerɛɛ dɛm.

MHB 138
2 . Yɛsom Nyametsir no,
Nyame Dɔ a ɔyɛɛ Nyimpa; 
Yɛsom hɛn Jesus Christ;
Yɛmfa asɛnkyerɛdze bɛn?

MHB 138
3 . Dɔ bɛyɛ asɛnkyerɛdze,
Dɔ nyɛ wodze, nyɛ medze; 
Dɔ nka Nyame na adasa, 
Dɔ a ɔserɛ, kyɛ adze, hyɛ nsew.

MHB 139
1 . NYIMPA a wɔhyɛɛ sum mu kyɛree n'
Ehu enyimnyam kan no;
Hɔn a wɔtsenaa owu sum mu
Wɔ adzekyee kan mu.

MHB 139
2 . Aman no boaboa hɔn ano,
Ba bohua W', sor Ewia;
Sɛ wɔba a, wɔdze enyigye dɛ 
Hɔn a wobu ndɔbaa.

MHB 139
3 . Wɔawo Enyidar Ba ama hɛn 
Wɔama hɛn Babanyin;
Ebusua nyina betsie No,
Sor dɔm nyina betsie N'.

MHB 139
4 . Wɔbɛfrɛ No asomdwee Hen,
Na wɔbɔsɔr No daa;
Ɔnwanwanyi, Ɔfotufo,
Ewuradze Tumfo pa.

MHB 139
5 . No tum bɔkɔ do atserɛw,
N'ahendzi nnkɔbɔ adze;
Pɛrpɛr botwa No sor egua n'  ho
Ma asomdwee eebu do ha.

MHB 14
1 . HOM nyi sor Hen no ayɛw,
Ɔkora N'aban wɔ ase;
Yi ɔdɔ Nyame n'ayɛw,
Da N'akeseyɛ edzi;
Yi N'ayɛw, Ne ndzeyɛɛ ho,
Kamfo No tum kɛse no:
Ndzepa nyina fir No ho,
Sor na asaase ntonton N'.

MHB 14
2 . Hom mfa nsanku na ndwom pa 
Nkamfo daa daa Nyame n',
Akasaa na akyem ndze mbɔ m;
Nhur Ne dzin kɛse mo:
Nyia ɔwɔ ndze biara ntonton N';
Ɔsor edwindze nyina,
Hom mfa asokwadze nyina mbra,
Mbɔtow N'akoma m'ndwom.

MHB 14
3 . Wɔmma abɔdze nyina ntow ndwom,
Mma Nyia wɔtse No mu n',
Wɔnhyɛ hɔn Bɔfo enyimnyam,
Wongu N'enyim ebiritsi:
Hom ntsew Ne dzin ho wɔ ase,
Dɛ mbrɛ wɔyɛ no wɔ sor;
Wɔmma abɔdze nyina ntonton 
Ewuradze aber nyina.   Amen.

MHB 140
1 . NYAME fi sor atse;
Hom ngyaa nkrumsi nyina;
Na hom nhwɛ, wimu ebue!
'Somdwee akyɛdze n' esian.

MHB 140
2 . Tsie! Sor abɔfo ndze 
Gyegye anafua esuom; 
Ɔsor dɔm tsea mu dɛ, 
Nyame aba asaase do.

MHB 140
3 . Ka nguanhwɛfo no hɔ 
Kɔhwɛ adom esumasɛm;
Dza enyi hu nyina nye
Ɔba a ɔda nguambuw m'.

MHB 140
4 . Nnyɛ Oyi nye Ɔdomakoma Ba a
Ɔtse sor ahengua n' do,
Nyia wonnyaa mmbɔɔ wiadze n'
Ɔnye Egya no wɔ hɔ n'?

MHB 140
5 . Gyedzi Wura, mununkum a 
Odura N'enyimnyam ho n'
Hua Ewuradze Nyame,
Nyia abɔdze nyina kotow N'.

MHB 140
6 . Gyedzi hu ahengua n', 
Bea a abɔfo wɔ afebɔɔ;
Abɔfo ho popo,
Wɔdze ahopopo sɔr N'.

MHB 140
7 . Akɔkowa, Wo kommyɛ n' 
Kyerɛ hɛn dɛ yɛmpow
Dza honam pɛ biara,
Yennkyir akɔndɔbɔn.

MHB 140
8 . Fa dɔ krɔnkrɔn mee hɛn,
Yi hɛn ahantan kɔ;
Hɛn akoma brɛfo biara m',
Na tsena mu afebɔɔ.

MHB 141
1 . WƆAWO adehyeba ama hɛn, 
Wɔdze anohoba Dzifo am;
Nyia wonnhu N' boka asaase do,
Nyimpa Ba n', Ɔsor Nyame no.

MHB 141
2 . Wɔawo Agyenkwa, dɔ kɛse mu,
Ɔaba rebɛma famufo do;
Ɔaba dɛ ɔdze N'adom kɛse n'
Robɔpɔn No nkorɔfo nyina.

MHB 141
3 . Christ no a wɔhyɛɛ No ho nkɔm no,
Sunsum No tum no hyɛɛ No ma
Ma ɔyɛɛ Nkɔnhyɛnyi, Sɔfo, Hen,
Nye ɔsor wiadze nyina Wura.

MHB 141
4 . Dɔm Ewuradze, sorsor Nyame,
Igyaa W'ahengua baa wiadze;
Yɛdze dɛw ma Wo akɔaba
Gyedzi mu to hɛn akoma mu.

MHB 142
1 . MA asaase na sor mbɔ m'
'Bɔfo na nyimpa mpen,
Wɔntow ayɛyi ndwom
Mma Nyame a ɔbɛbrae; 
Hɛn Nyame adan Noho nyimpa,
Yennkotum atse iyi ase.

MHB 142
2 . Ogyaa N'enyimnyam hɔ,
Ɔhyɛɛ hɛn honam bi, 
Ɔda hɔ no, nyimpa
Ennhu N' dɛ Nyame Ba a;
Ɔbɛyɛɛ akɔkowa wɔ ha,
Na wɔtoo No dzin Immanuel.

MHB 142
4 . Ɔdɔ a wonntum nnhwehwɛ m' 
Na ɔdze Agyenkwa aba;
Adom no bor nyimpa
Nye abɔfo adwen do;
O Nyame, ma yenhu no dɛ
Hɛn Nyame Noara ɔabɛbra.

MHB 142
5 . Ɔpeen dɛ ɔba honam m',
Dze sor na ase abɔ m';
'Bɛda hɛn bɔn edzi,
Ma yaayɛ Nyame dze;
Na yaabɔ Nyankopɔm do bra,
'Siandɛ Nyame ada edzi wɔ ha.

MHB 142
6 . Yeenya edzi mu dɔ mu,
N'adom atsew hɛn ho n',
Yebefi ase ha
Na yeehu N'enyim hyerɛn n';
Ber n' na ɔbɛkyerɛ No dɔ kɛse n',
Na nyimpa na Nyame bɔbɔ m'.

MHB 143
1 . CHRISTIANFO pa, hom mfa
Akoma, kra, ndze ndzi dwɛ! 
Hom ntsie dza yɛreka yi;
Nsɛm! Nsɛm!
Wɔawo Jesus Christ ndɛ da 'i,
Nantwi na asoaso kotow N'
Na ɔda mbowa edzidzidaka m';
Wɔawo Christ ndɛ da 'i.

MHB 143
2 . Christianfo pa, hom mfa
Akoma, kra, ndze ndzi dɛw!
Nkyii hom ntsie dɛw a ɔmmbɔ adze;
Dɛw! Dɛw!
Dɛm ntsi na wɔwoo Jesus,
Oebue sor abobow no,
Na woehyira nyimpa afebɔɔ
Wɔwoo N' wɔ yi ntsi.

MHB 143
3 . Christianfo pa, hom mfa
Akoma, kra, ndze ndzi dɛw!
Onnhia dɛ hom suro wumaa:
'Somdwee!
Wɔwoo Christ dɛ ɔmbɛgye nkwa;
Ɔfrɛ wo, ɔfrɛ hom nyina,
Hom mbɛtsena Ne nkyɛn afebɔɔ;
Christ baa bɛgyee nkwa.

MHB 144
1 . MO ndwom nye dɔ a wonnyim a 
M'Agyenkwa dze dɔ me;
Ɔdɔ hɔn a wɔnndɔ N',
Ama hɔn so eenya dɔ.
Woana nye me
Na emi ntsi
Mo wura bɛyɛɛ
Nyimpa na owui?

MHB 144
2 . Ofi N siar 'hengua
Do dze No nkwagye bae;
Na adasa ennhu
Christ a yɛahwɛ No kwan n';
O me nyɛnko pa!
Me nyɛnko pa,
Ohiaa me no,
Ɔfɛɛm m' No nkwa.

MHB 144
3 . Sɛ odu mber bi a,
Wɔdze berɛw sɛw No kwan m';
Wɔtow ayɛyi ndwom,
Hosanna ma hɔn Hen.
Afei wɔdɛ;
Bɔ No mbeamudua m'!
Wɔtseatseaa mu
Dɛ wonku No.

MHB 144
4 . Ebɛn na mo Wura ayɛ? 
'Bɛn ntsi na wɔtan No?
Ɔmaa mbubua nantsewee,
Enyifurafo hun adze,
Wopiraa No!
Wentwiwentwi
Sii hɔnara ntamu
Wɔsoɛree tsiaa N'.

MHB 144
5 . Wɔsoɛr, na wɔka dɛ 
Wɔmfa mo Wura nkɔ;
Wɔgye owudzinyi nkwa
Na woku nkwa Hen no!
Ɔdze enyigye
Hun amandze,
Ma N'atamfo
Eenya ahotɔ.

MHB 144
6 . Mo Wura ennya ofie
Wɔ asaase do anntsena m';
Owu m' oennya wumaa,
Gyedɛ dza ɔhɔho mae.
'Bɛn na menka?
Sor nye Ne fie;
Naaso medze
Nye bea a ɔdae no.

MHB 144
7 . Ma mentsena ha ntow ndwom,
Asɛm biara nnhia dɛm;
Ɔhen, dɔ na yaw bi
Nnyi hɔ a ɔtse dɛ Wodze n'.
Me Nyɛnko nye N',
Medze enyigye
Beyi N' ayɛw
Mo nkwa nda nyina.

MHB 145
1 . OWURA, ahoɔfɛw bɛn na annhyerɛn
Wɔ W'anan ho wɔ ha?
Ɔdɔ na yaw bɛn na Wo nkwa
Na wu mu annda edzi?

MHB 145
2 . Awerɛhow adzesoa durdur, 
Daa W'akoma do daa,
Naaso ehwinhwin biara emmfi
W'anomu emmpue ara da.

MHB 145
3 . W'atamfo bɛtan W', ayaw Wo,
W'anyɛnkofo apow Wo:
Ennkɛberɛ dɛ edze bɛkyɛ hɔn,
Na akɔ do adɔ hɔn.

MHB 145
4 . Ma hɛn akoma yɛndɔ dɛ Ɔwo, 
Na Ewuradze, yendzi yaw 
Kɛse mma binom bɔn ma ɔnsen
Dza wɔyɛ dze tsia hɛn n'.

MHB 145
5 . Hɛn a yɛyɛ Wo nuanom yi, 
Ma yɛnhwɛ adze dɛ Ɔwo,
Yenhu ahobrɛadze na adom a 
Ofi hɛn nye W' koryɛ m'.

MHB 146
1 . JESUS a ɔtse sor noho 
Bae bɛyɛɛ nyimpa na owui;
Nwoma Krɔnkrɔn no mu yehu 
Mbrɛ osii na ɔyɛɛ papa.

MHB 146
2 . Okyiin mbeambea, ɔyɛɛ ayamuyie, 
Ɔmaa enyifurafo hun adze
Ayarfo na ebubuafo,
Ohun hɔn mbɔbɔr saa hɔn yar.

MHB 146
3 . Ɔkaa nsɛmpa no so kyerɛɛ hɔn,
Dza Nyankopɔn pɛ dɛ wɔyɛ;
Ɔkyerɛɛ ɔdwe maa obiara,
Ma nkyɛ obetsie mbofra mpo.

MHB 146
4 . Naaso ohun owu yaayaw bi!
Wɔsɛɛn No wɔ mbeamudua do;
N-sa pa a ɔdze yɛɛ papa n',
Wɔdze mprɛgow bɔɔ m' wɔ dua do.

MHB 146
5 . Nwoma Krɔnkrɔn ka dɛ ofi sor
Bɛyɛɛ nyimpa ama oeewu;
Ma wɔdze hɛn bɔn aakyɛ hɛn;
Iyi ntsi na ɔbaa wiadze.

MHB 147
1 . ƆDƆ Wura wɔ ha no,
'Nyigye akoma soom No bo, 
Odzii yaw daa dze;
Hɛn ntsi ɔyɛɛ ankonam,
Naaso ɔdze too nkyɛn maa
Aberɛfo enyigye.

MHB 147
2 . N'akwan yɛɛ ahobrɛadze;
'No dɔ gyee hɛn ayɛyi,
N'adɔe,, hɛn mpaabɔ;
Tokyemfo nyina betsiee No;
Awerɛhofo twee bɛɛn No 
Benyaa awerɛkyekyer.

MHB 147
3 . Ber a ɔnam haban mu no, 
Ɔhwɛɛ nhyiren, nnoma na buw, 
Buu Nyame ho mbɛ;
Na No dɔ akoma m' kasa
Kaa nyimpa mba hɔn akra;
Hɔ na Nyame wɔ.

MHB 147
4 . Owura, fa Wo pɛ ma hɛn,
Ma yɛmfa Egya N' nkwa nkenyan 
Abɔnfo nyina;
Gye hɛn fi wiadze haw a 
Ɔhyɛ hɛn akoma do kɔ 
Berɛ na aperdzi m'.

MHB 147
5 . Ewuradze ma yensie
Wo tum wɔ awerɛhow mu,
Wo dɔ wɔ haw mu;
Yennya nyansa, botooyɛ m',
Na yemfi awerɛhow mu 
Nsoɛr nkɔ Nyame hɔ.

MHB 148
1 . YEENNHU Wo  aber a ebaa
Bɔn na wu wiadze yi mu no,
Yeennhu Wo wɔ Wo fie no mu
Wɔ Nazareth ekùraase ho;
Naaso, Nyame Ba, yɛgye dzi
Dɛ enantseew n’abɔntsen do.

MHB 148
2 . Yeennhu Wo ber a nyimpa bɔn
Maa Wo do sɛɛn hɔ wɔ sor no;
Yɛanntse ahobrɛadze ndze nò a
Edze sèrεe: Egya fa kyε hɔn.
Naaso yεgye dzà ɔmaà asaase
Wosowee na sum dwirii no dzi.

MHB 148
3 . Yeenngyina ndà a atɔ pan no ho,
Beà a Wo fun krɔnkrɔn no dae no,
Yɛanntsénà abansor no mu hɔ bi,
Yeennhu Wo petee mu hɔ so;
Mbom yεgyé abɔfo n’ nsεm n’ dzi dε:
Hom hwehwε ’nyikamfò ewufo m’?

MHB 148
4 . Yεannhyε nyimpa kakra no nsew,
Hɔn a wohun dε efoow sor n’;
Wɔdze ahobow hwεε sor hann,
Na wobutuuw famù wɔsɔɔr Wo;
Naaso yεgye dzi dε nyimpa
Enyi hun mbrε isii kr sor.

MHB 148
5 . Na afei idzi hen wɔ sor,
Na ’fi ho hyira Wo nkòrɔfo,
Na kan biara mmfi hɔ nnsian mmba
Mmbεhyerεn wɔ hεn sar yi do;
Naaso yεgye W’anosεm dzi,
Yεtwer hεn Pomfo Ewùradze.

MHB 149
1 . ANA edɔɔ nyimpa a wɔanndɔ Wo no?
Ana 'dze nyimpa enyim fowee kɔr sor? 
Edze nyimpa ndze serɛɛ wɔ po no ho?
Eyɛ n' busuanyi ndɛ.

MHB 149
2 . O Nyame, hɛn Nua a yɛanndɔ Wo yie!
O Nyimpa, W'enyim baa nyam owu ekyir!
Ɔwo a enantseew nkɔntɔnkye kwan do,
Iguu ahom dɛ nyimpa!

MHB 149
3 . Hwɛ ɔsɛ a yɛnye Wo sɛ no ho,
Hwɛ su kor a ɔma yɛnye W' bɔ ebusua,
Hwɛ sor a bɔn nnyi hɔ a Ɔwo hyerɛn hɔ ho
Na twe hɛn abɔnfo kɔ m'.

MHB 149
4 . Hwɛ Wo kommyɛ wɔ asɛndzii hɔ no,
Hwɛ dua do wu a inyim dada no ho,
Hwɛ sum, bɔwen na bɔwema no ho,
Meserɛ Wo, bɔhwɛ me.

MHB 149
5 . Bra, na annyɛ a akoma nwinwin no
Bowu ansaana no Hɔhoe n' aba m';
Annyɛ a enyi a oennhu Wo wiadze no
Runnhu Wo sor ahendzi.

MHB 15
1 . NHYIRA nka tsease Nyame!
N-hyira nka Ne dzin,
Ɔwɔ hɔ na ɔda ho wɔ hɔ,
Ɔtse dɛm daa!
Daapem Nyame kor no
Afei oeyi Noho:
Ɔwo nye Ahyɛse na Ewiei,
Onnyiewiei nye W'.

MHB 15
2 . Onnyi bɔbea naaso
Abɔdze nyim N'adɔe;
Krɔnkrɔnnyɛ mu a, wiadze nnkotum
Akyerɛ Nedze n'.
Ɔyɛ adze nyina Wura!
Abɔdze yi N'ayɛw,
Beebiara ɔsor nye ase
Ye N'apɛdze.

MHB 15
3 . No Sunsum no pem kwa
Kɔ beebiara a ɔpɛ:
Oduaa nkɔnhyɛfo do kasae,
'Da ho kasa.
Ne mbra nsem no etsim,
Na ɔrennsesa da,
Wɔakyerɛw no nyimpa akoma do,
Po, asaase do.

MHB 15
4 . Ɔdze onnyiewiei nkwa ahyɛ
Ɔkra biara mu ma;
No dɔ bɛyɛ hɛn ahoɔdzen,
Daa nyinara.
N-tonton nka Nyame!
N-tonton nka Ne dzin,
Ɔwɔ hɔ na oda ho wɔ hɔ,
Ɔtse dem daa.     Amen.

MHB 150
1 . Igyaa W' ahengua 
Na W' ahenkyɛw so,
Ber a 'baa wiadze wɔ me ntsi n';
Na woennya kwan wɔ
Bethlehem fie hɔ,
Amma Wo wiadze ha ne mbae:
Ao, bra m' akomam', Ewuradze,
Ɔkwan wɔ m' akomam' ma Wo.

MHB 150
2 . Sor nyina gyigyee 
Ber a abɔfo toow ndwom
Bɔɔ W' adehye dzin no dawur n';
Na mbrɛadzem' ara
Na, Ɔsor Wura,
Ebaa asaase do ha:
Ao, bra m' akomam', Ewuradze,
Ɔkwan wɔ m' akomam' ma Wo.

MHB 150
3 . N-sɔ wɔ etu, 
Na nnoma berɛbuw,
Wɔ nkyindur no nwin ase;
Na Wo mpa nye dɛtse,
O Nyankopɔn Ba,
Dɛtse, wɔ Galilee sar do;
Ao, bra m' akomam', Ewuradze,
Ɔkwan wɔ m' akomam' ma Wo.

MHB 150
4 . Ao, Ewuradze, 
'Dze nkasɛm no bae,
Dza nkyɛ ɔbɛma fahodzi;
Na wɔdze atwetwesi
Na nsoɛ katraka
Wosunsum Wo kɔr Calvary:
Ao, bra m' akomam', Ewuradze,
Ɔkwan wɔ m' akomam' ma Wo.

MHB 150
5 . Sor bɔwosow bio 
Na abɔfo atow ndwom,
Ber a 'bɛba konyimdzi mu n';
Ma Wo ndze mfrɛ me fie
Dɛ, Kwan da ho wɔ hɔ,
Kwan da ho wɔ me nkyɛn ma Wo!
Na, mo Wura, m' akoma bedzi dɛw
Ber a 'bɛba na ebɛfrɛ me n'.

MHB 151
1 . Woana na n-guanhwɛfo 
Kotow No mbowadan mu hɔ n'?

         Ewuradze a! O anwanwasɛm! 
         Ewuradze a, Enyimnyam Hen n' a. 
         Yetwa hwe N' ananadze; 
         O wɔnhyɛ No abɔso Hen.

MHB 151
2 . Woana na oridzi edwin 
Wɔ dan kakraba mu hɔ n'?

MHB 151
3 . Woana na ɔrekyen kɔm, 
Ɔreper wɔ sar do hɔ n'?

MHB 151
4 .	Woana na orusu wɔ 
Lazarus ne nda do hɔ n'?

MHB 151
5 . Woana na ɔrobɔ mpaa 
Esuom wɔ Gethsamane n'?

MHB 151
6 . Woana na ɔserɛ nhyira 
Ma abɔn wɔ Calvary do n'?

MHB 151
7 . Woana na oefi ewufom' 
Roboa hɛn, regye hɛn nkwa n'?

MHB 151
8 . Woana na No nko dzi Hen 
Sor na asaase nyina do n'?

MHB 152
1 . Na nyimpa a wɔayɛ petsee yi, 
Wɔnam ɔhyew do yi, ase ɛ?
Ebɛn nye adzekyee ehyia yi?
Wentwiwenti 'i ase nye dɛn?
Okuw n' sii ndze adze buaa dɛ,
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.

MHB 152
2 . Jesus nye woana? Ɔyɛ dɛn 
Na ɔbɔ kurow ebutuw dɛm?
Ɔkwantsennyi a ɔresen,
Ɔdze bɛn twe nyimpa pii yi?
Awɔse ndze no buaa bio dɛ,
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.

MHB 152
3 . Jesus! 'No na ɔbaa wiadze 
Boduaa mbusu kwan yi mu bi n';
Wɔdze ayarfo nyina brɛɛ No,
Etsitsifo ɔnye mpakye:
'Nyifurafo dze dɛw tsiee ntseamu n':
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.

MHB 152
4 . Ɔreba bio, fi ha kɔ ha, 
Yɛtse N' anamɔn wɔ mbeambea,
Oegyina hɛn abobowano,
Ɔahɛn dɛ ɔrobɔsoɛ hɔ;
Ana hɛn so yɛnnkɛpaam' dɛ,
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.

MHB 152
5 . Ao o! akobɔfo, hom mbra; 
Fakyɛ nye ahomgye wɔ ha;
Hom a hom efi Egya fie,
Hom nsan mbra bio mbɛgye N' adom;
Amandzehufo dɔbea nye 'i-
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.

MHB 153
1 . JESUS, Wo nka a atahye no, 
Me kra enyi gye dɛ ɔtse;
Wo dzin a ɔma ahoɔdzen no,
Ɔyɛ dɛw wɔ abɔn asomu.

MHB 153
2 . Awerɛkyekyer nsɛm na ayamuyie 
Dze gyee tsetseber do abɔnfo; 
Hɔn werɛ kyekyee, nyaa dza wohia;
Sa ayarfo yar, bue efurafo enyi.

MHB 153
3 . Ana ennda ho nnyɛ Agyenkwa
Wɔ beebiara na mber nyina? 
Wo werɛ efir W'adom akyɛdze n',
Anaa ayew Wo dzin pa no?

MHB 153
4 . Megye Wo dzin a ɔnnsesa n' dzi,
Eyɛ yarsafo a Wo yamu ye;
Itum dɛ egye hɛn akra nkwa,
Epɛ dɛ eyɛ hɔn fofor.

MHB 153
5 . Ana egye nyimpadua nkwa
Na ennhwɛ ɔkra a ɔyar?
Ɔkra yarfo a edɔ n' kɛse n'
Na ebɛma oeenya ahoɔdzen.

MHB 153
6 . Jesus, medze me yarba
Na mo bɔn nyinara brɛ Wo,
Hyɛ ase sa m' yar wɔ fakyɛ mu,
Na mindzi mu krɔnkrɔnyɛ mu.

MHB 154
1 . Metsee dɛ Jesus ne ndze se: 
Bra Mo hɔ na bɔhom;
Ɔwo a aberɛ fa wo tsir,
Bɔto Mara Mo bom'!
Mokɔree dɛ mbrɛ metse ara,
Maberɛ, Mo werɛ ahow;
Minyaa ahomgye wɔ No mu,
Na ɔmaa m' enyigye.

MHB 154
2 . Metsee dɛ Jesus ne ndze se: 
Ɔwo a sukɔm dze wo,
Hwɛ, mema n-kwa nsu no kwa,
Bɔ wo mu adze nom bi!
Mebaa Jesus hɔ mobɔnoom
N-kwa esutsen n' bi;
Mo nsukɔm gyaae, me kra nyaa nkwa,
Na afei metse No mu.

MHB 154
3 . Metsee dɛ Jesus ne ndze se: 
Emi nye wiadze Kan:
Hwɛ Me na adze bɛkye wo,
Wo kwan mu bɛyɛ kann!
Mohwɛɛ Jesus na minyaa N' ma
Ɔyɛɛ ewia maa me!
N-kwa Kan yim' na m' bɛnantsew
M' akwantu nda nyina.

MHB 155
1 . IMMANUEL, sa hɛn yar, tsie hɛn,
Fa Wo nsa no ka hɛn;
Akra epirafo yɛba Wo hɔ,
Agyenkwa, yɛtse dɛm.

MHB 155
2 . Yɛpaa m' ka dɛ hɛn gyedzi suar,
Yɛnngye W' asɛm nndzi yie;
Na ebɔhwɛ yi ho anaa?
Ɔmpar Wo, Ewuradze.

MHB 155
3 . Kaa nyia da bi ɔdze nyinsu,
Na ahopopo serɛe,
Ɔtseaa m', Ewuradze, megye dzi;
O boa m' ma mengye ndzi.

MHB 155
4 . Ɔbaa no dze ne nsa kaa Wo,
Na ɔtwee ayarsa tum n';
Esee n' dɛ; Fa asomdwee kɔ, 
Wo gyedzi agye w' nkwa.

MHB 155
5 . Yɛdze enyidar na suro ba,
Bɛka Wo do dɛ ɔno;
Yeserɛ W', mma yɛmmfa hɛn yaw
Na hɛn yar nnsan nnkɔ fie. 	Amen.

MHB 156
1 . Ɔwo a wɔpemee betsiee Wo, 
Wotsiee Wo nsɛm, wɔtsee Wo tum;
Ma abɔn kwan ma yɛmbɛn Wo,
Na gye hɛn adom mu ara.

MHB 156
2 . Ɔwoara na aka dɛ, 
Primprimfo nnhia oduyɛfo;
Emi meyar, mihia Wo mboa,
Mihia Wo tum a ɔgye nkwa n'.

MHB 156
3 . Wo tum, nokwar na nyamedɔ, 
Tsim hɔ mbersantsen mfesantsen;
W' asɛm, W' adom asɛm kor mpo,
Otu yarba dzendzen biara.

MHB 156
4 . Kaansa makyɛr esu yi bo, 
Ma mo sunsum nntum nnka noho a,
W' ano kasa bɛma masoɛr,
Ɔbɔbɔ  m' esu ntsɛmara.

MHB 156
5 . Ma dɔnhwer yi nyɛ ɔgyeber; 
Ao bra, me kra no Duyɛfo!
Da W' ahosan tum no edzi,
Ma munhu Wo nkwagye n' sesei.     Amen.

MHB 157
1 . Jesus frɛ hɛn! Sɛ hɛn bra po 
Wor mpo a, yɛtse Ne ndze,
Ne ndze dɛɛdɛw n' gyigye daa daa,
Ɔse: Christian, ka Mo do.

MHB 157
2 . Tsetseber do asomafo n' 
Tsee wɔ Galilee po do n',
Wogyaa ebusua, fie nye edwuma,
Kɛkaa' No a wɔdɔ No n' do.

MHB 157
3 . Jesus frɛ hɛn mma yɛnnsom 
Wiadze mu ndzɛmba huhuw;
Ɔhwɛ ndzɛmba a wɔsom hɛn bo a,
Ɔse: Christian, dɔ M' kyɛn hɔn.

MHB 157
4 . Enyigye nye awerɛhow mu, 
Dwumadzim' nye ahomgyem',
Ɔda ho frɛ hɛn dɛ yɛndɔ N'
Ma ɔkyɛn adze nyina.

MHB 157
5 . Jesus frɛ hɛn! O Agyenkwa, 
Yɛserɛ W', ma yɛntse Wo frɛ n',
Hɛn 'koma nyɛ setsie mma Wo,
Yɛndɔ W' nkyɛn adze nyina.

MHB 158
1 . ESE, onyimpa ba,
Fa w' mbeamudua dzi M'ekyir, 
'Nafua yɛ sum, anan mu agow, 
'So yebedzi W'ekyir.

MHB 158
2 . Ewuradze pa, yɛserɛ
Dɛ ma yenhu W'enyim,
Yehu W'enyim ber tsiabaa mpo a;
Na yebedzi W'ekyir.

MHB 158
3 . Mber a no mu yɛ sum 
Etwa mber pa no ntamu;
M-fe rugu m' n', Wo ndze sesa; 
Yɛnyɛ dɛn ndzi W'ekyir?

MHB 158
4 . Yɛtse Wo ndze wɔ ekyir, 
Fi Galilee bɔnsa m'; 
Tsetse nwin ka W'edwuma hyɛ; 
Yenyɛ dɛn ndzi W'ekyir.

MHB 158
5 . Gyedzi mbeamudua durdur 
Wɔ dza yenntum nnhu n' mu; 
Yi Woho kyerɛ dɛ mbrɛ eyɛɛ n', 
Boa ma yendzi W'ekyir.

MHB 158
6 . Sɛ ammba dɛ nyimpa, 
Dɛ ebaa ber bi no a, 
Bra bɛtsena akoma a ɔper 
Dɛ obedzi W'ekyir.

MHB 158
7 . Fa hɛn akoma nyina
Na bɛn hɛn mber nyina,
Bra bɛtsena Wo nkrɔfo mu; 
Kɔ, yebedzi W'ekyir.

MHB 159
1 . OBI a ɔmmfata koraa 
Dɛ ɔyɛ Wo suanyi n',
Edze Wo dɔ afa n'nyɛnko; 
Ao, ayamuyie nwanwa!

MHB 159
2 . Adom Wura, meyɛ mberɛw,
Na memmfata koraa;
Wo nan adze huntuma no
Mpo ye sen me koraa.

MHB 159
3 . Ɔwo etse kan kɛse mu,
Bɔn na 'nyimguase nnyi m';
Dɛ bɔsoa hɛn bɔn, 'nyimguase;
M'bɛyɛ dɛm dɔ n'?

MHB 159
4 . Ana oemmbu No sor ahengua
Dɛ adze tootooba,
Dɛ obegya hɔ wɔ 'dasanyi a 
Mennsɛ hwee koraa yi ntsi?

MHB 159
5 . Wɔdze mprɛgow bobɔɔ N' honam m', 
Ana oennhu amandze?
Dzin bɛn na ɔsɛ abotar
Na ɔbra krɔnkrɔn yi?

MHB 159
6 . Ɔdɔ ankasa bɛyɛɛ nyimpa, 
Mo ho dɔ ntsi na ɔbae;
Munntum mma m'enyi do monnhwɛ
N'enyim, 'nyimguase ntsi.

MHB 159
7 . Sɛ adze pa bi wɔ mo mu a,
Ofi Woara Wo nkyɛn,
Ntsi Ewuradze, fa me sie
Ma menyɛ Wodze koraa.

MHB 16
1 . MA ndwom do: na asaase ntonton,
Wɔ ebusua na kasa m',
M-fa N'ayɛyi nsan mma No,
Ma ndwom a ɔfata no do.
Amanaman, hom nhyira Ne dzin;
Hom mma No nokwar nda edzi:
Na adzekyee biara hom nka
No nkwagye no ho asem.

MHB 16
2 . Hom nka no wɔ wi yi ase,
Wɔ ebusua na kasa m',
Hom nka mfi anapa ma nwin ndwe
Wɔ ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze da m':
Hom nka dɛ hɛn Nyame dzi hen,
Ɔno na obɔɔ wiadze ntsem,
Ɔda ho ara hwɛ wiadze do
Kesi da a ɔsɛɛ bɛba.

MHB 16
3 . Ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ da no reba a 
Wobobu wiadze atsɛn:
Ɔsor enyimnyam bɛhyerɛn,
'Saase, po bɛyɛ ahomka.
N-yew, epo a ɔrowor no
Bɛba ne ndze mpempem do,
Na epo asorɛkye nyina
Beyi Nyankopɔn ayɛw.

MHB 16
4 . Asaase do mfuw na nhyiren,
Bofura hɔn atam pa,
Na kwaamu ndua nyinara na
N-haban bɛyɛ kusuww:
Sɛ wiadze Otsɛmbuafo no
Bobu atsentsenenee no a,
N-sisi na bɔn bɔbɔ adze,
Afei nokwar bedzi hen.  Amen.

MHB 160
1 . ƆWO nye Kwan n'; yeguan fi bɔn 
Na wu ho ba Wo nkyɛn; 
Na nyia ɔhwehwɛ Egya no, 
Ɔsɛ dɛ ɔfa Wo do.

MHB 160
2 . Ɔwo nye Nokwar: W'asɛm nko 
Na ɔkyerɛ nyansa mapa;
Ɔwo nko na ekyerɛ adwen
Na etsew akoma m'.

MHB 160
3 . Ɔwo nye Nkwa: nda a woebue do n'
Ka Wo konyim tum no;
Hɔn a wɔdze hɔn werɛ hyɛ Wo mu n', 
'Wu na hɛll nnkɛhaw hɔn.

MHB 160
4 . Ɔwo nye Kwan, Nokwar na Nkwa n';
Boa hɛn ma yenhu Kwan n', 
Yensie Nokwar no, na yeenya
Nkwa a ne dɛw pem daa no.     Amen.

MHB 161
1 . Ka 'sɛm dadaw no kyerɛ me, 
Sunsum ndzɛmbam' asɛm,
Dza ɔfa Christ N' enyimnyam ho
Dza ɔfa No dɔ so ho.
Ka 'sɛm no pefee kyerɛ m' dɛ
Ereka kyerɛ abofra;
Na meyɛ mberɛw na mafona,
Minnyi ahom, mo ho fi.
Ka 'sɛm dadaw no kyerɛ me, 
Jesus no dɔ ho asɛm.

MHB 161
2 . Tɔ w' bo ka 'sɛm no kyerɛ me, 
Na meetum medze esie-
Nyame No werdam kɛse a
Ɔdze yɛ bɔn edur.
Si do mber pii ka kyerɛ m'
Na meyar awerɛfir;
Ahanamakye bɔsu
Ewia fir a ɔpa.

MHB 161
3 . Ka 'sɛm no bɔkɔɔ kyerɛ me, 
Nwinwin mu dɛ ehiasɛm,
Kaa dɛ meyɛ bɔnyɛnyi a
Jesus bɛpeer mo nkwa,
Ka 'sɛm no mber nyinara,
Sɛ epɛ ampaara
Dɛ ema m' akomatɔm'
Wɔ ahokyer ber biaram'.

MHB 161
4 . Ka ' sɛm kor n' ara kyerɛ me, 
Aber a isuro dɛ
Wiadze enyimnyam huhuw n'
Ridzi m' adwen dodow.
Nyew, na ɔsor n' enyimnyam
No so regye mo do a,
Ka 'sɛm dadaw no kyerɛ m' dɛ,
Christ Jesus bɔ w' esu!
Ka 'sɛm dadaw no kyerɛ me, 
Jesus no dɔ ho asɛm.

MHB 162
1 . ƆWO nye mo nkwa; sɛ ekɔ gya me a,
M'abrabɔ 'wu ara nko; Ɔwo nye m' kwan;
Mennya Wo a, m'bɔfom kwan m'akwantu mu.

MHB 162
2 . Ɔwo nye m' kan; mennya W'enyimnyam kan a,
'Sum kebii bɛma n;enyi ayɛ kusuww;
Me Nyame nye mo kwan, n-kwa, na kan.

MHB 162
3 . Ɔwo nye m' kwan; ekɔ gya me a, meyew;
Ɔwo nye m' kan; isuma a, munnhu adze!
Ɔwo nye m' nkwa: etwe Woho a, muwu.

MHB 162
4 . Yi Wo nserɛmɛn kyerɛ m'; enye me ntsena;
Hwɛ, munnhu adze, mewu, m'afom kwan;
Ɔwo nye me kan, mo nkwa na mo kwan!

MHB 163
1 . MO Wura, Ɔwo a Wo bra m' muhu
Dza ɔwɔ dɛ meyɛ 'so munntum;
Ma Wo kan krɔnn no nhyerɛn daa,
Nhyɛ me bra fɛr, nkyerɛ me kwan.

MHB 163
2 . Me mberɛwyɛ ntsi mo nsusui
Na me ndzeyɛɛ nntum mmbɔ mu nnsaa;
Ɔwo a W'adwen na W' nyɛe yɛ kor,
Boa me ma menyɛ dza munntum.

MHB 164
1 . HWƐ! Abɔdomaba
Da mbowa edzidzidaka m';
Na ɔpɛ mframa nwinwin,
Ɔbɔ fa ne tsir ho.
Na woana nye Nyia ɔda hɔ n'?
Ɔno nye Nyia ɔbɔɔ wiadze 'i.

MHB 164
2 . O tsebea bɛn nye no,
Na yehu Nyame ba 'i? 
'Bɛn ntsi na Nyame so
Bɔsoɛ fie tantan yi m'?
Ama yeeguan efi ahantan ho,
Na yeedzi N'ahobrɛadze ekyir.

MHB 164
3 . Mbrɛ Joseph yɛ n'edwuma n',
Hwɛ! Jesus so wɔ hɔ;
Nsa a ɔyɛɛ adze nyina
Dzi wiadze edwin daa, 
Ma abrɛfo aahom wɔ no mu, 
Na anokwafo benya nhyira.

MHB 164
4 . Hwɛ Abofra n' dɛ ɔdze adom
Tse abemfo n' finimfin!
'Bɛn ntsi na ɔtse hɔn mu,
Ber a ɔkrɔn sen hɔn?
Ama Christian mbofra dze obu
Esua wɔ Jesus n'ananadze.

MHB 164
5 . Christ, ayɛ abofra pɛn;
Hɛn mbofraber m' Gyafo
Na hɛn kan nye hɛn dɛw;
Na kɔ do nye hɛn ntsena.
Ama Wo dɔ kɛse a wɔnntɔ n'
Aatwe hɛn abɛn Wo daa daa.

MHB 165
1 . Idzii mbuada adaduanan 
Adzekyee nye adzesaa,
Adaduanan wɔ sar no do
Wɔsɔɔ Wo hwɛe na annyɛ bɔn.

MHB 165
2 . Ewia sii Wo do adzekyee, 
Bɔw tɔɔ Wo do anago,
Mbowa abɔyafo paar wo ho,
Edaa fam', isum ɔbo.

MHB 165
3 . Ma yɛnsɔw Wo bene no bi, 
Yɛmpow wiadze edzifodze;
Na yɛnye Wo nweɔn mpaabɔm',
Nye Wo nsɔw yaw ahoɔdzenm'.

MHB 165
4 . Sɛ abɔnsam dze ebufuw 
Toa honam anaa sunsum,
'Wo a edzi no do nyim pɛn,
Dom hɛn mma yaannhwe ase.

MHB 165
5 . Nna yebenya W' asomdwee; 
Dɛw krɔnkrɔn bɛyɛ hɛndze;
Dɛ mbrɛ abɔfo soom Wo n',
Wɔbɛhyerɛn hɛn so hɛn ho.

MHB 166
1 . OSII wɔ ɔhyew-ber bi mu,
Ber a Jesus nenaam Galilee;
Abaatan fi nkuraase nkuraase
Dze hɔn mbofra brɛɛ No.

MHB 166
2 . Ɔgyee hɔn too N'abaw mu sɔnn,
Dze Ne nsa totoo hɔn tsir do;
Ɔkaa berɛww dɛ, Hom mma mbofra n'
Kwan ma wɔmbra me nkyɛn.

MHB 166
3 . Mma hom nnsiw hɔn kwan; gyedɛ hom
Nya mbofra akoma wɔ hom mu
Ana hom aba M'ahenman m',
Ɔno hom runntum nnhɛn m'.

MHB 166
4 . Mo Wura, mepɛ dɛ mokɔ hɔ; 
O mindzi W'ekyir nye Wo nkyɛ 
W'ahobrɛadze, botoo akoma n',
Mompow wiadze ndzɛmba.

MHB 166
5 . Wo dɔ, gyedzi, adwenmutsewee,
'Dwuma pa, kasafua a ho tsew,
Enyigye a pɛsɛankonya nnyi m',
Ewuradze pa, yɛ m' dɛm.

MHB 166
6 . Enyigye adwen na akwan pa nyina m',
Ma me ɔdɔ ayamuyie daa;
Menam setsie m' nya fahodzi,
M'akoma nyɛ W'ahenman.

MHB 166
7 . O memfa enyigye ntsena ase,
Nkyir wiadze dɛw, na mubohu
Nyame N'ahoɔfɛw wɔ beebi a 
No dɔ ye wɔ nyimpa m'.

MHB 166
8 . Egya, ma m' dɛm mbofra akoma 'I, 
Ama meetum aba Christ hɔ; 
Ma maatse Ne nsa nka wɔ m' do,
Wɔ nhyira, dɔ na ayarsa m',    Amen.

MHB 167
1 . EHUM dzendzen tuu po no do,
W'esuafo dze suro weɔnee,
Naaso Ɔwodze, ada koraa;
Komm na dzinn.

MHB 167
2 . Wɔtseaa m; Jesus, gye hɛn, yɛrehera!
O gye hɛn haw yi mu!
W'asɛm no boor ehum no do;
Ɔtaa dzinn.

MHB 167
3 . M-frama dzendzen no gyaae bɔ,
Po taa dzinn dɛ abofra a ɔada;
Asorɛkye dzendzen no gyaa bu,
Wɔ Wo pɛ m'.

MHB 167
4 . Ntsi sɛ ɔbra ehum rutu hɛn
Na asorɛkye twe hɛn fi mpoano a, 
Mbrɛ yɛnnkɛmem n', ɔyɛ a ka dɛ 
Komm na dzinn.

MHB 168
1 . EWURADZE, oye dɛ yɛnye W'
Tsena sor ha bepɔw yi do,
Wɔ mframa pa dɛɛdɛw yi mu,
Ɔtra akoma a wɔtseetsee hɔn;
Ekyingye, berɛ na hɔn yaw yi m', 
Wɔtwer hɔn ara hɔn ekyingye;
Kwa ara na efrɛ Wo nkowaa
Dɛ womfi hɔn yaw wenwen n' mu.

MHB 168
2 . Ewuradze, oye dɛ yɛnye W'
Na W' nokwafo baasa n' tsena
Ha na asomfo nya ahoɔdzen,
Dze ko tsia nsɔhwɛ no mbusu;
Ha na Nyankopɔn Ba no sua
Nyansa a mu dɔ na asɛm a ɔdzɛw;
Ha na yɛnye Nyia N'asɛm yɛ 
Dɔ n' yetu wɔ nkɔr ntsaban do.

MHB 168
3 . Ewuradze, oye dɛ yɛnye W'
Bɔ mu kyekyer yɛ kor ara;
Kɔ do hwɛ Wo ntar hyɛnhyɛn a
Ɔhoa sen Hermon do fufuw n';
Nyimpadua no n 'akwaa n' so dze,
Sunsum kan kyerɛn kesi dɛ 
Hɛn so yebenyin wɔ adom mu,
Ehu enyim a asakyer no.

MHB 168
4 . Ewuradze, oye dɛ yɛnye W'
Tsena bepɔw krɔnkrɔn yi do;
Yɛhyɛ sum kebii bi mu o,
Yɛhyɛ kan hyɛnhyɛn bi mu o,
Yɛkotow ɔsor ndze krɔnn a
Ɔma akra a wɔabɔm dzi dɛw,
Kaansa ɔdɔ tu na gyedzi sa a:
Me Ba nye yi; Hom nyina ntsie No.

MHB 169
1 . M’AGYENKWA, Wo dͻ a ewͻ ma m’,
Akyerɛ wͻ   enyimguase m’,hia m’,
Yaw m’,
Ama m’ wͻ mbeamudua no do;
Ikyii Wo bͻgyaa a ‘fͻdzi nnyi m’ n’,
Ma W’epirakur nka m’akoma a
Hwee nnkotum asesa no da.

MHB 169
2 . M’ Akoma yɛ dzen sen ͻbo,
Bͻn nkekaa dzendzen asɛɛ mu;
Na Ͻwo yɛ Agyenkwa tumfo,
Na Wo bͻgyaa krͻnn no mmpem kwa;
Ao! Gown a nan dɛm ͻbo yi na
Wo bͻgyaa nhohor dɛm ͻbo yin a
Wo bͻgyaa nhohor dɛmnkekaa n’.

MHB 169
3 . O emi a metse dɛ abofra
Bɛka Wo do a monnkͻhom da;
Kɛpem dɛ dɛw mu ebͻhom
W’ adwen pa no egu mo bo m’;
Anaa dɛ yɛnnkɛpaapaa m’ da,
Dɛ menye Wo yɛ kor sunsum m’!

MHB 169
4 . Ma Wo dͻ nkͻ do nhyrɛn mo kwan m’
Ndzɛmba nwanwa a Wo dɛ ayɛ n’!
Kͻ do kyerɛ m’ kwan amma maannyew;
Kyerɛ m’ dza menka, Kenyan m’adwen,
Na sɛ mohwe ase a, ma mentse
Wo ndze, munhu dɛ ͻdͻ  abɛn.

MHB 169
5 . Me haw m’ Wo dͻ mma m’ asomdwee,
Me mberɛwyɛ m’ Wo dͻ mma m’ tum;
Ber a ͻbra n’ehum begyaa n’,
Dɛm dͻnhwer soronko no mu,
Wͻ wu m’, dɛ eyɛ nkwa no, gya m’;
Gye me nkwa, Ͻwo a iwui maa m’.  Amen.

MHB 17
1 . ƆSƐ na ɔfata adwontow, 
Ber na bea biara mu,
Enyimnyam nka hɛn sor Hen,
Nokwar na adom Nyame:
Hɛn nyina dze ndze dɛɛdɛw
Bɔ m' wɔ ndaase kor mu dɛ;
Krɔnkrɔn, krɔnkrɔn, Ewuradze,
Ayɛyi nka Wo daa.

MHB 17
2 . Hom adzekyee m-bakan,
Hom mfa hom ndze dɛɛdɛw
Nyi No ayɛw mber nyina,
Na mma ɔmmbɔ adze da;
Abɔfo na akɛse nyina,
Hom nyi Ɔkorsa ayɛw,
Hom ntow ndwom na hom ntwa nhwe
N'ahengua no enyim.

MHB 17
3 . Yenye sor adwontofo a 
Woyi W'ayɛw wɔ sor,
N-kɔr atsabandofo,
Gyedzi na dɔ ntsaban:
Wɔtow Wo ndwom 'nyimnyam mu,
Ma Eguambaa a wokum Wo;
Sɛ hɛn n-dze kɔ famu a
Dza yegyina do yɛ kor.

MHB 17
4 . Egya, yɛkamfo Wo dɔ a
Ɔmaa Wo Ba n' bowui;
Adom na nokwar, Jesus,
Wo na yɛntonton Wo;
Sunsum, Ɔwerɛkyekyefo,
Obiara nyi Wo ayɛw;
Nkpem dɛ yɛbɔtow ndwom,
Na asaase adan ɔsor.   Amen.

MHB 170
1 . ENYITO na awerɛhosɛm nye 'i,
Dɛ mber bi a etwa mu no,
Mopoow m'Agyenkwa Ne frɛ a
Ɔdze mbɔbɔrhu frɛɛ me no;
Mubuaa dɛ, medze moho!

MHB 170
2 . Naaso ohun me, muhun N' dɛ 
'Rikyi bɔgyaa mbeamudua n' do,
Ɔbɔɔ mpaa; Egya, fa kyɛ hɔn!
M'akoma gyee do kakraabi;
Medze moho kakra maa N'.

MHB 170
3 . Daa nyina No mbɔbɔrhu no
Kɔr do maa me ayarsa,
Dze abotar brɛɛ me adze;
Na afei mekaa no berɛww dɛ
Medze me fa kɛse ma W'.

MHB 170
4 . Egya, Wo dɔ a ɔkrɔn sen sor,
No mu dɔ kyɛn po no bun n',
Afei edzi m'akoma do nyim;
Afei tsie mo ntotɔserɛ,
Medze moho nyina ma W'.  Amen.

MHB 171
1 . Jesus, motwer Wo, medze me kra twer Wo, 
Fɔdzifo a mayew, 'Wo na 'botum agye m',
Obi nnyi sor anaa ase a ɔnye W' sɛ;
Ɔwo wui maa abɔn, Ɔwo wui maa me. 

    Motwer Wo dɔ no na mohwehwɛ W' enyim; 
    W' adom nwanwa no ntsi na muhuhor Wo. 
    Jesus, motwer Wo, medze me kra twer Wo, 
    Fɔdzifo a mayew, 'Wo na 'botum agye me.

MHB 171
2 . Jesus, m' bɔtwer Wo, m' bɔtwer Wo Kyerɛwsɛm; 
Osiandɛ matse Wo mbɔbɔrhu ndze no.
Wo Sunsum kyerɛkyerɛ m' a, ɔyɛ m' dɛw dodow,
Ma mentsena W' anan ho ara mintsie.

MHB 171
3 . Jesus, m' bɔtwer Wo, mobɔdwen W' akwan do, 
Ewɔ wiadze n' eyɛɛ dɔ nye mbɔbɔrhu,
Ndzebɔnyɛfo fɔɔr Wo, 'kwatafo hwehwɛɛ W',
Hɔn mu biara ho annyɛ Agyenkwa nkɔw.

MHB 171
4 . Jesus, ' bɔtwer Wo, mennkɛgye Wo kyim da, 
Obiara a ɔba Wo nkyɛn no emmpam no.
W' anohoba si pi, Wo bɔgyaa som bo;
'Wo nye me kra no nkwagye, me nyankopɔn.

MHB 172
1 . NYIA mununkum esuma No 
Na abɔfo hu N' wusuww,
Ana wobohu dza wonnhu?
Na mehu Nyankopɔn?

MHB 172
2 . Obegyaa N'ahengua wɔ sor
Na ɔdze Noho ama m'?
Bua m', Ɔwo dɔ na yaw Nyimpa,
Kasa kyerɛ m'akoma.

MHB 172
3 . Ɔdɔ krɔnn mu ara kyerɛ Wo 
Nhyehyɛɛ nwanwa no mu;
Ebɛn ntsi na ikyii Wo bɔgyaa,
Ɔwo Nyimpa Ba a aberɛ.

MHB 172
4 . Ana ammba hɛn honandua mu
Ammbɛtsena na ennwu ha? 
Ama meehu Wo dɛ abɛn, 
Na meehu mo Pomfo.

MHB 172
5 . Afei bra na beyi adom
No bun, no krɔn kyerɛ m';
Wo pirakur a ɔsɛɛ W'enyim,
Eso otu m'awerɛhow n'.

MHB 172
6 . M'bohu 'Guambaa Noara Ne kan m', 
'No a abɔfo hu N' wusuww n',
Na medze dɛw kɛse ahwɛ N'
Onnyiewiei nda nyina m'.

MHB 173
1 . JESUS pɛ dɛ abɔnfo wu?
'Bɛn ntsi na ɔsɛɛn dua no do?
No wu ntseam' no ase nye dɛn?
Ɔbɔɔ mpaa maa abɔnfo nyina;
Fa kyɛ hɔn, Egya, fa kyɛ hɔn;
Wonnyim, Me ntsi na wɔtse ase.

MHB 173
2 . Ɔdɔfo pa, hɛn Mpataguan,
Enam W'ahoguan yaawaw n' do,
Bɔgya a ikyii na Wo yaw pii n',
Wo mbeamudua do owu yaayaw no,
Wo wu na nkwa a ɔsom bo ntsi,
Meserɛ, fa mo bɔn nyina kɔ.

MHB 173
3 . Ma memfew Wo nan ho bɔgya
Na memfa me nyinsu nhohor;
Wo dɔ asɛm n' si do ka bio,
Ma abɔn nyina aso ntse,
Ma obiara ntse ndze a okenyan,
Ama meenya ehumbɔbɔr.

MHB 173
4 . Ma wo dɔ nhyɛ m'akoma do,
Wo dɔ a wɔdze ma abɔnfo kwa;
Ma akra a wɔahwe ase nyina
Eehu adom a ɔgyee me no,
Na adasa nyina nye me eehu
W'adehye dɔ a onnyi ewiei no.

MHB 174
1 . MIHYIAA Guanhwɛfo pa n',
Sesei ɔwɔ sar do,
Nna ɔso Ne ba a ɔayew
No rokɔ fie bio.
Ɔyɛɛ me nwanwa dɛ
Ɔsoaa no bɔkɔɔ;
Na ɔpaa mo ho no,
Mubuu ntwɛr sɔɔr No.

MHB 174
2 . Ao, Oguanhwɛfo pa!
W'epirakur mu dɔ,
Mpataku n' piraa Wo,
Eregye Wo guan n';
Hwɛ mbrɛ bɔgya ayɛ
W'atar no mu kɔɔ!
Na Wo mfem akam yi
So ase nye dɛn?

MHB 174
3 . Ao, hwɛ mbrɛ nsoɛ n' esi
Abebar Wo nhwi,
Na afei awowɔ Wo,
W'enyimdua fɛɛfɛw n'!
Hwɛ mbrɛ egye ahom a
Ɔnnyɛ yie koraa;
Na hwɛ, owu sunsum
Agyegye W'enyim.

MHB 174
4 . Ao, Oguanhwɛfo pa!
Ɔyɛ emi ntsi na
Yaw kɛse a ɔtse dɛm
Aba Wo do yi.
Dɛm a na ma memper
Wɔ Wo dɔ no ntsi,
Mma minnyi W' awerɛhow
Dabiara da bio!

MHB 175
1 . Mma nnsu mma Nyia ɔso mbeamudua 
Dze rokɔ Calvary no;
Ɔnnserɛ dasanyi ne nyinsu,
Ɔapen dɛ obowu.

MHB 175
2 . Yaw huhu bi a atow N' enyim, 
Oegura ne nyimpadua n',
Mmfir amenhyɛ anaa 'nyimguase:
Onnsuro mbeamudua n'.

MHB 175
3 . Yaw wenwen a ɔbor do yi, 
Ahoguan a ɔnnka,
Dza Wo dɔ nnya mu ahotɔ yi,
Wo nko so ne nyina.

MHB 175
4 . Ohu akra a hɔn ntsi oruwu 
Dɛ wɔtar hɔn bɔn ho,
Hɔn a ɔsor-man dzi wɔ hɔn
Wɔmmpɛ dɛ wɔhɛn mu.

MHB 175
5 . Ao, ma menye Wo ndzi Wo yaw, 
Munsu dɛ emi mo bɔn
Bepira Wo dɔ akoma,
Dze yaw bɛhyɛ Wo do.   Amen.

MHB 176
1 . Yaw Nyimpa! Wɔnhwɛ dzin bi a 
Wɔdze frɛɛ Nyame Ne Ba a
Ɔbɛgyee adasa nkwa
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!

MHB 176
2 . Wɔhyɛɛ N' fɛr, woyii N' ehi, 
Wɔdze m' afɔdzi soaa No;
No bɔgyaa sii m' fakyɛ pi:
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!

MHB 176
3 . Yedzi fɔ, hɛn ho yɛ nkɔw 
Na Ɔno nye mpata-guan:
Bo adwe koraa!- aso ampa?
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!

MHB 176
4 . Ɔsɛn wimu na owui, 
Ɔkaam' dɛ, Afei mewie!
N-dɛ wɔakrɔn No wɔ sor
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!

MHB 176
5 . Na hɛn Enyimnyam Hen n' ɔba 
Ɔbɛfa No nkorɔfo kɔ a,
Ber n' yɛbɔtow ndwom yi bio:
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!

MHB 177
1 . Aa! Jesu krɔnkrɔn, ebɛn na ayɛ, 
Na nyimpa dze enyitan bu Wo fɔ yi?
Atamfo si W' atwetwe, wodze apa W',
Ao, mandzehunyi.

MHB 177
2 . Woana dzi so? Woana dze yi baa Wo do? 
Ao, Jesu, mo bɔn na ɔabɔ W' mbusu yi;
Mara a, Wura Jesu, emi na mepaa W':
'Mi mobɔɔ W' mbeamuduam':

MHB 177
3 . Wodze Guanhwɛfo n' abɔ afɔr ama nguan n'; 
Akowaa ayɛ bɔn, Ba n' agye ho ntsea;
Ber a nyimpa noara no nkwagye nnyɛ n' asɛm,
Nyankopɔn per no.

MHB 177
4 . 'Mi ntsi, Jesu pa, na ebɛyɛɛ nyimpa, 
Wo wuyaw wenwen, na wo nkwa afɔrbɔ;
Wo wum' ahoguan, W' amandzehu yawyaw,
'Mi mo nkwagye ntsi a.

MHB 177
5 . Dɛm ntsi, Jesu pa, dɛ murunntum kaw tua 'i, 
Muhuhor Wo, mobɔsɔr ama Wo daa,
Hwɛ W' ayamuhyehye na Wo dɔ a ɔnnsakyer,
Nnyɛ dɛ mefata.

MHB 178
1 . DƆ a mowɔ ma Christ mu gow a, 
Mohwehwɛ gyedzi mapa;
Na adwen m' mokɔ turo n' mu,
Gethsemane Turo no mu.

MHB 178
2 . Hɔ menatsew no nwin mu,
Ber a ewia akɔtɔ;
Hwɛ 'Baako a ohu amandze n',
No nko rusu, rubɔ mpaa.

MHB 178
3 . Dɔ a mowɔ ma nyimpa m' gow a,
Mohwehwɛ gyedzi a ɔyɛ dzen a, 
Mokɔ Calvary koko ko,
Bea a suro na awerɛhow wɔ.

MHB 178
4 . Hwɛ yaw ɔtsee wɔ hɔ a!
Ohun amandze wɔ dua n' do;
N'ahoguan na ne gyedzi,
'Dɔ edzi konyim wɔ wu m'.

MHB 178
5 . Medan ba abrabɔ ho bio,
Muhu yaw no bo a ɔsom,
Muhu tum biara a ɔwɔ a,
Medze moho bɔ afɔr.

MHB 178
6 . Na medze gyedzi a otsim
Nye dɔ ma ayɛyi ndwom do,
Ma Christ a oedzi owu do,
Ma Christ a wɔakrɔn N' wɔ sor.

MHB 179
1 . HƐN abɔnfo a yɛyɛ mbɔbɔr
Daa sum na ibun mu,
Bea a enyidado bi nnyi,
Na adzekyee nndu hɔ.

MHB 179
2 . Asomdwee Hen n'dze ayamuhyehye,
Ohun hɛn kɛse n';
O anwanwa dɔ bi a onyae a! 
Ɔyɛɛ ntsɛm bɛgyee hɛn.

MHB 179
3 . Osiaan fii sor ahengua n' do
Dze enyigye yɛɛ ntsɛm bae,
Dze nyimpadua hɛɛn wumaa mu,
Na ɔtsenaa ewufo mu.

MHB 179
4 . Ɔdɔ yi ntsi ma obotan 
Na akoko ngyaa kommyɛ, 
Na nyimpa tɛkyerɛma nyina
Nyi Agyenkwa n' ayɛw.

MHB 179
5 . Abɔfo, hom nye bɛn ndzi dɛw,
Hom mbɔ sika sanku;
Na hom pegya hom ndwom wɔ sor a,
Mma wonntum nnkyerɛ da.

MHB 18
1 . HOM mma yɛmfa enyigye adwen
Nye Ewuradze ayew, na oye:

MHB 18
2 . N'ehumbɔbɔr tsim hɔ daa,
Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.

MHB 18
3 . Yɛmfa Ne dzin no ntahye,
Ɔyɛ enyame mu

MHB 18
4 . Ɔno na ɔhyɛɛ ma kan
Baa wiadze a wɔayɛ n' fofor n'.

MHB 18
