Ɔma hɔn dza wohia nyina:

MHB 18
6 . Ohyira hɔn a ɔapaw hɔn
Wɔ sar a etwie no do:

MHB 18
7 . Afei yɛmfa enyigye adwen
Nyi Ewuradze ayɛw, na oye:

MHB 180
1 . Kokwaa bi wɔ ekyirkyir noho, 
Kurow bi ban ekyir,
Hɔ na wɔsɛɛn Ewuradze a
Owui dze gyee hɛn nkwa n'.

MHB 180
2 . Yennkotum yeehu, yɛakyerɛ yaw 
A ɔsɔwee no dur;
Na yɛgye dzi dɛ hɛn ntsi na
Ɔsɛɛn hɔ na owui.

MHB 180
3 . Owui ma yeenya bɔnfakyɛ, 
Owui ma yaayɛ yie,
N' adehye bɔgya n' aagye hɛn,
Ewiei n' yaakɔ sor manm'.

MHB 180
4 . Obi nnyihɔ a oye dɛ Ɔno 
Na oeetua  bɔn ho kaw n';
No nko na otum bue sor abow n'
Na ɔdze hɛn kɔ mu.

MHB 180
5 . O, ɔdɔ bɛn na ɔadɔ hɛn 
Otwar dɛ yɛdɔ N' bi,
Yɛtwer No bɔgyaa a ɔapon hɛn n',
Yɛper yɛ no ndwuma.

MHB 181
1 . Nyame Eguambaa, yɛrekaa, 
Wo dɔ a woepira no n',
Fi sor noho gye hɛn do,
Na bohu hɛn mbɔbɔr:
Kaa hɛn a yɛdwen Wo ho;
Na gye kra biara a ɔreper;
O, yɛserɛ W', kaa Calvary,
Na ma yɛnkɔ asomdweem'!

MHB 181
2 . W' amandzehu yayaw no, 
Wo bɔgyaa fifir no,
Wo dɔ a ɔmaa iwui ntsi,
Yɛserɛ W' , yi hɛn bɔn kɔ;
Bubu hɛn mpokyerɛ mu na
Gye hɛn emumuyɛ nyinam';
O, yeserɛ W', kaa Calvary,
Na ma yɛnkɔ asomdweem'!

MHB 181
3 . Gyedzi mfa Wo bɔgyaa no 
Nsɔw hɛn bɔfakyɛ ano;
Si n' pi dɛ woebu hɛn bem,
Yɛ hɛn yar nyina edur;
W' amandzehu wɔ dua n' do
Ntsi, twa hɛn yaw nye fona do;
O, yɛserɛ W', kaa Calvary,
Na ma yɛnkɔ asomdweem'!

MHB 182
1 . Moto m' enyi hwɛ anwanwa dua a 
Enyimnyam Hen no tɔɔr do n' a,
M' adze pa biara mummbu n' hwee,
M' ahopɔw nyina yɛ m' nkɔnkɔw.

MHB 182
2 . Mo Wura, ɔmpar me dɛ m' botuw, 
Gyedɛ m' Agyenkwa No wu  mu:
Egyangyandze a modɔ kɛse n',
Mobɔ n' afɔr ma No bɔgyaa.

MHB 182
3 . Hwɛ mbrɛ yaw na ɔdɔ rosɔn 
Ne tsir, Ne nsa, nye N' anan ho:
Dɛm dɔ na yaw yi mmbɔɔ mu pɛn,
Na nsoɛ kyɛw yi bi nnsoaa bi da.

MHB 182
4 . Wiadze nyina yɛ medze mpo a, 
N-kyɛ ɔyɛ akyɛdze a osuar koraa;
Dɔ nwanwa yi, Nyame dɔ yi,
Gye me kra, mo nkwa, m' adze nyina.

MHB 183
1 . CHRIST Mbeamudua no mu na mutuw;
Obunkam dza asɛɛ nyina do,
N-kwagyesɛm ne kan nyina
Gyina ne tsir fɛɛfɛw no do.

MHB 183
2 . Sɛ abrabɔ mu yaw to me,
Enyidar sa na suro ba a,
Mbeamudua no remmpa me da;
Ɔdze asomdwee na dɛw hyerɛn.

MHB 183
3 . Sɛ enyigye ewia dze kan
Nye dɔ hyerɛn wɔ mo kwan do a,
Mbeamudua no hyerɛn ka ho
Na ɔma da n' kan yɛ kɛse.

MHB 183
4 . Ɔsɛɛ, nhyira, yaw na enyigye,
Wɔtsew ho wɔ mbeanudua n' mu;
Hɔ asomdwee no, wonnsusu,
Enyigye a ɔwɔ dɔ daa a.

MHB 183
5 . CHRIST Mbeamudua no mu na mutuw;
Obunkam dza asɛɛ nyina do,
N-kwagyesɛm ne kan nyina
Gyina ne tsir fɛɛfɛw no do.

MHB 184
1 . AHEN frankaa no dzi enyim 
Mbeamudua n' hyerɛn kwan nwanwa do;
Mbrɛ Nyia ɔyɛɛ hɛn n' bɛyɛɛ honam,
Ɔsoaa hɛn afɔdzi, tuaa hɛn kaw.

MHB 184
2 . Bea a hɛn ntsi wɔwɔɔ no nkaamaa n'
Na nkwa esutsen fi ne mfem' pem; 
Bɔgya na nsu a edzi afora
No mu na wɔahohor hɛn ho.

MHB 184
3 . Dza David kae nyina baa mu
Wɔ tsetse nkɔnhyɛ ndwom no mu;
Nyankopɔn kaa wɔ amanaman m'
Dɛ ofi dua n'do edzi konyim

MHB 184
4 . O ahoɔfɛw dua, o kan dua!
O dua a wɔahyɛ ndwom no ahentar!
Dua soronko konyimdzifo a 
Honam krɔnkrɔn n' bɔhoom wo bom'.

MHB 184
5 . W'abasa a atserɛw mu n' do
Na wiadze nkwagye durdur sɛn,
Na woetua adasa tsir kaw,
Na wɔasɛɛ ne sɛɛfo no so.

MHB 184
6 . Wɔmfa enyidzi a ɔfata nyina
Mma Ɔdomankoma Ɔkorsa;
Hɔn a enam Wo mbeamudua n' do
Agye hɔn n', kora, dzi hɔn do daa.

MHB 185
1 . ƆBAATAN werɛhonyi dze su
Gyinaa mbeamudua no ase,
Mbrɛ Ewuradze a oruwu n' sɛn;
Nna ne kra enyigye asa,
Ahoguan ama no werɛ ahow,
Ɔtse afowa a ehwira N' mu n' nka.

MHB 185
2 . Ao, ɔbaataan siarfo! Afei
Mbrɛ yaw na awerɛhow ato no a!
Ne Ba a ɔwoo n' kor no ntsi:
Ɔhwɛ n'enyimnyam Ba no a
Ɔsɛn mbeamudua do no a,
Na yaw kɛse aka no.

MHB 185
3 . Ohun Ba a woebu N'enyimtsia,
Wɔaka N' mpire, asoa N' nsoɛkyɛw,
Wɔ No nkorɔfo hɔn ntsi.
Ɔhwɛɛ N' kɛpeem dɛ wobuu N' fɔ!
No wu mu obiara paa No,
Na ogyaa No sunsum mu.

MHB 185
4 . Jesus, ma n'etuhoakyɛ no 
Nkenyan me ma menyɛ dɛm bi;
Dɔba, Pomfo yamuyiefo,
Nkyɛ m'akoma eenya hyewbɔ fofor,
Na ɔdɔ mapa aahyɛ mu ma,
Ama meenya Wo nkyɛn kwan.

MHB 186
1 . Onyame dɔ! 'bɛn na ayɛ 'i? 
Bɛkyebo Nyame ewu ama m'!
Egya No domankoma Ba N'
Soaa mo bɔn nyina wɔ dua n' do;
Bɛkyebo Nyame ewu ama m'!
Mo Wura, mo Dɔ, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam'.

MHB 186
2 . Akwantsemfo nyina hom nhwɛ 
N-kwa na Asomdwee Hen ruwu!
Abɔn hom Bɔfo na oruwu 'il!
Aso yaw bi nye Nedze 'i sɛ?
Hom nye m' mbɔsɔ No bɔgyaa nhwɛ:
Mo Wura, mo Dɔ, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam'.

MHB 186
3 . Woeku No ama wo nye me, 
Ma yɛnye Nyame abɔ mu:
Hom ngye Nsɛmpa n' ara ndzi dɛ,
Jesus bɔgyaa pon hɛn nyina,
Fakyɛ pem Ne mfem' ma obiara;
Mo Wura, mo Dɔ, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam'.

MHB 186
4 . Wɔmma yɛnko dua n' n' ase ha, 
Yɛmfa dɛw ndɔw yarsa nsu n' bi,
Yembu adze nyina ahwerdze,
Yengyaa hɛn akomam' mma No;
Mma yɛnndwen hwee, yɛnnka  hwee, dɛ
Mo Wura, mo Dɔ, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam'.

MHB 187
1 . Hom mbra ma yɛnka mmɔm kakra; 
Hom mbra Agyenkwa Ne nkyɛn ha;
Hom mbra ma yɛmbɔm', yɛnka mmɔm:
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.

MHB 187
2 . Worisi No atwetwe yi, 
Ana yennkosu ama No?
Ao! hwɛ mbrɛ ɔayɛ komm sɛn hɔ:
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.

MHB 187
3 . Wɔbɔɔ Ne nsa nye N' anan mu 
Ne men mu wewee, nsukɔm twaar No!
Mbusu dze sum hyɛɛenyi do:
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.

MHB 187
4 . Ɔkaa ɔdɔ nsɛm mpɛn esuon; 
Ndɔnhwer ebiasa na ɔtaa dzinn
Serɛɛ mbɔbɔrhu maa adasa:
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.

MHB 187
5 . Ma yengyina mbeamudua n' ase, 
Na bɔgya a ofi Ne mfem' no,
Ɔbɔhor hɛn ho bɔn nyina:
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.

MHB 187
6 . Koma bobɔe na nyinsuwa, 
Wɔmmfa nnkam hɔn a wobisa;
Dɔ ahyɛse nye 'koma bobɔe:
Mo Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.

MHB 187
7 . Onyame dɔ! nyimpa no bɔn! 
Munnsu 'i asɔ hom tum ahwɛ;
Na Nyame dɔ edzi konyim:
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.

MHB 188
1 . HƆN a wotwa mu nyina
Wɔntwe mbɛn Jesus;
Ɔnnyɛ hom asɛm dɛ Jesus wu anaa?
Ɔyɛ hom asomdwee,
Hom kyigyinafo;
Hom mbra mbɔhwɛ dɛ yaw bi nye Nedze n' sɛ a.

MHB 188
2 . Owu dze pata
Binom hɔn bɔn koraa;
Wo kaw no oetua, na ɔayɛ w'edwuma n'.
Obiara benya
Asomdwee a ogyaae;
Ɔno na ɔserɛɛ dɛ: M'Egya, fa kyɛ hɔn.

MHB 188
3 . Ɔsɔree dua n' do,
Dze maa emi na ɔwo; 
Woetsie mpaabɔ n', ɔbɔnfo afa n' ho edzi, 
Ɔbɔnfo n' nye emi,
Na motwer Jesus,
Bɛgye fakyɛ a Nyame nnkotum dze akam.

MHB 188
4 . Megye me fakyɛ,
Meyɛ ɔbɔnfo;
Ɔdzebɔnyɛnyi, megye Jesus dzin dzi.
Ɔtɔɔ adom a\nAfei mesuo m' yi;
O Egya, inyim dɛ obowui maa me.

MHB 189
1 . WƆAKRƆN W' nyimguase dua n' do,
Awerɛhow Hen, menye W' weɔn;
Sum gye W'enyim a atow no do,
Obi nntum nnhu Wo yaw no;
Obi nntum nnkyerɛ amandze a 
Wo nko rosɔw no komm no.

MHB 189
2 . Eyɛɛ komm ndɔnhwer ebiasa n',
'Nye sum mu etumfo dzii aper;
Nyimpa bɔn daa Wo nko do,
Sum etwa Wo ho nyina ehyia,
Kodu dɛ aber n' bodu
Na Nyame Eguambaa ewu.

MHB 189
3 . Tsie Ne nkekam' dzendzen no a
Odua munumkum mu kɔ sor!
Ɔwo a 'yɛ Egya n' Ba kortoo n',
Ɔwo a Noara asera Wo ngo,
Ɔwo na ibisa No dɛ:
Ebɛn ntsi na apa me?

MHB 189
4 . Ewuradze, sɛ yaw nye suro
Dze sum kata me kra do a,
Ɔwo a edzi emia dɛm pɛɛn,
Ma Wodze annka ekyir n',
Da Wo su wenwen n' mu kyerɛ m',
Na meehu dɛ ebɛn m' sum m'.

MHB 19
1 . Wonyi Nyame Hen ayɛw! 
Wɔmfa ayɛyindwom mbrɛ N';

      N' ehumbɔbor tsim hɔ daa, 
      Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.

MHB 19
2 . Wonyi N' ayɛw: ɔayὲ ewia, 
Dὲ ɔkɔ aprɔw daa daa nyina:

MHB 19
3 . Na eso ɔayɛ bosoom, 
Ma odu anafua a ɔhyerɛn:

MHB 19
4 . Wonhyira N' dὲ ɔtɔ nyankom, 
Ma ɔma edziban fifir:

MHB 19
5 . Na ɔma asaase pa so 
Oyi no ndɔbaa ma hɛn:

MHB 19
6 . Ɔama buber so aba, 
Ɔahyɛ hɛn asan mama:

MHB 19
7 . Ɔama edziban a ɔsen dɛm, 
Daa daa dɛw ho ahobadze:

MHB 19
8 . Enyimnyam nka, Hen dɔyɛfo 
Abɔdze nyina ntow enyimnyam,

      Enyimnyam nka Egya, nye Ba, 
      Nye Sunsum, Ebiasa Kor.   Amen.

MHB 190
1 . O ƆDƆ bra mapa!
Dza ntsi ogyaa N'ahengua
Wɔ sor bɛyɛɛ maa hɛn wɔ ha n',
Ne nyina abɔ adze.

MHB 190
2 . Dza Egya n' pɛ nyina, 
Edwuma n' biara annka, 
Ne berɛ na yaw, ɔyɛɛ n' nkorkor;
Kyerɛwsɛm no ahyɛ ma.

MHB 190
3 . Hɛn yaw biara nnyi hɔ a
No so ɔammfa mu bi;
Nyimpa yaw na adwen nyina
Ehwira N'akoma mu.

MHB 190
4 . Ne tsir do nsoɛ kyɛw no, 
Na Ne kra a bɔn nnyi mu;
Ɔsoaa hɛn bɔn na afɔdzi nyina,
Na ɔama yeedzi mu.

MHB 190
5 . Owuu ɔdɔ mapa m';
Owui, owuu maa me!
Afɔr a ɔpata bɔn nyina,
Metetar Wo gyedzi m'.

MHB 190
6 . Ohiaber biara mu,
Atsɛmbugua n' enyim,
Nyame Eguambaa, Wo ndwuma no 
Na hwɛ ho gye me nkwa.

MHB 190
7 . Mo Wura, yɛ mo mu edwuma,
Dɛ mbrɛ ayɛ ama m', 
Na ma mo dɔ nyɛ mbuae mma adom a 
Wo dɔ dze aba no.

MHB 191
1 . NYAME a W'adom nnyi nhwɛdo,
Adasamba Gyefo,
Daa daa ayɛyi ho asɛm, 
Yehu W'amandzehu m';
Yɛda ho tow W' ndwom dɛɛdɛw, 
Yɛda ho yɛwɔ dɛw mu,
Yɛtow Abɔn Adamfo ndwom,
No dɔ yɛ fofor daa.

MHB 191
2 . Yehu daa anwanwadze
Fi nwanwa dua no do,
Yehun dɛ wɔbɔɔ N' mbeamudua m',
Bea a yehu hɛn Bɔfo;
Owura Jesus, ayɛ dɛn?
Yɛbɔ Wo wu ho dawur,
Yegyina hwɛ, kotow, gye to m'.
'Dɔ bi nntse dɛ Wodze.

MHB 191
3 . Ɔdɔ nye awerɛhow bi nnyi
Tse dɛ m'Agyenkwa dze n';
Hwɛ, ɔda mbeamudua no do!
Hɛn adzesoa ahyɛ No do;
Hom nka dɛ N'awoo fi sor!
Hom nhu dɛ ɔyɛ Nyame;
Gyedzi tsea m' dɛ, ɔyɛ Ɔno,
Me Nyame a ohu amandze!

MHB 192
1 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu! 
N-tar saw abowa no do;
Tsena do, na eyɛ Ɔhen mu,
David ne Ba, wiadze Gyefo.

MHB 192
2 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu! 
Ɔwo na Sion rotweɔn Wo;
Wɔdze n-tar nye mberɛnkɔnson
Egu Wo kwan mu dɛ fa do.

MHB 192
3 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu! 
Ɔkatakyi, hell ne sɛɛfo;
'Wo na ibue sor ahenman
To hɔ petee ma Wo nkorɔfo.

MHB 192
4 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu? 
Dɔmtutuw fi sor rohwɛ Wo,
Dɛ 'rokɔbɔ afɔr huhu
Ana akɔko W' ahengua do.

MHB 192
5 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu! 
Wiadze nyina hɛn Enyidar!
Dzi nyim, brɛ hɛn 'komatɔmu,
Ndzeyɛtsenenee, ɔdɔ, nye siar.

MHB 193
1 . Hwɛ adasa hɔn Agyenkwa 
Wɔ enyimguase dua n' ho!
Dɔ a ɔkaa N' ma okyii bɔgya
Wui maa wo n' so so pa!

MHB 193
2 . Tsie, ɔrepen! abɔdze rihim, 
Asaase rowosow;
Asɔrdan mu ntwamutam atsew,
Abotan repaapaa.

MHB 193
3 . Oewie! wer a ho hia n' ɔatɔ; 
Ɔrekam', Gye Mo sunsum!
Hwɛ mbrɛ ɔabɔ Ne tsir adze,
Ɔabɔ n' adze ewu!

MHB 193
4 . Na obobu wu apon mu ntsɛm, 
Na ɔahyerɛn enyimnyamm';
Nyame Eguambaa, yaw bɛn a,
Dɔ bɛn nye Wodze sɛ?

MHB 194
1 . HOM nkɔ sum Gethsemane, 
Hom a ɔsɔhwɛfo n' haw hom;
Hom nhwɛ hom Gyefo No ko,
Hom nye No nweɔn dɔnhwer kor;
Mma hom nndan mmfi Ne yaw ho;
Hom nhwɛ Jesus nsua mpaabɔ.

MHB 194
2 . Dzi ekyir kɔ atsɛmbu da n' mu;
Hwɛ Nkwa Wura a wɔakyer no,
O bɔwen na bɔwema!
O ɔhaw a Ne kra hunii a!
Mma nnguan yaw na enyimguase;
Sua No soa mbeamudua no.

MHB 194
3 . Fow Calvary awerɛhow koko n';
Kɔkotow N'ananadze,
Hwɛ anwanwadze a osii,
Nyame abɔ afɔr ewie,
Tsie! Ɔreka m' dɛ oewie!
Sua Jesus hu mbrɛ wowu.

MHB 194
4 . Dzi ekyir kɔ nda n' do ntsɛmara, 
Beebi a wɔdze fun no toe;
Abɔfo tse hɔ roweɔn;
Woana abɛfa No kɔ?
Christ asoɛr! Ɔpɛ akɔ sor;
Gyefo, kyerɛ hɛn ma yɛnsoɛr.

MHB 195
1 . OEWU! Abɔn Adamfo ewu!
Hwɛ! Salem mbabaa rusu No! 
Isum akata sor enyi,
Asaase wosow awerɛfir m;
Ahotsewfo, hom mbosu No,
Ohun amandze soaa hom adzesoa
Ɔtseaa m' na okyii nyinsuwa maa hom,
Ohuee No bɔgyaa gui maa hom.

MHB 195
2 . Ɔdɔ na yaw a onnyi kabea,
Enyimnyam Wura wu ma adasa!
Naaso hwɛ dɛw kɛse a menya!
Jesus a owui n' enyan bio!
Nyankopɔn asoɛr efi nda m';
Nda enntum annkora No do!
Abɔfo mpempem hyia No kwan,
Wɔyɛ no akɔaba kɔ sor.

MHB 195
3 . Ahotsewfo, hom ngyaa su na
Hom nka dɛ Gyefo no dzi hen;
Hom ntow ndwom d ɛ ɔasɛɛ hɛll dɔm n',
Ɔdze owu too mpokyerɛ mu.
Hom nka dɛ: Ɔhen, tsena ase daa!
Wɔwoo Wo Gyefo hoɔdzenfo!
Ɔsɛɛfo, wo tum no wɔ hen?
Ntuw wumaa, wo konyim n' wɔ hen?

MHB 196
1 . Yɛtow ayɛyindwom kamfo 
Jesus a owuu mbeamudua do n':
N-dzebɔnyɛfo enyidar;
Ne ntsi yemmbu wiadze yi hwee.

MHB 196
2 . Ne mbeamudua no kyerɛ petee 
Ma yehu dɛ Nyame nye dɔ:
Ɔsoa hɛn bɔn wɔ dua no do;
Ɔdze Nyame adom brɛ hɛn.

MHB 196
3 . Ne mbeamudua n' yi hɛn afɔdzi; 
Ɔtaa hɔn a wɔtɔ bitsi;
Ɔhyɛ hɛn dzen mbusu ber mu;
Ɔma dza ɔyɛ wen yɛ dɛw.

MHB 196
4 . Ɔma ohufo mbanyinndam; 
Ɔhyɛ okotoo dzen ma ɔko;
Ɔma kan hyerɛn hɛn wumpa do,
Mma yennsuro samanadze.

MHB 196
5 . O Jesus, Wo mbeamudua no yɛ 
Ɔbra ne dɛw, mbusu n' edur
N-dzebɔnyɛfo guandɔbea:
Abɔfo kamfo Wo dɔ daa.

MHB 197
1 . JESUS mbeamudua n' ase
Na mepɛ dɛ migyina;
Ɔbotan kɛse bi nwin mu, 
Asaase a etwee do;
Ofi bi a ɔwɔ sar bi do,
Ɔkwan m' ahomgyebea,
Ewia ketee ne hyew ano,
Na da no n'adzesoa.

MHB 197
2 . Jesus mbeamudua no do
M'enyi botum ehu
Nyimpa kor a oruwu no,
Ohun amandze maa me,
Mifi m'akoma m' kyi nyinsu,
Ka anwanwansɛm ebien;
Anwanwa dɔ ɔgyee me;
Na fata a memmfata.

MHB 197
3 . O mbeamudua, wo nwin ase
Bɛyɛ me tsenabea!
Mimmbisa ewia ne kan biara
Dɛ N'enyim kan no nko,
Mo bo dwe dɛ migyaa wiadze,
Minnya adze, mohwer adze,
M'enyimguase ara nye mo bɔn,
M'enyimnyam nye mbeamudua n'.

MHB 198
1 . YƐRONNKƆ nngya Wo mbeamudua,
Yerimmfi W'ananadze;
Wiadze mu ndzepa nnsɛ hwee,
Ndzɛmba a ɔyɛ wen ha yɛ dɛw.

MHB 198
2 . Yɛhwɛ ha a, yehu hɛn bɔn, 
Yɛrohwɛ yeesua Wo dɔ;
Bɔn a ɔmaa wɔbɔɔ W' mbeamudua m',
Dɔ a ɔsoaa mbeamudua n' maa hɛn.

MHB 198
3 . Ha, yesua ɔsom na ɔma, dzi
Dɛw dɛ yɛapa hɛnho ekyir;
Yenya ɔdɔ tsena ase ha,
Ha yenya gyedzi dze wu.

MHB 198
4 . Fahodzi ho nsɛnkyerɛdze
Na hɛn som wɔ ha ka bɔ m';
Wo mbeamudua n' gyaa adaduafo.
Yɛyɛ mbeamudua n' ho akofo.

MHB 198
5 . Yɛkɔ enyim dɛ yebotum,
'Yi na hɛn akoma hwehwɛ;
Bea a hɛn enyidado hyɛɛ ase,
Hɔ na yenya dza yɛpɛ.

MHB 198
6 . Na yɛaka Kan Dɔm no ho,
Wo mu wɔagye hɛn koraa;
Wo mbeamudua n' tsew hɛn ho,
Dze hɛn ahenkyew gu W'enyim.

MHB 199
1 . Jesus, fa m' sie mbeamudua n' ho, 
Hɔ na nsu a ɔyɛ edur n'
Fi Calvary koko no do
Pem kwa ma obiara.

       Mbeamudua n' mu, mbeamudua n' mu, 
       Na menhyehyɛ moho, 
       Nkɛpem dɛ me kra bɔhom 
       Wɔ esutsen n' ekyir hɔ.

MHB 199
2 . Mbeamudua n' ho na dɔ na adom 
Too me kra bɔbɔfo;
Adzekyee Nworaba hyɛnhyɛnn n'
Ne nserɛmɛn hyerɛɛn mo do.

MHB 199
3 . Dza osii mbeamudua no ho n', 
Nyame Eguambaa, yi kyerɛ m';
Ao, boa me ma mennantsew
No nwin ase daa daa.

MHB 199
4 . M' bɔweɔn matweɔn mbeamudua n' ho, 
Mahwɛ kan ekodu
Sika man no n' esuegya
Wɔ esutsen n' ekyir hɔ.

MHB 2
1 . NYIMPA a hom wᴐ wiadze nyina,
Hom mfa enyigye ndze ntow ndwom:
Hom mfa nyi Nyankopᴐn ayεw;
Hom mbra N'enyim hom mbedzi dεw.

MHB 2
2 . Ewuradze yε Nyame ampa;
Ͻnoara na ᴐyεε hεn;
Yεyε Nedze, ᴐnyεn hεn daa;
N’edzidzibea do nguan nye hεn.

MHB 2
3 . O hom nhεn N'aponkεse mu;
Hom mbedzi dεw N'abanguado;
Hom nyhira N', nyi Ne dzin ayεw;
Na hεn Nyame fata ndaase:

MHB 2
4 . Osiandε Ewuradze yε pa;
N'ehumbᴐbᴐr so tsim hᴐ daa;
No nokwardzi si pi ampa,
Na ᴐnnkᴐbᴐ adze ara da.	Amen.

MHB 20
1 . AHOTSEWFO, hom mbra,
Hom nyi Otumfo n'ayɛw;
Hom mma yɛnyɛ adwen kor,
Akoma, ndze na akyen:
Abɔdze biara ntow bi,
Obiara nnka n'ano nnto m'.
Wɔmma ndzɛmba a wonnyi nkwa 
So mfa kommyɛ ntow ayɛyi.

MHB 20
2 . Adasamba so hom mbra,
Hom mbra ma yɛntow ndwom pa;
Na beebi a nyimpa ehyia n',
Hom ndzi adwontow enyim.
Hom mma Nyame ayɛyi 
Ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze da do:
Ama hɛn ayɛyi ndwom
Aayɛ bɛkyebo dɛ Ɔno.

MHB 20
3 . Dɛm ntsi ofi sor dze nhyira
Bogu asaase nyina do;
Na wiadze tɛtɛr a yehu
Yɛ adwontofo asɔrdan kor;
Yɛbɛma hɛn ayɛyi ndwom
No atra mber na mbea nyina,
 Na afow edu sorsor
Otumfo kɛse n'asomu.

MHB 200
1 . JESUS m' enyidar,
Wɔdze Wo maa me,
Dede na wɔdze dzii W'ekyir 
   kɔr Calvary do,
Bɔgya a ekyi no,
Ma ondzi mma me,
Ɔmpaa m' nka dɛ ewu ama Wo 'wudzifo no.

MHB 200
2 . Afei fi sor bra,
Yi m'akomadzen,
Fa Wo dɔ kɛse no bedzi 
M'akoma do;
Wo dɔ wɔ dua n' do n',
Da n' edzi kyerɛ me,
Na bɔn akowaa m'benya me fahodzi ber no.

MHB 200
3 . Ahantan yɛ adze a
Wo mbeamudua no mmpɛ;
Na ɔnam bura a ofi Wo mfem' no mu,
Ma Wo nkwa bɔgya n'
Nyi m'adzesoa nyina,
Na ɔntsew me tsibowa ho, mfa m' 
   mbrɛ Nyankopɔn.

MHB 200
4 . Afei ma munhu
N'ayamuyie wɔ ase,
Ma ɔnhor mo ho na m'bɔhoa dɛ 
   esukwankyɛba,
Ma ɔntsew m'akoma m'
Na ɔnsesa me,
Owura, yɛ m' dɛ mbrɛ etse, wɔ wiadze yi mu.

MHB 200
5 . Ber biara medze
Me mberɛwyɛ suma,
Na ma bɔgya no nyɛ mo ho edwuma dabaa;
Me Dzimafo, fa m'
Kyerɛ sor Egya n',
Na ewiei no twe me bɛn W'ahengua no ho.

MHB 201
1 . Bura bi wɔ hɔ bɔgya ma, 
Wɔtwee n' Immanuel mfem',
Na ndzebɔnyɛfo bɔtɔm' a,
Wɔyew hɔn ho fi nyina.

MHB 201
2 . Owifo no ɔdze dɛw hun 
Bura n' wɔ n' aber do;
Hɔ na kaansa mo ho yɛ nkɔw a,
M' bɔhor mo ho bɔn nyina.

MHB 201
3 . Nyame Eguambaa, Wo bɔgyaa 
No tum ɔnnkɛpa da,
Gyedɛ W' asɔrmba nyina enya nkwa,
Mma wɔnnkɛyɛ bɔn bio.

MHB 201
4 . Ofitsi dɛ me gyedzi hun 
Esu a ofi Wo mfem',
Onyame dɔ ayɛ mo ndwom,
Na ɔbɛyɛ edu wum'.

MHB 201
5 . Na owu ma me gyirama 
Yɛ komm da dɛtsem' a,
Me kra bɔtow ndwom dɛɛdɛw bi
Akamfo Wo wɔ sor.

MHB 202
1 . O tsir Krɔnkrɔn, wopiraa Wo, 
Yaw mbordo hyɛɛ Wo do,
Wɔdze nsoɛ yɛɛ W' ahenkyɛw
Dze sii Wo atwetwe!
Mbrɛ W' enyim esi atow,
Ɔnam ahoguan ntsi;
Enyim a nkyɛ ɔkyɛn wi,
Hwɛ mbrɛ oesi enyam.

MHB 202
2 . Enyimnyam nye nkwa Wura, 
Dɛw krɔnkrɔn bi a nkyɛ ewɔ a!
Mekenkan nsɛm nwanwa yi a
Dɛw ka m' dɛ 'yɛ medze.
W' awerɛhow n', W' ayamuhyehye n',
Abɔn nya mu mfaso;
Emi mbom na motoo mbra,
Ɔwo na inyaa wuyaw.

MHB 202
3 . Minya gyirama wɔ hen 
Dze eyi Wo ayɛw
Wɔ W' amandzehu wu yi,
Wo tsema a ɔmmbɔ adze yi?
Mo Wura, fa m' yɛ Wodze koraa;
Mma memmpa W' ara da;
Pa gu ma m' dɛ m' betsiatsia
W' anwanwa dɔ yi do!

MHB 202
4 . Muruwu a, mo Wura, bɛn me; 
Ao, yi Woho kyerɛ m'
Ao, tu faa bra bohwim me,
Bɛgye m' fi mbusu nsa;
Gyedzi ntom' mma n' enyiwa
Ontsim Jesus Wo do;
Na nyia owu gyedzi mu n'
Wo dɔ ma owu sɔnn.   Amen.

MHB 203
1 . BƆNYƐNYI bɛyɛ dɛn 
Ehu adasa Agyenkwa? 
Innkotum etsie me mpaabɔ? 
Eremmfa W'adom nndom me?
W'ehumbɔbɔr no wɔ hen?
Jesus dzin tum no wɔ hen?

MHB 203
2 . Meremma nnkɔ ara da,
Gyedɛ mehu W'adom;
Ma mentse ndze dɛɛdɛw no,
Kasa, sɛ ennkɛfa akyɛ a;
Kasa, ma wonnya dza ayew,
Kasa, ma ewufo nnyan.

MHB 203
3 . Wo dɔ na meserɛ,
W'amandzehu dzi ma m';
Yaw na bɔgya a ikyii no,
Awerɛhow kɛse a idzii;
Meda W'ananadze, gye me,
Gyefo, gye nyia apon no.

MHB 203
4 . 'Bɛn na ayɛ ama me? 
O dwen Calvary ho!
Nyimpa apen a isii n',
Muguan toa Wo wu kɛse n',
Tsie me kra wufo no su,
Yi, o yi mo bɔn fi hɔ!    Amen.

MHB 204
1 . EWURADZE Christ asoɛr ndɛ: 
Alleluia!
Nyimpa nye abɔfo ka:
Alleluia!
Hom mma dɛw na ehurusi do:
Alleluia!
Ɔsor ntow, wiadze ngye do:
Alleluia!

MHB 204
2 . Ɔdɔ edzi dwuma no;
Ɔako, oedzi nyim koraa:
Ɔbo nye aweɔmfo n' yɛɛ kwa;
Christ efi samanadze:

MHB 204
3 . Hɛn enyimnyam Hen tse ase;
Owu, wo hwirom wɔ hen? 
Prɛko na owui gyee hɛn: 
Owu, wo konyim wɔ hen?

MHB 204
4 . Wɔakrɔn hɛn Wura Christ wɔ sor;
Yedzi N'ekyir rokɔ hɔ;
Yɛtse dɛ Ɔno a, yɛbɔsoɛr;
Mbeamudua n' nye sor man n' hɛndze a:

MHB 204
5 . Hɛn enyimnyam Hen siarfo!
N-kwa a onnyi ewiei nye dɛ
Yehu Wo, yɛtse Wo tum,
Na yɛkamfo, yɛdɔ Wo.

MHB 205
1 . Jesus Christ asoɛr n-dɛ, 
	Hallelujah! 
Hɛn konyim dapɔn krɔnkrɔn, 
	Hallelujah!
Ogyaam wɔ Mbeamudua no do, 
	Hallelujah!
Dze poom hɛn a yɛayew no, 
	Hallelujah!

MHB 205
2 . Wɔmma yɛmfa ayɛyindwom,
Ntonton Christ, hɛn sor Hen a, 
Ɔsɔɔw Mbeamudua nye wumaa, 
Dze poon abɔn gyee hɔn nkwa n'.

MHB 205
3 . Na amandze a ohunii n', 
Ɔdze nkwagye abrɛ hɛn; 
Afei odzi hen wɔ sor, 
Mbrɛ abɔfo tow ndwom daa.

MHB 205
4 . Yɛntow ndwom mma hɛn Nyame, 
Nkamfo No dɔ afebɔɔ, 
Ɔsormba, hom nyi N' ayɛw, 
Egya, Ba, Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn.

MHB 206
1 . Christ asoɛr o! Hallelujah! 
Hɛn konyim adamfo asoɛr.
Wonyi N' ayɛw! Hallelujah!
Christ asoɛr ewufo mu.
Hɛn 'koma dze ndaase tonton N',
Dɛ Ne kan ahyerɛn bio;
Yɛdze dɛw bu ntwɛr wɔ N' enyim,
Yɛsoɛr fi yaw na nyinsuam.
 
   Christ asoɛr o! Hallelujah! 
   Hɛn konyim adamfo asoɛr. 
   Wonyi N' ayɛw! Hallelujah! 
   Christ asoɛr ewufo mu.

MHB 206
2 . Christ asoɛr! No wiadze abrabɔm' 
Awerɛhow nyina abɔ adze,
Ɔnam enyigye mbotsen mu
Asan aba nkwa mu bio;
Owu na hɛll akotow No;
Ɔasoɛr, oedzi konyim ndɛ
Abɔfo dzi N' ekyir roweɔn N'
'Nyimnyam abɔ N' abɔtsir.

MHB 206
3 . Christ asoɛr! ofitsi ndɛ dze 
Owu na hɛll remmen hɛn,
Yɛyɛ Christ dze, Wɔ No mu na
Yeedzi adze nyina do nyim;
Ekyingye na mbɔbɔryɛ nyina
Na suro abɔ adze;
Ndɛ da yi nye No wusoɛr da,
Hom mma yɛnsoɛr yɛnhyɛ fa.

MHB 207
1 . Ewuradze Christ asoɛr bio; 
Christ ebubu mpokyerɛ nyinam';
Tsie, abɔfo robɔ se,
Rotow ndwom wɔ sor daa daa:
                          Hallelujah!

MHB 207
2 . Nyia ɔdze No nkwa maa hɛn n', 
Ɔno a hɛn ntsi ɔsɔɔw ko n'
Ɔyɛ hɛn Mpataguan ndɛ;
Hɛn so dɛw tow ndwom dɛ:
                          Hallelujah!

MHB 207
3 . Nyia ɔsɔɔw obene nyina 
No werɛ hoow wɔ mbeamudua n' do n',
Ɔtse enyimnyam' wɔ sor ndɛ,
Odzi ma hɛn, tsie hɛn su.
                          Hallelujah!

MHB 207
4 . Ɔno a wɔnnto No kwan dzin, 
Ɔno a osianee kɔr hɛll,
Nyia katakyi too n' mpokyrɛ n'
Ndɛ wɔasoa N' 'henkyɛw wɔ sor.
                          Hallelujah!

MHB 207
5 . Ɔno a ɔdaa nda n' mu n' 
Wɔakrɔn No dɛ ɔngye nkwa;
Ndɛ wohua N' Christianman mu
Dɛ Eguambaa N' yɛ ahemfo Hen.
                          Hallelujah!

MHB 207
6 . Ndɛ ɔse yɛmbɔ n' dawur 
Mbrɛ abɔn besi enya nkwa,
Mbrɛ nnuhofo enya fakyɛ
Mbrɛ hɛn so bɛyɛ ahɛn sor,
                          Hallelujah!

MHB 207
7 . Hɛn Mpataguan N' nye W' ampa 
Christ, nyɛn Wo nkorɔfo ndɛ;
Yi hɛn bɔn na hɛn mfom kɔ,
Ma hɛn nyina atow ndwom dɛ:
                          Hallelujah!

MHB 208
1 . OWUSOƐR da no nye yi, 
Wiadze nka wɔ mbea nyina;
Ahosɛpɛw Apaho,
Nyankopɔn Apaho n';
Yefi wu mu kɔ nkwa mu,
Yefi asaase kɔ Sor,
Hɛn Christ dze konyimdzi ndwom,
Na ɔdze hɛn aba.

MHB 208
2 . Hɛn akoma mu ntsew bɔn ho,
Ama yeehu adze yie;
Ewuradze a ɔwɔ daa kan m';
Ɔwɔ owusoɛr kan m',
Na yetsie Ne ndze no yie a,
Yetse n' pefee, bɔkɔɔ,
Nedze nyina bɔ ose a wɔtse, 
Wɔtow konyimdzi ndwom.

MHB 208
3 . Afei ma ɔsor enyi ngye,
Ma asaase ndwom nhyɛ ase;
Wiadze tɛtɛr ndzi konyim,
Na dza ɔwɔ mu nyina;
Dza wohu na dza wonnhu
Ntow enyigye ndwom pa:
Na Christ Ewuradze asoɛr,
Hɛn dɛw a onnyi ewiei.

MHB 209
1 . N-KWA kan ntsaban do,
Anapa tutuutu,
Na ɔbɔfo no bae
Bepireew ɔbo n' fii hɔ.
    Hom nyɛ kor mma hom ndze do yie,
    Ntonton Nyia ɔasoɛr efi owu m' no.

MHB 209
2 . Aweɔmfo a wɔbɛn No n'
Hun kan n', tsee ndze nwanwa n',
Suro m' wotwaa hwee famu birim!!
Woguu famu dɛ ewufo.

MHB 209
3 . Na Ɔnodze ɔsoɛɛr bum
Fii ewufo nda mu a 
Enyiwa ennhu No,
Sor na asaase Wura.

MHB 209
4 . Ne kan ho mbofraba,
Hom nsoɛr, hom nye No nsoɛr;
Hwɛ mbrɛ woraba no 
Rehyerɛn wɔ wimu hɔ!

MHB 209
5 . Oegyaa ndzɛmba adadaw
Nyinara wɔ nda n' mu;
Wosie ɔwo na Ɔno a,
'Nye no ntsena nkwa mu.

MHB 209
6 . O Ewuradze krɔnkrɔn,
Yɛtow Wo ndwom ndɛ da 'i, 
Yɛdze hɛn akoma nyina 
Ma Wo, eyɛ hɛndze.

MHB 21
1 . KAMFO Abraham Nyame,
Nyia odzi hen wɔ sor,
Nyia ofi tsetse tse ase,
Ɔdɔ Nyame.
Nyame Kɛse MARA! 
Sor na asaase gye to m';
Mokotow hyira dzin krɔnkrɔn n'
Wɔ afebɔɔ.

MHB 21
10 . Nyame a odzi hen sor,
Bɔfo mpanyimfo tow;
Wɔtsea m'Krɔnkrɔn, Krɔnkrɔn, Krɔnkrɔn,
Ɔhen Tumfo!
Mbrɛ ɔtse n' ɔnnsesa,
Na ɔbɛyɛ dɛm daa:
Jehovah, Egya, Kɛse MARA,
Yɛkotow Wo.

MHB 21
11 . Agyenkwa n'enyim hɔ,
Hɔn a wɔapon hɔn kotow;
N'adom kɛse tɔ hɔn bobor,
Daa daa nyina:
Ɔkyerɛ No dɔ akam,
Wokua ogya no mu,
Wɔpaa m'ka wo wiadze nyina,
Eguaambaa no.

MHB 21
12 . Konyimdzi dɔm nyina
Da ɔsor Nyame ase,
Hua Egya, Ba nye Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn!
Wɔtsea mu daa.
Hua Abraham Nyankopɔn!
Meka ɔsorfo ho;
Ahoɔdzen na tum nyina yɛ W'dze,
Ntonton a ɔmmbɔ adze.     Amen.

MHB 21
2 . Kamfo Abraham Nyame,
Ɔno a ɔhyɛ mbra,
Mosoer fi famu hwehwɛ enyigye
Wɔ Ne nyimfa.
Mopow wiadze nyina:
Ne nyansaa, dzin na tum,
Na medze No ye me kyɛfa,
Me kyɛm, m'aban.

MHB 21
3 . Kamfo Abraham Nyame,
Nyia N'adom no dɔɔ so;
Obegya m'menyigye nda mu,
M'akwan nyina m',
Ɔfrɛ sunsuma N'afɛ,
Frɛ Noho me Nyame;
Na ɔnam Jesus bɔgyaa do
bɛgye me nkwan.

MHB 21
4 . Ɔaka Noho ntam bi,
Migyina Ne ntam no do:
Wɔbɔsoa m' ɔkɔr ntsaban do,
Afow akɔ sor;
Hɔ na m'bohu N'enyim,
Mibedzi No tum nyi,
Na matow N'adom nwanwa ho
Ndwom afebɔɔ.

MHB 21
5 . Sɛ bɔbea ahoɔdzen sa,
Na asaase wɔ hɔ a,
Canaan nkowaa do m'enyi kyerɛ
Wɔ N'asɛm ntsi.
Menam n-su bun mu,
M'enyi tsim Jesus do;
Na menam sar huuhu no do a,
Mokɔ mo kwan.

MHB 21
6 . Muhu asaase pa a
Nhyira pii wɔ do no;
Asaase a fahodzi na daa
'Homgye wɔ do:
Numfunsu, wo, pem do,
Ngo na nsa ebu do,
Na nkwa ndua nyin prɔmm wɔ do daa,
Mbɔbɔrhu mu.

MHB 21
7 . Ewuradze Hen tse hɔ,
Ewuradze hɛn Tsenenee,
Oedzi wiadze na bɔn do nyim,
Asomdwee Hen;
Zion bepɔw no do,
N'ahendzi tsim hɔ daa,
Ɔnye N'ahotsewfo hyerɛn kan m',
Odzi hen daa.

MHB 21
8 . Ɔhwɛ Nedze do yie,
Ɔkora hɔn ntar pa fitaa dɛ
N'ayefor pa:
Ɔdze nsu a woehyira do,
Ɔdze ndua a ɔyɛ fɛw,
Ɔdze Paradisè nduadzewa,
Nyina ma hɔn.

MHB 21
9 . Korsa kɛse n'enyim
Wogyina ruhuhor No,
Na woka anwanwadze a oaye,
Hɔn asaase do:
Ɔsormba no tsie bi,
Wɔma Ne dzin tahye;
Na wɔtow ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze da,
Dzin nwanwa no.

MHB 210
1 . 'WU ahoma kyekyeer Jesus ho
Wɔ hɛn nyinara bɔn ntsi;
Afei ogyina Nyame nyimfa,
Ofi sor dze nkwa brɛ hɛn,
Ntsi ma hɛn enyi ngye yie;
Yɛmfa ndaase ntow Nyame ndwom,
Alleluia ndwom dzendzen!
	Alleluia

MHB 210
2 . Ɔyɛ aperdzi a ɔyɛ hu,
Ber a nkwa na 'wu dzii aper;
Naaso nkwa dzii konyim nwanwa!
Owu n'ahendzi bɔɔ adze,
Wɔagye ne nsamu tum nyina;
Ne nyimpadua nko na aka;
No bɔr etu afebɔɔ.
	Alleluia

MHB 210
3 . N-tsi wɔmma yendzi afahyɛ n',
Ewuradze to nsa frɛ hɛn;
Christ ankasa nye hɛn enyigye
Na ewia a ɔhyerɛn hɛn do;
Ɔnam N'adom no do ma
Akoma nya onnyiewiei kan;
Bɔn anafua no etwa m'.
	Alleluia

MHB 210
4 . 'Wusoɛr da 'i hom mma yɛnhyɛ fa 
Wɔ nokwar sor Edziban n' ho;
Adom asɛm no ahohor
Etsiɔdzen mbɔrkaw dadaw n',
Christ nko bɛnyɛn hɛn akra,
Ɔyɛ hɛn edziban nye nsa;
No nko do na gyedzi gyina
	Alleluia!

MHB 211
1 . ƆDAA nda no mu komm,
Jesus, m'Agyenkwa,
Rotweɔn adzekyee no,
Jesus, mo Wura.

MHB 211
2 . Ɔasoɛr efi nda no mu,
Oedzi N'atamfo nyina do nyim;
Ɔsoɛɛr dɛ konyimdzifo fii samanadze,
Na ɔtse ase daa nye N'ahotsewfo dzi hen:
Christ asɔɛr! Hallelujah! Christ asoɛr!

MHB 211
3 . Wɔweɔɔn Ne nda no gyan,
Jesus, m'Agyenkwa,
Wɔtoow Ne nda no kwa,
Jesus, mo Wura.

MHB 211
4 . Owu enntum annkora N',
Jesus, m'Agyenkwa,
Obubuu adaban mu, 
Jesus, mo Wura.

MHB 212
1 . ENYIGYE da, akɔaba! Mfesantsen nyina nka;
Wɔaka owu ahyɛ, yeenya ahenman n' ndɛ!
Ewufo tse ase, Nyame tse hɔ daa!
Abɔdze hɔn Bɔfo pa a hɔn nyina sɔr No
   Enyigye da, akɔaba! Mfesantsen nyina nka.

MHB 212
2 . Asaase a oenya efuw fofor no ka dɛ, 
No Wura No soɛr n' dze akyɛdze pa nyina ba; 
N-kyɛkyɛr do nhyiren, ndubaa do nhaban,
Dze kyerɛ dɛ N'awerɛhow etwa m' oedzi nyim.

MHB 212
3 . Ɔwo a eyɛ nkwa Mafo faa owu mu,\
Efaa sum kwan n' do dze kyerɛɛ Wonkwagye tum;
Afei Nokwafo, dzi W'anohoba n' do,
Wo ndaansa da nye yi; Ewuradze, soeɛr.

MHB 212
4 . Siansian akra a wɔdeda Satan mpokyerɛ m'
Fa hɔn a wɔahwe ase nyina bra nkwa mu bio;
Fa W'enyim ne hyerɛn kyerɛ, ma aman nyina nhu;
Ma adze nkye hɛn bio, 'Wo na edze da pa ba.

MHB 213
1 . ENYIMNYAM nka Wo, Ɔba a asoɛr,
Edzi owu do konyim a onnyi ewiei,
Abɔfo a wɔhyɛ ntar hyɛnyɛn pireew ɔbo n'.
Bea a edae no na wɔdze Wo ntar no gui.
     Enyimnyam nka Wo, Ɔba a asoɛr,
     Edzi owu do konyim a onnyi ewiei.

MHB 213
2 . Jesus rihyia hɛn, ɔasoɛr efi nda m';
Ɔdze dɔ kyia hɛn, oyi suro na awerɛhow;
Ma asɔr no mfa enyigye mbɔ ose,
Osiandɛ Ewuradze tse ase, owu nnyi tum.

MHB 213
3 . Yɛnngye Wo kyim bio, o n-kwa Wura;
Boa hɛn na sɛ innyi mu a, ɔbra nnyɛ yie;
Fa Wo daa dɔ no yɛ hɛn konyimdzifo;
Fa hɛn twa Jordan kɔ wo sor fie hɔ sɔnn.

MHB 214
1 . ƆKRA siarfo, nyan ɛ, nyan ɛ!
Ewuradze asoɛr dada; 
Fa ehurusi ndwom kɔ Ne nda n' do,
W'akoma bedzi dɛw.

MHB 214
2 . N-kwa rinyan nyimpa nyina yi,
Ɔdɔ ndwom gu do yi,
Wobenya nhyiren fɛɛfɛw bi 
Wɔ nkwa bura no do.

MHB 214
3 . Ɔbra mu sum kebii n' apa,
N-dɛ wusoɛ da yi;
Christ mu, ewufo nnyi hɔ bio,
Adakamaa nnyi tum.

MHB 214
4 . Yɛtse Christ mu, yɛda Christ mu,
Yenyan, yɛsoɛr Christ mu,
Na nyinsuwa yaayaw a owu ma n',
Christ bɛpepa ne nyina.

MHB 214
5 . Dɛm a ɔkra siarfo, nyan ɛ!
Par w' Ewuradze a ɔasoɛr n'; 
Nya enyigye wɔ No wusoɛr mu,
Awerɛhyɛm' wɔ N'asɛm m'.

MHB 214
6 .  Akwan nyina m' ma w'abrabɔ 
Nyɛ ndaase afebɔɔ;
W'enyigyesɛm, W'ayɛyi ndwom,
Christ wui na ɔsoɛɛr maa m'.

MHB 215
1 . Ɔko kɛse no abɔ adze; 
Afei hɛn Sahen edzi nyim;
Wɔnhyɛ ehurusi ndwom n' ase: 
	Alleluia!

MHB 215
2 . Owu hyehyɛɛ no dɔm petsee, 
Na Christ abɔ hɔn apetse;
Wɔmbɔ se ntow enyigye ndwom: 
	Alleluia!

MHB 215
3 . Aweɛhow ndaansa no etwam'; 
Ɔasoɛr konyim mu efi wum';  
Enyimnyam nka Hen tseasefo n'; 
	Alleluia!

MHB 215
4 . Ewuradze, W' amandzehu ntsi, 
Gye Wo nkowaa fi wu no bɔr mu,
Ma yeenya nkwa, yaatow Wo ndwom:  
	Alleluia!

MHB 216
1 . Christ tse ase! afei Owu, 
Wo hu nnkotum etu hɛn bo;
Christ tse ase! yi ma yehu
Dɛ samanadze nnkɛmen hɛn.
                        Alleluia!

MHB 216
2 . Christ tse ase! sor nye asaase 
Tum nyina wɔdze ama No;
Hɛn so yɛbɔkɔ Ne nkyɛn,
Yɛnye N' ekedzi Hen sor hɔ.
                        Alleluia!

MHB 216
3 . Christ tse ase! hɛn ntsi owui; 
Dɛm ntsi yɛbɛtsena ama No,
Yɛatsew nyɛe nye adwen ho,
Yɛdze hɛn bra eyi N' ayɛw.
                        Alleluia!

MHB 216
4 . Christ tse ase! yenyim ampa 
Dɛ hwee nnkɛpaa hɛn No dɔ ho;
Wu o, n-kwa o, samanadze o,
Nnkɔtwe hɛn efi No ho da.
                        Alleluia!

MHB 216
5 . Christ tse ase! afei owu 
Yɛ onnyiewiei nkwa abotsen;
Yi bɛka hɛn bo atɔm',
Ber a wu no sum bɔtɔ hɛn.
                        Alleluia!

MHB 217
1 . HOM akra a hom hwehwɛ Ewuradze,
Hom ntow hom suro nyina ngu;
Na hom nkotow na hom mbɔhwɛ
Bea a wɔdze Jesus toe.

MHB 217
2 . Dɛm na wɔbrɛɛ N-kwa Wura ase,
Dɛm na ɔdɔ tum yɛ;
M-fe a okyii bɔgya maa wo n',
Daa owu mu ara komm.

MHB 217
3 . Hom mma hom enyi do, hom ntow ndwom;
Agyenkwa n' tse ase bio;
Owu dadzeban nyinara
Enntum annkora No.

MHB 217
4 . Ne tsir a woemmbu no bi no,
Ɔakrɔn n' wɔ abɔfo do;
Nyia ɔnye ewufo tsenae no 
Dzi Ne hen afebɔɔ.

MHB 217
5 . Ahotsewfo dze enyigye
Bɔhwɛ Ne nda pan n' mu;
Wɔnye hɔn Wura bɔsoɛr akɔ
Kan a ɔmmbɔ adze n' mu.

MHB 218
1 . EKYIR tamfo, enyim bun a,
Hɛn dɔm dze 'kokodur etwa po n';
Na Pharoah dɔm atotɔ mpoano,
Na Israel enya fahodzi.

MHB 218
10 . Ne nyimfa wɔ hɛn do,
Ɔbɛɛkyerɛ hɛn kwan;
Christ edzi hɛn enyim kan,
Christianfo nka N' do!

MHB 218
2 . Hom nyina mmema hom ndze do!
Wiadze nyina abɔ m' ridzi dɛw!
Ewuradze edzi konyim!
Ewuarde bedzi hen daa daa.

MHB 218
3 . Ɔkyena hɛn yaw\nBɛdan enyigye,
Asomdwee bɛba!
Nkowaasom bɔ adze,
Ɔdɔ bɛba
'Saase do !

MHB 218
4 . Wɔasɔw ano,
Aweɔmfo weɔn
N'efiadze nda no;
Wɔasɛɛ nsɔwano n',
'Weɔmfo apetse,
Christ asoɛr ndɛ!

MHB 218
5 . Onnyi dɛ abefo su bio,
Wɔfrɛ hɔn a woetwa m' ewufo;
Na owu adan hɛn n-da,
Na adakamaa biara adan mpa.

MHB 218
6 . Prɛko bio
Eden pon
Ebue ama nyimpa ehu;
Christ asoɛr, na nyimpa so bɔsoɛr!

MHB 218
7 . Afei koraa,
Dadaw twa m',
'Nyidar, dɛw, 'somdwee, hyɛ ase;
Christ edzi nyim, yebedzi nyim.

MHB 218
8 . Nnyɛ ndɔmmum, ahomgye wɔ sor;
Nnyɛ awerɛhow; 'perdzi m' komm;
Ebɛda nn-kyerɛ dɛ ewu,
'Bɛtsena Christ mu nye ɔbra pa.

MHB 218
9 . Mbrɛ hɛn frankaa gya hɛn n',
Yɛbɔkɔ sɔkyee;
Mbrɛ hɛn Hen dzi hɛn kan n',
Yebehyia tamfo n'.

MHB 219
1 . NYAME dze konyimdzi
Ndwom afow kɔ sorsor;
Ɔsor totorbɛnto
Da abɔfo dɛw edzi!
   Hom nye wiadze nyina mbɔ m' ndzi dɛw
   Hom mfa enyimnyam nhyɛ Enyimnyam Hen.

MHB 219
2 . Nyame a nna ɔyɛ nyimpa,
Odzi hen sor ma hɛn;
Hom mma aman nyinara nhu
Hɛn Jesus konyim dɔ n'.

MHB 219
3 . Egya n' dzi tum nyina 
Ama hɛn Ewuradze;
Abɔfo tonton No,
Odzi hen daa wɔ sor.

MHB 219
4 . N'ahengua krɔnkrɔn n' do
Odzi tum tsenenee mu,
N'atmfo bɛmemem,
Ewuwu N'ananadze.

MHB 219
5 . Yɛnye N' wɔ atamfo kor,
'Bɔnsam, wiadze, nye bɔn;
Na obetsia hɔn do
Na ɔdze N'ahendzi aba.

MHB 219
6 . Kɛpem dɛ afei wɔayɛ 
Wiadze bea a ɔtsen fofor n',
Yɛnye sordɔm aabɔ m'
Atow ayɛyi ndwom.

MHB 22
1 . HOM mbra ma yɛmbɔ m'yɛntow ndwom:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!
Sor na asaase mfa ayɛyi mbra:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!
Ɔkra biara nnyan mfi bɔn mu,
Ntow ndwom dɛɛdɛw wɔ n'akoma m',
Na Jesus ntsi ɔntow ndwom dɛ:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!

MHB 22
2 . Hom nka no wiadze beebiara:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!
Yenya hɛn nkwagye wɔ Christ mu:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!
No bɔgyaa hor hɛn bɔn nyina;
No Sunsum dan hɛn sum no kan,
Na ɔma hɛn kra dze dɛw ka:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!

MHB 22
3 . Mbrɛ hɛn kyɛfa dua yɛ enyigye a!
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!
N'anohoba ma hɛn enyigye:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!
Adzekyee ɔyɛ Ewia na Kyɛm,
Anagò ɔbɛn hɛn ntamadan,
Ɔbɛka hɛn ho aber nyina:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!

MHB 22
4 . Yɛbɔtow ndwom bi wɔ Zion:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!
Nyew, yɛbɛtsea mu atow ndwom:
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!
Ber a mbersantsen rutwa m' akɔ,
Ɔnye ɔsor dɔm nyinara,
Yɛbɔkɔ do atow ndwom dɛɛdɛw
Nyame yɛ ɔdɔ!

MHB 220
1 . NYANKOPƆN afow kɔ sorsor, 
Alleluia!
Ɔdze totorbɛnto dɛw ndze, 
Alleluia
Na ɔtse N'ahengua m' wɔ sor, 
Alleluia!
Odzi wiadze nyinara do, 
Alleluia!

MHB 220
2 . Ɔdze Ne nyimpadua kɔree, 
Alleluia!
N'amandzehu 'piretua wɔ n' ho, 
Alleluia
Ɔdze kɛkyerɛɛ ɔsor mba no, 
Alleluia!
Ɔyɛ enyimnyam sen nworaba. 
Alleluia!

MHB 220
3 . Dɛm ntsi Ewuradze, bue hɛn adwen m',
Alleluia!
Kɔ hɛn man ankasa no ho,
Alleluia!
Na dwira hɛn ho afebɔɔ,
Alleluia!
Ma yaafata bea krɔnkrɔn no.
Alleluia!

MHB 221
1 . Hwɛ da a Christ fowee kɔr sor; 
	Alleluia! 
Ma hɛn enyi egyina N' 
	Alleluia!
Ɔannkyɛr adasamba nkyɛn, 
	Alleluia!
Na ɔasan kɔ no sor fie.  
	Alleluia!

MHB 221
2 . Wɔrotweɔn wɔabɔ No se:
M-botsen n' mma hɔn tsir do; 
Hom nyina mbuebue petee, 
Ma Enyimnyam Hen n' nkɔ mu.

MHB 221
3 . Kaansa ɔahɛn ɔsor mpo a,  
Ɔda ho dɔ nyimpamba; 
Ɔasan kɔ N' ahenguam' mpo a, 
Ɔda ho frɛ hɛn Nedze.

MHB 221
4 . Hwɛ! ɔama Ne nsa do sor,  
Hwɛ! No dɔ epiratua n'; 
Tsie! N' anofamfa kasa 
N-hyira gu N' Asɔr do.

MHB 221
5 . Hɛn Wura, sɛ afow kɔ sor,  
Afa wim' ekyir noho a, 
Ma hɛn so hɛn akoma 
Nka Wo do nkɔ Nyame manm'.

MHB 222
1 . HEN Ewuradze asoɛr efi wu m'!
Hɛn Jesus afow akɔ sor,
Ɔafa hɛll etumfo n' ndɔmmum
Dze hɔn kɔ sor abobowano.
Hallelujah!

MHB 222
2 . No konyim tseaseanam tweɔn hɔ,
Na abɔfo tow ndwom kamfo N'
Ahenman m' mbobow hom mbuebue,
Hom tsetse apon, hom nyina mbuebue.
Hallelujah!

MHB 222
3 . Buebue Wo ndadzeban nyina,
Na hom mma sor hyerɛn nda edzi;
Adan akɛse 'i yɛ Nedze,
Hom mma Enyimnyam Hen n' mbra mu.
Hallelujah!

MHB 222
4 . Woana nye Enyimnyam Hen yi?
Nyia oedzi hɛn nyina atamfo do n',
Oedzi wiadze, bɔn, wu, hɛll do;
Konyimdzinyi n' dzin nye Jesus.
Hallelujah!

MHB 222
5 . Hwɛ! No konyim tseaseanam tweɔn,
Na abɔfo tow awɔse ndwom';
Ahenman m' mbobow' hom mbuebue,
Hom tsetse apon, hom nyina mbuebue.
Hallelujah!

MHB 222
6 . Woana nye Enyimnyam Hen yi?
Ewuradze, 'nyimnyamfo tumfo n';
Ahotsewfo nye abɔfo Hen n';
Adze nyina do Nyame siarfo. 
Hallelujah!

MHB 223
1 . Hwɛ Konyimdzifo n' afow sor, 
Hwɛ Hen n' ahyɛ N' ahentar
Dze Ne tseaseanam fua do
Rokɔ No sor ahemfie;
Tsie! sor adwontow kuw ruhur
Hallelujah enyigyem',
Na sor mbotsen no ebuebue
Regye hɔn sor Hen akɔm'.

MHB 223
2 . Woana na ɔreba 'nyimnyam mu 
Ma ehurusi mbɛn ka do 'i?
Ɔko Wura, dɔm Nyankopɔn.
Ɔno na oedzi konyim
Ɔno a ɔsɔɔw mbeamudua do fona
Ɔno a ofi ndam' soɛree,
Ɔaka bɔn na Satan egu,
Nam wu do asɛɛ N' atamfo.

MHB 223
3 . Ɔama hɛn nyimpasu no do 
Fi fuam' kɔ Nyame nyimfa;
Ɔsor hɔ na yɛbɛtsena,
Yɛnye N' egyina 'nyimnyam mu:
Jesus dzi hen, abɔfo sɔr N';
Nyame Nyimpa tse ahenguam'
Ewuradze Tumfo, Wo sorkɔm'
Yɛdze gyedzi hu hɛndze.

MHB 223
4 . Enyimnyam nka Egya Nyame; 
Enyimnyam nka Nyame Ba a,
Oewu, ɔasoɛr na ɔafow sor,
Ɔno a oenya sor ahenman n'
Enyimnyam nka Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn;
Nye Nyame Baasa Kor no
Enyimnyam a onnyi ewiei nka
Hɔn wɔ sor nye asaase.

MHB 224
1 . Sika mbotsen no ebuebue, 
Kwan ada mu petee;
Enyimnyam Hen no ahɛn mu,
Ɔkɔ N' Egya Ne nkyɛn.

MHB 224
2 . Ewuradze, edzi hɛn kan, 
'Rekɛpɛ hɛn tsenabew,
Ama yeekefir mbrɛ ewɔ,
Na yeehu Nyame enyim.

MHB 224
3 . Dɛm n-tsi enyimnyam hyerɛn 
Hɛn kwan do wɔ asaase;
Fua a osiiw W' hɛn enyi do n',
Kan fi sor hotse no.

MHB 224
4 . Ma hɛn 'koma nye adwen do, 
Fa W' adom pa n' dom hɛn,
Na yɛnenam asaase ha 'i,
Hɛn 'koradze ada sor.

MHB 224
5 . Na hɛn enyidar na dɔ eegyina 
Nyame nyimfa mbrɛ 'tse n'.
Tsena hɛn mu na ndaamba hɛn so
Yaatsena Wom' afebɔɔ.   Amen.

MHB 225
1 . CHRIST, etsé enyimnyam nyina mu;
Hen katakyi a egye nkwa!
Wo wu edzi owu do konyim,
Wosiee Wo, n’ asɛɛ ‘Wumaa.

MHB 225
2 . Sesei akͻ beebi ekenya
Dza adasa tum nnkenya;
Este bɛkyebo ahengua n’ do.
‘Dzi hen W‘Egya No tum mu.

MHB 225
3 . Ha W'ahenman nyina nkotow Wo,
Heaven na asaase nyina,
Na hell bun dzé ahopopo twa
Hwe W’enyim wͻ nkogu mu.

MHB 225
4 . Ewuradze, hɛn akoma mu tonton
Pem dzi W’ekyir kͻ sorsor;
Yeresérɛ W’adom yi tsie hɛn,
Twe hɛn akra kͻ W‘ nkyɛn sor hͻ.

MHB 225
5 . Ntsi sɛ ehyérɛn W‘enyimnyam no mu
Bio sor mununkum no mu a.
Ma Wo nguan yengyina W'enyim
De yɛyɛ Wodze daapem.

MHB 225
6 . Wonhua Jesus! Yegye Wo dzi,
Dɛ aman nyina bͻtonton Wo,
Ͻwo a enye Sunsum kor tse
W’Egya No tum mu daapem.

MHB 226
1 . 'HOTSEWFO, hom nhwɛ enyimnyam dze n'!
Hom nhwɛ yaw Nyimpa n' sesei,
Oedzi nyim ɔko n' mu aba fie;
Nkotodwe nyina nkotow No,
Wɔnhyɛ N' ahenkyɛw! Ahenkyɛw 
Fata Konyimdzifo N' tsir.

MHB 226
2 . Abɔfo nhyɛ Gyefo ahenkyɛw;
Ɔdze empirenyimdze aba;
Wɔmfa No nsi tum egua n' do;
Ber a heaven rowosow yi,
Wɔnhyɛ N' ahenkyɛw! Gyefo no,
Ahemfo Hen no ahenkyɛw.

MHB 226
3 . Abɔn nam atwetwesi m' hyɛɛ
Agyenkwa no ahenkyɛw;
'Hotsewfo na abɔfo hyia N' ho,
Bɔ No abɔdzin, yi N' ayɛw, 
Hom nhyɛ N' ahenkyɛw na hom nhua N',
'Hemfo Hen, ewuranom Wura!

MHB 226
4 . Tsie dodow osebɔ kɛse n';
Tsie hɔn konyimdzi ndwom no;
Hwɛ, Jesus ekedzi sorsor;
Mbrɛ iyi si ma dɛw a!
Hom nhyɛ N' ahenkyɛw na hom nhua N',
'Hemfo Hen, ewuranom Wura!

MHB 227
1 . KONYIMDZI Hen, 'nyimnyam Ewuradze,
Woesi Wo hen wɔ kan mu;
Ɔsor nyina twa hwe W'enyim,
Wo tum tserɛw kɔ ekyir;
Onnyi dɛ mohwe W'enyim,
Na m'akoma bɔ hwinhwim, 
Ber a W'enyimnyam a ofi tsetse n'
Afei woeyi akyerɛ yi.

MHB 227
2 . Sɛ mohwɛ Wo a 'rofow wɔ ekyir
Kɔ ahengua n' n'enyimfa,
Hu dɔm a wɔrokotow W'enyim
Dze ndze dɛw riyi Wo ayɛw a, 
Onnyi dɛ W'ananadze
Ha motow abɔfo ndwom n' bi,
Na midzi dɛw, sor wosow
Wɔ me hen No konyim mu?

MHB 227
3 . Tum na Sunsum a ebu do no,
Bi nhue ngu mo so mo do;
Mo Wura, sɛɛ akwambew nyina,
Yɛ W'atamfo ananadzegua!
Mpo, ma wiadze ano noho
Ntse Wo tum tsenenee no,
Ma W'enyim kwan nyɛ petee;
Dzi akoma nyina do hɛn.

MHB 227
4 . Hwɛ, W'ahom rehyɛ W'asɔr a ɔwɔ,
Mbeambea nyinara no ma;
Hyɛ mo so m'akoma ma, na
Minya pɛ W'adom ber yi;
Bra, Ɔwo enyimnyam Hen, bra,
Fa m'akoma yɛ Wo fie;
Tsena m', na Wo nko dzi hen hɔ
Dɛ Wo sor ahengua n' do!   Amen.

MHB 228
1 . JESUS 'Wo a wobuu W' nyimtsia, mbo!
Galilee Hen, yɛma W' mbo!
Ihun amandze dze poon hɛn;
Edze nkwagye brɛɛ hɛn kwa,
Agyenkwa mandzehufo, mbo!
Esoaa hɛn bɔn na hɛn fɛr!
Wo ndwuma pa m' yenya enyimpa;
Yenya nkwa wɔ Wo dzin mu.

MHB 228
2 . Nyame N'afɔrbɔ Eguambaa,
Wɔdze hɛn bɔn nyina soaa Wo;
Enam ɔdɔ kɛse do na
Ebɔɔ werdam pa maa hɛn;
Wo nkorɔfo nyina enya bɔnfakyɛ,
Ɔnam Wo bɔgyaa no ntsi;
Woebue heaven abow n' petee;
Somdwee wɔ Nyame na nyimpa m'.

MHB 228
3 . Jesus, enyimnyam Hen, m-bo!
Ewɔ enyimnyam m' afebɔɔ;
Ɔsor dɔm nyinara sɔr Wo,
Etse Egya N'abanyimfa;
Ewɔ hɔ na idzi ma abɔn,
'Siesie tsenabew pa ma hɛn;
Idzi ma hɛn afebɔɔ, kɛpem
Dɛ yepue enyimnyam mu.

MHB 228
4 . Ɔsom nyimnyam, tum, na nhyira
Efata dɛ egye ne nyina;
Ayɛyi kɛse a ɔmmbɔ adze,
Ɔsɛ hɛn dɛ yɛdze ma,
Sor abɔfo hyɛnhyɛnn, hom mboa!
Hom mfa hom ndwom dɛɛdɛw mbra;
Hom nsuo m' yɛntow ndwom mma 
Gyefo n',
Hom nsuo m' yenyi Immanuel ayɛw!

MHB 229
1 . HOM nokwafo a hom nyim Jesus,
Sɛ hom nye N' asoɛr ampa ara a,
Hom akyɛn asaase do dɛw,
Hom nda No wusoɛr tum n' edzi.

MHB 229
2 . Hom mfa abotar nkyerɛ hom gyedzi,
Ndzeyɛɛ m' hom nkyerɛ fakyɛ a hom enya,
Hom nhwehwe sor enyimnyamdze,
Na hom nka tsir Christ do nkɔ sor.

MHB 229
3 . Hom bohu Agyenkwa n' wɔ hɔ,
Dɛ ɔtse Nyame abanyimfa
Wɔ N'Egya n'ahentum nyina mu,
Na obedzi hen afebɔɔ.

MHB 229
4 . Hom nhwɛ No na hom nsuasua No,
Ndzi aper hom sor fie no ho;
Na hom nsua sor adwontofo n',
Hom ntsena, hom ndɔ, hom nyi N' ayɛw.

MHB 229
5 . Hom a hom dze gyedzi agye Ewuradze n',
Mma hom nnhwehwɛ biribiara bio;
Hom nwu mma wiadze na bɔn nyina,
Hom wiadze dɔ n' wɔabɔ n'
mbeamudua m'.

MHB 229
6 . Wɔdze hom nkwa sumaa Christ mu,
Wɔ Egya No bo mu sɔkyee;
Dɛ mbrɛ Sahen nyimnyamfo n' kae n',
Hom behyia No wimu ntsɛntsɛmara.

MHB 23
1 . NYIMNYAN HEN, Asomdwee Hen,
Mobɔdɔ Wo;
Na dɔ no rommbɔ adze da,
Meserɛ Wo.
Ɔwo ama m' m'ebisadze,
Ɔwo etsie me;
Ɔwo hun mbrɛ mo bɔn tse,
Dze mo ho akyɛ m'.

MHB 23
2 . Medze me nyimdzee mapa
M'bɔtow Wo ndwom,
M'akoma m' ndzepa nyina
Medze bɛma W'.
Kaansa mo bɔn kaa m'tsiaa m' mpo a,
Esaan mo ho;
Wɔpraa ano guu mo do no,
Ɔwo 'tsiee me.

MHB 23
3 . N-da esuon na nnyɛ da kor,
M'beyi W'ayɛw;
Mudu sor mpo a, m'akomam'
M'bohuhor Wo.
Osuar, na ɔmmfata de
Medze ma Wo;
Onnyiewiei mpo yɛ tsia dɛ
Wɔtonton Wo.

MHB 230
1 . DZI dɛw mbordo ara! Hɛn Pomfo no aba;
Kɔhwɛ N'adasoe, mbeamudua na Ne nda.
   Yi No ayɛw; bo Nyia wokum No no ho dawur;
   Yi No ayɛw; fa dɛw ka dɛ ɔtse ase bio.

MHB 230
2 . Dzi dɛw mbordo ara! Wimutsewee n' asan aba;
Mununkum no apa, sunsuma no kɔ.

MHB 230
3 . Dzi dɛw mbordo ara! Wɔaka bɔgya n' egu, 
Woewie werdam no bɔ, kaw no so woetua.

MHB 230
4 . Dzi dɛw mbordo ara! Yeenya fakyɛ no kwa;
Tseneneenyi ewu ama abɔn wɔ dua no do.

MHB 230
5 . Dzi dɛw mbordo ara! Na Eguambaa a wokum No n',
Oedzi owu do konyim na ɔtse ase bio.

MHB 230
6 . Dzi dɛw mbordo ara! Hɛn Hen no wɔ sorsor;
Ofi No sor ahengua do dzi ma hɛn

MHB 230
7 . Dzi dɛw mbordo ara! Siandɛ ɔbɛba bio;
Eguambaa a wokum No n' bɛba enyimnyam m'.

MHB 231
1 . Egya, hyɛ Wo Ba enyimnyam, 
Yɛ dza Ne mpaabɔ bisa n':
Ma Kasamaafo no mbra,
Fa Werɛkyekyefo n' ma hɛn
Yɛnam gyedzi do regye N',
Jesus dzin ntsi, fa N' ma hɛn.

MHB 231
2 . Yɛnam gyedzi do bohu 
Na yɛatse Sunsum no nka;
Ɔdze N' adom nye No dɔ
Bɛtsena hɛn akoma mu:
Hɛn mboa nye papa nyina
Pem fi No nkotoo mu ba.

MHB 231
3 . Ennkɔsɔw asɛm n' ano, 
'Wo, nokwafo, yamuyiefo?
Ennkɛma Werɛkyekyefo n'
Abɛtsena hɛn 'komam' daa?
Ɔyɛ dɛn ara a 'dze N' bɛma:
Christ Kaa dɛ edze N' bɛma ampa.

MHB 232
1 . HƐN Sɔfopanyin dze N' akam,
No dɔ a ɔyɛ wu n' ho nsewhyɛ;
Ɔsɔɔw no enyimnyam mu no,
Kɛhɛɛn ɔsor krɔnkrɔnbea hɔ;
Ɔdze Ne yaw serɛ wɔ dua n' do,
Yi Noho kyerɛ Nyame ma me.

MHB 232
2 . M' Agyenkwa gyina ahengua n'enyim,
Ogyina dɛ m' Nyɛnko, Dzimafo;
Woekrukye me dzin wɔ Ne nsamu,
Ɔno na Egya n' tsie No daa;
Ber a m'kosɔw Jesus mbeamudua n' ho n',
Ɔtse bɔgya ne mpetsee no.

MHB 232
3 . Mubotum enya No tum mpaabɔ n'
Ho mbuae ha sesei ara mpo;
Ɔno ntsi metse ase sesei,
Meka dɛ ɔtse Nyame mu;
Ɔrennkyɛr, me kra a ɔwɔ N' nsamu n'
Begyina bea a me Kandzifo n' gyina.

MHB 233
1 . JESUS, yεba Wo hɔ,
Hεn enyi da Wo mboa do;
Wo nko nye hεn guandɔbea.
Ebrε hεn suro nyina adze;
Akoma biara ahomgye.
Ɔkra a oruwu biara nkwa.

MHB 233
2 . Yεma hεn enyi do,
Dze hwε akatua no,
Hwε Wo bɔgyaa atɔ hεn n’,
Edze ama abɔn kwa;
Ɔwo akyérε nkwa kwan no.
Ebue ɔsor ama hεn.

MHB 233
3 . Yεdze akokodur
Krɔnkrɔn gye akatua n’;
W’enyimnyam dεw yε hεndzc,
Wo dɔ egyapadze nyina;
Afei yεsɔ sor turn hwε,
Yεnye  Wo dzi hen wɔ sor.

MHB 233
4 . Yeatow hen sekyε dzen
Wɔ twamutam no mu;
Hεn enyidado a ɔmmpa n’
Si pi wɔ Krɔnkrɔn -bea hɔ;
Yebedzi W'ekyir afow
Ekohu Nyame N’enyim.

MHB 234
1 . Mbowa a Jewfo dze bɔɔ afɔr, 
Hɔn bɔgyaa nyinara
Nn-kotum ama etsidaa,
Anaa ɔatsew hɛn ho.

MHB 234
2 . Christ, sor Eguambaa n' dze, 
Oyi hɛn bɔn nyina;
Afɔrbɔdze a ɔwɔ dzin,
Na ɔsom bo kyɛn hɔn nyina.

MHB 234
3 . Me gyedzi nsa bɛda 
W' etsifi pampam' hɔ,
Ber a medze nnuho gyina ha
Mereka mo bɔn yi.

MHB 234
4 . Me kra twa n' enyi hwɛ 
Dza obuu Wo kɔn a,
Ohu dɛ n' afɔdzi ka ho
Ma 'sɛn mbusu dua n' do.

MHB 234
5 . Yɛgye dzi a yɛtse dɛ 
Mbusu no efi hɔ;
Yɛdze dɛw hyira Eguambaa n',
Yɛtwer N' anwanwa dɔ n'.

MHB 235
1 . MINYIM dɛ mo Pomfo tse ase,
Dɛw bi a siar awerɛhyɛmu yi ma a!
Nyia owui no, ɔtse ase,
Ɔtse ase dzi mo do hen daa.

MHB 235
2 . Ɔtse ase dze No dɔ hyira me,
Ɔtse ase, dzi ma me wɔ sor;
Ɔtse ase, nyɛn me kra daa daa;
Ɔtse ase, boame ohia ber m'.

MHB 235
3 . Ɔtse ase na ɔma m' ahom daa, 
Ɔtse ase, m' bedzi owu do;
Ɔtse ase risiesie fi ma m',
Ɔtse ase, 'dze m' bɔkɔ hɔ sɔnn.

MHB 235
4 . Ɔtse ase, 'nyimnyam nka Ne dzin,
Ɔtse ase, m'Agyenkwa daapem;
Dɛw a siar awerɛhyɛmu yi ma a!
Minyim dɛ mo Pomfo tse ase.

MHB 236
1 . YƐDZE dɛw dwen hɛn Sɔfopanyin
No mu adom no ho;
N'akoma yɛ mbɔbɔrhu nko,
Na ɔkyerɛ ɔdɔ daa.

MHB 236
2 . Ehumbɔbɛr ahyɛ N' mu ma,
Ntsi onyim hɛn mberɛwyɛ nyina;
Onyim dɛ mbrɛ nsɔhwɛ so tse,
'Siandɛ ɔafa mu pɛn.

MHB 236
3 . Ɔwɔ honam a ɔyɛ mberɛw mu n',
Osui na okyii nyinsu;
Ɔwɔ sor dze, naaso ɔtse
Ma No nkorɔfo adzesoa.

MHB 236
4 . Onnkodum ntɔn bi a ɔrehyew,
Mbom ɔbɛma adzɛw;
Onnkobu ndzembir a akonton,
Onnkobu obi 'nyimtsia.

MHB 236
5 . Afei dze ma hɛn gyedzi nka 
No mbɔbɔrhu, No tum;
Yebenya ɔgye adom no
Ahokyer ber no mu.

MHB 237
1 . OWURA, 'werɛhow bi nnyi hɔ a osuar
Dɛ yɛdze brɛ W' mpaabɔ m';
Na dadwen bi nnyi hɔ a osuar a
Onnkenyan W' mbɔbɔrhu.

MHB 237
2 . Ɔwo a afa ɔhaw yi mu,
Bɔhwɛ hɛn ahohia m' bi;
Ɔdɔ a ɔsoaa adzesoa kɛse n'
Bɔsoa dza osuar so.

MHB 237
3 . Ɔpen biara nnyi nsumaa mu a
N'aso krɔnkrɔn no nntse,
Na mbeamudua biara yɛ har
Wɔ Wo sunsum ase.

MHB 237
4 . Ɔbor bɔn, honam aperdzi,
Na akoma so do;
Dza ɔboa hɛn nye ɔdɔ a owui,
Ɔdɔ a ɔdze yaw sui.

MHB 238
1 . Me gyedzi tsim Wo do, 
CalvaryEguambaa,
Gyefo Krɔnkrɔn:
Morosɔr yi, tsie me;
Yi mo bɔn nyinara;
Ma ofir ndɛ menyɛ
Wodze koraa.

MHB 238
2 . Ma W' adom kɛse no 
N-hyɛ m' akoma dzen,
Ma menyɛ ndam;
Dɛ mbrɛ iwui maa me n',
Ao, ma mo so mo dɔ
Ɔmfram dzendzen mma Wo
Na mma ɔnndan da.

MHB 238
3 . Menam bra sum mu yi, 
Na yaw etwa mo ho 'i,
Woara kyerɛ m' kwan;
Ma sum ndan adzekyee,
Pepa me nyinsuwaEso mma monntɔ gon
Mimmfi Wo nkyɛn.

MHB 238
4 . Ber a bra bɔbɔ adze, 
Na owu n' esutsen
Bɛpram mo do n',
Ao, m' Agyenkwa siarfo,
Pa m' suro na ekyingye,
Fa me kra a apon no n'
Kɔ sor fie sɔnn.   Amen.

MHB 239
1 . EWURADZE, dwen mo ho,
Na hor mo bɔn nyina;
Yi me fi wiadze akɔndɔ ho,
Na ma mo mu so ntsew.

MHB 239
2 . Ewuradze, dwen mo ho,
Dadwen ahyɛ mo do;
Ma menyɛ W'akowaa dɔfo,
Na minnya W'ahomgye.

MHB 239
3 . Ewuradze, dwen mo ho,
Wɔ ɔko aperdzi mu;
Me yaw na m'awerɛhow nyina mu,
Yɛ m'ahoɔdzen, mo nkwa.

MHB 239
4 . Ewuradze, dwen mo ho,
Na mma mommfom kwan;
Sɛ sum dwir me dɛn ara mpo a,
Kyerɛ me ɔsor kwan.

MHB 239
5 . Ewuradze, dwen mo ho,
Sɛ ɔbra ehum tu me a,
Sɛ ɔtamfo n' tow hyɛ mo do a,
Agyenkwa, twe bɛn me.

MHB 239
6 . Ewuradze, dwen mo ho,
Na esuyirii no twa mu a,
Meehu kan a ɔwɔ hɔ daa no,
Na menye Wo edzi dɛw. Amen.

MHB 24
1 . AHOTSEWFO, hom mbra,
Hom nyi Otumfo n'ayɛw;
Hom mma yɛnyɛ adwen kor,
Akoma, ndze na akyen:
Abɔdze biara ntow bi,
Obiara nnka n'ano nnto m'.
Wɔmma ndzɛmba a wonnyi nkwa 
So mfa kommyɛ ntow ayɛyi.

MHB 24
2 . Adasamba so hom mbra,
Hom mbra ma yɛntow ndwom pa;
Na beebi a nyimpa ehyia n',
Hom ndzi adwontow enyim.
Hom mma Nyame ayɛyi 
Ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze da do:
Ama hɛn ayɛyi ndwom
Aayɛ bɛkyebo dɛ Ɔno.

MHB 24
3 . Dɛm ntsi ofi sor dze nhyira
Bogu asaase nyina do;
Na wiadze tɛtɛr a yehu
Yɛ adwontofo asɔrdan kor;
Yɛbɛma hɛn ayɛyi ndwom
No atra mber na mbea nyina,
 Na afow edu sorsor
Otumfo kɛse n'asomu.

MHB 240
1 . O MBƆBƆRHUSƐM a ɔserɛ ma hɛn,
Wɔka no ankonamyɛ na yaw ber mu;
O ndze a ofi tsetse, odzi ma hɛn
Frɛ hɛn dɛ yɛnye Nyame mbɔ mu bio.

MHB 240
2 . O awerɛkyekyesɛm a wɔka n' bɔkɔɔ,
Ber a wɔhyɛɛ afɔrbɔ huuhu n'ase,
Ɔwo a eyɛ ehumbɔbɔr, eda ho kyerɛ 
Bɔnfakyɛ a edze dom nyimpa mba

MHB 240
3 . Enyidado asɛm a edze hɛn bɛn sor,
Ber a akokodur na gyedzi apa hɛn n',
Akra a Christ sɔr ma hɔn no yɛ Christ Nedze,
Wobenya fakyɛ na dɛw wɔ No mu.

MHB 240
4 . O Odzimafo a etse ase daa daa,
Eserɛ ma akra ewufo eenya nkwa;
Ma yenhu hɛn bɔn a ohia bɔnfakyɛ,
Ma yenhu ɔdɔ a otum dze bɔn kyɛ.   Amen.

MHB 241
1 . O NYIMPA Ba, Gyefo katakyi brɛfo a 
Wo nkowaa nye asaase do ebirfo!
Yɛdze hɛn afɔrbɔ enyikan brɛ Wo,
Ɔwo a inyim hɛn yaw na hɛn dɛw nyina.

MHB 241
2 . Anan a ɔyɛ dzen na otum dzi dwuma,
Anofamfa krɔnkrɔn a ɔkaa nokwar n',
Enyi a ɔhwɛɛ nsukookoo n'ahoofɛw,
Akoma a odzii dɛw mbabun ahoɔdzen ho!

MHB 241
3 . Mbofra hɔn Dɔfo, Ɔwo a ikenyan mbofra,
Adasa nyina mu Akowaa na Ɔhen,
Ɔwo dɛw, enyindar, akomatɔmu Wura!
Yɛdze hɛn suro, dɛw na enyidar brɛ Wo.

MHB 241
4 . Nnyɛ hɛn asehwe na awerɛhow nko mu
Na yɛhwehwɛ W', Ɔwo Boafo, Nyɛnko,
Adzefo hɔn Hɔhoe, hɛn enyigye m' bɛn hɛn
Ehiafo Adamfo, bra hɛn dwumadzi m'.

MHB 242
1 . BRA, Jesus a yɛatweɔn Wo akyɛr,
Wɔwoo W' dɛ bɛgye W'nkorɔfo;
Yi hɛn fi hɛn suro na bɔn mu,
Ma yeenya ahomgye Wo mu.

MHB 242
2 . Israel 'hoɔdzen na awerɛkyekyer,
Wiadze nyina enyidar nye W';
Wiadze nyina ahwehwɛdze,
Akoma biara enyigye.

MHB 242
3 . Wɔwoo W' dɛ bɛgye Wo nkorɔfo,
Wɔwoo Wo abofra Ɔhen,
Wɔwoo W' ma eedzi hen hɛn mu daa,
Fa W'ahendzi n' bra sesei.

MHB 242
4 . Fa Wankasa Wo Sunsum no
Bedzi hen hɛn akoma m';
Dua Wo dzibew abɔso n' do ma
Hɛn do kɔ W'ahengua n' do.  Amen.

MHB 243
1 . KONYIMDZIFO n' dzi hen,
Wɔ ''nyimnyam ahoɔdzen m',
Odzi hen aman nyina do;
Ɔma wiadze enyigye,
Nyimpa mba,, hom nczi dɛw 
Jesus dɔ kɛse n' mu;
Hom mma hom akoma, na ndze do
Mma Nyia odzi hen wɔ sor n'.

MHB 243
2 . Yi N'ahentum ayɛw,
Hua ɔba a wɔakrɔn No n',
Owui, ɔtse ase, onnkowu bio,
Ɔtse N' Egya egua do;
Nyame m' hɛn Dzimafo,
Odzi hɛn asɛm ma hɛn,
Na ɔdze Ne mbeamudua n' konyimdzi
No tahye mbea nyina.

MHB 243
3 . Hom Sahen se, Hyɛ dzen!
Ɔno a onyim hom berɛ;
Hom bɛberɛ dze; hom mbu n'anhwer;
Medzi nyim ama hom,
Konyimdzi no nye yi!
Wɔhwɛ hɛn gyedzi enyim;
Jesus ewu ama me nye wo;
Gye dzi na dzi konyim.

MHB 244
1 . TSIR a wɔdze nsoɛ hyɛɛ n'ahenkyɛw n',
Wɔahyɛ n' enyimnyam kyɛw;
Ahenkyɛw na afei wɔdze
Ahyɛ konyimdzifo n'.

MHB 244
2 . Ɔsor dzibea a ɔkrɔn koraa
Yɛ Nedze, odzi wɔ N';
'Hemfo Hen, ewuranom Wura,
Ɔsor man mu kandzea.

MHB 244
3 . Ɔsor atsefo nyina dɛw,
Asaase mba nyin dɛw,
Hɔn a oyi No dɔ kyerɛ hɔn
Na ɔma wohu Ne dzin.

MHB 244
4 . Wɔdze mbeamudua nye n'enyiwu,
Nye n'adom nyina ama hɔn;
Hɔn dzin yɛ dzin a ɔwɔ hɔ daa,
Hɔn dɛw yɛ ɔsor dɛw.

MHB 244
5 . Wɔnye hɔn Wura hu amandze ha,
Wɔnye N' dzi hen wɔ sor,
Hɔn enyigye nyina nye dɛ
Wɔbɛtse No dɔ ase.

MHB 244
6 . Ne mbeamudua n' yɛ nkwa na ahoɔdzen,
Eso ɔyɛ wu na fɛr;
No nkorɔfo enyidar na ahonya,
Dza wɔdwen ho daa nyina.

MHB 245
1 . HUA Nyia Ewuradze asera n;
David ne Ba kɛse n'!
Hua N'! Ber a wɔahyɛ n' Hen mu, na
Ɔhyɛɛ ase dzii hen ha, 
Ɔbae bɛsɛɛ n-hyɛdo,
Bɛgyee adaduafo,
Ɔbae beyii bɔn fii hɔ,
Dze pɛrpɛr hyɛɛ anan m'.

MHB 245
2 . Ɔba ntsɛm dɛ ɔbɔboa
Hɔn a woruhu amandze;
Dɛ ɔbɔboa ehiafo,
Mberɛwyɛfo enya ahoɔdzen;
Hɔn apensi adan ndwom;
Hɔn sum adan ekan,
Hɔn a hɔn akra ruwu n,
Wɔsom bo wɔ N'enyim.

MHB 245
3 . Ɔbɛba dɛ mpetsema
Abɔfɔw asaase;
Ɔdɔ, dɛw enyidar, nhyiren
Bedzi N'awoe enyim;
'Somdwee bedzi N'enyim kan
Abɔ No dawur yie;
Na tsenenee bɛtsen dɛ nsu,
Fi bepɔw do esian.

MHB 245
4 . Ahemfo bɔhwe N'enyim,
Dze sika, nduhuam aba;
Aman nyina bɔtonton No,
Nkorɔfo beyi N'ayɛw;
Mpaabɔ a ɔmmbɔ adze da
Bɔfow edu N'enyim;
N'ahendzi bɛyɛ kɛse,
Ɔnnkɔbɔ adze da.

MHB 245
5 . Ɔdze N'ahengua besi 
N'atamfo nyina do;
Mfesantsen nyina ɔbɛyɛ
Onyimnyamfo, Siarfo,
Mbersatsen so runntum nnyi 
N'ahyɛmu mmfi hɔ da;
No dɔ dzin a ɔnnsesa da n'
Bɛtsena hɔ daapem.

MHB 246
1 . HOM ndzi dɛw, hɛn Wura yɛ Hen!
Nyimpa mba, hom nyi N' ayɛw,
Hom ntow ndwom wɔ konyimdzi m',
Jesus Messiah dzi Hen!

MHB 246
2 . Wɔdze tum nyina ama Jesus,
Hɛll, asaase na sor Wura,
Kotodwe biara bɔkotow N',
'Bɔnsam tse a, no ho wosow.

MHB 246
3 . Abɔfo nyina ka bɔ m';
Konyimdzi mu wɔyɛ kor,
Wɔtow Jesus N'ayɛyi,
Wɔtoa No konyimdzi n' do.

MHB 246
4 . Sɛ sum mba ma mbusu ba a,
Hɔn a wɔka hɛn ho sen hɔn;
Nyame ka hɛn ho, yennsuro,
Christ wɔ ha ntsi abɔn nsuro.

MHB 246
5 . Hwɛ! Gyedi gya no redzɛw
Wɔ bepɔw no do nyina,
Nyankopɔn bɛn hɛn sen hɛll,
Ɔdze ogya etwa hɛn ho.

MHB 246
6 . Agyenkwa Christ aba famu,
Ɔkyerɛ hɛn konyim ahenkyɛw n;
Ɔma hɛn egua wɔ sor,
Yɛyɛ N' dɔ m' konyimdzifo.

MHB 247
1 . Dzi dɛw, Nyame yɛ Hen! 
Kotow w' Ewuradze;
Ɔdasanyi, tow ndwom,
Na dzi dɛw daa nyina:

   Ma w' akoma nye wo ndze do; 
   Dzi dɛw, mese wo dɛ, Dzi dɛw.

MHB 247
2 . Agyenkwa Christ dzi hen, 
Nokwar nye dɔ dzi wɔ n';
Ɔhoor hɛn ho fi no,
Ɔgyee egua wɔ sor:

MHB 247
3 . N' ahendzi mmbɔ adze da, 
No tum wɔ sor na ase;
Wɔdze samandze;
Saafee ama Jesus:

MHB 247
4 . Ɔtse Nyame nyimfa 
Kɛpem dɛ N' atamfo
Bɔbɔ hɔn mu adze
Edzi N' ahyɛdze do:

MHB 247
5 . Obedzi nyim ewie, 
Oetu hɛn bɔn nyina,
Ma dasanyi biara
Eenya sor enyigye:

MHB 247
6 . Dzi dɛw enyidadom'; 
Hɛn Jesus bɛba bio
Abɛfa hɛn akɔ
Hɛn domankoma fie:

MHB 248
1 . JESUS, ka asɛm no,
Nokwar aba a onnwu n;
W'asɛmpa no bɛtserɛw kɛse
Wɔ hɛn asaase do nyina.

MHB 248
2 . Wiadze afanan nyina
Obedzi konyim yie,
Ɔbɛsɛɛ hɛn honam ndwuma,
Ɔawosow hɛll mbobow.

MHB 248
3 . Ma W'ahoɔdzen no nhɛn
'Kra gyedzinyi biara m';
Ma W'adom n; ngugu beebiara,
Na ɔntsew ne nyina ho.

MHB 248
4 . Ma Wo su pa nda edzi
Wɔ ɔdɔ krɔnkrɔn mu;
Fa Wo nkwa n' hyɛ hɛn ma wɔ ha,
Ma hɛn ahengua wɔ sor.  Amen.

MHB 249
1 . JESUS Ne dzin no mu
'Biara bobu ntwɛr,
Obiara bɛka dɛ
Ɔyɛ Enyimnyam Hen,
Ɔyɛ Egya Ne pɛ
Dɛ yɛfrɛ N' Owura,
Nyia ahyɛse n' ɔyɛ
Tum Asɛm pa no.

MHB 249
2 . Wɔbrɛɛ N' ase kakra
Ma oeenya abɔdzin
Efi abɔnfo ano,
Hɔn ntsi na ɔbae;
Ɔfaa mu nokwar mu
Dze kodur ewiei,
Na oduaa owu mu
Puee konyimdzi mu.

MHB 249
3 . Enuaam, ɔdɔ dzen mu,
Hom mma N' dzin kɛse,
Hom mfa suro na ahobow
Na ahopopo;
Ɔyɛ Nyame Agyenkwa,
Ɔyɛ Christ Owura;
Ɔsɛ dɛ yɛsɔr No,
Twer No daa nyina.

MHB 249
4 . Si No hen W'akoma m',
Ma ondzi dza ho
Nntsew na ɔnnyɛ nokwar,
No so nyina do;
Ma ɔnyɛ wo Sahen,
Wo nsɔhwɛ ber mu;
Ma Ne pɛ nka wo mfua,
Wɔ kan na tum mu.

MHB 249
5 . Enuanom Jesus yi
Ɔbɛsan aba;
Ɔdze N'Egya enyimnyam
Na N'abɔfo dɔm;
Wɔdze aman abɔtsir nyina
Bɛhyɛ N' ahenkyɛw;
Hɛn akoma gye No to m'
Dɛ ''Nyimnyam Hen ndɛ.

MHB 25
1 . CHERUBIM na seraphim nyina,
Etwa ehyia Ewuradze ho,
Wɔahyɛ N'asɔrdan no mu ma
Oyi ka a na oyi agye do:

MHB 25
2 . W'enyimnyam ahyɛ ɔsor ma
Wiadze esi ne sibea:
Ɔwo na yɛdze enyimnyam ma W',
Kronkron, kronkron, Ewuradze!

MHB 25
3 . Enyimnyam regyegye wɔ sor, 
Asaase gye ndwom no do,
Wɔtow no dɛ, krɔnkrɔn, 
krɔnkrɔn Dɔm Ewuradze a ewɔ sor:

MHB 25
4 . Seraph etwa ehyia N'enyim,
N'asɔr krɔnkrɔn no wɔ ase,
Ɔka hɛn bɔ m' ma yɛtonton N',
'Yi gya hɛn ma yɛtow ndwom:   Amen.

MHB 250
1 . N-KWAGYE ! O enyigye ndze!
Hɛn asomu ndwom dɛɛdɛw!
Seradze a wɔdze yɛ epirakur do 
Dza ɔdwedwe hɛn suro.

MHB 250
2 . Enyimnyam, ayɛyi nye tum
Ɔnka Eguambaa n' afebɔɔ!
Jesus Christ nye hɛn Pomfo no, 
Alleluia ! Yi N' ayɛw.

MHB 250
3 . N-kwagye ! O Eguambaa pa!
Ayɛyi yɛ Wodze;
Nkwagye bekenyan hɛn akoma,
Na atsena hɛn gyirama do.

MHB 250
4 . N-kwagye ! Hom mma ɔngyegye
Wiadze afanan nyina;
Sor abɔfo nyina nyɛ kor,
Na wɔmma ndwom no do.

MHB 251
1 . OTUMFO Kɛse, Pomfo,
Hɛn akra a apon hɔn tonton Wo;
W'edwuma a ayɛ
Yɛgye to mu,
Yɛdze enyimnyam nyina ma W';
Yɛdze n-daase gye hɛn
Nserahwɛ ber no to mu
Yɛgye W' nsaano 
Edwuma to m',
Hyira hɛn, nkwagye Nyame.

MHB 251
2 . Edze ndwuma ahyɛ Wo nkowaa nsa,
Ehyira hɔn mbɔdzen do;
Na hwɛ, Wo mu
Yehu dɔm pii,
Agyedzifo a atsew hɔn ho;
Ndzebɔnyɛfo a 'dze akyɛ hɔn
Yi hɔn Gyefo no ayɛw;
Wɔtow ndwom daa,
Asɛmpa ndwom n',
Dzi nyim wɔ W'ayamuyie mu.

MHB 251
3 . W'anwanwadze a ayɛ ewie
Fata hɛn daa daa ayɛyi ;
Na kyerɛ Wo tum,
Fa sor adom
Hyɛ nyimpa dɔm ma mbordo;
Fa nyam hyɛ hɛn asaase ma,
Na ɔman biara nyim Wo yi,
Adom Nyame,
Gye ayɛyi a
W'abɔdze fofor dze ma W'.  Amen.

MHB 252
1 . NYAME ka hɛn ho daa nyina,
Ndwom a hɛn egyanom towee nye n',
Ber a wɔwɔ akono ekyirekyir;
Hɔn ko ndwom krɔnkrɔn n' gyegyee;
Woennsuro na wɔanntɔ dɔnsuar,
Woenngyaa dɛ wɔtow ndwom dɛ.
    Nyame ka hɛn ho daa nyina,
   Christ hɛn Wura bedzi Hen!

MHB 252
2 . Wogyaa hɛn egyapadze kɛse,
Ɔwɔ dɛ yedzi konyim,
Dɔm a ɔwɔ dɛ yɛbɔ petse,
Dwuma kɛse a ɔwɔ dɛ yedzi;
Yɛntow ndwom a wɔkyerɛɛ hɛn no
Mfa ntwa wiadze nyina ho.

MHB 252
3 . Hom mfa mbeamudua n' nkyin mbea nyina,
Hom mma ɔdɔ ndzi konyim,
Hom nka ɔgye ho asɛmpa n'
Beebiara a nyimpa bɔkɔ;
Hom ntwe ɔkyena mbra enyim,
Hom mmia hom enyi ntow ndwom:

MHB 252
4 . Ɔnnkɛkyɛr ɔkɔ no botwa,
Yebenyam aperdzi frankaa n,;
Atamfo a yeedzi hɔn do n'
Boguan efi akono;
Hom nkɔ kan, hom nntsetsew hom mu,
Hom ntsea m' ntow konyimdzi ndwom.

MHB 253
1 . NYAME adzekyee, bra!
Ɔsor kan fɛɛfɛw pa,
Migyaa ne nyina mu ma W',
Mosoɛr fi mo mu pirim;
Nyame Eguambaa a Wo dɔ yɛ kan,
Hyerɛn me kra do na ɔnyɛ kann.

MHB 253
2 . Nyame adzekyee, bra!
Adze asa akyɛr;
Yesi nkrum wɔ hɛn mu,
Yesu wɔ hɛn bɔn ho;
O Anapa Woraba, twe bɛn;
O Tsenenee Ewia, pue na hyerɛn.

MHB 253
3 . Nyame adzekyee, bra!
Wiadze aberɛ aperdzi;
Aprandaa him akoko,
Nyimpa akoma werɛ how;
Nyame adzekyee, asomdwee da, bra,
Na ma akofo dede no ngyaa!

MHB 253
4 . Nyame adzekyee, bra
Dɛ sor adzekyee no!
Ma krɔnkrɔn no mbra,
Gyedzi, enyidar na ɔdɔ;
O hwɛ, yehu dɛ wimu rehyerɛn!
Ampa fɛɛfɛw no rebɛn.

MHB 254
1 . TSIE, ndze bi nye yi, ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn dodow,
Ɔwosow asaase na mframa mu!
Ewuradze aprandaa na orupue yi?
No nkorɔfo mpaabɔ ndwom nye yi anaa?

MHB 254
2 . Ampa, ɔreba na ndze mpempem tseatsea m'
Kyerɛ ahotsewfo ma mmum mpo tse;
Ampa, ɔreba na asaase dzi dɛw,
Hɔn enyigye wɔ ne mbae m' : Mereba.

MHB 254
3 . Iyi na ɔayɛ, na yɛnnkɔtonton No?
Ɔbɛyɛ yi, ana yɛbɛpa abaw?
Bra ma yɛnyɛ ntsɛntsɛm yentwa nhwe N'enyim,
Yɛmfa hɛn dadwen nto N'anan adze.

MHB 254
4 . N-kwa, owu, awerɛhow na bɔn mu no,
Ɔbɔdɔɔ me so 'siandɛ ɔdɔɔ so;
Christ nye ewiei osiandɛ nna ɔyɛ ahyɛse,
Christ nye ahyɛse, na ewiei nye Christ.

MHB 255
1 . NYAN, nyan, na anafua repa!
Aban do aweɔmfo no retsea m';
Jerusalem, afei dze nyan!
Esuom tse akɔaba ndze no,
Na ɔma hɔn enyi gye mbordo;
Mbaabun, hom mbra na adze akye!
Ayeforkun n' aba,
Hom mfa hom nkandzea no;
Halleluya!
Hom nyɛ krado mma Ayeforhyia n',
Na ɔwɔ dɛ hom kɔ hɔ kekyia N'.

MHB 255
2 . Zion tse aweɔmfo ndwom no
Na n'akoma dzi dɛw papaapa;
Onyan, ɔsoɛr fi no sum mu;
Na no Wura sian ba enyimnyam mu,
N'adom nye No nokwardzi dzi mu;
No Woraba epue, ne Kan aba!
Bra, Ɔwo a woehyira Wo,
Nyame No dɔ Ba no;
Halleluya!
Yedzi W'ekyir kohu dan a 
Enye hɛn bedzidzi mu no.

MHB 255
3 . Afei ma ɔsor nyina ntonton Wo,
Nyimpa nye abɔfo ntow Wo ndwom;
Hom mfa sanku a ɔyɛ dɛw;
Hom mfa bobaa hyɛnhyɛnn nkɔ hɔ,
Beebi a yenye adwontofo a wonnwu,
Abɔfo a woetwa ahengua n' ho;
Enyi nnhunii, aso
So mpo nnyaa nntsee nn-siei,
Dza ɔyɛ hɛndze;
Naaso yedzi dɛw na yɛtow
Wo hɛn dɛw ho ndwom daa nyina.

MHB 256
1 . EKAN bi wɔ koko no do na da no yɛ adzekyee,
Ber a hɛn enyi bohu ahoɔfɛw Hen no N'enyimnyam;
Yɛberɛe wɔ hɛn atweɔnee m', yɛweɔnee kɔr ekyir dodow,
Naaso No konyim da no reba na yɛdze ndwom behyia N'.

MHB 256
2 . Woraba kan a ɔrepa no mu yehu dɛ adze rekye;
Nyimpa hɔn kandzea ayɛ kusuww wɔ adzekyee hyɛnhyɛn n' mu;
Na boka wimu regyegye ber a nsumaa mu gya rehyerɛn n'
Ma nyimpa akoma dze ɔpɛ kɛse rowosow yi.

MHB 256
3 . Enyisun kommyɛ bi ɔnye dzinnyɛ bi so wɔ wimu
Na Nyankopɔn ahom bi keka no ho wɔ ndam mpaabɔ m',
'Siandɛ Jesus a oruwu n' nye Christ a ɔtse egua n' do
Na hɛn sunsum n'amandzehu yɛ No so N'amandzehu.

MHB 256
4 . Orububu mpampi nyina egu, orubue kwan no mu;
Ɔrefrɛ N'abɔfoe no dɛ wombuebue adzekyee mbobow n';
Mbom ha abɔfo no yɛ nyimpa, nnyɛ ɔsor dze a 
wɔhyerɛn no a,
Na No nsordaafo akyen ndze nyɛ dɛ dza hɛn akoma bɔtow.

MHB 256
5 . Tsie! Yɛtse ndwom fi ekyirkyir, n'ano dzen ara na ɔyɛ,
Ɔyɛ Jesus hɛn Hen Immanuel no konyimdzi ho ndwom;
Zion, soɛr na kehyia No; na me kra, wo so yɛ ntsɛm fa w'
Ndwom a ɔyɛ dɛw mapa, na ɔsom wo bo, brɛ hɛn Hen!

MHB 257
1 . O bra, O bra Immanuel, 
Na bɔpɔn ndɔmmum Israel,
Ɔka mmɔn ananabea ha
Kodu dɛ Nyame Ba bɛba.
 
Dzi dɛw! Dzi dɛw! Immanuel 
Bɛba wo nkyɛn, O Israel.

MHB 257
2 . O bra, O bra, Wura Tumfo, 
Ɔwo a tsetse n' edze mbra
Maa mbusuakuw wɔ Sinai do
Wɔ fua, hu, nye ahentum mu.

MHB 257
3 . O bra jesse Poma, bɛgye 
Wo man fi Satan tum ase;
Gye Wo nkorɔfo fi hɛll bun mu,
Ma hɔn konyimdzi wɔ wu do.

MHB 257
4 . O bra, Adzekyee Woraba
Ma wo mbae nkyenyan hɛn sunsum;
Bɔbɔ anago sum hwetse,
Bɔ owu sunsuma petse.

MHB 257
5 . O bra, David Saafee, O bra, 
Bue hɛn sor fie pataa ma hɛn,
Yɛ kwan a wɔdze kɔ sor n' sɔnn,
Na siw dza ɔdze mbusu ba n'.

MHB 258
1 . Ɔwo reba, reba ampa;
Yebehyia Wo wɔ kwan do,
Yebohu Wo, yebohu W' yie,
Yebehyira W', yɛbɛma eehu,
Hɛn akoma nnkotum aka;
Ndwom dɛɛdɛw na yɛbɔtow,
Yɛdze hɛn dɔ bɛma Wo,
Yɛbɔtow ayɛyi ndwom
Wɔ Woara W'ananadze hɔ.

MHB 258
2 . O hɛn Wura dɔfo, hɛn dɛw nye
Yehu W' dɛ eyɛ ɔhen!
Tɛkyerɛma nyina tonton Wo dzin,
Yɛbɔ anosɛɛ dze ɔsom,
Enyidzi, nyam na nhyira brɛ W';
Hɛn Ewuradze na Nyɛnko,
Ɔhen a wɔasam mu eyi,
Wiadze ekyirkyir nyina,
Wɔhyɛ W' enyimnyam, sɔr Wo!

MHB 259
1 . ANA aba rebɛnye hɛn atsena,
Hɛn Hen, hɛn Gyafo, hɛn Ewuradze?
Ana Wo dzin dze Emmanuel,
Nyame nye Ne wiadze abɔ m'?

MHB 259
2 . Wiadze enya Wo ho enyigye!
Hamu na kurow minstsiminti;
Amamio do na mbrɛ hɔ yɛ 
Kɔnn bɛyɛ tsenabea ama nyimpa.

MHB 259
3 . Edze hɔn nyina aba bio;
Wo mu wɔ kan, bea na ahom
Ma dza oye, yɛ dɔ, dzi n' ho do,
Ma wɔdze eenya nkwa prɔmprɔmyɛ.

MHB 259
4 . Akoma biara n'esumasɛm;
Apɛdze na etumayɛdze;
Dza ɔbra mmpotsi ho nkyerɛ nyina
Da edzi dɛ onnsuro afɔbu.

MHB 259
5 . Wo daa ahendzi nnkɔbɔ adze;
Wo mfesi pi, yɛ dɛw, na nyaa;
W'asomdwee wiadze kɛse 'i mu
Nyiren kumaa biara hyerɛn.

MHB 259
6 . Afei beyi Wo nkorɔfo yaw,
Na fa Wo ndɔmmum ka Wo ho;
Wiadze na akoma Agyenkwa,
Bra, yaw do konyimdzifo, bra.   Amen.

MHB 26
1 . ABƆFO a hom hyerɛn a
Hom gyina Nayme nyimfa,
Na sɛ hom Wura hyɛ hom a,
Hom tu fa kan mu no,
Hom ennsuo mu a,
Yerunntum nntow
Ɔsor ndwom a 
Ɔyɛ dzen no.

MHB 26
2 . Hom akra a hom rohom,
Hom hu hom Agyenkwa enyim,
N'enyimnyam m' dza osuar mpo
Bor hɛn adom do koraa.
Hom ntow ayɛyi
Ndwom mma Nyame,
Dɛ mbrɛ hom yɛ
Wɔ N'enyim no.

MHB 26
3 . Hom ahotsewfo pa a 
 Hom berɛ wɔ asaase do,
Hom ntonton hom sor Hen,
Ber a hom kɔ kan no;
Hom ntow dɛw ndwom,
Hom ngye dza ɔma.
Yie muo, bɔn mu o,
Hom nyi N'ayɛw.

MHB 26
4 . Me kra yɛ w'afamudze,
Dzi konyim Nyame mu,
Na siesie w'akoma.
Wo nkwa nda nyina
Kesi ewiei,
Dza ɔma biara.
Yi No ayɛw.	Amen.

MHB 260
1 . M'ENYI ehu Ewuradze Ne mbae no ho enyimnyam;
Orikyi nsa beebi a wɔdze ebufuw wenyin gu n o;
Oesian Ne nkrantsee hoɔharfo huuhu no n'enyinam no
No nokwar no ritsim.

MHB 260
2 . Oenya obɔ totorbɛnto a ɔnnkɛsam akofo ekyir da,
Ɔresa nyimpa akoma mu wɔ 
N'atsembugua no enyim;
O me kra, yɛ ntsɛm kɛma no mbuae;
M'anan, huruhuruw!
Hɛn Nyame rutu ntsen.

MHB 260
3 . Wɔwoo Christ sukooko fɛɛfɛw no mu wɔ po ekyir hɔ,
Ɔwɔ 'nyam wɔ No bo mu a ɔbɛsesa emi nye ɔwo;
Owui tseew nyimpa ho ntsi ma
yɛntsena ase mma hɔn ahotɔ,
Ber a Nyame rutu ntsen.

MHB 261
1 . HƆN a wɔda wuso Kandzea,
Bra na fa Wo dɔ n' dɛpam
Owu nye no sum kebii no,
Ma mununkum no nhwetse;
Sor na asaase fofor Bɔfo,
Soɛr wɔ hɛn sum kebii mu,
Na hwetse abɔdze sum nyina,
Na ma hɛn enyi nhu adze.

MHB 261
2 . Yɛrotweɔn Wo mbae no ara;
Wo kan mbrɛ hɛn nkwa na dɛw,
Ɔmpam nhɛn suro nyinara,
Ɔmfa dɛw nhɛn hɛn akoma m'
Bra na bɛda enyimpa no a
Nyame dze ma adasa edzi;
Bra, wiadze nyina Agyenkwa,
Fa asɛmpa adom no bra.

MHB 261
3 . Fa W'ehumbɔbɔr no gye hɛn,
Ɔhen a edwe koraa;
Ma hɛn n-kwagye ho nyimdzee
Fa hɛn bɔn nyina kyɛ hɛn,
Na W'amayɛ adom no ntsi
Soɛ akra a wɔaberɛ nyina;
Sunsum a wɔnenam nyina
Gye hɔn kɔ W'asomdwee mu.  Amen.

MHB 262
1 . NDAASE nka Nyame,
Ɔno na ɔpetse
N'adom beberee no
Gu No nkowaa a wɔwɔ wiadze nyinara do 
Nyia ɔma konyim n',
Hom nyi No ayɛw,
Oewie dwuma n' dzi;
Enyidzi nye enyimnyam nka Jesus nko!

MHB 262
2 . Hɛn konyim Wura
N'asɛm edzi mu,
Ɔnoara edzi nyim
Na ɔawosow hɛll ahenman no dzendzen,
Oeyi N'abasa,
Oesiesie No dɔm;
Ɔakyerɛ N'enyimnyam
Dze edzi N'amandzehu tum ho dase.

MHB 262
3 . Oebue abobow n'
Ama ehiafo,
Ɔagye hɔn wɔ bɔn m',
Ɔama ndwaman na atowgyefo aba m';
Wɔastse enyigye ndze,
Woenya fahodzi,
Eguambaa n' bɔgyaa m';
Woenya fakyɛ pii wɔ Jesus Ne dzin mu.

MHB 262
4 . Ana yɛnnkɔtow
Hɛn Agyenkwa Hen ndwom?
Yedzi Wo dase,
Yɛdze enyigye dze hɛn nkwage to Wo do,
'Wo Jesus, ehyira,
Agyedzifo adɔr,
Na yɛdze ndaase
Ka dɛ mbɔbɔrhu m' nko na wɔdze akyɛ hɛn.

MHB 262
5 . No Sunsum kenyan
No ndwuma wɔ hɛn mu;
N'adom anwanwadze n',
Ɔyɛɛ no tsetseber mu ma ɔboor do,
Nkyɛ nyimpa eehu
Ne nsɛnkyerɛdze no,
Wɔaagye hɛn Agyenkwa n',
Na woeefua fakyɛ na asomdwee nsɛmpa n' mu.

MHB 262
6 . Hɛn nyina Agyenkwa,
Erefrɛ abɔn a
Wɔafom ɔkwan no;
O ma wontum nnya ɔman kor wɔ da kor!
Na afei ma Wo
Ho nyimdzee ntserɛw
Wiadze mbea nyina,
Na Nyame enyimnyam nhyɛ wiadze nyina ma.   Amen.

MHB 263
1 . MBRƐ ogya kɛse n' si dzɛw a!
Adom nserama na ɔsɔe,
Jesus dɔ tɔ aman mu,
Ma ne nyina dzɛw framfram,
Ɔdze ogya baa wiadze;
Wɔsɔɔ no wɔ akoma m',
O nkyɛ nyimpa nyina eenya gya n'\n
Na woeenya enyimnyam dɛw n' bi.

MHB 263
2 . Ɔhyɛɛ edwuma no ase n',
Nna wonnyaa nntsee Ne nka;
Sesei asɛm no etu ntsen
Na ɔretserɛw kɔ mbea pii;
Ogu do petse na onyin
Kɔ ahoɔdzen konyimdzi mu;
Obubu bɔn akoban,
Wosow hɛll aponkɛse n'.

MHB 263
3 . Nyame mba, hom nyi Agyenkwa ayɛw;
Oebue abow no petee,
Ɔaka adom asɛm no,
Wɔahyɛ asɛm n'enyimnyam
Jesus wɔ tum dɛ ɔgye hɛn,
Ɔno nko dzii dwuma no;
Nyia N'asɛm bɔɔ wiadze no,
N'edwuma nyina dzi mu.

MHB 263
4 . Ennhu mununkum kumaa
Dɛ nsakum a ɔwɔ wimu no?
Sesei ɔatserɛw wɔ wimu,
Kata asaase nyina do
Hwɛ! Anohoba mpetsema
Fi sor rososɔ dada;
Ɔnnkɛkyɛr na Ewuradze ehue
No dɔ Sunsum no nyina!

MHB 264
1 . Hwɛ! Ɔdze mununkum risian, 
Nyia da bi ɔtɔɔr hɛn ntsi n';
Ahotsewfo mpempem ka ho,
Dzi N' ekyir kumbɔɔ reba:
Alleluia!
Nyame reba ebedzi hen.

MHB 264
2 . Enyienyi nyina bohu No 
Dɛ oewuna ahentar wusuww;
Hɔn a woemmbu N' bi, wɔtɔɔn No n',
Wopirapiraa N', bɔɔ N' mbeamudua mu n'
Wobotwa ewuo,
Da a wobohu Messiah n'.

MHB 264
3 . N' amandzehu ho nsɛnkyerɛdze 
Da ho ara wowɔ No ho;
Dza N' asomfo a wɔapon hɔn no
Dzi ho ehurusi daa n';
Yɛdze dɛw bɛn
Bɔhwɛ enyimnyam etua n'.

MHB 264
4 . Ɔnyɛ hɔ! nkorɔfo nyina mbu W' ntwɛr 
Wo domankoma ahengua n' enyim;
Gyefo, gye tum na enyimnyam no,
Gye ahendzi n' yɛ Wodze;
Alleluia!
Onnyiewiei Nyankopɔn, sian!

MHB 265
1 . MBOBOW pa, hom mma hom tsir do,
Ndadzeban, hom mbuebue,
Mom mma Enyimnyan Hen no mbɛsen;
Mbeamudua n' wɔ akono.

MHB 265
2 . Tseasefo Nyame N'akofo,
No nsordaafo krɔnkrɔn,
Hom ngyinangyina hom gyinabea,
Mbrɛ anan nntsiaa hɔ da.

MHB 265
3 . Hom suar na hom ahoɔdzen suar dze,
Hom Sahen N'ahoɔdzen m',
Hom nkedzi nyim nsaase nyina do;
Ne nyina bɛyɛ Nedze.

MHB 265
4 . Mma hom nnsuro, hom nntɔ bahaw;
Hom nko dɛ mbarimba;
Aman nyina bɔkotow Christ,
Nye hom atow ndwom yi.

MHB 265
5 . Ayewa mbobow n' ebuebue;
Ndadzeban n' ebuebue;
Hwɛ, Enyimnyam Hen no resen!
Mbeamudua n' edzi nyim.

MHB 266
1 . FI kwaam' 'naafo, boka, na anee,
Dabɛn na hͻn a wͻahwer nhyira
Hͻn nyina benya daa ahomgye
Wͻ Christ Wo mu?

MHB 266
2 . Dabɛn na 'sukwankyɛba man
Dze Asɛmpa kandzea bɛdzɛw
Na nyimpa eh nyina hͻn Pomfo
Wͻ Christ, Wo mu?

MHB 266
3 . Dabɛn na anaafo mpoano nyina
Mu dͻm a wͻapon hͻn nyinara
Bͻsoɛr na wͻahoahoa hͻnho
Wͻ Christ Wo mu?

MHB 266
4 . Dabɛn na boka nsaase n' do
Anhweahyew nkurow mu nyimpa
Bɛna hͻn nsa do wͻ som mu.
Ama Wo, Christ?

MHB 266
5 . Dabɛn na wiadzefo befi
Sum no mu aba kan no mu,
Na ͻkra biara benya daa
Kan wͻ Wo mu?

MHB 266
6 . Ewuradze, ma nkͻnhyɛ ber n’ mbra;
Tsetse ahenkyɛw na nhyiren n’.
Obiara benya guandͻbea.
Fie wͻ Wo mu.

MHB 267
1 . EWURADZE, W'asɔr no roweɔn;
Dabɛn na wiadze betsie W'?
Dabɛn na anafua su botwa?
Bɔhyɛ da n' bɛba dabɛn?
Hwɛ dɛ ndɔbaa ber enya edu
Rotweɔn apaafo n' ara!
Wo Ba N'ahoguan no yɛɛ kwa?
Hoɔdzenfo mfa asadze.

MHB 267
2 . Wɔdze nsɛmpa n' ama obiara,
Naaso mpempem nnyaa nntsee koraa;
Obi annka a, aso wɔbɛtse?
Owura Tumfo, ka asɛm no;
Ka asɛm no; aman nyina mu,
Ma asɛmpa abɛn nhɛn;
Ngye wiadze nyina nkwagye
Dase nkesi wiadze ano.

MHB 267
3 . Ewiei no, W'asɔr dzi mu a,
Hɔn a eyi hɔn nyina bɛba m'
Nye hɔn Hen n' atsena 'nyimnyam mu,
Wɔakyekyer abɔnsam na bɔn;
Osu, ɔkɔm awerɛhow,
Owu na yaw nnyi hɔ bio;
Hwɛ! W'asɔr so roweɔn ara;
Owur Jesus, bedzi hen!

MHB 268

MHB 269

MHB 27
1 . ABƆFO krɔnn,

MHB 27

MHB 270
1 . CHRIST wɔ m'akoma mu pɛ dɛ

Mo sor Hen N'enyimnyam ho ndwom.

MHB 270

Na ɔdɔ ahyɛ W'akoma m' ma;

Na yɛka dɛ amayɛ dzi wɔ W'.

MHB 271
1 . HOM nhyɛ Eguambaa N' 'henkyɛw 
Wɔ N'ahengua no do;
Tsie! Sor ndwom n'ahyɛ ndwom nyina do,
No ndwom n' nko na wɔtse,
Me kra, nyan na tow ndwom
Ma Nyia owui maa wo n',
Na hua N' dɛ ɔyɛ wo Hen tsitsir
Wɔ mbersantsen nyina mu.

MHB 271
2 . Hom nhyɛ nkwa Wura 'henkyɛw,

N'enyimnyam na yɛtow;
Owui na ɔfoow sor,
Ɔdze onnyiewiei nkwa brɛ hɛn;
Oedzi owu do, tse ase.

MHB 271

N'ahendzi nnkɔbɔ adze,
Na N'epiranan no ho n',
Paradise nhyiren fɛɛfɛw gugu,
Na oyi hua daa nyina.

MHB 271
4 . Hom nhyɛ No ɔdɔ Hen;
Hom nhwɛ N' nsa nye Ne mfemu
N'ekur a wɔda ho hu n' sor no,
Wɔahyɛ no enyinmyam,
Hom nyina nhua Pomfo n'!
Ɔwo iwui maa me;
W'ayɛyi na Wo ''nyam nnkɛpa
Wɔ mbersantsen nyina mu.   Amen.

MHB 273

MHB 278
1 . FA hɛn suro na haw,
Na hɛn nyinsuwa kɔ;
Sunsum no aba,

MHB 278
2345678 Jesus Ne dasefo n' asan kɔ Ne fie.

. Hɛn Wura No bɔhyɛ a
Ɔdze ama No sor n'
Fi wimu ebodu;
Ɔka kyerɛ hɛn dɛ wɔakrɔn hɛn Hen wɔ sor.

. Hɛn Dzimafo n' nam
N' bɔgyaa na mpaabɔ m'
Enya akyɛdze no,
Ɔaserɛ enya Werɛkyekyefo n' ama hɛn.

. Hɛn enyimanyan Hen n'
Ehue N' Sunsum ma
Ɔabɛnye N 'dɔm atsena,
Na onnkeyi No efi hɔn mu ara bio.

. Hɛn sor Kwankyerɛfo
Nye hɛn bɛtsena,
Akyekye hɛn werɛ,
Na ɔdze No dɔ ahenman aba hɛn akoma m'.

. Gyedzi akoma
Nya N'ahenman no,
No tum, N'asomdwee,
No nkwa, na N'enyigye mbordo afebɔɔ.

. Hom mma yendzi dɛw
Akoma nye ndze m',
Yɛmfa hɛn Wura,
Na yɛmbɔ ose ber a yɛnam sar no do.

. Hom nye Sunsum no
Ntu nkɔ sor Zion,
Hom nsoɛr konyimdzi mu,
Hom nye hɛn Nyame nnantsew nkɔ ɔsor fie.

MHB 279
1 . SUNSUM Krɔnkrɔn, Nyame,
Ahoɔfɛw yɛ Wodze;
Dza ɔso na dza osuar nyina wɔ W' mu,
Wimu yɛ W'asɔr dan.

MHB 279
2 . Ewia a ofir Nyame,
Nyimpa na nhyiren nkwa,
Nyansa na ahoɔdzen a ɔdze Wo
Tum hyɛ wiadze nyina ma.

MHB 279
3 . Ɔwo nye ɔdɔ bura,
Koryɛ Nyame nye wo;
Apapafo yɛ kor Wo mu,
Na wɔhyerɛn Wo kan mu.

MHB 279
4 . Ahotseweefo na
Wɔbɛyɛɛ W'asomafo;
Na kandzea a wɔkyerɛ wiadze kwan n',
Wɔsɔɔ no Wo gya n' mu.

MHB 279
5 . Nkra a ɔba hɛn nkyɛn no
Nam Wo mframa mu ba;
Kan a ɔhyerɛn hɛn adaaso ekyir no
Yɛ biribi a adwen ho.

MHB 279
6 . Yɛserɛ fɛkuwbɔ,
'Dɔ, dɛw na asomdwee mu
Ma yeenyin nyimdzee na ahoɔdzen m',
Na Wo ho nyansa mu.  Amen.

MHB 28
1 . Hɛn Nyame N' abɔdze nyina, 
Hom mma hom ndze do nye hɛn ntow
Alleluia, Alleluia!
Ewia hyeehyew, 'hyerɛn dɛ sika,
Bosoom nwinwin, 'tse dɛ dwetε,
      Yi N' ayɛw, yi N' ayɛw 
      Alleluia, Alleluia, Alleluia!

MHB 28
2 . M-frama a itu ehum dzendzen, 
Esuwusiw a esen wimu,
Yi N' ayɛw, Alleluia!
Bosoom, fa enyigye yi N' ayɛw,
N-woraba, hom mbɔ hom ndzem'
      Yi N' ayɛw, yi N' ayɛw 
      Alleluia, Alleluia, Alleluia!

MHB 28
3 . N-su krɔngyenn a erepem, 
Tow ndwom ma w' Ewuradze ntse,
Alleluia, Alleluia!
Ogya hurenhuren a eyɛ dzen,
'Wo a ema nyimpa hyew na kan,
     Yi N' ayɛw, yi N' ayɛw 
     Alleluia, Alleluia, Alleluia!

MHB 28
4 . Asaase pa a Nyame ama 
Daa daa iyi siar ma ne mba,
Yi N' ayɛw, Alleluia!
Wo mu nhyiren nye nduaba so,
Womfifir nkyerɛ N' enyimnyam, 
    Yi N' ayɛw, yi N' ayɛw 
    Alleluia, Alleluia, Alleluia!

MHB 28
5 . N-korɔfo a hom 'koma dwe nyina, 
Na hom dze bɔn kyɛ, hom so mbra,
Hom so ntow Alleluia!
Amandzehufo, 'werɛhofo,
Hom nyi N' ayɛw, mfa ne nyina nsoa N',
    Yi N' ayɛw, yi N' ayɛw 
    Alleluia, Alleluia, Alleluia!

MHB 28
6 . Ao, Owu, yamuyiefo a edwe, 
'Wo a itwa hɛn owu ngyam do,
Yi N' ayɛw, Alleluia!
'Wo na 'dze Nyame mba kɔ fie,
Hɛn Wura Christ faa wo kwan n' mu:
   Yi N' ayɛw, yi N' ayɛw 
   Alleluia, Alleluia, Alleluia!

MHB 28
7 . Ndzɛmba nyina nhyira Bɔfo n', 
Wɔmfa mbrɛhoadze nkotow No,
Nyi N' ayɛw, Alleluia!
Wɔmfa ayɛyi mma Egya, nye Ba,
Nye Sunsum no, Ebiasa Kor, 
   Yi N' ayɛw, yi N' ayɛw 
   Alleluia, Alleluia, Alleluia!

MHB 280
1 . MOHWEHWƐ Sunsum tum wɔ m' mu,
Ɔdɔ na adwen pa dze n' bi,
Tum a medze bedzi bɔn do;
Dɔ a medze bɔdɔ W' na adasa
Ahosan a yaw nntum nnka no,
Na owu mu mpo ɔyɛ dzen.

MHB 280
2 . Dabɛn na mebɛtse ndze no,
Dza anokwafo nko tse no?
Fakyɛ, asomdwee na enyigye
Nye Ɔwerɛkyekyefo no nam;
O bra, na tsenenenee krɔnkrɔn
Christ na N'adze nyina bɛyɛ m'dze.

MHB 280
3 . O nkyɛ Werɛkyekyefo no aaba
Na oeenntwa mu aannkɔ ara da,
Na mbom ɔaayɛ N' tsenabew wɔ m' mu
Ma ɔmfa m'akoma nyɛ Nedze,
Na ɔmfa No dɔ n' ntsena mo mu
Ma menyɛ Nyame W'asɔrfi.

MHB 280
4 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, kenyan m'akoma,
Dzi dase dɛ wɔawo m'fofor;
Fa ogya bonuma me sesei
Amma W'akyɛdze aannyɛ gyan,
Munnkotum atsena bɔnfakyɛ m' daa;
M'bɛyɛ dɛn akɔ heaven hɔ?

MHB 280
5 . Nsewhyɛdze a ɔkyerɛ dɛ 
Meenya ahenman no wɔ hen?
Mepɛ dɛ m'tse nsɔwano n' nka,
Onyame No dɔ nsewhyɛ no;
Hue ɔsor dɔ amayɛ no
Gu m'akoma mu nyinara.  Amen.

MHB 281
1 . ME kra, mma nnkɔhwehwɛ No koraa,
Innkohu No wɔ hɔ;
Onnyi asaase ase sum mu,
Onnyi ɔsor mframa mu.

MHB 281
2 . Sunsum no egua nnyi ekyir,
Na ɔbɛn hɛn wɔ ha ara;
Ɔwɔ akoma biara mu;
Na ɔtweɔn dɛ wobohu N'.

MHB 281
3 . Adwen nye adwen dzi ehyia
Na ɔkra nye ɔkra bɔ awɛ;
Nyia ɔnnhwehwɛ Nyame Noara n' mu n',
Onnkohu N' ara da.

MHB 281
4 . Na sɛ enyidoadzehu no,
Fi wo mu ara ba a,
Nyame N' Sunsum bɛhyɛ wiadze ma,
Na N'enyimnyam bɛhyerɛn.

MHB 281
5 . Ɔwo rinnhia mfɛfo ara da,
'Rennyɛ ankonam da,
Nyame a ɔtsena hɛn mu n' bɛka w' ho,
Na ɔakyerɛ wo dza ɔpɛ.

MHB 281
6 . Akyɛdze mapa nye adom,
Dɛ Nyankopɔn bɛpen
Ayɛ w'akoma N'atsenae,
Na ɔayɛ wo Nyɛnko!

MHB 282
1 . NYANSA Sunsum, yi hɛn enyi
Fi wiadze egyangyandze do
Kɔ ɔsor nokwar do;
Nokwar ntseasee Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn,
Fa W'sor kan no hyɛ hɛn akra ma
Wɔnhwehwɛ ɔsor ndzɛmba.

MHB 282
2 . Sunsum fotufo, kyerɛ hɛn kwan;
Dua aperdzi do kyerɛkyerɛ hɛn 
Ma yennya sor ahenkyɛw;
'Kokodur Sunsum, fa Wo tum
Ma hɛn wɔ hɛn nsɔhwɛ ber mu,
Na ɔmma yengyaa bɔn yɛ.

MHB 282
3 . Nyimdzee Sunsum, gya hɛn anan
Fa W'akwan a mbusu nnyi m' no do,
Mbrɛ abɔfo fa no;
Hɔ na ebɛyɛ hɛn hwɛfo sɔnn,
Ɔdwe Sunsum a eyɛ krɔnn,
Ama yaabɛn Nyame.

MHB 282
4 . Nyankopɔn suro ho Sunsum, 
Hɛn abrabɔ nyina mu, twe bɛn,
Wɔ hɛn akoma mu;
Fa obu krɔnkrɔn hyɛ hɛn akoma m',
Ma yɛnsom No, yendzi Ne pɛ
Tsenenee turodoo n' do.

MHB 282
5 . Gya hɛn asomdwee na ɔko m'
Kodu nkwa a onnyi ewiei no mu,
Na yeenya hɛn akatua;
Ama yaako hɛn bra mu ko,
Yaayɛ dzen wɔ Wo tum no mu,
Yɛnye Christ eedzi hen.

MHB 283
1 . Ansaana hɛn Gyefo siarfo 
Nye hɛn ridzi mpaamu n',
Ogyaa hɛn Ɔkwankyerɛfo dɛ
Ɔnye hɛn ntsena.

MHB 283
2 . Ɔbae wɔ ebubur suban mu, 
Dɛ ɔatrɛ n' atsabanm',
Ɔdze dɔ na asomdwee boguu
No nkorɔfo do.

MHB 283
3 . Ɔdze ogya ngyrama bae dɛ 
Ɔrebɛkyerɛkyerɛ hɛn;
Ɔtse dɛ mframa, ɔyɛ dzen,
Na wonnhu so.

MHB 283

MHB 283
5 . Ne ndze na yɛtse no bi 
Dɛ ewimbir mframa n';
Osiw mfomso kwan,
Ka sor ho nsɛm.

MHB 283

Konyim biara a yedzi,
Adwen krɔnkrɔn biara a yenya,
Ofir Noara.

MHB 283

Hwɛ hɛn mberɛwyɛ tsemam';

MHB 284

MHB 288

MHB 289

MHB 29
1 . NDZEMBA nyina nyi Ewuradze ayɛw;
Sor na asaase, po na wimu,
Eyɛe hyɛɛ Woho enyimnyam,
Dze daa Wo kɛseyɛ edzi
Yɛdze som nyina brɛ Wo;
Yɛnye adze nyina yi W'ayɛw.

MHB 29
2 . Adze nyina yi W'ayɛw 'nago,
Wɔtow kan adwom kommyɛ mu;
Woyi W'ayɛw 'dzekyee nyina,
Ewiaber wɔkyerɛ Wo tum;
Ber na bea riyi W'ayɛw,
Yɛnye adze nyina yi W'ayɛw.

MHB 29
