Nhaban na ndowa hɔn dede,
Yɛnye adze nyina yi W' ayɛw.

MHB 29

Yɛnye hɔn hyɛ W' enyimnyam.

MHB 29

Yɛkotow W'ananadze,
Yɛma akoma do yi W' ayɛw. 
Yɛnye adze nyina yi W' ayɛw.  Amen.

MHB 290

MHB 291
1 . SUNSUM Domfo, nye me ntsena!
Emi so m'bɛyɛ adom ba,
Na medze nkuranhyɛ nsɛm 
Bɛda Wo bra edzi mo mu,
Na medze ɔbrɛfo ndzeyɛɛ
Bɛkasa ama m' Gyefo Christ.

MHB 291
2 . Sunsum Nokwafo, nye m' ntsena!
Mo so m' bɛyɛ nokwafo.
Na medze nyansa mapa
Bɛda Wo bra edzi mo mu,
Na medze enuadɔ ndzeyɛɛ
Beyi m' Wura N' nokwardzi akyerɛ.

MHB 291
3 . Sunsum Brɛfo, nye me ntsena!
Emi so m' bɛyɛ brɛfo;
M'akoma bɔmonsom dɛ nhyiren
Wɔ nsɔhwɛber sunkamm n' mu;
Obobue ber a ewia abɔ,
Na m' benya No dɔ no huam.

MHB 291
4 . Sunsum Tumfo, nye me ntsena!
Emi so m' bɛyɛ tumfo,
Medze tum bedzi konyim
Ber a nyimpa ahom dzi kogu;
Medze tum enyidado
Bɔkɔ enyim daa egyina.

MHB 291
5 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, nye me ntsena!
Emi so m' bɛyɛ krɔnkrɔn;
M'bɛtsew moho efi bɔn ho,
M'bɔtɔ akɔ dza oye nko ho,
Medze dza m'benya biara
Bɛma nyia ɔdze W' maa me.

MHB 292
1 . SUNSUM Krɔnkrɔn, sor Ebubur, bra,
Fa Wo nkenyan tum nyina,
Sɔ ɔdɔ krɔnkrɔn gya n' ano
Hɛn akoma nwinwin yi m'.

MHB 292
2 . Yɛtow hɛn daa daa ndwom no kwa,
Yɛper dɛ yɛsɔr kwa;
Hosanna nenam hɛn anomu,
Na hɛn ayɛyi ewu.

MHB 292
3 . Na yɛbɛtsena owu gyangyan
Tsebea yi m' afebɔɔ?
Hɛn dɔ yɛ mberɛw, ɔyɛ nwin ma W',
Wodze n' so ma hɛn dɛ!

MHB 292
4 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, sor Ebubur, bra,
Fa Wo nkenyan tum nyina;
Fa Agyenkwa N' dɔ n' petse hɛn do!
Na onkenyan hɛndze.  Amen.

MHB 293
1 . SUNSUM Bɔfo; Ɔwo a ahyɛse
Etoow wiadze fapem n' pintsinn,
Bra adwen a ɔrotweɔn biara mu,
Fa W'enyigye ma adasa,
Gye hɛn fi bɔn na awerɛhow mu,
Na ma W'asɔrfi mfata Wo.

MHB 293
2 . Ɔhyew a wɔammbɔ farbaa,
Kyigyinafo a Egya n' dze maa hɛn,
Bura na gya krɔnkrɔn mprɛnsa;
Fa sor dɔ kenyan hɛn akoma;
Bra, na fa Wo ngo krɔnkrɔn no
Bɛtsew hɛn ho ber a yɛtow ndwom.

MHB 293
3 . Ɔwo a adom ahyɛ W' ma, fi sor sian,
Fa Wo mpɛn esuon tum no bra,
Ɔwo nye No tum nsa ahoɔdzen a 
Odzi sor na asaase do tum;
Guar na tsew hɛn nyimpadua ho,
Na fa Wo su hyɛ hɛn akoma m'.

MHB 293
4 . Yɛ ndzɛmba fofor hyɛ pɛ do,
Brɛ hɛn akra asoɔdzenfo adze;
Ma hɛn nsa nka daa nokwar no,
Yɛmfa hɛn gyedzi nyɛ edwuma;
Fa Woho ma hɛn ma yenhu,
Egya na Ba no wɔ Wo mu.

MHB 293
5 . Enyimnyam nye abɔdzin a ɔnnsa
Ɔnka Egya Tumfo Ne dzin;
Wɔnhyɛ Agyenkwa, Ba enyimnyam,
Nyia owui dze gyee nyimpa nkwa n',
Na Wo so n-tonton nka Wo,
Ɔwo daa Ɔwerɛkyekyefo.  Amen.

MHB 294
1 . ƆSOR Ebubur krɔnkrɔn, bra,
Bɛsera akoma werɛhonyi,
Beyi m'afɔdzi adzesoa,
Na fa awerɛhyɛmu brɛ me !
Wo nko na ibotum asoɛ
Ɔbɔnfo a no bɔn ahyɛ n' do,
Ama wɔaagye no ato mu,
Dze bɔgya n' aapetse n'akoma m'.

MHB 294
2 . Sɛ tsetse n' enye me peree,
Dɛ ebɛgye me efi bɔn ho,
Ebɔɔ mbɔdzen dɛ edze Wo dɔ
Bɛdaadaa me na atwe me a,
Kenyan W'ehumbɔbɔr ndwuma;
Ma Wo mbɔbɔrhu no ndɔɔ so,
Meserɛ, kɔ do na dzi aper
Kodu dɛ m'begyaa mu ama W'.

MHB 294
3 . Sɛ matse Wo frɛ no pɛn a,
Na misii nkrum dze gyee moho a,
Mepeen ɔpen a onnyi kabea,
Na pepɛɛ Wo mu enyigye a,
Hyɛ me pɛ a onndzi mu no ma;
Ma me tsibowa nhu W'asomdwee,
Kenyan me ma munhu W'adom,
Na ma mentse bɔnfatsɛ nka.

MHB 294
4 . Sɛ mama Wo werɛ ahow a,
Na medzi nkwaseasɛm ekyir a,
W'ehumbɔbɔr no agye me,
M'awerɛhow mu epegya me a,
Adom ehumbɔbɔr Sunsum,
Ma me ahotɔ bio, na gye
Mo sunsum wɔ krɔnkrɔnyɛ mu,
Ma n' do mma onnhu amandze bio.  Amen.

MHB 295
1 . SUNSUM siarfo a wͻsͻr Wo
Ka Egya na Asɛm no ho,
Nyame na Ewuradze kor:
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
10 . Ͻwo a eyɛ ͻdͻ krͻnkrͻn,
Ma hɛn W’akyɛdze nyina;
Mma mmfi hɛn nkyɛn ara da;
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
2 . Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, sor Ebubur,
Ͻbͻsu a isian fi sor, ’
N-kwa ahom, ͻdͻ gya:
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
3 . SunSum a ekyerɛ hɛn kwan,
Sunsum a ema sum yɛ kan,
Obi nntum nngyina Wo tum ano:
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
4 . Wo a Jesus fi N’egua do
Dze Wo mae dɛ bͻboa hɛn,
Amma yaannyɛ ankonam;
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
5 . Ku hɛn akͻndͻbͻn nyina;
Hyɛ hɛn asoadzen pɛ do;
Yesérɛ W’ nya abotar ma hɛn:
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
6 . Yehwe ase a, ma hɛn do,
Na hɛn kra tͻ efir mu a,
Fre hɛn bérɛww bra Wo nkyɛn bio;
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
7 . Bra bɛhyɛ mbérɛwyɛfo dzen;
Ma abrɛfo akokodur,
Kyérɛ hɛn ma yɛnkasa yie:
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
8 . Bra bͻboa akra a wͻpɛ
Esua Wo nokwar mapa n’,
Na woenya ͻdͻ pa no;
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 295
9 . Fa hɛn fa kwan tseabaa n’ mu.
Sɛ yɛfom a, bͻ hɛn kͻkͻ;
Yɛbͻ mpaa a, serɛ ma hɛn.
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, tsie hɛn.

MHB 296
1 . SUNSUM Krɔnkrɔn, hu m' mbɔbɔr,
Midzi yaw dɛ mafom Wo,
Murusu sesei yi dzi,
Tsie akoma a orusu n'.

MHB 296
10 . O hu me mbɔbɔr ara,
Afei midzi mo mu yaw,
Dza mayɛ etsia Wo Sunsum n',
Egya, fa kyɛ m' wɔ Ba n' mu.  Amen.

MHB 296
2 . Mo bɔn a ɔdɔɔ so pii n',
Meka ne nyina kyerɛ Wo;
Dza mayɛ etsia WO nko n',
Enyianyiakwa, Wo nko nyim.

MHB 296
3 . M'aso esiw wɔ Wo frɛ ho,
Me per mu mohwe ase daa,
Fa W'aba puw me kakra,
Na mammfa Nyame enndzi agor.

MHB 296
4 . Metakyeer edziban bɔn ho;
Masɔ ahwɛ dɛ Ewuradze ye;
Mema m'enyi do hwɛ wimu
Dze hwɛ dza Bɔadze bɛma.

MHB 296
5 . Wiadze dadwen hyɛ som ma;
Botae hun ka dwumadzi hyɛ,
Ahokyerɛ, ber a Nyame bɛn;
Akwadwer, ber a sum mba wu.

MHB 296
6 . 'Sɔryɛ nwinwin, apɛdze
Duum prɔwee gya tantan no;
'Mumuyɛ daadaa m'akoma,
 Ɔhyɛ Ɔwo a 'nyim n' awerɛhow.

MHB 296
7 . O mannda papa biara,
Dɛ mennsu mo mfom pii n' ho,
Mannhwehwɛ W'enyimtwuw no,
Mebu enyi egu Sunsum n' do.

MHB 296
8 . Minyan dwumadzi fofor do,
Yardɔm no wɔ mo wer mu;
Nyimpa enyi do sor bɔfo,
Kwatanyi wɔ Wo kan mu.

MHB 296
9 . Ma m' W'awerɛkyekyer no daa,
Dom me W'ayarsa no daa;
Soɛ mo mu abotar mu,
Idzi yaw, eso hyira m'.

MHB 297
1 . FA Wo mu nhyira kanea no
Bra hen su sunkamm no mu,
Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn a ’dzi mu,
’Wérɛkyekyer Nyame.

MHB 297
2 . Abͻnfo Wura, guar hɛn;
Yɛyar, yeafona, hyɛ hɛn dzen;
Yɛayew, gyedɛ etsen hɛn,
’Wérɛkyekyer Nyame.

MHB 297
3 . ‘W'asomdwee ba dɛ ͻbͻw:
Kyerɛ, hyɛ hɛn pɛ a ayew do,
Kͻ do bue Christ mu ndzɛmba,
’Wérɛkyekyer Nyame.

MHB 297
4 . Damfo a edwe krͻnkrͻnyi:
Si W’asͻrdan hɛn akoma m’,
Boa hɛn ma yɛntse Wo nka,
’Wérɛkyekyer Nyame.

MHB 297
5 . Dzi ntamugyina ma hɛn daa,
Na yɛmfa ndzé a wͻnntse mper
Hɛn ehiadzé a yenntum nnka.
’Wérɛkyekyer Nyame.

MHB 297
6 . Abba, Egya yɛtsea mu,
Ma yenya ͻsor hyira,
Onnyiewie ahyɛnsew no,
’Wérɛkyekyer Nyame.

MHB 298
1 . NYAME Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn;
Ber a ͻsɛ yi mu,
De mbrɛ Pentecost da n’ yɛe no,
Fa Wo tum nyina sian.

MHB 298
2 . Yɛdze koryɛ dzi ehyia
Wͻ bea a ahyɛ ama hɛn,
Yɛtweͻn hɛn Wura anohoba n’,
Adom nyina Sunsum no.

MHB 298
3 . Dɛ ehum kɛsé a ͻrobͻ
Wͻ asorɛkye n’ase,
Dze tum kenyan adwen nyina,
’Kra, atsenka ahom kor.

MHB 298
4 . Fa nyansa fi sor hyɛ
Mbaabun nye mpanyin ma;
Ma hɛn ’gya akoma nye gyirama,
Mfa nsͻr, nyi ayɛw, mfa ndͻ.

MHB 298
5 . Ekan Sunsum, hwehwɛ
Na pam isum fi hͻ;
Fa ahoͻdzen hyerɛn daa daa,
Kɛpem da pa no mu.

MHB 298
6 . Nokwar Sunsum, gye hɛn
Wͻ nkwa nye owu mu,
Sesei, Sunsum a awo hɛn,
Boa hɛn ma hɛn ho ntsew.

MHB 299
1 . BRA Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn, hyewbͻ gya,
Bra na fa dɛw bͻhom mo mu;
Dɛ pɛ dzendzen atwe W' aba 'i,
O bra bɛtsew m'akoma ho.
Si me kra m' asͻrfi wͻ hͻ.
Na fa W'nhotscw su tsim ha. '

MHB 299
2 . Mehaahaa bisa Wo dodow;
Sor ahom a ͻyɛ dzen yie,
Twe m’ pue ahotͻ dɛɛdɛw mu
Kɛpem dɛ me kra ayɛ Wodze;
‘Korsa po bun emunam mo do,
Na mayew Wo kokrokoyɛ m’.

MHB 299
3 . M’asomdwee, mo nkwa, m’ahotͻ,
M’akoradze nyina nye Woara,
M‘abayɛ ho dasefo pa,
Kurkye fakyɛ wͻ rn‘akoma m’,
Christ ntsi wͻdze mo bͻn akyɛ m’,
Dͻ ho enyimia, sor abͻbaado.

MHB 299
4 . Me Nyame bra, kyérɛ Wo wuodzi,
Ma n' enyimia kɛse wͻ sor, ,
Ondzi Wo ho dase pefee,
Ma mentse Wo nka wͻ mo mu,
Ma mo tum nyina nhu dɛ aba,
Na Woara yɛ dɛ nsͻwano pa.

MHB 3
1 . AMANAMAN, hom mfa dew nkotow 
Jehova ahengua huuhu enyim;
Hom nhu Ewuradze nko dɛ Nyame;
Ɔno na ɔbɔ na ono na Osɛɛ.

MHB 3
2 . N'ahentum no, onnhia hɛn mboa;
Ɔdze dɛtse nween hɛn nyimpa.
Yɛtse dɛ nguan a yɛtɔɔ gon n';
Ɔdze hɛn baa nguankuw n'mu bio.

MHB 3
3 . Yɛdze ndaase ndwom fum W'apon m',
Yɛma hɛn ndze do wɔ sorsor,
Na asaase dze ngyirama ɔpedu,
Dze ayeyi hyɛ W'abangua ma.

MHB 3
4 . W'ahyɛdze tserɛw tse dɛ wiadze
Wo dɔ so kodu mbersantsen,
Wo nokwar betsim dɛ botan,
Kodu Mbersantsen mfesantsen.

MHB 30
1 . EWURADZE, yefi enyimnyam m'kɔ'
 nyimnyam m' yi W'ayɛw;
Ntonton nka Wo dzin, ɔnka Egya
nye Sunsum no so,
Yefi ahom mu kɔ ahom m'
nantsew Zion kwan do,
Dze kopue Nyankopɔn enyim
wɔ kurow a adze nnsa mu da m'.

MHB 30
2 . Ndaase na enyimnyam, na ɔsom,
na nhyira nye ɔdɔ,
Akòma kor, na ndwom kor ;
  Nà ase nye sòr ahotsewfo wɔ,
O Ewuradze, daa daa nyina twe bɛn
W’asomfo,
Dua hɛn wiadze som do
    Siesie hɛn ma Wo sor edwuma.

MHB 300
1 . Nyame ahom, gu mo do; 
Hyɛ mo mu nkwa fofor,
Ma mondɔ dza Ɔwo edɔ
Na menyɛ dza eyɛ.

MHB 300
2 . Nyame ahom, gu mo do; 
Ma m' akoma mu ntsew,
Kɛpem dɛ menye W' nya pɛ kor
Dze sɔw fona, dze bɔ bra.

MHB 300
3 . Nyame ahom, gu mo do; 
Ma menyɛ Wodze koraa,
Kɛpem dɛ me nyimpadua mpo
Nyame kan bɛhyerɛn mu.

MHB 300
4 . Nyame ahom, gu mo do; 
Nna munnkowu ara da,
Na mbom menye Wo bɛtsena ase
Mber a onnyi ewiei mu.  Amen.

MHB 301
1 . PETSE Wo Sunsum gu asaase,
Asaase mfa tsénenee mfafor,
W’ahendzi mbra, ͻnka hɛll nhyɛ,
Na W’akomfowa mbrɛ dͻm nyina adze.

MHB 301
2 . Ma ͻnyɛ dɛ ehum dzendzen
Mbͻ mfa atamfo nyina do,
Ͻnsakyer bͻn no kwan biara,
Ma gyedzi na dͻ nka hͻn mbͻ m’.

MHB 301
3 . Nyew, ma Wo Sunsum beebiara
Ͻnda N‘ahom kɛse n’ edzi,
Ber a ndzeyɛɛ pa, adorn n’aba
Risiesie Wo Christ N'ahenman.

MHB 301
4 . Yɛ adom, nokwar Nyame krͻnkrͻn!
Ikenyaan tsetse adzehufo,
Hyɛ anohoba n’ ma ma hɛn,
Sian, fa gya soa hɛn ahenkyɛw.

MHB 302
1 . Mbɔbɔrhu Egya, W' asɛm mu 
Enyimnyam ahyɛ ma!
Abɔdzin nyinaa nka Wo dzin
W' adom nsɛmpa yi ntsi.

MHB 302
2 . Ha na akɔhweaban nyina 
Nya ahonya mbordo;
Ahonya a bi nnyi wi ase,
Otsim hɔ afebɔɔ.

MHB 302
3 . Ha na nyimdzee nduadzewa fifir 
Ma hɔn a kɔm dze hɔn;
Edziban pa a wiadze nnyi bi,
Rotweɔn nyia no kɔn dɔ.

MHB 302
4 . Ha na hɛn Pomfo N' ndze dɛɛdɛw 
Ka asomdwee kasa;
Na nkwa na dɛw a onyi ewiei
Wɔ Ne nsɛm nyinaa mu.

MHB 302
5 . Kyerɛkyerɛfo pa, adom Wura, 
Bɛn Wo ba daa nyinaa;
Kyerɛ m' ma mondɔ W' asɛmpa,
Na munhu m'Agyenkwa.    Amen.

MHB 303
1 . AO, NYAME Asɛm a abɛbra,
Ao, Nyansa a ifi sor,
Ao, Nokwar a 'nnsesa da,
Ao, hɛn wimu kadoo kan!
Yehuhor W' wɔ Wo hyerɛn ho,
Ifi siar bea ayɛ
Hɛn anamɔn ne kanea,
Hyerɛn fi ber to ber.

MHB 303
2 . Asɔrfi no Wura dɔfo
Nsamu nyaa sor akyɛdze,
Ɔda ho ama kan no do,
Ɔnhyerɛn wiadze nyina do,
Ɔyɛ sika adakaba;
Wosie mpɔkowa pa wɔ m',
Ɔyɛ Christ nkwa asɛm no
N'ahenman mu mfonyin.

MHB 303
3 . Orinyam tse dɛ frankaa,
Wɔ Nyame dɔm enyim,
Ɔhyerɛn tse dɛ ogyaabaa
Wɔ wiadze no sum do;
Ɔyɛ akyerɛkwan nwoma
Wɔ bra po pramee do,
Kusukuukuu, ɔbo, anhwea o,
Christ, wɔdze ba Wo nkyɛn.

MHB 303
4 . Gyefo pa, yɛ W'asɔrfi
Sika kanea hyɛnhyɛn,
Ɔmfa Wo nokwar kan no
Nkyin aman do dɛ tsetse,
Ma W'akwantufo a worikyin
Mfa yi nhwehwɛ hɔn kwan,
Nkodu dɛ fua, sum bɛpa,
Wobohu W' 'nyim na enyim.

MHB 304
1 . NYlMPA nyina Egya, Wo nko mu na
Yɛtse, kͻ ba, gu ahom,
Sor kan séremen kor na osian famu
Bɛsɛpɛw Wo mba ho.

MHB 304
2 . W'asɛm mu na yɛhwehwɛ Wo,
Yedze hu hwehwɛ Wo,
Bue hɛn enyi na ma yenhu
Wo mbra m' anwanwadze.

MHB 304
3 . Afei ma hɛn sum no nkata
Kan a ͻhyerɛn guam’ n’ do;
Afei soma Sunsum kyérɛkyérɛfo n’,
Bue hɛn asomu ma yɛntse.

MHB 305
1 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, bra hɛn 'komam', 
Ma yɛntse Wo tum no,
Wo na tsetse wɔdze W' hyɛɛ nkɔm,
Na kan na dɔ fir Wo.

MHB 305
2 . Bra, na Ɔwo na nkɔnhyɛfo n' 
Dze W' kyerɛwee, dze Wo kae;
Bue nokwar no, Ɔwo nye saafee n',
Tsew nwoma krɔnkrɔn n' ano.

MHB 305
3 . Sor Ebubur, trɛ W' atsabanm' 
Wɔ hɛn isum no do,
Butuw hɛn kra no sum no do,
Na ma hɔ ɔnyɛ kann.

MHB 305
4 . Sɛ 'hyerɛn hɛn mu a, yɛnam Nyame 
Nankasa do bohu N',
Na yɛnye Wo mba nyina esusu
Onyame dɔ no bun.   Amen.

MHB 306
1 . ASEKYERƐFO Krɔnkrɔn, bra,
Ma hɛn enyi mfa nkan Wo nwoma;
Aso ntsie esumasɛm no,
Nsɛm a ofi Wo nkyn ba,
Nsɛm a ɔma onnyiewie nhyira,
Yɛkora no setsie akomam'.

MHB 306
2 . Hɔn a wɔkan, tsie yɛ nhyira mba,
Sɛ wodzi W'ahyɛdze do a;
W'ahenman n' yebenya n' ha,
Na yeehu W'enyimnyam no,
Sɛ eba bɛtsena ase ha a,
Yenye W'eedzi hen konyim m'.

MHB 307
1 . SUNSUM n' gu ahom gu asɛm n' do
Na ɔma nokwar da edzi;
Afotu nye anohoba ma
Kan a ɔma ahotsew.

MHB 307
2 . Enyimnyam hyerɛn nwoma no do
Hyenhyɛnhyɛn dɛ ewia,
Ɔma hɛn wɔ ber biara mu,
Noara dze ma, ɔmmfɛm.

MHB 307
3 . Nsa a ɔma no gu do ma
Adom kan nye ɔhyew,
No nokwardzi soɛr aman do,
Wɔsoɛr na wɔnntɔ da.

MHB 307
4 . Ma ndaase a onnyi ewiei nyɛ Nedze
Wɔ dɛm kan hyɛnn no ho,
Dɛ ɔma wiadze sunkamm hyerɛn
Fi sor adzekyee nserɛmɛn m'.

MHB 307
5 . Me kra dzi dɛw dɛ ɔbɛka
Nyimpa a modɔ No n' do,
Kodu dɛ m'bohu enyimnyam
Wɔ sor man fɛɛfɛw n' mu.

MHB 308
1 . Ewuradze, W' asɛm tsim, 
'No na yɛhwɛ nantsew,
Nyia ɔgye no nokwar
Nya kan nye enyigye.

MHB 308
2 . Atamfo ba hɛn do a, 
W' asɛm yi hyɛ hɛn dzen,
Awerɛkyekyer nsɛmpa,
N-kwagye amandzɛɛ.

MHB 308
3 . Ɔbra n' ehum tu hɛn, 
Na sum gye hɛn do a,
Ne kan hyerɛn ma hɛn,
Na ɔkyerɛ hɛn kwan.

MHB 308
4 . Woana botum akyerɛ 
Ahotɔ nye dɛw a
W' asɛmpa yi dze ma
N-tsetsekwaa nyinaa?

MHB 308
5 . Ehumbɔbɔr nsɛmpa, 
Ɔboa atseasefo;
N-kwasɛm, ɔkyekye
Hɔn a wɔda wuso werɛ.

MHB 308
6 . Ewuradze, ma yenhu 
No mu adzesua krɔnkrɔn n',
Na yaadɔ, yeesuro Wo,
Daa nyinaa yaabɛn Wo!   Amen.

MHB 309
1 . EWURADZE, bu nkwa
Paanoo n' bi ma m',
Dɛ mbrɛ ibubuu bi mu
Po no ho no;
Nwoma krɔnkrɔn n' no mu
Na mohwehwɛ W',
Mo sunsum per hwehwɛ W',
O nkwa Asɛm!

MHB 309
2 . Ɔwo yɛ Nkwa Paanoo,
Ewuradze ma m'
W'asɛm nye nokwar no a
Ɔgyee me no
Ma menye Wo ndzidzi
Nnya nkwa wɔ sor;
Kyerɛ m' ma mondɔ W' nokwar
Na Ɔwo nye ɔdɔ.

MHB 309
3 . Owura, ma Wo Sunsum
No mbra mo do,
Na ɔnka m'enyiwa,
Na meehu adze;
Kyerɛ m' W'asɛm mu nokwar a
Ehuntsa no,
Nwoma a eyi akyerɛ n' mu
Muhu Ewuradze.

MHB 31
1 . Nyame da Noho edzi:
Hom mma yɛntonton No,
Yɛmfa enyidzi mbra N'enyim;
Nyame wɔ N'asɔrfi m'.
Hɔn a wɔwɔ m'nyina nyɛ komm,
Yɛmfa enyidzi ntwa nhwe N'enyim.
'No nko nye
Hɛn Nyame, Hɛn Gyefo:
Yi Ne dzin ayɛw daa.

MHB 31
2 . Nyame da Noho edzi:
Tsie, wɔrobɔ nsanku,
Hwɛ, dɔm n' etwa ahengua n' ho ehyia.
Krɔnkrɔn, Krɔnkrɔn, Krɔnkrɔn,
Tsie dɛ ndwom n' rofow sor,
'Bɔfo, hotsewfo tow ndwom n'bi.
Kyɛn W'aso 
Tsie hɛn ha;
Ewuradze Jesus, tsie
Hɛn ayɛyi a ɔmmfata.

MHB 31
3 . Ɔwo nye nhyira Bura,
Bɛtsew mo sunsum ho:
Memfa mo werɛ nhyɛ Wo nko mu,
Tse dɛ abɔfo krɔnkrɔn a
Wohu W'enyimnyam no,
Ma montonton Wo daa daa nyina.
Ma Wo pɛ 
Nhyɛ W'asɔr
Wɔ asaase yi do
Dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse wɔ sor.  Amen.

MHB 310
1 . BER a metse me dan mu komm.
Wo Buukuu n‘ nko nyɛ me damfo.
We nsem ne nkaakaa ye me dɛw.
Meka Wo pɛ a wͻakyérɛw n’ ho asɛm,
Na mohwehwɛ sor esumadze m’
Kodu dɛ m’benya akomatͻm'.

MHB 310
2 . Ao, nkyɛ Wo sor adom nsɛm no
Aayɛ botae wͻ me nsɛm nyina m’!
Na m‘bɛyɛ Ewuradze kadofo,
Na ͻnye m’ bɛnantsew akasa;
Dɛm na m'akoma bohu No,
Na ͻdze dͻ adzɛw dabaa.

MHB 310
3 . Mpɛn pii a meda morohom no
Ao nkyɛ W'abodwee kasa no
Aama mo bom' akomatͻmu!
Ber a motwer m' Ewuradze,
Rotͻ nkom, moroso siar daaso
Na da a onnyiewiei ho nyikyerɛ.

MHB 310
4 . M‘benyan atow Gyefo ayɛyi n’
Na daa m'bͻbͻ ne nyina dawur,
Na ma W’adom kasa pa no
Mpem W'akoma mbra me gyirama do,
Fa dͻ mapa hyɛ me bra ma
Na fa m’ ka sor Asͻr no ho.

MHB 311
1 . EWURADZE, yehu Wo nokwar no daa,
W'asɛm yɛ nokwar, yɛ dɔ na ayamuyie,
W'ehumbɔbɔr tsen du akra a ayew nyina do,
Ɔbɔnfo kɔbesae dan benya W'adom.

MHB 311
2 . O ma menkamfo m'Agyenkwa mma wo,
Misi mo bo ka, Christ yɛ nokwafo;
Hɔn a wɔgye Ne frɛ do nyina benya nkwa,
Bra m'Agyenkwa hɔ, N'adom du obiara do.

MHB 311
3 . Ofi sor bɛgyee hɔn a wɔahera nkwa;
Abɔn, hom mbra mbɛgye Jesus dzin ndzi;
Ɔdze bɔn kyɛ, ɔma obiara fahodzi;
Sɛ bɔn nye w'adzesoa a; O bra Me nkyɛn ha!

MHB 311
4 . Dɛm a hom mfa ahobrɛadze ngye N'adom,
Twa hwe N'ananadze, gye No dɛw mu;
Yenya bɔnfakyɛ koraa wɔ Jesus dzin mu,
N'ahonya nye hɛn abɔdzin a yɛdze kɔ sor.

MHB 312
1 . HWƐ Nyame Eguambaa a ɔsoa
Wiadze nyinara bɔn fi hɔ!
Botoo, ɔfaa nkowaa suban
Na ɔtsenaa dɛtse dan mu;
Na yennhu N'enyimnyam no bio,
Nyame nye nyimpa bɛtsenae.

MHB 312
2 . Hwɛ bea a Nyame-nyimpa gyina
Refrɛ N'abɔdze a ayew wɔ fie!
Da biara ɔtserɛw Ne nsamu,
Akra a wɔaberɛ, Jesus frɛ hom!
Hom mbra mbɔhom wɔ Mo bo mu;
Gye dzi na m'bɛma w' ahomgye.

MHB 312
3 . Abɔnfo, hom ngye nsɛmpa n' ndzi,
Jesus rebɛgye hom akra!
Jesus aba, hom Wura nye no;
Hom nyina benya fakyɛ wɔ N' mu,
Nyia ɔpɛ biara benya nkwa;
Nyimpa yi da ho gye abɔn.

MHB 313
1 . Enyimnyam nka Nyame! Ɔayɛ adze kɛse!
Ɔdɔɔ wiadze ara ma ɔdze N' Ba maa hɛn;
Ɔno a ɔdze No nkwa bɔɔ werdam maa abɔn,
Na obuee nkwa abotsen dɛ obiara nhɛn mu;

Yi N'ayɛw! Yi N'ayɛw!
Ma adasa ntsie Ne ndze!
Yi N' ayɛw! Yi N' ayɛw!
Ma nkorɔfo ndzi ehurusi!
Ao, dua Ɔba Jesus do bra 
Egya No hɔ,
Na hyɛ No enyimnyam !
Ɔayɛ adze kɛse!

MHB 313
2 . Ao, nkwagye a odzi mu, bɔgya atɔdze!
Gyedzinyi biara nya Nyame anohoba n';
Abɔn mu ɔbɔn biara a ɔgye dzi ampa n',
Aber no ara onya Jesus hɔ fakyɛ.

MHB 313
3 . Ɔakyerɛ hɛn adzeson ! Ɔayɛ adze kɛse!
Yɛnam Ne Ba Jesus do dzi dɛw mbordo;
Wɔbɛsan hɛn ho koraa, na wɔbɔkrɔn hɛn,
Hɛn ahodwiriw na enyigye ber a yehu Jesus!

MHB 314
1 . Ma yɛntow anwanwa dɔ bi ho ndwom, 
Nokwar ɔdɔ a,
Ɔdɔ a ofi Sor Egya N' akomam'
Rehyɛ adasamba ma:
Anwanwa dɔ
Ɔwɔ hɛn Ɔsor Egya N' akomam'.

MHB 314
2 . Jesus, Agyenkwa n', dze dɛw sianee bae 
Bɛkaa 'Sɛmpa n';
Ɔduaa N' amandzehu pii do hwehwɛɛ
Hɔn a hɔn enyidar asa n'.
Hɔn a wɔayew n',
Otuaa kaw mbordo na ɔgyee hɔn nkwa.

MHB 314
3 . Jesus da ho hwehwɛ hɔn a wɔayew n': 
Wokyin yɛ dɛn?
No dɔ pɛ dɛ ɔkata hɔn bɔn do:
Afonafo, hom mbra fie!
Anwanwa dɔ
Ɔwɔ hɛn Ɔsor Egya N' akomam'.

MHB 314
4 . Anwanwa dɔ, bra mo so m'akomam', 
Bra bɛtsena hɔ:
Tsew me kra ho na oeefi dza ɔnntsenm'-
Enyiber nye atorsɛm mu.
Ahobrɛadzem'
Na mepɛ dɛ mepɛ Wo suanyi bi.

MHB 315
1 . TSIE ! Nsɛmpa ndze no regyegye;
Christ atseetsee dua no do;
Ehumbͻbͻr nsu repem weͻͻ;
’Biara nya adorn bafuu kwa.
Nkyii, bͻnyɛnyi,
Hwɛ Nyia owui maa wo No.

MHB 315
2 . Ao, guan kͻ ekyir koko no do!
Nkyii hyɛ ase weͻn na sͻr;
Christ frɛ wo nsunyiwa no ho;
Bra bͻhohor wo bͻn no,
Mma nnyɛ ekyim,
Bra N‘ hͻ bér a ibotum yi.

MHB 315
3 . Adom repem de esutsen;
Ͻama ͻpepé enya bi;
Ͻda ho ara repem krͻngyee
Fi Agyenkwa mfe m‘ ‘piratua m’:
’Biara nnkɛehéra;
Christ ewu, hom benya nkwa.

MHB 315
4 . Christ nko na ͻbɛyɛ hɛn kyɛfa,
Ͻrennkyɛr yebehyia m' sor,
Nkyii yeboguar po kɛse n’ mu.
Wͻ Pomfo kɛse No dͻ mu,
N‘amayɛ nyina
Na vebeyi akyerɛ.

MHB 316
1 . YƐATSE enyigye ndze bi;
Christ gye nkwa!
Ma enyigyesɛm yi mpetse;
Christ gye nkwa!
Fa asɛm no kɔ mbea nyina,
Fow mbepɔw na twa po so;
Hom nduom! Ewuradze ndze nye n';
Christ gye nkwa!

MHB 316
2 . Tow ndwom ma ɔmbor ɔsa n' do;
Christ gye nkwa!
No wu nye onnyiewie nkwa ntsi
Christ gye nkwa
Tow no bɔkɔɔ wɔ sum no m';
Ber a akoma hwehwɛ ehumbɔbɔr;
Tow konyim wɔ owumaa do;
Christ gye nkwa!

MHB 316
3 . Hom mma ehum no ndze kɛse;
Christ gye nkwa!
Aman nyina mbɔ ose sesei;
Christ gye nkwa!
Tsea m', nkwagye a odzi mu, wɔnntɔ,
'Dze ma wiadze mbea nyina-
Hɛn konyimdzi ndwom nye yi;
Christ gye nkwa!

MHB 317
1 . OBIARA a ͻtse n‘, ͻmma ndze no do!
Mfa nhyira nsɛmpa no ntsérɛw wiadze nyina;
Tsérɛw ’nyigyesɛm wͻ mbea a nyimpa du n’ nyina:

    Obiara a ͻpɛ n’ ͻmbra.
    Obiara a ͻpɛ n’! Obiara a ͻpɛ n’! 
    Ͻmbͻ dawur n' wͻ mbͻnsa na
    nkokwaa do;
	Egya dͻfo no refrɛ’ akobͻfo fie;
	Obiara a ͻpɛ n’ ͻmbra.

MHB 317
2 . Obi a ͻreba n’ mma ͻnnyɛ ekyim,
Bér a abow no ebuei yi hɛn mu ntsɛntsɛm;
Jesus nye nokwar no na nkwa kwan no;
Obiara a ͻpɛ n’ ͻmbra. '

MHB 317
3 . Obiara a ͻpɛ n’, ’nohoba n’ si pi,
Obiara a ͻpɛ n’ betséna dabaa wͻ hͻ,
Obiara a ͻpɛ n’ benya nkwa a onnyi ewiei:
Obiara a ͻpɛ n’ ͻmbra.

MHB 318
1 . NYIMPA mba, ebɛn ntsi na hom,
Hwetse dͻ nguan a wͻaba hu’i?
Nkwasea, ebɛn ntsi na horn kyin
Fi dɛm nokwar dͻ yi ho?

MHB 318
2 . Oguanhwɛfo bɛn na ͻdwe
Wͻ ehumbͻbͻr na adͻe ho,
Dɛ Agyenkwa a ͻbɛma
Yɛabɛtséna N'ananadze?

MHB 318
3 . Nyame ehumbͻbͻr a ͻtsérɛw,
Tse dɛ epo tɛtɛr no a
Ayamuyie bi wͻ ne pɛryɛ m‘,
Ͻsen fahodzi koraa.

MHB 318
4 . Etuuyɛ wͻ hɛ ma abͻn.
Na adom pii ma apapafo;
Agyenkwa n’ wͻ ehumbͻbͻr,
Ayarsa wͻ No bͻgyaa m’.

MHB 318
5 . Nkwagye pii wͻ hͻ ma hɛn wͻ
No bͻgyaa a wohuei gui n’ mu;
Edɛw wͻ hͻ ma hɛn nyina
Wͻ Jesus amandzehu m’.

MHB 318
6 . Nyame No dͻ no, ͻtserɛw
Sen nyimpa n’adwen nsusui.
Na 'Domankoma N’akoma m’
Wo ayamuyie nwanwa.

MHB 318
7 . Sɛ ͻdwe wͻ hɛn dͻ mu a,
Nkyɛ yɛbɛgye W‘asɛm edzi,
Na hɛn bra nyinara bɛhyerɛn
Wͻ Ewuradze Ne dɛw mu.

MHB 319
1 . AKRA 'werɛfo a hom kyin
Fi nhyira finimfin no,
Hom nkɔ Jesu a wɔsɛɛn N' hɔ,
Hom nguan nkɔ N'epirakur ho;
Hom ntɔ ahosan nsu n' mu;
Hom nsoɛr nkɔ Nyame nkwa mu.

MHB 319
2 . Hwehwɛ asomdwee kwan Christ mu,
Asomdwee a onnyi kabea;
Ne yaw no ma w' ahotɔ,
Ne pen a ɔdze ruwu ma w' nkwa;
Ma N'asehwe no mpegya w',
Ma Christ nyɛ wo adze nyina.

MHB 319
3 . O hom ngye nokwasɛm n' ndzi;
Nyame dze Ne Ba ama hom,
Afei hom so enyi bɛgye;
Hom nnya sor nkwa wɔ ase,
Hom ntsena sor abrabɔ n' mu,
Wɔ enyimnaym dɔ asetsena mu.

MHB 32
1 . ABƆDZE Wura a idzi sor hen,
W'enyimnyam wɔ ewia na nworaba m';
Eyɛ adze nyina ne farbaa,
Naaso ebɛn hɔn a wɔwɔ dɔ.

MHB 32
2 . N-kwa Ewia a ikenyan hɛn
Ma adzekyee kan hyerɛn hɛn kwan mu;
Hɛn enyidado Woraba,
Wo kan no hyerɛn hɛn sum mu.

MHB 32
3 . Sɛ imuna a, hɛn bra yɛ sum,
W'adom gye a, na hɛn ewia epue;
Wo nyankontɔn kyerɛ ehumbɔbɔr,
Bɔn da nkyɛn a adze nyina Wodze a.

MHB 32
4 . Ase nye sor nkwa nyina Wura,
Wo kan nye nokwar, W'ewia n', dɔ a;
W'ahengua hyɛnhyɛnn enyim no,
Yɛnnhwehwɛ hɛnankasa hɛn kra.

MHB 32
5 . Ma Wo nokwar n' nyɛ hɛn adehye,
Nkenyan akoma a ɔhwehwɛ W',
Kɛpem dɛ W'asomfo benya
Kan krɔnn na sor gyaframee kor.
                  		Amen.

MHB 320
1 . Ana ahaw, na aberɛ, 
Na wo kɔn ebu?
Tsie! Obi dɛ, Bra, na m' bɛma w'
Ahomgye.

MHB 320
2 . Ana akam bi wɔ No a, 
Medze m' bohu No?
N' anan ho, Ne nsam', nye Ne mfem'
Wɔ epiratua.

MHB 320
3 . Ana kyɛw bi so N' a ɔma 
Ɔyɛ dɛ ɔhen?
Nyew, ahenkyɛw ara ampa;
Na nsoɛ dze a.

MHB 320
4 . Sɛ muhu N' n a meka No do a, 
Ebɛn na m' benya?
Amandzehu, nye ɔfona,
Nye nyinsuwa.

MHB 320
5 . Sɛ menngyaa dɛ meka No do a, 
'Bɛn na nkyii m' benya?
Ɔfona, nye yaw, nye Jordan
Botwa mu.

MHB 320
6 . Ana mese N' dɛ ɔngye m' a,

Etwam' kɔ.

MHB 320
7 . Muhu N', ka No do, meper a, 
Obehyira  m' ampa?
Ahotsewfo nye asɛnkafo
Bua dɛ, Nyew!

MHB 321
1 . Ewuradze, matse nka dɛ 
'Rowora nhyira nsu pii,
Edze rofɔw daadze a oetwie,
Ma bi nsosɔ mo so do,
                   'Mi dɛm yi.

MHB 321

M' akomam' wɔ bɔn so ampa;
Ɔfata dɛ igya m' hɔ dze,
Na fa mbɔbɔr hu me so,

MHB 321
3 . Mma mmpa mo ho, Agyenkwa brɛfo,

MHB 321

MHB 322
1 . Jesus gye ndzebɔnyɛfo;

Wɔahwe ase, reyɛ ekyim.

Christ ɔgye ndzebɔnyɛfo
(Christ ɔgye ndzebɔnyɛfo)
Amandzɛɛ n' ma wɔntse ase;
(Amandzɛɛ n', kyerɛ mu yie)

MHB 322

MHB 322
3 . M' akoma mmubu me fɔ bio,

MHB 322

MHB 323
1 . HOM mbra nsɛmpa aponto ase,
Abͻn, Jesus to nsa frɛ hom;
Mma obiara nnka ekyir ’siandɛ
Nyame afrɛ adasa nyina.

MHB 323
2 . Hom mbra, mo wura somaa m’ hom hͻ,
Ͻto nsa frɛ nyimpa nyina:
Obiara mbra, abͻnfo mpo,
Christ mu ndzɛmba nyina ayɛ krado.

MHB 323
3 . Hom mbra, akra a bͻn retseetsee hom,
Ekyimafo a horn hwehwɛ ahomgye,
Ehiafo, mpakye, efurafo,
Akͻaba wͻ Christ mu ma hom.

MHB 323
4 . No dͻ kɛse no hyɛ obiara,
Bra bͻsͻ konyimdzi dͻ n’ hwɛ;
Gyaa woho ma No dͻ tum no,
Na mma nnko nntsia wo Nyame bio.

MHB 323
5 . Aber no nye yi, mma nntwentweͻn!
Ewuradze da a ͻagyé ato m’ nye’ i;
Ͻfrɛ wo aber yi, bra mu,
Tséna ase ma Nyia owui maa obiara n’.

MHB 324
1 . Abɔn, 'kɔbesaefo, hom mbra, 
Bahatɔfo, epirafo,
Jesus rotweɔn agye hom nkwa;
Tsema na tum ahyɛ N' ma;
Ɔyɛ Tumfo
Ɔpɛ, mma hom nngye kyim bio.

MHB 324
2 . Hom mbra, akɔhweaban, hom mbra; 
Hom nhuhor Nyame ayamuyie,
Nokwar gyedzi, nnuho mapa,
Adom a ɔtwe hɛn bɛn N',
Wɔmmfa sika,
Bra Jesus hɔ bɔtɔ bi.

MHB 324
3 . Hom mbra, hom a hom kɔn ebu, 
Hom a asehwe epira hom;
Sɛ hom rotweɔn ayɛ yie ana a,
Hom nnkɛba dabiarada;
Nnyɛ atsenenee a,
Abɔn na Jesus bɛfrɛe.

MHB 324

                   'Yi ɔdze ma w';
Ɔyɛ Sunsum 'napawi.

MHB 324

Gyina No bɔgyaa do dzi ma W',
Fa woho ma N', fa ma N' koraa;
Mma adwen fofor nntwa ntamu!
           	Jesus nkotoo
na otum yɛ abɔn yie.

MHB 325
1 . ABƆN, hom mbra Ewuradze nkyɛn,
Christ mu paradise wɔ hɔ bio;
Suo ndzepa a ɔdze ama w' no mu,
Adom nsɛmpa a onnyi kabea.

MHB 325
2 . Fakyɛ a wɔdze No bɔgyaa akyerɛw,
Nyame asomdwee bata ho;
Enyi a ohu, nka a ɔtse
Esumasɛm nnuhu a ɔyɛ dɛw.

MHB 325
3 . Nokwar yaw a no ho yɛ har
Ɔmaa akoma a ebubu nan,
Nyinsu a ɔkyerɛ dɛ wɔdze akyɛ w',

MHB 325
4 . Bemdzi enyito, dɛw atsetsee,
Ayamuyie a onnyi kabea,

MHB 325
