4 . Medze me yaw brɛ Wo, 
Yaw a munntum nnka n' a;
Ɔnngye dɛ meka mpo,
Ɔnngye dɛ meka mpo,
Woara nyim ne nyina.
M'Agyenkwa a Woara so nyim yaw,
Medze m'awerɛhow brɛ Wo.

MHB 520
5 . Medze me dɛw brɛ Wo, 
Dɛw a Wo dɔ dze ana m',
Dɛ memfa nyɛ atwer a 
Mofow mipinkyɛn Wo.
Gyefo, Woara tɔɔ ne nyina maa m';
Medze ne nyina gu W'enyim.

MHB 520
6 . Medze mo nkwa brɛ Wo, 
Mennda ho nndze moho;
Gyefo, ma menya Wodze,
Wo nko Wodze daa nyina.
M'akoma, mo nkwa, m'adze nyina,
Medze brɛ Wo, me Hen, Gyefo.

MHB 521
1 . MOTWER Wo, Ewuradze Jesus,
Motwer Wo nkotoo,
Motwer Wo ma meenya nkwagye 
Kɛse kwa.

MHB 521
2 . Motwer Wo kotow W'ananadze
Serɛ bɔnfakyɛ;
W'adom nye ehumbɔbɔr kɛse n'
Na motwer.

MHB 521
3 . Motwer Wo ma aatsew mo ho
Wɔ bɔgya bura n' mu;
Motwer Wo ma aayɛ m' krɔnkrɔn,
Wo bɔgyaa m'.

MHB 521
4 . Motwer W' ma aayɛ m' Kwankyerɛfo,
Woara kyerɛ me kwan;
Daa na dɔnhwer nyinara m' ma m'
M'ehiadze.

MHB 521
5 . Motwer Wo ama meenya tum,
Irinngyaa me da;
Nsɛm a Woara dze bɛma me n'
Bedzi nyim.

MHB 521
6 . Motwer Wo, Ewuradze Jesus,
Mma monnhwe ase da;
Motwer Wo daa daa nyinara,
Na afebɔɔ.

MHB 522
1 . SƐ 'nnka m' ho a, munntum nnyɛ hwee,
Hɔn a wɔayew hɔn Gyefo,
Ɔwo a Wo bɔgyaa a ɔsom bo n' 
'Dze apon emi dɛm yi;
Wo tsenenee, Wo fakyɛ,
Wo bɔgyaa a ɔsom bo n' nyɛ 
M'enyidar, m'awerɛkyekyer,
M'enyimnyam, na m'asɛm.

MHB 522
2 . Sɛ 'nnka m' ho a, munntum nnyɛ hwee,
Mo nko nnkotum egyina,
Minnyi ahom anaa ayamuyie,
Me nyansaa nnyɛ medze;
Na Ɔwo Agyenkwa Dɔfo dze
Eyɛ m'adze nyina,
Sɛ motwer Wo nkotoo a,
Mberɛwyɛ dan ahoɔdzen.

MHB 522
3 . Sɛ 'nnka m' ho a, munntum nnyɛ hwee,
Nyɛnko biara nnyi hɔ a
Otum hu adze a me kra
Hwehwɛ na ɔatse ase,
Ɔdasanyi bi nnyi hɔ a,
Obohu m'akoma m' nsɛm
Na ɔakyekye mo werɛ
Dɛ Ewuradze nko.

MHB 522
4 . Sɛ 'nnka m' ho a, munntum nnyɛ hwee,
M-fe rutwa m' ntsɛntsɛm,
Na ɔnnkɛkyɛr na m' nko rutwa
Esutsen n' awerɛhow m';
Sɛ asorɛkye n' bu dɛn ara a,
Ɔwo innkegya m' da,
Minyim dɛ ebɛbɛn me
Na awasa dɛ, Mara a.  Amen.

MHB 523
1 . MINNKEGYAA W' ma aakɔ! Ɔwo a
eyɛ hia da m' boafo;
Mbusu dɔɔ so a,
Motwer W' ara,
Kaansa ɔyɛ dɛ epɛ abɔ me a,
Yɛ me dza Woara pɛ,
Mebɛtetar Wo ara;
'Dze W'enyim huntsa mpo a, hia da m' boafo,
Minnkegyaa Wo ma aakɔ!

MHB 523
2 . Mennkɛgyaa W' ma aakɔ! Ana me
nhyira mbɔ ,e a?
Dabi, 'yɛ m'dze,
Meyɛ Wodze;
Ndzɛmba nyina hwer m' mpo a, m' 
bɛtetar W',
'Nafua yɛ sum dɛn mpo a,
Wo kan dze enyigye ba;
Ɔwo a eyɛ m'Ewia, me nhyira mbɔ me a?
Minnkegyaa Wo ma aakɔ!

MHB 523
3 . Mennkɛma aakɔ! Me Nyame, mo
Nkwa, m'Ewuradze;
'Wu ruuntum nntsew m'
Ɔwo a emi ntsi ihuee Wo nkwa gui,
'Dɔ ntsi Ɔwo wui maa m';
Meka n' ɔdɔ m' kyerɛ Wo,
M'akoma tsew mpo a, me Nyame,
mo Nkwa, Wura,
Minnkɛgyaa Wo ma aakɔ!

MHB 524
1 . ME Nyame, meda W' ase wɔ Wiadze fɛɛfɛw,
Ɔhyerɛn, no mu yɛ dɛw, yɛ kan,
Yɛ ahomka;
Ndzɛmba a ɔyɛ nwanwa pii wɔ ha,
Dza ɔkrɔn na oye.

MHB 524
2 . Meda W' ase dɛ ama yenya
Dɛw pii wɔ ha,
Adwen pa nye ndzeyɛɛ pa so
Ehyia hɛn ho,
Na wiadze beebi a ɔyɛ sum 
Ɔdɔ wɔ hɔ.

MHB 524
3 . Meda W' ase dɛ dɛw nyina mu
Yaw so fam ho,
Dɛ wimu bunkam kan no do,
Nsoɛ so wɔ hɔ,
Ama wiadze dɛw akyerɛ hɛn kwan,
Na annkyekyer hɛn.

MHB 524
4 . Meda W' ase dɛ edze dza oye
Esie ama hɛn;
Yɛwɔ pii naaso ɔnndɔɔ so,
Yɛnnhwehwɛ bio;
Hɛn kɔn dɔ asomdwee mapa a
Ne saso nnka.

MHB 524
5 . Meda W' ase dɛ ha hɛn akra
Nya nhyira pii,
Naaso wonntum nnya ahomgye pa a 
Odzi mu koraa n',
Kodu dɛ wɔbɛba abɔtwer
Jesus No bom' n'.

MHB 525
1 . HƐN Agyenkwa Nyame dɔ ntsi
Ɔbɛyɛ yie;
N'adom a ɔdze ma kwa, ɔnnsakyer,
Ne nyina ye;
N'adehye bɔgya sa hɛn yar;
N'adom kɛse sɔw hɛn ano;
Ne nsa a ɔwowaw hɛn n' yɛ dzen,
Ɔbɛyɛ yie.

MHB 525
2 . Kaansa yɛnam ɔhaw mu mpo a,
Ɔbɛyɛ yie;
Christ atɔ hɛn nkwagye ewie,
Ne nyina ye;
Yedzi dɛw wɔ hɛn nkwagye ewie,
Yɛtse Christ mu a yɛsow aba,
Yɛyɛ krɔnkrɔn wɔ Sunsum mu;
Ɔbɛyɛ yie.

MHB 525
3 . Hɛn enyi da adzekyee pa kwan,
Ɔbɛyɛ yie;
Gyedzi tow ndwom awerɛhow da mu,
Ne nyina ye;
Yɛdze hɛnho to Egya n' dɔ do,
Jesus ma hɛn dza yehia nyina,
Ntsi nkwa mu o, anaa owu mu o,
Ɔbɛyɛ yie.

MHB 526
1 . O JESUS , mahyɛ bɔ dɛ
M'bɔsom Wo akɔ ewiei;
Ntsi pinkyɛn me daa nyina,
Mo Wura nye me Nyɛnko;
Murunnsuro ɔko no,
Sɛ ewɔ me nkyɛn a,
Sɛ Ɔwo yɛ me Kwankyerɛfo a,
Morommfom mmfi kwan n' mu.

MHB 526
2 . Ma mentse nka dɛ ebɛn me,
Wiadze bɛn me dabaa;
Muhu dza osiw enyiwa do,
Metse engyigye so nka;
M'atamfo bɛn me dabaa,
Wɔabɔ mo ho aprɔw;
Mbom Jesus, twe bɛn me, na
Gye me kra fi bɔn mu.

MHB 526
3 . O ma mentse wo ndze dɛ
Rekasa krɔnkrɔnkrɔn,
Wɔ akɔndɔbɔn ehum mu
Na pɛ n'ehwinhwin mu;
Kasa ma minnya awerɛhyɛm',
Tsea m' anaa hom mo do;
O kasa ma mintsie Wo,
Ɔwo m' kra Kwangyafo.

MHB 526
4 . Jesus, abɔ anohoba
Dɛ W'akadofo nyina
Mbrɛ etse enyimnyam mu n'
Na W'asomfo bɛba;
Na Jesus, mahyɛ bɔ dɛ
M'bɔsom Wo akɔ ewiei;
Mo Wura nye me Nyɛnko, ma m'
Adom mfa ndzi W'ekyir.

MHB 527
1 . KAN pue Christiannyi awora
Aber a ɔrotow ndwom;
Nyame na ɔdze 'yarsa tum
Botwa no ho hyia dɛm;
Ber a awerɛkyekyer repa n',
Ɔma awerɛhyɛm' bi
Bɛhɛn ɔkra no mu bio,
Na ɔma n' enyigye.

MHB 527
2 . Yɛnam adwen krɔnkrɔn do
Yɛdze enyigye hwehwɛ
Nyame No nkwagye ho asɛm,
Na yenya no fofor,
Woyi hɛn awerɛhow 'i mu a,
Yetum dze dɛw ka dɛ
Ɔkyena mpo a yennyim mu asɛm
Mfa dza ɔdze nam mbra.

MHB 527
3 . Ɔammfa hweeara mpo ammba a,
Obotwitwa hɛn hia m',
Nyia ofura 'sukooko tam n'
Bɛma hɛn efuradze;
Wi yantamm n'ase ha yi
Abɔdze biara mee;
Na Nyia ɔnyɛn wimu nnoma n'
Bɛyɛn No mbofra so.

MHB 527
4 . Sɛ wenyindua na adɔmba
Annsow aba a ohia n',
Sɛ haban mu nyina tɔ pan
Mbowa nnya edzidzibea a,
Nyame ankasa wɔ hɔ 'i dze,
N'ayɛyi bɛhyɛ m' ma,
Aber a metse No mu yi,
Otwar dɛ midzi dɛw.

MHB 528
1 . Metse sor man ho dɔ mu 'i, 
Munnsuro nsakyer biara;
M'awerɛhyɛmu yi dzi mu,
Biribiara nnsakyer ha;
Ehum botu abɔ m' ho aprɔw
M'akoma botu dze;
Na Nyame etwa moho ehyia 'i.
Ana m'bɛpa abaw?

MHB 528
2 . Beebiara a obegya me n'. 
Hia biara nnkɛsan me;
Mo Guanhwɛfo wɔ me nkyɛn,
Na minnkehia hweeara;
Ne nyansaa tse hɔ daa daa,
N'enyi nnyɛ kusuww da;
Onyim kwan a ɔfa do,
Na menye N' bɛnantsew.

MHB 528
3 . Mfunoma wɔ m'enyim a, 
Emidze minnyae nnhunii,
Wimu bɛtsew kann wɔ mo do,
Wɔ mbrɛ nkyɛ fua ahyɛ  n';
M'enyidar munntum nnsusu,
Mo kwan da hɔ kɔ nkwan',
M'Agyenkwa esie m'akoradze
Na ɔnye m' bɛnantsew.

MHB 529
1 . O SIAR nkwa bi a!' Homgye wɔ hɔ
Ma akoma, ber a dwumadzi asa -
Nyia ɔtwer sor apɛdze na obu n'
Adze tsitsir kyɛn nyimpa n' pɛ.

MHB 529
2 . O siar nkwa bi a! Adwen a ohu
Mbɔbɔrhu wɔ biribiara mu,
Na ohu esumasɛm nyina mu,
Kaansa afe n' dze nsakyer ba mpo a.

MHB 529
3 . O siar nkwa bi a! 'Kra hu ndzɛmba m',
Ber a adasa enyiwa yɛ kusuww,
Ɔtra ntseasee du Nyame hɔ,
Nyia No dɔ buebue sor mbobow.

MHB 529
4 . O siar nkwa bi a! Akoma, adwen, kra,
Nya nyimpa dwen na ɔpɛ m' 'hotɔ,
Wɔnye Nyame bɔ m' wɔ adze nyina m',
Na wɔhyɛ Ewuradze tum ase.

MHB 529
5 . O mbrɛ Nyame m' nkwa dua yɛ siar a!
Sor nkwa mapa a enyi da kwan;
Agyenkwa, hyɛ me pɛ no ma,
Na ma siar nkwa yi nyɛ medze.   Amen.

MHB 53
1 . NYAME nye dɔ, N'adom da edzi,
Wɔ kwan a yɛfa do nyina m';
Okenyan siar ma sum dan kan,
Nyam' nye nyansa, Nyam' nye dɔ.

MHB 53
2 . Ndzɛmba nyina rutwa m'akɔ;
Nyimpa sɛe na mber twa mu;
Naaso N'adom do nnhuan da koraa;
Nyam' nye nyansa, Nyam' nye dɔ.

MHB 53
3 . Ber ɔyɛ sum dodow mu mpo,
Ɔda ho kyerɛ N'ayamuyie;
Awerɛhow mu Ne kan hyerɛn: 
Nyam' nye nyansa, Nyam' nye dɔ.

MHB 53
4 . Ɔdze enyidar a ɔwɔ sor
Afora wiadze dadwen;
Beebiara N'enyimnyam hyerɛn:
Nyam' nye nyansa, Nyam' nye dɔ.

MHB 530
1 . Mber pii na maka n' mo mu; 
Dɛ, Woana bɔfow sor,
Akɛfa Ewuradze Christ,
Dze No esian famu?
Adwendwen dze me botu,
Ma mekohu Noara
Mbrɛ abɔfo yi No ayɛw,
Wonya adzekyee nwoaraba n'.

MHB 530
2 . Mber pii na maka n' mo mu: 
Woana besian bun n' mu,
Akɛfa Ewuradze Christ,
Efi ewufom' aba?
Medze nokwar mbrɛahoadze
Siesie m'akoma mu dze a,
Christ bɛhɛn mo mu hɔ ntsɛm,
Nye me abɛtsena daa.

MHB 530
3 . Na gyedzi mu tsenenee n' 
Akyerɛ me ndzɛmba pa:
Ɔdze Christ rebrɛ me no;
Ɔse: Hwɛ N' w'akkomam',
Christ ayɛ krado dze nkwa
Rema nyia ɔhaahaw ho n';
W'anomu nye w'akoma mu
Asɛm no abɛn wo.

MHB 531
1 . WIADZE Kan, mihyira Wo nserɛmɛn n';
Tsenenee Ewia, Wo nko do na
Me gyedzi enyi tsim;
Igya me 'i, mudua ne nyina m',
Munnsuro mbusu biara wɔ ha,
'Siandɛ ebɛn me da.

MHB 531
2 . Samanadze etumfo runntum mmpuw
Ɔkra a ɔnye Christ nam kan mu;
Ɔnantsew, ɔnnhwe ase;
Ohu adze kann, tsin no kwan do,
Ɔwɔw do hyerɛn kodu da pa n',
Odzi adze nyina do nyim.

MHB 531
3 . Mohom Wo tum kɛse n' ase;
Jesus Ne dzin yɛ abantsentsen,
Ɔkora me kra wɔ sor;
Onnkegyaa dɛ ɔyɛ mo Boafo;
Mo werɛ nyina hyɛ Wo mu,
Dɔ Nyame nokwafo.

MHB 531
4 . Dɛm ntsi, mobɔ mpaa daa nyina,
Mepra m'akoma m' tu me kra
Hyɛ Wo nsamu dabaa;
Minyim dɛ ɔbra yi m' 'bɛgye m' nkwa,
Na owu ekyir so akyerɛ me dɛ
Eyɛ m' Gyafo afebɔɔ.

MHB 532
1 . WƆMFA onnyiewiei enyimnyam nhyɛ Wo
Ahenkyɛw, m'Agyenkwa na m' Wura;
'Dze nkwagye fi sor esian famu,
Na akyerɛw nhyira n' wɔ W'asɛm mu.

MHB 532
2 . Hɛn ahopopo tsibowa hwehwɛ
Tsintsimbea pa bi ahom hɔ;
Abagura ntsi hɛn sunsum gow,
Kodu dɛ yɛba Wo nko hɔ.

MHB 532
3 . Mbrɛ Wo siar nokwar dua saa a! 
W'ahyɛdze yɛ nyansa na krɔnn,
Mbrɛ W'anohoba nyina dua tsim a!
Hɛn enyidar na awerɛkyekyer tsim.

MHB 532
4 . Sɛ nyimpa nhyehyɛɛ bɔn nyinara
Ko dzendzen tsia me gyedzi mpo a,
Ɔyɛ gyan na akohwi; medze
W'asɛmpa n' kyekyer m'akoma ho.

MHB 533
1 . MPAABƆ nye ɔkra n'akɔndɔdze,
Wɔka anaa wɔnnka a,
Ɔyɛ nsumaa m'ogya a ɔdzɛw a
Ɔwosow akoma m'.

MHB 533
2 . Mpaabɔ yɛ nkrumsi dzendzen bi a
Ɔyɛ nyinsuwakyi,
Enyi a otua sor, mbrɛ obi mmbɛn,
Gyedɛ Nyame nkotsee.

MHB 533
3 . Mpaabɔ yɛ kasa mberɛw bo a 
Mbofra ano mpo tum ka;
Mbaabɔ yɛ ndwom dɛɛdɛw na odu
Sor Tumfo no enyim.

MHB 533
4 . Mpaabɔ yɛ ɔbɔn a ɔasan efi
N'akwan bɔn ho ne ndze;
Abɔfo dze dɛw tow hɔn ndwom,
Tsea m' dɛ: Hwɛ, ɔrosɔr!

MHB 533
5 . Mpaabɔ yɛ Christian n'ahom pa,
Christian man no mu mfar,
Tum a ɔdze hɛn owu abotsen m';
Ɔdze mpaabɔ hɛn sor;

MHB 533
6 . Ɔwo a yedua W' do hu Nyame,
N-kwa Nokwar na Ɔkwan n'!
Woara edua mpaabɔ kwan no do;
Hɛn Wura, kyerɛ hɛn mpaabɔ.  Amen.

MHB 534
1 . JESUS, adasa Wura tumfo,
Ɔwo a nnsakyer dabiarada,
Tsie Wo mba mberɛyɛfo hɛn frɛ,
Na kyerɛ hɛn mbrɛ yensi mbɔ mpaa!
Hue mpaabɔ adom no gu hɛn do,
Na kenyan hɛn ma yɛnhwehwɛ W'.

MHB 534
2 . Yennkotum adwen adwen pa bi,
Yennkenya ɔpɛ pa bi, gyedɛ
Ɔwo a efrɛɛ wiadze fii hun mu n'
Dze Wo tum n' kenyan hɛn akoma,
Ma anohoba Ntamugyinafo n' mbra,
Na ma yennya Woara sesei.

MHB 534
3 . Dua Wo ntotɔserɛ Sunsum n' do
Bra hɛn a yɛrotweɔn Wo mbae n' nkyɛn;
Yɛserɛ W'akyɛdze n' mu kor pɛr,
Tum a wɔdze sɔr aber biara;
Yeewura, dom hɛn ebisadze yi,
Na mma mmfa nkaa no so nnkam hɛn.

MHB 535
1 . EHUM kɛse biara a otu,
Na ɔhaw asorɛkye biara a obu n',
Ɔbrɛ adze; guandɔbea mapa,
Wɔ ehumbɔbɔr egua n' ase.

MHB 535
2 . Bea bi wɔ hɔ a Jesus hue
Enyigye ngo gu hɛn tsir do,
Bea a hɔ yɛ dɛw sen mbea nyina;
Mbɔbɔrhu bɔgya egua n' ase.

MHB 535
3 . Bea bi wɔ hɔ a esunsum saa,
Na anyɛnkofo hyia fɛkuwbɔ m';
Wɔmmbɛn, naaso wohyia gyedzi m'
Wɔ ehumbɔbɔr egua kor n' ho.

MHB 535
4 . Hɔ, yɛdze ɔkɔr ntsaban tu,
Na mber nye adwen nnyi hɔ bio;
Na sor sian bɛyɛ hɛn akra etuu,
Enyimnyam ka mbɔbɔrhu egua n'.

MHB 536
1 . ME Nyame , ber bi wɔ anapa
Kodu ewimbir a ɔyɛ dɛw sen
Ber a efrɛ m' ba W'ananadze,
M-paabɔ ber n'.

MHB 536
2 . Nhyira aka anapa asomdwee ber,
Na ewimbir nhyira ber krɔnn no,
Ber a mudua mpaabɔ ntsaban do 
Gya wiadze hɔ.

MHB 536
3 . Ber 'i na anapawi tow nserɛmɛn a
Ɔsen anapa ewia hyerɛn gu m' do,
Na ahomka bɔsu a ofi Wo hɔ
Kyɛn wiadze dze.

MHB 536
4 . Inu m'ahoɔdzen mu fofor;
Na edze mo bɔn nyina kyɛ m';
Na edze sor enyidar kyekye
Ankonam werɛ.

MHB 536
5 . Kasa bi nntum nnkyerɛ siar ahomka n',
Hɔ minya m'ebisadze nyina;
Ɔko mu ahoɔdzen, yaw mu edur;
Asomdwee bɛn a!

MHB 536
6 . Ekyingye bɔm, suro nyina tu;
Mo sunsum pɛ akɔtsena sor;
Na m'awerɛhow mu nyinsuwakyi
So mpo pepa.

MHB 536
7 . Kɛpem dɛ m'bodu enyigye n' mu n',
Eyiedzi bi nnyi hɔ a ɔkyɛn
Dɛ muhue me kra ntunadze nyina
Mpaabɔ m' ma Wo.

MHB 537
1 . ME Nyame , ber bi wɔ anapa
Kodu ewimbir a ɔyɛ dɛw sen
Ber a efrɛ m' ba W'ananadze,
M-paabɔ ber n'.

MHB 537
2 . Nhyira aka anapa asomdwee ber,
Na ewimbir nhyira ber krɔnn no,
Ber a mudua mpaabɔ ntsaban do 
Gya wiadze hɔ.

MHB 537
3 . Ber 'i na anapawi tow nserɛmɛn a
Ɔsen anapa ewia hyerɛn gu m' do,
Na ahomka bɔsu a ofi Wo hɔ
Kyɛn wiadze dze.

MHB 537
4 . Inu m'ahoɔdzen mu fofor;
Na edze mo bɔn nyina kyɛ m';
Na edze sor enyidar kyekye
Ankonam werɛ.

MHB 537
5 . Kasa bi nntum nnkyerɛ siar ahomka n',
Hɔ minya m'ebisadze nyina;
Ɔko mu ahoɔdzen, yaw mu edur;
Asomdwee bɛn a!

MHB 537
6 . Ekyingye bɔm, suro nyina tu;
Mo sunsum pɛ akɔtsena sor;
Na m'awerɛhow mu nyinsuwakyi
So mpo pepa.

MHB 537
7 . Kɛpem dɛ m'bodu enyigye n' mu n',
Eyiedzi bi nnyi hɔ a ɔkyɛn
Dɛ muhue me kra ntunadze nyina
Mpaabɔ m' ma Wo.

MHB 538
1 . JESUS yɛ hɛn nyɛnko pa bi a
Hɛn yaw na bɔn da no do!
Yɛwɔ yiedzi bi dɛ yɛdze
Nsɛm nyina ma Ewuradze mpaabɔ m',
Mber pii yɛyew hɛn asomdwee,
Mber pii yehu amandze gyan,
Siantsire nyina nye dɛ yɛmmfa
Nsɛm nyina mma Ewuradze mpaabɔ m'!

MHB 538
2 . Yɛwɔ ahohiahia nye nsɔhwɛ?
Ana ɔhaw bi wɔ hɔ?
Mma yinom nnhyɛ hɛn abagura,
Yɛmfa mma Ewuradze mpaabɔ m',
Yebenya nyɛnko nokwafo a
Ɔnye hɛn dzi yaw dɛ Oyi?
Jesus nyim hɛn mberɛwyɛ biara;
Ka kyerɛ No wɔ mpaabɔ m'.

MHB 538
3 . Ana yɛahaw, hɛn kɔn ebu?
Yɛso dadwen durdur bi a?
Gyefo mapa n' yɛ guandɔbea;
Fa kɛma No wɔ mpaabɔ m',
Wo mfɛfo pow w', wommbu wo bi a?
Fa ma Ewuradze mpaabɔ m';
N'abasa bɔbɔ wo ho ban,
Ibenya akomatɔm'.

MHB 539
1 . Hɛn Wura, kyerɛ hɛn ma yɛnsɔr yie, 
Yɛmfia enyindzi na suro:
Kaansa yɛyɛ dɛtse na nso a,
Otwar dɛ yɛbɛn Wo.

MHB 539
2 . Yegyaa sɔr a na yeedzi emia: 
Dom hɛn tua ma yɛnsɔr!
Na yɛroboa hɛnho nye W' ehyia a,
Ewuradze, hyia hɛn kwan.

MHB 539
3 . Ma hɛn ahobrɛadze ɔnye 
Bɔn ho nnuho krɔnkrɔn,
Awerɛhyɛmu dzendzen a ɔma
Yɛtse Wo ndze nya nkwa.

MHB 539
4 . Dom hɛn gyedzi wɔ Afɔr a 
No nko tum pata bɔn n';
Ma yɛmfa enyidar enyi
Ntsim Christ n-ko ara do.

MHB 539
5 . Abotar a 'kyɛr dɛn ara a 
Ɔweɔn, ɔtweɔn na osu;
Mbanyinndam a osie hɛn kra
Na 'ruku n' mpo a ɔtwer Wo.

MHB 539
6 . Ma hɛn yi, na Wo pɛ nyɛ hɔ, 
Ma, yɛahyɛ dzen dɛm no,
Yeedua Wo Sunsum nye W' Ba do
Yɛasɔr dɛ mbrɛ ɔsɛ.

MHB 54
1 . ME kra, tsi N'ayɛyi m'
N'ehumbɔbɔr dɔ sō,
Na ɔfa ebufuw nyaa na
No bo dwe ntsɛmara.

MHB 54
2 . Nyame nnka enyim daa;
Na sɛ ɔtwe aso mpo a,
Asotwe no suar sen hɛn bɔn,
Onndu hɛn afɔdzi.

MHB 54
3 . Dɛ mbrɛ ɔsor krɔn koraa
Sen wiadze a yɛnam do n',
Dɛmara na N'adom so tse;
Ɔbor hɛn adwen do.

MHB 54
4 . Ewuradze ayamuhyehye
Wɔ hɔ ma hɔn a wosuro N', 
Ɔtse dɛ awofo baatanyɛ,
Onyim hɛn adwen do.

MHB 54
5 . Hɛn nda tse dɛ nkyɛkyɛr
Anaa anapa nhyiren;
Sɛ ehum kɛse tu fa efuw do a,
Ɔnnkyɛr na akyenkyen.

MHB 54
6 . Naaso Wo mbɔbɔrhu
Tsim hɔ mfe a ɔmmbɔ adze;
Na mbasantsen nyina bohu dɛ
W'anohoba n' si pi.   Amen.

MHB 540
1 . ME kra, fa wo nsɛm nyina bra,
Jesus dɔ dɛ ɔma mbuae;
Ɔnoara na ɔse bɔ mpaa,
Dɛm ntsi ɔnnkɛse W' oho.

MHB 540
2 . Ereba Ɔhen enyim;
Fa w'ebisadze nyina bra;
N'adom nye No tum dɔɔ so,
Ebisadze biara nnso.

MHB 540
3 . Medze m'adzesoa hyɛ ase;
Ewuradze, yi mo bɔn yi;
Ma Wo bɔgyaa a 'huee maa abɔn n'
Mpon me tsibowa mfi bɔn mu.

MHB 540
4 . Ewuradze, mepɛ ahomgye;
Fa m'akoma ndɔmmum nwionn;
Ma ɔnye Wo bɔgyaa atɔdze,
Wo nkotoo na dzi mu hen.

MHB 540
5 . Meyɛ kwantunyi wɔ ha 'i,
Wo dɔ n' nhyɛ mo sunsum dzen;
Mo Kwankyerɛfo na Nyɛnko,
Gya m' kɔ m'akwantu ewiei.  Amen.

MHB 541
1 . BƆ mpaa, kɔ do ara,
Wo Sahen na ɔka yi;
Fa enyigye yɛ setsie ma No,
Na su frɛ W'Ewuradze;
Fa w'ehiadze brɛ No,
Bɔ mpaa ka kyerɛ Nyame;
Bɔ mpaa daa;mma mmpa abaw da;
Bɔ mpaa, kɔ do ara!

MHB 541
2 . Dua fɛkuwbɔ mu nko,
Twe bɛn Nyame gyedzi m',
Fa tum a ɔwɔ mpaabɔ mu
Kɔ N'abangua enyim,
Kɔ N'asɔrdan no mu,
Mmfi N'afɔrmbukyia enyim;
Ma efiefi nyina nhu No som,
Na akoma nyina nhu No dɔ.

MHB 541
3 . Fa wo kra ma Nyame,
Fa w' kra kotow N'enyim,
Tserɛw w'akoma nye wo nsamu
Serɛ asomdwee ma Zion;
Kaa w'akwankyerɛfo
Nye wo nuanom nyina;
Tserɛw wo mpaabɔ abasa mu,
Ka adasamba nyina fua.

MHB 541
4 . Kɔ kan ahoɔdzen mu,
Aperper mu bɔ mpaa,
Tsia sum mu etumfo hɔn do,
Na dzi konyim wɔ ko m';
Ma Sunsum n' nkeka mu
Mfrɛ nsordaafo no mbra, 
Kodu dɛ Christ fi sor besian
Abɛfa 'nyimdzifo n'.

MHB 542
1 . JESUS, m'enyidado,
Me dadwen da Wo do,
Mbrɛhoadze mu na mohwɛ Wo,
Minyim dɛ etsie m' mpaabɔ,
Ma montweɔn Wo nkotoo,
Na meetum adze nyina yɛ
Wɔ Wo mu, Ɔwo ebɔɔ adze nyina,
Eyɛɛ adze nyina fofor.

MHB 542
2 . Mepɛ nyamesuro,
Enyiwa a ohu adze,
Ɔhwɛ Wo ber a bɔn abɛn,
Ɔma gyigyefo n' guan;
Sunsum ayɛ krado,
Ɔdze nhwɛyie bɔ ban,
Ogyina n'aweɔmber mu pi,
Mpaabɔ mu daa nyina.

MHB 542
3 . Mepɛ adwen pa bi a
Ogyina hɔ pintsinn,
Onnsuro hwee, ɔmmpɛ akatua,
Gyina ma Wo dzin kɛse n';
Ɔtwe W'ayɛyi a
Onnyi ewiei ho nyinkun,
Dze pɛ pa ahwehwɛ, esua dɛ
Wɔnkamfo W'adom no.

MHB 542
4 . Medan W'asɛm pa no,
Anohoba n' yɛ m' dze;
M'ekyigyina nkwagye, Ewuradze,
Fi Wo nkotoo hɔ ba;
Na mingyina dzen yie,
M'enyidar dɛmara,
Kodu dɛ edze mo sunsum
Bɛba Wo dɔ pa n' mu.

MHB 543
1 . EWURADZE, tsie m' mpaabɔ 
Na tsie mo sufrɛ so,
Kaa W'asɛm a ɔyɛ nokwar no,
Minya mbuae adom mu ara.

MHB 543
2 . Mma mmfa atsɛmbu mmba koraa,
Mma nnhwɛ W'akowaa abrabɔ m';
Wɔ W'enyiwa mu, tsenenee
Nnyi adasamba mu.

MHB 543
3 . Metsen me nsa kyerɛ
Wo krɔnkrɔn-bea hɔ no,
Nsukɔm dze me kra dɛ asaase a
Etwee hwehwɛ W'adom.

MHB 543
4 . O Ewuradze, bra ntsɛm
Bɛgye m'akoma fa,
Mma nnhunta na morohwe ase
Dɛ ɔkra a ɔahwe owumaa m'.

MHB 543
5 . Me gyedzi per ahwɛ
W'ehumbɔbɔr kan no;
Ma mennantsew W'enyim kan mu!
Medze me kra ma Wo.

MHB 543
6 . Ma Wo Sunsum nkyerɛ
M'anamɔn tsenenee akwan;
Na Ewuradze, Wo dzin ntsi ma
Me tsir do fi ngyigye m'.  Amen.

MHB 544
1 . Bɛkyebo Kan! Bɛkyebo Kan! 
Mbrɛ kra ho wɔ dɛ ɔtsew
Wɔ W'enyim a, Ehuntahunii;
Ɔmmpem adze, mbom ɔdze dɛw
Tum gyina na ɔhwɛ Wo.

MHB 544
2 . W'ahengua ho esunsum dze 
Tum sɔw siar hyɛnn no;
Na hɔn nko na hɔn su tse dɛm,
Osiandɛ wonnhum bɔn wiadze a
Ɔtse dɛ iyi pɛn.

MHB 544
3 . Ao, m'bɛyɛ dɛn na 'mi a wɔawo m' 
Sum mu, m'adwen kusuww,
Metum mepue, Nyame, Wenyim,
Na mo sunsum kwatserkwaa yi
Asɔw nserɛmɛn hyɛnn no?

MHB 544
4 . Kwan bi wɔ hɔ ma nyimpa dɛ 
Ɔdze fow kɔ sor fie;
Afɔr bi a wɔabɔ ama hɛn,
Nyame enyim Twitwagyefo,
Sunsum krɔnkrɔn No tum.

MHB 544
5 . Yinom na wɔyɛ hɛn krado 
Ma sor krɔnkrɔnyɛ no;
Sum mu mba a yɛyɛ atɔbɔ
Nam domankoma Dɔ no do,
Bɛtsena bɛkyebo Kanm'.

MHB 545
1 . YI W'enyim fɛɛfɛw n' kyerɛ m'!
Kenyan m'ahoɔdzen a agow;
Dom me kra a ɔatɔ bitsi
Dɛ asaase wesee hia nsu n',
Sian bra, m'Ewuradze, mma nnkyɛr,
Bra, m'Agyenkwa, bra ntsɛntsɛm!

MHB 545
2 . Woara nyim dɛ munntum nnhom,
Gyedɛ mohom wɔ Wo mu,
Gyedɛ wosow wɔ mo mu,
Gyedɛ migyaa bɔn yɛ koraa,
Gyedɛ 'hyɛ m'abrabɔ ma,
Minya sor dɔ dzi dɛw.

MHB 545
3 . O Ewuradze, nye me nkɔ!
'Nye me ntsena amma meennguan;
W'asɛm nhyɛ m' dzen wɔ mo mu;
Minya awerɛkyekyer mo mu;
Suo me nsamu ma munhu Wo,
Yɛ m' nokwafo kodu ewiei.  Amen.

MHB 546
1 . Agyenkwa Jesus, fi sor bra! 
Fa W'adom krɔnkrɔn n' bɔboa me:
Pra wiadze dɔ fi m'akomam'
Na siesie mu fa ma Woho.

MHB 546
2 . O, ma Wo krɔnkrɔnyɛ nhyɛ n' ma  
Na mo sunsum no kɔn ndɔ Wo!
Ewia o, anago, o, me pɛ kor
Nye dɛ minya Wo midzi mee.

MHB 546
3 . Kwan a m'Agyenkwa, W'anamɔn 
Hyerɛn mu n', nna m'boduam' mbrɛhoadzem';
Minnketsie na mennkɛka dɔ
Fofor bi ho asɛm dɛ Wodze n'.

MHB 546
4 .	Me kra a metu mahyɛ Wo nsa 'i, 
Mma enyigye huhuw nnyam' kyɛpɛn:
Woara fa, na Ewɔ ho kwan
Dɛ akoma n' nyina No Wura.

MHB 546
5 . Ɔwo nko ara na mutum, 
Medze enyigye krɔnn dɔ Wo;
Egyigye kɛse bɛn nye yi
Dɛ muhu dɛ edze m' yɛ Wodze!

MHB 546
6 . Moronnhwehwɛ wiadze 'i mu hwee 
Dɛ Wo dɔ krɔnn n' wɔ m'akomam':
Iyiara nko na m'bɔhwehwɛ
Na megyaa ndzɛmba nkaa nyinam'.

MHB 547
1 . ADZE a me Nyame kyir
Biara mennkɛyɛ bio,
Ewuradze, bɔ W'abɔdze bio
Yɛ me kra yi fofor.

MHB 547
2 . Me kra tse dɛ Wodze n',
Okyir adze a ho nntsew,
Na ɔsor dɔ n' atsew no ho
Ma oegyaa bɔn yɛ koraa.

MHB 547
3 . Wo nhyira mbrasɛm no,
Jesus, ma me nsa nka,
Sunsum no sor nkwa mbrasɛm no,
Kyerɛw wɔ m'akoma m'.

MHB 547
4 . Dua no mo mu ma ɔndɔ,
Mma onntutu nngu da,
Na bɔn nkoasom ndan fahodzi,
Ɔdɔ mapa mbrasɛm n'.

MHB 547
5 . Wo su nyɛ me mbrasɛm,
W'ahotsew krɔnkrɔn no;
Fa dɛw twe me kra enyigye m'
Mber nyina bɛn Woho.

MHB 547
6 . Me kra ne kra tsim
Ɔwo a ehyɛ ne nyina ma,
Ewuradze, hyɛ Egya Ne pɛ
Nyina ma wɔ mo mu bio.  Amen.

MHB 548
1 . Adze nyinaa ne yɛ nnyɛ dzen mma  
Nyia otum gye Jesu dzin dzi;
Munngu Wo nokwar n' ho fi bio,
Mo Wura, megye n' dɔ mu ara;
Mutum, megye Wo dzi ampa,
Adze nyinaa ne yɛ nnyɛ dzen mma m'.

MHB 548
2 . Dza ɔyɛ dzen sen adze nyina 
Nye dɛ m'begyaa bɔn yɛ koraa;
Naaso ne yɛ nnyɛ dzen, minyim:
Jesus, hwɛ Wo nokwaredzi no!
Sɛ biribiara nnyɛ dzen mma Wo a,
Adze nyina ne yɛ nnyɛ dzen mma m'

MHB 548
3 . Asaase nye hɛll gye kyim mpo a, 
Nyame N'asɛm nnkotwa apaw da;
Eguambaa n' beyi mo bɔn koraa,
Ampa, sɛ ɔyɛ dzen mpo a;
Dza ɔyɛ dzen mpo ɔbɛyɛ;
Adze nyina ne yɛ nnyɛ dzen mma m'.

MHB 548
4 . Adze nyina Nyame yɛ ma ɔyɛ, 
Christ so, nyimpam' Nyame tum no,
Mo so, wɔayɛ m'fofor koraa n',
Wɔayɛ m' fofor wɔ Christ mu no,
Midzi dase n', mefi bɔn nsa n',
Adze nyina ne yɛ nnyɛ dzen mma m'.

MHB 549
1 . EWURADZE, ma musua Wo,
Ma menyɛ ahobrɛadze koraa,
Ma me kra mbrɛ noho adze,
Ma m'enyi ntsim Wo nko do.

MHB 549
2 . Ma mingyaa me pɛ nsi nkyɛn, 
Mingyaa m'ahantan nyina,
Mingyaa moho mma Nyame,
Mfa m'adwen nto W'ananadze.

MHB 549
3 . M'ahantan nyansa nyɛ kwa,
Menyɛ botoo dɛ abofra,
Munhu adze wɔ Wo kan mu,
Mennantsew W'ahoɔdzen mu.

MHB 549
4 . Ma minnya W'adom nkyerɛkyerɛ,
Nokwar na tsenenee sunsum;
Minnya nyimdze nye sor dɔ,
Nye onnyiewiei nkwa m'akoma m'.   Amen.

MHB 55
1 . EWURADZE nsakyer nyina wura
Adze nyina eyɛ no fofor,
Ͻwo ennsakyer       da;
Mbrɛ eyɛ biara, mbrɛ etse biara,
Wo nkorͻfo wɔ Wo mu kyɛfa,
Eda ho yɛ hɛndze.

MHB 55
2 . Mbersantsen Panyin, yɛtse W’ mu;
Wo mfesantsen mu na yenya
Hɛn asomdwee na dɛw;
Yɛhom wͻ hɛn daa Nyame mu,
Yɛtsena dwudwoodwɔ, asomdweem’,
Wͻ Ͻwo a ennsakyer da m’.

MHB 55
3 . Sunsum a ‘yɛ adze nyina fofor,
Ͻwo dzi kan, yedzi ekyir,
Hɛn sor akwantu mu.
Wo nkenyan gya hɛn ma yɛhyerɛn,
Na yɛdze ahoͻdzen kͻ enyim,
Yɛkͻ do dzi konyim.

MHB 55
4 . Yɛgya sum na suro wͻ ekyir,
Yenya kan fofor na enyimnyam,
Yenya ahenman fofor;
‘Dze adom awoo na mpuei fofor ba;
Yɛtow konyimdzi ndwom fofor
Hyira Foforyɛnyi n’.

MHB 55
5 . Yɛsoɛr na yɛhom wͻ Wo mu,
Yɛtsena fie, yepue  kͻhwehwɛ;
Yɛda ho tse Wo mu.
Dɛw na ahodwuruw yɛ kɛse;
Ͻma yenya nkwa fofor fi
Nyame a ennsakyer da hͻ.

MHB 550
1 . Ao, nkyɛ meenya 'koma a bɔn nnyim  
Dze eyi Nyame ayɛw!
Dza ɔtse Wo bɔgyaa no tum,
Bɔgya a wɔkae gui maa m'.

MHB 550
2 . Akoma a ɔdwe, bɔbɔfo, 
Mo Pomfo N'ahengua,
Mbrɛ Christ n-ko na ɔkasa,
Mbrɛ Jesus nko dzi hen.

MHB 550
3 . Akoma brɛfo a ɔtwer Wo, 
Nokwafo a no mu tsew;
'Koma a nkwa anaa wu nntum mmpaa
Mmfi nyia ɔtsem' no ho.

MHB 550
4 . Akoma a ɔasakyer koraa, 
Na Nyame dɔ ahyɛm' ma;
Odzi mu, na no mu tsew koraa,
Nyame, ɔnye Wo sɛ!

MHB 550
5 . Ewuradze, fa Wo suban ma m'! 
Ma me nsa nka sesei!
Kyerɛw dzin fofor n' m'akoma do,
Wo dzin a ɔyɛ Dɔ n'.   Amen.

MHB 551
1 . SƐ yɛdze hɛn dadwen to W' do a;
Ewuradze, nkyɛ yebedzi dɛw;
Sɛ yɛsakyer hɛn su a,
Yɛtse hɛn akoma m' dɛ Obi wɔ sor,
Ɔyɛ nyansabuakwa nye ɔdɔ,
Ɔreyɛ edwuma pa.

MHB 551
2 . Ɔbra a yɛbɔ daa yi ntamu twe,
Ɔsɛɛ asomdwee awerɛfir m' daa,
Nkekam' a ɔma abagura,
O nkyɛ yeetum apow ne nyina!
Dza yɛtwer no wiadze nyina,
Dze aahyɛ Wo tum nsamu.

MHB 551
3 . Sɛ yɛkotow dze hɛn adzesoa
Gu Nyame enyim mpaabɔ mu,
Na yɛdze enyigye soɛr.
Yenyim dɛ Egya no ɔbɛn,
Ɔma akonkoran gyaa su a,
Yesuro N' ntsi obetsie hɛn.

MHB 551
4 . Nyame, ma hɛn akoma kyingyefo 'i
Nsua mfi nnoma nye nhyiren hɔ;
Na wɔmpow hɔnho koraa,
Wongyaa ndzɛmba nyina mma Egya n' pɛ,
Na wɔwɔ N'enyim ɔhaw mu n',
Wɔnsɔ asomdwee nhwɛ.

MHB 552
1 . JESUS, bɔn mpata Guambaa,
Wodze a, Wo nko Wodze nye m';
Fa mo honam, sunsum, kra,
Ne nyina yɛ Wo nko dze.

MHB 552
2 . M'ehiadze kortsee nye Wo,
Ma mentetar Wo afebɔɔ;
Ma memfa no mu dza oye,
Memfa m'akoma mma Wo.

MHB 552
3 . Adasa mu dansewa,
Mma me nnsan m'ekyir nkɔ bio,
Mimmfi nhyira esutsen ho,
Monnkotow enyigye bɔn mu.

MHB 552
4 . Mowɔ woana wɔ ase ha?
Wo nkotsee ara na minyim,
Mowɔ woana sor dɛ Wo?
Eyɛ m'adze nyinara.

MHB 552
5 . M'akoradze nyina wɔ sor,
M'ahodze nyina nye W' dɔ;
Woana tum twa dɔ no bo?
Onnyi ewiei nnyi nhwehwɛmu.

MHB 553
1 . SIAN, Sunsum Krͻnkrͻn gya a ema nkwa!
Sian bͻhom gu m’akoma mu,
Mpata bͻgya apetse do n' mu;
Yi Woho kyerɛ mo sunsum,
Mentse Wo tum adzeyɛ nka,
Munhu dɛ Nyankopͻn awo m’.

MHB 553
2 . Membrɛ moho adze ngye nkyérɛkyérɛ;
O ma menyɛ abofra a ͻdwe,
Ntsiatsia mo Wfira n’anamon mu!
Mma me kra nnhu W’ebufuwhyew,
'Nyitan, ’nyiber, nyinkuntwe nkͻ;
Ͻdo m’ na yɛ ndzɛmba fofor.

MHB 553
3 . Mma wiadze nye W’ nnkyɛ m’akoma,
Wͻmbͻ emi nye Christ mbeamudua m’.
Me kra nyina per hwehwɛ Wo;
Munwu mma wiadze mu ndzɛmba,
Nkotompn nye enyigye hun,
Wo nkotoo nyɛ m’apɛdze pa.

MHB 553
4 . Na Woara hye m‘apɛdze do;
Munhu kan a ͻwͻ Wo kan mu.
Memfa enyimtsewee nhwɛ Wo;
Wͻafrɛ m' dɛ menkyérɛ W‘ gyedzi tum,
Ma m’akoma a ho tsew nyɛ ͻdͻ,
Me bra a fi nnyi ho nyɛ ayɛyi.  Amen.

MHB 554
1 . SUNSUM a ema tum,
O bra bɛtsena mo mu!
Fa enyimnyam fahodzi no bra,
Fi yaw, suro nye bɔn mu.

MHB 554
3 . Bɔn yarba no n'aba n',
Apɔwmudzen Sunsum, yi;
Krɔnkrɔnyɛ a odzi mu Sunsum, 
Ɔdɔ Sunsum mapa.

MHB 554
4 . Ma ehurusi da n' mbra ntsɛm
Mbɛhyew mo bɔn nyina,
Da a ndzɛmba dadaw botwa mu,
Na adze nyina ayɛ fofor.

MHB 554
5 . Ewuradze, dzi m' dase
Dɛ dza meyɛ no ye,
Dɛ mbrɛ Wo pɛ nye W'asɛm kyerɛ,
Ɔyɛ W' enyisɔ koraa.

MHB 554
6 . Mennserɛ dzibew a ɔkrɔn;
Pen ebisadze yi do,
Ntsɛm anaa ekyim, Woara kyerɛ ase
Kɔ me nhyira m' afebɔɔ. Amen.

MHB 555
1 . AGYENKWA, ber bɛn ara na
M'begyaa moho ama Wo nwionn?
Hianyi a mennsɛ hwee enyi do,
Na ' wo bu me onyansafo.

MHB 555
2 . Wo nko na mepɛ meehu,
Minnyim wiadze yi mu hwee
Wo kan nko na ɔkyerɛ me kwan,
Wo tum nko na ɔhyɛ me dzen.

MHB 555
3 . Nkyɛ meehu Wo Sunsum No,
Ɔmfa me nyɛ dza ɔpɛ;
Sɛ minnyim ɔkwan no mpo a,
Dɛm na menye W' bɛyɛ kor.

MHB 555
4 . Makyerɛ m'abrabɔ mu yie,
Krɔnkrɔn no krɔn nyinara,
Ma mo sunsum nkyerɛ mbrɛ
Ahobrɛadze dɔ n' bun tse.  Amen.

MHB 556
1 . BUR pirakùr a Wo nsa atow no
Wɔ kra bɔbɔfo yi m’;
Kodu dέ ehumbɔbɔr besian,
Bɔboa m’ ma meedzi mu.

MHB 556
2 . Wo nkrantseѐ anofaenu ne ndam
Ɔma mutum gyina;
Medze ‘kokὸdur bɛkà dɛ
Ewùradzѐ asa me yar.

MHB 556
3 . Muhù ahyɛdzѐ a ɔsὸ mbordὸ a
 Wɔakà ne nyina abɔ m’;
Bue m’akoma mu ma mentse
Esùmaɛm n’ ase yie.

MHB 556
4 . Nkyɛ menye W’ahotsewfo no
Aasɔ Wo suahù ahwɛ!
Ne tsentsen, ne trɛ nye no krɔn,
Na dɔ mapa no bun.   Amen.

MHB 557
1 . HƐN frɛ enyidado no nye bɛn?
Dɛ hɛn mu bɛyɛ krɔnn;
'Yi ntsi mohwɛ Jesus Noara,
Medze abotar tweɔn yi.

MHB 557
2 . Motweɔn dɛ ɔbɛtsew mo ho,
Dze nkwa tum bɛma me,
'Bɛma m' gyedzi a ɔbɔ bɔn gu,
Na ɔtsew akoma mu.

MHB 557
3 . Iyi nye adom a ɔgye hɛn nkwa,
Dze kyɛ abɔnfo kwa;
Ampaara ɔbɛyɛ dɛm ama m',
Ndzebɔnyɛfo hen nye m'.

MHB 557
4 . Ɔbɔpon me efi emumuyɛ
Beberee nyina mu koraa;
Mowɔ gyedzi wɔ Jesus mu,
Medze moho ma No.

MHB 557
5 . Jesus yɛ m'akoma ne fie a,
Mo bɔn nyina bɔkɔ;
Na tsie, ɔse; Mereba ntsɛm,
Ebedzi w'akoma m' hen.

MHB 557
6 . Yɛ no dɛ mbrɛ W'asɛm no tse!
Pon me fi bɔn nyina m',
Afei m'akoma bɛgye Wo;
Bra mu, Ewuradze, bra!    Amen.

MHB 558
1 . ABϽN Gyefo, morotweͻn akyérɛ
De Jesus dzin nye m’ayarsa;
’Dͻ ewie n‘edwuma yɛ n’, mepɛ ahwer
Dza mowͻ, tum yɛ, na meyɛ.
W’asɛm na ͻma metse nkwa mu,
Akowaa bɛyɛ dɛ no Wura.

MHB 558
2 . Wo nkwa a ͻsom bo a dze mae no
Kyérɛ adorn n’ase wͻ mo mu;
Yi me fi emumuyɛ nyina m’;
Ma me dzibew. memfata sor:
Gyedɛ tsew mo ho fi nyina m’,
Wo yaw nye me gyedzi yɛ kwa.

MHB 558
3 . Ana ennwu ma maatséna ase?
Menntse ase mma moho bio,
Nyimpadua, ͻkra, nye sunsum,
Medze ma Wo a ’dze woho maa me n’;
Fa adzeson a edze W’bͻgyaa tͻe n’,
Bra, mo Wura nye me Nyankopͻn.

MHB 558
4 . Wo nokwar nye mbͻbͻrhu ntsi
Gye W'akowaa yɛ Woara Wodze;
Tsew W'enyimnyam dzin ho mo mu;
Fa m' yɛ Wo nko Wodze ndɛ ara,
Sesa m' na ma mo ho ntsew koraa;
Mentsena ase, nwu mma Wo nko.  Amen.

MHB 559
1 . NYAME, bɔsɔw bɔhyɛ n' ano
Dwuruw bɔn kokwaa yi gu;
Ma kra a ɔatɔ bitsi yi
Nkyerɛ Wo dɔ ne ndam.

MHB 559
2 . Mepɛ Wo bra na W' krɔnkrɔnyɛ,
Wo tsenenee mbra mo mu;
Mibisa, hwehwɛ, atwer Wo,
Ma wɔaapon m' efi bɔn m'.

MHB 559
3 . Bɔ ebufuw, 'nyihaw na ntsɛn ham,
Womfi hɔ dɛm ber yi m';
Wonkogu mo Pomfo bɔgyaa a
Orubu asorɛkye n' mu!

MHB 559
4 . Agyenkwa, me kra tsim Wo do,
Me mprempren Gyefo nye W'!
Awerɛhyɛm' enyidar nyina m',
M'bisa nhyira sesei.

MHB 559
5 . Woewiei yɛ! Ber yi, gye hɛn nkwa,
Fa nkwagye hyira hɛn;
Menya Wo bɔgyaa mu nkwagye,
'Dɔ mapa nye asomdwee.

MHB 56
1 . W'ADOM ho nkaakaa no yɛ dɛw, 
Me Nyame, mo sor Hen, 
Ma Wo tsenenee fi ber to ber 
Ntow enyimnyam ho ndwom.

MHB 56
2 . Nyame dzi hen wɔ sor naaso 
N'adɔe no nntsena hɔ nko: 
N'ayamuyie hyerɛn wiadze nyina,
Ɔma ehiadze nyina.

MHB 56
3 . Abɔdze nyina hwɛ Wo kwan,
Ma aama hɔn daa edziban; 
W'ayamuyie nsa no ma hɔn nam, 
 Dze ndzepa hyɛ hɔn anomu.

MHB 56
4 . Ewuradze yɛ ayamuhyehye, 
N'ebufuw so yɛ nyaa;
Ɔnnkyɛr na ɔdze ne fakyɛ asɛm
Ma ɔkra a ɔdɔ n' n'enyi gye.

MHB 56
5 . Abɔdze, mbasantsen nyina, 
Kamfo W', yi Wo tum ayɛw; 
Hɛn a yenya W'adom kɛse no, 
Dze dɛw hyira Wo dzin.

MHB 560
1 . JESUS wui na maatsena ase
Ama Nyame nkotoo,
No mu na minya onnyiewiei nkwa;
Yɛayɛ kor sunsum mu.

MHB 560
2 . Agyenkwa, meda adom 'i ho ase,
Akyɛdze a onnyi kabea!
Metserɛw gyedzi abaw m' yɛ W' ettu,
Na metse Wo dɔ nka.

MHB 560
3 . Me kra enya pɛ dzendzen a
Ɔtweɔn sɔ nhyira no hwɛ;
M'akoma a ɔhyew ekitsa n'
Hwɛ kwan dɛ ɔbɛnan dɔ m'.

MHB 560
4 . Fa Woho ma m' ma mingyaa ntuw
Nye ɔpɛ huhuw mu;
Mbrɛ metse biara nyew Wo mu,
Na fa Woho ma me.

MHB 560
5 . W'akyɛdze no nko mmee me koraa,
Gyedɛ Woara ka ho;
W'enyim yɛ me paradize sɔnn,
Bea a ewɔ n' yɛ heaven.

MHB 561
1 . M'EWURADZE Jesus Christ N'Egya,
M'Agyenkwa nye me Tsir,
Motwer Nyia Wo tum asɛm no
Onyaan No fii ewufo m' n'.

MHB 561
2 . Ama adasamba onnyiewiei nkwa,
Ne nyina wɔ Jesus mu;
Na hɔn a wɔhwehwɛ No nyina
Nya enyigye wɔ sor.

MHB 561
3 . Me gyedzi wohu wɔ W' tum mu,
Na gyedzi yi fir Wo;
Efrɛ ewufo fi adakamaa m',
Wiadzi fi W'asɛm m' ba.

MHB 561
4 . Enyidado hun m' enyidar,
Nyimpa - hun, megye dzi;
Wo nkenyan asɛm hyɛ me dzen,
Edze W' Sunsum bɛma m'.

MHB 561
5 . Gyedzi na anohoba no hwɛ,
No nkotoo na ɔhwɛ;
Ɔserew ndzɛmba a ne yɛ yɛ dzen,
Na ɔka dɛ otum yɛ!

MHB 562
1 . NYAME a Wo tum, nokwar na adom,
Betsim mbersantsen, mfesantsen,
Sor na ase twa mu kɔ mpo a,
N'asɛm betsim hɔ daa nyina.

MHB 562
2 . N-kyɛ maabɔ W'adom dawur
Ma adasa eehu Wo nokwar n'!
Tsew W'enyimnyam dzin kɛse n' ho,
Krɔnkrɔnyɛ ndzi mu wɔ mo mu.

MHB 562
3 . Hohor mo bɔn biara fi hɔ;
Totow m'ehonyi nyinara gu;
Tsew mo ho fi adwembɔn biara m',
Fi efifidze na ahopɔw m'.

MHB 562
4 . Ma m'akoma fofor a odzi mu,
Mimfi ekyingye, suro na yaw nsa;
Ma me adwen a nna Christ wɔ n' bi,
Na mo sunsum ntakyer Wo ho.

MHB 562
5 . Ao, nkyɛ afei meefi bɔn nsa,
W'asɛm no aaba mu pefee,
Maahɛn anohoba ahomgye m'!
Wo dɔ a odzi mu n' ne Caanan

MHB 563
1 . MO Wura, megye dzi dɛ ahomgye
Wɔ hɔ ma Wo nkorɔfo;
Ahomgye a dɛw mapa dzi m' hɛn
Na Wo ho dɔ wɔ mu.

MHB 563
2 . Ahomgye a ɔyɛ hɛn kra apɛdze
Gyina sor ndzɛmba do,
Mbrɛ suro, bɔn nye yaw nyina wu,
'Dɔ mapa tu go koraa.

MHB 563
3 . O nkyɛ meehu dɛm ahomgye n',
Me gyedzi aakɔ mu!
Afei m'Agyenkwa, fa tum ma m',
Na ma mingyaa bɔn yɛ.

MHB 563
4 . Dza ɔyɛ dzen mfi m'akoma m',
Na ekyingye yi mfi hɔ;
Gyedzi a aka no fa ma me
Wɔ dɔ ahomgye n' mu.

MHB 563
5 . M'bɛyɛ Wodze, Woara nyim dɛm,
Medze W' ayɛ me dze;
O m'adze pa a ɔsom mo bo,
Wo nko na mohwehwɛ.

MHB 563
6 . Wo dzin ama menya Wo su;
Iyi nko dze, fa ma m';
Memmpɛ hwee dɛ me Nyankopɔn,
Wɔ asaase do anaa sor.

MHB 564
1 . Egya, megye dzi pi 
Dɛ eyɛ mbɔbɔrhufo:
'Bɛsan me kra fɔdzifo n' ho,
Na ayɛ me fofor.

MHB 564
2 . Dɛm a, Jesus ntsi, bra, 
Ma m'akoma mu ntsew:
Botwa mo fona nyina do,
Na ma mingyaa bɔn yɛ.

MHB 564
3 . Adom do na menam 
Mesan meba Wo hɔ:
Ewuradze, to m'akoma pan
Na krɔnkrɔnyɛ nhyɛ n' ma.

MHB 564
4 . Mosɔr mberɛw mu serɛ tum, 
Hyɛ W'ahendzi no ma
Ndɛ a wɔfrɛ no n-dɛ yi,
Na mennkɛyɛ bɔn bio.

MHB 564
5 . Munntum nnhor m'akoma, 
Gyedɛ megye Wo dzi,
Na motweɔn Wo bɔgyaa a ɔma 
Wansayɛ krɔnkrɔn no.

MHB 564
6 . Meda W'asɛndua ase 'i, 
Jesus, dom me W'adom.
Fa Wo bɔgyaa a ɔhor bɔn no
Hoa m' dɛ esukwankyɛba.

MHB 565
1 . Minyim dɛ mo Pomfo tse ase, 
Na ɔsɔr ma me daa nyina;
Ɔma No dɔ ho sɛnkyerɛdze,
Eyiedzi ahobadze a.

MHB 565
2 . Muhu N' dɛ ɔrema me tsir do, 
Ɔdze nkwagye abɛn ha,
W'enyim yɛ me dehye ampaara,
Na ɔnnkɛkyɛr na ɔaba.

MHB 565
3 . Ɔpɛ dɛ meyɛ hotsewnyi;

Ɔbɛhyɛ m' ma ampaara

MHB 565

MHB 565

MHB 566
1 . NYAME, adom nyina Pomfo,
Wo fakyɛ dɔ no hyɛ hɛn
Ma yɛma hɛn kra do ma W',
Yɛdze hɛn nyimpadua ma W';
Gye hɛn afɔrbɔdze yi fa,
Yɛdze fa Wo Ba no do,
Yɛtse ase ma Wo nkotoo,
Sɛ yewu, a yewu ma Wo.

MHB 566
2 . Ɔfata na ɔtsen na oye,
Dɛ yɛbɛyɛ Wo nko dze,
Wo mu nko na hɛn enyi gye,
Yɛnka Wo nhyira som ho;
Nkyɛ edwuma nye asɛm biara
Aabɔ W' papayɛ dawur;
Krɔnkrɔnyɛ nka Ewuradze. 
Wɔnkyerɛw hɛn akoma pon do! Amen.

MHB 567
1 . ENYIGYE mapa mu na 
Medze moho ma Wo;
Wo nkotoo Wodze koraa,
M'bɛyɛ Wo nko dze daa.

MHB 567
2 . O Nyame Ba edɔ me,
M'bɛyɛ Wo nko Wodze;

MHB 567

'Bɛyɛ Wo nko Wodze.

MHB 567
4 . O Jesus, bra bedzi hen,
Dzi biribiara do hen;

MHB 568
1 . MENYA Ɔba n' nsamu fahodzi 'i,
Ma monsɔ m' fahodzi nhwɛ;

Ndzi nyim wɔ nkwa adom mu;
Mfa enyigye nkyerɛ Wo pɛ n',
Enyimnyam wɔ dɔ mapa m'.

MHB 568
2 . Abba, Egya, tsie Wo ba,
Ka me bɔ m' wɔ Jesus mu;
Tsie na petse adom nhyira n',
Wɔ dɛw, asomdwee nye tum m';
M'Agyenkwa, serɛ wɔ sor ma m',
Nkwa na sor dɔ nyinara.

MHB 568
3 . Ɔsor Adam, ɔsor Nkwa,
Dan mo su ma ɔnsɛ Wodze;
Hɛn me kra nyinara mu,
Hyɛ no dzen na hyɛ no ma;
Ɔnyɛ dɛ menntse honam m'
Na mbom mentse Wo mu.

MHB 568
4 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, mma nnyɛ ekyim;

Dzi dase mo sunsum mu,
Ɔnyɛ dzen na ontsim hɔ;
N-kwa nsunyiwa, hue ma m',
Tsena m'akoma m' afebɔɔ. Amen.

MHB 569
1 . Wodze daa! Ɔdɔ Nyame, 
Fi sor W'ahenguam tsie hɛn;
Yɛnyɛ Wodze afebɔɔ,
Wɔ ha na mbersantsen nyinam'.

MHB 569
2 . Wodze daa! n-kwa Wura, 
Kora hɛn wɔ bra aperdzim';
Wo nye Nkwa n', Nokwar n' na Kwan n',
Gya hɛn kɔ kan man no mu.

MHB 569
3 . Wodze daa! Ao, esiarfo 
Bɛn nye hɔn a wɔhom Wo mu!
Gyefo, Weɔmfo, Sor Nyɛnko,
Ao, twitwa gye hɛn kɔ ewiei!

MHB 569
4 . Wodze daa! Oguanhwɛfo, 
Wo nguan a wɔyɛ mberɛw;
Woara kora hɔn yie,
Fa W'ayamuyie dom hɛn nyina.

MHB 569
5 . Wodze daa! hɛn Kwangyefo, 
Ema hɛn dza yehia nyina,
Hɛn bɔn nyina edze kyɛ hɛn,
Ewuradze, gya hɛn kɔ sor.

MHB 57
1 . MENYE Wo ntamu dwumadzi mu n'. 
Ɔyɛ dzen ma me kra,
Dɛ obotum esuma efi
W'enyim a innhu no.

MHB 57
2 . W'enyi bɔ wiadze nyina aprɔw, 
Hu mo soɛr na me nda,
Me bagua m' na mo nsumaa m' asɛm
Na m'akoma mu nsɛm.

MHB 57
3 . Owura, inyim mo nsusui, 
Ansaana madwen mpo; 
Na m'bobue m'ano akà 
asɛm no, 
Inyim dza mepɛ akyerɛ.

MHB 57
4 . Nyimdzee nwanwa a ɔdɔ, ɔkrɔn;
Hen na abɔdze bosuma?
Meda W'abaw a atserɛw mu do;
Etwa mo ho ehyia.

MHB 57
5 . N-tsi ma W'adom n'ntwa mo ho, 
Na ɔmbɔ mo ho ban,
Na wo dɔ kɛse no nkora
Me kra mfi mbusu ho.    Amen.

MHB 570
1 . KRƆNKRƆN nye tsenenee Wura,
Mobɔtweɔn masɔ Wo pɛ ahwɛ;
Kaa dza W'adom asɛm no se,
Fa Wo Sunsum no hyɛ me nsew.

MHB 570
2 . W'adom nhyɛ m' fɛr, mfa me ndɔmmum,
M'bekyir mankasa mo suban;
Tum, akɛseyɛ, ayɛyi,
Enyimnyam nka m'Ewuradze Christ.

MHB 570
3 . Ma minnya emudzi a ɔkrɔn,
Afei mma monnhwe ase hwee ho;
Mma monntɔ sin wɔ W'enyim da,
Munhu dɛ Christ yɛ adze nyina.

MHB 571
1 . NHYIRA nye hɔn a hɔn akὸma m’ tsew,
Woesuà abɔfo hɔn ndzeyɛɛ,
Wɔ asaase do nye sor,
Wohu Nyamé a wonnhu no,
Wɔahor hɔn ho bɔn nkekãã,
Wonya No mu fɛkuwbɔ;
Aka kùmaa wɔato hɔn Wùrà a
Ɔyɛ hɔn mfaso kɛse n'.

MHB 571
2 . Wɔsom wɔ sunsum mu ndɛ
Kotow No N'abangua do;
Nkataenyim hyɛnhyɛn n’ enyim,
Nyame N’enyim hyérɛn dua mu.
Wɔwɔ ’nyiber, ‘wɔdwe,
Nkyérɛkyérɛ mu mbadwembafo.
Wɔhwehwɛ Kyérɛwsɛm no mu
Kodu dɛ wɔtse Ne ndze.

MHB 571
3 . Abɔdze m’ ɔyɛ hɔndze.
. Wohyia N’ wɔ N‘abangua do;
Tsitsir wɔ N‘ahomgye mu,
Adzekyee nye ewimbir.
Wɔtwer N’ abrabɔ nyina m’.
Yaw, dadwen nà akodzi mu;
’Yinom tse dέ ewiaber fua
Gyegye wo Ne hyerɛn mu.

MHB 571
4 . Hɔn ahomgu nyina ho tsew:
Owu, worunnhu bi da,
Wɔnye Owùra wɔ paràdisé,
Kesi wunyan da no mu.
Na wɔbɛbɛn seraphfo,
Ahotsewfo bohu No,
Egya n’ wɔ Ne Ba no mu,
Nam Sunsum no mù ayɛ kor.

MHB 572
1 . HWƐ, emi Ewuradze N'akowaa!
Motweɔn ehu W'akwankyerɛ,
Etsie, esie W'asɛm biara,
Asɔ Wo pɛ ahwɛ na mayɛ,
Dze dɛw egyaa mara mo ndwuma,
Dze enyigye ahyɛ tsenenee nyina ma.

MHB 572
2 . Emi a memmfata W'abɔdze m',
Sɛ W'adom pɛ dɛ ɔdze m' yɛ edwuma a,
Woara kyerɛ dwuma n', ber n', na yɛbea n',
Ma m'aba nyina mfir Wo mu;
Ma mindzi mo dwuma nyina Wo mu,
Na fa m' du emudzi mapa m'.

MHB 572
3 . Me mberɛwyɛ nhyehyɛɛ n', sɛ oye mpo a,
Bɔ gu, sesa n' dɛ mbrɛ ehwɛ a oye,
Jesus, ma mo ndwuma nyina nyɛ W'dze!
Ewuradze, Wo ndwuma nyina dzi mu,
Na ɔsɔ Ɔwo Egya W'enyi,
Wo nko na ayɛ adze nyina yie.

MHB 572
4 . Afei medan W'adze ma Wo,
Wen Wo dɛtse pɔtɔɔ 'i mbrɛ epɛ;
Mbom ma minya Wo nsewhyɛ no, 
Ma mindzi W'asɛm biara do,
Mfa akoma na enyi kor nsom,
Ntsena ase nwu nhyɛ W' enyimnyam.  Amen.

MHB 573
1 . NYAME, sor na asaase Wura,
Ebɛn afɔr na mombɔ mma W'?
Mo sunsum, kra na honam, gye
Nyikan afɔrbɔ krɔnkrɔn no;
Osuar dze, m'adze nyina nye n';
Mowɔ n' pii a, nkyɛ medze bɛma W'.

MHB 573
2 . Afei, Nyame, me kra yɛ W'dze,
Ɔnnyɛ m'dze bio, meyɛ Wodze;
Weɔn Woara W'dze, yɛ n' Wodze nwionn,
Ma enyidado na dɔ mfram;
Gye mo sunsum, ma W'enyimnyam
Nhyerɛn mu nkɛpem da a m'bedzi mu.

MHB 573
3 . W'asɔrfi krɔnn n' atsew mo ho,
Etu esi hɔ ama Wo pɛ;
Ma Wo kan nhyerɛn daa wɔ ha,
Bra bɛhyɛ fie ha daa nyina;
Nkwa Mafo, tsena mo mu, nunu m'
Kɛpem dɛ dɔ bɛhyɛ me ma.

MHB 573
4 . Soma Wo su n' ma omfi sor mbra,
Na ma ɔnyɛ m'ahyehyɛdze;
Fa nyansa, abotar na ɔdɔ fura m',
Mbrɛhoadze na ahotsew a no bo
Kyɛn sika na mbota koraa,
Na ɔhyerɛn kyɛn anapa nworaba.

MHB 573
5 . Dɛ wodze W' dzin kɛse n' frɛ me 'i,
Fa W' Sunsum hoɔdzenfo n' kora me;
Mo nsusui nyina mbɔ m' wɔ mo mu,
Mo ndwuma nyina mu n' yɛ mo botae;
Wo dɔ no ngya m' me mber nyina,
M'edwuma nye dɛ m'beyi W' ayew.

MHB 574
1 . EGYA, Ba, Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn,
Ɔkorsa, Ebiasa kor,
Wɔnyɛ Wo pɛ asaase do,
Dɛ mbrɛ sor dɔm yɛ n' ara;
Nkorɔfo nyina nyi W' ayɛw,
Sor nye asaase enyimnyam Wura.

MHB 574
2 . Emi m' yɛ dzebɔnyɛnyi,
Hwɛ! Megye Wo frɛ no do,
W'adom kuraba a ɔmmfata m',
Nyame adom so obiara do;
Hwɛ! Meba bɛyɛ Wo pɛ,
Midzi W'afotu nyina do.

MHB 574
3 . Hianyi, sunsuma tse dɛ emi,
Metsena ma W'enyimnyam a,
Tsew me ndzeyɛɛ nyina ho,
Gye me nsɛm na m'adwen nyina;
Fa me, fa me yɛ W'edwuma,
Dza mowɔ, metse nyina.

MHB 574
4 . Gye me kra na nyimpadua;
Gye m'adwendwen na me pɛ,
Me ndzɛmba na me mber nyina;
Dza minyim, metse nka nyina,
Dza modwen, meka, meyɛ;
Gye m'akoma na yɛ n' fofor.

MHB 574
5 . Afei, Nyame, meyɛ W'dze,
Medze W'adze san ma Wo,
Fahodzi, mfɛfo nye dzin,
Metsew ho ma Wo nkotoo,
Metse ase ma W', m'enyi gye;
Muwu ma Wo a, enyigye nko.

MHB 574
6 . Egya, Ba, Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn,
Ɔkorsa, Ebiasa kor,
Wɔnyɛ Wo pɛ asaase do,
Dɛ mbrɛ sor dɔm yɛ n' ara;
Nkorɔfo nyina nyi W' ayɛw,
Sor nye asaase enyimnyam Wura.  Amen.

MHB 575
1 . EWURADZE, ammpow dɛ ebɛyɛ
Nyimpa nyina akowaa na afona;
Ammfɛr dɛ edze W'ahentum n'
Bɛba abɔsom hɛn.

MHB 575
2 . Duadwimfo n' Ba, gye m'edwuma
Tootooba a ɔnnsɛ hwee 'i;
Twe mo ndwuma a ɔmmfata 'i bata
Wodze n' ho ma ɔnsom bo.

MHB 575
3 . Ɔwo nye dza m'yɛ nyina n'ewiei,
Muhu W'nko wɔ adze nyina m';
Afei gye mo ndwuma krɔnn yi,
Midzi ma Woara nko.

MHB 575
4 . Meka W' fasusu papa n' do
Abɛn W' adze nyina m';
Dza modwen, meka, meyɛ nyina
Yɛ afɔr kɛse kor.

MHB 575
5 . Mudua haw na atseetsee mu sɔnn,
Biribiara nntwe m' ekyir;
Ha 'i me nsa dzi dwuma ma Wo,
M'akoma da ho wɔ W' nkyɛn.

MHB 576
1 . MA m'adwen nyina wɔ ha nyɛ dɛ
Medze suro na ɔdɔ, ndaase
M'bɔsom Ewuradze dɛ ɔba;
Mobɔpow akwan bɔn nyina,
Akyerɛ dɛm adwen mu piw yi,
Maanantsew papa n' mu.

MHB 576
2 . Ao! Ma mimfi bɔn ho mfi ara,
Jesus, nkyɛ ama me nyansa
Na ntseasee akoma;
Ma mundua Wo Sunsum mu nhu
Mbrɛ m'bɛhyɛ W' enyimnyam wɔ ha,
Na munhu ɔsor kwan. Amen.

MHB 577
1 . DƆYƐFO Ewuradze, Ɔwo a dabaa rohwehwɛ
Wo nkorɔfo a wɔper ayɛ wopɛ,
Hɔn ahoɔdzen fir W', wɔka W' tum na adom kyerɛ;
Papa mu o, bɔn mu o, wonntwa W' abrɔdɔ.

MHB 577
2 . Yɛba Wo hɔ, na mberɛw mu yɛka hɛn bɔn,
Hɛn gyedzi suar wɔ adwen, kasa na nyɛe m',
Yɛserɛ Wo, ma yenhu ampaara dɛ yenya
W'adom fakyɛ wɔ ahokyer ber mu.

MHB 577
3 . Dwumadzi nkakraba m', Woara kenyan hɛn,
Dwumadzi akɛse m' so fa W' tum hyɛ hɛn;
Yɛsom nokwar mu a, na yenya nkwagye,
Yɛnsom W' dɛm, yendzi dɛw dɛ yɛyɛ W' pɛ.

MHB 577
4 . Mma yɛnnyɛ akɔmpew wɔ sor nyikyerɛ no ho,
Yendzi nokwwar daa, yemmbisa akatua,
Yedzi W'ekyir 'i, ma yɛnhyɛ hɛn somdwuma ma,
Yendzi nokwar mma hɛnho na Ewuradze.  Amen.

MHB 578
1 . Asodzi da mo do
Dɛ miyi Nyame ayɛw,
Megye me kra a onnwu da nkwa,
Na mema ɔsɛ sor.

MHB 578
2 . Mosom mbersantsen yi, 
Midze dwuma a wɔahyɛ m',
Ao, nkyɛ medze m'ahom nyina 
Maayɛ mo Wura Ne pɛ!

MHB 578
3 . Fa nhwɛyie bɔ me ban 
Ma mentsena dɛ ihu m';
Na, mo Wura, siesie Wo somfo
Na meebu nkontaa pa.

MHB 578
4 . Boa m' ma monweɔn, monsɔr, 
Na montwer Wo nkotoo
Minyim dɛ mogor m'edwuma ho a,
M'bowu wu a onnyi ewiei.

MHB 579
1 . Gyefo, Ɔwo, dɔ ntsi 
Iwui maa me,
Ɔmmfata dɛ medze,
Hweeara kam Wo;
Dɔm', me kra bɔkotow W',
M'akoma edzi ne nsew do,
Na ɔabɔ afɔr bi,
Ama W' sesei.

MHB 579
2 . Mbɔbɔr egua n' enyim 
Idzi ma me,
Jesus, me gyedzi to
N'enyi hwɛ Wo:
Boa m' ma monsoa mbeamudua n',
Mombɔ Wo dɔ n' dawur,
Montow ndwom, mbɔ mpaa bi
Mma Wo sesei.

MHB 579
3 . Ma m' nokwar 'koma a, 
Ɔsɛ Wodze N',
Na dabiara  a otwam'
Eehu me dɛ
Mahyɛ dɔ dwuma bi ase,
Mayɛ ayamuyie bi,
Matwe kobɔnyi bi,
Medze ama W'.

MHB 579
4 . Dza mowɔ o, mbrɛ metse o, 
W' akyɛdze kwa,
Dɛw mu o, yaw mu o, mo Wura,
Wodze nye me.
Na muhu W'enyim a,
Me kra a wɔapɔn no yi,
Mbersantsen nyina mu,
Ɔnyɛ Wodze.

MHB 58
1 . EWURADZE dzi hen;
N'ahengua si ɔsor,
Atar a ɔhyɛ no
Yɛ kan na ahentum:
N'enyimnyam hyerɛn dɛ ekan,
Dasanyi biara nntum nnhwɛ kan n'.

MHB 58
2 . Ne nsamu aprandaa
Ma wiadze nyina bɔ hu;
N'ebufuw na tsenenee
Weɔn Ne mbra krɔnkrɔn no;
Na mbrɛ No dɔ pɛ dɛ ohyira n'.
No nokwar si adom no pi.

MHB 58
3 . Nyansa nwanwa hyerɛn 
No ndwuma akɛse mu; 
Ɔsɛɛ hɛll etumfo
Na hɔn sum ndwuma nyina; 
Ne basa dzen ma Ne nhyehyɛɛ 
Na N'apɛdze nyina yɛ hɔ.

MHB 58
4 . Enyimnyam Hen kɛse
Yi bɛbrɛ No ho adze?
Na ɔakyerɛw Ne dzin dɛ
M'Egya na m' Adamfo?
Modɔ Ne dzin, modɔ N'asɛm.
M'ahoɛdzen nyina nkamfo
Ewuardze! Amen.

MHB 580
1 . EWURADZE, mma mmpam m'
W'edwuma ho,
Mbom kyerɛ me W' apɛdze;
Mo so dɛm yi maayɛ biribi
Wɔ Wo kwaa tɛtɛr 'i mu;
Na mbɔsom Wo daa nyinara,
Minnkebisa akatua.

MHB 580
2 . Pii wɔsom Wo, dodowara so
Na otwar dɛ wɔbɔsom W',
Ema binom tsɛw wenyindua,
Binom tsetsew aba n',
Wo mberantsɛ gyina akono,
Wo mbɔtoaba wɔ fie.

MHB 580
3 . Ndwuma nyina ye, biara ye koraa,
Sɛ ɔsɔ W'enyi dze a;
Dwumayɛnyi biara a ɔdze dɔ som
Ne mfɛfo n' sɔ W'enyi;
Ennhyira amma nyimpa na dwuma
Biara ho kwan a, onngyina.

MHB 580
4 . Hɛn Wura, dwuma biara a edzi n',
'Pɛ dɛ hɛn so yɛyɛ;
Yɛnye N' yɛ edwuma, ama obiara so 
Nye N' aakyɛ N'abayɛ n';
Ewuradze, mbɔsom, maayɛ ba;
Meserɛ W', mma nnyi m' tokyen.

MHB 581
1 . HOM Ewuradze nkowaa,
Obiara mfua n'edwuma m',
Hom a hom dzi No sor asɛm do
Nweɔn Nyame N'abow no.

MHB 581
2 . Hom mma hom nkandzea nhyerɛn
Hom nkeka n' framee n' yie,
Hom mbɔ hom ntoa ngyina N'enyim,
Ne dzin no yɛ nwanwa.

MHB 581
3 . Weɔn: dɛm na hɛn Wura se,
Yɛkasaa a, ɔbɛn hɛn;
Hom nhyɛ Ne nsa nsɛnkyerɛdze n' nsew,
Hom nyina nyɛ ntsɛm mpue.

MHB 581
4 . Ɔsomfo, homkanyi
Nye onyia ɔsom dɛm!
Ɔdze dɛw bohu n'Ewuradze,
Na ɔahyɛ N'enyimnyam.

MHB 581
5 . Christ Noara N'ahensa
Na ɔdze bɔto pon no,
Ɔama akowaa nokwafo n' tsir do,
Wɔ abɔfo dɔm no mu.

MHB 582
1 . HƐN Egya N'adom fi Ne kan
Fadum no m' hyerɛn hyɛnhyɛnn daa;
Na hɛndze ɔdze mpoano ha
Nkandzea no ahyɛ hɛn nsa.

MHB 582
2 . Wɔmma ase nkandzea no ndzɛw,
Mma ne hyerɛn ntra asorɛkye;
Ma aagye brɛfo bɔbɔfo bi a
Oridzi aper po do no nkwa.

MHB 582
3 . Bɔn anago kadoo no etwa m',
Po asorɛkye bɔ dzendzen;
Pii roweɔn, rotweɔn, rohwehwɛ
Eehu mpoano nkandzea no.

MHB 582
4 . Mo nua, ma wo kandzea no nhyerɛn,
Farnyi fonafo a ehum rutu n',
Reper hwehwɛ edu berano,
Rehara wɔ sum no mu.

MHB 583
1 . IFI bɔn wiadze mpokyerɛ mu a,
Mbrɛ odua yɛ dɛw a!
M'besi akoma na adwen tadua,
Ayɛ Ewuradze akowaa;
Edze enyigye bɛyɛ edwumason
Biara a ɔbɛhyɛ wo,
'Dze ahobrɛadze bɛyɛ edwumaba
Biara a edze bɛma m'.

MHB 583
2 . Medze ɔpɛ na enyigye
Bɔweɔn W'aponkɛse,
Mayɛ krado dɛ m'besi empire n',
Masoa dza ɔyɛ dur n';
'Nnkɛtse apranaa biara mbɔm',
'Bɛka N' do bɔkɔɔ ara;
Ɔdɔ nko na obotum akyerɛ
Ɔdɔfo N'apɛdze.

MHB 583
3 . Ma monsom dɛm, Domfo Ewuradze,
Wo nko ara Wodze daa,
Medze me kra na honam ma W',
Ɔwoara W'atɔdze a;
Atsenka pa anaa bɔn mu a,
Menye W' bɛnantsew ara;
Nyimpadua yi m' nkwa mu o, wu mu o,
Menhyɛ Christ enyimnyam.

MHB 583
4 . Mbrɛ dwumadzi ber wɔ som yi mu
Ɔnnkyɛr na oetwa m' kɔ a!
Ɔpon ber no ba ntsɛmara,
Ahomgye ber bɛn ntsɛm,
Na anokwafo dzi ehyia wɔ fie,
Ahomkafo ehyiadzi,
Owura Ne nkyɛn na No nkowaa
Esiarfo bɛtsena daa.

MHB 584
1 . O JESU, kenyan m'akoma,
Fa gya krɔnn ka m'anofamfa,
Siansian abɔtoaba gyirama;
Na siesie W'adom kuraba,
Fa ayɛyi egudo ntar n' hyehyɛ m',
Mo ndwom nyina bɛyɛ ehumbɔbɔr;
Obiara a onnyim Nyankopɔn,
Hɔn a Jesu bɔgyaa atɔ hɔn,
Ehumbɔbɔr a ɔtra sor na ase;
Dɔ a no war, trɛ, no bun, no krɔn,
Obunkam kan m' esiarfo do,
Nyame dɔ a ɔnnsa ara da.

MHB 584
2 . Fa m' hyɛ beebi a epɛ, menyɛ
W'adom n' ho nokwar dasefo,
Mindzi dza ahyehyɛ nyina do,
'Nantsew edwuma a Woara ahyehyɛ n' mu;
Ma akatua pa n' aayɛ medze,
Ɔsor tsenenee ahenkyɛw no,
Matsena ase ama Wo nko ara n',
Nkuranhyɛsɛm dɛ: Mbo-na-yɛ!
Na mentsena Wo nkyɛn wɔ sor,
Menhɛn mo Wura N'enyigye mu,
Onnyiewiei nyina minyi W' ayɛw,
Ndzi dɛw mbordo, na mondɔ Wo.

MHB 585
1 . Nyame asomfo, hom nsoɛr! 
Hom n-tow nsɛmhun ngu!
Hom mfa 'koma, adwen, ndamyɛ
Mbɔsom ahemfo Hen!

MHB 585
2 . Nyame asomfo, hom nsoɛr! 
N'ahendzi ekyim dodow;
Hom mma enuadɔ nda edzi,
Na sum nye manso nkɔ.

MHB 585
3 . Nyame asomfo, hom nsoɛr! 
Asɔr no rotweɔn hom;
N'edwuma so ma n'hoɔdzen;
Hom nsoɛr, hom nhyɛ no dzen.

MHB 585
4 . Hom mma Christ mbeam'dua n'do! 
Hom ntsia N'ananɔm m;
Onyimpa Ba, hom Nua n', dzi kan:
Nyame asomfo, hom nsoɛr!

MHB 586
1 . TWEƆN, Owura, tweɔn wɔ kokwaa yi do ha;
Tsintsim na nye hɛn ntsena ha kakra;
Yɛnye tsetsemba akatakyi nyina
Bɛtsena Nyame bea nwanwa yi do;
Begyina ahopopo m' wɔ kan ahengua enyim,
Abɔ nkɔtsen ahwɛ sunsum wiadze n'.

MHB 586
2 . Tweɔn, Owura, tweɔn! Yɛgye mfar pa wɔ ha;
Nnyɛ asetsena a ɔrotweɔn hɛn hɔ n' nye yi;
Adwen, atsenka, nyina dzi akɔnaaba;
Yennkotum aka ho asɛm, yennyim koraa;
Awɔw na kan kyekyer hɛn ma yɛhwɛ
Abɔ nkɔtsen ahwɛ sunsum wiadze n'.

MHB 586
3 . Ewuradze se, Dabi, ber apa ho;
Yɛnkɔ hɛn fie, 'bra na edwuma wɔ ase,
Yebu ntwɛr wɔ mpaabɔ koko do ha n',
Edwumadze wɔ ase hɔ rotweɔn hɛn,
Ha 'i yɛhwehwɛ Nyame ma yeehu N' pɛ;
Hɔ yɛyɛ N' pɛ, som No, hwehwɛ N' ara.

MHB 586
4 . Sɛ nyimpa per du Nyame ahengua n' ho a,
Kwan n' da asaase kusuww yi do ha ara;
Nyia ɔyɛ ne famu ha edwuma dɛ mbrɛ ɔsɛ n',
Wɔbɔkrɔn n' kɛse wɔ sor ahenman m';
Hɛn akra hwehwɛ ahom Nyame N'ananadze,
Na nyi ɔsom No yie n' bɛn No kɛse.

MHB 587
1 . O NDZEPA nyina Ewuradze!
Hɔn nyinara Bɔfo,
Ɔwo a ɔpɛber kɛsɛɛ ekyir n'
Etɔ nsu ma nduadzewa fifir,
Yɛbɔ Wo dzin kɛse n'.

MHB 587
2 . Idua mbɔnsa m' nhyiren do kyerɛ hɛn
Wo sor dɔ na nokwar;
Yɛnye nsu a ɔwor, nkokwaa na
Asorɛkye weɔɔ weɔɔ nyina bɔ m'
Kamfo dɛ yɛyɛ W'dze.

MHB 587
3 . Nnyɛ dɛ yɛyɛ W'dze nko 'siandɛ
Hɛn nkwa na ahom fir Wo;
Yɛyɛ W'dze 'siandɛ adom a ɔyɛ
Hɛn esunsum adehye n' wɔ Christ mu,
Hyɛ hɛn dzen ma nokwar n'.

MHB 587
4 . Kan hɛn for a esiarfo no a
Wɔbɔ W' dzin ho dawur n',
Fa sor nsanku kurakura hɛn nsamu,
Na fa ɔdɔ ndwom hyɛ akoma ma,
Nyame dɔ kɛse no a.

MHB 587
5 . Kodu dɛ yɛnye hɔn a wɔberɛe
Tsim W'ahendzi wɔ ha,
Hɔn a wɔyɛ wiadze ntɔmpamu,
Na dɔm a apon hɔn nyina,
Bɔbɔ m' epue W' fie hɔ.

MHB 588
1 . Nyan, soɛr, yɛ dɔ na edwuma, 
Nnoma asoɛr rusu,
Bɔsu atɔ egu nhaban do,
Wiadze nyina asoɛr
Rihyira, Nkwa Wura Ne Mafo
Ɔhobrɛadzefo No.

MHB 588
2 . Bra, ma wo ndze mfora hɔn dzem', 
Ka mu bi yi N' ayɛw;
Hwɛ mbrɛ ewia a ofir tsetse,
Asoɛr rehyerɛn dzendzen!
Dɛm na ma Jesus dɔ m'bɔsɔ
Gya wɔ w' akoma mu.

MHB 588
3 . Fa ma, fa ma, fa ma ara, 
Dza Nyame dze ama wo n';
Hwer woho mma mmbu ho nkontaa,
Enyimnyamm' ara som
Onyame a ɔmaa wiadze yi
Na dza ɔbɛba nyina.

MHB 589
1 . Yɛ edwuma; hwer, ma woho nkɔm', 
Fa dɛw yɛ w'Egya N'edwuma;
Kwan a wo Wura duaa mu nye n';
Na 'wo, somfo, na ennkɛfa do?

MHB 589
2 . Yɛ ara, ɔnnkɛyɛ gyam bi, 
Dza 'yew n' ha n', fa n' mfaso wɔ sor:
Nɛndze nnkamfo w', mmpɛ w', wommbu w' bi;
Owura pen wo; nyimpa nye bɛn?

MHB 589
3 . Yɛ ara, ber a kan wɔ do yi, 
Wiadze edwumayɛ ber resa:
Mma nnyɛ akwadwerɛ, yɛ w'edwuma ntsɛm;
Wonnsi n' dɛm twe sunsum ekyir.

MHB 589
4 .  Sum ruku nɛndze a wɔnye W' tse, 
Dɛ wonnyi enyidar wɔ wum';
Ma gya no do, na ka n' kɛse,
Gya a ɔma mbrɛ sum wɔ yɛ kan n'.

MHB 589
5 . Yɛ ara, mma mberɛ, weɔn na sɔr, 
Wɔdze nyansa twe kra ekyir;
Sir wiadze bra ne tsempɔn yim'
Pon akobɔfo ma wɔmbra.

MHB 589
6 . Yɛ ara, eso dzi mu dɛw; 
Na ahomgye pa wɔ ekyir;
Ɔrennkyɛr bi na atse kumfor n'
Ne ndze esuom dɛ, Hwɛ, mereba!

MHB 59
1 . IYE na eyɛ dza oye,
Ihu obiara mbɔbɔr,
Nkanka hɔn a wɔtwer Wo, Hwehwɛ Wo mbɔbɔrhu;
Anapa wɔyɛ fofor
Dɛ egyanom ber a hɔn mba su, 
Wo mbɔbɔrhu mu 'dze kyɛ, Hɛn ehiadze nyina 'dze ma.

MHB 59
2 . Mbɔbɔrhu hwɛ Wo ndwuma do; 
Dza 'dze ma hɔn da edzi,
'Da ho kora do na 'dze ma, 'Dza Wo nsa ayɛ nyina;
Edze ahwɛyie kora hɔn do,
Nyia ɔdze noho to Wo dɔ do n', 
 Eweɔn ne tsinhwi nyina,
Ehwɛ n'anamɔn nyina.

MHB 59
3 . Woana botum esusu
Wo nkwagye adom no? 
Adom a ɔmaa Wo Ba kor n' Bae dɛ ɔbɛgye abɔn.
M-bratofo m-pempem,
Jesus ntsi edze akyɛ hɔn,
Hɔn nsa aka W'adom ampa,
Agye hɔn efi hɛll.

MHB 59
4 . Epɛ dɛ egye mpempem bio, 
Na edze aakyɛ hɔn;
Ebɛgye ɔkra biara,
'Bɛgye nyimpa biara:
Egya, afei gye medze a
Menam Christ do dze ma Wo no; 
Afei ka n' ɔdɔ m' kyerɛ me 
Dɛ edze akyɛ me.

MHB 590
1 . Ewuradze, Wo dzinm' na misim', 
Mikedzi me daa daa dwuma,
Wo nko na mesua dɛ m'bɔhwɛ W'
Wɔ dza modwen, meka, meyɛm'.

MHB 590
2 . Edwuma a Wo nyansaa akyerɛ n' 
Ao, ma mempra mo mu nyina nyɛ,
Munhu Wo mo ndwuma nyinam',
Na menyɛ Wo pɛ a ɔsɛ n'.

MHB 590
3 . Ma memfa Wo ngyina me nyimfa, 
'Wo a W'enyi tua mo mu nyina,
Na mindzi dwuma a ebɛkyerɛ m',
Muntu mo ndwuma nyina nhyɛ Wo nsa.

MHB 590
4 . Ma monsoa Wo kɔndua harhar n' 
Na ber biara mohweɔn, monsɔr,
Na monhwɛ bɛkyebo ndzɛmba,
Nyɛ ntsɛm ndu W'enyimnyam da n' mu.

MHB 590
5 . Biribiara a W'adom dze akyɛ m' 
Ma memfa nsom Wo enyigyem',
Na memfa dɛw nsi m'empire,
Memfam Wo ho nnantsew nkɔ sor.

MHB 591
1 . MMA nngye hɔn a wɔse sor
Kwan no yɛ trontrom n' nndzi;
Annyɛ a efintsiw kwan no mu,
Na atɔ akɔtɔmborɔnsa.

MHB 591
2 . Noara nye kwan kor a
Wɔdze kɔ ahomka bea n';
Nyia ɔpɛ siar bea n' akɔ no
Mfa n'ahom nyina mper.

MHB 591
3 . Mia w'akodze hyia ko n',
Tow adzesoa gyangyan gu,
Weɔn adzesaa sum kadoo mu;
Na berɛ ewia ketee.

MHB 591
4 . Yɛ edwuma na yɛ dɔ,
Fa kyɛ, sɔw adze nyina 
Ma w'akoma do ma sor Nyame,
Wo tsibowa so nyɛ krɔnn.

MHB 591
5 . Ma 'yi nyɛ w' botae daa,
W'enyidar, wo dɛw kor;
Wɔwasa toa w', mmbu w' bi, hyɛ w' fɛr
Mpo a, ebɛnadze mbɔ a?

MHB 592
1 . M'ENYI daa kwan dɛ mibenya
Kyɛfa wɔ 'hoɔdzenfo m';
Medze botae a ho tsew, ɔkrɔn
Bɔfora mbɔdzembɔfo m';
Nyame ahyehyɛ kwan kor so,
Na ɔahyehyɛ no yie;
Medze yaw akoma kaa dɛm
Ber a dɛm ɔhaw yɛ bae.

MHB 592
2 . Dɛm ɔfona ber yi nnkɛyew,
Awerɛhow nda 'i mmfi hɔ;
Anago sum, ehumtu ber m',
Wo nkyɛn na mebɛba.
Abotar mu mobɔsɔw 'bra
Mu ekuturku nyina;
M'benya akokodur wɔ yaw mu,
Na krɔnnyɛ wɔ mbusu m'.

MHB 592
3 . Sɛ edze me san ba nkwa m' bio a,
Mebɛbrɛ moho adze;
Ɔko mu mibenya nyansa
Na ahoɔdzen atwer Wo,
Sɛ owu gyina abowano a,
M'bedzi mo bɔhyɛ do;
Dza ɔbɛba mo do biara,
Ma monsom Wo sesei.

MHB 593
1 . NDƆBAA n' yɛ bafuu o, mpɛpɛw o,
Adze sa, na edwuma bɔ adze;
Yedu botae n' ho o, yenndu o,
Obi nntum nsɛɛ, na obi nnyɛ n' yie.
Mbɔbɔrhufo tseneneenyi,
Yɛdze dza 'dze maa hɛn n' brɛ W';
Da mu aba kakraba n',
Yɛdze gu W'ananandze.

MHB 593
2 . Nyew, 'Wo Ewuradze Tsɛmbuafo,
Nyew, 'Wo krɔnkrɔnyi hoɔdzenfo,
Edze esie Wo bo mu no,
Fa Wo nsa krɔnkrɔn no sakyer
Ndzeyɛɛ na adwembɔn; ɔnyɛ
Dza omuo nyina ma ɔndan sika;
Yɛdze hɛn dɔ a ɔyɛ mberɛw 'i
Ma W', ma ɔaatsena ase Wo mu.

MHB 593
3 . Afei, yɛatse frɛ dɛɛdɛw 'i
Hɛn akoma bɛyɛ adom edwuma n';
Fie mframa pa na nda pa n'
Bɛkyekyer hɛn abɔ mu bio;
Mbukyia a yefii ho bae no,
Ɔdɔ gya bɛfram mu bio
Ekenyan hɛn mbofra dɔ n',
Ma yeenya kan fofor bi.

MHB 593
4 . Enuanom, hom a abrabɔ
Nkodzen twe hom dzi dwuma no,
Ɔma yenya no mu nhyira;
Yɛyɛ anyɛnkofo daa daa;
Ha na ekyirkyir mbew kor no,
Hɛn nkwagye woraba kor na
Ofi ahengua n' ho hyerɛn
Beebi a Ewuradze ka hɛn bɔ m'.

MHB 594
1 . EWURADZE, W'adom tum n'
Na medze akoma pa
Mutu moho, me nda nkaa nyina,
Dze hyɛ Wo nsa koraa.

MHB 594
2 . W'akowaa a apon me yi,
Medze Woara W'dze ma W',
'Fitsi ndɛ metse ase o, muwu o,
M'bɔsom me Nyame nko.

MHB 595
1 . ƆDƆ kɛse Nyame,
W'adom mbordo no ntsi,
Mema akoma do ma sor ndzɛmba
Na mohwehwɛ W'enyim.

MHB 595
2 . Jesus Christ tseneneenyi,
Tsie m'ebisadze yi,
Na ma montwer W'ayamuyie no,
Ntsena ase nhyɛ W' enyimnyam

MHB 595
3 . Monhwehwɛ W'enyimnyam
Wɔ dza meka, meyɛ m';
Mundua dabaa siar dzin no do
Mombɔ m'afɔr nyina.

MHB 595
4 . Ma memfa m'enyi ntsim
Jesu, Wo nko Wo do;
Wonhyira Wo dzin wɔ sor na ase,
Wɔnyɛ W' apɛdze so.

MHB 595
5 . Gyedzi Sunsum, kenyan
M'akoma a medze ahyɛ W' nsa;
Sor gya, fa krɔnkrɔnyɛ na dza
Ewɔ nyina hyɛ me ma.  Amen.

MHB 596
1 . NYAME, yɛ m' daduanyi,
Afei m'benya ahotɔ;
Hyɛ m' ma mingyaa me nkrantsee mu,
Ama meedzi konyim,
Sɛ mo nko migyina 
Ɔbra n'ehum men me,
Sɛ meda W'abaw mu dze a,
Mo ho bɛyɛ me dzen.

MHB 596
2 . M'akoma yɛ mberɛw,
Kɛpem dɛ obohu n' Wura;
Ɔnnyi ndzeyɛɛ pa ho awerɛhyɛm';
Ɔnye mframa sesa,
Onnyi ne fahodzi,
Gyedɛ atsew no mpokyerɛ m';
Yɛ n' akowaa wɔ Wo dɔ a ɔnnsa n' mu,
Na obedzi hen wɔ nkwa m'.

MHB 596
3 . Mo tum yɛ har, yɛ mberɛw,
Kɛpem dɛ mesua som;
Ɔhwehwɛ dɛ onya gya a ɔdzɛw,
Ɔpɛ mframa a ɔma ahom;
Onntum nndzi wiadze enyim,
Gyedɛ wɔdze n' bodu;
Wobotum ehim ne frankaa n'
Ber a ebɔhom efi sor.

. Me pɛ nnyɛ medze bi,
Gyedɛ eyɛ n' Wodze;
Sɛ obohu W'adom ahengua enyim a,
Ɔsɛ dɛ ogyaa nedze m';
Ogyina hɔ pintsinn,
Wɔ ɔko dzendzen mu,
Ber a ɔatwer Wo koko mu sɔnn,
Na oenya Wo mu nkwa.

MHB 597
1 . ME Nyame Hen, kyerɛ m'
Munhu W' wɔ biribiara m',
Na biribiara a mebɛyɛ no,
Ɔwo na meyɛ ma W'.

MHB 597
2 . Nyimpa a ɔhwɛ ahwehwɛ m' n',
No do na n'enyi tsim;
Anaa sɛ ɔpɛ mpo a, ohwira m',
Ma ntsi ohu heaven.

MHB 597
3 . Obiara tum dze W' yɛ a,
Biribiara nnkɛyɛ gyan,
Dza ɔnye W' bɔ awɛ n', Wo ntsi
Ɔbɛhyerɛn na n' ho atsew.

MHB 597
4 . Akowaa a ɔtse dɛm no
Bɛyɛ edwumadzen;
Nyia ɔpra dan m' wɔ Wo mbra ntsi n',
No dwumadzi n' dzi mu.

MHB 597
5 . Iyi nye ɔbo a agye dzin a
Ɔdan adze nyina mfutuw n';
Dza Nyame suo m' yɛ Nedze no,
No ho wɔ mfaso pa.

MHB 598
1 . 'GUAMBAA krɔnkrɔn, W'esuafo
Dzi Wo ho dase pa ara,
Daa hɔn enyi da Wo do,
Wobisa dɛ: Yɛnyɛ dɛn?
Wo pɛ kor a ɔhwɛ hɛn do ntsi
Yebedzi Wo nsɛm nyina do,
Na yɛbɛfa W'akwan do,
Yɛbɛnantsew dɛ mbrɛ eyɛe.

MHB 598
2 . Ber a ipuei wɔ asaase do n',
Eyɛɛ Somfo maa Wo nkowaa;
Edween Wo sor ahenman ho,
Wo bra yɛɛ mpaabɔ nye dɔ,
Dɛm na hɛn dwumadzi nyina tse,
Gyedzi na adzeyɛ ndwuma;
Ekyerɛɛ nyimpa ɔdɔ ndwuma
Na Nyame m' nkitahodzi.

MHB 598
3 . Hom mma yenkyia hɛn Agyenkwa
'Napatutu wɔ asɔrfi m';
Yɛnkɔ bepɔw n' do anafua,
Nkɛka hɛn Wura ho wɔ hɔ.
Yɛmper nnya gyedzi mfa nyɛ
Nyame N'edwuma wɔ hɔ,
Nye tum a yɛdze nya No su,
Na Wo tum a yɛdze tsena ase.

MHB 598
4 . Yɛdze adom ho ndzɛmba
Twa hɛn enyigye mber mu,
Wɔ nkokwaa na dɔm tutuw m;
Yɛyɛ papa, yɛgye bi;
Yɛdze dɛw bɔ mpaa, yɛ edwuma
Kɛpem dɛ hɛn bra bɔ adze,
Kɛpem dɛ dua krɔnkrɔn n' ho
Yebowu dɛ mbrɛ Ɔwo wui n'.

MHB 599
1 . DUA W'aba n' anapa,
Yɛ ntsɛm ewimbir no;
Mma mma suro na ekyingye kwan,
Bɔ n' dawur wɔ mbea nyina.

MHB 599
2 . Dua n' wɔ esu nkyɛnkyɛn,
Kwantsempɔn ho nsaase m';
Gu no wɔ nsoɛ na ndzɛmbir mu,
Petse no botan do.

MHB 599
3 . Mma nnhwehwɛ asaase pa
Wɔ ha anaa noho;
Wohu no nkokwaa na mbɔnsa m';
Kɔ do gu n' beebiara.

MHB 599
4 . Mbrɛ ɔtse biara obefir;
Ahoɔfɛw na ahoɔdzen m';
Ɔbɔwowɔ, oenyin afa mba,
Na afei ɔayɛ eburow-mu.

MHB 599
5 . Ennkɛberɛ egu kwa da;
Awɔw, 'hyew, nsu na ewia
Bɔbɔ m' ma aba n' eedzi mu
Ama sor edwumayɛfo n'.

MHB 599
6 . Ber a Nyame N'enyimnyam
Da no bodu hɔ no,
Abɔfo edwumafo n' besian,
Sor bɛtsea m': Buber fie.

MHB 6
1 . DOMANKOMA ! Wo sor tsebea
Yɛ fɛw dɛ mbrɛ osɛ Nyame:
Ɔtra wimuwimu n'ekyir noho.
Mbrɛ nworaba wɔkɔ aprɔw.

MHB 6
2 . Bɔfopanyin rotow W'Ndwom a.
N'enyim suma n'atsaban mu;
Ahotsewfo a woetwa ehyia.
Bom famu wɔ hɔ nyina som Wo.

MHB 6
3 . Nyame, dɛtse na nso nyɛ dɛn?
Hɛn so yɛbɔsom hen Bɔfo:
Yefi bɔn na huntuma m'frɛ Wo
Kɛse, Kronkronyi, Abɔso.

MHB 6
4 . Wɔatse Wo nka wɔ ekyirkyir,
Mbɔtoaba esua Wo dzin bɔ;
Na Wo nyansaa N'enyimnyam no
Ma hen adwen nyina tɔ sin.

MHB 6
5 . Nyame wo sɔr, nyimpa wɔ ase,
Hɛn ndwom nyɛ tsia, na hɛn nsɛm nsuar,
Wo ho enyidzi sianka hɛn ndwom,
Hɛn ayɛyi ka hɛn anomu.

MHB 60
1 . ANSAANA Nyam' bɔɔ mbepɔw,
Nkoko na no do ndua;
Ɔhyɛɛ nsubura amaama,
Ɔpem kɔ nsutsen mu;
Ofi tsetse wɔ mo mu n',
Ɔnwanwanyi MARA
Nyaa enyigye a odzi mu,
Na Nyansa nye me dzin.

MHB 60
2 . Ber a ɔtserɛɛw ɔsor mu no,
Tse dɛ ntamadan no,
Na ɔbɔ po yantamm ho ban,
Siiw po esuyirii ano.
Na osusuu ndzɛmba no,
Nna menye No wɔ hɔ;
Emi nye Egya n' enyigye,
Nyimpa mba yɛ medze.

MHB 60
3 . Dɛm na Nyansa nsɛm hwehwɛ 
W'enyimnyam na W'adom; 
Hɛn a yɛmmfata yi mpo, 
W'adom enyi no hun hɛn
'Nsaana wohum nworaba;
Nyansa mu na ayɛ hɛn
Na dɔ m' na 'wui maa hɛn.

MHB 60
4 . Ana W'enyi gyè abɔdze a
Wɔtse dɛ hɛn so ho?
Hɛn a yehum Wo yemmbu W' bi n',
Yɛsɛɛn Wo wɔ dua do?
Nwanwa a wonnhu ano,
Ɔsor esumasɛm;
Aprandaa ndze bɔbɔ mu,
Dɛ ɔbɔn, meyɛ wodze.

MHB 600
1 . Ao, mo Wura, ma menye W' nnantsew 
Som dwumadzi mbrɛadze kwan mu;
Kyerɛ m' W'esumasɛm, boa m' ma monsɔw,
Dwumadzi ne yaw, dadwen no dur;
Boa me ma memfa dɔ kasa
Mpuhim akoma nyaanyaa bi:
Kyerɛ me ma mingya akobɔfo,
Memfa hɔn nsi sor kwan no mu.

MHB 600
2 . Kyerɛ m' W'abotar; ma menda ho 
Ntsena Wo fɛkuwbɔ dɛɛdɛwm',
Dwumadzi a ɔhyɛ gyedzi dzen,
Awerɛhyɛm' a odzi bɔn do,
Enyidar a ɔtow nserɛmɛn
Dze hyerɛn nda a ɔreba kwan mu,
Asomdwee a Wo nko ara dze ma,
Mo Wura, ma menye Wo nnantsew mu. 
                                               Amen.

MHB 601
1 . HƆN a wɔyɛ edwuma no,
Wotsiatsia M'anamɔn mu;
Hɔn a wɔyɛ edwuma a wɔnnkasa n';
Wɔyɛ Nyame N' pɛ krɔnkrɔn;
Onnhia dɛ ebɔhwehwɛ M' bio,
Mowɔ wo nkyɛn beebiara;
Pirew ɔbo n' na ibohu Me,
Paa dua n' mu na mowɔ hɔ.

MHB 601
2 . Bea a dɔm yɛ edwuma bɔ mu n'
Na mowɔ mo nkorɔfo mu;
Bea a odwumayɛfo aberɛ ada n',
Na menye no nko wɔ hɔ.
Emi Asomdwee a ɔtra nyimdzee n',
Meka hom ho wɔ nkodzen m',
Emi nye ɔsor Paanoo a
Wɔdze M' ma nkwa sakramɛnt.

MHB 601
3 . Mbrɛ edwuma biara tse no,
Ma ɔkra a ɔyɛ n' fahodzi;
Dɔ na ehumbɔbɔr a wɔkyerɛ
Ma nyimpa n', wɔyɛ ma Me.
Onnhia dɛ ebɔhwehwɛ M' bio;
Mowɔ Wo nkyɛn beebiara;
Pirew ɔbo n' na ibohu me,
Paa dua n' mu na mowɔ hɔ.

MHB 602
1 . M'egya, minyim me bra nyina 
Akyekyɛm' ama me,
Na nsakyer a otwar dɛ ɔba n'
Munnsuro dɛ m'bohu;
Dza meserɛ nye adwendahɔ a
Ɔper sɔ W'enyi daa.

MHB 602
2 . Meserɛ Wo adwendwen ɔdɔ a 
Ɔyɛ aweɔn ho nyansa,
Dze ma ahomkafo enyigye,
Pata nyinsuwakyifo;
Ɔnye 'koma a ɔpow noho
Na ɔtse ma binom so.

MHB 602
3 . Monnhwehwɛ ɔpɛ ɔnnda hɔ komm, 
Odzi akɔnaaba,
Ɔhwehwɛ akɛsedze ɔayɛ
Na oehu esumasɛm;
Mepɛ dɛ meyɛ abɔtoaba a
Woara gye me taataa.

MHB 602
4 . Wiadze mu mbrɛ m'bɛfa biara, 
No mu dzibew biara,
Menye nkorɔfo edzi nkitaho a
Meper ara ma oeenyin,
Na medze ahobrɛadze nye dɔ
Mayɛ Mo Wura edwuma.

MHB 602
5 . Meserɛ daadaa ahoɔdzen a 
Yebisa a hɛn nsa ka n'; 
Ɔnye adwen a onnhwinhwin
Na ɔka Woara ho daa;
Ɔdan mbrɛ mahyɛ W' enyimnyam
Mepen som biara do.

MHB 602
6 . Som biara a Wo pɛ kyerɛ me no 
Mennyɛ ho akɔmpew;
Na me kra ehu nokwar n' a
Ɔyɛ Wo mba adehye n';
Na ɔdɔ etuhoakyɛ bra
Yɛ adehyedzi koraa.

MHB 603
1 . JESUS, ma W'adɔfo nyina nhyerɛn 
Wɔnhyerɛn fɛɛfɛw dɛ ewia,
Wɔmfa Nyame ewia nserɛmɛn
Ntu hɔn enyimnyam kwan n'.

MHB 603
2 . Beebiara mbrɛ nyimpa wɔ no
Wɔmma hɔ nyina nhyerɛn;
Na ɔsor ahoɔdzen nyina
Nkata ase ha nyina.

MHB 603
3 . Dɛm tsenenee ewia hyɛnhyɛn no,
Ntserɛw hɔn 'yarsa ntsaban m'
Na hɔn enyim hyerɛn ntahye
Nkodu emudzi da n'.

MHB 604
1 . O EWURADZE, me Nyankopɔn,
Fa ayɛyi hyɛ m' bra ma,
Ama me nyimpa-mu aakyerɛ
Wo subea nye W'akwan.

MHB 604
2 . Nnyɛ m'anofamfa ara nko bi,
Na nnyɛ m'akoma nko,
Na mbom, mibisa abrabɔ bi a
Ayɛyi ahyɛ mu ma.

MHB 604
3 . Ntonton wɔ adze biara mu,
No kɔsu, ne basu,
Dwumadzi na ndzeyɛɛ suar dɛn mpo a,
'Twar dɛ yeyi W'ayɛw.

MHB 604
4 . Fa ayɛyi hyɛ mo mu nyina,
Me nyimpadua nkasa
Mfa Wo dɔ na Wo ho, mo Wura,
Kaansa mennsɛ bi mpo a.

MHB 604
5 . Mo Wura, ama mo so dɛm yi
Maahyɛ Wo enyimnyam;
Na dɛm na m'bɛhyɛ ase wɔ ha
Matow W'ayɛyi ndwom n'.

MHB 604
6 . Dɛm ntsi adzekyee na adzesaa nyina
'Twar dɛ meyɛ krɔnkrɔn,
Ama manamɔntu biara m'
Menye W' abɔ fɛkuw.

MHB 605
1 . JESUS, Nyame akyɛdzé a minyim,
Mibisa Wo sor akyɛdze n’;
Hue nkwa nsu gu mo do sesei,
Ͻnye Wo Sunsum na Wo su;
Ewuradze, Ͻwo nye nkwa nsunyiwa n'
Afei ma munhu W' m'akoma m’. '

MHB 605
2 . Ma monnom W’ mma nsukͻm nndze m’ bio,
Enyigyé a ͻkye ho nsu no a;
O nkwa nsu, pem bra wͻ sor ntum m’,
Wͻ esutsen a ͻyɛ daa asomdwee m,’
Wͻ dɛw a obiara nnkotum agye m’,
Wͻ ͻbra a obetsim afebͻͻ m’.

MHB 605
3 . Egya hue adorn gu mo do
No ma mindzi bem wͻ W‘enyim,
Bea a 'humbͻbͻr ’sutsen fi pem,
Ehumbͻbͻr, W'apɛdze pa n’,
Jesus dzin mu ntsi fa ma me
Na dua Wo su wͻ m‘akoma m’.

MHB 605
4 . Mo nkwa nda nyina m' munhu W’adwen.
Bér a metsé abͻbͻfo hͻn su,
Ekunafo, ngyanka, hͻn nkrumsi.
Mutu ehumbͻbͻfo ntsaban do
Kɛgye ehiafo na abͻbͻfo.
Dze mo nkwa, m’adze nyina ma hͻn.

MHB 605
5 . Dɛm na m‘bɛkyérɛ sunsum a ͻwͻ m’ mu.
Ͻtsew mo ho fi bͻn ho koraa.
Wonnhu no wͻ bͻn wiadze yi m’.
Otsim me gyedzi ne nyansaa;
Ͻma m' som no nokwar da edzi
Wͻ ahosan pa na ͻdͻ mu.

MHB 606
1 . Hom a hom enyi tsim 
Zion kwan do, hom mbra,
Wɔmma yɛnyɛ kor nyi
Hɛn Wura No ayɛw;
Wɔmma yentu ntsen Jesus mu
Nkɛpem dɛ yebopue N'enyim.

MHB 606
2 . Mber nyina yɛda ho 
Tow kɔ hɛn man no ho,
Kɔ sor kokwaa no ho
Kwantunyi fonafo fie;
Sor Jerusalem fofor no
Ɔdomankoma dɔ fie no.

MHB 606
3 . Ma daa nyina yennya 
Gyedzi ho asomdwee,
Dɛ woeyi hɛn efi
Bɔn, wiadze, wu, na hɛllm';
Hɛn yɛbɔkɔ hɛn Egya fie,
Hɔ yeekehyia hɛn Nua panyin n'.

MHB 606
4 . Hɛn Nua, Agyenkwa, Tsir 
Ɔyɛ hɛn adze nyin;
Hɛn a yɛka No do n'
Yebohu N'enyim ntsɛm,
Ɔno nye hɛn nsɛfo esiarfo n';
Hɔ hɛn akwantu bɔbɔ adze.

MHB 607
1 . Bethel Nyame, 'Wo a Wo nkorɔfo 
Dan Wo na wonya dzi;
Ɔwò a igyaa tsetse mpanyin
Hɔn akwantu nyinam'.

MHB 607
2 . Yɛdze nsewdzi na mpaabɔ ba 
W'adom ahengua enyim;
Hɛn egyaam Nyame, yɛserɛ Wo, yɛ
Hɔn mba so hɛn Nyame.

MHB 607
3 . Ɔbra n'akwan nyinara mu 
Gye hɛn anamɔn taataa;
Ma hɛn hɛn daadaa edziban
Na hɛn efuradze so.

MHB 607
4 . O trɛ W'atsaban wɔ hɛn do 
Kɔ hɛn akwantu ewiei,
Na hɛn akra eetum edu
Hɛn Egya fie asomdweem'.

MHB 607
5 . Dɛm n-hyira na yɛserɛ 
Fi W'adom n-samu;
Yɛdze Wo yɛ hɛn Nyankopɔn
Na kyɛpɛn afebɔɔ.  Amen.

MHB 608
1 . Israel akodɔm Sahen, 
Sor akwantufo hɔn kwangyafo,
Wo nwinwin ase na yɛtse,
Wo dɔ mununkum kata hɛn do;
Hɛn tum, W'adom; hɛn mbra, W'asɛm;
Hɛn ewiei, Ewuradze N'enyimnyam.

MHB 608
2 . Dɛ Wo Sunsum gya hɛn yi dze, 
Yɛnnkɔfom kwan wɔ sar yi do;
Yennhia dɛ daa wɔkyerɛ hɛn kwan,
Yɛnnkɔfom hɛn Nyame kwan no;
Mbusu nye suro bɔkɔ ekyir,
Ber a ɔdɔ kɛse bɛn hɛn.

MHB 609
1 . GYEFO, gya hɛn dɛ Guanhwɛfo;
Yehia Wo nhwɛdo pa no;
Nyɛn hɛn wɔ W'edzidzibea do;
Isiesie hɛn ma W'edwuma;
Jesus Siarfo,
Atɔ hɛn, yɛyɛ Wodze.

MHB 609
2 . Yɛyɛ Wodze, fa hɛn nyɛnko,
Yɛ hɛn kwan mu Kwankyerɛfo;
Kora Wo nguankuw, gye hɛn fi bɔn m',
Sɛ yɛfom kwan a, hwehwɛ hɛn:
Jesus Siarfo,
Yɛkamfo W', sɔr Wo a, tsie hɛn.

MHB 609
3 . Abɔ anohoba a 'bɛgye hɛn,
Yɛyɛ abɔn na abɔbɔfo a
'Wɔ ehumbɔbɔr a edze gye hɛn
Na adom a ɔtsew hɛn ho;
Jesus Siarfo,
Ma yɛnyɛ ntsɛm mbra Wo hɔ.

MHB 609
4 . Ma yɛnhwehwɛ W'enyimpa ntsɛm,
Ma yɛnyɛ ntsɛm nyɛ Wo pɛ;
Domfo Ewuradze, hɛn Agyenkwa,
Bra na bɛhyɛ hɛn mu ma;
Jesus Siarfo,
Adɔ hɛn, kɔ do dɔ hɛn.

MHB 61
1 . ASAASE, fa wo ndze mpempem, 
Tow ndwom yi Bɛkyebo ayɛw; 
Yi N'ayɛw, Nyia aso tsie No,
Tɛkyerɛma dze dɛw tow N' ndwom; 
Asaase dze n'enyigye ndwom
Fi ekyirkyir, mbrɛ nyimpa tse,
Bɔkotow aka W'akɛseyɛ,
Atow W'ayɛyi, ehyira W' dzin.

MHB 61
2 . Hom mbetsie anwanwasɛm no,
Mbrɛ tsetse Nyame tumfo a
Ɔdaa N'enyimnyam edzi no,
Ɔmaa asorɛkye saan ekyir,
Ɔmaa po nsu daan afasu,
Ɔmaa yɛfaa po bun mu;
Israel mbabaa dzii ehurusi,
Tontoon tum a ɔdze gye nkwa.

MHB 61
3 . Nyia ɔtse ase, hyira Ewuradze; 
Hom nyi N'ayɛw wɔ mbea nyina, 
Ɔdze hɛn akra san ba nkwa mu,
Ne basa suo hɛn mu gyina. 
Yɛdze enyigye dze hɛn afɔr
Bogu W'afɔrmbukyia do,
Anohoba a yɛbɔɔ n' yaw mu n',
Yɛdze dɛw tua n' anapa.

MHB 61
4 . Ɔkra biara a osuro Nyia ɔtse
Ahengua do no Ne mbra n',
Ɔmfa enyigye mbetsie dza
Nyame ayɛ ama hɛn ntotɔserɛ;
Ber a yɛdze hɛn ndze do wɔ mpaabɔ m', 
Yehun N'enyigye nkwagye no,
Yɛkamfo No mbɔbɔrhu.

MHB 610
1 . Agyedzifo hɔn Kwankyerɛfo a  
lgya sor akwantufo kwan,
Bra na enye hɛn so mbɛtsena,
Yɛpɛ yɛatwer Wo nkotonoo,
Dze hɛn sunsum adan Wo nko
Ber a yɛnam ɔbra kwan mu.

MHB 610
2 . Ahɔho nye amamforafo, 
Wiadze ha ɔnnyɛ hɛn tsenabew;
Na yetwa mbusu bɔnsa yim',
Yɛper dɛ yebohu W'enyim,
Yɛpɛ ntsɛm yeedu hɛn kurom',
Hɛn domakoma fie wɔ sor.

MHB 610
3 . Yennyi mantsimadze wɔ ha,
Yɛhwɛ kurow a wonnhu no kwan;
Yɛhom do nantsew kɔ noho,
Yereper yeedu kan mbew no do,k
Jerusalem kurow krɔnkrɔn a ɔ
Tsease Nyame ɔkyekyeree n'.

MHB 610
4 . Yɛdze abotar tu empire n', 
Yegya fona wiadze 'i ekyir:
Fi ahoɔdzenm' kɔ ahoɔdzenm',
Hwehwɛ Jerusalem fofor n';
Hɛn mbɔdzembɔ nyina nye dɛ,
Yenya Jerusalem fofor n'.

MHB 610
5 . 'Wo a asoa hɛn bɔn nyina kɔ, 
Na adom hɛn bɔnfakyɛ kwa,
Yɛnam Wo do kɔ hɛn sor fie,
Yɛdze adwontow yɛsan Zion;
Hɛn 'nyimnyam Hen N'ahenkurow no,
Yɛrotow ndwom nna ɔrebɛn hɛn.

MHB 610
6 . Nyame dɔ ne mfar ma hɛn do
Nu hɛn ahoɔdzen mu kɔ kan
Yɛrokɔ Nyame bepɔw n' do
Yɛakɔdɔm mbakan Asɔr no,
Yɛdze dɛw bɛyɛ abɔtsir
Yeekehyia hɛn Sahen wɔ sor.

MHB 611
1 . Gya hɛn, ɔsor Egya, gya hɛn 
Wɔ wiadze po pramee do,
Gya hɛn, weɔn hɛn, kora hɛn, nyɛn hɛn,
Yennyi boafo dɛ Wo nko,
Naaso yɛwɔ nhyira nyinak
Sɛ Nyame ne hɛn Egya a.

MHB 611
2 . Agyenkwa, fa hɛn bɔn kyɛ hɛn; 
Hɛn mberɛwyɛ nyina Ɔwo nyim;
'Wo dzii hɛn kan nantseew wiadze,
'Wo tsee no mu yaw wenwen;
Eyɛɛ ankonam, dze berɛ,
Na fona kyiin sar no do.

MHB 611
3 . Hɛn Nyame Sunsum a 'risian, 
Fa sor dɛw hyɛ 'koma ma,
Na yɛmfa ɔdɔ mbɔ dɔ mu,
Wɔ enyigye a ɔnnsɛɛ dam',
Edom, dze kyɛ, weɔn hɛn yi dze,
Hwere rennsɛɛ hɛn asomdwee.

MHB 612
1 . Gya m', Kan dɔyɛfo wɔ sum a etwa ehyia yim' 
Gya m' ara kɔ!
'Nago n' yɛ sum, menye fie ntam' so war;
Gya m' ara kɔ!
Weɔn m'anamɔn, mimmbisa dɛ munhu
Mbrɛ kan hɔ tse, namɔn kor ara ma m'.

MHB 612
2 . Nkyɛ menntse dɛm, monnsɔɔr pɛn dɛ Woara 
Gya m' ara kɔ.
Nkyɛ mefa mo kwan, na muhum', afei
Woara gya m' ara kɔ!
Modɔɔ apɔmpɔmpɛ, na musuro mpo a,
Ntsɛn hyɛɛ me ma, mma nnkaa mfe a-etwam' kɔ.

MHB 612
3 . Wo tum ehyira me dze, ɔbɛda ho 
Egya m' akɔ
Atra sar, abo na nsu, 'kɛpem dɛ
Sum yi bɛpa;
Na adze kye a, adɔfo a mayew hɔn n'
M'bohu hɔn bio dɛ wɔreserew kyerɛ m'.

MHB 613
1 . O EGYA, gya hɛn wɔ asomdwee akwan mu;
Wo nsa enngya hɛn abamba a, yɛtɔ gon,
'Kyingye tu hɛn bo, 'werɛhow yɛ kɛse;
Gya hɛn Christ mu, nokwar, nkwa na kwan no.

MHB 613
2 . O Egya, gya hɛn wɔ nokwar akwan m';
Ammboa hɛn a, yɛtotɔ mfom abaw m',
Akɔndɔ na nsɛmfun sɛɛ hɛn mbabun,
Mpanyinyɛ a gyedzi na enyidar nnyi m' ba.

MHB 613
3 . O Egya, gya hɛn wɔ akwan pa no mu;
Sɛ hɛn nko nam a, yefintsiw enyifura m',
Sɛ yɛnam anafua sum kebii mu a;
Wo nkotsee na yɛnye W' tu hɛn kwan sɔnn.

MHB 613
4 . O Egya, gya hɛn kɔ sor ahomgye m',
Mbrɛ kwan n' bun na ne tantan tse biara,
Dɛw anaa yaw mu, dɛ mbrɛ ehwɛ a oye;
Kɛpem dɛ hɛn bra bedzi mu Wo mu.   Amen.

MHB 614
1 . SOR Egya, Ɔwo na edze hɛn
Aba ndɛ da yi mu sɔnn;
Ekyerɛ hɛn anamɔn kwan berɛww,
Ehwɛ hɛn do wɔ hɛn kwan m'.
Ɔbra m' Damfo na Kwankyerɛfo,
Yɛdze ndaase akoma brɛ W';
Sɛ nnyɛ Wo dɔ a ɔnnsakyer no a,
Nkyɛ yebesi dɛn akamfo W'?

MHB 614
2 . Mbɔrbɔrhu bi a ɔnnkɛpa da
Hyerɛn yie wɔ dza etwa m' mu,
Nhwɛdo mapa na ayamuyie 'dɔ
Bɛn hɛn fi ahyɛse kɔ ewiei,
Ɔdɔ na ntwitwagye mapa 
Wɔ hɛn nkyɛn daa daa nyina;
Nhyira a ɔdɔɔ so a yenntum nnkan
Dze kan hyɛnn ba hɛn kwan mu.

MHB 614
3 . Isum kebii aba hɛn kwan mu,
Hɛn ho apopo wɔ ehum n' mu;
Mununkum etwa hɛn ho ehyia sunkamm
Ma yennhu Wo su mbrɛ ɔtse:
Naaso Wo dɔ n' nngyaa hɛn hɔ dɛ 
Ankonam wɔ hɛn yaw m' da,
Na mboa a obiara dze maa n' nkyɛnko n'
Yɛ ahoɔdzen a ofir Egya W' nkyɛn

MHB 614
4 . Nkorɔfo a yɛdɔɔ hɔn kɔ gya hɛn,
Edzi kan wɔ akwantu ewiei;
Wɔrotweɔn ama hɛn akɔaba,
'Nuanom, mba na ndamfo so.
Sɛ ewiei hɛn akwantu n' bɔ adze
Na yɛyew fi enyi do a,
Egya, fa hɛn dua sum kebii m'
Nye hɛn nkɔ onnyiewiei kan mu.  Amen.

MHB 615
1 . Gya m', O gya m', Jehovah tumfo, 
Kwantunyi a menam sar do;
Meyɛ mberɛw, 'wo yɛ hoɔdzenfo;
Fa Wo tum nsa n' suo mo mu;
Sor edziban!
Nyɛn me ndɛ na mber nyina.

MHB 615
2 . Bue nsunyiwa hyɛnhyɛnn n' sesei, 
Mbrɛ yarsa nsu fi pem no;
Ma ogya na mununkum fadum
Ngya m' m'akwantu nyina mu:
Gyefo tumfo!
Yɛ mo mboa na me kyɛm daa.

MHB 615
3 . Na mudu Jordan nkɔnkɔnoa a, 
Bɔ mo suro ham ma ɔnhera;
Wu no kumfo, hɛll ne sɛɛfo,
Fa me kodu Canaan sɔnn.
Ayɛyindwom
Na medze m'bɛma Wo daa.

MHB 616
1 . EKYINGYE na awerɛhow anafua m',
Kwantufo kuw no pem do,
Wɔtow enyidar ndwom ahorow
Dze kɔ bɔhyɛ asaase do.

MHB 616
2 . Yehu kan a ɔkyerɛ hɛn kwan no
Wɔ hɛn enyim anafuasum m';
Onua suo no nua ne nsamu
'Kododur m' dua sum no mu.

MHB 616
3 . Nyame N' kan wɔ hɛn ho yɛ kor,
Ɔhyerɛn wɔ No nkorɔfo do;
Ɔpam sum na suro kɔ ekyir,
Ɔhyerɛn wɔ hɛn kwan mu.

MHB 616
4 . Hɛn akwantu botae yɛ kor,
Hɛn gyedzi a ɔmmbɔ adze yɛ kor,
Dza hɛn enyi da kwan yɛ kor,
'Nyidar kor a ofir Nyame.

MHB 616
5 . M-pempem hɔn ntseamu n' yɛ kor
Dɛ mbrɛ ofi akoma kor mu;
Aperdzi kor na mbusu kor,
Nyame m' nserabɔ kor hyɛ ase.

MHB 616
6 . Ekyirkyir onnyiewiei mpoano
No mu dɛw na osebɔ kor,
Hɔ na Egya tumfo kor no
Dzi hen wɔ dɔ m' afebɔɔ.

MHB 616
7 . Hom nkɔ do, 'nuanom akwantufo,
Hom mfa mbeamudua no nduom!
Mma hom mmfɛr, hom nko ɔko no
Nkɛpem dɛ yɛbɔhom nwin m'.

MHB 616
8 . Ɔnnkɛkyɛr, wɔsoɛr da n' bɛba
Na woebuebue ndakamaa;
Afei sunsum nyina bɔhwetse,
Ɔberɛ na sum bɔbɔ adze.

MHB 617
1 . HƐN frankaa kan hyerɛn,
Na ɔkyerɛ sor,
'Nyam ma Christ nsordaafo
Dze kɔ hɔn sor fie.
Yɛdze enyigye bɔ mpaa
Bɔ nsera wɔ sar n' do.
Yɛdze akoma kor
Tow ndwom wɔ hɛn kwan m'.

MHB 617
2 . HƐN frankaa kan hyerɛn,
Na ɔkyerɛ sor,
'Nyam ma Christ nsordaafo
Dze kɔ hɔn sor fie.

MHB 617
3 . Jesus, Ewuradze,
W'ananadze ha
Wo mba a woridzi dɛw
Etwa ehyia ha.
Mpɛn pii na yeefi W' nkyɛn
Na yɛatɔ dɔnsuar;
Kora hɛn, Agyenkwa tumfo,
Wɔ kwan tseabaa n' mu.

MHB 617
4 . Hɛn nda nyina m' kyerɛ hɛn
Kwan a yɛmfa do;
Gya hɛn konyim mu ara
Wɔ atamfo nyina do;
W'abɔfo nwowaw hɛn
Ber a mbusu abɛn;
Fa kyɛ hɛn na gya hɛn
Wɔ da bɔn no mu.

MHB 617
5 . Yɛnye ahotsewfo na
Abɔfo mbɔ m' wɔ sor,
Mbɔ mpaa nyi Wo ayɛw
Wo dɔ ahengua n' ho;
Ber a nserabɔ n' abɔ adze,
'Homgye na asomdwee m',
Jesus wɔ N'ahoɔfɛw m';
Nyɛ ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze

MHB 618
1 . ENYIGYE akwantufo kuw,
Sɛ hom bɔkɔ hom enyim a,
Hom mfa Jesus ndzi hom kan,
Mma Jesus nyɛ hom Tsir.

MHB 618
2 . Sɛ hom fona ma nkorɔfo dɛ
Jesus a, hom dzi dɛw;
Sɛ kɔm dze hom dɛ Jesu a,
Ɔno hom so dzi dɛw.

MHB 618
3 . Mbeamudua a Jesus soae no,
Hom ara ntsi na ɔsoae;
Ahenkyɛw a Jesus soae no,
Hom ara ntsi na ɔsoae.

MHB 618
4 . Gyedzi a hom dze hu No n',
Enyidar a hom dze per n',
Ɔdɔ a ɔhaw dan hwɛ No nko n'
Bɛsan akɔ No nko hɔ.

MHB 618
5 . Nkodzen a ɔhaw hom adwen,
Awerɛhow a hom dzi no,
Nsɔhwɛ beberee a hom kɔ mu n',
'Wu nko na otum twa do.

MHB 618
6 . Ebɛnadze na ɔsom bo dɛ
N'egudze a ɔwɔ sor hɔ n'?
Ebɛnadze na ɔkyɛn
Atwer a wɔfow kɔ sor?

MHB 618
7 . Enyigye akwantufo kuw,
Hom mma hom enyi do sor,
Hɔ na hom haw kakra yi
Bɛma hom dza ɔsom bo.

MHB 619
1 . WONDUOM! Hɛn asɛm nye n';
'Namɔn na ndze mbɔ m',
Hwehwɛ dza ɔwɔ enyim,
Yenntwa hɛn kɔn 'kyir;
Ogya fadum no dzɛw
Dzi nsordaafo kan;
Hɛn Sahen dzi enyim yi,
Woana bɔbɔ hwea?
Hom mfa sar n' do nkɔ enyim,
Wɔ fona nye ɔko m';
Jordan pem wɔ hɛn enyim,
Zion ne kan hyerɛn.

MHB 619
2 . Enyimnyam mbordo koraa
Na Nyame esiesie,
Da kor ɔdze bɛma
Akra a wɔdɔɔ No n';
Enyi nnhun hɔn pɛn mpo,
Asowa nntsee da,
Wɔnnkaa hɔn ho asɛm,
Wɔnndween hɔn ho so,
Hom nduom, hom nkɔ hom enyim!
Hom nhyɛ akontar hyɛnn
Nkɛpem dɛ woyi enyim a
Yehu hɛn gyedzi.

MHB 619
3 . Borɔ ekyirkyir noho
Kuropɔn abantsen pue
Mbrɛ hɛn Nyame tse no;
Fie fɛɛfɛw n' hɛndze a;
Nhwehwɛ mbobow ara nko,
Sika hyerɛn n'abrɔn m',
Ahomka esutsen pem
Dze dɛw a wɔnnka ba.
Hom nduom, hom nkɔ hom enyim!
Wɔ Sunsum No tum m';
Akwantufo, hom nkɔ
Hom kan man no mu.

MHB 62
1 . ƆDƆ, mbrɛ osi dɔ, tserɛw ɔkrɔn!
Ɔdze dɛw hyɛ akoma ma,
Dɛ Nyame Ba, Nyame bɛfa
Hɛn nyimpadua wɔ nyimpa ntsi.

MHB 62
2 . Ɔannsoma ɔbɔfo biara
Wɔ bea a ɔkrɔn anaa osuar,
Nankasa faa hɛn nyimpadua,
Ɔbaa wiadze a ayew yi mu.

MHB 62
3 . Wɔbɔɔ no esu wɔ hɛn ntsi,
Odzii mbuada, ɔkɔm dzee No;
Hɛn ntsi ohyiaa nsɔhwɛ yaayaw,
Ɔkaa sɔhwɛfo n' gui maa hɛn.

MHB 62
4 . Ɔbɔɔ mpaa maa hɛn, kyerɛkyerɛɛ hɛn, 
Ɔyɛɛ Ne daa edwuma maa hɛn:
No dwumadzi, Ne nsɛnkyerɛdze,
Ne nsɛm nyina mu, ɔhwehwɛɛ hɛn.

MHB 62
5 . Woyii No hyɛɛ abɔnfo nsa,
Wɔkaa No mpire, dzii No ho fɛw,
Ɔsoaa 'nyimguase mbeamudua,
Hɛn ntsi oguu ohomtsen, wui.

MHB 62
6 . Ɔsoɛɛr fii wu mu bio maa hɛn;
Ɔfowee kɔr sor ma odzi hen;
Ɔsomaa No Sunsum brɛɛ hɛn
Dɛ ongya hɛn na ɔnhyɛ hɛn dzen.

MHB 62
7 . Nyia No dɔ nnyi mbanano agye
Nkwagye ama hɛn Ne Ba mu;
Enyimnyam nka Nyame Egya,
Sesei na nfesantsen nyina. 	  Amen.

MHB 620
1 . NYIA ɔpɛ akokodur n',
Ɔmbra enyim mbɔhwɛ;
Onyia no begyina daa,
Ehum na aahow mbra;
Abagura bi nnyi hɔ a
Ɔbɛma oeegyaa sua,
No suakan dɛ ɔbɛyɛ
Ɔkwantunyi no.

MHB 620
2 . Hɔn a wɔkeka nsɛmbɔn
Twa no ho aprɔw n',
Wogu hɔn enyim ase,
N'ahoɔdzen mu piw,;
Gyata bi nnkopuw no,
Ɔnye ɔkraban bɔko,
Na obenya ndzinoa dɛ
Ɔyɛ kwantunyi.

MHB 620
3 . Sunsum bɔn bi nnyi hɔ a
Obogura n'abaw;
Onyim dɛ ewiei no
Obenya daa nkwa.
Nsusuhum nyina boguan;
Onnkosuro dza wɔka
Ɔbɛyɛ edwuma ber nyina
Ayɛ kwantunyi.

MHB 621
1 . JESUS yε Oguanhwεfo pa;
Jesus wui gyee nguan no nkwa;
Ɔyε m’dze, meyε Nedze;
Dza mihia No mu n’ minya,
N-kwà ahomgye edziban, ’
Nyame mu ndzepa biara.

MHB 621
2 . Jesus dɔ nà ɔweɔn Nedze,
Ɔnyεn m’ ’dzidzflaea pa do,
Ɔma me da famu dzinn,
Ogya m’ kɔ abodwee nsu ho:
Menye No kɔ beebiara a,
M’akoma mu dεw bu do.

MHB 621
3 . Meyar a ɔma metsé apɔw,
