Ogya me kɔ asomdwee mu;
Okenyan me kré a ɔahaw,
Ɔma tsénenee tsim mo mu;
Ɔno a obowui gyee me n’,
Ɔda ho dɔ m’ - menntsé ase!

MHB 621
4 . Nyame dɔ bεda ho efua m’,
Ɔda bohwε m’ do akɔ ewiei;
M’enyigye nda nyinara
Mibedzi no W’asɔrfi m’,
Kεpem dε m’botù aba W’ fie,
Wo sor fie a ɔwɔ hɔ daa!

MHB 622
1 . EWURADZE, kyerɛ m' kwan
Ma ɔnda hɔ;
Mibetsie W'asɛm no,
San si do bio;
Munntu anamɔn kor gyedɛ muhu
Kwan kor a Ɔwoara bɛkyerɛ me.

MHB 622
2 . Ewuradze, munnhu adze,
Yɛ kan ma me;
Fua no tu m'akoma,
Munnhu adze:
Suo me nsamu na ma mindzi Wo nkyɛn,
Mma mo nko monnkɔ, yɛ me Kwangyafo.

MHB 622
3 . Ewuradze, abotar m'
M'bɔtwer, etsim;
Menngye W'asɛm ho kyim,
M'enyidar tsim;
Metar Wo ho a mebɛyɛ dɛn ahera,
M'awerɛkyekyer, Agyenkwa, Kwangyafo?

MHB 623
1 . MENYE annda dɛ ebɛba abɛfa
M'akoma bɔbɔfo 'i ayɛ Wo fie,
Dɛ Ɔwo ahemfo Hen bɛba abɔsoɛ
Mo mu edzi bɛyɛ dɔnhwer kor mpo;
Naaso ewɔ ha daa dɛ ibehyira m',
Aboa m' na eyi mo bɛn adzesoa n'.

MHB 623
2 . M'enyi annda dɛ m'benya W' Kwankyerɛfo,
Ma aagye m' taataa, atsentsen m'anamɔn;
Sɛ mohwe ase a, suo mo mu, motɔ gon a,
Gya m' nkakrankakra kɔ kwan pa no mu.
Naaso ewɔ me nkyɛn aber biara,
Eyɛ me Pamfo na Werɛkyekyefo.

MHB 623
3 . Monnkɔ mbrɛ Ɔwo gya me daa nyina,
Mennyɛ aso mma Wo ndze a ewasa m' no;
Meka kan afofor bi do, na mo bɔn m',
Kakraabi na mehyɛ m' Nyɛnko ebufuw;
Naaso idzi yaw mpo a, inngya me hɔ,
Mbom eweɔn Wo tsenabea wɔ m'akoma m'.

MHB 624
1 . JESUS, dzi hɛn kan,
Ma yennya ahomgye,
Na kwan no nnyɛ enyigye mpo a,
Yɛbɛka W' do berɛww a yennsuro;
Fa Wo nsa gya hɛn
Kɔ hɛn Egya fie.

MHB 624
2 .  Sɛ kwan yɛ hu dɛn,
Sɛ atamfo bɛn a,
Mma suro gyangyan bi mmen hɛn,
Mma ɔdɔ na enyidar mmbɔ hɛn;
Yɛnam atamfo m'
Kɔ hɛn efiefi.

MHB 624
3 . Ber a yɛper ahotɔ
Fi yaw dzendzen mu,
Ber a nsɔhwɛ fofor hyɛ hɛn do n',
Owura, ma hɛn abotar ndzi mu,
Kyerɛ hɛn bea hyɛnhyɛnn a
Yennsu wɔ hɔn bio n'.

MHB 624
4 . Ber a 'saase na wimu
Yew hɛn enyi do n',
Ber a yɛnam 'wu m' hwɛ heaven kwan
Na wɔdze hɛn bɔn nyina akyɛ hɛn, 
Fi Wo kan man n' mu
Frɛ hɛn Nyame fie.

MHB 624
5 . Jesus, dzi hɛn kan,
Ma yennya ahotɔ;
Sor Kandzifo, kɔ do gya hɛn,
Wowaw, weɔn hɛn, kyekye hɛn werɛ, 
Kɛpem dɛ hɛn nyina
Bodu hɛn Egya fie.  Amen.

MHB 625
1 . MEMA m'enyi do hwɛ mbepɔw n',
Hɔ na mo mboa fi ba;
Me bambɔ fi Ewuradze hɔ ba,
Ɔno a ɔbɔɔ sor na ase.

MHB 625
2 . Ɔremma w'anan mm-patser,
Na ɔronntɔ nkom so:
Hwɛ, Nyia ɔhwɛ Israel do no,
Ɔnntɔ nkom, na ɔnnda.

MHB 625
3 . Ewuradze nkora w' No nwin ase,
Ongyina w'abanyimfa;
Bosoom nnkɛsɛɛ wo anafua,
Ewia nnsɛɛ w' adzekyee.

MHB 625
4 . Ewuradze bɔkora wo kra do,
Ɔbɔhwɛ wo yar ber m';
Ɔdzekɔ 'i w'edzifir na mbae
Nyame bɔhwɛ afebɔɔ.  Amen.

MHB 626
1 . MOROHWEHWƐ nyamesuro
Nhyehyɛɛ bi wɔ mo mu,
Ɔnye bɔn ho adwendahɔ a
Ɔma metse ne yaw.

MHB 626
2 . Mepɛ kwan a m'bɛfa do metu
N-tuw na akɔndɔbɔn,
Medze esiw 'kwankwambɔ pɛ kwan,
Medze bodum bɔn gya.

MHB 626
3 . Dɛ monnkɔtɔ dɔnsuar mmfi W' hɔ n',
Mennka W'ayamuyie fi n',
Ma m' etsidaa wansawansa
Na enyidahɔ akoma.

MHB 626
4 . Nyame, ma m'adwendahɔ nyɛ
Dza obiara enyi gye ho;
Na nyan me kra, ber a bɔn abɛn,
N'enyi do ntsetsew no.

MHB 626
5 . O nkyɛ me kra a wɔatsetse n' yie 'i
Eehu dza ofura adwen,
Ɔaatwe m' akɔ bɔgya no ho,
Bɔgya a ɔma ahosan.

MHB 627
1 . MBRƐ adom ba a enyi si gye
Wɔ no bɔnfakyɛ ho a!
Osu dɛ: Me fie nnyi ase ha,
Meper me fier wɔ sor!
Ɔman a nyimpa enyi nnhu,
O menam gyedzi m' hu;
'Homgye man, 'hotsewfo enyigye,
Heaven a woesiesie ama m'.

MHB 627
2 . Meyɛ hɔho wɔ wiadze ha,
'Hobrɛadze m' mosoɛ ha;
No mu enyigye na fona
Nnkenyan enyidar na suro;
Mber tsiabaa siw n'adzesɛɛ ano,
No mu dɛw twa mu ntsɛm;
O mbom ahomka a meka do n'
Betsim hɔ afebɔɔ.

MHB 627
3 . Jerusalem a ɔwɔ sor hɔ n',
Menam adwontow m' kɔ hɔ;
Metse ase yi, m'enyidar, dɔ,
M'akoma, kra, wɔ hɔ.
M'Agyenkwa a wɔakrɔn N' gyina hɔ,
Sɔfo mbɔbɔrhufo,
Ɔda ho tsen N'epir nsa n'
Twe me kɔ No bomu.

MHB 627
4 . O hɛn enyidar yɛ nhyira dɛ!
Ber a yɛwɔ asaase 'i do,
Ɔkyɛn dɛ yɛka sor tum hwɛ,
Na yɛtwe dɛm da n' bɛn;
Yɛtse dɛ wusoɛr na abɛn,
Hɛn bra hyɛ Christ No mu,
N'enyimnyam fɛɛfɛw a ɔwɔ ase ha n'
Hyɛ hɛn nyimpadua ma.

MHB 628
1 . HOM a hom yɛ hom Wura Ne pɛ,
Hom akoma nyɛ botoo daa;
Dabiara hom nka hom bɔn,
Hom a hom nantsew tsenenee mu;
Akra pa a hom wɔ adom mu,
Hom nhwehwɛ hom Ewuradze.

MHB 628
2 . Akra a hom enyi gye mper
Nkɔ sor a ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn no;
Hom ngye N'anohoba no,
Nye adom a ɔwɔ dze ma;
Hom nka do, mma wɔnngow mu,
Kɛpem dɛ hom hu N'enyim

MHB 629
1 . DZA Nyame nyansafo pɛ ayɛ,
Ɔbɛma, anaa ɔnnkɛma,
Na onyim m'ehiadze nyina yie
Sen dza me mpaabɔ ka.

MHB 629
2 . Dem nhyira a memmfata yi
Ahyɛ mo mfom kwan n' nsew;
Na beebiara a matɔ dɔnsuar n',
Ne ntsea san me ekyir.

MHB 629
3 . Dem ɔdɔ mu ndzepa piigyan n',
Ntseasee wɔ mu koraa;
Okenyan mber ɔnye adwen
Wɔ eyiedzi dɛɛdɛw m'.

MHB 629
4 . Owu yɛ dɛ kwan bi a oesiw,
Na obue kɔ kan mu,
Na ɔba onyifurafo biara
Nntɔ gon mmfi Egya enyim.

MHB 629
5 . Afei 'hwɛyie na nkodzen ba,
Nam witɔree m' nkaakaa
Dɛ mbrɛ wohu mbepɔw wɔ ekyir
Ber a wɔatra edu bea pa.

MHB 629
6 . Abrabɔ mu dede nyina
Bɔ mu yie wɔ ndwom mu,
Na abrabɔ aperdzi bea nyina
Yɛ berɛww taa dzin koraa.

MHB 629
7 . Afei sunsum hyɛ ase pa,
Ma anee mframa so bɔ;
Na mubue m'akoma nyina
Mu dze ma dɛm da no.

MHB 63
1 . ONYAME dɔ a no bun nnyi ase, 
Jesus mu Nyame da edzi;
Hwɛ mbrɛ W'enyimnyam hyerɛn pa!
W'ayarsa nsu pem mbea nyina!

MHB 63
2 . Epɛ nye woananom atsena?
Ndzebɔnyɛfo, bɔnnyiayɛfo: 
Onyankopɔn, tɛkyerɛma bɛn 
Botum akyerɛ Wo dɔ na adom?

MHB 63
3 . Dɛw mu yɛdze akoma m' ndaase 
Gye dza Wo dɔ pɛ ka kyerɛ hɛn,
Fa W' enyigye nyina ma hɛn, 
Yɛdze hɛnho nyina ma Wo.

MHB 63
4 . Yɛdze hɛn honam, 'kra, sunsum, 
Hyɛ Wo dɔ nye W'ayamuyie nsa:
O ma Wo krɔnkrɔnyɛ ntsena hɔ,
Na sɔw hɛn ano dɛ Wodze.

MHB 63
5 . Enyimnyam Hen, W'adom kɛse n'
Bor hɛn adwen no do koraa;
Hɛn bɔn mpo dɔɔ so dɛn ara a,
W'ehumbɔbɔr bor ne nyina do.

MHB 63
6 . Ewuradze, da Wo nkwagye edzi,
Ma hɛn akra Wo sor ahoɔdzen;
Na yennsuro dɛ yɛkɔ enyim,
Wɔ asaase na hɛll etumfo m'.

MHB 630
1 . O MA hɛn kan, ama yeehu
Nyansa a Wo nko tum dze ma no;
Ama nokwar aakyerɛ hɛn kwan,
Na nhyira aaba beebi a yɛbɛtsena.

MHB 630
2 . O ma hɛn kan, ama yeehu
Esintɔ a ɔwɔ nyimpa n' nyimdzee m',
Hɛn adwen a ohinhim n' yaadan ama W',
Yaadɔ W'asɛm pa no yie daa.

MHB 630
3 . O ma hɛn kan, ama yeesua
Dɛ bra a 'Wo nnkaho n' yɛ owu;
Hɔn a wɔdze akoma a osi pi
Ba Wo hɔ n', yeehu hɔn dɛw pa.

MHB 630
4 . O ma hɛn kan, 'werɛhow na yaw m',
Yɛmma hɛn akoma a ɔaberɛ n' do,
'Dze eehu dɛ mbeamudua n' yɛ mfaso,
Na yeehyira No dɔ a osuma n'.

MHB 630
5 . O ma hɛn sesei; ndaamba
Wiadze abrabɔ nyina twa mu a,
Yeehu abow a woebue n' wɔ Wo mu
Dze kɔ fie a 'wu nnyi m' afebɔɔ.    Amen.

MHB 631
1 . NANTSEW kan n' mu: na ibohu 
Ɔdɔ fɛkuwbɔ no a
No Sunsum nko tum dze ma no
Nyia odzi hen sor wɔ kan m'.

MHB 631
2 . Nantsew kan n' mu: na ibohu 
Dɛ w'akoma ayɛ N'dze koraa,
Nyia ɔtse kan a fua biara nnyi m' mu
Sum biara nnyi No mu.

MHB 631
3 . Nantsew kan n' mu: na ibohu 
Dɛ wo sum etwa m' kɔ,
'Siandɛ dɛm kan n' ahyerɛn wo ho,
No mu na da pa wɔ.

MHB 631
4 . Nantsew kan n' mu: na 'wumaa mpo
Nnkenya sum bi ama w';
Enyimnyam bɛpepa no sum,
Christ edzi nyim wɔ do.

MHB 631
5 . Nantsew kan n' mu: wodze bɛyɛ
Kwan a nsoɛ wɔ m' mpo a, ɔhyerɛn;
Adom ntsi Nyame bɛtsena w' mu,
Nyame Noara nye Kan.

MHB 632
1 . M'AKOMA Wura, yɛ dza osi m'enyi do;
Minnyi biribiara bio, gyedɛ Wo nko
'Dzekyee anaa adzesaa, Ɔwo, nye m'adwen pa,
Minyan anaa meda a, Ɔwo yɛ m' kan.

MHB 632
2 . Yɛ m' Nyansaa, Ɔwo m'Asɛm nokwafo;
Mowɔ Wo nkyɛn, Ewuradze, 'nye m' wɔ hɔ;
Eyɛ m' Egya kɛse, meyɛ W' ba pa;
Sɛ etse mo mu a, menye Wo yɛ adze kor.

MHB 632
3 . .Ɔko no mu, yɛ m'akokyɛm na peaa,
Yɛ m'enyimpa, Ɔwo yɛ dza mepɛ;
Eyɛ m' kra n' tsenabew, yɛ m'abantsentsen,
O mo Tumfo, pegya me kɔ heaven.

MHB 632
4 . Mennka ahonya anaa ayɛyi hun do,
Eyɛ m'egyapadze, sesei na daa;
Wo nko na idzi kan wɔ m'akoma m',
Heaven Ɔhempɔn, eyɛ m'akoradze.

MHB 632
5 . Heaven Ɔhempɔn, nsa aka konyimdzi n',
Ma minnya sor, heaven Ewia hyɛnhyɛn n'
M'akoma Wura, dza ɔbɛma biara,
Yɛ dza osi m'enyi do nyinara Wura.

MHB 633
1 . O adom Hen, fi sor ahengua n' do 
Fa dɔ hwɛ na tsie hɛn mbɔbɔr su.

MHB 633
2 . Hwɛfo pà a edze bɔgya tɔɔ Wo nguan, 
Kora Wo nguankuw a wɔnnkyɛr kwan fom.

MHB 633
3 . O Pomfo pa, Wo wu mu na agye hɛn: 
Ma abɔn awerɛhofo daa nkwa.

MHB 633
4 . Sor Edziban, yɛdze Wo nyɛn hɛnho: 
Pin bɔboa hɛn akra hɛn hia ber mu.

MHB 633
5 . Apatasu, ndzebɔnyɛfo Dɔfo, 
Edɛw na siar nsunyiwa a ɔnnsa da.

MHB 633
6 . Ao, fa sor adom kyekye hɛn werɛ; 
Yi W'enyim fɛɛfɛw n' enyimnyam kyerɛ.

MHB 633
7 . Adzekyeem' mununkum, adzesaam' ogya, 
Bɛn hɛn na dan hɛn sum ma ɔnyɛ kan.

MHB 633
8 . Nye hɛn nnantsew, nye hɛn kwan daa daa, 
Hɛn nkwam' na wum' Werɛkyekyer, Tum, Gyafo.

MHB 633
9 . Fa Wo dɔ enyi n' gya hɛn kwan daa daa, 
Na fa hɛn du hɛn sor fi nom' sɔkyee. Amen.

MHB 634
1 . WO kra sekyɛ botum ɔbra n'ehum,
Ber a nsuframa dzendzen robɔ yi?
Ma asorɛkye dzendzen retsetsew nhama m',
Wo sekyɛ betsim, anaa obegyina dzen?
   Sɛ ɔbra pram, ma asorɛkye bu a,
   Dɛm sekyɛ yi kora hɛn kra pintsinn;
   Ɔmontan ɔbotantsim a onnhim,
   Na otsim hɔ pintsinn wɔ Gyefo No dɔ m'.

MHB 634
2 . Wo sekyɛ botum egyina suro ber mu
Ehumtu kɛse nye abotar enyim?
Ber a po nye mframa tu hɔn tsir gu do n',
Ana nsu bɛpram ebunkam wo hɛmba?

MHB 634
3 . Wo sekyɛ botum wu n'esuyirii?
Ber a nsu nwinwin twa w'ahomtsia do?
Asorɛkye dzen mu mpo eronntɔ bahaw
'Siandɛ wo sekyɛ tsim enyidar man n' mu.

MHB 634
4 . W'enyiwa bohu anapa kan fɛɛfɛw n'
Zion sika kurow na ahɛndwirii hyɛnhyɛn n'
Ber a ɔbra n'ehum bɔbɔ adze nwionwion n',
Ibodwir sɔkyee wɔ ɔsor mpoano hɔ?

MHB 635
1 . JESU, mo N'okwar, Kwan,
Me kan a ennyew da,
Mo bͻn anamͻn tsim Wo do, .
’Wo begya m’ abamba.

MHB 635
2 . Me Nyansaa, Kwankyérɛfo
Ͻwo yɛ mo Pomfo,
O mma mimmfi Wo nkyɛn ara da
Anaa W’akwan so do!

MHB 635
3 . Kyérɛkyerɛ m’ enyigyadze
Na mendan W’ adze nyina m;
O m'Ewuradze, mma nngyaa me da,
Mbom, dͻ me kͻ ewiei!

MHB 635
4 . Fa me dua ogya na nsu m,’
Kodu ahonya bea hͻ;
Kyérɛ me ndowm fofor ma montow
Ber a mo ho astew adom m’.

MHB 635
5 . O yɛ m’ dɛ Ͻwo ara,
’Saana meetu efi ha!
Gye me to m’ na ma mentséna ha
Na siesie me wͻ dͻ m’.

MHB 635
6 . Ma mentséna ndzi W’ dase
Ber a bͻn nyina asé etu n;
Gye me kra a nkekaa nnyi ho no,
Na fa m’ kͻ Nyame fie.  Amen.

MHB 636
1 . WIADZE kan, hɛn anan a agogow n' hinhim
Wɔ ekyinkyin pii m',
Naaso 'bekyiaa hɛn akoma bɔbɔfo n',
'Napa Woraba;
Emaa yɛmaa hɛn enyi do tsim sor
Dze hwɛɛ ewia hyɛhyɛnn no n'enyimnyam.

MHB 636
2 . Tsetseber a etwa m' n', yɛyeew hɛn fie kwan;
Nna yennhu adze;
Hɛn enyi furae, hɛn anamɔn tɔɔ dɔnsuar;
Yeennhu Wo koraa!
Na Ɔwo Ewuradze hun hɛn mbɔbɔr;
Wo nsa kaa hɛn enyi ma obuebuei.

MHB 636
3 . Sesei Alleluia gyegye hɛn kwan m' 
Enyigye mu;
Wo dɔ eyi hɛn yaw na adzesoa duudur
Kan wɔ hɛn enyim;
Enyimnyam nka Wo, Ɔwo a W' dɔ agye hɛn,
'Nyimnyam nka W' wɔ ndzɛmba akɛse a ayɛ ntsi.

MHB 636
4 . Owu hwirom na 'wumaa konyim wɔ hen?
Yaw nyina wɔ hen?
Ber a twamutam a ɔkata wo do n' wo Hen 
Atsew mu yi?
Wiadze kan, yɛtse dɛ Ɔwo refrɛ hɛn
Kɔ W'onnyiewie kan na dɔ fie no mu.

MHB 637
1 . BER n'anhwea no remen ntsɛm
Heaven adzekyee n' yi enyim;
Wi puei ber a m'enyi daa kwan,
Da pa dɛɛdɛw n' aba,
Esuom yɛɛ sum dodoodow;
Adzekyee kan abɛn ,
Na enyimnyam mapa wɔ
Immanuel Ne man m'.

MHB 637
2 . Hen n' wɔ N'ahoɔfɛw m' wɔ hɔ n',
Yehun N'enyim petee;
'Kwantu a odzi mu na yetui,
Sɛ 'wu esuom wɔ mu mpo a;
Eguambaa n' nye N' nsordaafo
Gyina kokwaa Zion do,
Na enyimnyam mapa wɔ
Immanuel Ne man m'.

MHB 637
3 . O Christ, Ɔwo yɛ fapem
'Dɔ bura fɛɛfɛw a ɔdɔ;
Manom wiadze esu ahorow,
M'bɔnom papa wɔ Sor;
Na po yantamm bi w hɔ a
N'ehumbɔbɔr n' pem wɔ m',
Na enyimnyam mapa wɔ
Immanuel Ne man m'.

MHB 637
4 . Ehumbɔbɔr nye atsɛmbu m'
Ɔwo awen me mber
Na ampa, awerɛhow bɔsu n',
Wo dɔ n' pepaa no koraa;
M'benyira nsa a ogyaa me no,
M'behyira akoma a ɔhyehyɛe,
Ber a wɔahyɛ N' enyimnyam wɔ
Immanuel Ne man m'.

MHB 638
1 . NYAME Nyansabuakwa,
Hɔn Hen nye Agyenkwa,
Abɔfo a wɔwɔ ase ha
Mfa hɔn ayɛyi mbrɛ Wo.

MHB 638
2 . No dɔ kokroko na 
N'apam nye N' nhwedo pa
Kora hɛn sɔnn fi bɔn na owu mu,
Na efirsua yaayaw mu.

MHB 638
3 . Ɔbɔkora hɛn akra
Na ɔatsew ho nwionnwionn,
Wɔ N'enyim enyimnyam no mu,
Wɔ sor enyigye pa m'.

MHB 638
4 . Aba a wɔasan mu eyi n'
Behyia wɔ ahengua n' ho;
Wobehyira N'adom nwanwa n',
Wɔaka N'anwanwadze.

MHB 639
1 . CHRIST a onyim No nguan nyina
Bɔhwɛ hɛn nyina do sɔnn;
No bɔgyaa no anaa
N'amandzehu no
Rennyɛ kwa ara da,
Dɛ ɔtɔɔ hɛn ntsi n'.

MHB 639
2 . Minyim me Nyame tsen,
Ɔno na motwer No;
Dza mowɔ, meyɛ nyina
M'enyindado nyina
Dza mekeka hwɛ n' ha
Yɛ nokwar pefee.

MHB 639
3 . Jesus, gye mo sunsum,
Motwer Wo bra na su;
Fa 'guan yi kɔ fie na
Ahwehwɛ n' biara;
Kora ɔkra yi do sɔnn
Na Ɔwo atɔ no.

MHB 64
1 . Ayɛyi nka Ewuradze, Tumfo, abɔdze nyina hen; 
O me kra, yi N' ayɛw, Ɔno nye w' ahom na nkwagye;
Hom a hom tse,
Enuaam na nkyerɛbaa, hom mbra,
Hom ntonton No enyigye mu.

MHB 64
2 . Ayɛyi nka Ewuradze a otu w' edwuma 
    mpon, weɔn wo,
Ampaara Ne yie nye N' adom ka wo do daa wɔ ha:
Dwen ho bio hwɛ
Dza Otumfo No tum yɛ,
Sɛ ɔdze No dɔ fa w' nyɛnko a.

MHB 64
3 . Ayɛyi nka Ewuradze, ɔno a ehumtuber no mu, 
Ɔno na ber a abɔdze nyina etwa ayer wo no,
Ɔma wogyaa,
Begyabegyayɛ taa dzinn,
Ɔma ehum na po yɛ komm n'.

MHB 64
4 . Ayɛyi nka Ewuradze, ɔno a ber a bɔn na sum agye, 
Ɔno na abosonsɔrfo dzi nyim mmbu papayɛ bi a
Ne kan hyerɛn,
Pam sum mu ewurkadze,
N' adom bɔ esiarfo ho ban.

MHB 64
5 . Ayɛyi nka Ewuradze! Ao, dza ɔwɔ mo mu 
     nyina ntonton N'!
Dza wɔwɔ nkwa nye ahom m-fa ayɛyi mbra N' enyim!
Wɔmma Amen
Ngyegye bio wɔ nkorɔfom'
Yɛtonton No enyigyem' daa.

MHB 640
1 . WITƆREE, 'wimbir woraba,
Na frɛ kor a wɔdze afrɛ m'!
Na asorɛkye a orubu n' bɛda fɛmm,
Ber a migyina po enyim n;
Asorɛkye a orubu a ɔtse dɛ ɔada n',
Ɔnnkɛkyerɛ hwee koraa,
Ber a dza opuei fii bun yantamm no mu
San kɔ n'anan m'.

MHB 640
2 . Serɛmen na ewimbir dɔn n',
Na afei n'ekyir sum no!
Na mma wɔmmfa awerɛhow nngya me kwan
Ber a mesi m' no,
Kaansa yefi bea na ber yi mu mpo a,
Nsuyirii n' dze m'bɔkɔ ekyir,
Ber a mefi wiadze yi mu n', minyim dɛ
M'bohu Sutwafo n' enyim.

MHB 641
1 . BER a ’werɛhow ahyɛ mo do ’I,
Me Nyame yɛ m’ kyɛfa
Kodu dͻnhwér a ͻdze
Mo sunsum bɛma Wo n’.
Ber a honam na nkwa agow,
Tsen Wo nsa mu na gye
Me kra to W’abaw mu
Kodu dɛ minyan Wo m’.

MHB 641
2 . Anapa wi bɛhyérɛn
Ewimbir kan bͻtͻ m’,
Dɛm na ase ha kan n’ tse,
Sor dze n’ ͻnnsesa da;
Nyɛnko nnhwɛ nyɛnko enyim,
Kor dzi yaw wͻ mpoano;
Wo mba dze wommpue mmfi
Wo bea krͻnkrͻn no do.

MHB 641
3 . Mununkum kata hɛn do;
Yennsuro asehwe biara,
Yɛpɛ edu koko n’ do,
Hͻ na mboa pii fi ba:
Ͻhyérɛn wͻ anafua ber m’,
Ewufo twa m’, ba W’ hͻ,
Ͻwo a ayɛ anapa kan;
O ewiei n’ mma mmpa hɛn!

MHB 642
1 . BER a adzesaa rotɔ mo nkwa da do,
Na ehum tu bea a ewia mmbɔ wɔ hɔ n'
Metse ndze ekyirekyir sum mu refrɛ
M'anan kɔ bea a minnyim.

MHB 642
2 . Sɛ biribiara rifi mo ho akɔ a, bɛn me,
Asaase, wi, fie ndzɛmba, sum na kan
Na enyimtsewee a ɔma me nkenyan,
Ɔdɔ a ɔgye mo do.

MHB 642
3 . Dza mowɔ nye Ɔwo Egya; ma Wo Sunsum
Nka mo ho nkyekye mo werɛ, nsuo mo mu;
Memmfata ahodze pa abow, memmfata berɛw,
Anaa sika abrɔn.

MHB 642
4 . Oye ma m', me papa na bɔn wɔnnkan;
Na ɔnam W'adom pii do ntsi edze kyɛ,
Na muhu Wo dɛ' roto nsa afrɛ me
Akɔ tsenabew a ɔsɛ m'.

MHB 642
5 . Ndwom dɛɛdɛw a asaasaa do wɔ hɔ a metse n',
Me bɛpɛ esua ndwom fofor krɔnkrɔn n' tow,
Na ewiei n' W'ayarsa ndua no ase no
M'benya nkwa a mo kɔn dɔ n'.   Amen.

MHB 643
1 . SƐ wiadze yi twa mu wie a ,
Sɛ ewia a ɔhyerɛn yi tɔ mu a,
Yɛnye Christ gyina enyimnyam m',
Mohwɛ ɔbra n'ewiei mu nsɛm a,
Dɛm ber n' ankasa na m'bohu
Kaw a medze W', Ewuradze.

MHB 643
2 . Sɛ mibegyina ahengua enyim
Hyɛ atar fɛɛfɛw a ɔnnyɛ m'dze,
Sɛ muhu W' dɛ mbrɛ Ɔwo tse a,
Medze akoma a bɔn nnyi m' bɔbɔ W',
Dɛm ber n' ankasa na m'bohu
Kaw a medze W', Ewuradze.

MHB 643
3 . Sɛ metse heaven ayɛyi
Ngyegyee dzendzen wɔ m'asomu,
Tse dɛ esu dzendzen n' dede,
Ne dɛw tse dɛ sanku ndze a,
Dɛm ber n' ankasa na m'bohu
Kaw a medze W', Ewuradze.

MHB 643
4 . Wɔammpaw m' wɔ me papa ntsi,
Wonyaan m', munguan mfi ebufuw m',
Dɛ munsuma me Gyefo nkyɛn,
Fa Sunsum no tsew mo ho,
Nyame, kyerɛ m' asaase 'i do,
Ma mo dɔ nkyerɛ kaw a medze W'.

MHB 644
1 . NKWA na 'wu Tsɛmbuafo,
W'atsɛmbu bea enyim
Enyigye krɔnn anaa afɔdzi mu,
Yebehyia m' ntsɛmara;
Woesiesie hɛn akra ama
Da kɛse a ɔtse dɛm n',
Fa ahwɛyie a ɔsɛ hyɛ ma,
Kenyan hɛn ma yɛnsɔr.

MHB 644
2 . Yɛbɔ mpaa dze tweɔn da n',
Dɔnhwer huuhu a wonnyim,
Ber a ehyɛ ahentar na tumdzi n',
Bɛsan efi sor aba ha,
Bɛkyebo, Egya Ne Ba n',
Bobu nyimpa nyina atsɛn,
Enye Egya n' No sor dɔm nyina
'Dze W'enyimnyam adom nyina.

MHB 644
3 . O ma wonhu hɛn dɛ
W'asɛm ho setsiefo,
Yɛnyɛ aso pɛnn mma abɛn no,
Na yɛrohwehwɛ hɛn Wura;
O ma yɛmper yennya
Dodow mfora esiarfo n',
Na yɛnweɔn ara dɛ yebenya
Ahomgye a onnyi ewiei.  Amen.

MHB 645
1 . EBUFUW da no a ɔyɛ hu n',
Ber a sor na asaase botwa m' no,
Bɔn no tum benya egyinaanan a?
Yebesi dɛn ehyia da huuhu n'?

MHB 645
2 . Ɔsor dze gyaramee wodow
Dɛ nwoma bi a wɔabobɔw,
Dede na nkekamu huuhu
Kenyan abɛn a onyan ewufo n'.

MHB 645
3 . O dɛm da n', dɛm enyiber da n',
Ber a yefi dɛtse m' kɔ atsɛmbu m' n,
O Christ yɛ abɔn kyirtaafo
Kaansa sor na asaase twa m' mpo a.  Amen.

MHB 646
1 . Ebufuw da! Ao, nyinsuwa da! 
Dza nkɔnhyɛfo kae n' abam',
Sor nye asaase rotɔ nso.

MHB 646
10 . Eku Woho ara ahwehwɛ m', 
Atɔ m' wɔ fona mbeamudua n' do;
Aso dɛm adom yi nyɛ gyan?

MHB 646
11 . Ɔtsɛmbuafo tseneenyi, 
Dom hɛn brafi ho bɔnfakyɛ,
Ansaana werdzi da n' aso.

MHB 646
12 . Midzii fᴐ; medze nyinsuwa gye
M'enyimguasebra nyina tom';
Nyame, meserɛ W', fa mo ho kyɛ m'.

MHB 646
13 . Egyee ɔbaa dzebɔnyɛnyi n', 
Edze wifo n' no bɔn kyɛɛ no,
Mo so ama menya enyidar.

MHB 646
14 . Me mpaabɔ na mo mbɔɔ nnsɛ  hwee,
Naaso, Nyame, kyerɛ W'adom
Na gye m' fi onnyiewiei gya n' mu.

MHB 646
15 . Ao, fa me ka Wo nguantsen n' ho, 
Mma mmpem m' adze nnka mberɛkyi n' ho,
Mbom ma m' do si W'abanyimfa.

MHB 646
16 . Mifi m'akoma mu bu ntwɛr, 
Hwɛ, mo nnuho ayɛ dɛ nso;
Sɛ m'ewiei to m' a, ɔno boa m'.

MHB 646
17 . Mewu o! Su na ewuotwa da n' a! 
Nyimpa fi huntumam' reba n' a,
Onsiesie noho mma atsɛmbu.

MHB 646
18 . Ao, Nyame, hu n' mbɔbɔr na gyaa n',
Tse ma hɔn a Jesus ehyira,
Dom hɛn W'ahomgye a onnyiewiei.
		Amen.

MHB 646
2 . Akomatu a ogura nyimpa, 
Ber a Tsɛmbuafo n' fi sor besian,
Ɔno a ɔka a, obi nnka bi.

MHB 646
3 . Totorobɛnto ndze huhu, 
Ɔgyegye ndakamaa nyinam'
Rotwe dɔm nyina kɔ asɛndzii.

MHB 646
4 . Wɔatsea Wu, wiadze rowosow, 
Abɔdze nyina rinyanyan,
Eyi ano akyerɛ Tsɛmbuafo n'.

MHB 646
5 . Hwɛ, bukuu no mu nsɛm si pi, 
Wɔ dza wɔakyerɛw n' mu nyina ho,
Ɔno na wɔdze bobu atsɛn.

MHB 646
6 . Sɛ Tsɛmbuafo n' tsena N'eguam' 
Na esumasɛm biara da edzi a,
Obiara nnkɛfa noho gyan.

MHB 646
7 . Emidze m'beyi m'ano dɛn? 
Woana no obotwitwa agye m'
Ber a anokwafo mpo hia adom?

MHB 646
8 . Hen a W'ahentum krɔn mbordo, 
Ɔwo a ebɔ werdam ma hɛn, 
Tsema Wura, pinkyɛn hɛn ɛ.

MHB 646
9 . Hwɛ Jesus pa, mo nkwangye ntsi 
Na ebɛbraa adasa mu;
Mma nnto me seraha mma bɔn.

MHB 647
1 . Ewuradze, ɔnnyɛ 'mi m'asɛm 
Muwu anaa metse ase o;
M'afamudze nye m'bɔdɔ W', masom W'
Yi gyedɛ W'adom ma.

MHB 647
2 . Sɛ nkwa war a, m' enyi bɛgye 
Ama maasom Wo akyɛr,
Tsia so a, bɛn ntsi na m'bedzi mbɔɔ
Dɛ m'botu akɔ onnyiewieim'?

MHB 647
3 . Christ ɔmmfa m' ndua mbrɛ hɔ yɛ sum 
Sen mbrɛ Noara koduae n';
Nyia ɔba Nyame ahenman mu n'
Gyedɛ ɔfa abow yim'.

MHB 647
4 . Bra, Mo Wura, sɛ adom ma mesɛ 
Dɛ muhu W'enyim a;
Na W'asaase edwuma yɛ dɛw a,
W'enyimnyam bɛyɛ dɛ dɛn?

MHB 647
5 . Na m'botwa mo suhuhun do, 
Na fona na bɔn ndafua,
Makɔdɔm esiarfo a wɔtow
Jehovah N'ayɛyi.

MHB 647
6 . Me nyimdzee wɔ hɔ bra n' ho suar, 
Gyedzi enyi yɛ kusuww;
Na ɔdɔɔ so dɛ Christ nyim Ne nyina,
Na menya N' bɛkɛtsena.

MHB 648
1 . YI hɛn awerɛhow na hu akwa!
Ɔnnkɛkyɛr na yeenya hɛn fie n',
Ahotsewfo man no bɛba,
Onnyiewiei da no so bɛba;
Yebefi asaase yi do ntsɛm,
Na yeetu akɔ hɛn ndamfo do,
Hɛn Egya fie a ɔwɔ sor hɔ;
Abɔfo na Nyame ahemfie.

MHB 648
2 . Hɛn suhuhun nyina ano botwa,
Sɛ n-kwasɛm no kenyan hɛn a,
Yehu kurow fofor n' no mpuei dɛ
Ayefor a wɔahyehyɛ ama n' Wura;
Kuropɔn krɔnkrɔn a no mu tsew yie,
Awerɛhow biara nnyi hɔ koraa 
Na atseetse anaa bɔn nnyi hɔ,
Sunsum fi biara so nnyi hɔ.

MHB 648
3 . Yɛnam hɛn gyedzi do ehu
Jerusalem enyigyebea;
N'afasu yɛ jasper na sika,
N'adan ne hyerɛn ma noho tsew;
Adom n' mma ne fapem nnhinhim,
Osi hɔ dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse a ahyɛse n',
Ne dansifo no da no edzi n',
Nyame N'enyimnyam hyerɛn hɔ.

MHB 648
4 . Ewia ho nnkehia dɛm da no,
Osiandɛ 'nafuasum nnyi hɔ,
Bea a Jesus N'ahoɔfɛw hyerɛn n',
Kan mapa wɔ hɔ dabaa no,
Eguambaa n' nye hɔn kan na ewia,
Na hwɛ, kan mu na ɔma wɔnye
Jesus hyerɛn krɔnkrɔn mu,
Na wɔhyerɛn wɔ sor 'nyimnyam mu.

MHB 649
1 . Man bi wɔ hɔ a dɛw mapa wɔm', 
Ahotsewfo dzim' hen;
Adzekyee nko, adze nnsa da,
Hɔ enyigye tu yaw.

MHB 649
2 . Hɔ na nhaban wuna dabaa. 
Na hɔ nhiren nnyam da;
Wu tse dɛ po tseabaa a, otwa
Sorman na hɛndze yi ntamu.

MHB 649
3 . Nhaban huanhuam wɔ esuegya hɔ 
Woewuna dukuduku;
Dɛm na Jewfo hun Canaan ma n'
Dɛ Jordan pem twa ntamu.

MHB 649
4 . Na adasa suro bɔ piriw dɛ 
Wobotwa po tseabaa n',
Wɔbɔ ngyangyan wɔ esukɔn do,
Wosuro dɛ wobepia.

MHB 649
5 . Ao, nkyɛ yeeyi ekyingye akwa, 
Na adwen kusukusu n',
Na yɛdze enyi a do tsew eehu
Canaan a yɛdɔ no.

MHB 649
6 . Nkyɛ yaafow mbrɛ Moses kegyinae n', 
Na yaankwɛ noho mbew n',
Jordan esu anaa owu nwin,
Runntu hɛn bo wɔ hɔ.

MHB 65
1 . NYAME a ofir Nyame, ifua
Onyame dɔ no krɔn, no bun, 
Yɛdze ndaase akoma tow W' ndwom, 
Hɛn akoma haahaw hwehwɛ Wo,
Dɛ ogya a ɔredzɛw dzendzen;
Bra, fa Wo ngo krɔnkrɔn no bra.

MHB 65
2 . Ɔdɔ Tumfo, yɛkotow Wo, 
Hɛn ahwehwɛdze nyina nye Wo, 
Hɛn akoma da W'enyim adagyaw, 
Igyaa Wo daa ahengua no hɔ; 
Too W'enyimnyam pan wɔ ase ha. 
Penee, kyii bɔgya, wui maa hɛn.

MHB 65
3 . Yɛserɛ adom wɔ asorɛkye mu.
Adom nye ɔkra ne sekyɛ,
Adom na ɔsa yar nyina,
Adom brɛ apɛdze nyina adze,
Sɛ wiadze tsew etua mpo a,
Ɔma hɛn abotar yaw mu.

MHB 65
4 . Ma sor nyɛ hɛn kra tsenabea ndɛ,
Yɛnka Christ ho nsuma Nyame m',
Hɛn sunsum nye Nyame dze mbɔ m',
Yɛnyɛ hɛn edwuma nyina Wo mu,
Hɛn nsusui nyina ngyina Wo do,
Kesi dɛ Wo su hyerɛn hɛn mu.

MHB 650
1 . Jerusalem, m'ahomka fie, 
Dzin a ɔsom me bo,
M'edwuma bɔbɔ adze dabɛn
Wɔ wo siar asomdweem'?

MHB 650
2 . Dabɛn na m'enyiwa bohu 
W'afasu nye mbotsen?
N-kwagye ahyɛ w'aban dzen,
W'abrɔn mu hyerɛn sika.

MHB 650
3 . Ehɔ nhyiren n' kyɛn Eden turem'; 
Na bɔn nye yaw nnyi hɔ:
Menam abo nye ehum do
Per kɔ siar bea yi do.

MHB 650
4 . Ebɛn ntsi na m'bosuro mbusu, 
Anaa wu mbɔ me hu?
M'enyi da Canaan man pa n' do,
Mbew a adze nnsa do da.

MHB 650
5 . Asomafo, atɔfo, nkɔnhyɛfo, 
Abɔ Agyenkwa ho aprɔw;
Na ɔnnkɛkyɛr so na m'adɔfo
Akɔdɔm 'nyimnyam kuw n'.

MHB 650
6 . Jerusalem, mahomka fie, 
Me kra per hwehwɛ wo!
Da n' na m'dwuma bɔbɔ adze,
Da n' na m'bohu wo dɛw.

MHB 651
1 . TSIE! Me kra, tsie! Sor abɔfo ndwom ruhur
Wɔ kwaamu ɔnye mpoano nyinara;
Nokwar bi a dɛm ndwom no rowasa a,
Wɔ nkwa fofor a bɔn biara nnyi mu bio!
   Jesus abɔfo, kan abɔfo,
   Rotow ndwom ama akwantufo akɔaba!

MHB 651
2 . Yɛkɔ hɛn enyim, yɛda ho tse hɔn ndwom no,
Akra a hom aberɛ, Jesus frɛ dɛ hom mbra!
Ndwom no gyegye dɛɛdɛw wɔ hɔ sum no mu,
Asɛmpa ndwom no dze hɛn rokɔ fie.

MHB 651
3 . Jesus Ne ndze gyegye asaase na po do,
Dɛ ewimbir dɔn a wɔrobɔ n' ekyirekyir,
Akra mpempen a wɔso adzesoa aberɛ;
Oguanhwɛfo pa, frɛ hɔn bra Wo nkyɛn.

MHB 651
4 . Ahomgye ba; sɛ ɔbra war, yɛ basaa mpo a,
Adzekyee n' twar dɛ ɔba ma sum pa;
Gyedzi akwantu bɔ adze wɔ akɔaba-ma mu,
Na ɔkra n' nsa ka heaven, ne fie mapa n'.

MHB 651
5 . Abɔfo, hom ntow ndwom, ber a hom roweɔn yi,
Hom ntow sor ndwom dɛɛdɛw no nkyerɛ hɛn,
Kɛpem dɛ anapa dɛw bɛpam anafua su,
Na ɔbra mu sum no pa ɔdɔ mu.

MHB 652
1 . Hɛn nkwaber yɛ tsia wɔ ha 
Yaw tsia, adwendwen tsia
Nkwa a ɔmmbɔ adze da,
Nyinsu nnyim' wɔ noho,
Ao, ndzinoa a ɔyɛ dɛw
Fona tsia, ahomgye daa;
Adasa ndzebɔnyɛ
Nye esiarfo bɛtsena.

MHB 652
2 . Akobɔfo abɔbɔfo a, 
Yebenya fi wɔ sor!
Nsaamaa a yɛrohwehwɛ kobew
Wɔ nworaba n'ekyir!
Ndɛ dze yɛwɔ akono,
'Kyena na yɛso ahenkyɛw
A, odzi mu afebɔɔ
Na ne fɛw mmpa ara da.

MHB 652
3 . Sesei dze yɛroweɔn, yɛreper, 
Yɛtse enyidadom',
Zion wɔ dɛ n'ahoguam'
Ɔnye Babylon si;
Na nyia sesei yɛtwer No n'
Ndaamba yebohu N' kann,
Hɔn a wonyim N' na Wohu N'
Benya N' ayɛ hɔndze.

MHB 652
4 . Ao, enyigye na siar man, 
Nyame Ne mpamufo fie!
Ao, enyigye na siar man,
Akoma kɔn dɔ W', hwɛ W' kwan!
Jesu, mbɔbɔrhum' ara
Fa hɛn kɔ ahomgye bea n',
Ɔwo a 'nye Nyame Egya
Na Sunsum n' woehyira hom.

MHB 652
5 . Jerusalem sika kurow, 
Numfonsu na wo ma
Wo ho adwendwen no ma
Akoma na ndze bɔm
Minnyim ara, ao, minyim
Dɛw a ɔrotweɔn hɛn hɔ,
Enyimnyam a ɔhyerɛn
Nhyira a ɔnntɔ ka.

MHB 652
6 . Zion asa n' nyina mu 
'Nyigye ndwom ahyɛ n' ma,
Abɔfo hyirenn na atɔfo
Ahyɛ mpemdo wɔ hɔ,
Ɔhenba n' tse hɔn finimfin
Adzekyee kan n' tsew wann;
Na esiarfo edzidzibea n'
Ayɛ nomanoma fɛɛfɛw.

MHB 652
7 . David n'ahenguan n' si hɔ; 
Hɔ na konyimdzifo a
Woefi dadwen nsa bɔ se,
Na apontofo tow ndwom
Hɔn a wɔnye hɔn Sahen
Ako edzi konyim n'
Mbersantsen mfesantsen nyina
Woewuna hɔn ntar fitaa.

MHB 652
8 . Nyimpa, per nya enyimnyam n'; 
Ku wo ntsin nya kan no;
Ma enyidar ndzi kan nkosuom'
Kyerɛ ɔyew W'enyi do,
Dzi dɛw, ao, dɛtse na nso,
Nyame bɛyɛ wodze;
Nedze nye w', No nko Nedze
Na 'bɛyɛ afebɔɔ.

MHB 653
1 . BEA a hɔ yɛ dɛw nko!
Nyame a ɔwɔ sor abangua,
Ɔsor mu sor ahengua,
W'ahentum no dzi mu.
    Enyigye bea! O dabɛn na
    M'bohu me Nyankopɔn enyim?

MHB 653
2 . Mo Wura, me Hen tse hɔ,
Memmfata hɔ tsena,
Hɔ, abɔfo tow ndwom
Butuw famu, kotow No.

MHB 653
3 . Tsetse mpanyimfo no
Kowiee hɔn akwantu n' hɔ;
Nkɔnhyɛfo no hun hɛn
Asomdwee Hen enyim.

MHB 653
4 . Medze enyigye bohu
Eguambaa N'asomafo,
M'betsie nsankubɔfo n'
Wɔ sika nsanku do.

MHB 653
5 . Atɔfo anokwafo n'
Wɔ abangua no do,
Wɔhyɛ n-tar fitaa
'Nyimnyam hyɛ hɔn etua ma.

MHB 653
6 . Ɔsor Jerusalem
Nye mo ndwom na mo kurow;
Na mo wu ekyir no,
Mibenya me nhyira.

MHB 654
1 . ƆSOR fie! Ɔsor fie!
Adehye-mba hɔn fie;
Adzesaa so nnyi ɔsor fie,
Mbom anapa a ɔmmpa a;
M'enyi akɛda ɔsor fie,
M'akoma dzi yaw wɔ ha;
Wonndzi yaw biara wɔ hɔ,
Merebɛn ho kakra.

MHB 654
2 . M'Ewuradze wɔ ɔsor fie,
'Nye N'abɔfoe wɔ hɔ;
Na bɔn bi nnyi ɔsor fie
Na nsɔhwɛ so nnyi hɔ;
Ndze bi a ofi sor fie
Rowosow m'asowa mu;
Na sɛ modwen ɔsor fie ho a,
Nyinsu hyɛ m'enyiwa ma.

MHB 654
3 . Hɔn a modɔ hɔn wɔ sor fie
Refrɛfrɛ me akɔ hɔ;
Ahomgye na asomdwee wɔ sor fie,
Na bra a ɔnnsɛɛ ara da;
Na owu bi nnyi sor fie hɔ,
Awerɛhow so nnyi hɔ;
Christ nye hɛn nkɔ ɔsor fie
Wɔ dɔ a onnyi ewiei mu.  Amen.

MHB 655
1 . JERUSALEM, m'ahomka fie!
M'bɛba wo hɔ dabɛn?
M'awerɛhow bɔbɔ adze dabɛn?
Dabɛn na m'bohu

MHB 655
10 . Magdalene egyaa n'apensi
Na ɔtow ndwom dɛw, m' wɔ hɔ,
Ɔnye ahotsewfo a hɔn ndwom
Yɛ dukuu wɔ abrɔn mu n'.

MHB 655
11 . Jerusalem, Jerusalem,
Nyame mboa ma munhu
Wo dɛw a ɔmmbɔ adze n', na menyɛ
Ne fafafo so daa.    Amen.

MHB 655
2 . Ahotsewfo ahomka mpoano!
O dɛw na ahotɔ bea!
Wo mu dze awerɛhow nnyi hɔ,
Yaw, dadwen na berɛ nnyi m'.

MHB 655
3 . W'afasu yɛ sika abotan,
W'aban yɛ ndɛnkyɛmbo;
Wo mbotsen yɛ man pa m' ndzepa,
Ahodze a ho yɛ na.

MHB 655
4 . W'adan no srɔnsrɔmbea biara
Kandzea hyɛnhyɛnn hyerɛn do;
W'abɔntsen yɛ sika mfutuw,
Ɔyɛ fɛw, odzi mu.

MHB 655
5 . Wo w'enyinaba na nduaba kwa
Yɛ ahomka dodow;
Ndua na nduaba pa ahyɛ mu ma,
Ɔyɛ nwanwa dodow.

MHB 655
6 . Wo turo ahorow na mfuwa
Yɛ ebunebun daa;
Nhyiren huanhuam fɛɛfɛw wɔ hɔ,
Hɔn saso nnyi beebi.

MHB 655
7 . W'abrɔn a dwetɛ gyegye mu n',
N-kwa esutsen pem m' weɔɔ;
Ne nkyɛnkyɛn, afa na afa nyina,
N-kwa dua wuna wusuww.

MHB 655
8 . W'ahotsewfo hyɛ 'nyam 'henkyɛw,
'Hu Nyame enyim na enyim;
Wodzi nyim ara, wodzi dɛw ara,
Wɔwɔ ahomka m' daa.

MHB 655
9 . David dze ne sanku m' wɔ hɔ
Dɛ adwontow kuw panyin;
Nyia ɔbɛtse hɔn ndwom no bi n'
Woehyira n' mbɔho piigyan.

MHB 656
1 . MBOFRA mpempem etwa ehyia
Nyame N'ahengua enyim,
Mbofra a wɔahor hɔn ho bɔn nyina,
Ahotsewfo fɛkuw.
     Wɔtow : 'Nyimnyam
     'nyimnyam, 'nyimnyam!

MHB 656
2 . Hwɛ wɔhyɛ ntar pa fitaa bi a
Nkekaa biara nnyi mu,
Wɔtse daa daa kan na dɛw a
Ɔmmpa ara da mu.

MHB 656
3 . Mframa bɛn bɔɔ hɔn kɔr sor hɔ?
Sor a pɛrpɛr tsim hɔ daa,
Bea a asomdwee, dɛw na dɔ nsu pem;
Mbofra 'i sii dɛn kɔr hɔ.

MHB 656
4 . Agyenkwa N' bɔgyaa a okyii no
Hohoor hɔn ho fi no:
Woguar adehye nsu krɔnn no mu;
Hwɛ, hɔn ho atsew fitaa!

MHB 656
5 . Wɔtse ase n', wɔhwehwɛɛ Agyenkwa
N'adom, wɔdɔɔ Ne dzin,
Ntsi na ndɛ wohu N' siar enyim n',
Na wogyina Eguambaa enyim n'.

MHB 657
1 . Hɔn a wu ntwamutam suma hɔn n', 
Hɛn 'gyafo a nkyɛ wɔka hɛn ho n',
Woedu sor adzekyee mu ntsi
Yɛda W' ase.

MHB 657
2 . Hɔn nkwa no yɛ n-kwa ampa, 
Woedu empiresi n'ewiei,
Afei wohu W'enyim petee:
Hwee nnsiw hɔn kwan.

MHB 657
3 . Dɛ mbrɛ yehun hɔn wɔ fonam' 
Na ahohia mu n', wɔnntse dɛm bio:
Hɔn enyi hu adze kann: Wo dzin
Wɔ hɔn pɔw do.

MHB 657
4 . Kɔdaann-da efi hɔn do koraa, 
Na woehu W'apɛdze nyina;
Wɔdze dɛw a yennyim wɔ ha 
Som Wo daa daa.

MHB 657
5 . O nkwa a ɔahyɛ hɔn amaama a! 
Sor mframa a wɔgye n' yɛ dɛw;
Enyigye n' bor hɛn adwen do;
Onnyi kabea.

MHB 657
6 . Edwuma so a seesei wɔyɛ n', 
Dza ɔsɛ nyimdzee a oedzi mu a,
Na dza ema wɔyɛ ma hɛn
Yenntum yennhu.

MHB 657
7 . Wonnkyi nyinsuwa hɔ ara bio, 
Dɔ nko na wɔdze edzi ehyia;
Sor hɔ dwuma, nkamfo, ahomgye
Nyina yɛ kor.

MHB 658
1 . EWURADZE Wo nkyɛn ara!
Amen; ma ɔnyɛ hɔ;
'Wu mu nkwa wɔ dɛm asɛm no m'
Yɛ bɛkyebo nkwa pa;
Metse honam mu yi,
Mikyima fi Ne nkyɛn,
Anago biara misi me
Ntamadan bɛn Ne fie.

MHB 658
2 . M'Egya fie a ɔwɔ sor,
Me kra fie a ɔbɛn,
Ma gyedzi enyiwa pa nhu
Wo sika mbobow no!
Afei me kra reper
Dɛ obodu man a modɔ n',
'Hotsewfo egyapadze a ɔhyerɛn,
Ɔsor Jerusalem.

MHB 658
3 . Ewuradze, Wo nkyɛn ara!
Egya, ɔyɛ Wo pɛ a,
Ma me nsa nka anohoba n',
Asɛm no mu dze no.
Gyina me nsa nyimfa
Na monnkɔhwe ase;
Suo mo mu na mibegyina
Ko m' na m'bedzi konyim.

MHB 658
4 . Sɛ m'ahomgu bɔ adze a,
Tsew nkataenyim no mu a,
Menam owu mu benya nkwa,
N-kwa a onnyi ewiei.
Dɛ mbrɛ metse 'i ara,
M'bɛyɛ dɛn adɔ asɛm n'
Na daa maka n' ahengua enyim?
Ewuradze, Wo nkyɛn ara!

MHB 659
1 . AHOMGYE na enyigye da,
O dɛw na ekan da,
Dadwen na awerɛhow edur,
Ɔyɛ fɛw na ɔhyerɛn;
Wo mu, akɛse na nkuma
Bɔ m' mfesantsen nyina
Tow: Krɔnkrɔn, Krɔnkrɔn, Krɔnkrɔn
Ma Ɔkorsa Nyame.

MHB 659
2 . Wo mu na abɔdze mu no,
Wodzii kan yɛɛ ekan;
Wo mu na hɛn nkeagye ntsi
Christ soɛree fii nda mu;
Wo mu, hɛn konyimdzi Wura
Somaa Sunsum n' fii sor,
N-tsi nyimnyamfo, Wo mu
Na emaa kan mprɛnsa.

MHB 659
3 . N-dɛ sor manna tɔ wɔ
Aman a wɔaberɛ do;
Dwetɛ totorobɛnto no
Frɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn n' wɔ 
Beebi a asɛmpa kan no 
Da kan ne nserɛmɛn edzi,
Na nkwa nsu pem wɔ hɔ dɛ
N-su a ɔdwedwe akra.

MHB 659
4 . Yenya adom fofor daa
Fi ahomgye da yi mu,
Hɛn nsa ka ahomgye a ɔyɛ 
Akra a woehyira hɔn n' dze;
Ayɛyi nka Egya, Ɔba
Nye Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn no;
Asɔr no ma ne ndze do
Ma Ɔwo, Baasa Kor.  Amen.

MHB 66
1 . ADOM nyina Nyame,
Yɛkamfo W'adɔe,
Edze Wo Ba ama dɛ ombowu mma hɛn.
Ofi ɔsor bae,
Ribeyi hɛn ndom;
Ɔadɔ, ɔadɔ hɛn osiandɛ ɔpɛ ɔdɔ.

MHB 66
2 . Ɔdɔ gyaa N' ma owui,
Hɛn enyi da 'yi do,
 Ɔadɔ, ɔadɔ hɛn, yennkotum atse ase,
Yebotum aka 'yi,
 Ɔadɔ hɛn kɛse,
Dɛ ɔdze No nkwa too hɔ gyee hɛn fii hɛll.

MHB 66
3 . Ɔagye hɛn asefo;
Yensi dɛn nkamfo
Anaa yɛntow W'adom a onnyi kabea ho ndwom?
Yennkohu hweeara
Wɔ ha akwantu yi m',
Mbom yɛtow W'adom ho ndwom kɔ paradisè.

MHB 66
4 . Na sɛ yefi ha
Pue W'enyim wɔ sor,
Hɛn sor bɛyɛ Wo dɔ ho ndwom ara nko,
Hɛn nyina bɛkamfo,
Hɛn Nyɛnko No dɔ,
Dza wɔhyɛ ase no rommbɔ adze da.

MHB 660
1 . N-dɛ yɛ ekan da; 
Nyame, ma kan mbra ndɛ;
Hɛn Anapawi, hyerɛn hɛn do,
Na pam hɛn sum nyina.

MHB 660
2 . N-dɛ yɛ ahomgye da; 
Hyɛ hɛn ahoɔdzen mu;
Hue Wo bɔw nwinwin no ma hɛn,
Dwedwe 'koma a ɔahaw,

MHB 660
3 . N-dɛ yɛ asomdwee da; 
Fa W'asomdwee ma hɛn;
Ma mansotwe nyina mbɔ adze 
Ma wongyaa n-tokwaa.

MHB 660
4 . N-dɛ yɛ mpaabɔ da: 
Ma asaase mpinkyɛn sor;
Ma hɛn akoma nhwehwɛ Wo,
Bra behyia hɛn wɔ ha

MHB 660
5 . N-dɛ yɛ mpaabɔ da: 
Bɔ mfar a ɔma nkwa;
Na nyan akra a woewuwu ma
Wɔndɔ Wo, wɔnsom Wo

MHB 661
1 . HOM mbra ma yɛnye hɛn Wura nsoɛr,
Hɛn wura a ͻyɛɛ asaase na wimu;
Owui gyee wiadzé a ͻbͻe no
Na ͻsoɛɛr konyim mu fii wu m’,
N-kwa nyé asomdwee Hen scarce
Na ͻdze da no yɛɛ Nedze daa.

MHB 661
2 . Iyi nye da a Ewuradzé ayɛ
Ma obiara eehu No dͻ no,
Atse No wusoɛr tum no nka
Na ͻaasoɛr a ͻnnhwé ase bio;
Wͻayɛ N' fofor wͻ tsenenee mu,
Na Nyame nkwa ahyɛ no ma.

MHB 661
3 . Hom mma yɛmfa Nedze mma No,
Yɛmfa mpaabͻ mbɛn ahengua n’
Mfa ahobrɛadze ntsie asɛmpa n’,
Mfa ndaase mma ͻdͻ a ͻdze wui n’;
Yɛma hɛn akoma na ndze do
Dzé ayɛyi ndwom kͻ abangua n' do.

MHB 661
4 . ’Nyidzi na ayɛyi nka Jesus,
Ne da krͻnkrͻn yi mu nyina;
Obia’a ntow Jesus N'ayɛyi;
Mma wonngyaa ber kakraabi mpo,
Ma iyi nkͻ do ber nyina;
Hom nka N'ayɛyi na dͻ nko.    Amen.

MHB 662
1 . EWIA ekyir nsutɔ yɛ dɛw,
Na yaw ekyir n-da yɛ dɛw;
Ahomgye da dze ahom dɛɛdɛw
Ba wiadze a ɔaberɛ do.

MHB 662
2 . Sor 'sɛnkyerɛdze, asaase asomdwee,
Hianyi kyɛfa, na akyenkyendur;
Nyame dase, sor ndzɛmba ho;
Ewia wɔ ayarsa wɔ no mu.

MHB 662
3 . Nkyenan fofor wɔ asɛmpa 'i mu
Na ne kan m-pɛn esuon mu,
Nyame nhyira da! Yehua ne kan,
Ɔdze ndaase na ɔsom ba.

MHB 662
4 . Kusuww nye ahantan biara
Nnkotum nye ber krɔnkrɔn atsena;
Yɛyɛ Nyame edwuma ɔdɔ mu,
Yɛyew edwuma no dɛw mu.

MHB 662
5 . Ewuradze, hom gu hɛn do
Ma yengyina pintsinn wɔ dɔ mu,
Na ma hɛn hɛn ehiadze daa
Ma yɛntsena gyedzi mu nwu.

MHB 663
1 . KAN a ofir kan, bue m'enyi,
Afei adze rekye fofor;
Adom Ewia, pam sum no;
Ma m'Ahomgye da anapa nhyerɛn
W'enyigye nhyira ewia n',
M'ahomgye da yɛ enyika.

MHB 663
2 . Hɛn dɛw na asomdeee bura,
Gya me kɔ Wo nkwa esu ho;
Ɔwo gye m' kra fi wiadze;
Fa adom na mbɔbɔrhu nyɛn 
Hyira W'asɛm do ma ɔnsow
Aba bafuu nkyerɛ Wo dɔ.

MHB 663
3 . Sɔ W'afɔr no a ɔda
M'anomu no mu ogya no;
Yi m'enyi do sum fi hɔ
Ma meegyaa mfomdo biara yɛ,
Mma ogya fofor bi nndzɛw
Mo mu a W'afɔrmbukyia nnyim.

MHB 663
4 . Ma memfa m'akoma ntow
Krɔnkrɔn, Krɔnkrɔn, Krɔnkrɔn n-dɛ
Ntwe m'ho mfi wiadze kakra;
Na me kra ntow mbra Wo hɔ sor
M'bɔsɔ mbrɛ wosi som Wo
Wɔ sor tsenabea hɔ no nhwɛ

MHB 663
5 . Hom mo mu, mowɔ Wo mu,
Hyehyɛ paradise wɔ mo mu;
O yi Woho kyerɛ me,
Ɔdɔ siarfo a iwui gyee me,
Wo toa mu ngo a ɔnnsa da n'
Bɛma me kandzea adzɛw daa.

MHB 663
6 . Dadwen nye egyangyandze nyina
Nyɛ da no krɔnkrɔn mma Nyame;
Bra, Otumfo nyimyamfo,
Na bɛhyɛ asɔrdan yi ma;
Me kra nnkehinhim n-dɛ,
M'bɔhom Wo dɔ mu ara nko.

MHB 664
1 . O EWURADZE Jesus, ber a
Yɛtwe bɛn Wo n' yɛ nhyira,
Yɛtse anohoba dɛɛdɛw pii a
Ɔsom bo fi W'anomu.

MHB 664
2 . Ka hɛn ho ndɛ na hyira hɛn,
Amma yaannyɛ gyan wɔ mu;
Ma yenhu nkwagye nokwar no,
Abrabɔ mu n-sɛm no.

MHB 664
3 . Bue hɛn adwen na mu na gya hɛn.
Sɔkyee kɔ hɛn sor kwan do;
Nokwar kandzea no ndzi hɛn kan
Na amma yaanntɔ dɔnsuar.

MHB 664
4 . Ma hɛn ɔdwe na ahobrɛadze,
Eso yɛnyɛ dza ɔtsen;
Pam isum amma yeemmfintsiw;
Nyimpa nantsew sɔnn kan mu.

MHB 664
5 . Ma hɛn ɔdwe na ahobrɛadze,
Eso yɛnyɛ dza ɔtsen;
Pam isum amma yeemmfintsiw;
Nyimpa nantsew sɔnn kan mu.

MHB 664
6 . Ma hɛn adom ma yɛngye dase
Wɔ nokwar a yeesuo m' no ho;
Na ma binom so n-sɔ nhwɛ,
Ne dɛw nye ne kan pa no.

MHB 665
1 . ME NYAME, me Hen, W'ayɛyi
Ndaase, adwontow ho edwuma yɛ dɛw;
Wɔkyerɛ Wo dɔ anapa kan,
Wɔka Wo nokwar anafua.

MHB 665
2 . Ahomgye da krɔnkrɔn yɛ dɛw,
Adwendwen biara nnhaw mo bo;
O ma m'akoma ntow ndwom dɛ
David sankutsen dɛɛdɛw no.

MHB 665
3 . M'akoma dzi nyim Ewuradze m'
Na oehyira No ndwuma nye N'asɛm;
Mbrɛ W'adom ndwuma si hyerɛn a!
W'afotu mu dɔ, no ho tsew.

MHB 665
4 . Na m'benya enyimnyam kyefa
Ber a adom atsew m'akoma ho,
Na menya enyigye fofor,
Dɛ ngo krɔnkrɔn asera me tsirmu.

MHB 665
5 . Afei mobohu na matse
Dza mohwehwɛ wɔ ha nyina,
Na abɔdze nyina benya enyigye
Wɔ dɛw bɛkyebo wiadze n' mu.

MHB 666
1 . Yɛdze adwontow hyɛɛ ase ndɛ, 
Wɔ mbɔbɔr ahengua n' enyim;
Ansaana 'nafua sum bɛba n',
Yɛtow ewimbir ndaase ndwom.

MHB 666
2 . Dza ofir nokwar akomam', 
Enyidzi suro a wɔdze hwɛ W',
Sua a yesua, n-tam a yɛka,
Hɛn Wura Jesus, pen do gye.

MHB 666
3 . Dza W'enyi ehwiram' ehu 
Dɛ ogu hɛn afɔr ho fi n',
Yɛakotow komm wɔ W'enyim yi,
Hɛn Wura Jesus, fa kyɛ hɛn.

MHB 666
4 . Kyerɛ hɛn ma yɛngye akra nkwa, 
Na yɛnkata bɔn mpempem do,
Yensi Christ Ne penkyɛr kwan n' mu,
Na yensuasua N' yɛnye N' nsɛ daa. Amen.

MHB 667
1 . Hɛn Wura, da a 'dze kyɛɛ hɛn n' asa, 
Sum etsin W'asɛm do rehyɛ;
Yɛtoow hɛn anapa ndwom maa Wo
W'abɔdzin bɛtsew hen nda ho.

MHB 667
2 . Ndaase nka W' dɛ W' Asɔr risi pi, 
Ber a wiadze rokɔ kan mu;
W' Asɔr roweɔn wɔ wiadze nyina,
Ɔnngye n' ahom dabiara pɛn.

MHB 667
3 . Aber a 'napawi hyerɛn ka 
N-kurow a wɔda ham' na pom',
Asɔryɛ ndze ɔda ho ara,
Ayɛyindwom ɔmmbɔ adze da.

MHB 667
4 . Ewia rinyan hɛn enuanom a 
Wɔtse anee ber a yɛadeda;
Dɔnhwer nyina ano fofor ma
Wɔtse Wo nyɛe nwanwa n' wɔ sor.

MHB 667
5 . Ɔnyɛ dɛm daa, hɛn Wura; W'ahengua 
Nnkotwam' da dɛ amansuon tum;
W'ahenman betsim hɔ akɛpem dɛ
Ibedzi adze nyina do hen.

MHB 668
1 . Sor abɔfo ndze nye nsanku 
Twa W'ahengua ho,
Wɔwosow n-dwom dɛɛdɛw a
Ɔmmbɔ adze ara da;
M-pempem na wohyira Wo
Dɛ tum nyina 
Ewuradze.

MHB 668
2 . Ɔwo a ewɔ sorsor noho 
Mbrɛ nyimpa nntum nnhu n',
Aso abɔn yɛtow ndwom a,
Ɔwo 'bu no bi?
Na yetum hu dɛ ebɛn hɛn
Na itsie hɛn?
Nyew, yetum.

MHB 668
3 . Nyew, yenyim dɛ idzi ehurusi 
Wɔ W'edwinsa ho;
Eyɛɛ asowa na nsa na kɔmɛr
Dze maa W'ayɛyi;
Dwimfo nyansa, sanku ne dɛw,
Ne nyina bɔm' ma W'
Enyigye.

MHB 668
4 . Tumfo Nyame, Woara Wodze 
Na yɛdze brɛ Wo,
Ɔmmfata dze, naaso yɛserɛ
Dɛ gye n' dɛmara:
'Koma, adwen, nsa, na kɔmɛr,
Yɛdze bɔm' wɔ
Hɛn ndwom pam'.

MHB 668
5 . Tum nye enyidzi nye enyimnyam. 
Bɛyɛ Wodze daa,
Egya, Ba, na Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn,
Ɔkorsa siarfo.
Dza edze ama no mu mapa n',
Na sor na ase
San dze ma W'.    Amen.

MHB 669
1 . EWURADZE pa, adasa Egya,
Fa hɛn m-fom kyɛ hɛn;
Ma hɛn adwen a ɔfata
Wɔ abrabɔ krɔnkrɔn som mu,
Wɔ enyidzi ayɛyi mu.

MHB 669
2 . Yɛntwer Wo tse dɛ hɔn a wɔtsee
Wɔ Syrian epo ho n',
Ewuradze N'adom frɛ no;
Mma hɛn so yɛnnka asɛm biara,
Na yɛnsoɛr ndzi W'ekyir.

MHB 669
3 . O Galilee ahomgye da
O mbepɔw do kommyɛ,
Mbrɛ Jesus buu n-kotodwe!
Na ɔkaa onnyiewiei ho nsɛm,
Ɔdze ɔdɔ kyerɛɛ ase!

MHB 669
4 . Dɛ kommyɛ a no mu dɔ no
Bor hɛn nsɛm nye ndwuma do;
Wo frɛ a ɔwasa bɔkɔɔ no,
Dɛm na ma Wo nhyira no ngu
Dɛ Wo manna tɔe no.

MHB 669
5 . Ma Wo bɔsu nkɔ do nsosɔ
Nkɛpem hɛn aperdzi ewiei!
Yi hɛn akra adzesoa no,
Na hɛn bra a ahyehyɛ ama hɛn nka
W'asomdwee ne fɛw no.

MHB 669
6 . Gu ahom gu hɛn apɛdze do,
Wo kommyɛ eduyɛ mu,
Adwen ntaa dzinn, honam nyɛ komm;
'Saasewosow, ehum nye gya m'
Yɛntse Wo ndze tseaa no.

MHB 67
1 . EPO pa a no mu dɔ Nyame!
Woana nnkɛfa n'akoma ama W'?
Na ɔnnkɛfa n'ahoɔdzen adɔ W'?
O Jesus, adasa Dɔfo,
Woana nnkɛpɛ dɛ ɔdze ne kra,
N'adwen, n'ahoɔdzen bata W' ho?

MHB 67
2 . Wo hyerɛn no mmbɔ adze da
Wɔ gya a ɔnnhyehye enyim;
'Bɔfo dze ntsaban bua hɔn enyim. 
Naaso W'adɔe tse dɛ mframa,
Ɔbɔ fa Wo ndwuma nyina do,
Ɔhwetse ber a W'ewia pue.

MHB 67
3 . Imuna a, ahodwuruw ma
'Saase, hɛll na sor edum hinhim;
Tum a ɔyɛ hu yɛ Wodze,
Woana botum akyerɛ ɔdɔ a
Ɔtwe Wo bɛn emi dɛm yi,
Kesi dɛ ebɛyɛ medze?

MHB 67
4 . Ɔwo a idzi hen wɔ sorsor
Wɔ ndzɛmba na adze nyina do;
Edze dɛw hyɛ hɔn nyinara m',
Naaso 'pɛ dɛ eba me nkyɛn. 
Na gya m' taataa dɛ menye Wo
Bedzi hen dɛw mu afebɔɔ.

MHB 67
5 . Bura pa! Nhyira nyina pem
Fi Wo hɔ; W'amayɛ nnyim hia,
Ebɛnadze na Ɔwo hwehwɛ?
Naaso hweeara mpo nnhia Wo da;
M'akoma a ɔmmfata yi,
Iyi ara na ehwehwɛ.

MHB 67
6 . Tsetsentsetredee Ɔhoɔfɛfo!
Kan mba a hɔn ho yɛ fɛw, mbakan
Hu Wo a, hɔn 'nyimnyam hyerɛn pa:
W'enyi bɛyɛ dɛn aba mo do,
Ɔbaa ba a wonyinseen n' bɔn mu, 
Sunsuma, ahataw nye nwin?

MHB 67
7 . Sɛ ebɔ Wo tsir adze ara a,
Hɛll nsordaafo hɔn ho popo; 
Wonyim yie dɛ Nyame Tumfo
Nye asaase, hɛll na sor Hen:
Woana n'atar m'bɔgya nye yi?

MHB 67
8 . Nyame pa, epo a no mu dɔ!
Woana nnkɛfa n'akoma ama W'? 
Woana nnkɛfa no tum adɔ W'?
O Jesus, adasa Dɔfo,
Woana nnkɛfa ne kra adɔ W'?
N'adwen, 'hoɔdzen bata Wo ho.

MHB 670
1 . JESUS, hɛn enyigye nyina,
Ɔwo a yɛma hɛn ndze do ma W',
Yɛdze hɛn ahoɔdzen ma W',
Ma adom a yɛserɛ ahobrɛadze mu
N-dan nyɛ ndaase ara nko,
Na ɔnsesa Wo nkorɔfo.

MHB 670
2 . Yɛbɔ m' yɛ ɔsor edwuma yi,
W'enyimnyam no nyɛ hɛn botae;
W'enyimnyam, nnyɛ hɛndze,
Yɛnkɔ do n-hwɛ hɛn ewiei.
Yɛnkɔ do ndzi dwuma a ɔsɔ enyi,
Na aasɔ Nyame nko enyi.

MHB 670
3 . Mma ahantan, enyitsew bɔn
Nnwiawia hɔnho mmba mu mmbɛsɛɛ,
Mmbɛhyɛ Wo ebufuw;
Onngu hɛn adwontow ho fi,
Na wɔmma hɛn som no nnyɛ gyan,
Na wɔnnsɛɛ, hɛn afɔrbɔ.

MHB 670
4 . O ma hɛn nkwa nda nyinara
Yɛmfa kommyɛ dɛw a fɛr wɔ m'
Nda Wo dɔ no edzi;
Yɛmma hɛn konyim do wɔ wu m'!
Yɛnye ɔsor dɔm nyina ntow ndwom,
Ɔsor ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze n'.

MHB 671
1 . Hom ntow Alleluia nkyerɛ hom ndaase, 
Ao, ɔsor mba, hom mfa ndze dɛɛdɛw nhur
Alleluia a ɔmmbɔ adze.

MHB 671
2 . Kuro krɔnkrɔn no bɛgye hom ndwom no do, 
Na wɔdze ehurusi ndwom enyan
Alleluia a ɔmmbɔ adze.

MHB 671
3 . Hɔ na hom bɔbɔm' atow afebɔɔ, 
Ndwom a ɔkyerɛ hom Hen N'enyimnyam,
Alleluia a ɔmmbɔ adze.

MHB 671
4 . Iyi nye afonafo hɔn ahomgye, 
Edziban na nsu a obi nnkehia,
Alleluia a ɔmmbɔ adze.

MHB 671
5 . Bɔadze a eyɛ adze nyina Yɛfo, 
Yɛdze ndwom bɔ de yi W' ayɛ afebɔɔ
Alleluia a ɔmmbɔ adze.

MHB 671
6 . Ɔdomankoma Ba, yɛma hɛn ndze do ma W'; 
Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, hɛn nyina bɔm' tow Wo
Alleluia a ɔmmbɔ adze.

MHB 672
1 . GYEFO, Agyenkwa siarfo;
Tsie hɛn adwontow;
Hɛn akoma na ndze da m'
Yi hɛn Hen ayɛw,
Dza yɛwɔ ma W' biara,
Yɛwɔ enyidar dɛ
Nyimpadua, kra, sunsum,
Yɛdze ne nyina ma W'.

MHB 672
2 . Hɛn enyim ara na, Christ,
Yɛba dze bɛn Wo;
Yɛsɔr Wo enyidzi m',
Na yɛkotow Wo,
Osian hɛn nkwagye ntsi
Ɔwo 'bae bowui;
Edzi hɛn enyim kan
Wɔ sor dɛ yɛmfa W'.

MHB 672
3 . Ɔsor kandzea no pue
Hɛn enyim hyɛnn ara,
Ɔdze fakyɛ ho nsɛm
Pam hɛn awerɛhow;
Abrabɔ sum ahera,
Kan hyerɛn hɛn mu;
Edze Wo kan ahyerɛn
Hɛn bɔ wiadze 'i do.

MHB 672
4 . Yɛkɔ hɛn enyim ara
Wɔ hɛn akwantu n' mu,
Kwan a 'hotsewfo duaa m'
Dzii kan Nyame fie;
Yengyaa wiadze ekyir,
Yɛmpem nkɔ kan ara;
Yennkobu hɛn kɔn 'kyir,
Na yeenya ahenkyɛw n'.

MHB 672
5 . Gyefo, gya akra a apon hɛn
Ma yɛnkɔ sor ara;
Hɛn werɛ mfir wiadze fona,
Yɛmbɛn hɛn ahenman n',
Bea a 'hotsewfo, abɔfo,
Bɔ m' tow ndwom dɛw mu;
Wɔmmberɛ, wɔmmfona ara wɔ
Hɛn Hen N'ayɛyi m'.

MHB 673
1 . ESUSOW ewia robɔ 
Po nye asaase do;
Enyigye kan rehyerɛn
A wɔdze ma kwa.
Biribiara ridzi dɛw
Wɔ kan fɛɛfɛw mu;
Wiadze ndze mpempem nyina
Tow ayɛyi ndwom.

MHB 673
2 . Nyame No mbɔbɔrhu
Wɔ wiadze nyina,
Na Ne frankaa rihim
Wɔ mbea nyinara,
Ɔtserɛw, ɔyɛ enyimnyam,
Ɔtse dɛ ɔsor
Ne bɛkyebo dɔ no,
Ɔhyerɛn konyimdzi m'.

MHB 673
3 . Ewuradze, hue Wo kan
Gu hɛn enyifura do;
Osian W'ayamuyie ntsi
Ma yɛndɔ W' mbordo.
Na mununkum boa ano
Tumm wɔ sor mpo a,
Yi nkataenyim n' fi hɔ,
Egya, twe bɛn hɛn.

MHB 673
4 . Wo kan enyim siw mpo a,
Yɛnnkɛgye Wo kyim;
Ennka ho a ɔbra yɛ sum;
Wo mu owu mpo hyerɛn.
Kan mu Kan, hyerɛn hɛn do
Hɛn akwantu mu;
Kɔ do dzi hɛn enyim
Kɛpem da a onnyi ewiei.

MHB 674
1 . O NYAME Dɔ! Wo daa nserɛmɛn
Hyerɛn enyiwa a onnhu adze do,
Na ihyira hɛn wɔ adaaso m',
Yɛdan Wo gya a, Wo so gyaa hɛn.

MHB 674
2 . Akra a wɔper hwehwɛ W' nyina
Ikenyan akoma a ɔbɔ mpaa;
Sum mu o, kan mu o, Wo gyirama gya n'
Sisi ebusua nye aman do.

MHB 674
3 . Innyim ɔhe ɔnye gyedzi,
W'adom tsen du obiara do;
Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn n'atasaban no,
Gyina etsir nyinara do.

MHB 674
4 . Nokwar a nkɔnhyɛfo hunii no,
Wɔhwehwɛe, wohum wɔ hɔn mu;
Ɔdɔ mbra a ɔbor mbra nyina do,
Abrabɔ bunkam wu, bɔn do.

MHB 674
5 . Hyerɛn, Nyame Kan! Yi Woho edzi
Kyerɛ hɔn a wohu amandze nyina;
Ma ɔnkyɛn dza hɛn enyi da do n',
Fa Wo dɔ sɛɛ hɛn apɛdze.

MHB 675
1 . JESUS, bea a Wo nkorɔfo hyia nyina,
Wohu W'ehumbɔbɔr egua hɔ;
Bea a wɔhwehwɛ Wo, wohu Wo,
Na beebiara yɛ krɔnkrɔn bea.

MHB 675
2 . Ɔwo a wonntum nnsiw Wo kwan,
Etse ahobrɛadze akoma m';
Wɔdze Wo ba beebi a wɔba,
Wɔdze Wo kɔ hɔn efiefi.

MHB 675
3 . Hɔn a woeyi hɔn hɔn Hwɛfo pa,
Yɛ Wo kan mbɔrbɔrhu fofor,
Wo nkwagye dzin a ɔyɛ dɛw n',
Hɛn akoma paa mu ka wɔ ha.

MHB 675
4 . Yɛbɔsɔ mpaabɔ tum ahwɛ,
Ahyɛ gyedzi nye nhwɛdo dzen;
Akyerɛkyerɛ hɛn apɛdze a abotow
Ma yeehu dza ɔwɔ sor nyina.

MHB 675
5 . Owura, yesuar naaso Ɔwo bɛn,
Wo nsa nnyɛ tsia, W'aso nnsiwii;
O fi ɔsor bra famu ntsɛm,
Bɛfa akoma mpem yɛ Wodze.

MHB 676
1 . Hɛn Nyame yɛ Kɛse, 
N'ayɛyi nyɛ kɛse;
Ɔyɛ N'asɔrasɔr Ne fie,
N' egua a N'enyi gye mu.

MHB 676
2 . N'adom Asɔrfi horow, 
Mbrɛ wodua yɛ fɛw a!
Hɛn asaase do enyidzi,
Hɛn man twitwagyefo.

MHB 676
3 . Zion na wonyim dɛ 
Nyame yɛ guansumabew;
Mbrɛ No nkwagye esi ahyerɛn
Wɔ n'ahemfie nyina a.

MHB 676
4 . Ɔhaw fofor biaram'! 
Yɛbɛkɛhyɛ Ne fie;
Yɛbɔdwen N'adom nwanwa n' ho,
Na hɔ yɛanhwehwɛ ɔgye.

MHB 677
1 . Nyame, Yɛdɔ Wo Fie, 
Mbrɛ W'enyidzi wɔ no;
Wo tsenabea no mu dɛw
Kyɛn wiadze dɛw nyina.

MHB 677
2 . Ɔyɛ m-paabɔ fie, 
Mbrɛ Wo nkowaa dzi ehyia;
Na 'Wo, Ewuradze,
Eba behyira Wo mba.

MHB 677
3 . Yɛdɔ n-kwasɛm no; 
Ɔma hɛn asomdwee,
Nye dzenhyɛ wɔ ko mu,
Nye dɛw a ɔmmbɔ adze.

MHB 677
4 . Yɛdɔ dɛ yɛtow ndwom 
Kamfo Wo mbɔbɔrhu;
Na mbom yɛpɛ yeesua
Ɔsor konyimdzi ndwom.

MHB 677
5 . Hɛn Wura Jesus, dom hɛn 
Ma yɛndɔ Wo mbordo,
Na ndaamba yeebohu
Na yaasom Wo sor hɔ.    Amen.

MHB 678
1 . Sor wiadze horow Nyame, 
Mbrɛ Wo dɔ tsenabea
Na ase ha asɔrfi
Dua yɛ fɛw yɛ ahomka a!
M'akoma per
Ba Wo tsebea
Ama oeehu
Me Nyankopɔn.

MHB 678
2 . Ao, akra esiarfo na  
Wɔsɔr bea a Nyame tsie,
Ao, esiarfo nye hɔn 
A wɔsom wɔ hɔ daa!
Wɔtonton Wo,
Wɔyɛ esiarfo
Hɔn a wɔfow
Zion kokwaa n'!

MHB 678
3 . Wofi ahomm' kɔ ahom mu, 
Wɔ nyinsu bɔnsa yim',
Kɛpem dɛ obiara dzi nyim,
Kɛpem dɛ obiara pue sor,
'Nyimnyam egua!
Hɛn Hen Nyame
Dze hɛn pɛ anan
Dze bodu hɔ.

MHB 678
4 . Nyame nye hɛn 'kokyɛm, 
Hɛn kan na akoban;
Ne nsamu akyɛdze ma,
Yenya hɛn nhyira fir mu
Ɔbɔdom hɛn
Nkorɔfo nyina
Nkwagye adom,
Nye enyimnyam so.

MHB 678
5 . Nyame dɔ No nkorɔfo, 
Hɔn a wɔsɔ N'enyi n'
Akra krɔnkrɔn botoo n',
Ɔnnkan hɔn Ne ndzepa:
Nyia ne kra twer
Dɔm Ewuradze 
Wo nkotoo n', yɛ 
Siarfo mprɛnsa.

MHB 679
1 . Wo sor abangua yɛ fɛw, 
Wɔ kan na dɔ man no mu;
Ha so W'abangua yɛ fɛw,
Wɔ bɔn na mbusu man yim'
Ao, mo sunsum no kɔn dɔ
W'asɔrmba hɔn fɛkuwbɔ,
W'enyim ne hyerɛn fɛɛfɛw n',
W'amayɛ n', Adom Nyame!

MHB 679
2 . Abɔso Nyame, nnoma a 
Wosu kyin Wo fie, woewie!
Na akra a wɔhom sor Egya
No bom' no, woewie dodow!
Wɔtse dɛ ebubur n' a
Oennya 'saase do sibea n',
Wɔsan kɔ hɔn hɛn no mu,
Hɔ na hɔn enyi gye daa.

MHB 679
3 . Woewie ampa! hɔn ayɛyi 
Pem mbusu bɔnsa 'i mu mpo;
N-su pue sar do ma hɔn,
Edziban fi sor nyɛn hɔn.
Wofi ahom mu kɔ ahom mu,
Dze kodu W'ahengua n' ho;
W'anan ho na wobom som,
'Wo a agye hɔn ne nyinam'.

MHB 679
4 . Mo Wura, ma muntu ehu dɛm: 
Gya m' twa bɔn wiadze yi mu;
Fa W'adom no suo mo mu,
Ma minnya kwan wɔ Wo nkyɛn.
M'ewia nye me kyɛm nye 'Wo;
Gya mo mfom 'koma 'i, weɔn no;
Adom nye enyimnyam fir Wo;
O mo Wura, hue gu mo do.   Amen.

MHB 68
1 . OBI nnsɛ Jeshurun Nyame,
No ho yɛ dzen, ɔkrɔn;
Hwɛ! Ɔtserɛw Ne ntsaban mu,
Ɔnantsew wɔ wimu!
Israel ɔnye N'abakan;
'Tumfo Nyame yɛ wodze,
Ofi sor robɔbor wo,
Nyame a bor adze nyina do.

MHB 68
2 . Jehovah Kɛse pɛ dɛ
Ɔboa na ɔgye wo;
Daa Nyankopɔn wowaw wo,
Wo Bɔfo, wo Nyɛnko;
Israel ɔbɛn na isuro?
Mbusu biara rennhaw wo,
Abasa a ɔwɔ hɔ daa n',
Aka wo efua yie.

MHB 68
3 . Nyame yɛ wodze; mma nnsuro
'Tamfo a ɔwɔ wo mu;
Nyame bɛba wo honam m',
Ma bɔn aabɔ adze;
Nyame bɛsɛɛ ɔbɔnfo n',
Ama wo konyimdzi m' dɛw; 
Nyame bɛpam n' na ɔaka
Dɛ, Sɛɛ hɔn, sɛɛ hɔn nyina!

MHB 68
4 . Aperdzi nyina abɔ adze,
Akokoeko egyaa;
Israel nnkɛyɛ bɔn bio da,
Na ɔbɛtsena asomdwee mu;
N'atamfo nyinara kɔ,
Bɔn nnyi kyɛfa wɔ no mu,
Israel nko bɛtsena hɔ a
Jesus wɔ n'akoma m'.

MHB 68
5 . Israel woehyira wo!
Ɔman bɛn nye wo sɛ?
Jesus agye w' efi bɔn m',
Ennkɛtsena bɔn mu bio,
Jesus nye w' kyɛm mpɛm esuon;
W'afowa a gya wɔ ano,
Nyame Tumfo Asɛm bedzi
Wiadze, bɛn na hɛll do.

MHB 680
1 . M'akoma dzii ehurusi 
Dɛ me mfɛfo see dɛ,
Bra ma yɛnkɔ Nyame Ne fie;
Afahyɛ da nye ndɛ.

MHB 680
2 . Hɛn anan bɛyɛ ntsɛm 
Ahɛn asɔrdan nom'
Ber a mobra na mpanyin pii
Rehyɛ som-bea no ma.

MHB 680
3 . Ebusua wɔtɔ dɛ 
Wɔbɔ punkum ba ha;
Ehumbɔbɔr egua n'enyim
Wɔdze dɛw kotow hɔ.

MHB 680
4 . Sɔr ma Jerusalem, 
Nyankopɔm ahenkurow n';
Nyame ntɔ Ne nhyira ngu hɔn a
Wɔdɔ Ne fie papa.

MHB 680
5 . Ha 'i dze wɔmma koryɛ 
Na asomdwee ntsintsim daa;
Zion, ahonya pii nhyehyɛ
W'ahemfi amaama.

MHB 680
6 . Hɛn afɛ nye enuanom 
Nnkɛpa hɛn mpaayim' da;
Wohyiam' asɔryɛm' ara pem a
Nyame mma N'asomdwee!  Amen.

MHB 681
1 . MBƆBƆRHU nye adom Nyame,
Da W'enyim ne hyerɛn edzi;
Hyerɛn hɛn do, Gyefo, hyerɛn,
Ma Wo kan nhyerɛn W'asɔr mu,
Ma Wo nkwagye ahoɔdzen
Ondu wiadze beebiara.

MHB 681
2 . Ma nkorɔfo no nyi W' ayɛw,
Hɔn a wɔtse ase ntonton Wo;
Ma aman no ntsea m' ntow ndwom,
Enyimnyam nka Hen Gyefo!
Mfa hɔn adwontow mbra W'enyim,
Wobetsie Wo pɛ krɔnkrɔn n'.

MHB 681
3 . Ma nkorɔfo no nyi W' ayɛw,
Na asaase bɔsow n'aba,
Nyame behyira nyimpa;
Nyimpa dze n' ho ma Nyame;
Ase mba nye ɔsorfo nyina
Bɛtsena dɛw na dɔ kor mu.

MHB 682
1 . MBƆBƆRHU nye adom Nyame,
'Hobrɛadze m' yɛhwɛ W'enyim,
Fi ɔsor Wo tsenabea
    Tsie, fa kyɛ, gye nkwa.

MHB 682
2 . Yehyia W'asɔrdan no mu
Dze dza yehia ba W'enyim,
Serɛ wɔ W' mbɔbɔr egua enyim;
   Fi ɔsor gye hɛn.

MHB 682
3 . Wo dɔ hyɛ akoma ma,
Na yɛpɛ ayɛ Wo pɛ;
Wɔkɔ W' koko krɔnkrɔn n' do,
  Owura, suo m', gye nkwa.

MHB 682
4 . Yɛman fi Wo nguankuw ho
Na hɛn dɔ ma Wo yɛ nwin a,
Fa mbɔbɔr enyi hwɛ hɛn;
  Fa kyɛ na gye nkwa.

MHB 682
5 . Awerɛhow nsa mia hɛn,
Wiadze haw hiahia hɛn ho;
Ma hɛn kra nnya W'asomdwee;
  Jesus, gye hɛn nkwa.

MHB 682
6 . Mbrɛ hɛn sufrɛ tse biara,
Yɛma hɛn akoma do ma W' a,
Yi hɛn adzesoa fi hɔ!
Tsie, fa kyɛ, gye nkwa.  Amen.

MHB 683
1 . HWƐ, Nyame wɔ ha! Yɛntonton N'
Na yenhu dɛ bea yi yɛ hu!
Dza ɔwɔ hɛn mu nyina ntse No tum,
Wɔmbɔ hɔn mu adze komm N'enyim;
Hɔn a wonyim No tum, N'adom
Dze suro som No, dze enyidzi dɔ N'.

MHB 683
2 . Hwɛ, Nyame wɔ ha! Ɔno na
Abɔfo adwontofo tow N' ndwom,
Ɔno na wɔakrɔn N' ɔsorsor;
Ɔsor dɔm dze ayɛyi ma N',
Ewuradze, mma mmpow hɛn ndwom no,
Gyirama a ɔdodow yi W' ayɛw.

MHB 683
3 . Atseasefo mu Ɔtseasenyi,
Hɛn ayɛyi mfow ndu Wo nkyɛn, 
Ma yɛnda ho ngyina W'enyim,
Yɛnda ho ntse, yɛnyɛ Wo pɛ;
Hɛn adwen nyina mbra Wo do,
Mma nngyaa dɛ egye hɛn afɔr.

MHB 683
4 . Dɛ mbrɛ nhyiren paa na ɔgye
Ewia ne hyew enyigye mu n',
Ma hɛn nsa nka Wo kan biara,
Na ma Wo tum no nkenyan hɛn;
Eyɛ bɛkyebo kan mu Kan,
Ogya a ɔhyew na okenyan

MHB 684
1 . Jesus, fa wusoɛr tum n' 
Gyina hɛn finimfin;
Ma hɛn asɔryɛ yi
Ɔnyɛ mber krɔnkrɔn.

MHB 684
2 . Hue Wo Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn 
Gu akoma nyina do;
Tu suro na yaw fi
Akra nyina mu.

MHB 684
3 . Na yebemia mu dzen 
Yeetu hɛn kwan yi,
Dɛ hɛn enyiwa da
Bɛkyebo da n' kwan.   Amen.

MHB 685
1 . HOM nsoɛr nhyira Ewuradze,
Hom nyimpa a woeyi hom,
Hom nsoɛr mfa akoma, kra nye ndze
Nhyira Ewuradze, Nyakopͻn.

MHB 685
2 . Ͻsén ayɛyi nyina dze,
Ͻbor nhyira nyina do dze;
Woana na onnkosuro Ne dzin,
Nnyi N’ aysw, nnkamfo No?

MHB 685
3 . Nkyɛ ogya a onndum da
Fi N’afͻrmbukyia do
Aaka hɛn ano, ekenyan hɛn,
Dze hɛn adwen eetsim sor!

MHB 685
4 . Hͻ ͻbrɛ N’aso adze
Dze tsie ndwom a yɛtow;
Onnyi Noho nnkyérɛ nyimpa dze,
Hɛn sunsum tse Ne nka.

MHB 685
5 . Nyame nye hɛn ahoͻdzen,
No nkwagye yɛ hɛndze;
Yɛdze hɛn ahoͻdzen nyina
Bɛka No dͻ ho asɛm.

MHB 685
6 . Hom nsoͻɛ nhyira Ewuradze,
Hom ntonton Ewuradze;
Hom nsoɛr nhyira N’enyimnyam dzin n’,
Ofi ndɛ nye daa nyina.

MHB 686
1 . HOM mma hom akoma do! Yɛma do ma Wo;
Yennyi obi bio wɔ Wo nan adze;
Hom mma hom akoma do! Yɛbɔ mu ma do,
Yɛma do, yɛma do ma Ewuradze!

MHB 686
2 . Yɛma do kɔ sor sen mfe a abɛsen n',
Bɔn a ogu hɛn ho fi, suro a ɔhyɛ hɛn do,
Ekyingye bɔw nye dɔ aprɔw mu,
Kan Wura, yɛma hɛn akoma do ndɛ.

MHB 686
3 . Akɔhwi nye enyiwa atɛkyɛ,
Ndzeyɛɛ nye nsusui a ɔnnhyɛ enyimnyam,
Tɛkyerɛma a ɔdodow asɛnka ho,
Nokwar Wura, yi Christianfo fi mu.

MHB 686
4 . Ma akyɛdze biara a edze ama no do;
Adze pa da famu a, gyedɛ wɔama do,
Akoma nye adwen a wɔakyekyer da famu,
Nyame dze mae, na ɔsan kɔ Ne nkyɛn.

MHB 686
5 . Afei, ekyir yi totorobɛnto hɛn a,
Hom mma hom akoma do! Ɔgyegye hɛn asomu;
Akoma nyina bɔbɔ mu agye do;
Yɛma do, yɛma do ma Ewuradze!

MHB 687
1 . MOBϽ mo mu adze komm W’enyim,
Bra na besiesie me kra na
Ͻmfata dɛ odzi sor edziban,
Mo Wura, nkwa, m’adze nyina.

MHB 687
2 . Ͻwo nyim mo mu adwembͻn,
Ͻmma munntum minndzi nyim koraa,
Wͻ nankasa ͻnye bͻn do;
Mo Wura, nkwa, m’adze nyina.

MHB 687
3 . Wo so yɛ nyimpa, nyim ne nyina,
Ͻbɛkaa me dɛ edͻ me;
Bɛn me, annyɛ a m’bͻhwease;
Mo Wura, nkwa, m’adze nyina.

MHB 687
4 . Minnyi tum ka Wodze nko ho,
Boa ma memfa m’akoma mma Wo;
Dzi me bra do, fa yɛ ahengua,
Mo Wura, nkwa, m’adze nyina.

MHB 687
5 . Mobͻ mo mu adze komm W’enyim;
Tsie me mpaabͻ a misi do yi; 
O ma m’afͻrbͻ yi ndzi mu,
Mo Wura, nkwa, m’adze nyina.

MHB 688
1 . NYAME hɛn Egya, Ɔwo ayɛ hɛn kor,
Akoma fam akoma ho, wɔ Wo Dɔba n' mu;
Yeridzi mpaa m' na obiara akɔ no kwan,
Ma ano na ndze biara nyi W' ayɛw.

MHB 688
2 . Ayɛyi nka Wo hɛn fɛkuwbɔ ntsi,
Akoma, kra, nye adwen fɛkuwbɔ;
Ayɛyi nka Wo, ɔdɔ nuayɛ ntsi,
Koryɛ a ndzepa Wura edze ba n' ntsi.

MHB 688
3 . Owura, hyɛ dzen na Wo nko na inyim,
Inyim mber a yeguan fi atamfo enyim;
Mpɛn dodow a yɛkɔ sum mu nsɔhwɛ mu n',
Yɛyew Wo tum nye W' nsa aɔda hɛn do.

MHB 688
4 . Ewuradze, ofi ndɛ kɔ nye hɛn nkɔ,
Ka hɛn ho wɔ hɛn daa dwumadzi mu;
Ber a eka hɛn ho n' obira bohu
Dɛ ɔsor nhyira hyɛ ase wɔ ha.

MHB 689
1 . 'EWimbir ansaana wi rotɔ n' 
Ewuradze, nna ayarfo gu W' nkyɛn;
Ao, yaw horow bɛn nna ɔannka hɔn!
Ao, dɛw bɛn nna wɔammfa annkɔ!

MHB 689
2 . Bio, edu 'wimbir, na hɛn so 
Yɛdze yarba horow twe pin;
Sɛ Yennhu wo mpo a, ɔyɛ dɛn?
Yenyim na yɛtse dɛ 'wɔ ha.

MHB 689
3 . Agyenkwa Christ, pam hɛn mbusu, 
Na binom abɔm,
Na binom nndɔɔ W' nokwar mu pɛn,
Binom so ayew dɔ a wonyae.

MHB 689
4 . Binom hu dɛ wiadze yɛ gyan, 
Naaso wonntum mmfi wiadze nsa;
Binom hɔn mfɛfo how hɔn werɛ,
Naaso wɔmmfaa Ɔwo nnyɛɛ nyɛnko.

MHB 689
5 . Ewuradze hɔn nyina serɛ ahomgye, 
Na wobefi bɔn mu koraa;
Hɔn a wɔper asom Wo yie n'
Nna wohu bɔn a ɔwɔ hɔn mu.

MHB 689
6 . Agyenkwa Christ, Nyimpa nye W' so; 
Wɔatseetsee Wo, wɔasɔ W' ahwɛ;
Ema Wo dɔ enyi do a, ihu
Epirakur a fɛr dze rusuma n'.

MHB 689
7 . Wo nsaano wɔ tum dɛ tsetse n', 
W'anomusɛm biara nnkefir gyan;
Ewimbir bɔw nwinwin yim' tsie,
Na W'ehumbɔbɔbɔrm' sa hɛn yar.

MHB 69
1 . Oyi nye Nyame a yɛsɔr No n', 
Hɛn Dɔfo pa a ɔnnsakyer da n',
No dɔ so dɛ No tum kɛse n',
Onnyi mbanano, nnyi ewiei.

MHB 69
2 . Jesus, Kandzifo, Kyirdzifo n', 
No Sunsum dze hɛn bodu fie;
Yeyi N' ayɛw wɔ dza etwam',
Yɛtwer No wɔ dza ɔreba.

MHB 690
1 . HԐN ayɛyi da asa,
Ewimbir sum aba,
Na sɛ ewia tͻ a, mum mmfi hɛn nkyɛm;
Adze nyina m’ nokwar kan.

MHB 690
2 . Ͻsor ahengua no ho.
Mbrɛ adze nnsa da no,
Nsankubͻfo hyɛ ntar fitaa,
Tow Wo ndwom daa nyina.

MHB 690
3 . Hɛn adwontow ya mberɛw,
Yɛbérɛ ayɛyi mu ntsɛm;
Na sor adwontofo no dze
Hͻn ndwom dzi mu, yɛ dɛw.

MHB 690
4 . Naaso Ewuradze, Ͻwo pɛ
Dɛ edan hɛn Akoma a,
Hɛn so yɛbͻtow ndwom kakra
Aka abͻfo ndwom ho.

MHB 690
5 . Ͻwo na edwedwé akra,
Na etwé etuatsewfo nyina,
Na ema ayɛyi hyɛ hɛn bra ma,
Dze hyɛ Wo dzin enyimnyam.

MHB 690
6 . Aka kumaa bi ma
Enyimnyam ewiei no aba,
Ma abͻfo na nyimpa hͻn ndwom
Aabͻ m’ W’ayɛyi mu.

MHB 691
1 . AGYENKWA, yɛma Wo dzin pa n’ do bio
Akoma kor m’ yɛtow hɛn mpaamudzi ayɛyi;
Yegyina hͻ hyira Wo ansaana yɛapon,
Na yɛkotow tweͻn W’asomdweesɛm no.

MHB 691
2 . Ma hɛn W’asomdwee bér a yɛrokͻ fie,
Yɛdze Wo hyɛɛ ase, na yɛdze W’ bowie;
Hɛn ano nnka bͻn, hɛn enyim nngu ase,
Na ofie yi mu na yeabͻ Wo dzin.

MHB 691
3 . Ma hɛn W’asomdwee, wͻ anafua yi mu,
Dan sum no ma ͻnye ekan mma hɛn,
Gye Wo mba fi ͻhaw nye mbusu mu,
Na sum nye kan nyina yɛ pɛr W’enyim.

MHB 691
4 . Ma hɛn W’asomdwee hɛn asetsena mu,
Hɛn awerɛhow mu na hɛn aperdzi mu,
Afei, ber a Wo ndze ma akodzi bͻ adze,
Ewuradze, frɛ hɛn kͻ W’asomdwee mu.

MHB 692
1 . AGYENKWA, hyira hɛn ana yɛakɔ;
Fa W'asɛm hyɛ hɛn adwen mu;
Na ma akoma mu nkenyan,
Ahobrɛadze dɔ na pɛ pa.
   Wɔ nkwa adzekyee nye wu sum mu,
   O Jesus brɛfo, yɛ hɛn kan.

MHB 692
2 . Da no asa, ne mber etwa m',
Na Ɔwo nyim no mu nsɛm nyina;
Konyim kakra a adom dze bae n',
Oebu anohoba do, ahwe ase.

MHB 692
3 . Owura, gye hɛn fi akwan bɔn do,
Fakyɛ turodoo nye ɔgye;
Fa ahotsew nye asomdwee
Hyira hɛn ma ɔnsen nda no a etwa m'.

MHB 692
4 . Fa kyɛ mbordo, ma hɛn dɛw,
Suro mapa ɔnye fahodzi,
Na dɔ akoma a nkekae nnyi mu,
Dza ɔpɛ dɛ ɔnye Wo sɛ.

MHB 692
5 . Yɛfrɛ hɛn adɔfo nyina brɛ Wo
Ehiafo, 'werɛhofo, abɔn;
Ma W'ehumbɔbɔr n' mma hɛn dɛw,
'Wo nye hɛn Jesus, hɛn adze nyina.

MHB 693
1 . Nyame, fa Wo nhyira gya hɛn kwan, 
Dom hɛn dɛw na asomdwee;
Ma ankorankor yennya Wo dɔ
Mfa ndzi nkwagye adom ho dɛw;
Ao, hyɛ hɛn dzen
Wɔ bra sar akwantu yim'.

MHB 693
2 . Yɛdze ndaase na ntonton ma W' 
Wɔ Wo nsɛmpa dɛɛdɛw n' ho;
Nkyɛ Wo nkwangye no ho aba
Asow hɛn akoma nye bram';
Nkyɛ Woara so
Yeehu W' hɛn nkyɛn afebɔɔ.    Amen.

MHB 694
1 . EWURADZE, ayɛ hɛn tsenebea
Wɔ mbasantsen nyina mu;
Wo nkorɔfo da ho hu W'adom,
Woehyira W'awerɛkyekyer;
Etsie hɛn sufrɛ ber biara,
Yehu dɛ ebɛn ber biara,
Hɛn ahoɔdzen nye hɛn nkwagye.

MHB 694
2 . Yɛtɔ dɛ yesu hɛn bɔn ho,
Yɛyɛ dze akyerɛ W'abotar,
Naaso yɛda ho kura W' gyedzi m'
Yɛda ho dɔ Wo dzin no;
Na akora hɛn na adɔ hɛn yie,
'Ma hɛn kwan dɛ yɛntsena Wo mu,
Na yennhinhim, yenntutu.

MHB 694
3 . Ewuradze, biribiara nnkotum
Agye W' nkorɔfo efi Wo nsamu,
Hɛn Boafo nnkefi hɔ ara da;
Nyame nnkedzi hɛn huambɔ,
Wo nkorɔfo atsena Wo mu;
'Bɛda ho ayɛ hɛn tsenabea
Daa, afebɔɔ, afebɔɔ.

MHB 695
1 . AYƐYI rotweɔn Wo Zion,
Mpaabɔ bɛhyɛ W'asɔrdan ma;
Nyimpa nyina bɛba W'egua ho,
Enya Christ mu nkwagye wɔ hɔ.

MHB 695
2 . Hɛn sunsum fɔn, hɛn bɔn dzi nyim,
Mma hɛn ahopopo akoma nnsuro;
Ɔwo a itsie mpaabɔ, sian bra
Bɛyɛ ndzebɔnyɛfo nyɛnko.

MHB 695
3 . W'ahotsewfo n' woehyira hɔn,
Wɔakora hɔn do, wɔnyɛn hɔn daa;
Asaase nye po nyina Agyenkwa,
Hɔn a wɔdan Wo nya enyigye.

MHB 695
4 . Wo nsa na edze yɛɛ mbepɔw,
Wo ndze taa po asorɛkye dzinn;
'Napa, 'wimbir, woyi W'ayɛw,
Emaa asaase yii no ndɔbaa.

MHB 695
5 . W'ayamuyie ahyɛ afe n' mu ma,
Wo mununkum tɔ asaase do nsu,
Wo mu sar pradada tow ndwom,
Abɔdze serew, ohu ne Hen.

MHB 695
6 . Hue Wo Sunsum gu hɛn akra do;
Fa abrabɔ pa san ma hɛn;
O ma Wo dɔ no nkenyan hɛn,
Na ma yɛnsow aba Wo mu.

MHB 696
1 . HOM a hom yɛ ɔsor Hen mba,
Hom ntow ndwom hom akwantu mu;
Hom ntow hom Agyenkwa ayɛyi,
Enyimnyam wɔ No ndwuma m'.

MHB 696
2 . Yerutu kwan akɔ Nyame nkyɛn,
Ɔkwan a egyanom faa do n'.
Hɔn enyi agye sesei,
Ɔnnkɛkyɛr na yeehu yi.

MHB 696
3 . Okuw ketseaba, hom ntsea m',
Hom mbɔhom Jesus Ne nkyɛn,
Woesiesie hom ngua wɔ hɔ,
Hom ahenman nye akatua.

MHB 696
4 . Hom mma hom enyi do, kan mba;
Zion kurow da hom enyim,
Hɔ, ɔbɛyɛ hɛn fie daa,
Yebohu hɛn Wura ntsɛm.

MHB 696
5 . Enuanom, hom nyina mfa
Dɛw ngyina hom ahe do;
Jesus Christ, hom Egya Ne Ba n'
Hyɛ hom dɛ hom nkɔ kan ndam m'.

MHB 696
6 . Ewuradze, yetsie kɔ kan,
Dze dɛw gya ne nyina wɔ ha,
Wo nko ara dzi hɛn bano
Na yebedzi W'ekyir daa.

MHB 697
1 . NHYIRA nye akra abrɛfo a
Wohu hͻn hia dɛ wͻnnsɛ hwee;
Wͻama hͻn adom akyɛdze,
Nye dɛw ahenkyɛw a ͻwͻ sor.

MHB 697
2 . Nhyira nye hͻn a hͻn akoma ebubu,
Bͻn ntsi wodzi yaw wͻ hͻn mu;
Christ No bͻgyaa krͻnkrͻn pem dɛ
Ayarsa ma hͻn yaw nyinara.

MHB 697
3 . Nhyira nyé akra a wͻhwehwɛ adorn;
’Kͻm nye nsukͻm wo tsénenee ntsi,
Wͻdze nkwa nsu nye edziban
Bɛmema hͻn ama wͻaamee.

MHB 697
4 . Nhyira nye akomamutsewfo,
Woefi bͻn no tum no ase;
Wodze enyigyé a onnyi ewiei
Bohu Nyamé a ͻyɛ krͻnkrͻn.

MHB 697
5 . Nhyira nye amandzehufo,
Jesus ntsi wohu amandze;
Hͻn kra bedzi nyim Nyame mu.
'Nyimnyam, dɛw nye hͻn akatua.

MHB 698
1 . OWURA Jesus, fa W‘adom no
Bɛtséna hɛn mu afebͻͻ,
Na mma yɛmma bͻn kwan koraa,
Na yɛnnhow Wo werɛ.

MHB 698
2 . Fa W’asɛm bɛtsena hɛn mu.
Pomfo a yɛdͻ Wo;
Ma hɛn Wo mboa nye mbͻbͻrhu
Na tsenabew wͻ sor.

MHB 698
3 . Fa Wo kan bɛtsena hɛn mu,
Kan a ͻhyérɛn hɛn do,
Na ma Wo nokwar nkyérɛ hɛn kwan,
Na amma yaannhwé ase.

MHB 698
4 . ’Nye hɛn ntsena na hyira hɛn,
Asomdwee Ewuradze;
Adom na tum aahyɛ hɛn ma,
To hɛn gyedzi na dͻ m’.

MHB 698
5 . Bɛtsena hɛn mu dɛ hɛn kyɛm,
Dzi Wo dͻm do Ͻsahen,
Na yeenngyaa hɛnho amma wiadze,
Na yemmfi hɛn gyinabew.

MHB 698
6 . Bɛtséna hɛn mu wͻ dͻ mapa m’,
Yɛ hɛn Nyamé Agyenkwa;
Yɛnkyerɛ Wo mboa wͻ ahokyer mu,
Kora hɛn Wo mu nokwar m'.    Amen.

MHB 699
1 . HƐN Pomfo, Wura yɛ kɛse,
Tum, nokwar nye adom mu;
Ɔsorsorfo tonton N' daa,
N'asɔrmba yi N' ayɛw.
Hɛn Nyankopɔn kurow no mu,
Bepɔw krɔnkrɔn a ɔwɔ ase n',
Hom mfa Ne dzin no ntahye,
Hom nda N' kɛseyɛ edzi.

MHB 699
2 . Ewuradze, W'adɔyɛ ntsi
Yɛtsena W'asɔrdan mu,
Ha Wo nokwar dɔ no da
Wo nkwagye tum edzi;
Wo dzin ma yeyi W'ayɛw,
Na W'emudzi no hyerɛn,
Wiadze nyina bɛgye ato m',
Wo ndwuma yɛ krɔnkrɔn.

MHB 699
3 . Hwɛ, Asɛmpa Asɔr n' tsim hɔ,
Na osi botan do;
N'anohoba yɛ nokwar,
Woana behim N'aban?
Kan no sombea a ɔsom bo;
Ka kyerɛ nkyirmba so bi.
Nyame tum abɔ ho ban,
Asɔr no ronnhwe ase.

MHB 699
4 . Zion Nyame yɛ hɛndze,
Hɛndze, yɛtwer No dɔ;
Yeehu Ne fakyɛ dɔ no,
Yɛtse ase, wu ma Christ:
Ɔbɛyɛ hɛn Kwankyerɛfo
'Kɔ Jerusalem fofor m';
Yɛgye N', na yɛhom No mu,
Wɔ mfesantsen nyin m'.

MHB 7
1 . O ƆSORSOR Hen, fi sor hwɛ famu ha,
Boa hen yɛntow W'ehumbɔbɔor nye dɔ,
Ɔrepem dɛ osunsuan ebunkam hɛn do,
Naaso gu do ara dze pii kã hɛn ho.

MHB 7
2 . Hen nkwa Nyankopɔn, yɛtsew Wo dzin ho;
Hɛn edwuma nye dɛ yɛper tahye Wo dzin,
Gye hɛn ndaase wo adom a edze bɔɔ hɛn,
Atseasefo nyina bɛkyere W'ayɛyi.

MHB 7
3 . Hɛn Egya, hɛn Wura, eyɛ Otumfo,
W'asɛm a akora hɛn ntsi na yɛrosor yi;
Ndzepa a yenya nyina fi Wo nko hɔ ba,
Hɛn gyirama na hɛn nkwa yɛdze bɔsom Wo.

MHB 7
4 . Dza ɔkyen ne nyina, yetow W’ayamuyie.
Agye wiadze a ayew efi bɔn na yaw m'.
Edze Wo Ba abɔ werdam apon wiadze,
De omfa hen a yetwer No mbra hen sor fie.

MHB 7
5 . Wo dɔ ntsi yɛtow ndwom dzi ehurusi.
Yɛnye sor abɔfo ma hɛn ndze do;
Agyedzifo nyina bɔtonton Wo dɔ
Mbersantsen mfesantsen a ɔmmbɔ adze da

MHB 70
1 . M'ENYIDAR wɔ Nyankopɔn mu;
Ɔyɛ me gyedzi fofor,
Ogya m' fa ɔbra adandan mu,
Oye na ɔyɛ nokwafo.
Wonnyim No,
No nkotoo,
Ɔfrɛ m'akoma Nedze.

MHB 70
2 . Nyimpa ahantan na n'enyimnyam, 
Afowa na ahenkyɛw sɛɛ no;
Ɔdze berɛ tow abantsentsen
Na ne nyina bubu gu famu,
Nyame tum,
Ber nyina nye
m'asɔrdan na abantsentsen.

MHB 70
3 . Nyame N'ayamuyie wɔ hɔ daa,
Ne nyansaa bor adwen do:
Enyimnyam, kan na nkwa fir no,
Ahoɔfɛw mapa fir no.
Afebɔɔ
Na No mu
Aman fofor soɛr som No.

MHB 70
4 . Otumfo Mafo no ma hɛn 
Ndzepa pii daa nyinara,
Hɛn akra enyi gye Ne pɛ ho,
'Nyigye gya hɛn bea a yɛkɔ.
No mu na
Ɔdɔ gyina;
Ɔma enyigye gyina.

MHB 70
5 . Adasa nkɔ do ara daa,
Mfa ayɛyi afɔrbɔ 
Mma ɔdomankoma Nyame,
 Wɔ Christ a ɔdze No mae,
Jesus frɛ
Obiara:
Nyia otsie No nnhwe ase.

MHB 700
1 . NYIA no werɛ hyɛ Nyame m',
Na ɔtse bɔgya no tum n',
Gyina pintsinn wɔ ehumtu ber m'
Dɛ Nyame Ne bepɔw:
Onnhinhim, osi pi,
Ne Zion nnkodwuruw da;
N'agyedzifo gyina pintsinn
Wɔ Jesu No dɔ mu.

MHB 700
2 . Dɛ mbrɛ nkokwaa etwa
Jerusalem ho ehyia n',
Dɛm na Nyame bɔ hom ho ban
Fi atamfo nyina nsamu;
Ogyina akwan nyina m',
Twitwa gye N' Israel,
Na No tum nsamu na ɔdze
Hɔn akra sie afebɔɔ.

MHB 700
3 . Ewuradze Domfo, ma
Wɔnda ho ntsena Wo mu,
Nkɛpem dɛ akra nyina ho bɛsan,
Na woedzi mu koraa;
Akomamutseweefo nyina
Kɔ do bɔ hɔn ho ban;
Yɛ hɔn yie, gye hɔn nkwa wɔ ha,
Na dɔ hɔn kɔ ewiei.

MHB 701
1 . Asɔr ne fapem kortoo 
Nye Jesus Christ hɛn Wura;
Ɔnam nsu nye N'asɛm do
Yɛɛ n' N'abɔdze fofor.
Ofi sor bɔhwehɛɛ no.
Yɛɛ n' N'ayefor krɔnkrɔn.
Ɔdze No bɔgyaa tɔɔ no
No nkwa ntsi na owui.

MHB 701
2 . Wɔpaam' yii n' aman nyinam', 
Naaso ɔyɛ Asɔr kor.
No nkwagye tum ɔnye yi-
Wura kor, gyedzi kor,
Dzin krɔnkrɔn kor na ohyira;
N'edziban krɔnkrɔn kor,
Enyidar kor na ɔper ho,
Adom nyina wɔ mu.

MHB 701
3 . Sɛ mpo nyimpa si atwetwe 
Hwɛ N'ahokyer kɛse,
Dɛ mpaapaam' atsetsew mu
Nkyerɛkyerɛ bɔn tseetsee N' a,
Ahotsewfo n' weɔn, wosu
Dɛ, ondu da bɛn ara?
Anago su n' nnkyɛkyɛr na
Ɔadan anapa ndwom.

MHB 701
4 . Berɛ nye amandzehu mu, 
N'akodzi dede n' mu,
Ɔtweɔn daadaa asomdwee a
Ɔmmbɔ adze n' n'emudzi n',
Kɛpem dɛ n'enyi bohu
'Nyimnyam enyidado n',
Na Asɔr konyimdzifo no
Bɛhɛn n' ahomgye mu.

MHB 701
5 . Na ɔwɔ wiadze yi, ɔnye 
Ɔkorsa Nyame bɔm',
Na ɔnye hɔn a wɔrohom
Dzi nkitaho dɛɛdɛw.
O ahotsewfo esiarfo!
Ewuradze, dom hɛn,
Dɛ abrɛfo yinom, ma
Yɛnye W' mbɛtsena sor hɔ.  Amen.

MHB 702
1 . CHRIST hɛn kutuwdo - bo,
No nko do na yɛtow;
N'ahotsewfo nko hyɛ
Sor abanguado ma;
Yɛdze hɛn enyidar na enyigye
Hyɛ No dɔ na adom mu sesei.

MHB 702
2 . O dɛm ayɛyi ndwom 'i
Bɔwosow abangua 'i do;
Yɛbɛma hɛn ndze do
Atow Ɔkorsa ndwom,
Dɛm na yɛdze N'enyimnyam dzin n'.
Bɔtow ndwom a ohur daa nyina.

MHB 702
3 . Ɔdomfo Nyankopɔn,
Twe penkyɛn hɛn mber nyina
Gye nokwar nsew biara,
Na hyɛ nkrumsi so nsew;
Hue Wo nhyira gu mpaabɔ do
Wɔ da krɔnkrɔn biara no mu.

MHB 702
4 . Adom a yebisa n'
Wɔmfa mfi sor mbrɛ hɛn;
Sɛ hɛn nsa nya ka dze a,
Ɔnye hɛn ntsena afebɔɔ,
Nkodu da no a esiarfo nyina
Wɔbɛfrɛ hɔn akɔ ahomgye m'.  Amen.

MHB 703
1 . Nyame kurow mbrɛ odua so 
Na n' afasu war a!
'Nokwafo nye W' adehye dɔm,
Wɔ mbew na mber nyinam'.

MHB 703
2 . Asɔr krɔnkrɔn kor, nkodɔm kor, 
Botae a ɔkrɔn kor,
Dwumadzi kuw kor, ndɔbaa ndwom kor,
Ɔhen Otumfo kor.

MHB 703
3 . Ofitsi nyimpa n' ahyɛse 
Mbrɛ W' asɛm esi edwir n'!
Mbrɛ W' aman esi atserɛw
Wɔ ahotɔ na dɔm' a!

MHB 703
4 . Mbrɛ Wo gya si dzɛw anago 
Dze weɔn na ɔnnhwer a!
W' akoban hyerɛn sunm' ara
Dze kɛpem adzekyee.

MHB 703
5 . Asorɛkye bu akɛse kwa, 
Anhwea dwurudwuruw gyan;
Onntum mmpuhim botantsim a
Bɛkyebo kurow si do n'.

MHB 704
1 . AKOKO a ho tsew etwa ehyia,
Ne fapem no tsim hɔ pintinn daa,
Ewuradze ahenkurow no tsim hɔ;
Wonnkotum edwuruw n'afasu;
Mbanyin dze asuro na nwanwa hwɛ no,
Na wɔhyɛ nyia ɔweɔn no nsew.
Nyia ɔhwɛ Israel no,
Ɔnntɔ nnkom na ɔnnda,
Halleluja!
Enyigye dɔm\nNye hɔn a adom n'
Bɛba hɔn tsenabea mu daa daa!

MHB 704
2 . Jehova dɔ Zion n'apon!
Na ɔdze adom nwanwa gye to m';
Na ɔdze ndadze hin ekyir,
Ohyira hɔn a wɔtse no mu,
Ɔkyekye hɔn werɛ ber a wɔabɔm,
Na wɔdze yaw, dadwen gu N' do n',
Adom a ɔdze fua
No nkorɔfo nyinara n',
Ɔyɛ nwanwa!
Nyame ahenkurow,
Enyigye bea a,
Hɔ na dɛm nhyira nyina wɔ!

MHB 704
3 . N-kwagye a aman pii nnyim no,
Zion no nko mu na wɔkyerɛ:
Hɔ, wɔtse dza ɔso, yɛ krɔnkrɔn;
Ber a Wo nkorɔfo tse wo mu no,
Etsentsen hɔn, kyekye hɔn werɛ,
Ewɔ Sunsum na Asɛm no;
Asomdwee bɔ hɔ aprɔw,
Na wɔtse ndwom dɛɛdɛw,
Nya adom tsema,
Ɔyɛ dɛw ma!
Ɔma asomdwee
Na enyigye kɛse tsim hɔ daa.

MHB 705
1 . NYAME yɛ sumabew ma Ne mba,
Sɛ ehum a ɔyɛ dzen tu mpo a;
Ansaana yɛka hɛn ayawdzi n',
Hwɛ ɔwɔ hɛn nkyɛn roboa hɛn!

MHB 705
2 . Ma mbepɔw ntutu mfi hɔn mbea
Mbra bun mu na wonsie hɔn hɔ;
Asaase dzendzen no nwosow,
Hɛn gyedzi nnkosuro hwee koraa.

MHB 705
3 . Po woree no bɛyɛ dede,
Hɛn akra tsena asomdwee krɔnn mu;
Ber a aman na mpoano nyimpa
Ho popo, suro asorɛkye kɛse n'.

MHB 705
4 . Esu bi wɔ hɔ a ne mpemee
Ma hɛn Nyame man enyigye;
Nkwa, dɔ na enyigye gu do pem,
Fow kɔ hɛn man krɔnkrɔn no mu.

MHB 705
5 . Dɛm esu krɔnkrɔn n', W'asɛnhia n',
Ɔhyɛ hɛn suro dzendzen do;
Asomdwee a Wo bɔyhɛ n' dze ma n'
Ma ɔkra a ɔagow ahoɔdzen bio.

MHB 705
6 . Zion dzi ne Hen N' dɔ ho dɛw,
Ɔgye n' fi dɔnhwer huuhu n' mu;
Ne fapem dzendzen n' nnokobubu,
Woetsim n' wɔ No nokwardzi do.

MHB 706
1 . Wɔka wo ho enyimnyam nsɛm, 
Zion, hɛn Nyame Ne man;
Nyia ɔnnsan N' asɛm no kyekyeer
Wo dɛ No kurow a ɔtsenam'.
Tsetse Bo no nye wo fapem,
Ebɛn botum awosow w'?
N-kwagye yɛ wo ho afasu;
Ebɛserew w' atamfo.

MHB 706
2 . Hwɛ, n-kwa nsu a ofi Nyame 
Ne daadaa dɔ mu pem no
Ma wo mba wɔmee, na oyi
Hia ho suro fi hɔn do.
Woana na ɔbɔtɔ bitsi
Wɔ dɛm esutsen yi ho?
Adom a ɔpem daa nyina
Wo Nyame dze dom wo daa.

MHB 706
3 . M' Agyenkwa, menam W' adom do 
Mofora Zion mamfom' a,
Ma wiadze nsi me atwetwe,
Ɔno mpo bɛyɛ mo ntuw,
Wiadze nye no mu enyigye
Nye ahokyerɛ resen.
Enyigye nye ahonya a otsim
Zion mba nko na wonya

MHB 707
1 . ϽWO wͻammfa nsa annyɛ W’,
Eso wͻannkrͻn wo sor,
Wͻanntow w’aban hyɛnhyɛnn,
Wͻnndzé aboͻdzen bo yɛ w';
Ehyerɛn sen sika,
Nyame N’ Jerusalem.

MHB 707
2 . Ber a akoma brɛfo,
Benya sor ’kokodur n’,
Mbrɛ akoma apa n’,
Onya nkenyan fi ͻdͻ m’
Ber a gyedzi apam suro n’;
Eyɛ Nyame N’ kuropͻn.

MHB 707
3 . Ewͻ beea a ahopͻw
Dan yɛ ahobrɛadze,
Bea a suban yɛ botoo n’;
Bea a atͻfo nya ahenkyɛw,
Bea a agyedzifo nyina
Nya asomdwee mapa.

MHB 707
4 . Ͻbra n’akwan horow mu,
Yɛdzé enigye nantsew;
Hɛn a yeduaa mbusu mu n’,
Yetsia N’anamͻn mu,
Ber a ͻwͻ akoma biara mu n’;
Nya Nyame N’ kuropͻn.

MHB 707
5 . ϽWo a wͻannkrͻn w’ wͻ sor.
Wͻanntow w’aban ekyirkyir,
Na bér a beenu, baasa
Ehyia mu wͻ Christ mu n’,
Tsena hͻn finimfim,
Nyame N’ Jerusalem.   Amen.

MHB 708
1 . OWURA, yɛdͻ Wo man,
Ofie a etse mu no.
Asͻr a hɛn Pomfo n’ dze N’ bͻgyaa a
Ͻsom bo gyee sii hͻ n'.

MHB 708
2 .  Owura, yɛdͻ W’asͻr
’Hotsewfo wͻ W’enyim;
Wͻsom W’ bo dɛ W’enyiwa kyirefuwa,
Woekrukye wͻ Wo nsamu.

MHB 708
3 . Ͻno ntsi yebosu
Na hɛn mpaabͻ edu sor;
Yɛdze hɛn haw, hɛn bérɛ bɛma n’
’Kodu dɛ ͻbͻbͻ adze.

MHB 708
4 . Hɛn dɛw mbordo ekyir n’,
Yebu no sor akwan,
Ne nkitahodzi anohoba,
No dͻ, ayɛyi ho ndwom n’.

MHB 708
5 . Jesus, Nyɛnko krͻnkrͻn,
Hɛn Gyefo na hɛn Hen,
Wo nsa bɛgye hɛn yie efi
Atamfo nyé efir mu.

MHB 708
6 . Dɛ Wo nokwar tsim hͻ n’,
Asaasé enyimnyam pa n’,
Wͻdze ne nyina bɛma Zion,
Na dɛw kɛse wͻ sor.

MHB 709
1 . Yɛda ho yɛtse nkwam'? 
Yeehu hɛn enyim bio?
Christ N' adom a ɔapon hɛn ntsi
Hom mma yenyi N' ayɛw.

MHB 709
2 . Nyame tum akora hɛn 
Wɔ nkwagye a odzi mum';
Yɛbɔm' bio wɔ Christ N' ayɛyim',
Yedzi N' enyim ehyia.

MHB 709
3 . Mbusu pii a yeehu a! 
Akodzi a yeeduam' a!
Guado ɔko', na hɛn mu hu' a!,
Fitsi dɛ yehyiaa nkan n'.

MHB 709
4 . Ewuradze No dɔ 
Agye hɛn ne nyinam',
Na ɔda ho dze No mboa ma hɛn
Na osie hɛn nkwa wɔ sor.

MHB 709
5 . Dɛm a hom mma yentuw 
No nkwagye tum no mu,
Tum a ɔgye hɛn nkwa koraa
Kɛpem dɛ yeetua bɔn.

MHB 709
6 . Hom mma yɛmfa mbeamudua n' 
Na yeenya ahenkyɛw n';
Sɛ yebenya Jesus Noara a
Dza aka n'- yemmbu no hwee

MHB 71
1 . YƐBA hɛn egyanom Nyame nkyɛn; 
Hɔn Botan nye hɛn nkwagye; 
Daa abasa nye hɔn tsenabea, 
Yɛdze yɛ hɛn tsenabea,
Yedze hɛn ayɛyi brɛ Wo,
Yɛhwehwɛ W' dɛ ahotsewfo n'. 
Wɔ mbasantsen nyina mu.

MHB 71
2 . Onyame gya a odzii hɔn kan n'
Da ho hyerɛn dzi hɛn kan;
Ɔsor kyɛm a ɔnweɔɔn hɔn no 
Da ho so kata hɛn do;
Adom a ɔbrɛɛ abɔnfo adze,
Ahoɔdzen a ɔhyɛɛ mberɛwyɛ dzen, 
Da ho dzi nyim, hyɛ hen dzen.

MHB 71
3 . Bɔn a ɔbrɛɛ hɔn adze no
Da ho hyɛ hɛn kra do ndɛ; 
Nyinsuwa a wokyii n' nyinara, 
Yɛdze enyito ka hɛn bɔn; 
Dɛ mbrɛ itsiee hɔn sufrɛ no, 
Dɛm na hɛn mpaabɔ fow kɔ sor, 
Na ɔdze Wo nhyira ba.

MHB 71
4 . Yɛdze hɔn dɛw brɛ hɔn Wura;
Hɔn ndwom sian ba hɛn so nkyɛn; 
Sunsum a ɔtoow ndwom wɔ hɔn mu n', 
Ɔdze No ndwom so ma hɛn;
Yɛnye hɔn tow ndwom kor ara;
Yɛma do, yɛdze kɔ sorsor,
Ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze da.

MHB 71
5 . Ahotsewfo a hom reba nyina,
Hom nkɔ do ntow ndwom dɛɛdɛw;
Mma hom nngyaa ndwom n' tow ara da; 
Hom nkɔ do ntow afebɔɔ;
Hom wɔ ahotɔ wɔ hom tsenabea,
Adom a onnyi ewiei wɔ ha,
Hyira Nyia ɔma mbordo n'.

MHB 710
1 . NUANOM na adɔfo wɔ Christ mu,
Hom ho hia Jesus na No dɔm;
Hom mbra mbɛda hom ho edzi,
M'bohu dɔ Ewuradze wɔ ha.

MHB 710
2 . Akɔaba fi asaase do;
Yɛyɛ hom etuu fɛkuwbɔ mu;
Ofi akoma mapa mu,
Na hom ngye no Jesus dzin mu.

MHB 710
3 . Jesus, yi Woho kyerɛ wɔ dɔ m';
Ana yennhyiaa W' dzin nwanwa n' mu?
Yɛtweɔn hɛn Wura wɔ hɛn finimfin,
Ogyaframee no na yɛtweɔn.

MHB 710
4 . Nyame a edze ogya kasa,
Ma ogya a ɔdzɛw Sunsum mfir edzi,
Ma ɔpɛ krɔnkrɔn gyaframee
Mfi hɛn akoma afɔrmbukyia n' do.

MHB 710
5 . Ampa, koryɛ a ofir Egya n'
Nam Wo do baa asaase do;
Onnyiewiei nkwa wɔ W' mu, na ma 
Hɛn sor ahotɔ a onnyi kasu.

MHB 711
1 . O EWURADZE, Wo sor tsenabea
Ne fɛw, ne dɛw na no nwanwa a!
Me kra dzi aper tɔ bitsi
Dze hyia W'ahotsewfo kuw no.

MHB 711
2 . N-hyira nye ahotsewfo a 
Wotwa ahengua ho wɔ sorsor;
W'enyimnyam kɛse m' hyerɛn sor hɔ
Dze dɔ yi Wo ndwuma ayɛw.

MHB 711
3 . N-hyira nye akra a wohu bea 'i
Wɔ W'adom asɔrfi yi mu;
Hɔ wohu Wo hyerɛn fɛɛfɛw no,
Hwehwɛ W'enyim, sua W'ayɛyi.

MHB 711
4 . N-hyira nye hɔn a hɔn akoma
Hwehwɛ Zion abowano kwan;
Nyame nye hɔn ahoɔdzen pa,
No kwan do na wɔtwer No mboa.

MHB 711
5 . Wɔnam enyigye na ahoɔdzen m'
Kodu dɛ yebehyia ahenman m',
Kɛpem dɛ yebɛba W'enyim
Abɔsom ɔsom pa m' wɔ hɔ

MHB 712
1 . NHYIRA nyé ͻdͻ a ͻka hɛn bͻ m’,
Dza ͻmma yɛmmpaa mu n’,
Hɛn honandua fi hɛn ho mpo a,
Yɛyɛ kor wͻ akoma m’.

MHB 712
2 . Yɛnye Egya n’ yɛ sunsum kor
Yɛkͻ beebi a ͻkyérɛ,
Yetsiatsia Jesu N’anamͻn m’,
Kyerɛ N’enyimnyam wͻ ha.

MHB 712
3 . O ma yenye N’ nnantséw afebͻͻ
Dɛ yennyim hweeàra bio,
Yɛnndwendwen hwee, mmbu hwee, gyedɛ
Jesus Ne mbeamudua n’ nko.

MHB 712
4 . Hom mma yɛntwe mboa ano yie
Wͻ N’abasa n’ ase;
Hɛn enyi nda N'emudzi kwan,
Adom ngu adom do.

MHB 712
5 . Agyenkwa n’ N’adom m‘ kyɛfafo,
Adwen. akoma m’ koryɛ.
Edɛw na yaw, aber anaa bea.
Nkwa anaa ’wu nntum mmpaa m’.

MHB 713
1 . NYAMƐ hyɛ hɛn dɛ yɛmbͻ m’
Yɛnkà akoma na nsa mbͻ m’;
Yennya hɛn frɛ ho enyidar,
Yɛmboaboa hɛnho nkorkor;
Hɛn werɛ mfir dza etwa mu,
Mfa akomà, adwen ndzi Christ ekyir
Mper nko botae no ho pɛɛ
Nkɛfa nokwàr ahenkyɛw no.

MHB 713
2 . Yɛnye Nyame nam kan mu a,
Nyame ka hɛn akoma bͻ mu a;
Yɛyɛ anyɛnkofo pa,
Jesus dͻ mu anyɛnkofa:
Dɛw mu na yɛkà bͻ mu,
Na yɛdze dzi hɛn dwuma,
Yɛtse bͻgyà à ͻtsew hɛn ho m’,
Daa yɛtse dɛ Christ ewu.

MHB 713
3 . Nyame, hyɛ hɛn gyedzi dzen,
Hor hɛn ho dza ͻnntsen nyina m’;
Ͻwo nntum nnhwɛ dza ͻnntsen;
O ma yɛmfata mma Wo!
Ku akͻndͻbͻn biara,
Tu aba bͻn biarà ase,
Gu bͻn nyinà ase koraa,
Kyérɛw Wo dͻ mbra wͻ hɛn mu.

MHB 713
4 . ’Fi ndɛ ma hɛn ndzeyɛɛ nyina
Nkyerɛ dͻ dɛ yenyim Christ;
Ma dͻ no nyɛ asɛnkyérɛdze.
Dɛ yɛyɛ Wodzé, Ewuradze:
Fa Wo dͻ suban n’ ma hɛn.
Tsim n‘wͻ hɛn enyim nà akoma m’!
Ma hɛn Wo dͻ no nkotoo!
Nyame, yemmbisa hwee bio.

MHB 714
1 . NYIA ɔwɔ Wo dɔ no nnhia ndamfo,
Ɔnye Wo nantsew dzi nkɔmbɔ;
Menye W'ahotsewfo nyina
Bɔbɔ awɛ sesei na daa.

MHB 714
2 . Ahotsewfo nkitahodzi m'
Wɔ nyansa, 'tsidaa na enyigye;
M'akoma yɛ mberɛw, motɔ bahaw a,
Hɔn hyew na kan wɔma mo do.

MHB 714
3 . M'ayɛnkofo dze, wɔnnyewee;
W'ahɛn a ɔdɔɔ so pii no,
Sɛ ehum bɔ hɔn petse mpo a,
Wobehyia m' sɔkyee berano.

MHB 714
4 . Hɛn nyina da ho ara tse Wo mu,
Yɛapetse mpo a, yɛyɛ Wodze,
Yɛwɔ ebusua noara mu,
Gyedzi, Sunsum kor kyerɛ hɛn kwan.

MHB 714
5 . W'ahengua enyim na daa yehia,
Na yɛbɔ m' totɔ serɛ Wo;
Yekyiakyia hɛnho sunsum mu,
Yebohu hɛnho nkorkor bio.

MHB 714
6 . Ɔsor dɔm no nyina bɛyɛ 
M'aanyɛnkofo daa daa nyina,
Na Ɔwo me Nyɛnko mapa;
Woana bɛtsew me efi W' dɔ ho?

MHB 715
1 . W'ABASA dzen ntsi yehyira Wo, hɛn egyanom Nyame;
Ɔwo dze Wo poma na W'abaa abɔ 
W'akwantufo ho ban;
Ɔwo afrɛ hɛn akɔ kwan a ekyingyefo enntu da ho;
W'abasa dzen ntsi yehyira Wo, hɛn egyanom Nyame.

MHB 715
2 . Christ No dɔ a osiw kwan, ka akoma bɔ mu no ntsi,
Nokwar gyedzi na fahodzi a wɔdze yɛɛ hɔn edwuma ntsi,
