Nyankopɔn Nsɛmpa n'asomdwee a wɔdze nantsewee ntsi,
W'abasa dzen ntsi yehyira Wo, hɛn egyanom Nyame.

MHB 715
3 . Yɛyɛ kandzea bi a onndum da ho aweɔmfo mapa;
Yɛyɛ afɔrmbukyia ho ahwɛdofo a ebɛn hɛn;
Yɛyɛ Wo fahodzi mba a yɛdeda famu;
W'abasa dzen ntsi yehyira Wo, hɛn egyanom Nyame.

MHB 715
4 . Ma W'enyim no sunsuma no ntwa hɛn mpasuar no ho nyia;
Fa akokodur a edze maa ewuakɔr no bɔ hɛn esu;
O fa hɛn dua kwan a W'ahotsewfo duaa mu no mu;
W'abasa dzen ntsi yehyira Wo, hɛn egyanom Nyame.

MHB 716
1 . NOKWAR na dͻ Nyame,
Yɛhwehwɛ W’akwan pa;
Yɛgye Wo pɛ to mu,
Yɛyɛ setsie ma Wo:
Bɛhɛn Wo nyansaa kwan no mu,
Yengyaa hɛn pɛ mma Wo dɛw mu.

MHB 716
2 . ’Bɛn ntsi na edze hɛn
Aba ha ber yi mu?
’Bɛn ntsi na ’dze hɛn aba
Dɛ yenhu hɛn enyim?
Yɛdze dͻ na tsema ka bͻ m’
Ma yaabͻ mu kor wͻ Wo mu?

MHB 716
3 . Ana annyɛ hɛn kor,
Dɛ yɛmbͻ mu kor daa,
Yaabͻ mu anantsew,
Yaatsé obiara ne yaw;
Ama yeehu Wo papayɛ,
Na yaasoɛr ͻdͻ emudzi mu?

MHB 716
4 . Dɛm a horn mma hɛn enyi ‘
Ntsim siar ewiei no do,
Na yɛmbͻ mu yɛmper,
Yɛnko nkͻ hɛn enyim;
Yɛmfa ayamuyie mboa hɛnho,
Dɛ yebenyà ahenkyɛw hyɛnhyɛnn n’.

MHB 716
5 . O ma Wo Sunsum nsͻw
Hɛn akra ano da no,
Fa W’amayɛ dom hɛn,
Na fa hɛn fi ha kͻ
Hɛn onnyiewie ahomgye mu,
Fa hɛn kͻ hɛn Pomfo No bo m’.

MHB 717
1 . O EWURADZE, boa hɛn ma
Yɛmboa hɛnho nkorkor;
Ma obiara mboa ne nyɛnko,
Yennya tsema mma hɛnho.

MHB 717
2 . Boa hɛn ma yɛmboa hɛn mfɛfo,
Kakra a yɛwɔ nyɛ yie;
Gyedzi na enyidar nsi pi,
Yendzi mu wɔ dɔ mu.

MHB 717
3 . Hɛn Wura tseasefo, ma yɛmbɛn W',
Adze nyina m' yennyin,
Nkɛpem dɛ asan hɛn ho koraa,
Ma nkekaa nnyi hɛn ho.

MHB 717
4 . Na edwumason bɔ adze a,
Fa W'ayefor kɔ fie;
Ma yɛnye ahotsewfo nyina
Eedzi dɛw wɔ heaven.

MHB 718
1 . JESUS, yehwɛ Woara,
Yɛgye W’anohoba n’;
Ͻwo bɛba hɛn finimfin,
Sɛ yehyia Wo dzin mu a.

MHB 718
2 . Yɛrébɛgyé ato m’ wͻ ha
Dɛ Wo dzin yɛ nkwagye;
Wo dzin yɛ nkwa na asomdwee,
Ͻyɛ onnyiewiei dͻ.

MHB 718
3 . Yehyia gye adom a 
Ͻwo dzé ama hɛn kwa n’;
Wo ntsi na yehyia mu ase ha,
Ama yeehyia heaven.

MHB 718
4 . Yenyim dɛ ewͻ ha,
O yi Woho edzi kyérɛ!
Afei, Ewuradze, ma akoma
Biara nnya awérɛkyekyer.

MHB 718
5 . Ma Wo ndzé a okenyan n’
Nyi owu n’ bͻn mfi hͻ nkͻ;
Na ma hɛn akra enyi ngye
Enyidar dͻ mapa m’. Amen.

MHB 719
1 . HWԐ Jesu, hwɛ W’esuafo no,
Pon W’anohoba no;
Yeehyia Wo dzin m’ rohwɛ Wo kwan,
Ma Wo nhyira no mbra.

MHB 719
2 . Yɛtweͻn W’, Ewuradze nokwafo,
Yɛbͻ m’ kor wͻ Wo dzin m';
Yɛtweͻ, dɛ mbrɛ W’asɛm no tse n’,
Dɛ yebohu W’ hɛn ntamu.

MHB 719
3 . Enye hɛn ehyia mu wͻ ha;
Ewuradze, yi W’ho kyérɛ!
Tseasefo Nyame Ba, pue ha!
Ma yɛntse W’ nka wͻ ha.

MHB 719
4 . Ma yenhu Nyia yehwehwɛ no!
Jesus a wokum Wo,
Fa Wo nsa, W’anan m’ bͻgya n’ kyérɛ,
Ͻwo a hɛn ntsi iwui.

MHB 719
5 . Ma hɛn nsa nka kyerɛwsɛm no,
Kasa na kyérɛ biribi;
Mma nnye okyingyefo, gye Me dzi,
Emi a muwui maa wo!

MHB 72
1 . ME kra, hyɛ ɔsor ndwom bi ase;
Me ndze, nyan na tow ndwom,
Hɛn domankoma Hen n' ndwuma akɛse, 
Ne dzin kɛse ho ndwom.

MHB 72
2 . Ka No nokwar nwanwa n' ho asɛm, 
Na ma No tum ntahye;
Tow N'adom anohoba ho ndwom,
Nyame nkenyan asɛm n'.

MHB 72
3 . Bɔ Ewuradze nkwagye n' dawur
Ma akɔhweaban a woruwu:
Ɔdze akyerɛw dze dua a ɔnnsɛɛ da, 
Akyerɛw asɛm krɔnkrɔn n'.

MHB 72
4 . N'anohoba kɛse n' hyerɛn 
Dɛ ɔwɔ ayewa do;
na sum m' 'tumfo nnkotum apepa
Akyerɛw a ɔwɔ hɔ daa n'.

MHB 72
5 . N'adom asɛm biara yɛ dzen
Tse dɛ dza ɔdze bɔɔ sor;
N-dze a ɔdandan nworaba no,
Ka anohaba nsɛm nyina.

MHB 72
6 . M'akoma a atɔ bahaw dze dɛw
Hu dɛ W'adom tsim hɔ;
Motwer ndze a ɔbɔɔ adze nyina,
Na onnhia gyedzi bio.

MHB 720
1 . Christ a nhyira nyina fir Wo, 
Ema ahosewfo dzi mu,
Tsie hɛn a Wo su sɛ hɛn,
Yɛyɛ Wo honam nwanwa n'.

MHB 720
2 . Ka hɛn ho wɔ sunsum korm', 
Ma yɛnda ho nya Wodze n';
Yɛba bebisa mbordo,
Ɔwo a ehyɛ adze nyina ma.

MHB 720
3 . Kenyan, nunu na gya hɛn  
Kyɛn ankorankor akyɛdze,
Wɔahyehyɛ n' dɛ mbrɛ epɛ,
Ma hɛn ndwuma nyina nhyɛ ma.

MHB 720
4 . Dɛw mu ara yɛnyɛ kor 
Yennya tsema mma hɛnto:
Na yɛmboa hɛnho nkorkor;
Obiara nyɛ n'afamudze.

MHB 720
5 . Ɔdɔ tse dɛ wu, ɔasɛɛ 
Mpaapaamu na adehyesɛm nyina
Edzin, ekuw nyina gu
Christ yɛ adze nyinam' adze nyina.

MHB 721
1 . JESUS, W'adom no ka hɛn bɔ m'
Na yɛdodɔ hɛnho a,
Yɛdze awerɛhyɛm' hwehwɛ W'enyim,
Yenyim dɛ itsie hɛn asɔr.

MHB 721
2 . Ma yɛnda ho nnya hɛn Nyame,
Yɛnsoa W' kɔndua haahar n',
Ɔdɔ ahoma mbɔho ebisa a 
Wonnkotum atsew mu.

MHB 721
3 . Ma yɛnnom nkɔ sunsum kor mu;
Bɔ hɛn esu wɔ Wo dzin m';
Na daa yɛndwen ahobrɛadze m',
Na dua dɛw mu kasa.

MHB 721
4 . Wo dɔ a ɔtwetwe hɛn bɛn Wo n'
Ma yenya akoma kor;
Ma daa yɛntwetwe mbɛn hɛnho,
Na yɛntwe mbɛn Wo daa.

MHB 721
5 . Ka hɛn sunsum nyina fam Wo ho,
Mma mpaapaamu mmba da;
O ma hɛn nyina nnya Wo mu
Ɔdɔ ho adwen no daa.

MHB 721
6 . Iyi nye nkabɔm' pa a ho tsew,
W'adɔyɛ a fi nnyi ho;
Ma yennya adwen a ɔwɔ Wo mu n',
O ma yɛnsɔr dɛm daa.   Amen.

MHB 722
1 . HOM mfa akoma ngyina sor ndzɛmba do,
’Guambaa N’akadofo,
Hom nsuo m’ ma yɛntonton No dͻ,
Yɛnhyɛ Ne dzin enyimnyam.

MHB 722
2 . Hom ntow ndwom, ndaase m’ mma Ne dzin,
Ͻno a N’adom mmbͻ adze:
Dzi dɛw! Dzi dɛw! ‘Wuradze yɛ ͻhen;
Ͻhen n’ yɛ hɛn Nyɛnko!

MHB 722
3 . ’No ntsi biribiara yɛ ahwerdze;
Yemmbu wiadze ’i mu hwee.
Yɛsoa mbeamudua no wͻ enyigye m’ ,
Gyedɛ yeenya ahenkyɛw n’.

MHB 722
4 . Ma yenkenyan hɛnho nkorkor,
Hɛn ndwuma nkyérɛ hɛn gyedzi,
Yendua krͻnkrͻn enyidado m’,
Nà ͻdͻ dɛɛdɛw ndwuma do.

MHB 722
5 . Yɛkͻ do dwen wo ho daa daa,
Ͻwo a ekotow Jesus;
Tsérɛw wo gyedzi na mpaabͻ abaw m’,
Na hwɛ, yɛabɛn w’ sesei.

MHB 722
6 . Wodze nyɛ ehumbͻbͻr, asomdwee,
Ondu adwen nyina mu,
Mannà a wͻdzé esuma na nkwa dua n’,
Ͻnyé ͻbo fitaa no.

MHB 722
7 . Wͻmfa nhyira nyina mma wo,
Dza Nyame na Christ ma;
Yɛsérɛ dɛ hen Hen No Sunsum
Mbra akoma nokwafo m’.

MHB 722
8 . Tweͻn dɛ Ewuradze bɛbà enyimnyam m’.
Tweͻn nya heaven m’ kyɛfa;
Hɛn Pomfo n’ risiesie hɛn fie:
Kͻ do; yebehyia m’ hͻ.

MHB 723
1 . HƐN tsetse egyanom Nyame, tsie,
Ma yenhu W' nokwar ehumbɔbɔr n',
Yɛnam Jesus No mu bɛn Wo,
Wo Dɔba a oruhu amandze n',
No m' na yehu W'enyim fɛɛfɛw n',
No mu na menam sɔ W'enyi.

MHB 723
2 . Yɛdze awɔse gyedzi bɔ afɔr,
Yɛma do kyerɛ W'enyimnyam n',
Hɛn enyidar nyina n' kutuwdo - bo n',
Bɔgyahue afɔrbɔ a ɔsom bo n',
Ɔdze W'adom brɛ abɔn wɔ ase,
Ɔma hɛn akra nyina bɔ m' dzi mu.

MHB 723
3 . Wɔnam Ne dzin m' nko gye hɛn to m',
No bɔgyaa m' yenya bɔnfakyɛ,
Yɛnam No do bisa nkwa pa,
Ɔno a owui dze gyee hɛn akra,
Ɔdze No bɔgyaa tseew hɛn ho,
Na ɔdze Nyame bra hyɛ hɛn ma.

MHB 723
4 . Egya, hwɛ Wo Ba a oruwu n',
Na tsie bɔgya a ɔkasa sor n';
Na ma W'adom nyin mbra hɛn do;
Asomdwee, tsenenee, dɛw na dɔ,
Dza ewɔ nyina, na mbrɛ etsie biara,
W'ahenman mbra akoma biara m'.  Amen.

MHB 724
1 . JESUS, nkwa nà enyimnyam Wura,
Brɛ W’adom aso n’ edze daa,
Bér a hɛn akra rotweͻn asͻr Wo ’i,
Abͻnfo adamfo, tsie hɛn:
      Ewuradze pa,
      Fa W’ehumbͻbor gye hɛn!

MHB 724
2 . Fi wiadze enyifura bͻn n’ mu,
Fi bͻn a epirim no tum mu,
Fi ewurkadze na etsiͻdzen mu,
Fi akoma m’ ahokyérɛ mu:

MHB 724
3 . Bér a nsͻhwɛ mu ayɛ dzen no,
Ma Abͻnsam kyérɛ no tum no,
Wͻ hɛn ahohia ber no mu,
Dͻnhwér a ͻyɛ sum, yɛ dzen mu:

MHB 724
4 . Bér a wiadze nyina resérew no,
Ahonya na asetséna pa m’,
Hɛn akoma twe bɛn wiadze dɛw n’,
Wͻ ahoͻdzen na asomdwee da m’:

MHB 724
5 . Yarba dͻnhwér a ͻyɛ bérɛ mu,
Ͻhaw na ͻyaw ber mu,
Ber a yɛtse honam mberɛwyɛ,
Ber a abͻdze mboa yɛ kwa n’:

MHB 724
6 . Owu dͻnhwer mu kommyɛ mu n’,
Atsɛmbu da huuhu mu n’.
Ma hɛn akra, bér a wͻtwer Wo no,
Mfa W’ nyɛ enyidar na tsénabea.

MHB 725
1 . HԐN Wura, W'ehumbͻbͻr da  ‘i,
Ansaanà obotwa m’ akͻ n’,
Yɛhwe W’anànadze sͻr Wo.

MHB 725
2 . Jesus krͻnn, pa hɛn nyinsu,
Fa akoma m' suro hyɛ hɛn mà:
Ansaana da huuhu n’ aba.

MHB 725
3 . Yɛkotow W'abow ekyir yi,
Hue Wo Sunsum gu hɛn do,
Ansaana atow m’ afehͻͻ.

MHB 725
4 . W’ahoyera anago n'.
Wo nkotͻserɛ su no ntsi.
Dɛ epɛ dɛ ’bowu n’ ntsi.

MHB 725
5 . Wo nyinsu wenwen a ikyii
Maa Jerusalem ha n’ ntsi,
Mma mma Wo dͻ no mmbͻ hɛn.

MHB 725
6 . Hɛn Tsɛmbuafo na Gyefo,
Yehu W' enyim na enyim a,
Dom hɛn W'atsaban ase tséna.

MHB 726
1 . GYEFO, wɔ huntuma mu na
Yɛdze nkotoserɛ sɔr Wo;
Ber a nnuhofo yenntum mma
Hɛn nyinsuwa enyi nnhwɛ sor;
O yaw na mbusu a edze
Hun amandze maa nyimpa ntsi,
Bɔ W' mu adze fi ahengua enyim,
Tsie hɛn mbɔbɔr nkotɔserɛ.

MHB 726
2 . Wo mbofraber m' botooyɛ,
Wo hia na nyinsu bra ntsi,
W'ahokyer yaayaw nda no,
Wo mbusu sar no do ntsi,
Osian dɔnhwer huuhu no a
Satan sɔɔ W' hwɛ wɔ mu n' ntsi,
Dan, O dan W'adɔe enyi n',
Tsie hɛn mbɔbɔr nkotɔserɛ.

MHB 726
3 . Yaw krɔnkrɔn a 'dze kyii nyinsu
Wɔ Lazarus ne nda do ntsi,
Nkuranhyɛ nyinsu a ɔpemee
Guu Salem do tsenabea n',
Adwembɔn a osii W' nkorɔfo ntamu
Ma hɔn enyim towee ntsi,
Fi Wo sor tsenabea hɔ 
Tsie hɛn mbɔbɔr nkotɔserɛ.

MHB 726
4 . W'abawpa dɔnhwer no ntsi,
Na W'ahoguan mpaabɔ ntsi,
Mbeamudua, mprɛgow na nsoɛ n' ntsi,
Peaa ne yaw na enyimtsiabu,
Sum kebii a ɔhyɛɛ no ntsi,
W'afɔrbɔ huuhu no ntsi
Tsie hɛn mbrɛhoadze sufrɛ,
Tsie hɛn mbɔbɔr nkotserɛ.

MHB 726
5 . Pen dzendzen a ɔdze W' kɔr wu m',
Ɔbo adakamaa no ntsi,
Samanadze sunkamm a oenntum
Enndzi Nyame a ɔsoɛree do n';
O Nyame Tumfo a wɔdze W'
Fi asaase do asan kɔ sor,
Ewuradze, tsie, tsie hɛn su
Wɔ hɛn mbɔbɔr nkotɔserɛ m'

MHB 727
1 . Jesus, 'nye W' Asɔr ntsena, 
Yɛ n' Agyenkwa, Wura, Gyafo;
Wɔrosɔ ne gyedzi ahwɛ n',
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

MHB 727
2 . Tsew ne bra na nkyerɛkyerɛ ho; 
Dom n' abotar ma ɔnsɔw
Na ɔntwer W' anohoba n',
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

MHB 727
3 . Ma ne ndze nyɛ wansa daa; 
Ɔmbɔ nkaa wɔ atsɛmbu ho;
Ɔnka Agyenkwa pa ho nsɛm,
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

MHB 727
4 . Tsetsew ne nkyehoma mu; 
Tseam ma ko na 'nyiber ngyaa;
Dom no ɔsor asomdwee n',
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

MHB 727
5 . Ongya ehiafo na efurafo, 
Nda ho nhwehwɛ dza ayew n',
Ɔnkyekyer 'koma bobɔe,
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

MHB 727
6 . No nokwar kanea n' nhyerɛn; 
Ɔmma ne kan n' do wɔ sor
Wɔ abosom-man sum mu.
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

MHB 727
7 . Ma ne nyimdzi nyɛ krɔnkrɔn; 
Ɔnka bɔn no dɔm nyina ngu;
Ɔmboa aman nyina ngu;
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.    Amen.

MHB 728
1 . MBƆBƆRHUFO, Nyame Tumfo!
Wo dɔ na tsema nnyi ewiei!
Kyerɛkyerɛ hɛn wɔ W'enyim daa ma
Yɛmbɔ hɛn bra mma Wo.

MHB 728
2 . Ɔwo a 'bowuu wɔ asaase 'i do
Ma nyimpa aafa do enya nkwa,
O tsie hɛn, 'Wo na yesu frɛ W'
Enyidado m', Nyame.

MHB 728
3 . Kyerɛkyerɛ hɛn Wo nkyerɛkyerɛsɛm no,
Yɛntse mma hɔn a W' bɔgyaa atɔ hɔn,
Ma asɛm, ndzeyɛɛ, adwen biara
Aayɛ edwuma ama Wo.

MHB 728
4 . Hɛn nyina yɛ enuanom wɔ wiadze,
Dɛ Ɔwo iwuu maa hɛn ntsi;
Kyerɛ hɛn, mbrɛ ɔtse biara,
Ma yɛndɔ hɔn Wo mu.

MHB 728
5 . Yarba m', yaw mu, ohia m', dadwen m',
Mbrɛ ɔtse biara, ɔyɛ hɛndze;
Ma yɛmboa bea a wohia mboa no,
Dɛ yɛdze rema Wo.

MHB 728
6 . Na ma Wo Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn no
Nka hɔn a wɔtsena dɔ mu nyina,
Kodu dɛ hɔn a wɔtse Wo mu
Behyia m' wɔ sor ahenman m'.  Amen

MHB 729
1 . HƐN Wura, nye hɛn nkwagyefo Nyankopɔn,
Hɛn anago woraba nye aman enyidar,
Tsie na gye W'asɔr hɔn mbɔbɔr nkotɔserɛ,
Ewuradze Tumfo.

MHB 729
2 . Hwɛ ehum dzendzen a otwa
W'Ahyɛm'-daka n' ho,
Hwɛ mbrɛ W'atamfo si tserɛw hɔn frankaa mu;
Ewuradze, ber a wɔtow hɔn bɔwema n',
'Botum akora hɛn.

MHB 729
3 . Nyame, wiadze akodze sa a, 'botum aboa;
Nyame, bɔn ruku hɛn a, 'botum agye nkwa;
Nyame, Wo botan do, 'wu anaa hɛll nnyi tum;
Dom hɛn W'asomdwee.

MHB 729
4 . Dom hɛn Wo mboa ma atamfo nsan hɔn ekyir,
Dom hɔn Wo nokwar ama wɔdze aakyɛ hɔn;
Ma asaase asomdwee, na hɛn aperdzi ekyir no,
Wo heaven asomdee. Amen.

MHB 73
1 . Me Nyame, mbrɛ 'dua yɛ nwanwa a 
W' ahentum ne hyerɛn a!
Wo mbɔbɔrhu egua n' ne fɛw a
Wɔ kan a ɔhyerɛn mu!

MHB 73
2 . Wo mfe a ɔmmbɔ adze n' no hu a, 
Domankoma Ewuradze,
Esunsum wotwa hwe W' enyim
Tonton Wo daa nyina.

MHB 73
3 . Mbrɛ odua yɛ fɛw, yɛ fɛw a, 
Dɛ yebohu W' enyim
Wo nyansaa bun n', Wo tum kɛse n'
Nyame W' ahotsew nwanwa.

MHB 73
4 . Ao Nyame, mbrɛ misi suro Wo a, 
Suro a no mu dɔ,
Na medze ahopopo enyidar,
Nnuhu nyinsu som Wo!

MHB 73
5 . Ma mo so maadɔ W', Ewuradze, 
Ɔwo a 'yɛ Tumfo yi,
Abɔ Wo mu adze ebisa
M' akoma brɛfo no dɔ.

MHB 73
6 . Egya bi nnyɛ dɔ dɛ Ɔwo; 
Na bi nndwe dɛ Ɔwo,
Wonnyi abotar dɛ mbrɛ ewɔ n'
Emi babɔn yi ho.

MHB 73
7 . Jesus N' egya, dɔ n' akatua, 
Na enyigye bɛn a
Dɛ m' botwa ahwe W' ahengua enyim,
Mahwɛ Wo, na mahwɛ W' !

MHB 730
1 . ADOM a onnsa da Egya,
Yɛkamfo W‘adͻe na nokwar.
Yɛkyérɛ: W’adͻyɛ nye nokwar,
Wo Ba n' N'enyidzi ntsi ama
Akyɛdzé a onnyi kabeà esian.
N-kwa Sunsum, tum nye ͻdͻ.

MHB 730
2 . Fa Wo Ba n' No Sunsum brɛ hɛn
Ma woeehu Nyametsir n' no bun.
Na yeenya Wo nkwa n‘ mu kyefa;
Soma N' ma ͻmbɛpɛtse bͻgya n',
Soma N' mà ͻmbɛtsew hɛn akra ho,
Ma ͻnkyérɛ, nsͻw hɛn ano dɛ W‘dze daa.

MHB 730
3 . Dɛm na yɛbͻ mpaa, yenngyaa da.
Na yɛdze ndaase kà hɛn bͻn.
Wo nymsaa, nokwar, tum na dͻ n';
Yɛdze dɛw a onnyi kabeà aasͻr,
Na yeehyira W', yoeyi W' ayɛ daa,
Yaasom W’ dɛ mbrɛ Wo sor dͻm som W'.

MHB 730
4 . Yɛbͻfora sor adwontofo kuw n’,
Yɛama bɛn konyimdzi ndwom n' do
Kɛse na yeeyi Wo ayɛw,
Yeetu akͻ sor akyɛn nkan seraph,
Na yenye kan m’ 'nyɛnkofo nyina
Aatow Wo dͻ à onnyi ewiei ho ndwom.
		Amen.

MHB 731

MHB 732

’Nafua nyina.

Biara do.

MHB 735

MHB 736
1 . Guanhwɛfo pa, dom hɛn Wo mboa 
Wɔ hɛn mbusu nda yim',
Tum a wɔdze weɔn, wɔdze sɔr,
Fa ma Wo mba nyina.

MHB 736
2 . Ber a yɛda ho da nsɔhwɛm', 
Ber a yɛso mbeamudua 'i,
Ma yɛmfa hɛn kra nto Wo do
Wɔ mpaabɔ a ɔmmbɔ adzem'.

MHB 736
3 . Ma yendua gyedzim' hɛn nsa nka 
M-paabɔ sunsum no;
Yemmia ndzi ako gyedɛ yehu
W' enyim nye Wo dzin pa n'.

MHB 736
4 . Ma 'koma biara nsu nka dɛ: 
Minnkegyaa Wo ma akɔ,
Gyedɛ ama m' dɔ a odzi mu,
Na edze Woho akyɛ m'.

MHB 736
5 . Minnkegyaa Wo ma akɔ gyedɛ 
Ebɔ Wo dzin kyerɛ m',
Na egye me kra nkwa nwionn nwionn,

MHB 736

Wɔ adzehu nye ayɛyim'.  Amen.

MHB 737
1 . JESU, yɛma hɛn akoma do ma W';
Ma ɔdɔ mbu hɛn akoma nyina do,
Yɛda W' ase, daa akyɛdze n' ntsi 
Yɛda ho nyim W' dzin a ɔsom bo n',
Yenyim dɛ edze hɛn bɔn kyɛ hɛn 
Na yɛtweɔn heaven a ɔwɔ hɛn mu n'.

MHB 737
2 . Ɔhaw kɛse bi a edze akyerɛ
W'ekyirdzifo a wɔasɔ hɛn ahwɛ a!

Yehun dɛ epue nsuyirii mu,
Yɛtsee nka dɛ 'gyina gyaframee m',
Na yɛkaa m' bɔɔ hɛn Pomfo N' dzin.

MHB 737

Hɔn enyi gye W'enyimnyam ho,
Wobu mbeamudua 'nyimguase n' bi,
Wɔhwehwɛ nkamfo a ofir Egya n'.

MHB 737
4 . Ɔwo a ahwɛ hɛn do ebodu ndɛ,

Hɛn Jesus besian abɛfa
N'anyɛnkofo na adasefo,
Akɛtsena 'nyimnyam ahengua n' do.  Amen.

MHB 738
1 . Kenyan W' edwuma yi,

Na ma Wo nkorɔfo ntse.
    Kenyan W' edwuma yi, 
    Ber a yɛkotow Wo yi, 
    Sian, ao Ewuradze domfo, sian! 
    Bra behyira hɛn sesei.

MHB 738
2 . Kenyan W' edwuma yi, 
Ma akra nhwehwɛ nkwa-su n':
O ma hɛn esunsum kɔn ndɔ
N-kwa edziban no!

MHB 738
3 . Kenyan W' edwuma yi, 
Krɔn W' enyimnyam dzin no;

MHB 738

MHB 738

MHB 739
1 . HƐN Egya, tsie hɛn mpaabɔ yi,
Boa ma mpaabɔ yi mpem,
Na ma adwen brɛfo a ofir Wo n',
Mbɛtsena hɛn mu na onyin.

MHB 739
2 . Akoma brɛfo no bɛtse
'Somdwee na dɛw n' ase,
Dza ɔwɔ Wo sor asetsena mu
'Homka wɔ W'enyi do.

MHB 739
3 . Ma hɛn ahobrɛadze ama
W'ahendzi aaba hɛn mu,
Na sɛ Wo mba no rokɔ fie a,
Hɛn so yaakɔ hɔ bi.

MHB 739
4 . Gyefo tsie hɛn! Yɛyɛ Wodze,
Sɛ yɛnntse dɛ Ɔwo mpo a;
Fa Wo Sunsum n' hyɛ akoma
Brɛfo a ɔtwer Wo mu.  Amen.

MHB 74
1 . AYƐYI nka sor Krɔnkrɔnyi,
Wonyi N'ayɛw wɔ ase:
Ne nsɛm a ɔyɛ nwanwa nyina m',
N'akwan nyina tsim hɔ.

MHB 74
2 . O hɛn Nyame Ne nyansa dɔ,
Bɔn na enyimguase mu,
Adam a ɔtɔ do ebien bae
Bɛgyee hɛn nyina fii mu.

MHB 74
3 . Nyansa dɔ! Honam, bɔgya a
'Hwee famu wɔ Adam mu n',
Bɛsan nye tamfo no aper,
Bɛper edzi konyim.

MHB 74
4 . Akyɛdze kɛse a ɔkyen adom
Ntsew honam, bɔgya ho;
Nyame ankasa nye No su
Na odzi dɛm dwuma n'.

MHB 74
5 . Ɔdɔ ayamuyie nye yi,
Dɛ Nyia ɔsɛɛ tamfo n'
Nyimpa n'amandzehu mprɛnu n',
Noara so duaa mu bi.

MHB 74
6 . Nsumaa mu, wɔ turo no mu,
Na mbeamudua no do so,
Ɔkyerɛɛ No nuamom, hyɛɛ hɔn dzen, 
Wɔ amandzehu na wu m'.

MHB 74
7 . Ayɛyi nka sor Krɔnkrɔnyi,
Wonyi N'ayɛw wɔ ase:
Ne nsɛm a ɔyɛ nwanwa nyina m',
N'akwan nyina tsim hɔ.

MHB 740
1 . NYIMPA nyinà Egya, yɛdze
Dͻ akoma bͻ Wo mpaa,
’Nam Nyià ama N’ mbͻbͻrhu,
Nkwa, nokwar ͻkwan do;
Fi sor ahengua do hue W’adom
Na Wo nhyira N’ gu hɛn etsir do.

MHB 740
2 . Nyimpa nyinà Egya, yɛdze
Akomà a yaw ahyɛ n’ mà,
Bͻn na yaw biara nnyi m’,
Tow Wo ayɛyi ndwom;
Hom Wo mfar no gu hɛn mu daa,
Ma yɛmfa ntow ndwom pa mma Wo.

MHB 740
3 . Nyimpa nyinà Egya, yɛdze
Suro a ommpue gu ahom
Fi hɛn akoma bun mu,
Ͻnnkasa, nyinsu nko;
Suo hɛn nsamu twa mbusu bea mu,
Egya, gyà ͻba biara a ͻtwer Wo.

MHB 740
4 . Nyimpa nyinà Egya, yɛdze
Hɛn ngyirama yi W’ ayɛw,
Bér a dɛw hyɛ hɛn akra mà
Nà enyigyé a no mu dͻ;
Ehum nà aahow mu ma yenhu
Asomdwee kwàn a ͻdze ba W' nkyɛn.
		Amen.

MHB 741
1 . YENNHUN Wo dɛ mbrɛ ɔfata,
Yennsuaa W'adom, nyansa na tum;
Wiadze egyapadze na ber yi m'
Ndzɛmba ahyɛ hɛn adwen ma;
Ewuradze, ma yenhu W' nokwar n;
Yɛ hɛn enyansafo ma yenhu W'.

MHB 741
2 . Yensuroo Wo dɛ mbrɛ ɔfata,
Yɛmmbɔɔ hɛn mu adze wɔ W'enyim,
Yɛnnkoraa ndzeyɛɛ, kasa na adwen,
Ber a yɛkaa dɛ Nyame bɛn hɛn;
Ewuradze, ma yenhu dɛ ebɛn,
Na ma hɛn suro mapa ho adom.

MHB 741
3 . Yɛnndɔɔ Wo dɛ mbrɛ ɔfata,
Na ammfa hɛn ho dɛ Ɔwo dɔ hɛn;
Yɛnnhwehwɛɛ bɛn a ebɛn hɛn n' yie,
Hɛn kɔn nndɔ yie dɛ yebohu W';
Ewuradze, ma hɛn akoma a m' tsew
Ma yenhu dɛ Ɔwo nye ɔdɔ n'.

MHB 741
4 . Yɛnnsoom Wo dɛ mbrɛ ɔfata,
Ebei! Yɛannyɛ hɛn asɛdze no,
Edwuma n' so yɛayɛ n' bi-na-bi,
Yeedzi 'kogu; hɛn konyim nnye!
Ewuradze, ma hɛn mbanyinndam,
Yɛmfona mma W', yɛnko mma Wo.

MHB 741
5 . Ber bɛn na yebohu Wo yie,
Yeesuro Wo, yɛasom Wo yie?
Wobeyi hɛn nsɔhwɛ m' ber bɛn
Ma yeedzi mu kan asaase n' do?
Hɛn Wura, ma daa yɛnyɛ ahoboa,
Nhu W'enyim na yɛnsom W' wɔ hɔ.  Amen

MHB 742
1 . YԐBϽϽ mpaa dɛ W’ahendzi mbra,
Mfe a etwa m’ yebuu ntwɛr;
Akrà anokwafo pɛ ehu
Ahendzi n’ saase do.

MHB 742
2 . Naaso anafua weͻn nyaa no,
Onnye mma Nyame koraa,
Na komm nworaba no yɛ dzen
Ma kyɛfa afebͻͻ.

MHB 742
3 . Hwɛ, wͻwͻ akoko n’ do dada,
Adzekyee mfrankaa pue,
Nkͻnhyɛfo, hom mbͻ hom asen do,
Hom nkà dɛ da n’ abɛn:

MHB 742
4 . Da no a ne kan bɛhyerɛn petee n’,
Bͻn nyina bɛdà edzi,
Ber a pɛrpɛr betsim hͻ pintsinn,
Na yaw biarà efi hͻ.

MHB 742
5 . Nyimdzee nye asomdwee bͻ mu a,
Nà okyin wiadze do hyia;
Tsenenee a odzi mu da no,
Nyame anohoba da n’.

MHB 743
1 . ƆNNYƐ hɛn bɔn nko ntsi
Na yɛserɛ W' mbɔbɔrhu;
Fa W' mbɔbɔrhu enyi
Hwɛ hɛn adzeserɛ yi
Wɔ dza yɛayɛ ama Wo
Na dza yɛdwen ho yɛ.

MHB 743
2 . Yɛdze mber krɔnkrɔn no
Bu nkotodwe bɔ mpaa,
Mber a yesusu dɛ
Hɛn ndwom bɔsɔ W'enyi
Ɔwo a 'hwehwɛ akoma m',
Dom hɔn W'ehumbɔbɔr.

MHB 743
3 . Na akyɛdze a yɛdze brɛ W',
Anohoba a yɛbɔ
Ɔdɔ ndwuma nyina a
Ɔwo ntsi yɛhyehyɛ n',
Ehumbɔbɔr Nyame,
Fa kɔ adwendwen mu.

MHB 743
4 . Nkanka hɛn Wo nguan kuw
Ba W'afɔrmbukyia enyim a,
Na adwenbɔn a ɔyɛ hu 
Nye mber dɛɛdɛw dzi afora a,
Nyia a owui ntsi yɛserɛ W',
Dɛ Owura pa, boa hɛn.

MHB 743
5 . Brɛ W'aso adze na tsie,
Bue W'enyiwa na hwɛ;
Hɛn dɔ yɛ enyimguase;
Ɔsɛ dɛ yɛba W' nkyɛn,
Yɛyɛ n' dɛ W'adom tse,
Yɛ no dɛ mbrɛ epɛ.

MHB 744
1 . Ahomka da ɔnye da n' a 
Medze moho maa m' Agyenkwa!
Ɔsɛ dɛ mo 'koma dzi dɛw
Na ɔka ne dɛw kyerɛ aman.

  Ahomka da! ahomka da! 
  Da a Jesus hoor mo ho bɔn nyina 
  Ɔkyerɛɛ m' dɛ monweɔn na monsɔr 
  Na mindzi dɛw aber nyina 
  Ahomka da! ahomka da! 
  Da a Jesus hoor mo ho bɔn nyina!

MHB 744
2 . Siar n-hyehyɛɛ! ɔsɔw nsew a 
Midzii kyerɛɛ mo Dɔfo n' ano!
Ber a meba N' asɔrfim' yi,
Wɔmma ayɛyindwom nhyɛ hɔ ma.

MHB 744
3 . Ahyɛmu kɛse no yeewie dzi! 
Mo Wura dze nye m', No so yɛ medze;
Ɔtwetwee m' ma mekaa No do,
Ne Nyame ndze n' ɔyɛ me dɛw.

MHB 744
4 . M' akoma a ekyima akyɛr 
Bɔhom wɔ ahomka bea ha:
Mma mmfi w' Ewuradze nkyɛn da
Afa N' a, afa siar nyina.

MHB 744
5 .  Sor man nyina a hom tsee me nsew n, 
M' besi do daa ma hom aatse,
Akɛpem da a owu bɛba a
M' behyira me kra wɔ nsew yi ho.

MHB 745
1 . WϽNKAMFO hɛn pomfo Ewuradze,
N’adom kà hɛn bͻ mu,
Ͻhyɛ hɛn nyina dɛ yɛnyɛ kor;
Yɛbͻ m’ hwehwɛ N’enyim.

MHB 745
2 . Ͻhyɛ hɛn dɛ yɛmboa hɛnho;
Na yɛbͻ mu yɛ kor,
Hɛn enyidar frɛ a ͻkrͻn,
Yetu anamͻn kͻ enyim.

MHB 745
3 . Akyɛdzé a ͻdze ma nkorkor n’,
Yɛdze dͻ bͻsͻ ahwɛ;
Adom pem fa kuraba biara m’,
Wͻ dͻ esu a odzi mu m’.

MHB 745
4 . M-po yɛdwen, ka asɛm kor,
Na nokwar mu yɛpen;
Nam Jesus dzin mu ba fakor.
Wͻ koryɛ a odzi mu m’.

MHB 745
5 . Yɛbͻ m’ yenya enyigye kor,
Tse asomdwee kor nkà,
Asomdweé a wͻnntse n’ adwen mu.
Dɛw a onnyi kabea.

MHB 745
6 . Sɛ hɛn anyɛnkoyɛ wͻ famu ha
Wͻ Jesus mu yɛ dɛw a,
Yehyia mu ahengua no ho a,
Enyi bɛgye mbordo.

MHB 746
1 . OWURA, Wodze nye m’; matse Wo ndze,
Na ͻkàa Wo dͻ kyerɛɛ me;
Naaso mo kͻn dͻ dɛ mosoɛr gyedzi m’,
Na wͻbͻtwe me abɛn Wo.
   Twe me bɛn ho, bɛn ho siar Ewuradze;
   Kͻ mbeamuduà à iwui wͻ do n’ ho;
  Twe me bɛn ho, bɛn ho, siàr Ewuradze,
  Kͻ W’epirakur à ͻsom bo n ’ ho.

MHB 746
2 . Owura, tsew mo ho ma Wo som sesei.
Fa W’adom tum krͻnkrͻn no:
Ma me kra mfà enyidado a otsim hͻ.
Na me pɛ bɛhyɛ Wodze m’.

MHB 746
3 . O mber kakraabi no mu enyigyé a
Midzi wͻ W’ahengua enyim,
Menye W’ me Nyame, bu ntwɛr we mpaabͻ m’,
Dɛ nyɛnko nye nyɛnko hyia.

MHB 746
4 . Ͻdͻ ebun wͻ hͻ a munnkontum ehu,
Gyedɛ mutwa po tseàa no;
Dɛw nkokwaa wͻ hͻ a munnkotum edu
Kɛpem dɛ m’bͻhom Wo mu.

MHB 747
1 . NDAASE nkà Eguambaà a
Ͻma yehyia mu:
Yɛka N’ dͻ ho asɛm,
Yɛtow N’ayɛyi;
Jesus yɛ hɛndze daa,
Ͻbɛn hɛn dabaa,
Dze mfom kyɛ na ohyira hɛn,
Na ͻma yedzi mu.

MHB 747
2 . No mu wͻ asomdwee,
No mu yɛwͻ tum,
N’adom no kora hɛn
Wͻ anago sum no m’;
Hɛn nsͻhwɛ nyina mu no,
Ͻkora hɛn ma
Yehu No nkwagye na
No dͻ a odzi mu.

MHB 747
3 . ’Homado na ͻpɛ m’
Yeedua yi mu sͻnn;
Yefaa nsu na ogya m’ n’,
Ͻno nà ͻgyee hɛn;
Wiadze nɛ abͻnsam nsamu
Yedzi nyim we N’ mu;
Ͻyɛ hɛn Gyefo pa,
Ͻtse dɛm daapem.

MHB 747
4 . O yɛbɛyɛ dɛn
Yeedua hɛn Agyenkwa n’?
Nyame, fi sor bra
Bɛyɛ hɛn fofor:
Ma hɛn W’ayamuhyehye
Na krͻnkrͻnyɛ aba,
Ma hɛn nkwagye no a
Obiara gye dzi n’.

MHB 747
5 . Ka enyigyesɛm n’ kyerɛ,
Na yɛ hɛn adehye;
Sɛ nnyɛ Ͻwo Ewuradze a,
Me nhyira fi hen?
Asomdweé a edzé ama n’,
Ma me bi sesei,
Na bue Wo dͻ ahenman n’
Wͻ m’akoma mu.

MHB 747
6 . Christ, bra na besian
Dodopo gyirama,
Na kyerɛ hɛn so
Sunsum mu ndwom no;
Mma yenngyaa ara da dɛ
Yɛda W’adom ase,
Nye enyimnyam, na nhyira,
’Nyidzi na ayɛyi.

MHB 748
1 . HOM mbra na yɛmbͻ m’ yenyi
Christ ayɛw wͻ adwontow mu;
Hɛn nyina mbͻ mu nyɛ kor,
Mfà enyimnyam mma Ewuradze.

MHB 748
2 . Yɛmma nsa, akoma nye ndze do
Yɛntow ndwom dɛ tsetseber n’,
Yɛmfà adwen ntsim sor dɛw do,
Ndzi ͻdͻ afahyɛ no.

MHB 748
3 . Yedzi aper wͻ dͻ mu;
Ma ogyaframee no nkenyan
Dɛ mbrɛ ͻyɛɛ wͻ atͻfo n’ mu,
Wowui maa hͻn Nyankopͻn.

MHB 748
4 . Yɛbɛtséna, adͻ dɛ hͻn,
Dɛ yɛnda hͻn dɛw edzi;
Wͻagye hɛn nyina wͻ ebufuw m’,
Yɛnye hͻn bͻ m’, gyedzi kor m'.

MHB 748
5 . Yɛntow ndwom Jesus dzin mu,
Dɛ mbrɛ ͻtse wͻ ndeda;
Yɛyɛ kor wͻ beebiara,
Nokwar nyé adom ahyɛ hɛn mà.

MHB 748
6 . Yegyina ma Christ, hɛn wura,
Kan ma wiadze a ntseasee nnyi m':
Yedzi hɛn Wura ho dase;
Yedzi dase ma Jesus.

MHB 748
7 . Yedzi dase, Christ ewu,
Wͻabͻ hɛn nye N’ mbeamudua m’;
Christ atsew wu hu no mu,
Yɛhom Ne nkenyan Sunsum m’.

MHB 748
8 . Afei Christ afow kͻ sor,
Hɛn apɛdze nyina kͻ hͻ;
Ͻtse Nyankopͻn nyimfa,
Yɛnye N’ dzi hen wͻ dͻ mu.

MHB 749
1 . HOM mbra ma yɛmfa Nyamé adom,
Hɛn nyina nyɛ ano kor,
Yɛmbͻ m’ yɛnye hɛn Christ nyɛ kor
Yendzi ahyɛmu afebͻͻ:

MHB 749
2 . Jesu tum m’ , yɛdze hɛnho ma W’,
Hyɛ Ne dzin enyimnyam;
Yɛhyɛ bͻ dͻnhwer krͻnkrͻn yi m’,
Yɛatséna, yeewu Nyame m'.

MHB 749
3 . Ahyɛmu a yeridzi dem ber yi,
Yemfa nsie hɛn adwen m’ daa:
Yɛnnkapa hɛn Nyamé ara bio,
Yennkegya N'asɛm ekyir.

MHB 749
4 . Yennkegyaa Nyià a otsie hɛn nsewdzi n’
No ho suro n’ ekyir,
Na sɛ epɛ dɛ itsie hɛn a,
Sian, behyia hɛn sesei.

MHB 749
5 . Fa ahyɛm' bͻgya n’ ka obiara ho,
Ma onyi hɛn bͻn nyina nkͻ;
Na kyerɛw hɛn edzin Wͻ sor,
Kora hɛn kodu da no.              Amen.

MHB 75
1 . EGYA a Wo dɔ a onnyi ewiei
Dze Wo Ba kortsee n' maa abɔn,
W'adom a edze ma kwa no,
'Somaa No bɛgyee wiadze nkwa.

MHB 75
2 . Boa ma yɛnkamfo W'mbɔbɔrhu,
Ɔso, dɔ, ɔwɔ mbea nyina;
Yɛnkamfo Eguambaa a owui maa hɛn,
Adasa nyina Agyenkwa.

MHB 75
3 . Nyiyimu a ennyɛ no da n',
Edze sii Adam asehwefo do,
Na esiesie nkwagye adom a, odzi mu,
Ama obiara wɔ Christ mu.

MHB 75
4 . Ohun amandze dze gyee wiadze, 
Na ɔpataa maa obiara;
Ɔdze No nkwa so bɔɔ afɔr
Maa hɔn a wɔmmpɛ aba Ne nkyɛn

MHB 75
5 . Nyame, soɛr ma W'asɛm do,
Na frɛ amanaman nyina;
Ma Wo mbeamudua frankaa no do,
Na Wo wu n' bɛyɛ adasa dze.

MHB 750
1 . O NYAME, mpɛn pii na atse m’ su,
Na enam ehumbͻbͻr m’ etsie m’!
Bér a morosͻr W’afͻrmbukyia ho n’,
Musuu bͻkͻͻ, mehyɛɛ bͻ bi,
Na aa! Onyimpa ne mbérɛwyɛ a!
Mennhyɛɛ bͻ na munnsuu gyan bi?

MHB 750
2 . San W’ekyir, dͻm Ewuradze, san!
Hwɛ W’akowaà a n’abaw egura;
Musu me gyedzi a minnyi ntsi;
Bio, fa kyɛ m’ dɛ minnyi gyedzi;
Mo sunsum nsan mbɛda W’abaw m’,
Na Agyenkwa no ntsi, hyira me.

MHB 750
3 . Mbͻbͻr a ihu ͻkra a edͻ n’ ntsi,
Sesei pam bͻn a ikyir n’ ma ͻnkͻ;
Ma menyɛ dza Ͻwo egye to m’,
Ͻwo nà egye dza mepɛ to m’;
Ͻwo bɛpɛ dɛ efrɛ m’ Wodze,
Mobͻbͻ mbͻdzén afrɛ W’ medze.

MHB 750
4 . Ndɛ da ’i, megyé ahyɛmudzi n’ moto m’.
Bͻhyɛ nà asomdwee nkyekyeree n’;
M’adwen nnkɛyɛ m’ nàà, No tum ho,
Wͻdze Jesu bͻgyaa asͻw ano ’i.
Bͻgyà a motwer, dɛm bͻgya n’ nko,
Me nsa nkà ahyɛmudzi n’asomdwee n '

MHB 750
5 . Dɛ me gyedzi nnkohu nsakyer,
Mber ntamu, anaa ewiei bio n’,
Boa m’ ma mennantsew W’akwan mu,
Na tsie me ndze sesei, dɛ daa n’,
Na fa mbuae pa hyɛ m’akoma m' dɛw,
Nà Egya, ’nye W’ Ba ndzi nkitaho.
		Amen.

MHB 751
1 . Hwɛ mbrɛ Israel Guanhwɛfo 
Esi dze dɔ gyina hɔ;
Tsie! ɔrefrɛ m- bɔtoaba,
Ɔreyɛ hɔn etuu.

MHB 751
2 . Ɔse, Hom ngyaa hɔn ma wɔmbra, 
Mma hom mmbu hɔn 'nyimtsia!
Osian akra yinom n-tsi
Na Ewuradze bae.

MHB 751
3 . O, Ewuradze, ndaasem' ara 
Na yɛdze hɔn brɛ Wo,
Yedzi dɛw dɛ yɛyɛ Wodze,
Hɛn mba so nyɛ Wodze.   Amen.

MHB 752
1 . SIARFO Jesus, yegyina ha, 
Yeehyia m’ dɛ mbrɛ Ͻwo kae no;
Yɛdze dɛm abofra yi brɛ W’,
Dɛ mbrɛ ahyɛ hɛn dɛ yɛnyɛ n’,
Christ, yɛdze no ma W’ wͻ ha dɛm,
Yinom dɛm na wͻsɛ W’ heaven.

MHB 752
2 . Ntsi yɛyɛ ntsɛm ba Wo hͻ:
O gye bͻhyɛ a yɛdze ba yi; 
Yenhu W’enyimnyam wͻ ha,
Na mbeberhu mapa mu ya n'
Wo ba sesei na mma nngyaa n’ da,
Yɛ n’ Wodze wͻ ha, na afebͻͻ.

MHB 752
3 . Afei ͻda W’akoma mu.
Dza hɛn akoma pɛ no yie; 
Gyaa hɛn haw ho nkrumsi n’ sor;
Wo nhyira a wonnsusu no;
Kyerɛw dzin a yɛdze ama W’ sesei n’,
Kyerɛw n’ wͻ heaven buukuu no mu.
		Amen.

MHB 753
1 . FIE Nyɛnko, dɛ mbrɛ osii Galilee ma
Abaatan dze hɔn mbɔtoaba brɛɛ Wo n',
Dɔ Ewuradze, hɛn so yɛdze mbofra 'i ba,
Na yɛpɛ dze hɔn ahyɛ W'astaban ase.

MHB 753
2 . Wɔyɛ Wodze wɔ Wo dɔ a onnyi ewiei m',
Yenuma hɔn wɔ Nyame Ɔkorsa dzin mu:
Yɛnntwer nsɛmkyerɛdze, mbom Nyame N'adom n',
Ama eesiesie bea ama Wo nguambaa.

MHB 753
3 . Ewuradze, W'asɔr nyɛ dɛ ɔbaatan n' dɔ,
Ontur nguambaa yi wɔ no bom' mma Wo;
Na dom hɔn sɛ anapa twa m' ma ewia pue a,
Wɔnkɔ do ntsena dɔ na som krɔnkrɔn mu.

MHB 753
4 . Fa abofra yi do twe awofo n' bɛn Wo,
Ma hɔn fie nkɔ do wɔ ahotsew mu;
Aka wiadze efi abɔ m 'i, boa hɔn ano
Wɔ sor, o Christ, ber a wiadze nda asa n'.  Amen.

MHB 754
1 . Ɔkofo, soɛr gyina, 
Suo Christ mbeamudua n' mu;
Fa wo Pomfo dzin ka ntam dɛ
Apow wiadze ndzɛmba

MHB 754
2 . Soɛr ma wonnuma wo- 
Wɔnhor wo ho bɔn nyina;
'Nye wo Nyankopɔn ndzi ahyɛmu,
Ndɛ to wo gyedzi dzin.

MHB 754
3 . Ndɛ Christ akowaa nye wo 
Wɔkan wo fora esiarfo n',
Ndɛ edɔm tsetse nkɔnhyɛfo n',
Na asomafo n' na atɔfo n'.

MHB 754
4 . Ma Nyame akodze nyina 
Nhyɛ w' dzen; 'nye abɔnsam nko:
Ɔsa n' bɛyɛ dzen, ɔbɛkyɛr,
Na otwar dɛ yedzi nyim.

MHB 754
5 . Konyim abɔtsir n' a! 
Sor ndwom dɛɛdɛw bi n' a!
Yi na Sahen n' dze ma hɔn a
Hɔn gyedzi bedzi nyim!

MHB 755
1 . HƐN Ewuradze pa Jesus Christ,
Ɔwo yɛɛ obofra pɛn wɔ ha,
Yɛserɛ Wo, ma W'abofra yi
Wo nhyira na W'adom dabiara.
       O Jesus krɔnkrɔn, Sor Ewuradze,
       Yɛserɛ Wo, weɔn W'abofra yi.

MHB 755
2 . Ewuradze, Wo sor Ahenman mu n',
Ndzɛmba nyina tsie W'asɛm krɔnkrɔn n',
Osian dɛm ntsi ma hɛn Wo mboa,
Na kora abofra yi mber nyina.

MHB 755
3 . Ma abɔfo nweɔn n' ntwa no ho nhyia
Beebiara, oenyan o, ɔada o;
Ma ɔnsoa Wo mbeamudua krɔnkrɔn n',
Ɔnye ahotsewfo aasoa ahenkyɛw n'. Amen.

MHB 756
3 WIADZE paanoo a wobubuu n' adom m',
Ɔkra wenyin a wokyii n' mbɔbɔrm';
Ɔwo na ekaa nkwa asɛm no,
Ɔwo ewu ma hɛn bɔn ewu;
Hwɛ akoma a yaw epira no,
Hwɛ nyinsu a ndzenbɔnyɛfo kyi,
Ma, W'edziban nyɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze
Dɛ W'adom nyɛn hɛn akra ampa.

MHB 757
1 . WƆNTSERƐW Ewuradze pon no m',
Bubu paanoo na hue nsa n',
Yeehyia pon krɔnkrɔn no ho,
Yebedzi sor edziban no.

MHB 757
2 . Gyedzi m', 'hotsewfo atɔfo,
Adan hɔn enyi ahwɛ mbeamudua n',
Wɔwɔ afɔrbɔ yi m' kyɛfa,
Hɔn nkwa na hɔn wu mu nyina.

MHB 757
3 . 'Hobrɛadze m' yɛper kyɛfa
Wɔ enyimnyam kuw no mu,
Dze dzin no hoahoa hɛnho;
O Christ, yɛnye W' bu paanoo n'.

MHB 757
4 . Wo dɔ ho nkaakaa no ntsi,
Yɛma mbeamudua n' do wɔ sor,
Dze hyɛ Ɔwo Nyame enyimnyam;
Fa W' Sunsum afowa twa hɛn ho.

MHB 757
5 . Wo tum nsa n' gya hɛn abamba ''i,
Yɛbɛhyɛ W'adwen nyin ama;
Yebedzi W' mbra biara do,
Yɛdze ɔpɛ pa bɔsom Wo.

MHB 758
1 . Ewuradze Krɔnkrɔn, memmfata 
Dɛ 'Wo 'bɛba mo hɔ,
Kasa ara: ka adomsɛm kor, 
Na me kra ho bɛsan.

MHB 758
2 . Memmfata: me kra mu tsenabew 
Yɛ nwinwin, yɛ nkɔnkɔw;
Ebɛyɛ dɛn ahɛn mu hɔ?
Kasa, na m'bɛtse apɔw.

MHB 758
3 . Memmfata dze; na m'bɛyɛ dɛn 
Mesiw me Nyame kwan?
Ɔwo a Wo honam nye bɔgyaa
Edze tɔɔ nkwa maa me.

MHB 758
4 . Obra! Anapa *bɔw yi mu 
Fa Woho bɛnyɛn me;
Fa Wo dɔ nye Wo tum nyina
Bɛyhɛ m'akoma ma. Amen.

MHB 759
1 . Afei hɛn Egya yɛrekaa Wo dɔ n', 
Dɔ a ɔtɔɔ hɛn prɛko wɔ mbeamudua n' do n';
Na hɛn sor Dzimafo n' so wɔ ha yi,
Yɛtrɛ hɛn afɔrbɔdze mu ma Wo,
Afɔrbɔdze a no nko fata W'enyim,
Jesus, nokwar afɔrbɔdze a otsim.

MHB 759
2 . Jesus a wɔasera No n' na hwɛ N'enyim, 
Ehwɛ hɛn a, hwɛ hɛn wɔ Christ no mu;
Mma nnhwɛ hɛn dɛ yeetsiatsia W'adom do;
Mma nnhwɛ hɛn mpaabɔ nye gyedzi nwinwin n':
Na hwɛ! hɛn mfom nye hɔn ho akatua,
Wo Ba, hɛn Wura, N'amandzehu so ntam'.

MHB 759
3 . Hɔn so a yɛdɔ hɔn kyɛn adze nyina n', 
Yedua Christ do yɛtotɔ serɛ ma hɔn;
O fa W'ehumbɔbɔr fua hɔn Wo bom',
Bɔ mbɔdzen nyina hɔn kra ne yie ho;
Sie hɔn krɔnn fi emumuyɛ nkekaa ho,
Fa dzenhyɛ wie dwuma n' ma wɔnkɔ kan.

MHB 759
4 . N-tsi yɛaba; twe hɛn pin W'anan ho, 
Agyenkwa pa a yɛafom mpo a edɔ hɛn;
Edziban dɛɛdɛw mu yɛ hu yi,
Dua do yi hɛn fi mbusu nyina ho:
Ma hɛn dɛw na fahodzi Wo som mu,
Na mma nngya hɛn mma yemmfi Wo 
nkyɛn da.   Amen.

MHB 76
1 . Ɔdɔ Hen nye mo Guanhwɛfo, 
N' ayamuyie mmpa ara da;
Meyɛ Nedze ma ɔyɛ medze aba,
Mirinnhia hweeara da.

MHB 76
2 . Mbrɛ nkwa esutsen fi pem no, 
Hɔ na ogya me kra kɔ,
Ɔdze sor edziban nyɛn me
Wɔ mbrɛ m-funoma wɔ no.

MHB 76
3 . M-ber pii na mikyiin bɔn mu, 
Na ɔdze dɔ hwehwɛɛ me;
Ɔdze me too Ne batsir do
Dze me baa fie edɛw mu.

MHB 76
4 . Owu bɔnsam' munnsuro mbusu, 
Ber a, mo Wura, ebɛn me;
W' abaw na Wo poma hyɛ m' dzen,
Na Woara idzi m' enyim.

MHB 76
5 . 'Wo na eto pon wɔ m' enyim; 
Ihue adom gu mo do;
Ao, enyigye bɛn na ofi
Wo kuraba mu bu do!

MHB 76
6 . Dɛm na W' ayamuyie mmpa ara da, 
Mo nkwa nda nyinara mu;
Mo Guanhwɛfo pa, ma montow
W' ayɛyi wɔ Wo fie daa!   Amen.

MHB 760
1 . GYEFO, na ɔbɛyɛ dɛ
Ebɛtsena emi mo mu?
Ifi W'ahengua pa do,
'Hengua a nhyira wɔ ho afebɔɔ 'i,
Obirɛpɔn ''bɔto W'ho famu
Abɛhɛn dɛm fie yi mu?

MHB 760
2 . Ewuradze, memmfata,
Mo ho yɛ nkɔw yie!
Dɛ me Nyame, megye Wo
Wɔ akoma a aprɔw yi mu:
'Mi bɔnyɛnyi kohwinyi;
M'abrabɔ ka mu dɛ: Gya m' hɔ.

MHB 760
3 . Na bra, Ɔwo a fi sor,
Na bɛtsew mo bo ho;
Bra, Ɔwo ''nyimnyam Hen pa,
Ber a mokotow Wo mbeamudua ''i,
Woara fa Wo nkwagye n' bra,
Bɛhɛn fie yi mu tsew ho.  Amen.

MHB 761
1 . JESUS, yetsie W'asɛm,
W'ewiei na adɔyɛ asɛm;
Wɔ Wo mber pa mu wɔ ha no,
Hɛn Wura, yɛba bheyia W'.

MHB 761
2 . Yebua hɛn akoma m',
Ma Agyenkwa n' aaba m',
Na hwɛ! Eguambaa a wokum No n',
Abɔn adamfo n' aba.

MHB 761
3 . Wo mbae ma hɛn enyigye:
Ndɛ ma hɛn sunsum ntse
Enyimnyam a onnyi kabea,
Enyigye a wɔnnka mpo:

MHB 761
4 . Edze ahenman mu dɛw
Kyekye hɛn akra werɛ.
Fie yi yɛ W'apontu fie pa,
Na edze hɛn aba ha.

MHB 761
5 . O fa sor edziban
Nyɛn hɛn akra dabaa,
Na tserɛw Wo dɔ a onnyi ewiei
Frankaa no wɔ hɛn do.  Amen.

MHB 762
1 . Agyenkwa no dɔ ho nkaa ntsi 
Na yɛaba pon yi ho:
Ha na Jesus to nsa dze frɛ
Hɔn a woenu hɔnho.

MHB 762
2 . Yɛnam gyedzim' fa nkwa paano 
Yɛdze nyɛn hɛn akra;
Yɛnom wenyin dze kaa bɔgya a
Ogui maa abɔn no.

MHB 762
3 . Ha na yɛtow ndwom yɛkamfo 
Jesus N'anwanwa dɔ;
Da bi sor aponto edziban
Na yɛsɔ hwɛ wɔ ha.

MHB 763
1 . Dɛ mbrɛ W'adom Asɛm no tse, 
Ahobrɛadzem' ara
Yi na m'bɛyɛ, m'Ewuradze a
'Ruwu, mebɛkaa Wo.

MHB 763
2 . Wo honam a 'mi ntsi wobui n' 
Bɛyɛ mo sor paanoo;
W'ahyɛmudze kuraba n' na megye,
Ma medze makaa Wo.

MHB 763
3 . Sɛ medan m'enyi hwɛ mbeamudua n' 
Na mohom Calvary hɔ a
Nyame Egumba e, m'afɔrdze e,
Otwar dɛ mekaa Wo.

MHB 763
4 . M'bɛkaa W' ɔnnye Wo fona nyina, 
Nye Wo dɔ a adɔ m' nyina 
Nyew ber a ahom kakra wɔ hɔ 'i
M'bɛda ho ara makaa W'.

MHB 763
5 . Na aber a mobɔtɔ mmum 
Na adwen na nkaa bɛhera n'
Ber a 'nam W'ahendzim' bɛba n'
Jesus, ɔyɛ a kaa me.

MHB 764
1 . ƆSOR n-kwa Mafo,
Ɔwo a ''dze sunsum m' nsa
Na onnyiewiei paanoo,
Ato hɛn pon nwanwa,
Kora nkwa a edze ama hɛn no,
Nyɛn hɛn, tsetse hɛn ma heaven.

MHB 764
2 . Hyɛ hɛn akra ehiafo dzen
Wɔ ɔdɔ fofor koraa mu;
Ber a yenya Wo nkwa no,
Na yehu W'emudzi n',
Na W'adom mapa ahyɛ hɛn dzen n',
Dɛm na yehu W'enyim petee. Amen.

MHB 765
1 . BRA, Ɔwo Sunsum bɛkyebo,
Ma Agyenkwa N' wu ho siar
Na N'adasa ho amandzehu n',
Mbra adwen a ɔwɔ nkaa biara m'.

MHB 765
2 . No dɔ ho Kyerɛwfo nokwafo,
Petse gyedzi a otsim hɔ daa n';
Da No nkwagye kɛse n' edzi,
Bɔ N' nsɛmpa n' dawur kyerɛ hɛn.

MHB 765
3 . Bra, o No wu ho Dasefo;
Bra, Ɔwo sor Kaakaafo,
Ma yɛntse Wo tum ne nka, na
Ma emi na ɔkra bia 'a nya Christ.   Amen.

MHB 766
1 . Ma yenhu W' ber a yeridzidzi, 
Na mma nn-dan hɛn nngya;
Agyenkwa, nye hɛn ntsena, na to
Wo pon hɛn 'koma mu.

MHB 766
2 . Enye hɛn ndzidzi Nyame dɔm'; 
Wo honam na bɔgyaa,
N-kwa paanoo, sor wenyin no,
Nyɛ hɛn edziban daa.   Amen.

MHB 767
1 . SUNSUM Krɔnkrɔn, bɛhyɛ hɛn do,
Na yenhu nsɛnkyerɛdze;
Ma Wo nkwa mbra paanoo no mu,
Wo tum nhyɛ nsa no mu.

MHB 767
2 . Ma nsɛnkyerɛdze 'i nda edzi petee,
Na ma ɔmfa sor kwan do;
Siesie akwan ma wɔmfa W' dɔ n'
Nhɛn nokwar akoma biara m'. Amen.

MHB 768
1 . O AKWANTUFO paanoo,
Edziban a abɔfo dzi,
O Manna a ofi sor ba
Ma hɔn a hɔn awoo fo sor, 
Fa ma hɛn, hɛn enyi da kwan
Dɛ yebedzi amee,
'Kodu wiadze enyigye ewiei,
Hɛn pɛ nyina bɔbɔ adze.

MHB 768
2 . O Nsu, ɔwo a ema nkwa,
Fi Agyenkwa n' N'akoma m',
N-subura krɔnn a ɔpem,
Eyɛ ɔdɔ nsubura,
O ma hɛn so nsɔ Wo nhwɛ,
Na dwedwe hɛn nsukɔm;
Wo dɛw no nnsa ara da,
Ɔwɔ hɔ afebɔɔ.

MHB 768
3 . Jesus, yɛgye edziban yi,
'Wo a yennhu W; yehuhor W';
Yɛgye Wo nokwasɛm dzi,
Yɛgye, yɛnngye kyim bio:
Nokwafo dɔyɛfo, dom hɛn,
Yɛntsena Wo mu wiadze;
Sɛ owu twamu tam rifi hɔ a,
Yeehu W'enyim ne hyerɛn n'. Amen.

MHB 769
1 . Sor paano a enyɛn me, 
'Wo 'yɛ edziban ampa:
Ma nokwar nkwa paano yi
Nyɛn me kra daa daa nyina;
Ɔwo a iwui na etse ase,
Minnya Wo mu ahoɔdzen daa.

MHB 769
2 . Sor Wenyin, fa Wo bɔgyaa 
Hyɛ afɔr kuraba yi ma:
W'epirakur ma n-kwa ,
Mohwɛ W'asɛndua n' nya nkwa;
Ɔwo a eyɛ mo nkwa,
Ma mintsim wo mu pintsinn. Amen.

MHB 77
1 . Minsi dɛn mondɔ me Nyame, 
Minsi dɛn nyi N' ayɛw?
Minsi dɛn nhu N' adom no war,
Ne trɛ, no krɔn, no bun?

MHB 77
2 . W' adom tsen du obiara do, 
Na onnyi mbanano;
Ɔto adasamba nyina;
Ɔwɔ hɔ afebɔɔ.

MHB 77
3 . Odu wiadze tɛtɛr nyina, 
Ne trɛ nnyi mbanano;
Ɔtrɛ ma onngya baako mpo,
N-kyɛ ɔpaa mo ho.

MHB 77
4 . Mo mfom nyinii dur sorsor no; 
W' ehumbɔbɔr traa hɔ;
Christ no mu edoom me fakyɛ,
Fakyɛ a wɔnnto n' abaw.

MHB 77
5 . Sor abɔfo bɛn botum akyerɛ 
Wo nkwagye dɔ n' no bun?
W' akyɛdze a onnyi kabea yi,
Ao, ma monsɔ monhwɛ.

MHB 77
6 . Bra ntsɛm, adom Ewuradze, 
Bɛfa Woara Wodze;
W' adaworom, bɛyɛ m' akoma
W' ahengua afebɔɔ.     Amen.

MHB 770
1 . JESUS, yɛaba Wo pon ho,
Fa nkwa paanoo mapa no
Nyɛn akoma biara sesei.

MHB 770
2 . Yɛdze nnuho kotow ha 'i,
Ma yenhu W'enyim fɛɛfɛw n',
Yi Wo dɔ nwanwa n' kyerɛ hɛn.

MHB 770
3 . Ber a yɛhwɛ W'asɛndua yi,
'Ridzi mbɔɔ wɔ hɛn bɔn ho 'i,
Ma hɛn awerɛhow ndan ayɛyi.

MHB 770
4 . Sɛ yɛnom wenyin nwanwa a
Ɔkyerɛ Wo bɔgyaa a ihuee a,
Fa sor dɔ n' hyɛ hɛn akoma m'.

MHB 770
5 . Twe hɛn bɛn W'epirakur ho,
Mbrɛ 'yarsa nsu fi pem no,
Hɔ hɛn bɔn na yaw suma.

. Ma Wo pira nsa n' nkyerɛ hɛn kwan
Nkodu W'ahengua no ho,
Wɔ kan na man pa no mu.    Amen.

MHB 770
6 . Gye hɛn fi bɔn no mpokyerɛ m',
Hɛn gyedzi nwinwin ndzi mu,
'Guambaa, ma hɛn W'asomdwee.

MHB 771
1 . 'MANDZEHUNYI, yɛgye W'adom,
Ber a yɛkyerɛ Wo wu a ɔsom bo n',
'Guambaa krɔnn a wɔdze W' mae prɛko,
Eyɛɛ mpata maa adasa nyina
Wɔ W'asɔrfi m' wɔ asaase ha,
Na igyina ahengua n' enyim.

MHB 771
2 . Ɔwo gyina krɔnkrɔnbea ha,
Ber a woekum Wo ama abɔn;
Bɔgya petsee n' kasa, bɔ mpaa,
Na ɔwɔ hɔ ma nyimpa abrɛfo;
Wo bɔgyaa n' da ho ara pon hɛn
Na ɔka nkwagyesɛm wɔ mbea nyina.

MHB 771
3 . Onnhia dɛ yɛbɔkɔ heaven
Akɛfa Agyekwan n' aba ha;
'Dze Woho ama obiara dada,
W'aponto ase na wɔakrɔn Wo:
Yi Woho kyerɛ akra nokwafo,
Na yenhu W'ankasa wɔ ha.  Amen.

MHB 772
1 . O Ewuradze, ha na muhu W'enyim, 
Ha na mepɛ mesuo dza wonnhu mu;
Morohwehwɛ menya Nyame N'adom,
Na medze me berɛ mato Wo do.

MHB 772
2 . Ha na m'bedzi Onyame edziban, 
Na menye Wo anom ɔsor wenyin;
Na medze m'adzesoa mato n-kyɛn
Na makaa Wo fakyɛ ne dɛw no bio.

MHB 772
3 . Edzidzi na adwontow aber nye yi, 
Ɔsor pon na wɔato ama me yi.
Ma menye Wo mbɔ mu yendzidzi ha,
Na enye me ndzi nkitaho dɛɛdɛw.

MHB 772
4 . Ɔnnkyɛr na wɔakata nsɛnkyerɛdze n' do: 
Aponto n' etwam'; dɔ no dze nntwam' da.
Woyi paano na wenyin no kɔ mpo a
'Wo, hɛn Kyɛm na Ewia, ebɛn hɛn daa.

MHB 772
5 . Minnyi mboa bi dɛ Wo nko Wodze no, 
Na onnhia mpo dɛ motwer obi so.
M'Ewuradze, Woara dɔɔ so ma me,
Wo tum n-ko ara nye m'ahoɔdzen.

MHB 772
6 . Mber pii na yɛaba W'edzidziase: 
Ne nyina kyerɛ hɛn sor dze kɛse no,
Sor edziban a da bi yebedzi 
Na yɛsɔ ne dɛw hwɛ ase ha yi.

MHB 773
1 . Christ abɔ werdam apon hɛn, 
No ho nkaabɔdze na yɛyɛ yi;
Yɛkyerɛ hɛn Wura No wu kɛpem
Da a ɔbɛba.

MHB 773
2 . No honam a wobui maa hɛn 
Wɔ nkaabɔ paano yi mu ha,
Ɔno na ɔnyɛn hɛn dɔ kɛpem
Da a ɔbɛba.

MHB 773
3 . Bɔgya a oruwu a okyii no 
Wenyin yi yɛ ho sɛnkyerɛdze.
Yɛbɔnom ara akɛpem
Da a ɔbɛba.

MHB 773
4 . Anago bɔn a wonyii N' mae n' 
Na Ne mbae a odzi ekyir no
Yɛdze dɔ nyɛbea bɔm' kɛpem
Da a ɔbɛba.

MHB 773
5 . O, asɛm pa a ɔhyɛ hɛn dzeen!  
Ɔma hɛn akomatɔmu.
Hom mma yengyina dzen nkɛpem
Da a ɔbɛba.

MHB 774
1 . O ƆDƆ Nyame, yɛkotow W',
Na bɔ mpaa ma hɔn a wɔaba ha 'i,
Wɔaka abɔ m' wɔ nsewdzi krɔnkrɔn m',
Ma wɔnye Wo nyɛ kor.

MHB 774
2 . Ber a enyigye pa ahyɛ nda mu n',
Ber a akwan m' da hɔ na wimu yɛ kann,
Wɔnam gyedzi m', nnyɛ dza wonnhu m',
Ma wɔnye Wo nyɛ kor.

MHB 774
3 . Sɛ ehum hyɛ hɔn pɛ ma a,
Na hɔn ndzepa nyinara sɛɛ a,
Na wɔgye Wo dzi koraa ntsi,
Ma wɔnye Wo nyɛ kor.

MHB 774
4 . Dza ɔwɔ ɔbra m' bɛyɛ hɔndze,
Enyigye anaa dadwen mu o,
Tum a wɔdze yɛ, adom a wɔdze sɔw o.
Ma wɔnye Wo nyɛ kor.

MHB 774
5 . Onnyiewiei Dɔ, enye hɔn ntsena;
Fa hɔn sie Wo mu afebɔɔ,
Na owu mpo nnkotum atsew hɔn mu,
Hɔn a Ɔwo yɛ hɔn kor n'.

MHB 775
1 . N-dze a wɔtsee wɔ Eden 
Ayerhyia kan n-dze n',
Asɔpɔn awar nhyira n'
Ɔda ho ara wɔ hɔ.

MHB 775
2 . Christian ɔbaa na barimba 
So rokɔ awar a,
Nyame Ɔkorsa wɔm' bi,
Na yɛserɛ Ne nhyira:

MHB 775
3 . Dɛ ɔndom hɔn m-ba pa, 
Nye dɔ na nokwardzi,
Na ɔndom hɔn koryɛ bi a
Biribiara nntum mmpa mu.

MHB 775
4 . Sor Egya, Woara bɛfa, 
Ayefor yi ma awar,
Dɛ mbrɛ 'dze Eve maa Adam,
Fii noara ne mfem' no.

MHB 775
5 . Agyenkwa domfo, bra na 
Bɛka hɔn bɔm' ɔdɔm',
Dɛ mbrɛ edze su ebien
Bɔɔm' wɔ Woara Wo mu n'

MHB 775
6 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, behyira hɔn, 
Ber a wɔrobɔ mpaa yi,
Dɛ mbrɛ ehyira Christ N'Asɔr
Ma ɔyɛ N'Ayefor n'.

MHB 775
7 . Tserɛw W'atsaban wɔ hɔn do, 
Pa hɔn mbusu nyina,-
Ber a worutu anamɔn
Ba W'afɔrmbukyia ho,

MHB 775
8 . Dze hɔn 'nyimnyam abɔtsir 
Abɔbɔ Wo afɔr,-
Kɛpem dɛ wɔnye Agyenkwa
N' Ayefor no bɔsoɛr.

MHB 776
1 . Egya, adze nyina Yɛfo, 
Wo nyansaa, tum na dɔ
Dzii kan dze akra ebien bɔɔm'
Wɔ Eden ture mu;
N-dɛ fa nkan n' akyɛdze n'
Ma Wo mbofra yi so,
Ofi a W'asomdwee wɔ mu,
Ɔdɔ a nokwardzi wɔm'.

MHB 776
2 . Gyefo a ekɔr Galilee 
Ayeforase hɔ,
N-dɛ so fa enyimpa ma
Hɔn a wɔfrɛ Wo yi:
Ma hɔn wiadze enyigye
Ɔndan sor enyingye
Na wɔsɔ hwɛ a, ma wonhu
Dɛ Woara W'akyɛdze a.

MHB 776
3 . O Nyame Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, 
Ɔwo a Wo dɔ yɛ dzen,
W'ahotsewee so dzi mu,
Fi sor gu hɔn do ahom,
Ama Woara wowaw hɔn
Fi ntokwaa ho n-tsi,
Hɔn bra aakyerɛ dɛ 'Wo na 
Ehyɛ hɔn 'koma do.

MHB 776
4 . Egya, Woara ennsi dan yi a, 
Wɔnnkɛfa edu beebi;
Gyefo, Woara ennhyira do a,
Hɔn dɛw bɛdan hɔn yaw;
Na hweeara nnkotum asɛɛ
Awar a ehyira do;
Ɔdɔ a Wo Sunsum tsew ho
Yɛ dɔ a ɔmmbɔ adze da.

MHB 777
1 . O ƆDƆ mapa, ebor nyimpa adwen do,
Yɛkotow W'ahengua enyim na yɛserɛ
Dɛ hɔn a eka hɔn bɔ m' afebɔɔ yi
Nnya ɔdɔ a no do nntwa da biara da.

MHB 777
2 . O N-kwa mapa, yɛ hɔn awerɛhyɛm' koraa,
Ayamuyie mapa na gyedzi a otsim,
Abotar enyidar, 'kokodur a ɔsɔw berɛ,
Awerɛhyɛmu a onnsuro yaw na owu.

MHB 777
3 . Dom hɔn dɛw a ɔsesa wiadze awerɛhow,
Dom hɔn asomdwee a ɔdwedwe 
wiadze haw;
Ma hɔn nkwa nda mu enyimnyam adzekyee,
Dza ɔdze onnyiewiei dɔ na nkwa ba.  Amen.

MHB 778
1 . HƆN a wogyina Zion ho n',
Mbrɛ hɔn anan ho yɛ fɛw a!
Wɔka nkwagye nsɛmpa no daa,
Na wɔda asomdwee edzi.

MHB 778
2 . Hɔn ndze ma awerɛkyekyer,
Hɔn nsɛm so ne dɛw a!
Zion, hwɛ W'Agyenkwa Ɔhen no;
Odzi Hen, dzi nyim ha.

MHB 778
3 . Mbrɛ woesi ehyira hɛn aso a!
Ɔtse dɛ ndze dɛɛdɛw a
Nkɔnhyɛfo na ahemfo tweɔnee,
Na wɔhwehwɛe a woennhu n'.

MHB 778
4 . Mbrɛ woehyira hɛn enyiwa a
Ohu dɛm sor kan yi a!
Nkɔnhyɛfo na ahemfo peer ho,
Na wowui a woennhu.

MHB 778
5 . Aweɔmfo n' dze ndze kor,
Maa ndwom dɛdɛɛdɛw do;
Jerusalem so ma ndwom do,
Sardofo tse ne dɛw n'.

MHB 778
6 . Ewuradze tserɛw N'abaw m'
Wɔ wiadze nyina do;
Wɔmma wiadze nyinara nhu
Hɛn Gyefo na Nyame

MHB 779
1 . SUNSUM Krɔnkrɔn, tsena hɛn kra mu,
Na ma Wo gya mfi sor nhyerɛn;
Edze sunsum ngo sera hɛn,
Na ema akyɛdze horow.

MHB 779
2 . W'adom ngohuam a ofi sor
Yɛ awerɛkyekyer, nkwa na dɔ;
Na Wo kan a onndum da no
Nhyerɛn hɛn do, ɔmpa hɛn sum.

MHB 779
3 . Fa W'adom mbordo n oma hɛn,
Ɔnsera hɛn, ɔntsew hɛn enyim;
Pam atamfo, ma asomdwee;
Mbrɛ ewɔ mbusu nntum mmba hɔ.

MHB 779
4 . Kyerɛ hɛn ma yenhu dɛ Egya n'
Ɔnye Ɔba n' nye Wo yɛ kor;
Ama ber a onnyi ewiei mu
Iyi nko aayɛ hɛn daa ndwom, -
     Ayɛyi nka Wo dzin mbersantsen;
    Egya, Ɔba, nye Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn!  Amen.

MHB 78
1 . M'BƐYƐ dɛn atow ahentum a
Abɔfo pɛ ho n' ndwom?
Huntuma m' huntuma nyɛ komm;
Ma sor adwontofo ntow,
Mpempem gyina W'ahengua ho,
O ɔsorsor Nyame;
Ɔpedu tow W'ayɛyi ndwom,
Na mo so nye woana?

MHB 78
2 . Wo hyerɛn da edzi ma hɔn;
Mitsin W'anamɔn do a,
Metse Nyame ndze wɔ m'asomu, 
Hɔn dze, wohu W'enyim,
'Yɛ hɔn Ewia ntsi wɔtow ndwom;
Tow nserɛmɛn to mo do,
Na beebi a heaven hyɛ ase n',
Alleluia wɔ hɔ.

MHB 78
3 . Ma gyedzi kan nhyerɛn m'akoma m',
Ma 'gya dɔ nsɔ wɔ mu;
Ma menye sor adwontofo
Aabɔ m' aatow Wo ndwom,
Musuro, mowɔ kan na gya nyina,
Dɛ m'bɛyɛ sum, na nwin;
Sɛ 'regye hɔn sika mfutuw a,
Gye mo so me dwɛɛtɛɛ.

MHB 78
4 . Ewuradze, mbrɛ idua so a,
Ekora abɔdze nyina!
Wo nyimdzee nkotoo na otum
Susu po n' trɛ na bun,
Ɔwo nye po a onnyi mpoano,
Ewia a onnyi ɔhe;
Ewɔ hɔ sesei nye daa nyina,
Na ewɔ beebiara.

MHB 780
1 . MO Wura Kasa! W'akowaa ritsie,
Morotweɔn W'adom asɛm no,
Mo kɔn dɔ W'akomatɔm' ndze,
Mo Wura, Ma mentse n' sesei,
Mo Wura, mayɛ aso ritsie W',
Ewɔ bɛn ka kyerɛ me?

MHB 780
2 . Mo Wura, bɔ me dzin na kasa,
Ama meehu dɛ enye m';
Frɛ m' na medze anan haahar
Bɛka W' do ahotɔ m' akɔ
Bea a 'Guanhwɛfo n' dzi nguan enyim,
Wɔ Botan no nwin ase.

MHB 780
3 . Mo Wura, kasa! Mennsɛ bi mpo a,
Sɛ enntsee me ndze a, mma monnkɔ;
Mo Wura kasa! Na Woara nyim
M'akoma n'akɔndɔdze;
Woara nyim n'ehiadze nyina,
Kasa na hyira m' prɛko.

MHB 780
4 . Mo Wura, kasa! Na yɛ m' krado,
Sɛ metse Wo ndze ampa a;
Setsie mu na enyigye mu,
Ma mindzi W'asɛm ekyir;
Mo Wura, mayɛ aso ritsie,
O mo Wura, kasa kyerɛ me!

MHB 781
1 . Ewuradze, kasa kyerɛ me, 
Ma munsusu Wo do nkasa;
Ahwehwɛ me yi ma mo so
Monhwehwɛ Wo mba a wɔayew no.

MHB 781
2 . Mo Wura, gya me kwan ma mo so 
Mingya W'akobɔfo taataa;
O nyɛn me ma mo so memfa
Manna mma hɔn a kɔm dze hɔn.

MHB 781
3 . O hyɛ me dzen ama ber a 
Migyina pintsinn wɔ Wo mu n',
Maatsen me nsa ama hɔn a
Woridzi aper wɔ bra po do.

MHB 781
4 . Kyerɛkyerɛ m' na meetum makyerɛ 
N-dzɛmba pa a ada n' edzi;
Ma m'anosɛm n-hwira ndu
Akoma pii ase noho.

MHB 781
5 . Fa W'asomdwee dɛɛdɛw n' ma me, 
Ma minnya nyansa memfa nka
Asomdwee nsɛm nkyerɛ Wo mba
Asonafo wɔ mbusu mber mu.

MHB 781
6 . Mo Wura, fa Wo mayɛ no ma m', 
Kodu dɛ m'akoma bu do,
Ma memfa ndam mombɔ dawur,
Menka Wo dɔ, minyi W' ayɛw.

MHB 781
7 . Fa me yɛ dɛ Woara 'pɛ, 
Aber nyina na bea biara,
Kodu dɛ mubohu W'enyim
Wɔ ahomgye, dɛw, na enyimnyam ma.
                                   Amen.

MHB 782
1 . EWURADZE, hyerɛn hɛn do,
Ɔwo, adasamba Kan;
Dua Wo kyerɛwsɛm do
Yi Woho kyerɛ hɛn ndɛ;
Na yɛhwɛ W'enyim a
Hɛn akoma dzɛw ntsi
Nkɔkowaba nam hɛn do
Eesua W'adom nwanwa n'.

MHB 782
2 . Ewuradze, hue Sunsum
Gyaframee n' gu hɛn do,
Ma yɛdze ano kor
Yaabɔ Wo dzin dawur.
Ma Wo mba aso pa,
Ma hɔn adwen ontsim,
Na hɔn nyina eehu
Ndzɛmba akɛse a ayɛ.

MHB 782
3 . Hɛn Wura, kasa ma hɛn,
Dza yɛka nyina mu,
Ma dza yɛkyerɛ nyɛ dɛ
Mbrɛ W'asɛm tse ara;
Ama nguambaa aatse
Hɔn Guanhwɛfo n' Ne ndze,
Na wɔaaka No do daa,
Na woeedzi No mu dɛw.

MHB 782
4 . Hɛn Wura, tsena hɛn mu;
Ma hɛn W'adwen no bi;
Ma yɛmfa hɛn ahom
Nyina ndɔ Wo, nsom Wo;
Na hɛn bra aakyerɛ
Wo mbofra mbrɛ etse,
Na yɛdze hɛn suban
Aatwe Wo mba nyina.    Amen.

MHB 783
1 . NA nyimpa a ɔyɛ mberɛw ho suro
Besiw sunsum a ɔwɔ mo mu n' kwan?
Ana me ndzeyɛɛ na kasa
Kyerɛ dɛ meyɛ m' Wura dasefo?

MHB 783
2 . Adasa Agyenkwa, Enyiasombea,
Ihu mo mu adwen nyinara;
'Bɛn na mohwehwɛ wɔ wiadze,
No mu enyigye anaa ayɛyi a?

MHB 783
3 . Christ dɔ n' hyɛ me ma mohwehwɛ
Nyimpa akra a wɔatɔ dɔnsuar;
Metsea m', dze su na ntotɔserɛ
Hwim hɔn fi adakamaa mu.

MHB 783
4 . Sɛ W' nokwar ntsi mo bɔgyaa na
Nkwa ho wɔ mfaso a, medze ma W';
Ewuradze, ma Wo tsirmpɔw mbra m',
Wo pɛ nyɛ hɔ, ayɛyi nka W' dzin.

MHB 783
5 . Ma m' W'ahoɔdzen, Nyame Tumfo,
Nkyii ma aahow mbɔ, nsenaman mbobɔ m';
Mbɛyɛ W' dasefo nokwafo;
Mutum ne nyina yɛ Wo dzin m'.

MHB 784
1 . AFƆR bɛn na hɛn atɔbɔ
Dze ma hɛn Wura, wɔ N'adom ntsi?
Yɛbɔbɔ Ne dzin kɛse no,
Na yeeyi N'ayɛw dɛ mbrɛ ɔsɛ.

MHB 784
2 . Ɔwo a yɛdɔ W' mbordo daa daa,
Ɔwo a esen hɛn adze nyina,
Bue sor nsunyiwa gu hɛn do,
Ma ɔnhyɛ hɛn akra amaama, mbu do.

MHB 784
3 . Dɛm na hɛn bra bɔbɔ W' tum na
W'adom a 'dze kyɛ abɔn kwa n' dawur,
Kodu dɛ adasa bohu W'dzin,
Na wɔatsen hɔn nsa nyina ama W'.

MHB 784
4 . Bue abow a wiadze nye hɛll
Per dɛn ara a, wonnkotum atow mu;
Ma W'asɛm ngye ntaa wɔ hɛn mu;
Na hɛn adom aba ntsena hɔ.

MHB 784
5 . O ma ogufo n'aba n' ndɔr!
Na yɛbɔsow aba mber nyina;
Ma W'asɛmpa n' mpetse wiadze,
Yɛmbɔ Wo daa nokwar n' dawur.

MHB 784
6 . Wo dɔ mapa ayɛ hɛn fofor n',
Yebohu W' kɛseyɛ no tum n'
Yegyina hɛn Nyame N'asɔrfi m'
Dɛ edum, na yennkefi hɔ bio.

MHB 785
1 . JESUS, sɛ yɛka hɛn akoma m'
Ehiasɛm kyerɛ Wo a,
Yehu dɛ yehia adom a
Ɔyɛ akyɛdze a ofir Wo;
Hɛn a yenyim hɛn mberɛwyɛ no,
Yebenya akyɛdze pii,
Yebenya adom nye nhyira mbordo,
Ne nyina Nyame dze ma.

MHB 785
2 . Yenyim dɛ dza yɛwɔ suar koraa,
Yenyim hɛn esintɔ dɛ
Yenntum nnyɛn akra a kɔm dze hɔn;
Ewuradze, yɛdze brɛ W';
Yɛdze hɛn ehiadze gu W' nsamu a,
Ɔyɛ ahonya mbordo;
Yɛ ɔdodow ebisadze ma hɛn,
Na fa W' dɔ hyɛ hɔn ma.  Amen.

MHB 786
1 . OWURA, ma yɛnweɔn dɛ beenum n',
Yɛntweɔn Wo mbaa, na obiara
Mper nkeka ne kandzea;
Na osiandɛ ngo a ofi Wo hɔ no
Wora adom daa gu akoma biara m' ntsi,
Kandzea biara mmonsom.

MHB 786
2 . Mma yɛnntsena pɛsɛankonya m',
Mbom yɛmfa asɔryɛ mfora edwumayɛ,
Ama kandzea n' aadzɛw;
Na pii efi hɔn bɔn sum kadoo m' n',
Wɔnye hɛn aabɔ mu epue
W'enyim aponto ase.

MHB 786
3 . Ewuradze, nnyɛ hɛn nko bɛba
W'aponto kɛse no ase,
Abɛtsena dɛw m' ahwɛ W',
Yɛdze akobɛɔfo, ayarfo,
Ankonam na mbofra brɛ Wo,
Ama yaahwɛ W'enyim.

MHB 787
1 . N-dɔbaa Ewuradze, tsie 
Wo nkowaa ehiafo hɛn su;
Tsie hɛn gyedzi mu mpaabɔ yi
Na dom hɛn dza yehia.

MHB 787
2 . Yɛtweɔn Wo mbɔbɔr mu; 
Inyim hɛn hia nyina:
Ampa dɛ n-dɔbaa no so,
Na edwumafo no suar.

MHB 787
3 . Sakyer wobinom so 
Na soma hɔm W'asɔr mu
Ma wɔnka Wo tum kasa no
Dɛ 'Wo nye hɔn wɔ hɔ

MHB 787
4 . Ma wɔnka W'asɛmpa a 
Adom ahyɛ no ma n',
Wɔnkyerɛ dɛ 'Wo nye Ewuradze,
Adasamba Gyefo.

MHB 787
5 . Ma wɔntrɛ Wo dzin mu, 
Ma wɔmfata hɔn frɛ,
Wɔmbɔ W'adom kɛse no mu,
Wo dɔ a onnyi ewiei n'!

MHB 788
1 . DOMFO Abɔso, wiadze Tsɛmbuafo,
Ɔwo a efa mberɛwyɛ nye ehiafo yɛ W'dze;
Efa dɛtse nkuraba hun na ebubudze
Na ehyehyɛ hɔn Wo ndzepa a ɔmmpa ara da.

MHB 788
2 . Kaansa Wo kan hyɛ m' mpo a, nkuraba n' nnkyɛr pa,
Wotsin Wo mom do bubu, na woetwa m';
Afei Wo nokwar kan no pue n'ahoɔdzen m'
Dɛ mbrɛ enyinam nyinam mununkum mu no.

MHB 788
3 . Dɛ mbrɛ mununkum kyin yɛ Wo pɛ kɛse n'
Na mframa dzendzen bɔ wiadze ho aprɔw n',
Asɛm n' dze Ne nyansaa hyɛ hɔn sunsum ma,
Wɔbobɔ mu, wɔhyerɛn, na wobu do.

MHB 788
4 . Wɔbɔ hɔn ndze m' Jesus Christ nye Ewuradze!
Ntsi Satan bɔ hwea, n'aban dwuruw gu famu,
Dɛ mbrɛ ekasae ma totorobɛnto hɛnee
Ara a Canaan afasu dwuruwii no.

MHB 788
5 . Afei ma totorobɛnto n' nhɛn dzendzen,
Ewuradze, ma onnyan hɛn mfi bɔn nda m';
Nkandzea a Ɔwo asosɔ wɔ hɛn sum mu n',
O ma ɔnhyerɛn wɔ hɛn esunsum mu!

MHB 788
6 . 'Nyimnyam, ayɛyi, tumdzi na ahoɔdzen nyina
Nka Nyame Ebiasa kor afebɔɔ;
Ɔama Ne kan nwanwa n' ahyerɛn hɛn ho,
Ɔafrɛ hɛn sum mu ma yeehu N'enyimnyam!

MHB 789
1 . CHRIST, mma W' werɛ mmfir
W'adɔntsen dɔm a
Woridzi ako wɔ amanadze.

MHB 789
2 . Yɛserɛ W', kora na ma hɔn tsir do,
Wɔ nsuyirii, gya, sum na suro m'.

MHB 789
3 . Hyɛ hɔn dzen wɔ suro biara m',
Na Woara bɛn hɔn wɔ mbusu m'.

MHB 789
4 . W'edwuma na wɔper ayɛ,
Wosuar, na atamfo no dɔɔ so.

MHB 789
5 . Christ, 'nye W'akofo adɔfo a
Wɔwɔ ehum asaase do ntsena.

MHB 79
1 . HOM nyi Ewuradze ayɛw, oye dɛ 
Hom ma akoma na ndze do kamfo N';
No su na No ndwuma gya hɛn ma 
Yɛdze enyigye yi N' ayɛw.

MHB 79
2 . Ɔyɛɛ nworaba a wɔhyerɛn wɔ sor,
'Kan hɔn dodow, bɔ hɔn edzin;
Ne nyansaa so, onnyi ewiei,
Bun kɛse a hɛn nsusui yew mu.

MHB 79
3 . Hom ntow ndwom mfa nkrɔn Ewuradze!
Ɔtserɛw No mununkum mu wɔ sor; 
Hɔ na ɔhyehyɛ nyankonsu,
Anaa ɔmma nsu nngu famu kwa.

MHB 79
4 . Ɔdze sar kata akoko do,
Na eburow hyɛ hɛn kwa amaama; 
Ne nsa ma mbowadoma edziban,
Na ɔnyɛn nnoma nyina so.

MHB 79
5 . Ebɛn na abɔdze tum yɛ?
Nyimpa ahoɔdzen anaa mpɔnkɔ? 
Nyansa anaa ahoɔdzen so ɛ?
Yinom nyina nnka hwee wɔ N'enyim.

MHB 79
6 . 'Hotsewfo dze, wɔsɔ N'enyi,
Ne mba ho yɛ no enyigye;
Onyim hɔn 'nyidar, hɔn suro,
Ɔhwɛ, na ɔdɔ Ne saso hɔ.

MHB 790
1 . NYAME mbɔbɔrhufo tumfo,
Fi Wo sor bea a adze nnsa hɔ n'
Na fa tsimberɛw frɛ hɔn a wɔayew,
Wɔnam sum mu no, bra kan mu.

MHB 790
2 . Beebi a dɔm wo anaa ho atɔ pan,
Dɔmtutuw a wɔwɔ nsuano, nkurow m',
Nyimpa dodow pii na wɔnntsee
Asɛmpa no a edze ma hɛn n'.

MHB 790
3 . Ewuradze, ma W'asomfo mfrɛ
Mberantsɛ atam, nkɔdaa akomapirimfo,
Nguankuw a wɔapetse, ma hɔn nyina 
Mbɛka W'asomdwee nguankuw n' ho.

MHB 790
4 . Soma ma wɔnkɛka W'asɛm n'
Ma gyedzi aaba ma ekyingye aakɔ,
Bɔn eetu ma mberɛwyɛnyi eetsim,
Na akoma bobɔe aahyɛ dzen.

MHB 790
5 . Afei nsaase a woetwie nyina
Dza yɛhwɛ a ɔgye hɛn awerɛhow n',
Nkwa nsu bɛma efuw ahaebun,
Ma ndze aafow sor aakyerɛ W'ayɛyi

MHB 791
1 . Wɔabɔ akwankwan kɔ ekyirkyir,
Wɔdze yaw, ɔberɛ nye ɔkɔm kɔ;
Wonnyi guanhwɛfo pa a ɔkyerɛ
Ayarfo a wɔayɛ mberɛw no kwan.

MHB 791
2 . Ɔwo na ayɛ Guanhwɛfo no,
Guanhwɛfo pa a apon Wo nguan;
Boa hɔn ano na ma hɔn edziban,
Na asɔfo a asan mu eyi hɔn.

MHB 791
3 . Ma W'asɛnkafo n' adom nsɛm,
Ma woeenya etsiefo piinara;
Asɛnkafo a wɔkyerɛ abɔnfo
Kwan ba nkwagye bɔgya no ho.

MHB 791
4 . Bue hɔn ano, ma hɔn anotsewee
Ma hɔn totorobɛnto ndze,
Wɔmfa mfrɛ adasa mbra nkwagye m',
Wɔ Nyia owui maa hɔn n' ho gyedzi m'.

MHB 791
5 . W'enyimnyam nko na wɔnhwehwɛ;
O ma ɔdɔ mbu do hɔn akoma m',
Ma wɔngye ndzi na wɔmpaa m' nka,
Na wonyi W'ehumbɔbɔr ayɛw.

MHB 792
1 . Hɛn Wura, sɛ W'asɛm ntsi 
Yedua n-kwasɛm n' a,
Wo tum nsa no gugu do yi
Aba no befifir.

MHB 792
2 . W'adom ne ndam ara 
Na ɔbɛma ndɔbaa pii,
Na ɔadɔr agyedzifo a 
Wɔtse ma W'enyimnyam.

MHB 792
3 . Nsɛmpa n' ne nhyira nsu n', 
Ma ɔntɔ mma hɛn daa,
Ma tum a ɔsakyer akra n'
Ɔmbra W'asɔfoe do.

MHB 792
4 . Ma ɔdodowara 
Nnya dɔ a ɔdan 'koma n',
Ma W'adom ne dɛw nsiesie hɔn
Mma ɔsor dɛw kɛse n'.

MHB 793
1 . OWURA a Wo ndɔbaa 'nyikan
Kata asaase do,
Bea a abɔfo boaboa hɔn 
Ndɔbaa a wɔaber ano,
Gye nsa yi yɛ W'edwuma,
Ma hɛn akoma ntwer W', ndɔ W',
Dua hɔn do ma W'ahendzi
Mfi sor noho mbra ntsɛm.

MHB 793
2 . Soma hɔn Wo wenyin turo m',
Dɛ wɔyɛ W'apaafo n',
Wɔpɛ dɛ wɔsoa ndzesoa
Wɔ ɔberɛ nda mu ma Wo,
Owura, sɛ frɛ hɔn ba fie a,
Wɔnnkɛgye akatua koraa,
Ma wɔaakyɛ 'fona no a
Ɔma W'ahendzi ba n'.

MHB 793
3 . Nyame Egya, nye hɔn ntsena,
Nyame Ɔba, nye hɔn ntsena,
Nyame Sunsum, nye hɔn ntsena;
Onnyiewiei Ɔkorsa!
Yɛ hɔn asɔfo adehye,
Ma wɔmfa nsom Wo yie,
Fa W'amayɛ hyɛ hɔn ma,
Sesei nye daa nyina.   Amen.

MHB 794
1 . ƆDOMANKOMA Ɔba, Ɔdɔ a ɔkye,
Woara fa Wo tum kɛse no;
Ma adasa nhu W'ehumbɔbɔr,
Ma wonhu Wo nkwagye adom.

MHB 794
2 . Kyerɛ Wo dɔ no konyimdzi no,
Wo nko dzi hen akoma biara m'.
Kodu dɛ atamfo bɛtse W' tum,
Ma enyimnyam eewie adom edwuma n'.

MHB 794
3 . Adom Sunsum na ahoɔdzen tum,
Kan nsunyiwa nye dɔ wɔ asaase,
Fa W'ayarsa tum no petse
Ma ɔmpem aman nyina do.

MHB 794
4 . Sɔ ɔdɔ mapa gya wɔ hɛn akoma m',
Gyedzi ndwuma nda edzi hɛn mu;
Amma sor dɔm aannyɛ W'edwuma
Ntsɛntsɛm annsen hɛndze wɔ ha.

MHB 794
5 . Tease, Ɔkorsa 'Tsipɛmfo
Sor na asaase, wo ndwuma nyina
Mfa nhyira nyidzi, ntonton na ɔdɔ
Nsom Wo aber nyinara daa.

MHB 794
6 . W'ahendzi yɛ Krɔnn mprɛnsa,
Tum nyinara so yɛ Wodze;
Sɛ abɔdze nyina twa m' kɔ a,
W'enyimnyam a ɔmmpa da bɛhyerɛn.

MHB 795
1 . O NYAME N'asɔr, soɛr;
Fa Wo dɔ kandzea no,
Kandzea a onndum ara da
Wɔ asaase do nye sor.

MHB 795
2 . Fa nyansa na nokwar
Huw gya n' ma ɔndzɛw hoo,
Ɔdɔ na mbabun kan
Mpam wiadze m' fɛr mfi hɔ.

MHB 795
3 . Twuw abɔnsam enyim,
Yi akra fi efiadze,
Kyekyer akoma bobɔe
Ma dɛw na asomdwee.

MHB 795
4 . Adze biarà à ɔyɛ fɛw,
Adze biara a ɔtsen,
Ma ɔnyɛ fow dɛ mframa,
Ɔndɔɔso dɛ huntuma!

MHB 795
5 . Beebiara a sum wɔ no,
Tow kan nserɛmɛn gu hɔ,
Kɛpem dɛ enyim a esuam
Bohu Nyame enyigye.

MHB 795
6 . Se dasanyi biara,
'Birɛmpɔn nye kɔhweaban,
Dɛ ɔdɔ frɛɛ no awoo m'
Dɛ ɔhen na sɔfo.

MHB 796
1 . EWURADZE, W'asɔr a apon no
Rinyan fi nda m' mbea nyina a 
Wonyim dɛ adzekyee reba a
Okumfor n' beyi N'enyim;
Worinyan agye akoradze a
'Dze W' bɔgyaa a ɔsom bo tɔe n',
Na wɔatwer wo dwumason a
W'anwanwa wu no edzi.

MHB 796
2 . Gye W'ayɛyi nka wɔ Wo nsu ntsi,
Ekyir nsutɔ a ɔsom bo;
Yeyi Wo ayɛw dɛ Wo Sunsum
Tum no ekenyan hɛn bio;
Dɛ W'asɛmpa akoradze mapa n'
Wɔso dze rokɔ mbeambea,
Dɛ Egya n' N'apɛdze dzi mu.
Wɔ Wo nsamu epiratwa no mu.

MHB 796
3 . Ayɛyi nka Wo wɔ esiarfo a
Wɔper hwehwɛ hɔn a wɔayew,
Yɛtonton Wo dɛ ndze bi sua
W'ayɛyi ndwom no fofor;
Ntonton nka W'ayarfo a wɔper
Suo W'atar ano ndwow m' ntsi,
Yɛtonton Wo, hɔn a wɔagye edzi,
Ehu Wo dɔ enyadze n' ntsi.

MHB 796
4 . Fa Wo dzin ho dɔ no sɔ gya
Wɔ hɛn akoma nyina mu;
Kesi dɛ aman nyinara,
Bɛgye Wo mbeamudua no;
Ma hen enyi ntsim Wo mbeamudua n' do;
Nweɔn nkesi dɛ ebɛba,
Yɛabɔ asen do, asɔ nkandzea hoo;
Ewuradze, fa W' nkowaa kɔ fie.   Amen.

MHB 797
1 . EWURADZE, yɛbɔ mpaa bio
Ma mbofra a wɔwɔ ekyirkyir,
Hɔn a wɔnntsee Wo dzin mpo da,
Jesus dzin dɛɛdɛw n' pɛn koraa.

MHB 797
2 . Nkɔkoaba a ama hɔn ano
Gyina ekyirkyir asɔrdan mu,
Nwin ase, dze W'ayɛyi n'
Ma ndua, abosom nye abotan.

MHB 797
3 . Nsa nkakraba a edze ama
Hɔn dɛ wɔmfa nyɛ Wo pɛ n',
Wɔdze suro som, bɔ afɔr
Ma abosom a wonnhu, wɔnntse.

MHB 797
4 . O sor Hen, kyerɛkyerɛ hɔn ma
Wɔmfa akyɛdze nye ayɛyi
Mbrɛ Wo Ba a obowui dze
Kyerɛɛ Wo fakyɛ nkwagye dɔ n'.

MHB 798
1 . WO mba tow hɔn ndwom wɔ wiadze nyina:
Hɔn ndze bɔ m' dɛɛdɛw fi anee na boka;
Wohuhor Ewuradze a ɔma mbofra ahoɔdzen,
Jesus, hɛn Kwankyerɛfo, Sahen, Nyɛnko.

MHB 798
2 . Beebiara a Wo po asorɛkye bu
Gu nsupɔw mpoano mfesantsen nyina n';
Wohuhor hɔn Wura a nkwagye wɔ N' nko asɛm m',
Ɔno a No dɔ po etwa hɔn ho ehyia.

MHB 798
3 . Wo mba a ewia hyerɛn hɔn do wiadze mu,
Mbrɛ Asia esutsen fɔw asaase nyina do,
Wohuw ndwom ber a hɔn haban eyi ndɔbaa;
Ayɛyi nka Ewuradze a ɔnyɛn hɔn.

MHB 798
4 . Aman pii wɔ hɔ a bi nnhun W'enyim pɛn,
Mbofra akoma nnsɔɔ Wo dɛw nnhwɛɛ pɛn,
Naaso bohue W'adom egu hɔn nyina do;
Ma nkataasia na mberantsɛ W'ahoɔdzen.

MHB 798
5 . Ma mbofra ntow Wo ndwom wɔ wiadze nyina,
Hɔn ndze bɔ m' dɛɛdɛw, fi anee na boka;
Wohuhor Ewuradze a ɔma mbofra ahoɔdzen,
Jesus, hɛn Kwankyerɛfo, Sahen, Nyɛnko.

MHB 799
1 . BUBER no edu
Na edwumayɛfo no suar;
Hɛn mbofra dze yɛpɛ, 
Na yebesi dɛn\nAyɛ hɛn Wura No twadwuma yi bi?

MHB 799
2 . Hɛn nsa susuar koraa,
Hɛn asɛnka yɛ mberɛw,
Yenntum nnkyerɛ binom;
Yɛyɛ dɛn hwehwɛ,
Yɛyɛ hɛn Wura No twadwuma yi bi.

MHB 799
3 . Yɛbɔbɔ mpaa aboa,
Yɛbɛma bi dze aboa;
Yɛbɛpa hɛnho ekyir;
Kakra a yɛbɛyɛ n'
Bɔboa hɛn Wura No twadwuma yi bi.

MHB 799
4 . Ɔbɛyɛ bɛyɛ n'
Na mfe rutwa m' kɔ no,
Hɛn so bɛyɛ etwafo,
Yɛakɔ enyim ahoɔdzen m'
Yɛayɛ hɛn Wura No twadwuma yi bi.

MHB 8
1 . HOM nkotow Hen nyimnyamfo a ɔwɔ sor;
Mfa ndaase nkamfo No tum nye No dɔ;
Hɛn kyɛm nye hɛn Gyefo, Mbersantsen Panyin,
Ahoɔfɛw nye No buw, ayɛyi abɔ N' do.

MHB 8
2 . Hom ntow No tum nye N'adom so ho ndwom:
N'atar nye ekan, No buw pretetee;
N'ebufuw tseaseanam hye senaman fua tum,
No kwan yɛ sum wɔ ehum atsaban do.

MHB 8
3 . Asaase nye N'anwanwadze a wɔnnka:
Otumfo! Wo tum bɔɔ adze fi tsetse;
Nam 'mom a wɔnndan n' da etsim no pintsinn,
Na edze epo abᴐ no ho abᴐmprᴐw.

MHB 8
4 . W'ayamúyie no gyirama hɛn botúm aká?
Ogú ahom wɛ wimú, ɔhyerɛn kan mu;
Ofi akoko do pem siansian sar mu,
Na ɔsɔw fénemfénem wɔ bɔw nye
nyankom mu.

MHB 8
5 . Huntuma m' mbá a yɛnnkye so yɛyɛ mbérɛw,
Hɛn wérɛ hyɛ Wo mu, W'ayamúyie
mmpada;
Mbrɛ W'adom dua gow a otsim hɔ dú ewiei,
Hɛn Bɔfo, hɛn Gyefo, Pomfo na Dɔfo!

MHB 8
6 . Tum a wonnsusu! Dɔ a onnyi kabea!
Mbér a abɔfo dzé enyigye tow ndwom no,
Abɔdzé adedafamú so nam hɛn mbérɛwyɛ m'
Bɔtonton Wo atow ndwom eyi W' ayaw!
				   Amen.

MHB 80
1 . MEDZE m'akoma bɛkamfo Wo, 
Maka W'ayamuyie akyerɛ adasa; 
Mbrɛ W'adom ndwuma yɛ nwanwa a! 
Medze ndwom bɛkamfo Wo dzin,
M'bedzi dɛw wɔ m'Ewuradze mu,
M'bɛda W'ase, makamfo Wo.

MHB 80
2 . Ewuradze bɛgye No nkorɔfo,
Ɔboa hɔn wɔ ahokyer ber m',
Hɔn a bɔn nye hɛll ahyɛ hɔn do,
Hɔn a wonyim Wo n'bɔtwer Wo, 
Ɔwo a idzi W'anohoba do
Nnkɛma ɔkra biara ho akyer n'.

MHB 80
3 . Wɔdze Ewuradze atsɛmbu hu No;
Ɔboa bɔbɔfo a ohu amandze:
Onyim n'awerɛhow nyina;
Ɔwerɛhonyi nnkɛka mmɔn daa,
Nyia ɔdze su dua dze dɛw bobu,
Nyia ɔdze yaw hwehwɛ dze dɛw hu.

MHB 80
4 . Ɔkra bɔbɔfo a ɔhwɛ Wo
Otwar dɛ ohu W'enyim ara,
Na ne nsa ka W'adɔe nyina;
Dzebɔnyɛnyi a osu hwehwɛ W',
Nyia ɔhwehwɛ dɛ ɔgye dzi n',
Innkegyaa no dabiara da.

MHB 800
1 . AGYENKWA, kenyan amanaman,
Ma W'awerԑhow nsow aba,
Ma Wo yaw nye awerԑkyekyer
Ntwe amanamamfo mbrԑ Wo,
Wɔnka Wo mbeamudua ho nsԑm 
Nwanwa n' nkyerԑ aman nyina;
Na wonhu Wo W'enyimnyam mu 
Nye Wo mbɔbɔrhu beberee n'.

MHB 800
2 . Nkorɔfo a wonnyim Wo wɔ
Ekyirkyir nyina kɔn dɔ Wo;
Adasa kyi nyinsuwa wɔ W' ho,
Adasa pԑ W' mu ahomgye;
Wo ho nsukɔm dze hɔn mbordo
Dԑ sar a woetwa n' 'mon hia nsu n',
Wɔhwehwԑ Wo dԑ sor Nyame
Dԑ Nyia wokum N' maa abɔn.

MHB 800
3 . Agyenkwa, hwԑ! Nsupruw rotweɔn,
Atsen hɔn nsa, agyen hɔn enyi,
Rohwԑ Wo Sunsum ndwumafor n';
Rema ɔdɔ gya dzԑw, nyansa hyerԑn;
Ka asԑm n', ma ɔsԑnkafo n',
Ahoɔhar, ka ne gyirama
Kodu dԑ abɔdze nyina bɔtow
Eguambaa, W'enyimnyam ndwom.  Amen.

MHB 801
1 . GREENLAND nkokwaa nwinwim n' do,
India adantse abo ho,
Ebibiman, mbea a nsu pem
Fefa anhwea pii do so;
Fi tsetse esutsen pii mu,
Fi mbԑ asaase do,
Wɔfrԑ hԑn dԑ yenkeyi
Hɔn aman mfi mfom mpokyerԑ m'.

MHB 801
2 . Ana hԑn a sor nyansa
Eguar hԑn akra yi
Botum dze nkwa kan n' akam
Nyimpa a wɔtse sum mu?
N-kwagye o, nkwagye nye yi;
Hom mpaa m' nka enyigyesԑm n'
Nkodu dԑ aman nyina
Bohu Messiah N' dzin.

MHB 801
3 . Mframa, hom mbɔ N'asԑm n' nkɔ,
Na hom nsu, hom mpem daa,
Nkɔ nkodu wiadze n'ano
Dԑ enyimnyam po bun;
Kԑpem dԑ Eguambaa a wokum
No maa abɔn nyina n'
Pomfo, Ɔhen Bɔfo no,
Bԑsan ebedzi hen, dԑw m'.  Amen.

MHB 802
1 . EWURADZE, sor kyerԑ W'enyimnyam,
Wo nyansa hyerԑn woraba biara m';
Sԑ hԑn enyi bɔ W'asԑm n' do a
Yԑkenkan Wo dzin n'enyigye m'.

MHB 802
2 . Ewia a ɔhyerԑn, kan a odzi ndan,
'Nago na adzekyee ka W' tum kyerԑ,
Mbom Wo nhyira Nwoma a akyerԑw no
Kyerԑ Wo tsenenee na W'adom.

MHB 802
3 . Ewia, bosoom, na nworaba nngyaa
W'ayԑyi wɔ wiadze mu da;
Ntsi Wo nokwar hyԑԑ ase kyinii n'
Okodur aman nyina mu.

MHB 802
4 . W'asԑmpa no bԑtserԑw araa
Ma wiadze nyina eehu Wo nokwar n',
Kԑpem dԑ Christ behyira aman nyina a 
Kan anaa wi pue wɔ hɔ no.

MHB 802
5 . Tsenenee Ewia kԑse, pue,
Fa sor kan hyira sum wiadze yi,
W'asԑmpa n' bue ntsetsekwaa enyi,
Wo mbra yԑ krɔnn W'atsembu tsen!

MHB 802
6 . Eyԑ akra afofor dze bɔn kyԑ
Ma yehu Wo tum kԑse no,
Mo Wura, pepa m' bɔn, yԑ m' fofor,
Ma W'asԑm ngye m' taataa nkɔ sor.  Amen.

MHB 803
1 . BEGYABEGYA na sum
Tsee Wo tum asԑm no,
Na woguanee;
Yԑserԑ Wo, tsie hԑn,
Na beebiara a asԑmpa
Ne nserԑmԑn nnhyerԑn hɔ n',
Ma hɔ nyԑ kann.

MHB 803
2 . Ɔwo a edze ayarsa
Na adzehu gyee hԑn
W'atsaban do,
'Maa adamfo adwen m' tseew hɔn,
Efurafo hun adze,
Afei ma Wo kan nhyerԑn Adasa do.

MHB 803
3 . Nokwar na dɔ Sunsum,
Nkwa Mafo, Ebubur Krɔnn,
Tu faa bra ntsԑm;
Butuw nsu no enyi
Tow adom nserԑmԑn no,
Wiadze sum kebii n' mu
Ma hɔ nyԑ kann.

MHB 803
4 . Siarfo, Ɔkorsa Krɔnkrɔn,
Enyimnyam Ɔkorsa!
W'adom, dɔ tum n',
Tse dԑ popramee a 
Obubu n'asorԑkye,
Wɔ wiadze afanan nyina
Ma hɔ nyԑ kann.

MHB 804
1 . TSERƐW O asԑm tumfo tserԑw,
Tserԑw Ewuradze ahenman n' mu;
Beebiara a N'adom esiesie
N-kwa ama ɔsorfo.

MHB 804
2 . Nkwasԑm krɔnn a ɔyԑ dzen
Aman nyina kɔn dɔ Wo;
Tserԑw, ma sum kebii no mpa,
Na ma kan nhyerԑn wiadze.

MHB 804
3 . Soԑr hwԑ! Haban no reber
Ndɔbaa no bԑyԑ kԑse,
Etwafo no suar dodow,
Edwuma a wɔbԑyԑ no so.

MHB 804
4 . Otwa edwuma no Wura, ma hԑn
Dԑw na ahoɔdzen nyԑ W'edwuma,
Kԑpem dԑ aman nyina bohu
Wo kan n' hyerԑn na woesuro Wo.  Amen.

MHB 805
1 . YƐDZE Christ kyerԑ wiadze;
Yԑdze wiadze brԑ Christ,
Wɔ dɔ nsiyԑ m';
'Hiafo na mbɔɔdzifo
Mberԑwyԑfo, nkrumsifo,
Ayarfo, 'werԑhofo a,
Christ sa hɔn yar.

MHB 805
2 . Yɛdze Christ kyerԑ wiadze;
Yԑdze wiadze brԑ Christ
Wɔ mpaabɔ mu;
Akobɔfo a wɔyewee,
Hɔn a nna wonnyi etsidaa n',
Wɔpoon hɔn aboɔdzen
Fii enyidɔ mu.

MHB 805
3 . Yɛdze Christ kyerԑ wiadze;
Yԑdze wiadze brԑ Christ
Wɔ ɔnosԑԑ kor m';
Wɔnye hԑn yԑ edwuma n',
Wɔnye hԑn ka asԑm no,
Nye hԑn soa mbeamudua n'
Ma hԑn Wura Christ.

MHB 805
4 . Yԑdze Christ kyerԑ wiadze,
Yԑdze wiadze brԑ Christ,
Wɔ enyigye ndwom m';
Hɔn a wɔawo hɔn fofor n,
Wɔtwee hɔn fii bɔn mu,
Enyidar na ayԑyi m'
Dze hɔn maa Christ.

MHB 806
1 . MA ndwom no ndu wiadze nyina;
Jesus Christ yԑ Owura;
Tow N'ayԑyi, bɔ dawur,
Ntonton nka Ne dzin.
Ɔman na gyirama biara
Mbɔ m' ntow enyimnyam ndwom no.

MHB 806
2 . Ma ndwom no ndu wiadze nyina;
Omfi boka pomu,
Beebi a adzekyee hyԑ ase,
Dԑw, kan na ahotɔ m';
China dɔmpepe nsuo m' bi,
Mfa nkodu India mbew do.

MHB 806
3 . Ma ndwom no ndu wiadze nyina;
Beebi a Kramosom
Agye ntaa wɔ fie nyina m';
Twitwa hɔn mpokyerԑ m'
N'ayԑyi mfi Ebibirim pomu
Mfow nkodu ne mbew nyina do.

MHB 806
4 . Ma ndwom no ndu wiadze nyina;
Bea a hyewber yԑ dԑw n',
Ma ndwom krɔnkrɔn no mu nsԑm
Ngyegye ekyirekyir;
Kwaa tuntu sunkamm nyina mu 
Na mpoano so ngye ndwom n' do.

MHB 806
5 . Ma ndwom no ndu wiadze nyina,
Jesus Christ yԑ Hen,
Wiadze nyina mfa no ho nsԑm 
Mbɔ Ne dzin dawur;
Abɔdze nyina nsɔr No,
Mbersantsen na mfesantsen.   Amen.

MHB 807
1 . Ma hɛn honam ndzi mpaa 
Nkɔ mbew horow do mpo;
Jesus N'adɔfo dze, dabaa
Hɔn akoma yɛ kor.

MHB 807
2 . Jesus na odzii kan 
Dze hɛn akoma bɔɔm';
Hɛn a yɛnye N' nantsew fufuwn'
Ɔma yɛka koryɛm'.

MHB 807
3 . O wɔmma yɛnkɔ do 
Wɔ Jesus N'edwumam';
Asɔr ne Tsir konyimdzifo n',
Yɛnka No do ndzi nyim.

MHB 807
4 . Christ no wenyin ture n' 
Saw n'edwumafo enyim;
Na hwɛ! akatua kɛse no 
Da sor hɔ rotweɔn hɛn.

MHB 807
5 . O hɛn 'koma nye adwen 
N-da ho ara mfow sor,
Nkɔhwɛ hɛn ahomgye bea no,
Mbrɛ hɛn fona bɔ adze.

MHB 807
6 . Hɔ dwumadzen nyina, 
Nye amandzehu nye yaw
Wotwa do wɔ siar mpoano hɔ;
Hɔ yehyia a yɛmmpaam' bio.

MHB 807
7 . Ahomka bea dɛɛdɛw, 
Hɔ na abɔfo hyia hɛn,
Hɔ yebohu hɛn enyim bio,
Na yeekyiakyia hɛnho.

MHB 807
8 . Abakamfo Asɔr, 
Hɔn nhyira n' yebenya,
Na yɛdze dɛw ayɛ abɔtsir
Yɛakɔ sor ahomgyem'.

MHB 808
1 . AGYENKWA pa, bɔ Wo nkowaa hyew

Wɔdaa mpokyerԑ m', Ɔwo siaan hɔn,
Wɔrokɔpon nkowaa binom so;
Ka hɔn ho daa,
W'abasa nko na ɔgye nkwa.

MHB 808
2 . Woegyaa nyԑnko, fie na ebusua,

W'anohoba na ogya hɔn,
Ber a wotwa po na asaase;
O ka hɔn ho!
Woara gya hɔn dwudwoodwo.

MHB 808

Ma enyidar yԑ bisiww,

Wɔnntse hwee dԑ ekyingye suro a,

Tsie hɔn nkrumsi, kaa hɔn su.

MHB 808
4 . Sԑ wɔnnsow aba biara,
Na hɔn fona reyԑ ayԑ gyan a,

Na ma hɔn enyidar ngyina;
Na ahyԑ hɔn dzen n',
Kenyan hɔn nsiyԑ no bio.

MHB 808
5 . Sԑ wɔwɔ atamfo finimfin a,

Sԑ konyim ba hɔn dwumadzi mu a,
Ma Wo nkowaa mbrԑ hɔnho adze,
Mma nngya hɔn ekyir,
Kԑpem dԑ wohu W', wɔ sor.

MHB 808
6 . Hɔ na wobohu dza woduaa n'
Wɔ asaase do n' afebɔɔ,
Hɔ na wɔnye Wo bԑtsena daa,
Ɔwo a ekora Wo nkowaa sɔnn;
Na wɔdze dԑw
Beyi Wo nkotoo ayԑw.   Amen.

MHB 809
1 . MURUNNTUM nnkyerԑ siantsir a Nyia abɔfo sɔr N',
Dze No dɔ bɔto hɔ ama nyimpa mba,
Anaa ɔyԑ 'Guanhwԑfo n' ɔhwehwԑ hɔn a wɔayew,

Minyim 'yi mbom dԑ Ɔbaabun Mary woo No,

Na dԑ ɔtsenaa Nazareth yԑԑ edwuma,
Dԑm ntsi na Agyenkwa n', wiadze
Agyenkwa no aba.

MHB 809

Anaa mbrԑ wobubuu n'akoma mbeamudua n' do
Ɔsoaa yaw ahenkyԑw n' mfe eduasa ebiasa.

Ɔpepa hԑn bɔn na otu hԑn suro;
Oyi afonafo hɔn adzesoa durdur kyen;
'Yi ntsi na Agyenkwa n', wiadze Agyenkwa no wɔ ha.

MHB 809

Na obohu dza Ɔnoara oduae no,
Na da bi N'ewia bԑhyerԑn 'nyimnyam mu,
Ber a ɔno Agyenkwa n', wiadze Agyenkwa no wobohu N'.

MHB 809
4 . Murunntum nnkyerԑ mbrԑ wiadze nyina bɔsom N',
Ber a ɔkasa a, ehum biara taa dzinn,
Anaa nyia obotum akyerԑ dԑw kԑse no,
Ber a dɔ ahyԑ nyimpa nyina akoma mu ma.

Na nyimpa ahorow ndze a atow ndwom bi;
Asaase na sor beyi hɔn ano nkorkor;
Afei dze Agyenkwa, wiadze Agyenkwa no yԑ Hen!

MHB 81

MHB 810

MHB 811

MHB 812

MHB 813

MHB 814

MHB 815

MHB 816

MHB 817

MHB 818

MHB 819

MHB 82

MHB 820

MHB 820
2 . Jesus enndze sika
Na dwetԑ tɔɔ hԑn;
Mbom W'adehye bɔgya n'
Ayԑ hԑn ahenkyԑw,
Ewora nhyira nsu gu
Nyia ɔba Wo hɔ n' do,
Ama yeenya pԑ bi,
Ayԑ hԑn adehye.
Wo dɔ a ɔapon hԑn ntsi,
W'adom nwanwa n' ntsi,
Yewɔ W'afa Gyefo,
Yԑyԑ Wodze daa.

MHB 820
3 . Sԑ ɔko n' y hu mpo a,
'Tamfo n' yԑ dzen mpo a,
Ɔhen N'akofo n' dze,
'Biara runntum hԑn.
Yedzi N'ekyir yi dze,
Konyimdzi wɔ hԑn;
No nokwar a ɔnnsakyer n'
Ma hen awerԑhyԑm'.
Yԑdɔm W'akafo no,
W'adom nwanwa n' ntsi,
Yewɔ W'afa Gyefo,
Yԑyԑ Wodze daa.

MHB 820
4 . Wɔayԑ hԑn nsordaafo
Wɔ ananabea ha;
Yԑyԑ agyedzifo ma
Hԑn Sahen No kuw.
Adehyesom no mu,
Mma yԑnnyԑ nwin da;
Hom mma yengyina pintsinn,
Nokwar m', 'kokodur m'.
Hԑn Wura, ebɔkora, hԑn,
W'adom nwanwa n' ntsi,
Yԑwɔ W'afa, Gyefo;
Yԑyԑ Wodze daa.

MHB 821
1 . Hom ngyina, hom ngyina mma Jesus! 
Mbeamudua ho nsordaafo;
Hom mma N'ahen-frankaa n' do;
Onnyi dɛ ofi nsa
Obedzi No dɔm kan fi
Konyimm' akɔ konyimm'
Kyerɛ wɔka atamfo nyina hyɛ
Ma Christ dzi hen ampa.

MHB 821
2 . Hom ngyina, hom ngyina mma Jesus! 
Hom ntsie abɛn ne frɛ;
Hom nduom ɔko kɛse n' mu
Wɔ N'enyimnyam da yim'!
Mbarimba, afei hom nsom no
Mfa ntsia atamfo dɔm n'
Hom mfa ndam ngyina mbusu ano,
Hom ntutu dɔm nka dɔm.

MHB 821
3 . Hom ngyina, hom ngyina mma Jesus! 
Hom ngyina N'ahoɔdzen nkom'
Honam abaw bɛpa hom;
Mma hom nntwer hombo da.
Hom nhyɛ Christian akontar,
Na hom nweɔn asɔryɛm',
Edwumayɛ mu o, mbusu mu o
Mma hom nntwa abrɔdɔ.

MHB 821
4 . Hom ngyina, hom ngyina mma Jesus! 
Aperdzi no rennkyɛr 
Ndɛ dze ɔko mu dede
'Kyena konyimdzifo ndwom a 
Nyia obedzi konyim no
Wɔbɛma n' nkwa ahenkyɛw
Ɔnye enyimnyam Hen no
Bedzi hen afebɔɔ.

MHB 822
1 . Christian n-sordaafo, 
Hom nduom akono!
Jesus Ne mbeamudua n'
Dzi hɛn enyim kan.
Hɛn Hen Christ etu sa 
Roko tsia tamfo n',
Hom nduom n-seraban do,
Hom nhwɛ ne mfrankaa n'.
  
    Christian n-sordaafo, 
    Hom nduom akono! 
    Jesus Ne mbeamudua n' 
    Dzi hɛn envim kan.

MHB 822
2 . Yɛma Ne frankaa n' do a, 
Abɔnsam dɔm gu;
Dɛm a Christ akofo,
Hom nkedzi konyim!
Yɛbɔ se yi ayɛw a,
Hɛll fapem wosow;
Enuanom, hom ntow ndwom,
Hom mma hom ndze do.

MHB 822
3 . Nyame N'asɔr tse dɛ 
Dɔm a wɔyɛ dzen:
Yɛnam ahotsewfo
Hɔn anamɔn mu.
Hɛn mu nnyi mpaapaamu,
Yɛyɛ adze kor.
Hɛn botae, hɛn nkyerɛkyerɛ
Hɛn dɔ nyina kor.

MHB 822
4 . Ahengua botutu, 
Ahenman etwam',
Na Jesus N'asɔr dze
Betsim afebɔɔ;
Samanadze akoban
Runntum ahyɛ do:
Christ Noara na ɔkae,
N'asɛm so yɛ hɔ.

MHB 822
5 . Mo nkorɔfo e, hom mbɔdɔm 
Egyigye kuw yi;
Hom mfa hom ndze mbɔto
Hɛn konyim ndwom yim':
Enyimnyam na nkamfo
N-ka hɛn Hen Christ!
Yi nyimpa na abɔfo
Bɔtow afebɔɔ.

MHB 823
1 . HƐN nkwa suma Christ mu wɔ Nyame m',
Hԑn nkwa bopue ntsԑntsԑm,
Eeyi N'enyimnyam akyerԑ mbeambea,
Wɔ no nkorɔfo nyina m'.

MHB 823
2 . Hԑn akra kitsa No tum nsamu,
Ɔbɔkora hɔn daa;
Emi na ɔwo begyina Ne nkyԑn
Wɔ Zion bepɔw do.

MHB 823
3 . O enyigye nhyiamu bԑn a!
Yebowuna ntar fitaa,
Ekitsa mberԑnkɔnson daa,
Na yԑasoa ahenkyԑw.

MHB 823
4 . Afei yԑmfa no dԑm wɔ mbra m'
Na yԑnko nkɔ hԑn enyim;
Yԑnkaa ewiei no hԑn adwen nu
Ndwen mpirenyimadze no ho.

MHB 824
1 . HOM mma yɛnye sor adͻfo a
Woenya akyɛdze n’ mbͻ m',
Yɛmfa ͻkͻr dͻ atsaban do
Yentu nkͻ sor dɛw mu:
Wͻmma ahotsewfo nye hͻn a,
Wͻkͻ ’nyimnyam m' ntow ndwom,
Na hɛn Hen N’asomfo a wͻwͻ
Sor na ase nyina yɛ kor.

MHB 824
2 . Ebusua kor a yɛtse No mu.
Sor nyé ase Asͻr kor,
Mbom sesei, esutsen twa hɛn ntamu,
Owu esutsen tséabea n’;
Nyame tseasefo nsordaafo a
Yɛhyɛ No tum ase;
No dͻm no bi etwa esupramee,
Bi so gu do rutwa.

MHB 824
3 . Mpem du rokͻ onnyiewie fie’,
Dɛm awͻse ber yi;
Na hɛn so yɛaba berano,
Na hɛn enyi da owu kwan;
Sesei mpo yɛnyé edzikamfo n'
To nsa wͻ gyedzi mu,
Kyià ekuw a bͻgye atsew hͻn ho
Wͻ onnyiewiei mpoano.

MHB 824
4 . Hɛn so hɛn akra bͻkͻ ekɛka
'Nyimnyamfo akra no ho,
Yɛatsea mu Sahen N’ahyɛnsew n’ ho,
Ber a yɛatse N’abɛn ndze n’;
O nkyɛ yeesuo Kwangyafo n’ mu!
Nkyɛ wͻama hɛn asɛm no!
Dͻm Ewuradze, paa asorɛkye n' mu bra,
Bɛfa hɛn kͻ heaven.    Amen.

MHB 825
1 . NYAME ahotsewfo, hɔn haw etwa m',
Woedzi konyim wɔ ɔbra ko yi m',
Wonnhia kyɛm na nkrantsee biara;
Wobubu mu gu hɔn Wura enyim;
O 'hotsewfo a woehyira hɔn,
Jesu N'anan ase na wɔhom.

MHB 825
2 . Nyame ahotsewfo ewie kyin,
Wonntu fona mbirika bio,
Wɔnntɔ bitsi, wɔnnhwe ase bio,
'Tamfo nnhyɛ hɔn do, suro nnyi hɔ;
O 'hotsewfo a woehyira hɔn,
Wɔhom yie wɔ dɛm fie pa n' mu.

MHB 825
3 . Nyame ahotsewfo bra abɔ adze,
Wodwir berɛww wɔ 'nyigye mpoano,
Wonnsuro ehum dzendzen no bio,
'Sorɛkye dzendzen biara nnyi hɔ;
O 'hotsewfo a woehyira hɔn,
Wɔhom yie wɔ asomdwee bea n' do.

MHB 825
4 . 'Hotsewfo Nyame, yesu frɛ W';
O Agyenkwa, dzi ma hɛn sor;
Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, Gyafo, Nyɛnko,
Fa W'adom boa hɛn kesi ewiei;
O 'hotsewfo a woehyira hɔn,
Atsena paradise ahomgye m'.  Amen.

MHB 826
1 . NYAME, agyedzifo a woewu
Da ho ara nye hɔn Tsir tse ase,
Yɛnye hɔn wɔ Wura kor;
Yehyira Wo dzin krɔnkrɔn no
Wɔ W'ahotsewfo a woefi mu,
Wɔ Wo gyedzi na suro m' ntsi.

MHB 826
2 . Adom kor a okura hɛn no mu
Yentsiw hɔn a wodzii W'ekyir no,
Na yɛnye hɔn aakyɛ
Ɔsor dɛw akatua kɛse n';
Mbɔbɔrhu Egya, dom hɛn yi
Wɔ hɛn Pomfo no ntsi.   Amen.

MHB 827
1 . HƆN edzin yɛ ahemfo edzin,
'Sor adehye a;
Wiadze ndzepa mu dɛw n',
Wɔpoow ne nyina.

MHB 827
2 . 'Hemfo a wɔdze nkrantsee
Na akokyɛm koe;
Nyame N' nkonyimdzifo
Wɔ akono.

MHB 827
3 . Hɔn wiadze nda yɛɛ yaw
Wɔ ɔtan yerɛyerɛw m',
Ɔbra a enyigye nnyi m',
Na owu ara nko.

MHB 827
4 . Mbusu n' mpo nhyira wɔ mu
Dɛ yaw nda n' so;
Nyimpa afɔbu wɔ ase;
Sor Egya n' ayɛyi a.

MHB 827
5 . Wɔakyekyer kuropɔn bi
Dze ama hɔn;
Ɔwɔ enyimnaymm kɛse,
Jerusalem!

MHB 827
6 . Adehye bɔgya gyee n'

Hɛn mu kɔ fie.

MHB 827
