MHB 828
1 . 'HOTSEWFO nsordaafo ɔpedu,
Ɔpedu wɔapon hɔn
Hyehyɛ hɔn ntar hyirenn rofow
Kan bepɔw tsentsen no;
Owu na bɔn ho akodzi no
Woewie ko ampaara;
Hom mbuebue sika mbotsen no,
Ma nkonyimdzifo n' mbra m'.

MHB 828
2 . Ɔhyew do hallelujah ahyɛ 
Asaase na ɔsor ma!
N-sankutsen apem robɔ 
Dze kyerɛ konyim a abɛn n'!
O dɛm da yi ntsi na wɔbɔɔ
Wiadze na nyimpa nyina!
O dɛw a oetua fona dadaw
Nyina kaw pem mbɔho!

MHB 828
3 . Dɛw nkyiakyia bi a obesi
Canaan enyika mpoano a!
'Nyɛnkoyɛ a no mu atsetsew,
Bɔfrɔm bio a onnkogu!
Na enyiwa a nyinsu hyɛ n' ma n'
Dze dɛw bɛhyerɛn da no;
Ngyanka benya hɔn egyanom,
'Kunafo werɛ nnkɔhow.

MHB 828
4 . Fa Wo nkwagye kɛse no bɛn,
Eguambaa a bɔn ntsi iwui;
Hyehyɛ hɔn a afrɛ hɔn n' nyina ma
Na fa Wo tum dzi hen,
Aman nyina Ahwehwɛdze, bra,
Wo ndɔmmumfo afe fie;
W'anohoba ahyɛnsew n' mpue wimu;
Ɔhen Ba Agyenkwa, bra. Amen.

MHB 829
1 . TSIE! Mfeduonum 'fahyɛ ndwom;
Ne dede tse dɛ aprandaa;
Anaa po a ɔapram kɛse
Bu asorɛkye bogu mpoano,
Hallelujah! Ewuradze
Nyame Tumfo bedzi hen;
Hallelujah! Ma asɛm no
Ntahye wiadze nyinara.

MHB 829
2 . Hallelujah! Tsie! Ndze no a
Ofi bun mu kɔ wimu no,
Nyan abɔdze nyinara,
Wɔ sor, ase beebiara 
Wɔabobɔw Gyefo frankaa n';
Ɔnntwe nkrantsee; ɔka a ɔba m';
Na wiadze yi mu ahenman
Nyina yɛ Ne Ba N'ahenman.

MHB 829
3 . Ɔdze tum a onnyi mbanano,
Bedzi hen wɔ mbea nyina;
Sɛ ɔsor bobɔw kɔ mpo a
Ɔbɔkɔ do eedzi hen;
Ewiei n', dasanyi n' tamfo n'
Bɔhwe ase wɔ N' poma ase;
Hallelujah! Nyame m' Christ,
Christ m' Nyame, yɛ adze kor.

MHB 83
1 . EGYA No dɔ na ɔwoo No
Ansaana wiadze reba,
Ɔno nye Alpha na Omega,
Ɔyɛ ahyɛse na ewiei;
Sesei ndzɛmba na dza etwa m'
Na mfe a ɔreba nyina,
Afebɔɔ na afebɔɔ.

MHB 83
2 . Ɔdze N'asɛm bɔɔ adze nyina;
Ɔhyɛɛ dɛ ɔmbra na ɔbae;
Asaase, ɔsor na po nyina,
Ka bɔ mu yɛ wiadze kor;
Ndzɛmba a wohu bosoom hyerɛn, 
Na dza wɔhom wi yi ase,
Afebɔɔ na afebɔɔ.

MHB 83
3 . Oyi na tsetse adzehufo
Bɔɔ anosɛɛ toow No ho ndwom;
Nyia nkɔnhyɛfo no dze hɔn ndze
Kaa No ho asɛm nokwar mu;
Afei Nyia enyi daa N'kwan n' hyerɛn;
Ma abɔdze nyi Ewuradze ayɛw,
Afebɔɔ na afebɔɔ.

MHB 83
4 . Afei mpanyin na mbofra nyina
Nka mbɔ m' ntow Wo ndwom dɛɛdɛw;
'Baawa na no wura nyi' W'ayɛw,
Mbofra so ntow W'ayɛyi,
Mbanyimba, mbasiaba mbɔ m' ntow, 
Mfa akoma pa nyi W' ayɛw,
Afebɔɔ na afebɔɔ.

MHB 83
5 . Ɔsorsor, hom ntonton No;
Abɔfo dɔm nyi N'ayɛw;
Etumfo nyina nkotow No,
Hom nkrɔn hɛn Nyame Hen no;
Mma tɛkyerɛma biara nnyɛ komm,
Ma ndze nyinara ntow ndwom,
Afebɔɔ na afebɔɔ.   Amen.

MHB 830
1 . TSIE! Ahotsewfo hɔn ndze da m',
Gyegye po hyɛnhyɛn no ho:
Alleluja! Alleluja!
Alleluja nka Ewuradze.
Dɔntutum a wonntum nnkan hɔn
Dɛ nworaba gyina 'nyimnyam mu;
Woewuna fitaa na wokitsa
Konyimdzi ho mberɛnkɔnson.

MHB 830
2 . Wofi ahohia mu aba,
Wɔahor hɔn ntar bɔgya n' mu,
Jesus bɔgyaa n' atsew hɔn ho;
Wɔsɔɔ hɔn hwɛe, wogyinaa dzen;
Wɔsereew hɔn guu fiadze,
Siiw hon abo, paa hɔn seradaa;
Wɔnam Christ No tum do woedzi
Owu na Satan do nyim.

MHB 830
3 . Wɔdze Wo mbeamudua bɔɔ nsera;
Woedzi W'ekyir edzi konyim,
Ɔwo a eyɛ nkwagye Sahen,
Hɔn Agyenkwa na hɔn Hen.
Ao, Ewuradze, enyigye m' na
Wɔnye W' berɛɛ na wɔnye W' wui!
Wɔnam owu do enya daa nkwa,
Wɔawo hɔn enyimnyam mu!.

MHB 830
4 . Nyame mu Nyame, Ba kortoo,
Kan mu Kan, Immanuel,
Wo nyimpadua mu na dabaa
Ahotsewfo bɔ mu tsenae.
Hue W'amayɛ no gu hɛn do,
Ama daa nyina yaasɔr
Nyame Egya, Nyame Ɔba 
Na Nyame Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn.  Amen.

MHB 831
1 . Ma m' gyedzi ntsaban na muntu 
Nkɔ fua n' mu hɔ nkɔhwɛ
Sor esiarfo hɔn dɛw kɛse n',

MHB 831
2 . Ber bi nna wogyam wɔ ase ha, 
Na wɔkaa m' kyii nyinsu;
Wɔnye bɔn, ekyingye na suro
Dzii aper dzen dɛ hɛn so.

MHB 831
3 . M'bisa dɛ hɔn konyim n' fir hen?

MHB 832
1 . Ahotsewfo a apon hɔn edwuma a 
Wiadze enyim wɔbɔɔ Wo dzin no ntsi,
O Jesus, nhyira nka Wo dzin daa daa.
                             Alleluia!

MHB 832
2 . Hɔn Bontan, Aban, Ahoɔdzen, nye 'Wo, 
Eyɛɛ hɔn Sahen wɔ nkodzen no mu;
Sum kadoo no mu hɔn nokwar kan kor.
                             Alleluia!

MHB 832
3 . O ma Wo nkowaa anokwafo wɔnko 
M-barimbam' dɛ tsetse ahotsewfo n',
Ama wɔnye hɔn eenya ahenkyɛw no!
                            Alleluia!

MHB 832
4 . Siar nkitaho bit! fɛkuwbɔ krɔnkrɔn! 
Yɛper mberɛwm', wɔhyerɛn enyimnyam mu;
Naaso wɔnye hɛn bɔm' yɛ kor Wo mu.
                             Alleluia!

MHB 832
5 . Sɛ aperdzi n' yɛ dzen, ko n' war m-po a, 
Konyim ndwom no fi 'kyirekyir du asomu,
Ma akoko yɛ dur, abaw hyɛ dzen.
                             Alleluia!

MHB 832
6 . Witɔree dze sika hyerɛn wim' guann, 
Ɔnnkyɛr na akofo enya ahomgye.
Wohu siar Paradise no mu dɛw no.
                             Alleluia!

MHB 832
7 . Hwɛ! enyimnyam da bi so ɔreba a, 
Ahotsewfo n' bɔsoɛr konyimdzi mu,
Enyimnyam Hen no bopue No kwan do.
                             Alleluia!

MHB 832
8 . Dɔm kukuankoma fi wiadze nyina 
Dze ndwom bɛpem bota mbotsen no mu,
Woeyi Egya, Ba, nye Sunsum ayɛw;
                            Alleluia!

MHB 833
1 . Woanam' wɔhyɛ futuw yi, 
Wɔhyerɛn sen wigyinae mpo 'i?
Kan no mu mba a wodzi kan,
Wɔbɛn Nyame N'ahengua 'i?
Yinom na wɔsoaa mbeamudua n',
Wodzii Christ ho dase pa,
Hɔn Wura N'asɛ ntsi wowui,.
Wɔkaa Nyame a owu n' do n'.

MHB 833
2 . Wofir fona kɛsem' bae, 
Wɔdze gyedzi hoor hɔn ntar
Wɔ Eguambaa n' bɔgyaa mu,
Bɔgya a ɔma ahosan krɔnn:
N-tsi wɔbɛn ahengua n',
Na wɔsom hɔn Wura daa daa,
Nyame ko No nkorɔfo mu.
Nyame pɛ N'apapafo.

MHB 833
3 . Wɔkyɛn ekonyimdzifo, 
Ha na hɔn nsɔhwɛ asa;
Hɔn berɛ nyina etwam',
Kɔm na nsukɔm nnyi hɔ bio;
Wɔnntse ɔhyew a ɔyɛ dzen a
Ofir ewia ne mfirii no mu,
Wɔtse ahomka mbew no mu,
Domankoma bea no do.

MHB 833
4 . Nyia ɔtse ahengua n' do n', 
Bɛnyɛn hɔn aber nyina,
Dze nkwadua no bɛnyɛn hɔn,
Dze hɔn bɔkɔ nkwa nsu n' ho;
Bɛpa hɔn mbusu nyina,
Nye hɔn ehiadze biara,
Ɔbɛpepa hɔn nyinsuwa.
Ɔdze dɔ bɛhyɛ hɔn ma.

MHB 834
4 . O nkyɛ W'asɛm krɔnkrɔn n'
Aatahye wiadze nyina,
Hɔn nyina aayɛ ano kor
Aama dɛw ndze no do:
Hallelujah!
Yɛbɔtow ndwom
Ama Nyame,
Hallelujah!

MHB 835
1 . JESUS dze nkwagye reba n'
Zion hɔ na ɔbae,
Mbofraba nyina soɛree
Wɔtoow Hosanna maa N'.
Hɔn ho annyɛ No ebufuw
Na ɔtse abowa do n',
Ɔmaa wɔkaa No do ara:
Hɔn ndwom yɛɛ N' enyigye.

MHB 835
2 . Na osiandɛ Ewuradze
Da ho dɔ mbofra ntsi,
Kaansa n-dɛ odzi hen
Wɔ sor Zion m-po a,
Yɛbɔfɔr Ne frankaa ho,
Ɔhen Jesus frankaa n',
Na yɛatsea n' dɛ, Hosanna 
N-ka David ne Ba.

MHB 835
3 . Osiandɛ sɛ hɛn yeenntum 
Yɛannkamfo hɛn Pomfo a,
Abo bɔtow Hosanna
Ahyɛ hɛn enyito.
Na aso hɛn ano nko
Na yɛdze bɔsom No?
Dabi? Yɛdze hɛn akoma
So bɛma Ewuradze.

MHB 836
1 . MBOFRA nkumaa tseaa mu toow
Hosanna enyigye mu;
Ahemfie na asɔrfi mu,
Ndwom dɛɛdɛw no gyegyee;
Jesus a ohyiraa hɔn,
Fuaa hɔn No bomu no,
Mbofra n' toow ayɛyi ndwom maa N',
Ndwom bɔkɔɔ a odzi mu.

MHB 836
2 . Wofi Olivet kaa No do,
Wɔ enyigye dɔm no mu,
Wohiim konyim mberɛnkɔnson,
Wɔyɛɛ dede kɛse.
Abɔfo hyirenn toow bi,
Wɔ wimu kann n' ekyir,
Hosanna ɔwɔ sorsor!
'Nyimnyam nka sor Nyame.

MHB 836
3 . Wɔtotow Olive ndubaa
Fɛɛfɛw pii guu famu,
Na hɔn ndwom dɛɛdɛw gyeyee
Salem mbepɔw no do.
Nyimpa na abɔfo Wura
Tse abowa do kɔr bɔkɔɔ,
Na ɔammpow dɛ mbofraba
Bɛpem edzi N'ekyir.

MHB 836
4 . Hosanna wɔ ɔsorsor!
Yɛtow tsetse ndwom no;
Na Christ nye hɛn Pomfo no,
'Sor Wura nye hɛn Hen:
O wɔmma yɛmfa akoma,
Nkwa na ndze nyi N' ayɛw,
Na yendzi dɛw daa nyina,
Wɔ N'enyim 'nyigye n' mu.  Amen.

MHB 837
1 . Jerusalem mbofraba 
Toow Jesus N'ayɛyindwom;
Ndɛ mber yi mbofraba so
Bɔm' tow Gyefo N'ayɛyi:
Tsie! mbofra kekam' dzendzen 
Dɛ, Hosanna nka hɛn Hen.

MHB 837
2 . Wɔkyerɛ hɛn Ewuradze dɔ, 
Wɔkyerɛ hɛn N'asɛm kenkan,
Wɔkyerɛ hɛn ɔsor do kwan:
Yi ntsi yeyi Nyame ayɛw.

MHB 837
3 . Abaatan na akyerɛkyerɛfo, 
Mpanyin na mbofra nhur ndwom n';
Wɔmma do kɛsenara
Ma Hosanna ngyigye wim'.

MHB 838
1 . JESUS, fi enyimnyam m'
Yɛ aso ma hɛn:
Yebu ntwɛr wɔ W'enyim a,
Tsie mbofra ayɛyi.

MHB 838
2 . Kaansa eyɛ krɔnn mpo a,
Heaven Hen tumfo,
Yɛtow W'ayɛyi ndwom a,
Ebɔkotow etsie.

MHB 838
3 . Mbofraba nkumaa a
Yɛyɛ mberɛw, yɛfom;
Gyefo, wowaw kora hɛn,
Wɔ heaven kwan mu.

MHB 838
4 . Hɛn Wura, gye hɛn fi bɔn m',
Hwɛ hɛn do daa daa;
Boa hɛn ma yɛndɔ Wo,
Yi hɛn bɔn fi hɔ.

MHB 838
5 . Afei, sɛ efrɛ hɛn
Kɔ hɛn ɔsor fie a,
Yɛbɛgye do dɛw mu;
Agyenkwa, yɛaba!

MHB 839
1 . NYƐNKO bi wɔ hɔ ma mbofra
Wɔ sor fua kan n' ekyir,
Nyɛnko a ɛnnsakyer da,
No dɔ so mmbɔ adze da,
Ɔnntse dɛ nyimpa m' ndamfo a
Wɔnye mber sesa no,
Nyɛnko 'i som bo aber biara,
Ɔwɔ dzin mapa bi.

MHB 839
2 . Fie bi wɔ hɔ ma mbofraba
Wɔ sor fua kan n' ekyir,
Hɔ, Jesus dzi hen 'nyimnyam m',
Asomdwee na dɛw fie.
Fie bi nntse dɛm wɔ ase ha,
Anaadɛ ɔnye n' bɛsɛ;
'Siandɛ obiara wɔ enyigye a
Onnkehia enyigye bio.

MHB 839
3 . Ndwom bi wɔ hɔ ma mbofraba
Wɔ sor fua kan n' ekyir,
Ndwom a wɔtow no dodow mpo a 
Ɔnnkɔfon obiara,
Ndwom a ɔsor abɔfo mpo
Nnkotum atow ara da;
Wonnyim Christ dɛ Agyenkwa,
Mbom wɔsom No dɛ Ɔhen.

MHB 839
4 . Atar bi wɔ hɔ ma mbofra
Wɔ sor fua kan n' ekyir
Na sanku a ɔbɔ ndwom dɛɛdɛw
Na konyim mberɛnkɔnson,
Ne nyina som bo wɔ sor,
Na wohu n' Christ mu nko;
O hom mbra, mbofraba pa,
Ma ne nyina nyɛ homdze

MHB 84
1 . Enyimnyam nye ntonton nka 
Wo, hɛn Hen Agyenkwa,
Ɔwo a mbofra ndze dɛɛdɛw,
Toow Hosanna maa Wo!

MHB 84
2 . Ɔwo nye Israel Hen, 
Ɔhen David ne Ba a
Enam Ewuradze dzin mu
Reba dɛ hɛn siar Hen.
	Enyimnyam nye¬—

MHB 84
3 . Abɔfo dɔm nyinara 
Kamfo Wo Nyame manm':
Nyimpa nye abɔdze nyina
Bɔ ose gye hɔn do.
	Enyimnyam nye¬—

MHB 84
4 . Hebrewman mu nkorɔfo dze 
Mberɛnkɔnson huaa Wo;
Hɛn so yɛdze ayɛyi
Nye mpaabɔ ba W' enyim.
	Enyimnyam nye¬—

MHB 84
5 . Irikehyia mbusu no, 
Wɔtoow ndwom yii W' ayɛw;
N- dɛ a wɔakrɔn Wo sor yi,
Hɛn so yehuhor Wo.
	Enyimnyam nye¬—

MHB 84
6 .  Egyee Jewfo ayɛyi; 
Gye hɛn so hɛn mpaabɔ,
Ɔhen dɔyɛfo, yamuyiefo a
Ndzepa nyina yɛ W' fɛw. 
 	Enyimnyam nye¬—

MHB 84
7 . Enyimnyam nye ntonton nka 
Wo, hɛn Hen Agyenkwa, 
Ɔwo a mbofra ndze dɛɛdɛw, 
Toow Hosanna maa Wo! 
	Enyimnyam nye¬—

MHB 840
1 . M'EGYA Nyame dɔɔ me no,
Ɔmaa Ne Ba yɛɛ m' nyɛnko;
'Maa Ne Ba faa mo frɔdɔɔ,
Soaa adze nyina wɔ me ntsi.

MHB 840
2 . Jesus da ho tse dɛm daa
Dɛ mbrɛ ɔbae tsetseber do n';
Dɛ mo nua a ɔbɛn me daa,
Da ho per weɔn m'anamɔn.

MHB 840
3 . M'besi dɛn etua Wo dɔ kaw,
Ɔsor dɔm nyina Wura?
Emi abofra, mowɔ 'bɛn
Brɛ Ɔwo hɛven Ɔhen?

MHB 840
4 . Medze moho nyina ma Wo:
Ma me ntsena mma W'enyimnyam,
Ma menka Wo do daa nyina,
Monkɔ mbrɛ Woara bɛkyerɛ.

MHB 841
1 . JESUS mbofraba hɔn nyɛnko,
Yɛ mo so m' nyɛnko
Suo me nsamu na daa twe me
Pin Wo nkyɛn.

MHB 841
2 . Kyerɛ m' ma minyin papayɛ m'
Ber a mirinyin yi;
Wo so ayɛ abofra pɛn ntsi
Inyim ampa.

MHB 841
3 . Nkakrankakra, gya me kɔ kan
Wɔ ɔbabunyɛ mu;
Ma munhu nyansa, nnya ahoɔdzen
Wo nokwar m'.

MHB 841
4 . Mma nngyaa m' eso mma mmpa me da,
Yɛ me Nyɛnko daa,
'Siandɛ mihia W' fi bra ahyɛse
Kesi ewiei.    Amen.

MHB 842
1 . JESUS brɛfo a edwe,
Kyea W'enyi hwɛ W'abofra;
Hu mo botooyɛ mbɔbɔr,
Ma me kwan membra Wo hɔ.

MHB 842
2 . Mepɛ dɛ wɔdze m' brɛ Wo;
Adom Wura, mma nnsiw kwan,
Ma W'abɔtoaba yi kwan,
Wɔ W'adom ahenman n' mu.

MHB 842
3 . Mepɛ dɛ meyɛ dɛ Ɔwo;
Ma m' Wo mbrɛhoadze akoma,
'Wo yɛ dɔ, yɛ mbɔbɔrhu;
Ma minnya Wo dɔ adwen no.

MHB 842
4 . Ne nyina ekyir ma menyɛ
M'Egya a ɔwɔ sor Ne pɛ,
Ma No Sunsum pa eenndzi yaw
Mentsena ase mma N'enyimnyam.

MHB 842
5 . Nyame Eguambaa, mohwɛ Wo;
Ɔwo bɛyɛ m' fasusu,
Ɔwo yɛ brɛfo a edwe,
Ɔwo so ayɛ abofra pɛn.

MHB 842
6 . Ɔwo tsenaa ase maa Nyame;
Annhwehwɛ Wo nko W'dze da;
Wo nko W' yieyɛ ennhia Wo da;
Nyame nko nye W'ahomka.

MHB 842
7 . Dɔfo Jesus, 'Guambaa pa,
Mehyɛ W'adom nsamu ara;
Agyenkwa, yɛ m' dɛ mbrɛ etse,
Bra bɛtsena m'akoma mu.

MHB 842
8 . Dɛm na m'bɛkyerɛ W'ayɛyi,
Masom Wo m'enyigye nda m';
Na ber nyina wiadze bohu
Christ, Krɔnkrɔn Ba n', wɔ mo mu.

MHB 843
1 . HƐN Wura dɔfo turo mu,
Wɔ asaase ha,
Nhyiren nkumaa pii nyin
Wɔ ahoɔfɛw mu.

MHB 843
2 . Christ, dɔfo turo Hwɛfo
Hwɛ nhyiren nkumaa no;
'Dɔ nsukookoo nkumaa
Na ndua akɛse so.

MHB 843
3 . Biribiara nnsuar pii a
Ɔremma N' nsa nnka;
Biribi nnyɛ tokyen
Ma ɔnndɔ no bi !

MHB 843
4 . Jesus dɔ mbofra no,
Mbofra tse dɛ hɛn;
Ohyiraa hɔn ber a nanom
Dze hɔn kɛmaa No n'.

MHB 843
5 . Jesus frɛ mbofraba n'
Dɛ wɔmbra N'enyim,
Wɔ No turo fɛɛfɛw n' mu,
Noara gugu do.

MHB 843
6 . Hɛn Wura, yɛgye W' frɛ do,
Gye hɛn hwɛ hɛn do,
Tsetse hɛn Wo turo n' mu,
Yɛnyɛ W'edwuma bi.

MHB 844
1 . JESUS Guanhwɛfo pa, tsie me;
Hyira W'eguambaa anafua yi;
Anago sum yi mu bɛn me;
Kora me sɔnn ma adze nkye.

MHB 844
2 . Adzekyee yi, Wo nsa akyerɛ m' kwan,
Meda W' ase dɛ ahwɛ m',
Ɔwo efura m' tam, anyɛn me,
Tsie m'ewimbir mpaabɔ yi.

MHB 844
3 . Ma bɔn nyina fa kyɛ m' koraa;
Hyira 'nyɛnkofo a modɔ hɔn;
Sɛ muwu a, fa me kɔ heaven,
Menye W'bɛtsena hɔ enyigye m'.  Amen.

MHB 845
1 . NYAME nyɛ m' bra kan kakraba a
Ɔdzɛw wɔ wiadze ha;
Gya kakraba a ɔdzɛw hyɛnhyɛnn, 
Beebiara a mobɔkɔ.

MHB 845
2 . Nyame nyɛ m' bra nhyiren kakraba a
Ɔbɛma obiara dɛw;
N'enyi sɔ dɛ ɔhyerɛn wɔ fie,
Kaansa bea no suar mpo a.

MHB 845
3 . Nyame nyɛ m' bra ndwom kakraba a
Ɔkyekye ayarfo werɛ,
Na ɔboa nkorɔfo ma wɔyɛ dzen,
Na ɔma nyia ɔtow enyigye.

MHB 845
4 . Nyame nyɛ m' bra poma kakraba a
Mberɛwyɛfo bɔtwer,
Ama mo mpɔw na m'ahom nyina
Aaboa me mfɛfo yie.

MHB 845
5 . Nyame nyɛ m' bra ndwom kakraba a
'Yɛyi na ɔdwe ahyɛ m' ma,
Dza ɔma gyedzi a onnhinhim,
Nyame akwan nwanwa do.

MHB 846
1 . EWURADZE, sɛ adze sa ara
Na hɛn nanom deda a,
Anafua sum kommyɛ no mu,
Hwɛ Wo mbɔtoaba do.

MHB 846
2 . Ber a sum ahyɛ dan komm no mu no,
Boa hɛn ma yenhu dɛ
Enye hɛn wɔ hɔ sum no mu,
Na ibosuo hɛn nsamu.

MHB 846
3 . Kaansa nnyɛ aber biara na
Yehu Abɔfo n' mpo a,
O ma yɛmfa hɛnho nhyɛ W' nsa,
Na mma yennsuro hwee.

MHB 846
4 . Dɛm na yɛbɔsoɛr anapa,
Ber a 'napawi rupue,
Dɛ yɛwɔ dɔ mema hɛnho
Wɔ hɛn Egya no ntsi.

MHB 847
1 . JESUS, yɛtse apɔw wɔ ahoɔdzen,
Na yetum tu mbirika dzi agor;
Yarba rehaw mbofra binom
Ma da biara wɔda mpa mu.

MHB 847
2 . Hɛn apɔwmudzen ntsi yɛda W' ase,
Yɛserɛ W', Egya dɔfo, hyira
Mbofra a wɔayɛ mberɛw na wɔyar,
Na wɔtse yaw, hu amandze.

MHB 847
3 . Fa dɔ akoma a ɔdwen ma hɛn,
Kyerɛ hɛn dza yɛnyɛ nkyerɛ dɔ,
Jesus dzin mu dɛ yɛdze roboa
Mbofra a hɔn werɛ ahow, rofona.   Amen.

MHB 848
1 . EWIMBER som ekyir,
Asɔrfi sunkamm no m'
Krɔnkrɔn 'daka n'enyim
Kanea n' ayɛ munsumm,
Awerɛfir mu ara na
Nyame Ne ndze ɔgyegyee hɔ.

MHB 848
2 . Nna akɔdaa brɛfo,
Israel sɔfo n' ada;
Levinyi kakraba n'
Roweɔn asɔrfi m' hɔ:
Na dza ohuntaa Eli no,
Ewuradze yii kyerɛ Hannah ba n'.

MHB 848
3 . O Ewuradze, ma me
Samuel asomkyɛn a
No mu yɛ har, ɔtse
W'ano wasa biara;
Emi so m'bɛgye Wo frɛ do,
Na m'bedzi kan metse Ɔwo.

MHB 848
4 . O ma m' Samuel akoma,
Akoma brɛfo a ɔtweɔn 
W'asɔrfi mbrɛ ewɔ mu
Anaa ɔweɔn W'abow;
Adzekyee na adzesaa akoma a
Otsin Wo pɛ do dzi dwuma.

MHB 848
5 . O ma m' Samuel adwen;
Gyedzi pa a onnhwinhwin,
Ɔyɛ setsie ma Wo,
Wɔ nkwa na owu mu,
Na medze abofra enyiwa eehu
Nokwar a wɔdze esie enyansafo n'.

MHB 849
1 . EGYA, dzi m'enyim dabaa,
Memfa Wo kwan pa no do;
Kyerɛ m' ma mindzi nokwar daa,
Menyɛ dza ɔwɔ dɛ meyɛ.

MHB 849
2 . Ma m' akokodur mbusu m',
Munhu dɛ Ɔwo tum gye nkwa;
Kora me sɔkyee wɔ Wo nkyɛn;
Ma mentsena Wo dɔ mu.

MHB 849
3 . Sɛ mokɔ bɔn nsɔhwɛ mu a,
Ma mingyina pintsinn nyansa m';
Na sɛ ɔka mo nko a,
Fa Wo tum n' bɔ mo ho ban.

MHB 849
4 . Sɛ dɛw hyɛ m'akoma ma a,
O boa me ma menkaa Wo,
Ma mindzi dɛw kɛse bi,
Dɛ Ɔwo m'Egya, dɔ me.

MHB 849
5 . Sɛ m'edwuma yɛ dzen a,
Ma monkɔ do dɛw mu ara,
Boa ma memfa abotar nsoa
Amandze, 'haw na dadwen.

MHB 849
6 . Gyinabew nyinara mu,
Ma munhu dza oye nyina,
Ma mentse ɔsor n-dze
Ber a ahotsewfo dzi dɛw.

MHB 85
1 . HOM mbra ma yɛnye abɔfo ntow
Ndwom ntwa ahengua no ho;
Hɔn gyirama no yɛ mpempem mpo a,
Hɔn dɛw n' dze ɔyɛ kor.

MHB 85
2 . Wɔka dɛ Eguambaa a owui n' fata
Dɛ wɔbɔkrɔn No dɛm;
Hɛn akoma so ka dɛ ɔfata,
'Siandɛ wokum N' maa hɛn.

MHB 85
3 . Enyimnyam na sorsor tumdzi
Fata hɛn Jesus Christ;
Na nhyira a ɔkyɛn dza yɛma n'
Nka Ewuradze afebɔɔ.

MHB 85
4 . Abɔdze nyina bɔ m' kor hyira 
Nyia ɔtse ahengua n' do
Ne dzin krɔnkrɔn no, na wɔhyɛ 
Eguambaa n' enyimnyam.

MHB 850
1 . HƐN enyi da sor daa nyina,
Ewia hyerɛn hɛn enyim;
Yɛwɔw do daa nyinara
Dze hɛn enyim tsim heaven.

MHB 850
2 . Yenyim daa nyina wɔ suro m'
Wo dzin krɔnkrɔn no ntsi;
Yesua daa dɛ yɛbɔdɔ
Wɔ ɔdɔ bɔkɔɔyɛ mu.

MHB 850
3 . Daa nyina yɛbɔ m' nantsew
Wɔ hɛn Nua panyin N' nkyɛn;
Yenyin daa wɔ nokwardzi m',
Dze ma hɛnho nkorkor.

MHB 850
4 . Daa nyina ndaase mu ara,
Yɛgye W'ayamuyie pii,
Daa nyinara yɛpen do
Dze mfom kyekyɛ hɛnho.

MHB 850
5 . Ewuradze, daa yɛsɔr dɛ,
Tsie hɛn Wo mbɔbɔrhu m',
Ama ewiei no yaaba
Kuropɔn krɔnkrɔn n' mu.  Amen.

MHB 851
1 . Dza ɔyɛ fɛw na ɔhyerɛn, 
Abɔdze nyinara,
'Nyansadze na anwanwadze,
Nyame yɛɛ ne nyina.

MHB 851
2 . N-hyiren biara a ɔpae, 
Nyame maa n' ahoɔfɛw;
Anomaba a ɔtow ndwom,
Nyame yɛɛ ne ntɛkyerɛ.
Dza ɔyɛ fɛw—

MHB 851
3 . Bepɔw a osi habanm', 
'Sutsen a ɔda ho,
N-woraba na bosoom,
Adzekyee na adzesaa.
Dza ɔyɛ fɛw—

MHB 851
4 . N-su a ɔtɔ esusow, 
Ewia a ɔpae pɛber,
N-duaba a ɔsow ndua do,
Na hamu edziban.
Dza ɔyɛ fɛw—

MHB 851
5 . Enyiwa wɔ hɔ ma yeehu, 
Ano so ma yaaka,
Dɛ saa Nyame yɛ tumfo,
Ɔayɛ adze nyina yie.
Dza ɔyɛ fɛw—

MHB 852
1 . ABƆDZE a wɔwɔ wi n'ase
Anaa wɔnenam pomu,
Wɔyɛ ɔsor Hen N'abɔdze
Na mo so mo nuanom.

MHB 852
2 . Modɔ dɛ metse anoma a
Osi dua do no su;
Dɛ daa muhu nnoma fɛɛfɛw 
Tu faa kyin wɔ wimu.

MHB 852
3 . Modɔ dɛ mohwɛ esunoma
Ber a otu kyin nsu enyi;
Modɔ dɛ muhu tutugya,
Ne kandzea adzesaaber.

MHB 852
4 . Nsuborɔkɔ a ɔhoa sakoo,
Nam a okyinkin nsuadze;
Anantwi a worusu ba fie,
Mpɔnkye a wogu efuw mu.

MHB 852
5 . Hɛn nyina wɔ kyɛfa Ne wiadze m';
Ɔnyɛn obiara daa,
Ohu ɔsorɔm tantan a ɔatɔ
Kwan mu a obiara nnhu n'.

MHB 852
6 . Egya Tumfo, ahenfo Hen,
Botooyɛfo hɔn Dɔfo,
Yɛ m' ndzɛmba a wɛnnsɛ bi nyɛnko,
Mberɛwyɛfo bambɔfo.  Amen.

MHB 853
1 . ABOFRA botum ehu
Hɛn Egya No dɔ dzin no;
Wɔakyerɛw n' famu asaase ha,
Na wimu so wɔ sor.

MHB 853
2 . Sɛ mohwɛ moho hyia a,
Muhu Ne nsaano edwuma;
Wiadze tse dɛ mfonyin buukuu,
Ɔkyerɛ me Ne dzin no.

MHB 853
3 . Yehu nhyiren nkumaa
Apem wɔ hɛn turo mu 
Nyankontɔn na esusom nsu,
Yɛtse ngyegyee dɛɛdɛw.

MHB 853
4 . Nnoma a wosu dɛɛdɛw 
Bosoom a ɔhyerɛn anafua,
Ɔma abɔdze nkakraba
Mpo dzi dɛw wɔ kan n' mu.

MHB 853
5 . Na woraba biara a,
Ɔwɔ wimu wɔ sorsor,
Ne nyina kyerɛ m' dɛ Nyame yɛ dɔ,
Ne nyina kyerɛ m' dɛ ɔbɛn.

MHB 854
1 . ƆYƐ anwanwadze mapa,
Na ɔyɛ nwanwa mbordo mpo,
Dɛ Nyame Ba befi sor aba,
Ebowu agye abofra dɛ emi.

MHB 854
2 . Naaso minyim dɛ ɔyɛ ampa,
Ɔfaa abrɛfo na ehiafo,
Osui, berɛe, kaa mmɔn na owui
Maa hɔn a wɔanndɔ No ara da.

MHB 854
3 . Ɔyɛ a modwen mbeamudua n' ho,
Mumua m'enyi, per dɛ m'bohu
'Tsirmuɔdzen mprɛgow na nsoɛ kyɛw n',
Jesu a wɔbɔɔ N' mbeamudua m' maa me n'.

MHB 854
4 . Sɛ mpo m'bohu mbrɛ ɔyɛɛ wui a,
Ɔdɔ kɛse a ɔdzɛw dɛ ogya,
Wɔ N'akoma mu dabaa no,
Ne fa kumaabi na m'bohu.

MHB 854
5 . Murunntum nnka mbrɛ osii dɔɔ 
Afra a ɔyɛ mberɛw na bɔn fa n';
Sɛ owui dze tɔɔ mo dɔ ampa a,
Na No dɔ no yɛ nwanwa ampa.

MHB 854
6 . Ɔyɛ nwanwa dɛ No dɔ a ɔwɔ,
Ma me n' wɔnntɔ na odzi mu;
Na ɔyɛ nwanwa pii dɛ mo dɔ a
Mowɔ ma No suar, yɛ mberɛw.

MHB 854
7 . Naaso me pɛ dɛ modɔ Wo Owura;
O sɔ gya no wɔ m'akoma m'
Na m'bɔdɔ Wo mbordo, mbordo,
Kɛpem dɛ m'bohu W' dɛ mbrɛ etse.

MHB 855
1 . MUSUAR 'so modɔ dɛ modwen,
Nna m'Agyenkwa yɛ afra;
Dɛ Jesus dze krɔnkrɔnyɛ pa
Nantseew 'saase yi do.

MHB 855
2 . Osiee N'Egya No nokwar nsɛm,
Wɔkyerɛ m' dɛ menyɛ dɛm;
Kaansa ɔbɔɔ mbabun bra mpo a,
Ɔnantseew nyansa m' so.

MHB 855
3 . Modɔ dɛ modwen, Nyia ɔkasaa
Buee enyifurafo enyi,
Na onyaan hɔn a wɔdaa ewufu nda n',
Yɛɛ abofra dɛ emi.

MHB 855
4 . Dɛ Nyia ɔsoaa nsoɛ ahenkyɛw,
Na ɔsɔɔ owu hwɛe no,
Nyaa ena pa bi tse dɛ medze 'i,
Ohun no hwɛ na n' dɔ.

MHB 855
5 . Minyim dɛ dɔ a ɔdɔ me ntsi
Na ɔbɛyɛɛ abofra,
Na ogyaa heaven bea fɛɛfɛw n',
Bɛfaa wiadze akwan do.

MHB 855
6 . Afei Gyefo a eyɛɛ abofra pɛn,
Afra tum ba Wo nkyɛn;
Na m'Agyenkwa Dɔfo, mbɔbɔr m'
Ara, o bra me nkyɛn.   Amen.

MHB 856
1 . Modɔ dɛ metse nsɛm a 
Abɔfo ndze ka no,
Dɛ enyimnyam Hen n' mber bi
Ɔbɛtsenaa asaase do.
Bɔnyɛnyi a meyɛ mberɛw so,
Na 'yi minyim petee
Dɛ, Ewuradze bae bɛgyee m' nkwa.
Osiandɛ ɔdɔ m' kɛse.

MHB 856
2 . M' Agyenkwa siarfo bɛyɛɛ 
Abɔdomaba dɛ emi,
Ma ɔaakyerɛ No nkɔkowaba
Krɔnkrɔnyɛ mu akwan;
Na sɛ mobɔ ho mbɔdzen
Tsiatsia N' anamɔnm' a,
Ɔnnkɔtow m' akyen ara da
Osiandɛ ɔdɔ m'kɛse.

MHB 856
3 . No mbɔbɔrhu nye No dɔ n', 
M' bɔtow ho ndwom dɛɛdɛw;
Muhu N' a ɔnnyɛ mpo a, minyim
Dɛ ɔtse m' ayɛyi.
Na ɔabɔ m' anohoba
Ayamuyiem' dɛ monkɔ
Menkɛnye abɔfo ntow ndwom,
Osiandɛ ɔdɔ m' kɛse.

MHB 857
1 . Nyame ama hɛn Buukuu a nsɛm ahyɛ mu ma,
Wɔyɛɛ maa tsetseber do nyimpa,
Ɔdze turo bi mu nsɛm hyɛ ase kyerɛw,
Na ɔdze sika kuropɔn wie.

MHB 857
2 . Dza odzi mu yie nye Jesus ho nsɛm,
Abɔdoma a ɔnye nantwi hyɛ buw m',
Na ndwom a abɔfo towee wɔ No ho,
Nye nsɛm a ɔyɛ dɛw kyɛn ne nyina.

MHB 857
3 . Nsɛm wɔ hɔ ma awofo na mbofra,
Mpanyin a wɔayɛ krado dɛ wɔhom,
Na hɔn a wotum kenkan na hɔn a wotsie n',
Jesus ho asɛm na odzi mu yie.

MHB 857
4 . Ɔka mbrɛ osii fii Egya n' hɔ bae,
Bɛfrɛɛ Ne mba a wɔwɔ ekyirekyir,
Ɔdze nguan a wɔayew bɛbrɛ hɔn Wura n',
Asɛm a ɔyɛ dɛw kyɛn ne nyina.

MHB 858
1 . Ka Jesus ho n-sɛm kyerɛ m', 
Mepɛ metsie;
Ndzɛmba a nkyɛ mibebisa No,
Sɛ ɔwɔ ha a:
Ɔkwan nkyɛn ndzɛmba,
Epo do nsɛm,
Jesus No ho nsɛm,
Ka kyerɛ me.

MHB 858
2 . Ma mindzi kan ntse mbrɛ mbofra 
Kɔbɔɔ N' aprɔw;
Na emi so me nsa bɛka
Ne nhyira n' bi.
Ayamuyie kasa,
Adom ndzeyɛɛ,
Dze ɔdɔ hyerɛɛn
Jesus N' enyim.

MHB 858
3 . Kyerɛ m' enyinyandze a osii 
Ture no mu n';
Na mbeamudua n' a wɔdze kum
M' Agyenkwa no:
Ne yaw na Ne dɛw,
Dɛ mbrɛ wɔyɛ
Jesus No ho nsɛm n',
Ka kyerɛ me.

MHB 859
1 . David ahenkurowm' prɛko bi, 
Nantwibuw tantan bi mu,
Ɔbaatan dedaa ne ba bi
Wɔ mbowa dzidzidaka mu.
Mary nye ɔbaatan pa n',
Jesus Christ ɔnye ne Ba n'.

MHB 859
2 . Nyame, adze nyina Wura, 
Fi sor siaan asaase do;
M-bowadan ɔnye No dɔbea,
Ne dabew nye mpɔnkɔbuw,
Hɛn Agyenkwa Krɔnkrɔnnyi
Ɔnye abɔbɔfo tsenaa ase.

MHB 859
3 . No mbofraber nwanwa nyina 
Ɔyɛɛ enyidzi na setsie;
Ɔdɔe, ɔweɔn ne na brɛfo a
Ɔdaa n' abaw mu foo n' yie.
Christian mbofra nyɛ setsie,
Wɔndwe, nyɛ pa dɛ mbrɛ ɔyɛe.

MHB 859
4 . Mbofra hɛn fasusu nye No, 
Onyinii dɛ hɛnara,
Kakrabaa, m-berɛmberɛw;
Osui, serewee dɛ hɛnara;
Ntsi hɛn yaw ɔtse ma hɛn,
Na hɛn dɛw onyam' kyɛpɛn.

MHB 859
5 . Ɔnam No nkwagye dɔ no do 
Da bi hɛn enyi bohu N'
Osiandɛ abofra fɛɛfɛw n'
Nye Ewuradze a ɔwɔ sor;
Na ogya No mbofra kwan
Kɔ mbrɛ Ɔnoara oedu n'.

MHB 86
1 . NYAME Ba tumfo, daa Ɔdɔ, 
Ɔwo na hɛn yennhu W'enyim,
Yɛdze gyedzi nko suo Wo mu,
Yɛgye dza yenntum nntse ase dzi.

MHB 86
2 . Innkegyaa hɛn wɔ huntuma m';
Ebɔɔ nyimpa, ɔnntse W' ase; 
Ɔdwen dɛ wɔammbɔ n' dɛ ombowu;
Naaso ebɔɔ n', Ɔwo etsen.

MHB 86
3 . Ɔwo yɛ nyimpa na Nyame,
Eyɛ nyimpa krɔnkrɔn, ekrɔn; 
Yɛdze hɛn pɛ, yɛnntse ase;
Yɛdze hɛn pɛ nyina ma Wo.

MHB 86
4 . Hɛn nhyehyɛɛ nyina wɔ hɔn mber;
Wodzi hɔn mber na wotwa m' kɔ; 
Wɔyɛ Wo kan ho gyansenama,
Na Ɔwo, Ewuradze so sen hɔn.

MHB 860
1 . Akɔkowaba Jesus ennya adasoe; 
Wɔdedaa N' wɔ mbowa edzidzidaka mu.
N-woraba fi sorsor hyerɛɛn mbrɛ ɔda no,
Nna Jesus ada komm wɔ efuw no do.

MHB 860
2 . Anantwi no sui na Ɔba no nyanee, 
Naaso, hwɛ, oennsu, na mbom ɔdaa hɔ komm.
O Jesus, modɔ Wo; fi sor hwɛ mo do,
Tsena me nkyɛn araa kodu adzekyee.

MHB 860
3 . Ewuradze Jesus, meserɛ Wo dɛ 
Bɛn me nkyɛn na dɔ me aber nyinara,
Hyira mbofra nyina wɔ W' abaatan dɔ mu,
Na tsew hɛn ho ama yaafata Wo nkyɛn.

MHB 861
1 . O MBOFRABA, meserɛ hom dɛ hom nyina mbra,
Hom mbɛka Bethlehem nguanhwɛfo no ho;
Hom nhwɛ dza hɛn Egya pɛ dɛ hɛn enyi gye ntsi
Ɔdze aba asaase do 'nyimnyam anafua 'i.

MHB 861
2 . O hom mbɔ hom mu adze nkotow na hom nsɔr,
Hom nka hom nsa mfua, nda Nyame ase dɛ hɔn;
Mbofra, hom mfa sanku ndze ntow ndwom dɛw mu,
O hom nye abɔfo ntow ndwom, nye hɔn ndzi dɛw.

MHB 862
1 . 'NYANSAFO n' paar Jesus,
Wotuu kwan fi ekyir,
Woraba fɛfɛɛfɛw bi
Gyaa hɔn akwantu n' mu.

MHB 862
2 . Na sɛ yɛhwehwɛ No a,
Ɔbɛn hɛn koraa;
Hɛnara hɛn man yi yɛ
Hɛn Asaase Krɔnkrɔn.

MHB 862
3 . Akra a wɔsɔr bohu N'
Hɛn esutaae ho,
Wobehyia N' nkokwaa do,
Ber a adze rekye.

MHB 862
4 . Hɛn mburokwa mu, ber a
Yɛaboaboa eburow no;
Hɛn eguadzibea hɔɔ do,
Wotum hu Jesus.

MHB 862
5 . Afarfo nye N' kasa
Wɔ Etsifo Po do,
Dɛ mbrɛ nkan esuafo n'
Yɛe wɔ Galilee n'.

MHB 862
6 . Jesus ba hān asomdwee
Kuroba biara mu a,
Ne mbae no dan no ma
Ɔyɛ Bethany.

MHB 862
7 . Sɛ yɛdɔ No yie ampa a,
Ɔbɛn hɛn koraa;
'Siandɛ ɔhwehwɛ daa dɛ
Ɔtsena hɛn akoma m'.

MHB 863
1 . NGUANHWƐFO n' nyaa ɔbɔfo,
'Nyansafo n' nyaa woraba:
Ebɛn na emi abofra mowɔ?
Obegya m' efi ekyir akɔ fie?
Bea a dɛw nworaba tow ndwom bɔ m',
Na abɔfo so tow ndwom?

MHB 863
2 . Mo Wura Jesus nye m' hwɛfo,
Dɛm ntsi mirinnhia hwee:
Ɔbra basaa yi nyina mu,
Nguambaa no gu No bomu;
Nguambaa asokyewfo a wɔfom yew n',
Okyi bɔgya twe hɔn.

MHB 863
3 . Dɛm nguanhwɛfo no tsenaa
Ase esuom weɔɔn hɔn nguan,
Kesii dɛ wohum sor dɔm no a
Wɔmmberɛ annda na mbom
Wɔtoow Enyimnyam, Enyimnyam,
Dze dzii afahyɛ no.

MHB 863
4 . Christ hwɛ N'eguambaa kumaa mo do,
Ɔhwɛ m' do aber biara,
Ma maayɛ Nedze wɔ heaven:
'Bɔfo a woenwuna fitaa
Bɔtow hɔn ndwom, Enyimnyam, 'nyimnyam,
Wɔ me ntsi wɔ sorsor.

MHB 863
5 . Ewuradze, fa m' bɛn Wo ho daa,
Kɛpem dɛ me ndze bɔfora
'Bɔfo a wɔayɛ fitaa ndze
Na yɛatow enyimnyam,
Enyimnyam nyina yɛdze ama Wo,
Wɔ sorsor noho nyina.

MHB 864
1 . KAA nyimpa nyina a wɔtse
Ekyirekyir nsaase do,
Wɔ nkuropɔn nwanwa fɛɛfɛw m',
Anaa wokyin anhwea m',
Wɔyɛ kua wɔ nkokwaa do,
Nye nsaase a ɔda famu do,
Bea a mbofra nenam emo fuw m',
Hwɛ efupɔnkɔ a wɔsen.

MHB 864
2 . Binom yɛ edwuma kwaa tuntu m',
Bea a ndow dzi afow sian,
Binom nu nam nsu akɛse m,
Yɛ ha 'sukwankyɛba m';
Kaa Nyame Ne mba nyina a
Wonnyaa mpo nntsee nokwar a 
Ofi Jesus hɔ ba no,
N'asɛm n'enyimnyam no.

MHB 864
3 . Nyame nhyira mbanyin na mbaa a
Wɔsom No wɔ po ekyir;
Nyame mfrɛ pii nka hɔn ho
Ma amanaman eenya fahodzi,
Kɛpem dɛ ekyirekyirfo a
Wɔwɔ ananabea n'
Bɛtse N'ahenman n' ase,
Na wɔaba N'adom mu.

MHB 865
1 . MEKENKAN asɛm dadaw dɛɛdɛw bi no a,
Ɔfa mbrɛ Jesus wɔ wiadze n'
Osii frɛɛ mbofraba kaa No nguaakuw ho no a,
Me yamu ara a nkyɛ mekaa hɔn ho;
Me yamu a nkyɛ ɔdze Ne nsa too me tsir do,
Na ɔtserɛɛw Ne nsa mu baam me,
Na nkyɛ meehu N'enyim serew ber a ɔsee dɛ,

MHB 865
23 Hom mma mbofra no mbra Me nkyɛn no!.

. Naaso sesei mpaabɔ m' m'bɔkɔ n'ananadze,
Na makɛserɛ N' No dɔ no bi;
Na sɛ nokwar m' mohwehwɛ N' yie ase ha a,
M'bohu No atse Ne ndze wɔ sor,
Bea fɛɛfɛw no a ɔakɔ rikesiesie dze ama
Hɔn a woeguar hɔn dze hɔn bɔn akyɛ hɔn n';
Na mbofra papa pii rihyia mu wɔ hɔ,
Yinom na ahenman n' yɛ hɔndze.

. Naaso mpempem a wokyin hwehwe ase,
Nntsee dɛm ɔsor fie no nka;
Mepɛ dɛ wohu dɛ kwan wɔ hɔ ma hɔn nyina,
Na dɛ Jesus ato nsa afrɛ hɔn.
Mokɔn dɔ 'nyimnyam ber no mu dɛw no,
Dza ɔyɛ dɛw, ɔhyerɛn, dzi mu,
Ber a mbofra pa a wofi wiadze nyina 
Bokogu N' bomu na oehyira hɔn n'.

MHB 866
1 . BER a Salem abaatan
Dze hɔn mba kɔr Jesus hɔ n',
N'esuafo n' dze ebufuw see hɔn dɛ 
Wonfi hɔ wɔnkɔ.
Na Jesus hun hɔn ntsɛmara,
Na ɔyerɛɛw N'ano na ɔsee hɔn dɛ,
Wɔmma mbofraba no kwan ma wɔmbra
Me nkyɛn.

MHB 866
2 . Hɛn Agyenkwa n' kyerɛɛ ɔdɔ
Dɛ ɔyɛɛ mbofra n' eetuu;
Na mpempem bi so wɔ hɔ a
Hɔndze wɔnntsee Ne dzin no;
Agyenkwa pa, yɛsɔr a tsie hɛn,
Ama ese hɔn dɛ, Wɔmma 
Mbofraba no mbra Me nkyɛn a, wɔaatse.

MHB 866
3 . Ɔnnkɛkyɛr na aman nyina
Do abosonsɔrfo eetsie
Na woeedzi W'asɛm no do
Aatow hɔn abosom egu;
O fi sor hyerɛn wɔ hɔn do;
Yi Woho kyerɛ dɛ ɔdɔ Nyame;
Agyenkwa pa, kyerɛ hɔn ma wɔmbra 
W'nkyɛn.

MHB 867
1 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo, 
Ber a adze akye bio,
Yebu ntwɛr wɔ fie hyira Wo,
Wɔ adzekyeem' adom ho.

MHB 867
2 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo, 
Ber a yeetu hɛn ndwom wɔ skuul,
Dabaa yɛdze W' ayɛyi hyɛ
Dwumadzi ase, yɛdze wie.

MHB 867
3 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo, 
Wɔ hɛn ndwomm' ana yɛada;
Abɔfo tsie, wɔweɔn hɛn,
Christ no nguambaa anago nyina.

MHB 867
4 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo, 
Nnyɛ ayɛyi nsɛm mu nko;
Nokwardzi na setsie mu so
Yɛkyerɛ Woara W' enyimnyam.

MHB 867
5 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo, 
Dɛ ɔnam Jesus ara ntsi
Yɛdze abotar sɔw mfom nyina,
Na yeku ɔbɔn biara.

MHB 867
6 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo, 
Gyedɛ hɛn nda bɔ adze,
Gyedɛ yɛhom fi hɛn berɛm',
Yɛrotweɔn Wo da n' asomdweem'.

MHB 868
1 . AGYENKWA pa nokwafo,
Gye m'adwen na dzi do tum;
Nyansa na pɛ a mowɔ no,
Hyira do, yɛ do kwangyafo.

MHB 868
2 . Ber a murusua nwonma yi
Jesus Christ, meserɛ W', bɛn me,
Kaakaa me, bue m'adwen mu,
Monhwehwɛ nyimdzee mminya.

MHB 868
3 . Na mowɔ ɔbra ntsetsee ase;
Ma menyɛ no W'adom mu;
Moroboa m' ho ama ɔbra akodzi;
Ma menyɛ no Wo tum mu.

MHB 868
4 . Ɔwo ama m' adwen na ɔkra;
Medze bɛyɛ edwuma ama Wo:
Ɔwo wui ma maatsena ase;
M'ahom nyina medze ma Wo.

MHB 868
5 . Meper, m'adwendwen, mo sua m',
Ma mindzi Wo pɛ no do,
Kɛpem dɛ mibedzi mu
Ama W'edwuma na Woara. Amen.

MHB 869
1 . AYƐYI nka Nyame a ɔdze dɔ a ɔnnkyea
Dzi hɛn enyim wɔ hɛn dwumadzi m' fi ɔsɛɛ mu;
Ohue asomdwee na ahonya a yɛmmfata,
Dua N'ayamuyie nsa mu ma hɛn daa.

MHB 869
2 . Edwumayɛ, dɛw na awerɛhow etwa m';
Hwɛ, ewiei no, yɛtwe bɛn Wo, sɔr Wo,
Sesei a hɛn ndaamba abrabɔ nnyaa mmbaa yi;
Mbofrasɛm etwa m', na mpanyinyɛ wɔ kan.

MHB 869
3 . Akra Guanhwɛfo, O nkwagye abotsen,
Fa Wo nhwɛdo a ɔnnsakyer no hwɛ Wo nguan,
Ka hɔn hɔ m' dɛ mbrɛ wɔyɛɛ dze sɔɔr Wo no,
Ansaana hɔn ntamu atsetsew ndaamba.

MHB 869
4 . Kaansa hɛn nyina nnkehyia mu wɔ fakor bio,
Kaansa ɔbra akodzi m' tsetsew mpo a,
Hɛn Gyefo yɛ kor, na, hɛn Egya yɛ kor,
Ka hɛn bɔ m' wɔ gyedzi na akoma mu.  Amen.

MHB 87
1 . JESUS dze N'adom nyina ba, 
Ɔbɛgye asehwefo;
Hɛn 'nyimnyam enyidado,
Jesus ba bɛma hɛn do.

MHB 87
2 . Ma enyikan abo nsea m',
Ma Abraham mba mbɔ ose;
Yenyi hɛn Hen brɛfo ayɛw,
Nda N' ase, ndzi dɛw, ntow ndwom.

MHB 87
3 . Ɔayɛ hɛn nkwagye ho edwuma, 
Ɔafa hɛn akra ndɔmmum,
Ɔdze hɛn abrɛ Nyame,
Ɔdze No bɔgyaa ahor hɛn.

MHB 87
4 . Afei yɛyɛ Nedze koraa,
Hom nnantsew dɛ ekan mba;
Ɔnnkɛkyɛr na yeenya adom,
Akoma pa, ma yeehu No.

MHB 87
5 . Yɛbenya hɛn frɛ akatua;
Yebedzi Nyame ekyir,
Enyigye, dɔ na asomdwee,
Krɔnkrɔnyɛ bɛhyɛ hɛn ma.

MHB 870
1 . Ewuradze, fa Wo nhyira dom hɛn, 
Yebehyia mu bio wɔ ha;
Ma yentu anamɔn nkɔ kan
Wɔ Wo dɔ, gyedzi na surom';
Bɔ hɛn ho ban
Dɛ ebɛn hɛn daa nyina.

MHB 870
2 . W' ehumbɔbɔr ho yɛsɔr Wo, 
Edze dom hɛn kwan nyinam',
Nyame yetwa hwe W' enyim bio
Ma hɛn edwuma nkɔ do daa
Ma hɛn sunsum
Na adwen nnya W' akyɛdze pa.

MHB 870
3 . Ma fidua mu enuadɔ ntsim 
Akoma biara mu daa,
No tum nkyerɛkyerɛ hɛn ma
Yenyi pɛsɛankonya akwa
Ndu dɛ Wo mba
Bohu dɛ hɔn Egya nye W'.
    
       Mpaamudzi

MHB 870
4 . Nyame fa Wo nhyira gya hɛn kwan,
Yɛda ase na ehumbɔbɔr;
Fa nnuhofo nyina mfom kyɛ hɔn;
Wonnya mber mfa ntsen dza asɛɛ n'
Na mma Wo mba
Mmfom Wo Sunsum ara bio.

MHB 870
5 . Ma Wo Sunsum pa no nkenyan 
Ndzepa biara a yeenya n' ha,
Na dza ndzebɔn dze na nyina nsɛɛ,
Fa Wo tum kɛse n' siw ano,
Na yɛmper daa
Nnya nyimdzee na dɔ mapa.

MHB 870
6 . Egya baatan, kora hɔn a 
Worinnhyia mu bio wɔ ha;
Ma dza woedua n' nsow aba pa
Bafuu ofi ber to ber;
Hɔn a wɔresan n'
Nnyɛ anokwafo nsen nkan' n'.  Amen.

MHB 871
1 . HƐN dwumadzi na hɛn agodzi m',
Jesus, 'nye hɛn ntsena daa;
Aber nyina yɛmbɔ mbɔdzen
Ndzi nokwar, ngyina mma Wo.
     Dɛm n' na yebotum atow dɛ
     Yɛyɛ ɔhen no Ne mba.

MHB 871
2 . Ma yendua Wo tum do nhyɛ
Ebufuw na atorsɛm do,
Adwembɔn na ndzeyɛɛ bɔn,
Nye dza Ɔwo kyir nyina so.

MHB 871
3 . Jesus, fi W'ahengua do
Fa Wo dɔ no hyɛ hɛn ma,
Ama obiara eehu dɛ 
Nyame pa, yɛyɛ Wodze.

MHB 871
4 . Yɛyɛ Ɔhen no Ne mba,
Hom mma yendzi nokwar mma N',
Na yɛnsɔ N'enyi daa daa,
Hɛn dwumadzi na hɛn agodzi m'.

MHB 872
1 . YEHYIRA Wo, Nyame, dɛ dɛm bra yi ara
Tum ma ahomgye na dɛw wɔ no kō mu;
Asaase, ndua, po, fua na nsunyiwa ntsi
Edwuma na adzesua biara a ɔdze ba ntsi.

MHB 872
2 . Dɛ hɛn Pisgah ma hɛn nokwar fofor a,
Mber rokɔ n' ɔma mbahun foforyɛ;
Dɛ yɛnye nyimdzefo na enyansafo a
Wɔtse sor ndwom ngyegyee yɛ fɛkuwbɔ.

MHB 872
3 . Nyimpa berɛ mu enyadze biara ntsi;
Dza amandɔfo yɛ na akyerɛwfo ka ntsi,
Wɔ dadaw kan a ɔda tsetsesɛm edzi ntsi,
'Nyidar fofor a mber danee dze ba ntsi.

MHB 872
4 . Yendzi nokwar mma hɛn nkandzea yinom,
Nnya 'nyidar, 'hoɔdzen na dɛw fofor daa,
Nyɛ 'setsie mma ɔsor ndzɛmba nko daa,
Onntwa m' da, Mbra a Otumfo Dɔ ahyɛ no.   Amen.

MHB 873
1 . Nyame dɔyɛfo a W'ehumbɔbɔr 
Dom hɛn fie kan na enuadɔ,
Fa hɛn nguankuw gu W' abaw mu,
Dɛ mbrɛ eyɛɛ n' tsetsebaado n'.

MHB 873
2 . N-dze a yɛdze tow ndwom yɛserew, 
Ma hɛn fie yɛ enyigye yi,
Yɛdze tow ndwom yi Wo ayɛw a,
Aso, Ewuradze, innketsie hɛn?

MHB 873
3 . Ɔbram' nhyira na awerɛhow ntsi, 
Enyigye a wɔtse ase n-tsi,
Nye hɔn a woewu nyina ntsi,
Yɛda W' ase, hɛn Egya pa.

MHB 873
4 . Hɛn mber pam' dɛw a etwam' ntsi, 
Enyigye a yɛwɔm' sesei ntsi,
Hɛn bra n' ewimbir mu kan ntsi,
Yɛda W' ase hɛn Egya pa.

MHB 873
5 . Ma W' adom mbɔ hɛn ho aprɔw, 
Ma W' ehumbɔbɔr mbra hɛn do,
Ma W' asomdwee ntsena hɛn nkyɛn
M-berantsen nyinara mu.    Amen.

MHB 874
1 . YI hɛn suro kɔ!
'Nyigye da no a wɔwoo
Nkwagye dzifo bi n' aba ampa!
Mifi Jehovah mu,
Na mehyɛ N' enyimnyam,
Na medze adwontow san so kɔ N' hɔ.

MHB 874
2 . Mekamfo W'adom
Dɛ ofi m'ahyɛse n'
Ɔabɛn, atwe me, abɔ m' ho ban;
Ɔwo agye m' bɔn mu
Ara dze ebodu ndɛ 
Na minyim dɛ edze m' bodu ewiei.

MHB 874
3 . O daa daa dadwen,
Nsɔhwɛ, na mfir horow
Wo nsa egya me abamba afa mu!
O nhyira beberee na 
Domfo Nyame dze ama,
Ɔnye mbɔbɔrhu a ɔyɛ fofor daa.

MHB 874
4 . Mbɔbɔrhu bɛn nye 'i?
Na dɛw tsebea so bɛn a!
M'enyigye dɔɔ so a onnyi kabea;
Dɛ modɔm Wo kuw no,
Na wɔakan me afora hɔn 
Dɛ menye hɔn ntsena nkesi wu m'.

MHB 874
5 . Medze enyidzi na
'Yɛyi ma adom Egya,
Ɔba no na Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn no;
Edwuma a ohia no,
Ɔahyɛ me ma mayɛ,
Na midzi dɛw pii dɛ wɔwoo me.

MHB 874
6 . Medze dɛw kɛse
Tu me bra nyina dze
Bɔ me Nyankopɔn No ho dawur;
Ɔsɛ dɛ meyɛ 'yi,
Dɛ medze ma Jesus
Ne dɛw na No nkwagye no tahye.

MHB 874
7 . Mo nkwa nda a aka n',
Medze beyi N' ayɛw;
Ɔno na owui gyee wiadze nyina;
Mbrɛ me nda tse biara,
Odzi wɔ m' Pomfo no,
Na meetu ne nyina esi hɔn ama No.

MHB 875
1 . Ahomka fi nye mbrɛ wɔdɔ wo kɛse, 
'Wo, Nyɛnko pa, adasa Agyenkwa,
Na wɔdze Wo tsena mpanyin tsenabea
Wɔ ahɔho a wɔba hɔ nyina mu.

MHB 875
2 . Ahomka fi nye mbrɛ beenu abɔ mu 
Ayɛ kor gyedzi na enyidar mu,
Ma owu nkotoo na otum paa hɔn mu,
Na ɔno mpo nntum nnsɛɛ koryɛ n' koraa.

MHB 875
3 . Ahomka fi nye bea a wɔdze no mu mba 
Hyɛ Wo nsa wɔ gyedzi nye mpaabɔ mu,
Na Ɔwo, hɔn Damfo, ifi sor weɔn hɔn,
Na ehwɛ hɔn do kyɛn mbrɛ na bɔhwɛ.

MHB 875
4 . Ahomka fi nye mbrɛ obiara som Wo 
Ahobrɛadze mu wɔ no dwumadzim',
Dze kodu dɛ fam' dwuma nyina ho tsew,
Dɛ wɔdze rema Wo, Ewuradze.

MHB 875
5 . Ahomka fi nye beebi a werɛ mmfir Wo 
Ber a enyigye na dɛw abor do;
Ahomka fim' na wɔdze sunsum pirafo
Brɛ Wo, Duyɛfo, Werɛkyekyefo.

MHB 875
6 . Dze kɛpem dɛ sɛ wiadze dwumadzi sa a, 
Hɔn nyina behyia Wo wɔ sor fi n' mu,
Mbrɛ ifir bae, na efowee kɔree no,
Ɔdɔ na asomdwee domankoma fi n'.

MHB 876
1 . NYAME a ewɔ mbea nyina
Na eboa hɔn a wɔdan Wo,
Anafua 'i bra me mpa ho
Besi adwembɔn nyina mpa;
Fa Wo nsa to me kra do,
Ɔwo m' mbusu ber Nyame,
Dzi m'atamfo, hɛll, wiadze
Na abɔdze mu tum nyina do.

MHB 876
2 . Yi me fi wiadze akɔndɔ m',
Ma m' honam mu fahodzi,
Fa tum pa kɛse twe me
Kra fam Woara Wo ho daa;
Mo Wura, yi Woho kyerɛ me.
Fa dɛw ahobow hyɛ m' ma,
Sɛ minyan a, ma mentse W' nka,
Ma monsoɛr Wo su no mu.

MHB 876
3 . Ma minnya Wo nkwa m' kyɛfa,
Wo krɔnkrɔnyɛ n', ma me bi,
Kɛtseankyɛ meehu n' yie dɛ
M'Agyenkwa aba m'akoma m'!
Na meehu Wo dɛ medze,
Kɛtseankyɛ maayɛ W' etuu!
Maabɔ sunsum mu bra nko
Dze ahyɛ Wo nko enyimnyam.

MHB 876
4 . Eso sɛ ihia me kra
Ansaana adze akye a,
Mo Wura, ma m' kra n'apɛdze,
Dɛ m'bedzi mu dɔ m' 'nafua 'i;
Wie Wo dɔ dwuma kɛse n',
Twa no tsia wɔ tsenenee mu,
Ma memfata sor noho,
Sakyer m' na munwu
Asomdwee m'.    Amen.

MHB 877
1 . MBRƐ Wo mbɔbɔrhu si fua m' a!
Wɔntonton Wo dzin afebɔɔ!
Mefɛr dɛ m'bɔkrɔn wɔ bra mu,
Akowaa bi a ɔkyɛn no Wura!

MHB 877
2 . Ohia na yaw tsɛɛ mo Wura,
Na amandzehu bra nko na ɔbɔe;
Nyankopɔn Ba, Nyimpa Ba no,
Ennya Ne tsir mpo tobew da.

MHB 877
3 . Naaso hwɛ, oesiesie beebi
Ama me, na abɔfo weɔn me;
Ampa, Noara gya m' abamba,
Siesie me mpa na ɔma meda.

MHB 877
4 . Jesus weɔn me; mo suro, kɔ!
Ebɛn puhim Tsetse Botan n'?
Wo domankoma dɔ abaw no mu
Medze moho to hɔ da sɔnn.

MHB 877
5 . Ber a ewɔ me nkyɛn dɛm yi,
Woana botum asɛɛ me nda?
Muhoro bɔn, wiadze na hɛll mpo;
Motwer m'Agyenkwa No bo mu.

MHB 877
6 . Mohom Tumfo n' No nwin ase,
Mo nkrumsi pa, me haw so twa;
Ɔwo mo Wura a me kra twer Wo n'
Bɔkora m' asomdwee mapa m'.

MHB 877
7 . Edɔ dɛ efa m' yɛ Wodze,
Sesei na daapem nyina so;
Ɔwo nnkɛpa 'kra bɔbɔnyi a
Ɔtwer Wo turodoo daa no.

MHB 878
1 . Nyame hɛn mboa mber a ɔasen, 
Hɛn ndaamba enyidar,
Hɛn sumabew wɔ ehumtu ber,
Hɛn domankoma fi.

MHB 878
2 . W' ahengua no no nwim ase 
Na yɛbɛda ho ahyɛ;
W' abaw no nko mpo ɔdɔɔ so,
Obotwitwa agye hɛn.

MHB 878
3 . Ansaana wɔreyɛ nkokwaa, 
Mbrɛ Wonnyae mmbɔɔ wiadze
Ofi tsetse eyɛ Nyame,
Eyɛ so afebɔɔ.

MHB 878
4 . M-fe apem yɛ W' enyi do 
Dɛ da kor a ɔasen,
Ɔyɛ tsia dɛ anago sum
Na anapa kan ehyiae.

MHB 878
5 . Adasamba a wɔtse wiadze 
Na hɔn dadwen nyina,
Ɔnnkyɛr biara na wɔapem kɔ,
Wɔayew hɛn enyi do.

MHB 878
6 . M-ber soa ne mba nyina kɔ 
Dɛ esu a ɔrepem;
Wɔhera dɛ mbrɛ adaaso hera
Ber a adze rekye.

MHB 878
7 . Nyame hɛn mboa mber a ɔasen, 
Hɛn ndaamba enyidar,
Yɛtse nkwa mu yi wowaw hɛn,
Yɛ hɛn fi a onnyi ewiei.   Amen.

MHB 879
1 . Nyame ngye hɛn Hen pa, 
Hɛn Hen kunyin nnyin nkyɛr,
Nyame ngye Ɔhen!
Ɔmma n' konyimdzi daa,
Ahomka nye enyimnyam,
Ma ɔnhwɛ ɔman do nkyɛr;
Nyame ngye Ɔhen!

MHB 879
2 . Wo nsam' nhyira papa n', 
Kyɛw nye yi, wora gu no do
Ondzi hen nkyɛr,
Nkyɛ ɔaawowaw hɛn mbra,
Ma daa hɛn so yɛdze
'Koma na dɛw yaatow
Nyame ngye Ɔhen!

MHB 88
1 . YƐNAM gyedzi do nyim ampa,
Nyame Ba no aba,
Ɔada Noho edzi wɔ ha,
Na Ɔtse hɛn akoma m';
Ɔnam N'adom nye No dɔ mu 
Ama hɛn nyina ntseasee, 
Dɛ yɛnhwɛ ɔsor nhu No dɛ 
Sor nye asaase Wura.

MHB 88
2 . Yɛtonton Nyame Otumfo, 
Ɔno a obi ammbɔ No, 
Ɔno nye daa nkwa nsunyiwa, 
Yɛsɔr No daa nyina;
N'amayɛ no mu na yenya
Enyigye a ɔnnsa da,
Yɛbɛtsena ase wɔ N'enyim dɛ 
Nkonyimdzifo daa nyina.

MHB 880
1 . NYAME nhyira hɛn man,
No sor bambɔ nsa no
Nhyira hɛn mpoano;
Asomdwee mu ntserɛw.
Ɔtamfo ndan nyɛnko,
Na Ghanaman yiedzi
Eenntsim ɔko do.

MHB 880
2 . Nyame, fa ahoɔdzen na
Pɛrpɛr ma Ɔmampanyin;
Ma n' tum n'aber m';
Fa nyansa kɛse fi
Sor nunu n'adwen daa,
Na ɔman no ndɔ no
Wɔ n'aber do.

MHB 880
3 . Ma pɛrpɛr na mbra pa
Ntsim n'amambu ber mu,
Hyira hɛn man;
Adehye, konyim man,
Fahodzi asaase,
Yɛsɔr dɛ sor Nyame
Nserew nkyerɛ wo.

MHB 880
4 . Nnyɛ hɛn man yi nko bi;
Nyame mbɔbɔrhu no,
Nka mbea nyina;
Nyame mma aman n' nhu dɛ
Wɔyɛ enuanom, ampa,
Na wɔbɔ ebusua kor,
Wɔ wiadze ha.

MHB 881
1 . EWURADZE, ber a yɛrosɔr ma
Wiadze nyimpa nyina yi,
Tsie hɛn wɔ hɛn awobea ntsi,
Bea a yɛdɔ n' mbordo no.

MHB 881
2 . Hɛn egyaam ndakamaa wɔ ha,
Ha na hɛn nkorɔfo tse;
Hɛn mba so: na yebesi dɛn
Adɔ beebi kyɛn ha?

MHB 881
3 . Bɔ hɛn ahe ho ban ma hɛn,
Na dom hɛn asomdwee;
Ma hɛn nkurow nya prɔmprɔmyɛ,
Hɛn mfudze nyɛ bafuu.

MHB 881
4 . Dua nyimdzee nye nokwar ho dɔ m'
Ka hɛn na Ɔwo bɔ mu;
Na ma hɛn mbepɔw na mbɔnsa
Mbɔ m' nhuhor fahodzi.

MHB 881
5 . Aman nyina Ewuradze;
Hɛn man hyɛ Wo nsamu;
Ma onsuma Wo mu, ntwer Wo,
Dɛ ne daapem Nyɛnko.  Amen.

MHB 882
1 . 'SAASE, dzi dɛw wo tum Nyame m',
Yɛ setsie ma No, som no yie,
'Wo na ahotsewfo bɔ ndze ma W';
'Saase nnsuro, dzi dɛw Nyame m'.

MHB 882
2 . W'enyi bɛgye na nhyira aka w';
Wo dɛw na asomdwee bobu do,
Nyew, ɔdɔ nye wo bɛtsena
Kesi sor Ahenman ne mbae.

MHB 882
3 . Ɔdze wo bɔn pii no bɛkyɛ w',
Kaa No dɔ a ofi tsetse no,
Fa N'akwan do, kamfo N'asɛm,
Na sie No nokwar no daa daa.   Amen.

MHB 883
1 . ƆHEN domankoma tsɛmbuafo,
Ewuraam Wura 'hemfo Hen,
Fa W'atsɛmbu gya nyikamfo n',
Hyew man yi mu dza omuo no;
Fa W'atsaban mu yarsa no
Numa n'amantam nyina.

MHB 883
2 . Abɔbɔfo n' da ho rohwɛ
Ahotɔ dɔnhwer no kwan;
Na nkuropɔn m' begyabegya
No retsea mu dɛ bɔn ngyaa;
Na efiefi nye ndɔtɔ ase
Totɔ serɛ asomdwee.

MHB 883
3 . Nyame, sɔw W'edwuma n' ano,
Fa nkrantsee paa hɛn sum mu:
Fa W'asɛm ne mayɛ no mee
Wiadzefo a kɔm dze hɔn no;
Fa Ewuradze enyimnyam n'
Tsew ahenman mba no ho. Amen.

MHB 884
1 . YEBU ntwɛr wɔ W'ahenguan' enyim,
Ma hɛn tsibowa ma yɛmfa nhu,
Na adwen-har ma yɛmfa ntse
W'asotwe nsa no ase yie;
Sɛ yaw na fɛr no tse dɛn mpo a,
Hɛn Egya, twe hɛn bɛn Wo nkyɛn.

MHB 884
2 . Hwehwɛ akoma m' ma hɛn nokwar,
Yɛmfa obiara ne kyɛfa mma n';
Yemfi enyigyedze akɔndɔbɔn m',
Yemfi bɔn a ɔma akoma yɛ mberɛw m';
Twe hɛn, na fa Wo poma no
Kyerɛ hɛn na yenhu hɛn mfom.

MHB 884
3 . Hɛn kasaa na ndzeyɛɛ no bɔn,
Mpirenyim ho apɛbiakyerɛ;
Enyitsew bɔn a wɔfa do
Daa dze bu ekotobɔfo;
Na hɛn bra a no botae nn-hyerɛn,
Hɛn Wura, yɛserɛ, fa n' nyina kyɛ hɛn.

MHB 884
4 . Ma gya dzendzen a ɔpo kra n'
Ntsew hɛn bɔbew mu sunsum ho:
Hyew bɔn na tu enyimguase ase;
O Nyame! Ka hɔn ho ogya n' mu;
Ma yempue dɛ nyimpa fofor,
'Hotsewfo, nokwar, nyimdzefo.  Amen.

MHB 885
1 . HOM mfa akoma kor ndzi dɛw ndɛ,
Hom mfa dɛw kɛse ntow ndwom,
Ndzi dɛw, nyi hɛn Wura tumfo ayɛw,
Nyia N'abasa ama nkwagye n',
No dɔ dwuma no bɔ
Ne kɛseyɛ dawur;
No nkotsee nye Nyame a,
Ɔakyerɛ No mbɔbɔrhu;
Wɔmma N'ahotsewfo nsɔr N'.

MHB 885
2 . Mbusu ber mu yesui frɛɛ No n',
Otsiee hɛn mbɔbɔr su no,
Dza osi biara mu, hom ntwer No.
No dɔ ma yetsim bra mu;
Yefi akoma m' bɔtow
Konyimdzi ndwom ama N';
Sesei ndze nyina nse dɛ,
Wonyi hɛn Nyame ayɛw,
N'ahotsewfo nyi N' ayɛw.

MHB 885
3 . HOM mfa akoma kor ndzi dɛw ndɛ,
Hom mfa dɛw kɛse ntow ndwom,
Ndzi dɛw, nyi hɛn Wura tumfo ayɛw,
Nyia N'abasa ama nkwagye n',
No dɔ dwuma no bɔ\nNe kɛseyɛ dawur;
No nkotsee nye Nyame a,
Ɔakyerɛ No mbɔbɔrhu;
Wɔmma N'ahotsewfo nsɔr N'.  Amen.

MHB 886
1 . NYAME, yɛba bɛgye
W'adom mbɔbɔrhu no;
O tsie hɛn mbɔbɔr su,
Na mmfa W'enyim nnsuma!
     Ewuradze, tsen Wo nsa kɛse n',
     Kora hɛn awobea Ghana.

MHB 886
2 . O Dɔm Ewuradze, soɛr;
Twe Wo dzin ho nyinkun,
Na pam bɔn a ɔhyɛ fɛr n'
Fi hɛn man yi nyina m'.

MHB 886
3 . Hue W'akyɛdze etsitsir n'
Fi sor dɛ nhyira pii,
Ama yeehuhor Wo,
Eeyi Wo ayɛw mbordo.

MHB 886
4 . Hɔn a ama hɔn tum no,
Fa sor nyansa ma hɔn,
Ma wɔnyɛ W'asomfo,
Mbu man tsenenee mu.

MHB 886
5 . Fa dɔ ne gya krɔnn no
Nunu Wo Ba N' Asɔr n';
Kyekyer hɔn bɔ mu bio,
Na nkwa na nokwar mbra.

MHB 886
6 . Fa adom na tum hyehyɛ 
Wo nguankuw do asɔfo,
Ma hɔn gyedzi nye ndam
Ma wɔnyɛ asɔfo pa.

MHB 886
7 . O ma yɛndɔ Wo fie
Na yɛntsew Wo da ho,
Mfa hɛn anohobadze
Nye hɛn 'nyidzii mbrɛ Wo.

MHB 886
8 . Ma hɛn asomdwee, hɛn ber mu',
Mma tamfo biara mmbɛn,
Mma yɛmmfa emumuyɛ
Nngu W'ahentum ho fi.

MHB 886
9 . Yɛyɛ mberɛw, tsew etua,
Naaso yɛyɛ Wodze;
Yɛnnkɛfrɛ 'biara dɛ
Hɛn Nyame gyedɛ Ɔwo.   Amen.

MHB 887
1 . HƐN egyanom Nyame, Ɔwo na
Hɛn egyanom sui frɛɛ W' mbusu m',
Na Ɔwo maa wohun Wo tum nsa n'
N'anwanwandze a otum yɛ no.
Wosui tɔɔ Wo do, na itsiei;
Wɔfrɛɛ Wo, na egyee hɔn nkwa:
Ndɛ, hɔn mba so, yɛtwe bɛn Wo 
Yi Wo dzin ayɛw, serɛ Wo mboa.
     Dɔm Ewuradze, ma Wo nsa do,
     Bɔ hɛn man ho ban, hyira hɛn.

MHB 887
2 . Ewuradze, ahentum n' Wodze a,
Na idzi ndzɛmba nyina do;
Sɛ Ɔwo ehyɛ a, ahemfo na
Aman soɛr anaa wɔhwe ase.
Ma boka nye anee nsupruw
Nyina so mbɔ m' ntow ayɛyi
Mma Wo, dɔm Nyankopɔn kunyin,
Nnyɛ hɛn bi à a na mbom Ɔwoara a.

MHB 887
3 . Sɛ W'adom bɛma yɛahyerɛn
Wɔ ndaamba ber bi a ɔreba a,
Ɔno yɛserɛ Wo, boa hɛn
Ma yɛnhwehwɛ W' mboa, ntonton Wo:
Yɛnnsɛ wɔ kasa na awoo mu,
Mbom yɛbɔ m' som W'ahengua enyim,
Na hɛn Egya Ne nyɛe dzi hɛn 
Nyina do wɔ wiadze nyina. Amen.

MHB 888
1 . O AHEMFO Hen na dɔm Wura a
W'ahengua Wɔ sorsor,
Na ɔtra asaase do aman nyina,
Ɔsor nsordaafo no,
Hɔn a woedzi mu n' hɔn esunsum
Na wotum tow Wo ndwom,
Na hɛn, Wo mba so yɛsom Wo a,
Ayɛyi nyina yɛ W'dze.

MHB 888
2 . Ɔwo a edze Wo nkorɔfo fiir edzi
Na igyaa adaduafo;
Edze po ato hɛn asaase
Yi n'anaafo afamu ara,
Na ayɛ ha dɛ bea krɔnkrɔn,
Bea a sika nkanea hyerɛn,
Na nyimpa akoma dze dɔ weɔn
Apam adaka no.

MHB 888
3 . Ɔwo a edze nworaba apetse wimu,
Dze ada W'adwen edzi,
Na edze adom pii abɔ hɛn man
Yi abɔtsir mapa;
Wo mbɔbɔrhu, yenntum yɛnnkan!
Wo dɔ, W'adom, nhwɛdo;
'Yinom bor hɛn hia nyina do,
Ɔtra hɛn mpaabɔ mpo.

MHB 888
4 . O ahemfo Hen, dɔm Wura,
Egyaam na hɛn Nyame
Ka hɛn ho; na sɛ ehum bi
Rubotu hɛn ndaamba a,
Ma Wo dɔ n' nhwira mununkum n' mu,
Mpepa hɛn nyinsuwa,
Gya hɛn fa mber pa m' kɔ heaven
Da a ɔmmbɔ adze no mu.

MHB 889
1 . EGYAAM Nyame a ifi tsetse,
Hɛn akodzi mpasuar do Sahen,
Wo tumdzi ase na yedzi nyim,
Eehum na aaham nyinara do;
Dɔm Ewuradze, ka hɛn ho,
Amma hɛn werɛ eemmfir da!

MHB 889
2 . Gyigyeegye na ntseamu n' bɔ adze,
Supifo na ahemfo no kɔ;
Wo tsetse afɔr no tsim hɔ,
Akoma a abobɔ na abotow.
Dɔm Ewuradze, ka hɛn ho,
Amma hɛn werɛ eemmfir da!

MHB 889
3 . Hɛn nsordaafo kɔ akono
Kodum anhwea m' na akoko do gya;
Naaso hɛn ndeda hyerɛpɛɛ nyina
Tse dɛ Nineveh na Tyre dze n'!
Aman Tsɛmbuafo, fa kyɛ hɛn,
Amma hɛn werɛ eemmfir da!

MHB 889
4 . Sɛ hɛn eyiedzi kɔ hɛn tsir mu,
Ma dɛm ntsi yɛhyɛ ase horan.
Dɛ mbrɛ ɔyɛ a aman nkaa no a,
Wɔnnto hɛn koraa mpo n' yɛ n';
Dɔm Ewuradze, ka hɛn ho,
Amma hɛn werɛ eemmfir da!

MHB 889
5 . Na abosonsɔr akoma a
Ɔtwer ndadze etur na nkrantsee,
Mbanyinndam hun a onntum nngyina,
Na ɔroweɔn a ɔmmfa Wo nnweɔn,
Ntuw gyangyan na nkwanseasɛm so -
Ewuradze, dom hɛn tsia yinom.

MHB 89
1 . CHRIST, m'enyidado fapem, 
Christ, me dɛw no nsubura,
Ma menda ho ntsena WO mu; 
Memfa m'ahoɔdzen nsom WO.

MHB 89
2 . Ma Wo dɔ n' ndzɛw m' akoma m', 
Fa Wo ho suro hyɛ mo mu;
W'ayɛyi nyɛ mo botae,
W'anoyerɛw nyɛ m'enyigye.

MHB 89
3 . 'Mandzehu ba m'akwan mu, 
Na ɔbra n'ehum tu me a,
Ma W'ehumbɔbɔr enyiwa n'
Nhyɛ me nkuran wɔ sum ber mu.

MHB 89
4 . Konyimdzi fi Wo dzin m' ba
Bɛhyɛ sor dɛw ndwom no ma a, 
Ma mentse nka bi wɔ m' mu, 
Dwumadzi nye dɔ nhyɛ m' ma.

MHB 89
5 . 'Bra ne dɛw, m'bɛkamfo Wo, 
Wo nsɛmpa bɛhyɛ m'ano; 
Wo kan no m'bɔsɔ n' daa nyina, 
Na m'botu sum ndwuma nyina.

MHB 89
6 . Adom mbordo nsunyiwa, 
Ma minnya dza mihia kwa; 
Kɛpem mewie adasa bra n',
Menkyerɛ dɛ metse ma Christ.

MHB 89
7 . Motwer Wo bɔgyaa n' ampa, 
Biribi nnkɛhaw m'akoma; 
M'botwa nsuyirii no sɔnn,
M'bodua 'Manuel bea n' do sɔnn.

MHB 89
8 . Dɛm a, bue me abow no, 
Ma monkɔ kan bea no do;
Mehu dɛ m'tse ma Christ yi,
Munhu dɛ owu yɛ m' mfaso.  Amen.

MHB 890
1 . APONKƐSE, hom mbuebue yie,
Hom nhwɛ, enyimnyam Hen n' rotweɔn!
Ahemfo Hen no rotwe bɛn,
Wiadze Agyenkwa no wɔ ha;
Nkwa na nkwagye na ɔdze nam,
Ntsi hom ndzi dɛw na hom ntow ndwom.
Egya, yeyi W' ayɛw,
Bɔadze, nyansfo nye W'.

MHB 890
2 . Ewuradze yɛ pɛrpɛr boafo,
Ɔyɛ mbɔbɔrhu daa nyina,
Krɔnkrɔnyɛ nye N'ahenkyɛw daa,
Mbɔbɔrhu nye N'ahempoma
Ɔdze hɛn mbusu n'ewiei nam,
Ntsi wiadze dze enyigye tow ndwom,
Egya, yeyi W' ayɛw,
Ɔwo a eyɛ etumdze.

MHB 890
3 . O nhyira nye asaase na kurow a 
Wɔbɔ Ɔhen Christ no Ne dzin,
O siar nye akoma na fidua a
Dɛm konyimdzi Hen yi ba mu!
Ɔno nye dɛw, Ewia ketee a
Ɔdze enyigye mapa nam.
Sunsum Werɛkyekyefo,
W'adom dɔɔ sō, ampa.

MHB 890
4 . Bue w'akoma n' apon n' petee,
Yɛ n' asɔrfi a woeyi esi
Nkyɛn ama sor dwumadzi nko,
Na mpaabɔ, dɔ na dɛw aahyɛ n' ma;
Dɛm n' na Ɔwo Hen no bɛhɛn mu,
Na bra fofor kɛse aahyɛ ase.
Nyame, Ɔwo na ayɛyi 
Nka W' kasa na nyɛe mu.

MHB 890
5 . Pomfo, bra, yebue hɛn akoma
Petee ma Wo dɛ tsena mu!
Ma yɛntse Wo nka dɛ ewɔ m';
Da W'adom dɔ n' edzi, hɛn mu,
Ma Wo Sunsum no ndzi hɛn kan,
Kesi dɛ yebenya botae n'.
Ayɛyi a ɔmmbɔ adze
Na yɛdze ma Wo dzin.  Amen.

MHB 891
1 . KUROW fɛɛfɛw no ne Hen,
Wimu man a otsim hɔ daa,
Nkyɛ hɛn nkurow nyina aayɛ
Krɔnkrɔn wɔ W'enyi do,
Wɔaasan efi sum ndwuma ho
Aayɛ kan nkurow!

MHB 891
2 . Mbofra a wonnyi dɛw bi dzi n',
Kyerɛ dɔ fa ma hɔn;
Woeyiyi hɔn ndzinoa ntsi
Fɛw bi nnyi hɔ ma hɔn;
Wo hɔn fofor kɔ ndaamba
Enyidar n' ho.

MHB 891
3 . Ma etutuwpɛ mbɔ adze,
Tu asabokwafo bɔr;
Ɔwo nye Duyɛfo kor a
Esa akoma yarba,
Ema adwen ntanta si pi,
Na etsen brafun.

MHB 891
4 . Ma nkrumsifo nyina dɛw,
Na awerɛhofo ntow ndwom;
Ma kan nhyerɛn nsaaba biara a
Sum na wu ahyɛ hɔ mā n';
Ma W'ahendzi no nsian mbra
Bɔn mpasuar do.

MHB 891
5 . Mma ɔnnkyɛr na ma hɛn nkurow
Nhyɛ W'enyimnyam ntar no;
Ma edwumabea nyɛ asɔrfi,
Fie biara mpaabɔ fie;
Kurow biara nya ahoɔfɛw;
Nyame wɔ hɔ!

MHB 892
1 . ONNYIEWIEI Nyame a idzi hen wimu na
Nsaase do, na wɔtow ndwom ma Wo daa,
Ɔwo a igya aman abamba fi sum
Kebii mu kɔ enyimnyam da kɛse n' mu;
Dzi hen hɛn akoma mu, ama yeenya
W'akwankyerɛ, W'ahoɔdzen na Wo mboa.

MHB 892
2 . Yefi Wo mu, Wo dɔ n' mu mba nye hɛn,
Na Wo dɔ Ba kortoo no No nuanom;
O Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, sian dɛ ebubur
Bra hɛn akoma mu, ama yaayɛ kor,
Dɛ mbrɛ yɛnye Wo a yɛhwɛ W' no yɛ no;
Na yɛnye hɛn Nua, hɛn Nyɛnko yɛ no.

MHB 892
3 . Yɛbɛyɛ kor ako etsia bɔn nyina,
Ayɛ kor dɔ m' wɔ dza oye nyina ho;
Ayɛ kor wɔ dɛw a ɔma adwontow mu,
Ayɛ kor wɔ nkrum a ɔba mpaabɔ mu,
Ayɛ kor wɔ tum a ɔma adehyehyɛ m',
Ma yeetsin nokwar do, eedzi W'ekyir.

MHB 892
4 . Ewuradze, fa W'sor akodze hyɛ hɛn,
Nye kyɛm na Sunsum dɔ nkrantsee no so;
Ma W'asɛm no nnunu hɛn 'ber nyina;
Yɛnnserɛ konyimdzi biara a ommfir Wo,
Ma hɛn, fa kam hɛn; ma dɛw anaa yaw;
Dza ohia nye yebohu dɛ yɛsom Wo.

MHB 893
1 . O HOM a hom ehu dɛ dɔ yɛ dɛw,
Hom nyɛ akwankyerɛ mma 'kyingyefo a
Wofintsiw kwan do hwehwɛ dɔ n'.

MHB 893
2 . Hom ntow dɔ ho ndwom ama nyia
Ɔbɛtse n' ekyirekyir n' eetsie,
Aasoɛr, aadwendwen, aatwe abɛn.

MHB 893
3 . Hom mbɔ dɔ ho bra, daa ma hɔn a
Wohu hom bra n' hɔn so dze dɔ
Aahyerɛn na wɔabɔdɔm hom.

MHB 894
1 . EGYA a ihue akyɛdze pii
Fi W'akorae ma nyimpa mba,
Ma Wo nkorɔfo tum amma
Wɔannsɛɛ W'akyɛdze no kwa.

MHB 894
2 . Ma enyigye pa ahomgye mu,
Ahohyɛdo wɔ enyigye m'
Yɛmfa ha ndzɛmba nyɛ papa,
Hɛn ho ntsew, hɛn sunsum nhyerɛn.

MHB 894
3 . Yi dza ɔsan hɛn adze fi
Ɔman yi nye aman nyina mu;
Dwedwe nsɔhwɛ no bɔr ano,
Ma W'atamfo mfi hɔ nguan.

MHB 894
4 . Kā hɛn ho, ma hɛn W'ahoɔdzen,
Ama yɛdze ahoɔdzen a ɔnnsā 
Eehyia hɛn atamfo biara
Na yeegyina kō no mu.

MHB 894
5 . Ɔwo a eyɛ hɛn Sahen daa,
Dzi hɛn enyim wɔ nkodzen mu,
Ma W'Asɔr ngye wiadze nsi hɔ;
Ma hɛn nyansa na ahoɔdzen.

MHB 894
6 . Egya a ahwehwɛ hɛn ehu hɛn,
Nyame Ba a Wo dɔ akyekyer hɛn,
Sunsum a ewɔ hɛn mu, hɛn nkyɛn,
Nyame Egya kɛse, tsie hɛn.   Amen.

MHB 895
1 . BEEBI a ɔbra akwan hyia,
Beebi a nyimpa horow sū,
Adasa gyigyeegye nyina m'
Yɛtse Wo ndze, O Nyimpa Ba.

MHB 895
2 . Mbɔbɔrwa na ohia mpasuar do,
Sum akwan a suro wɔ do,
Akwan a emim etsim do,
Mbea yi na yehu Wo nyinsu.

MHB 895
3 . Mbofraber mberɛwyɛ nyina m'
Mbaa su, na mbanyin fona mu,
Nye akra a wɔato bahaw so,
W'akoma mmfii yinom ho da.

MHB 895
4 . Nsu a wɔdze ma wɔ Wo dzin mu,
Da W'adom no foforyɛ edzi;
Naaso dɔmpepe rohwehwɛ
W'enyim fɛɛfɛw noara ahwɛ.

MHB 895
5 . O hɛn Wura, fi bepɔw n' do
Ntsɛmara bɛsa 'yinom yar;
Bɛnye ahoperfo yi ntsena,
Bɛnantsew hɛn abrɔn mu bio.

MHB 895
6 . Kesi dɛ yebosua Wo dɔ n',
Na yeedzi W'ekyir W'akwan do,
Na hɛn Nyankopɔn Kurow no
So nam enyimnyam mu aba.

MHB 896
1 . AFEI yeyi ekunyin ayɛw,
Egyanom a wɔgyee hɔn dzin;
Na yɛkamfo Ewuradze no a
Ɔkyerɛ N'enyimnyam nyimpa m'.

MHB 896
2 . Yɛkamfo enyansafo nà abràn a,
Wɔhyɛɛ hɔn dɔm enyimnyam;
Woyinom boaa ndzepa, tsiaa bɔn,
Dze maa nkorɔfo yɛɛ ɔman.

MHB 896
3 . Yeyi ekunyin nyinara
Na adwontofo so ayɛw;
Hɔn ndwom pegyaa akra kɔr sorsor,
Tse dɛ mframa dzendzen bi.

MHB 896
4 . Yeyi edwimfo a wosisii
Adan fɛɛfɛw so ayɛw,
Wodzii edwin mapa, nam dɛm
Kaa edwumayɛfo bɔɔ mu.

MHB 896
5 . Yehuhor edzin a yɛkaa,
Na hɔn a ɔnam mber ntsi
Yenntum nnkaa hɔn no so nyina,
Yembu hɔn ɔdɔ kɛse mu.

MHB 896
6 . Hɔn mbiew rohom asomdwee mu,
Woewie hɔn edwuma yɛ;
Wohyiraa asaase wɔ hɔn bra m',
Nyame na adasa ehyira hɔn.

MHB 896
7 . Dɛm ntsi yeyi ekunyin ayɛw,
Egyanom a wɔgyee hɔn dzin;
Na yɛkamfo Ewuradze no a
Ɔkyerɛ N'enyimnyam nyimpa m'.

MHB 897
1 . YENSI dɛn nsom wo yie papa,
Hɛn Awobea a yɛdɔ wo?
'Bɛn na hɛn nsa, akoma na adwen
Bɛyɛ akyerɛ hɛn dɔ?
Ndaamba regye hɛn mboa daa daa,
Wo tsetse ndze n' pia hɛn;
Ana hɛn Wo mba nye mbabaa
Nnkɛfata dɛ hɛn egyaam?

MHB 897
2 . Nnyɛ akodzi nko na yɛnam do
Som anyɛnkoyɛman no;
Akodzi a ɔkrɔn kɛse kyɛn dza
Yenyim n' sesei bɛba;
Asomdwee ho ndwuma m' empiresi,
'Brabɔ m' nyimpa ho som
Yinom bɛhyɛ akodzi anan mu,
Adwedwe hɛn aperdzi.

MHB 897
3 . Mber tsentsen na bɔn tum afa
Wiadze nyina ndɔmmum,
Mber tsentsen na akodzi amen
Dasanyi n' frɛ a mu dɔ.
O m'afɛ, hom nhwehwɛ dza ɔkrɔn!
Hom mfua dza ɔsom bo m'!
Ɔtan ne mber etwa mu kɔ:
Hom mbɔ Christ mbra dawur.

MHB 897
4 . Aman nyina Ewuradze, soma
Wo nkwa mframa n' sesei,
Siesie hɛn ma nkwa ho ndwuma,
Gye hɛn fi owu ndwuma m';
Fa hɛn ka W'akodɔm no ho,
Yɛnko nyɛ adehye,
Akofrɛ no nye Enuadɔ a
Ɔkyekyer aman nyina.

MHB 898
1 . BER wɔ hɔ ma nyimpa na aman
Dɛ wɔfa adwen pa bi,
Wɔ nokwar na ator akodzi n' mu,
Dɛ wɔfa papa anaa bɔn;
Nyankopɔn Ne Christ no, anaa
Apam bi a ɔkyerɛ siar anaa ndom;
Na sum anaa kan n' ne nyii no a
Otwa mu a, ɔnnsan mmba bio da.

MHB 898
2 . Sɛ yɛgye nokwar nwen no
Ber a yennhun ne nhyira a,
Na yebohu siar a ɔdze nam,
Na pɛrpɛr mu prɔmprɔmyɛ;
Ber n' na ɔkatakyi bɛyɛ adwen
Na okotoo begyina nkyɛn,
Kesi dɛ ɔdodow n' bohu dɛ
Gyedzi a wɔapow no ho hia.

MHB 898
3 . Atɔfo a wɔrehyew hɔn kan n' m',
Christ, yehu W' bɔgyaa anamɔn
Dɛ ɔdze mbeamudua pii rotow
Kɔ kan ridzi ako daa.
Mber fofor kyerɛ asodzi fofor,
Mber sɛɛ dza wɔagye ato mu,
Na hɔn a wɔnye nokwar besian n'
Wɔ dɛ wɔtow kɔ kan daa.

MHB 898
4 . Bɔn ne pɛ bɛyɛ prɔmprɔm dze,
Naaso nokwar na otsim;
Kaansa ne kyɛfa nye ɔsɛntwer,
Na bɔn tse ahengua do mpo a,
Ɔsɛntwer n' bɔwosow ndaamba,
Nyame so wɔ sum n' ekyir
Rohwɛ dza yennyim nyina mu,
Rohwɛ Nankasa N' dze do.

MHB 899
1 . HƐN Awobea, yɛdze hɛn dɔ
Na berɛ sua ma wo ber nyina;
Ber a yeenyin na yeesi do
Dɛ mbanyin na mbaa wɔ hɛn man m'.

MHB 899
2 . Hɛn sor Egya a edɔ obiara,
O boa Wo mba ber a wɔfrɛ;
Ma wɔaakyekyer ɔman krɔnkrɔn
Wɔ mbersantsen nyinara mu.

MHB 899
3 . Kyerɛ hɛn yɛnsoa kɔndua n' mbabun m',
Yɛmfa mbɔdzembɔ, nokwardzi;
Ma hɛn ber mu aadom Wo nkowaa
Nokwar a ɔma aman gyina.

MHB 899
4 . Kyerɛ hɛn ma yendzi hɛnho do,
'Hohyɛdo na ahotsew m' ber nyina,
Ma yɛdze enyikan afɔrbɔ
Eepue W'enyim ber a ɔsɛ mu.

MHB 899
5 . Kyerɛ hɛn ma nyina m' yɛnhwɛ Wo
Dɛ Tsɛmbuafo, na nnyɛ nyimpa a,
Ama yɛnye Wo aanantsew a
Yenkosuro nyimpa, nnhwɛ hɔn enyim.

MHB 899
6 . Kyerɛ hɛn ahoɔdzen a wɔmmfa nnsisi
'Bɔbɔfo, wɔ ndzeyɛɛ na adwen m',
Ama yɛhyɛ W'ase n' yeenya
Mbanyinndam dze ahyɛ nyimpa ma.

MHB 899
7 . Ma hɛn enyi ngye ndzɛmba nkumaa ho,
Ndzi dɛw a ommfi binom yaw mu,
Yɛmfa hɛn mfom nkyekyɛ hɛnho,
Na yɛndɔ adasamba nyina!

MHB 899
8 . Hɛn Awobea, yɛdze wo tuw;
Wo yieyɛ ntsi na hɛn egyaam wui;
Yɛdze hɛn tsir, akoma, nsa,
Sua ma wo mbersantsen nyina.

MHB 9
1 . O SƆR Ewuradze wɔ krɔnkrɔnyɛ fɛɛfɛw mu
Kotow N'enyim, bɔ N'enyimnyam dawur; 
Fa setsie mapa ɔnye mbrɛhoadze huanhuam,
Kotow huhor No, Ne dzin nye Ewuradze.

MHB 9
2 . Fa w'adwendwen adzesoa to N'ananadze, 
Ɔbɔsoa ama wo wɔ N'akoma mu,
Ɔbɛkyekye wo werɛ, na oetsie wo mpaabɔ, 
Na oegya w' taataa dɛ.mbrɛ oye ma w'.

MHB 9
3 . Mma nnsuro dɛ ebɛhɛn N'abangua do hɔ, 
Dɛ ahodze a ewɔ no suar ntsi:
Afɔrbɔdze a wɔdze gu N'afɔrmbukyia do 
Nye nokwar fɛɛfɛw na ɔdɔ mapa.

MHB 9
4 . Yinom, sɛ yɛdze ba suro na ahopopo m' mpo a, 
Ɔbɛgye wɔ dzin a ɔsorn bo no ntsi; 
Ɔbɛpepa hɛn nyinsu, ɔama yeedzi dɛw, 
Oetu hɛn suro, ɔarna hɛn awerɛhyɛm'.

MHB 9
5 . O sɔr Ewuradze wɔ krɔnkrɔnyɛ fɛɛfɛw mu!
Kotow N'enyim, bɔ N'enyimnyam dawur;
Fa setsie mapa ɔnye mbrɛhoadze huanhuam,
Kotow huhor No, Ne dzin nye Ewuradze.
Amen.

MHB 90
1 . M'APƐDZE a odzi kan,
Jesus a owui maa me;
Enyigye a mohwehwɛ, 
Wo mu nko na mubohu.

MHB 90
2 . M'beyi W' ayɛw, m'bohu Wo,
Ɔno nye me nhyira wɔ ha;
M'bohu Wo na madɔ Wo,
Ɔnyɛ me nhyira wɔ sor.

MHB 90
3 . Ewuradze mohwer Wo a,
M'abrabɔ rinnkesi hwee, 
Ewuradze, sɛ minya Wo a,
Minyim dɛ munnkowu da.

MHB 90
4 . Ahomgye nyina Mafo,
Ofi Wo serew mu nko, 
Asomdwee na dɛw fir Wo;
Minya Wo a, 'bɛyɛ medze.

MHB 90
5 . Meserɛ Wo, ma minnya Wo;
Ɔwo nye enyigye nyina;
Mibenya enyigye mapa,
Wɔ asaase ha na sor. Amen.

MHB 900
1 . ME man, medze famu ha ndzɛmba a odzi mu na ɔkrɔn
No mu tsitsir kɛse a ɔyɛ mo dɔ som hyɛ wo bɔ,
Ɔdɔ a ɔnnyɛ nyiyiano, na ɔsɔw nsɔhwɛ nyina,
Na ɔdze dza ɔsom bo na oye nko bɔ afɔr,
Ɔdɔ a ɔmmpa ara da, ɔdɔ a otua kaw nyina,
Ɔdɔ a onnsuro dɛ ɔdze noho botwa akyer mpo.

MHB 900
2 . Na ɔman kor bi so wɔ hɔ a matse nka dada,
Ɔsom bo kɛse ma n'adɔfo, na afei ɔso;
Yɛnnkɛkan n'akofo, na yennkohu ne Hen da;
N'akoban nye nokwar akoma, ne dɛw nye ɔhaw;
Na nkakrankakra, wɔ kommyɛ mu, ne mamfoe dɔr,
No suban nye botooyɛ, n'akwan yɛ asomdwee.

MHB 901
1 . NYAME a Wo ho yɛ hu! Ɔhen a ehyɛ ma
Ehum yɛ W' mbɛn, na enyinam Wo nkrantsee;
Fi sor W'ahendzi bea kyerɛ ayamuhyehye,
Ewuradze, ma hɛn asomdwee hɛn ber m'.

MHB 901
2 . Nyame a eyɛ tsimbɔbɔr! Wiadze apow
Wo siar kwan n', etsiatsia W'asɛm no do;
Mma mma W'ebufuw huuhu no nnosɛr hɛn do,
Ewuradze, ma hɛn asomdwee hɛn ber m'.

MHB 901
3 . Tsenenee Nyame! Yeehur Wo bo kɛse,
Naaso W'asɛm tsim hɔ kesi daapem;
Ator na mfom nnkotum atsena Wo nkyɛn;
Ewuradze, ma hɛn asomdwee hɛn ber m'.

MHB 901
4 . Nyansabuakwa Nyame! W'enyimka n' ne gya m'
Wiadze bedzi n' ho do; nokwar etsim,
W'ahendzi no nam sum kebii mu rebɛn;
Ewuradze bɛma asomdwee ber yi m'.

MHB 901
5 . Dɛm no na Wo mbofra dze ɔsom ndaase
Bɛma Nyia ɔgyee hɔn fii mbusu mu n',
Wɔbɔtow ndwom fi mpoano kesi mpoano,
'Somdwee nka aman, 'yɛyi nka Ewuradze.

MHB 902
1 . ENYIMNYAM nka Nyame wɔ wimu,
Na asomdwee ntsim wɔ asaase do!
O Jesus Wo a wɔakrɔn Wo sor,
Bra bɛyɛ hɛn Wura tumfo!
'Wo a wɔwoo W'hianyi Bethlehem,
Na 'gyee wiadze a ɔayew no nkwa,
O san bra W'abɔdze nkyɛn bio;
Dzi hen W'adom ahenman n' mu.

MHB 902
2 . Ebaa nyimpa honandua mu n',
Abɔdze nyina peen W'awoo do;
Enyisɔ afe no nyae bae,
Na heaven so buei ma asaase;
Wiadze a oenya no sor Wura n'
Dze adwensaa kor bɔɔ mu tontoon
Amandwee na dɔ Mafo no,
Asomdwee Wura nye Ɔhen no.

MHB 902
3 . O nkyɛ wɔama woeehu Wo bio!
Sian wɔ Wo Sunsum su n' mu bio,
Na bɛkyekyer wɔ W'akowaa
Biara m' onnyiewiei ahenman;
Wo nkotoo na itum hyira
Na ema siar aman tsie Wo,
Na ema ɔtan bɔ adze,
Na ema wiadze dzi W'ekyir.

MHB 902
4 . Ntsi bra Wo nkowaa a wɔrepɛ
Ehu Wo mbae no hɔn nkyɛn bio,
Dua mbɔbɔrhu do fa kyekyer
Wo kommyɛ asomdwee man no;
Awerɛhow boguan W'enyim,
Na ebufuw na tan abɔ adze;
Enyiber na adwembɔn bowu,
Na wentwiwentwi nnkɛhaw hɛn.

MHB 903
1 . O ƆDƆ Nyame, 'somdwee Hen,
Ma ko mbɔ adze wiadze nyina:
Siw nyimpa bɔn ebufuw kwan,
O Nyankopɔn, ma asomdwee bio.

MHB 903
2 . Ewuradze, kaa Wo tsetse ndwuma n',
Anwanwadze a hɛn egyaam kae n',
Mma nnkaa hɛn bɔn ne nkekaawa n',
O Nyankopɔn, ma asomdwee bio.

MHB 903
3 . Woana na yɛngye n' ndzi dɛ Ɔwo?
Yɛntwer ebɛn dɛ Wo nokwasɛm n'?
Obi mmfrɛɛ Wo nngyinaa gyan da;
O Nyankopɔn, ma asomdwee bio.

MHB 903
4 . Bea a 'hotsewfo na abɔfo wɔ n',
Akoma nyina bɔ mu wɔ dɔ m';
Fa sor nkyehoma n' ka hɛn bɔ m',
O Nyankopɔn, ma asomdwee bio.

MHB 904
1 . HOM nhwɛ, Ewuradze bepɔw no
Bɔkrɔn ekyir nda n' mu
Akyɛn akoko no nyina,
Na nkorɔfo ahwɛ.

MHB 904
2 . Aman nye kasa horow pii
Dze dɛw bɛpem akɔ
Nyame bepɔw n' do ase dɛ,
Ne fie na yɛbɔkɔ.

MHB 904
3 . Kan a ofi Zion bepɔw do n'
Bɛhyerɛn aman nyina pii do;
Nyia odzi hen wɔ Salem 'bansor n'
Bɛyɛ aman nyina Hen.

MHB 904
4 . Obobu aman ntamu atsɛn,
Nokwar bɛkyerɛ no kwan,
N'ahempoma bɛma bambɔ,
Esi ɔbɔn no mpa.

MHB 904
5 . Aperdzi na manso biara
Nnkɛba asomdwee ber no m',
Wɔdze hɔn nkrantsee bɔbɔ nsɔw,
Na mpeaa so ayɛ ndar.

MHB 904
6 . Akodɔm nnkehyia akodɔm bi,
Na asafo dɔm nnkɔtɔr;
Wɔdze akobɛn bɛsɛn ban ho,
Wonnkosua akodzi bio.

MHB 904
7 . Afei Jacob fifo, hom mbra
Mbɔsom N' krɔnkrɔn-bea do,
Na hom nam Nyame kan no mu n',
Hom ahyerɛn ahoɔfɛw mu.

MHB 905
1 . Hom nhotse nkrumsi nyina ngu,
Hom nwosow mma ewuakɔr so;
Hom nwosow ntu hia ne haw nkɔ,
Hom nwosow mfrɛ dɛw mma adasa.

MHB 905
2 . Hom nhotse dza etwa mu ngu,
Nye tsetse aperdzi nyina;
Hom nwosow mfrɛ abrabɔ ho siar,
Ndzeyɛɛ pa, nye ɔbra pa a odzi mu.

MHB 905
3 . Hom nwosow ntu guasohantan
Nye dza ɔhyɛ fɛr nyina so;
Hom nwosow mfrɛ ɔdɔ nokwar a ɔtsen,
Hom nwosow ma yie ho dɔ mbra.

MHB 905
4 . Hom nhotse koannkɔ yar mfi hɔ,
Nye sikanyiber nyina so!
Hom nhotse ntokwaw dadaw n' gu,
Hom nwosow mfrɛ mfe apem asomdwee.

MHB 905
5 . Hom nwosow mfrɛ adehye abran
Nye ebirɛmpɔn na ayamuyiefo;
Hom nwosow ntu hɛn man no sum,
Hom nwosow mma Christ a ɔreba n'.

MHB 905
7 NDƆMBA, hom nwosow ngu wimu,
Nkyerɛ mununkum nye awɔw;
Afe n' rokɔ ewiei anafua 'i,
Ndɔmba, hom nwosow ngya no kwan.

MHB 906
1 . OWURA Christ, ebaa nyimpa nkyɛn n'
Wɔkyekyeer Wo mbeamudua do:
Sii Ɔwo ɔgye-ahentum n' atwetwe,
Na wɔsoaa Wo nsoɛ ahenkyɛw;
Sesei so hɛn bɔn da ho wen
Nsoɛ fofor wowɔ W'enyi ekyir
Na ɔdze nyinsu atar hyɛ Wo.

MHB 906
2 . O ɔdɔ nwanwa a oennya kwan
Biara wɔ bra bɔn mu no;
Ɔdze W' bɔkɔ wu dze, na ebɛfa
Do edzi Wo kumfo n' do
Kesi dɛ ɔbo nnkɛda ɔbo do,
Na ɔman biara ahopɔw bogu
Dɛ huntuma wɔ W'enyim.

MHB 906
3 . Christ No dɔ a asan aba bio,
Ana yɛnsan mpow Wo bio
Nkesi dɛ ɔtan na ɔko sum no m'
Yɛbɔhwer Wo na yɛ ahera?
Gye hɛn fi ekyingye dadaw n' mu,
Ma yɛnhwehwɛ W'asomdwee man n',
Ama hɛn nsa aaka Wo.

MHB 906
4 . O Jesus, Wo nsa a wopirae n',
Nyɛ W'adzebɔ n' bio hɛn mu;
Hɛn ntsɛn dɛtse a, hɛn ntuw egu,
Na yɛrotweɔn Wo nyikyerɛ;
O dɔ a odzi nkogu do nyim,
Hɛn akoma ba Wo Dua n' enyim,
Dɛ yɛdze wie Wo nkwagye n'.

MHB 907
1 . TUM nyina Egya, Ɔwo a edze
Nkwa akyɛdze ma atseasefo kwa,
Kyea W'enyi hwɛ bɔn na aperper,
Na fa hɛn kɔ bra a ɔkrɔn mu.

MHB 907
2 . Ahemfo Hen, krɔn hɛn akoma
Kɔ dza ɔhyerɛn na oye ho;
Eyiedzi kɛse ho mfonyin
Nye enuadɔ krɔnn ho enyisun.

MHB 907
3 . Wo wiadze ne yaw n' ekitsa n',
Emim na mfaso a onnsi kwaa;
Enyidzi a no ho egu fi,
Na ne tsetse bɔn ndwuma no.

MHB 907
4 . Tsie mpaa a Wo nkowaa robɔ no
Aman nyina mu ndɛ da yi,
Na ma W' nkwagye kɛse n' mbɛpram
Bɔn no tum a egu no do .  Amen.

MHB 908
1 . TSETSE nkwa a wohuee guu weɔɔ,
Nyame dɔ a ɔnnsa, wɔnntɔn a
Ɔpem kwa wɔ nkɔnhyɛsɛm
Na adasa hɔn fahodzi m'.

MHB 908
2 . Wɔannkam adze biara do
Amma hɔn a woeyi hɔn n' nko;
Mber na mbea nyina dzi wɔ Wo,
Akoma na adwen pa n' bura.

MHB 908
3 . Mbadwemba nyinara na
Akatakyi mpo twer Wo, 
Ema adwen na ndzeyɛɛ pa,
'Dze nokwar na yie bɔ hyew.

MHB 908
4 . Etsew edwindzi na ndwom na
Kyerɛwsɛm na akwantu so ho,
Isiw aperdzi na bɔn kwan,
Na 'bue kwan ma fahodzi.

MHB 908
5 . Tsetse nkwa a wohuee guu weɔɔ,
Nyame dɔ a ɔnnsa, wɔnntɔn a 
Ɔpem kwa wɔ nkɔnhyɛsɛm
Na adasa hɔn fahodzi m'.

MHB 909
1 . MBƆBƆRHU Nyame, dabɛn
Na ebɛgye adasa?
Ewuradze, ɔyɛ nyimpa,
Nnyɛ ahengua na ahenkyɛw,
Na wɔyɛ W'akoma ho nhyiren;
Na mma wonnwu dɛ nkyɛkyɛr kwa,
Na mma sum kebii mmpram hɛn do,
Nyame ngye adasa!

MHB 909
2 . Ana bɔn bɔwo bɔn daa?
Na abran ho ayɛ dzen daa?
Egya, ɔyɛ Wo pɛ dɛ 
Nyimpa bɛhyɛ bɔn ma?
Wo mbepɔw na wimu se dabi!
Nyimpa n'ewia bɛhyerɛn bio,
Na ndwom, nnyɛ nkrum, na wɔbɛtse;
Nyame ngye adasa!

MHB 909
3 . Mbɔbɔrhu Nyame, dabɛn
Na ebɛgye adasa?
Ewuradze, nyimpa yi nye
W'akoma ho nhyiren!
Wɔyɛ Wo mba dɛ abɔfo n' pɛr;
Nyame, gye nyimpa, wɔyɛ W'dze,
Fi bɔn, nhyɛdo, na abawpa mu,
Nyame ngye adasa?

MHB 91
1 . Nkorɔfo nyina nhua Jesus dzin; 
Abɔfo nhwe No fam';
Wɔmfa ahenkyɛw no mbra mbɔsoa N',
Na wɔnhyɛ N' abɔso Hen.

MHB 91
2 . 'Sɛmpa n' ho atɔfo, hom nhua N' 
Wɔ N' afɔrmbukyia n' do;
Hom nhua nyia hom tsia N' anamɔnm'
Na hom nhyɛ N' abɔso Hen.

MHB 91
3 . Israel mbasantsen, hom a 
Woeyi hom asehwem',
Hom nhua nyia ɔdze N' adom gye hom n',
Na hom nhyɛ N' abɔso Hen.

MHB 91
4 . Bɔnyɛfo, mma hom werɛ mmfir 
Bɔwen na bɔwema n';
Hom mfa hom asadze nkɔ nkɛma N',
Na hom nhyɛ N' abɔso Hen.

MHB 91
5 . Ebusua na ngyirama nyina, 
Wontwa nhwehwe N' enyim;
Na hɔn nyina wɔntow ndwom nhua
Nyia wɔahyɛ N' abɔso Hen.

MHB 91
6 . Ao, nkyɛ yɛnye sor dɔm yeetwa 
Yɛahwehwe N' ananadze,
Yeekua ho ma wɔaatow daa ndwom n',
Na yaahyɛ N' abɔso Hen!

MHB 910
1 . 'YINOM besi : Ɔsantsen a
Wiadze nnhun hɔn saso, dzedze
Fahodzi gya wɔ hɔn akra m',
Na nyimdzee kan wɔ hɔn enyim.

MHB 910
2 . Wɔbɛyɛ akofo bɔkɔɔ,
Wɔnnkɛka bɔgya bi, na mbom
Wɔbɛfa gya m', pomu, na wimu
Etsia nyimpa wiadze tumdzi.

MHB 910
3 . Aman nye aman bɛtsena daa
Wɔ asomdwee mu dɛ anyɛnkofo,
Na dɔ bɛka akoma biara,
Na wɔatse amema hɔnho.

MHB 910
4 . Nyimpa dze akoma krɔnn bɔdɔ
No nua, na wɔdze ndamyɛ tum
Atow ɔsorsor ndwom dɛɛdɛw,
Wɔ Nyankopɔn enyim daa daa.

MHB 910
5 . Edwindze pii na obopue,
Ba ndwom dehye ahyɛ wimu ma,
Na ndwom bɛhyɛ obiara mu,
Ber a asaase bɛyɛ heaven n'.

MHB 911
1 . DASANYI, fua wo nyɛnko nyimpa wo bom'!
Bea a tsema wɔ n' Nyame asomdwee wɔ hɔ;
Ɔsom pa nye dɛ hom rododɔ homho,
Serew yɛ ndwom, papayɛ so yɛ asɔr.

MHB 911
2 . Nyia Jesus dɔɔ no n' akasa nokwar mu:
Som krɔnkrɔn a ɔsɔ N'enyi daa nye dɛ
Edze dza ayew san ba na ekyekye werɛ,
Na enyɛn ekunafo na ngyanka.

MHB 911
3 . Fa enyidzi kɛse tsin Nyia N'edwuma
Krɔnn nye papayɛ n' ne fasusu do,
Ama wiadze aayɛ hɛn Egya N'asɔrfi,
Na dɔ abrabɔ aayɛ ndaase ndwom.

MHB 911
4 . Na mpokyerɛ bobubu, na wiadze ha
Ɔsatu ndwom gyigyeegye so begyaa;
Ɔdɔ botutu ebufuw ne gya egu,
Na no nso mu oedua asomdwee dua no.

MHB 912
1 . O NYIMPA, san w'ekyir, pow w'akwan bɔn n';
Wiadze yi rutwa mu, ne mber asa,
Naaso Ɔwo a ewɔ kan abɔtsir no
'Da ho nntse dza wo Nyame ka no dɛ,
O nyimpa, san w'ekyir, pow w'akwan bɔn n'.

MHB 912
2 . Bi a wiadze yɛ fɛw, na nyimpa tse dɛw m';
Mber nyina hɔn aman nyin ma ɔsɛɛ;
Wɔkyekyeer aman fi osu adaaso mu;
O nkyɛ nyimpa eenyan efi ne nda m'!
Ma asaase eedzi mu, nyimpa eehu nyansa.

MHB 912
3 . Wiadze bɛyɛ yie, na nyimpa ayɛ kor;
Gyedɛ 'yi ba na Nyame N' pɛ n' wɔayɛ;
Sesei mpo nyimpa nnsuro dɛ ɔtsea mu
Wɔ dɛw mu fi asaase kɔ sor dɛ;
Asaase ndzi mu, adasa nyɛ kor.

MHB 913
1 . ASOMDWEE dɛɛdɛw na
Yɛdze gya hɛn nuaam kwan;
Asomdwee nyir dɛ esutsen,
Mma ɔnnwew da.

MHB 913
2 . Mpaabɔ ndze bɔkɔɔ na
Yɛdze tu hɛn nuanom
'Nyiber do hyɛ Wo nhwɛdo nsa,
Daapem Nyɛnko.

MHB 913
3 . Ɔdɔsɛm tsiaa bi na
Yɛdze ma nantsew yie;
Famu ha hɛn dɔ, na sor Wodze n'
Nye hɔn bɛtsena.

MHB 913
4 . Gyedzisɛm dzendzen do
Na yɛnam dze twer Wo;
Dɛ Ɔwo Ewuradze bɛyɛ hɔn
Mboa nkwa na wu m'.

MHB 913
5 . Na enyidado mapa
Bɛhyerɛn hɛn do ampa,
Na ɔama dɛw a ɔbor wiadze
Enyisun do.

MHB 913
6 . Da yie, enyidado dɔ,
Gyedzi, asomdwee, mpaabɔ m';
Kodu dɛ Nyia Ne fie wɔ sor
Dze hɛn bɔbɔ m'.

MHB 914
1 . NYAME nye wo ntsena; yebehyia m' bio,
Mfa N'apam ngya wo, nsuo wo mu,
Mfa wo nka No nguan ho nsie yie,
Nyame nye wo ntsena, yebehyia m' bio.

MHB 914
2 . Nyame nye wo ntsena; yebehyia m' bio,
Mfa W' nhyɛ No bomu mbɔ wo ho ban,
Ɔmma wo daa daa edziban,
Nyame nye wo tsena, yebehyia m' bio.

MHB 914
3 . Nyame nye wo ntsena; yebehyia m' bio,
Sɛ ɔbra m' mbusu kyekyer wo a,
Ɔmfa N'abaw mbɔ wo ho ban,
Nyame nye wo tsena, yebehyia m' bio.

MHB 914
4 . Nyame nye wo ntsena; yebehyia m' bio,
Onyam dɔ frankaa wɔ wo do,
Mbɔ owu mpuw mfi w'enyim daa,
Nyame nye wo ntsena; yebehyia m' bio.

MHB 915
1 . HƐN Egya a Wo nko ara
Nye hɛn boafo daa daa,
Tsie hɛn, ber a yɛsɔr
Ma adɔfo a wɔadɔ mu,
Na fa W'abaw dzendzen no gye
Po na asaase do akwantufo.

MHB 915
2 . 'Siandɛ Ɔwo hɛn Egya,
Ewɔ mbea nyinara,
Na ebrɛ W'aso adze
Tsie mpaabɔ bɔkɔɔ mpo,
Na etweɔn ara so hyira
Wo mba a wɔwɔ ase ha nyina.

MHB 915
3 . Fa Wo dɔ no numa
Beebi a wɔnam biara,
Ma Wo kan na nokwar
Ngu hɔn akoma do,
Na sɛ hɔn pɛ nye Wodze sɛ a,
Ma hɔn so asomdwee na dɛw.

MHB 915
4 . Sɛ mbusu bɛn hɔn a
Yi hɔn fi ne nyina m';
Na kyerɛ hɔn dɛ Wo
Tum no nnkɛpa ara da;
Yennkotum akɔ mbrɛ wɔwɔ,
Naaso yɛdze hɔn hyɛ Wo nsa.

MHB 915
5 . Yɛyɛ ɔbra n'akwan
Do akwantufo wɔ ha,
Yehyia, dzi mpaam', kesi
Dɛ yɛkɔ Nyame hɔ;
Yɛnye hɛn adɔfo bɛtsena
Wɔ sor Egyaman no mu hɔ.

MHB 916
1 . KRƆKRƆN Egya, mbɔbɔr mu ara
Tsie hɛn mpaabɔ yi;
Hɛn adɔfo a woetu kwan no,
Hwɛ hɔn do.

MHB 916
2 . Agyenkwa Jesus, twe bɛn hɔn,
Ma hɔn kan kwankyerɛ;
Hɔn mberɛwyɛ mu fa hɔn sie
Wo nkyɛn daa.

MHB 916
3 . Awerɛhow na mbusu mu,
Ma obi nnkɔ mmba no,
Wo dɔ mu, hwɛ kyekye hɔn werɛ 
Hɔn haw mu.

MHB 916
4 . Na ma Wo nkwagye ho dɛw no
Nyɛ hɔn mboa na ahom;
Ma wɔndɔ Wo, nyi Wo ayɛw
Daa nyina.

MHB 916
5 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, ma Wo nkyerɛkyerɛ
Ntsew hɔn abrabɔ ho;
Dom hɔn ma wondzi konyim daa
Wɔ ɔko n' mu.

MHB 916
6 . Egya, Ɔba, Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn,
Ɔkorsa Nyame,
Hyira hɔn, gya hɔn abamba
Bɛn Wo ho.

MHB 917
1 . DAA daa Egya, Ɔwo a egye nkwa,
Ɔwo a W'abaw si asorɛkye ban,
Ɔwo a ehyɛ po mma onnyir nntra
Bea a Ɔwo ahyɛ no biara do :
O sɛ yesu frɛ Wo ma hɔn a
Worihyia mbusu po do a, tsie hɛn !

MHB 917
2 . Agyenkwa, Ɔwo a mframa na
Asorɛkye yɛɛ setsie maa Wo,
Ɔwo a enantseew po bun enyi,
Na edaa ne gyigyeegye mu mpo:
O sɛ yesu frɛ Wo ma hɔn a
Worihyia mbusu po do a, tsie hɛn!

MHB 917
3 . O Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, Ɔwo a nkan n'
Ibutuuw sum kebii n' enyi,
Ɔwo a emaa ogyaa weɔweɔɔ yɛ
Na emaa kan, nkwa na asomdwee:
O sɛ yesu frɛ Wo ma hɔn a
Worihyia mbusu po do a, tsie hɛn.

MHB 917
4 . O dɔ na tum nyina Ɔkorsa,
Kora hɛn dɔm do, mbusu mu;
Beebi a wɔwɔ biara gye hɔn,
Abo, ehum, gya na ɔtan mu,
Na wɔntow dɛw ayɛyi ndwom
Asaase na po do mma Wo.

MHB 918
1 . O NYAME dɔ a ebaa bɔsɔɔw
Hɛn yaw na hɛn nyinsu wɔ ha,
Yɛtow hɛn dadwen gu Wo do;
Sɛ Ɔwo bɛn a, yennsuro yaw.

MHB 918
2 . Sɛ hɛn kwan no war dɛn ara
Na awerɛhow hyɛ hɛn mber ma a,
Hɛn hyɛber na sum mpo yɛmmpow;
Hɛn akoma se : Ɔwo bɛn hɛn.

MHB 918
3 . Sa enyigye tsiaa dan yɛ nkrumsi,
Na gyedzi a ohim dan suro a,
Mfar na haban a ohinhim mpo
Bɔwasa dɛ : Ɔwo bɛn hɛn.

MHB 918
4 . Yɛtow hɛn ndzesoa gu Wo do,
Ɔwo Nyame dɔ a emmpa ara da;
Nkwa mu o, 'wu mu o, sɛ yehu dɛ;
Ɔwo bɛn hɛn a, yennsuro yaw.

MHB 919
1 . O EWURADZE, Wo nsa saa yar,
Gyee nkwa tsetsebaado;
Odzii yarba na 'wu, na sum,
Na wumaa do konyim daa.
Ɔwo na efurafo, nye emum,
Ndwedweefo nye mpakye
Na akwatafo nyinara so
Pemee baa Wo hɔ daa.

MHB 919
2 . Hwɛ, Wo nsa maa nkwa na mpɔwmudzen,
Obuee ano na enyi,
Maa abran foforyɛ, dedaa adwen,
Ma ɔgyee Wo kan no;
Sesei, Ewuradze, twe bɛn,
Fa Wo tum n' hyira hɛn,
Abrɔn mu na yar mpa ho dɛ
Mbrɛ osii Genesaret n'.

MHB 919
3 . Kɔ do ara yɛ hɛn Pomfo,
Ɔwo nkwa na owu Wura;
Fa W'ahom kɛse no dwedwe,
Ma do si, na hyira.
Fa sor nyansa no ma hɔn a
Wɔfona, wohu Wo n',
Ma ahoɔdzenfo, na ayarfo
Nyina nyi W' ayɛw daa.

MHB 92
1 . Jesus dzin bɔ adze nyina do, 
Wɔ hɛll, nye ase, nye sor,
Abɔfo na nyimpa kotow n',
Na mbɔnsam fi enyim guan.

MHB 92
2 . Jesus! dzin a ɔyɛ abɔn dɛw, 
Dzin a wɔdze akyɛ abɔn;
Ɔhotse hɔn suro nyina,
Na ɔdan hɔn hɛll yɛ heaven.

MHB 92
3 . Jesus! otu adaduafo apo, 
Otsia abɔnsam tsir do;
Ɔdze tum hyɛ nyia onnyi ahom,
Na ɔma ewufo nkwa.

MHB 92
4 . Ao, nkyɛ N' adom ahonya no 
Wiadze nyina aasɔ ahwɛ!
N-kyɛ No dɔ abaw n' bofua
Adasamba nyina.

MHB 92
5 . Ne tsenenee na No nkwagye 
Na mobɔ no dawur,
M' edwuma nye dɛ mekam' dɛ,
Wɔnhwɛ Eguambaa no!

MHB 92
6 . Edɛw bɛn na nkyɛ ɔbɛyɛ, 
Dɛ mo wumpa no do,
Mobɔbɔ Ne dzin na matseam'
Dɛ, Wɔnhwɛ Eguambaa n'!

MHB 920
1 . ƆWO a ayarfo na hɔn a woruwu
Baa Wo hɔ, na wɔammba n' kwa,
Na eda ho dze 'yarsa kasa
Dwedwe akoma a wɔwɔ yaw,
Yɛaba W'egua n' enyim yi,
Jesus, mbɔbɔr mu, tsie hɛn.

MHB 920
2 . Yɛdze dadwen na awerɛhow,
Akɛse na nkumaa so,
Bɔ m' ba W'enyim aber biara a
Wɔtsetsew totɔ hɛn do n'.
Yɛba W'ahengua n'enyim
Ntotɔserɛ mu ara.

MHB 920
3 . 'Bahatɔfo, ayarfo na
Hɔn a woruwu hia ahwɛfo,
Yɛtwer Wo sor mboa kɛse n' yi,
Ma yɛngye hɔn ndzesoa no,
Mfa hɛn ayɛyɛdze mbra,
Ntotɔserɛ mu ara.

MHB 920
4 . Ma Wo ba pa biara nnya pɛ
Wɔ ndzeyɛɛ na akoma mu
Mfa ndzi ɔdɔ ho mbra no do,
Wɔnkyerɛ awerɛkyekyer,
Mfa ayɛyɛdze mbra,
Ntotɔserɛ mu ara.

MHB 920
5 . Ma yardɔm na hɛn awerɛhow
Ntu, W'ayarsa tum n' enyim,
Kesi dɛ nyinsukyifo n' na
Hɔn a wɔapon hɔn nyina
Dze dɛw bɔbɔ mu ehyia
Wɔ W'atsɛmbugua n' enyim.  Amen.

MHB 921
1 . NYIMDZEE, na suahu nyina so,
Ayamuhyehye na dɔ,
Ne nyina fi Wo nkyɛn nko ba,
O hue, 'yinom fi sor;
Na afei, Ewuradze, kyekyɛ n'
Dɛ mbrɛ hia horow tse,
Ama woeetu hua ama Wo
Wɔ adwen na nyɛe pa mu.

MHB 921
2 . Na Ewuradze, ma da n' a
Yaw na 'wu botwa n' mbra,
Ber n' na Wo pɛrpɛrdzi bɛma
Apɔwmudzen, kan, 'somdwee;
Wimu bɛtsew nwann wɔ mbea nyina,
Na kwaa bɛyɛ tumm daa,
Na dasanyi ne ndzebɔn no
Nnkɛsɛɛ paradise bio.

MHB 922
1 . Krɔnkrɔn Nyame a w' enyim 
Atantandze remmba,
Naaso edze mbɔbɔrhu
Ehwɛ bɔn wiadze yi;
Ma hɛn akɔndɔ pa ma
Yembubu bɔn mpokyerɛm',
Ma hɛn Christ mbɔbɔrhu ma
Yɛmpɛ hɔn a wɔayew.

MHB 922
2 . Hɛn tamfo n' yɛ nyitsewfo; 
No dɔm so ho yɛ hu
Ɔdze mbusu piinara
Sɛɛ hɛn asaase pa;
Hɔn a wɔko tsia hɔn no
Wɔ ɔko dzendzen no mu n',
Wɔ dɛ wɔyɛ dzen mbordo
Wɔ Christ akodze mu.

MHB 922
3 . 'Wo na ayɛ wɔ hɛn mu 
Ndwuma akɛse a yehu 'i,
Yɛda W' ase dza ayɛ,
Ɔnye dza ebɛyɛ;
Yɛda W' ase wɔ enyidar
A ɔhyɛ hɛn nsa dzen,
Ma yɛper hwehwɛ nhyira a
Ɔkyɛn dza hɛn nsa aka.

MHB 922
4 . Ahotsew na Mbɔbɔrhu 
Na Dɔ na Tum Nyame e!
Dzi kan kodu dɛ ko yi
Ɔbɔ adze asomdwee mu.
Na hɔn a wɔdze mpaabɔ
Peer gyee hɔn enuanom
Dze konyindwom behyia Wo
O Ɔkorsa Krɔnkrɔn!    Amen.

MHB 923
1 . Dza yɛdze ma W' biara, 
Hɛn Wura, Woara Wodze a;
Dza yɛwɔ nyina yɛ Wodze:
Edze maa hɛn esie.

MHB 923
2 . Ma yɛngye W' akyɛdze 
Dɛ ahwɛdofo pa,
Dɛ mbrɛ ihyira hɛn n', yɛmfa dɛw,
Mfa hɛn ndɔbaa mbrɛ Wo.

MHB 923
3 . 'Koma pii abobɔ, 
Hia wɔ efi pii mu,
Na nguambaa pii a Guanhwɛfo n'
Wui maa hɔn n' atɔ gon.

MHB 923
4 . Ebɛkyekye werɛ, 
'Behyira abɔbɔfo,
Bɔhwehwɛ ankonam nye ngyanka,
Iyi nye nyamesom.

MHB 923
5 . Ebɛgye adaduafo, 
'Dze abɔn bɛbrɛ Nyame,
'Bɛkyerɛ nkwa na asomdwee kwan n',
Yɛ Christianyɛ ampa.

MHB 923
6 . Hɛn gyedzi yɛ mberɛw dze, 
So yɛgye W' asɛm dzi;
Nyame, dza yɛyɛ ma Wo mba,
Yɛyɛ ma Woara.

MHB 924
1 . Christ, W' enyimnyam hyɛ wim' ma, 
Christ, Wo nko nye nokwar kan,
Ndzeyɛtsenenee Ewia, pue,
Hyɛ anago sum nyina do;
Sor Adzekyee, bra me nkyɛn
Hyerɛn m' akomam', yɛ hɔ kann.

MHB 924
2 . Annka adzekyee ho ammba a, 
Nna da n' nyina ayɛ awerɛhow;
Metse sum nye mbusu mu,
Kɛpem dɛ W' ehumbɔbɔr
Hyerɛn dze dɛw hyɛ mo mu,
Na ɔbɔ m' akoma mu hyew.

MHB 924
3 . Dem ntsi bra bɛsera me kra; 
Pa bɔn nye awerɛhow sum no;
Nyame kan, hyɛ mo mu ma;
Pa m' ekyingye nyinara;
Da Woho edzi mbordo ara
Kodu da a onnyi ewiei n' mu.

MHB 925
1 . ANAPA woraba epue :
Ewuradze, yɛserɛ Wo,
Kan a ofi kan a obi annyɛ Wo,
Kyerɛ hɛn kwan.

MHB 925
2 . Gyirama na nsa ho ntsew,
Na adwen mu nyɛ wansann,
Ma nokwar no nda hɛn ano,
Yɛnyɛ adɔyɛ.

MHB 925
3 . Adzekyee resen yi,
Kɔ do yɛ hɛn Hwɛfo;
Ewuradze, kora hɛn akoma
Sɔnn fi bɔn mu.

MHB 925
4 . Ma yendzi hɛn dwuma
Daa nhyɛ Wo enyimnyam;
Na sɛ hɛn mber nye Wo hyɛ ase a,
Ma ɔnye Wo nwie.

MHB 926
1 . M'EGYA, anafua fofor so
Mu nda na ahomgye pa,
Na anapa kan ho dɛw nyina ntsi
Nhyira nka Wo dzin krɔnkrɔn n'.

MHB 926
2 . Mutu moho ka da fofor
Yi ho dze hyɛ Wo nsa,
Dɛ me bra nyɛ dɛ dza Ɔwo pɛ,
Na ma Wo pɛ nyɛ hɔ.

MHB 926
3 . Kɛse na kumaa a m'bɛyɛ n' ndɛ,
Dza m'bɛka na m'bɔdwen.
Ma memfa nhyɛ Wo enyimnyam
Wɔ Jesus Ne dzin mu .

MHB 926
4 . M'Egya, Wo dzin ntsi na mosɔr,
Gye W'abofra, hyira no.
Na ndɛ dua W'adom do gya m'
Fa tsenenee akwan do.

MHB 927
1 . AKOMA a wɔgye wi nyan,
Na enyiwa a wohu sor kan no a
Ɔyɛ adze nyina fofor n',
Nya enyigye, yɛ enyansafo.

MHB 927
2 . 'Napa biara dɔ a onyan hɛn
Na ɔma yɛsoɛr no yɛ fofor;
Ɔdze hɛn twa nda na sum sɔnn
San ba nkwa, tum na nyansa mu.

MHB 927
