3 . Adzekyeenyim biara a yɛsɔr n',
Mbɔbɔrhu fofor kyin hɛn ho;
Mbusu pa, yenya bɔnfakyɛ,
Nyame ho adwen, sor enyisun.

MHB 927
4 . Sɛ hɛn daa daa dwumadzi mu
Yɛtsew dza yɛyɛ biara ho a,
Nyame bɛma hɛn ndzepa a ɔsom
Bo pii ma yɛdze aabɔ N'afɔr.

MHB 927
5 . 'Nyɛnkofo na mbea adadaw
Sakyer yɛ dɛ heaven ma hɛn;
Dɔ na mpaabɔ kan bi bɛhyerɛn
Hɛn amandzehu biara do.

MHB 927
6 . Hɛn nkukubɔ, hɛn dwumadzi,
Bɛma hɛn dza yehia nyina;
Yebenya kwan apa hɛnho,
Na ɔama daa yaabɛn Nyame.

MHB 927
7 . Ewuradze, Wo dɔ kɛse n' mu,
Siesie hɛn ma sor ahomgye n';
Na boa hɛn ndɛ na daa nyina
Na yɛrosɔr n' yeepinkyɛn Wo daa.

MHB 928
1 . ANAPA dze enyigye kan ba,
Anago sum eguan kɔ;
Kan ne farbaa, 'ma Wo mpuei no
Mpam sum nyina mfi hɛn adwen mu.
Ɔwo ehyira hɛn wɔ hɛn nda m';
Da yi m' kyerɛ hɛn kwan, kora hɛn.

MHB 928
2 . Asaasè a enyan riyi W' ayɛw,
Wo ndwuma nyina tow
W'enyimnyam,
Ma hɛn akoma a dɔ ebu do no,
Mfa hɔn ayɛdze mbra enyigye m'.
Ɔwo akyerɛ nnoma ndwon,
Ma hɛn akoma nnyi W' ayɛw.

MHB 928
3 . Boa hɛn ma yenyi W' ayɛw daa,
Na yɛnko ntsia bɔn nyina;
Yennya hɛn mboa nyina mfi Jesu m',
Ɔno a odzii konyim maa hɛn;
Wɔsɔɔ No hwɛɛ wɔ ase ha,
Na onyim hɛn mberɛwyɛ nyina.

MHB 928
4 . Nyimpa yɛ edwuma du ewimbir a,
Ahomgye a yehia san ba;
Dom hɛn ma yɛngye W'adom no,
Yennya nhyira wɔ dza yɛyɛ m';
Na bea biara a yɛwɔ no,
Yɛnsɔ W'enyi wɔ enyigye m'.  Amen.

MHB 929
1 . ME kra, bra, soɛr fi wo nda mu;
Adzekyee no
Dze da fofor so reba;
Bra Nyia ɔyɛɛ adze fɛɛfɛw n' nkyɛn,
Hwɛ, fa W'ahom
Kakraba n' nyina tua kaw.

MHB 929
2 . Fa dɛw hyia ewia a ɔreba n';
Ma w' ahoɔdzen
Nduhuam nyɛ krado ntu hua;
'Nafua sum no etwa mu kɔ,
Edaa hatsee n',
Nyankopɔn hwɛɛ wo do sɔnn.

MHB 929
3 . Sɔr ma ɔmma dzi mu daa wɔ
Akwan nyina mu;
Ɔmma wo mbɔdzen ndzi mu;
Mbom sɛ epɛ aka bɔn do a,
Ɔnsɛɛ w'akwan,
Nsakyer wo mfa w' nyɛ Nedze.

MHB 929
4 . Hu dɛ ɔhwɛ w'akwan mu daa,
Ɔda mfom a
Ɔhyɛ hɛn mu biara edzi;
'Nyimguasedze a wɔakata do n'
Oyi to gua,
Na ɔhwehwɛ bɔn biara mu.

MHB 929
5 . Wo nkwa mber da a odzi ekyir n',
'Werɛhow apa n',
Ntwa mu wɔ nda dɛɛdɛw mu;
Na efi owu nyinsu sum mu n',
Aasoɛr dɛw mu
Eekehyia Ewia hyɛnhyɛɛn no.

MHB 929
6 . Mma nnsɛɛ hɛn Nyame akyɛdze,
Na mma mmpow kan,
Mbom tsie No Sunsum Ne ndze;
Enye N' bɛtsena, na ibohu
Mbrɛ kan reda
Ndzɛmba nyina edzi petee.

MHB 93
1 . HOM mma yɛmfa ayɛyi, 'nyidzi, 
Mma hɛn nkwagye dzin pa no,
Dza mfesantsen a etwa m' no 
Wɔdze siee Nyame mu no,
Naaso yɛdzi enyigye krɔnkrɔn
Yɛatsea mu yɛatow ndwom ndɛ.

MHB 93
2 . Jesus nye dzin a ɔsom hɛn bo,
Dzin a yenntum nnkyerɛ ase; 
Enyigye dzin, enyika dzin,
Aso na akoma dzi dɛw;
Dzin dɛɛdɛw a ɔbor nsusui,
Ɔgye hɛn fi bɔn na hɛll.

MHB 93
3 . Ɔyɛ dzin a wɔdze tonton,
Wɔdze tow konyimdzi ndwom,
Dzin a wɔdze bɔ mpaa krɔnkrɔn 
Wɔ awerɛhow bɔnsa yi m',
Dzin a sorfo dze enyidzi
Kotow som enyigye mu.

MHB 93
4 . Ɔyɛ Dzin a sɛ wɔbɔ a,
Ɔyɛ dɛw ndwom wɔ asomu;
Nyia ɔdze Dzin yi kotow serɛ 
Nya awerɛkyekye dɛɛdɛw;
Nyia odu ne nyansaa mapa ho n'
Nya sor enyigye n' wɔ ha.

MHB 93
5 . Jesus nye Dzin a wɔakrɔn no 
Wɔ edzin nyinara mu;
Sɛ obi ka hɛn a, Dzin yi mu
Yegu tamfo n'enyim ase;
Ɔhyɛ hɔn a wonntum nnantsew,
Efurafo, na mpakye dzen.

MHB 93
6 . Dɛm ntsi yɛdze ɔdɔ tonton
Dzin a wodzi no nyi yi;
Jesus krɔnkrɔn, yɛserɛ Wo,
Kyerɛw W' dzin wɔ hɛn mu wɔ ha,
Ama yefi ha fow sor a,
Yɛnye abɔfo aatow ndwom.	  Amen.

MHB 930
1 . O NKWA Wura, Wo nkenyan ndze n'
Ma motow anapa ndwom;
Medze enyigye nsɛm bedzi dɛw
Dɛ meyɛ Wodze daa.

MHB 930
2 . Muhu Wo kan, metse W' mframa,
Wiadze yi yɛ W'asɛm;
Dza onyan m'akoma na m'adwen nye
W'enyim nhunii, Ewuradze.

MHB 930
3 . Dɛm ntsi mefa dza ɔkrɔn no' na,
Medan m'enyi kyerɛ Wo,
Dɛm ntsi mikenyan m'akoma
Dze som ahokeka mu.

MHB 930
4 . Ewuradze, ma mentsena nkwa m' na
Monkɔ do nsoɛr mfi owu m';
Mo Wura, ma m' sunsum enyi ngye,
Ma m' daa daa edziban.

MHB 930
5 . Ewuradze, kasa m'akoma m'
Ma onya ahokeka;
Kesi dɛ sum na ɔpon bɛba,
Ma mada wɔ Wo mu.

MHB 931
1 . Me kra, yɛ ntsɛm nye ewia nnyan 
N-si mu ntu wo daadaa kwan;
Sun akwadwer to nkyɛn na soɛr
Fa dɛw bɔ w' anapa afɔr.

MHB 931
2 . Mber a asɛɛ n' kwa hyɛ ananm'; 
Bɔ bra dɛ ndɛ owu nam kwanm';
Kɔ kan kora akyɛdze a Nyame ama n';
Siesie woho ma atsɛmbu da n'.

MHB 931
3 . Fa nokwar ka w' asɛm biara; 
Mma wo tsibowa mmbu w' atsɛn da;
Nyame enyi hu mbea nyina do
Hyɛ nsumaam' adwen nye nyɛe nsew;

MHB 931
4 . Me kra, nyan na ma woho do, 
Fa woho bɔ abɔfo ho,
Na hɔndze, anago nyina
Wɔtow ndwom ma Ɔsor Hen daa.

MHB 931
5 .	Ayɛyi nka W', Ɔwo a esie m' 
Na ama m' ahomgye a ɔwɔ ndam':
Sɛ mifi wum' so minyan a
Ma mo so me nsa nka daa nkwa.

MHB 931
6 . Mobɔ W' anohoba fofor: 
Ma mo bɔn ntwamm' dɛ bɔsu nkɔ,
Woara weɔn m' adwen nsunyiwa,
Fa Wo Sunsum hyɛ me kra ma.

MHB 931
7 . M' adwen, me nsɛm, nye me ndeyɛɛ- 
Woara dzi ne nyina do ndɛ,
Na dza mowɔ na dza mutum
Nyina aabɔm' wɔ Wo nkamfom'.

MHB 931
8 . Ayɛyi nka Nyame dɔyɛfo; 
Asaasemba, hom nkamfo No;
Sor abɔfo hom so ntonton N',
Egya, Ɔba, Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn!    Amen.

MHB 932
1 . O NYAME, enyimnyam hyɛnn n' ne fɛw,
Ɔwo a edze kan fi kan m' ba;
O kan mu Kan, kan nsunyiwa,
O Da a ɔma nda nyina kan.

MHB 932
2 . 'Wo nokwar Ewia, ma W'ahentum
Hyerɛn nwanwa n' ngyegye hɛn do;
Sunsum N'ahosan nserɛmɛn no
Nhyerɛn hɛn nyimpasu no do.

MHB 932
3 . Yɛdze hɛn ntotɔserɛ so ba
Daapem enyimnyam Egya N'enyim,
Adom na tum nyina Egya n',
Dɛ ɔmpam hɛn mfi bɔn ho enyigye m'.

MHB 932
4 . Ongya hɛn wɔ papayɛ mu,
Ma yɛmfa ɔdɔ nka enyiber nhyɛ,
Ɔmma sasabɔn ndan nyɛ siar,
Na yennya adom ngye hɛn mfom nto m'.

MHB 932
5 . Hɛn adwen-nhyɛ Noara Ne nsamu,
Hɛn honam ho ntsew ndzi N' nokwar;
Na gyedzi gya n' na ɔndzɛw hɔ 
Na ɔnhyew Satan no Nworahaban n'.

MHB 932
6 . Na Christ bɛyɛ hɛn edziban,
Hɛn nsu fi No hɔ bɛpem kwa,
Sunsum m' wenyin a ɔhyɛ ma n',
Onnsi atwetwe, na ɔma kra n' do.

MHB 932
7 . Ma yɛmfa dɛw nhyɛ da yi ase,
Hɛn nwansann nsɛ anapahema,
Hɛn gyedzi ndzɛw dɛ wigyinae,
Na nkrumsi bi mmba witɔree.

MHB 932
8 . Anapa-wi epue kɔɔ dɛ nhyiren;
Ma hɛn Anapa-wi mapa n' mbra;
Asɛm no a ɔnye Egya n' yɛ kor n',
Egya n' dzi mu wɔ Ba no mu.

MHB 933
1 . O CHRIST, yɛdze W'akyɛdze
Da fofor yi hyɛ Wo nsa;
Dza ɔdze nam no yennyim
Ntsi yehia Wo mboa mbordo;
Agyenkwa, fa W' mbeamudua n'
Hwɛ do, mma ɔannyɛ ɔsɛɛ ber.

MHB 933
2 . Sɛ ɔyɔ bɔkɔɔ fɛɛfɛw a,
Woara yɛ hɛn dɛw farbaa;
Sɛ ɔdze haw bi nam so a
Dza ihyira do n' nyina yɛ yie;
Dza yɛserɛ nye dɛ ofi
N'ahyɛse n' mma yɛnnyɛ bɔn.

MHB 933
3 . Yenyim hɛn me m' bi,
Na yenyim hɛn tamfo n' so, 
Ɔdɔɔ so mpo ma hɛn dɛ
W'enyi tua hɛn mbusu nyina;
Yɛreserɛ Wo yi, mma nnkam hɛn
Wo tsema na dza yehia.

MHB 933
4 . Ao, nkyɛ yeefua W'asɛm mu,
Yaatsena W'adom no mu daa!
Yeetu hɛnho ahyɛ Wo nsamu
Dze hɛn pɛ nyina ahyɛ W' pɛ ase;
Aadwen, aakasa, aayɛ dza
Ɔbɔsɔ W'enyi ara nko.

MHB 933
5 . Ewuradze, tsie hɛn ntsɛm;
Tsie na ma hɛn akyɛdze
Kɛse a Wo dɔ dze ma n',
Nokwar akoma a ɔhwɛ W' nko,
Ma ndɛ na hɛn nkwa nda nyina
Yeeyi W' Christ hɛn Nyame ayɛw.

MHB 934
1 . AYƐYI nka Nyia ɔtse dɛw mu,
Nyia ɔbɔɔ kan na sum no;
N'ahengua yɛ sum wɔ maa a
Wɔammbɔ no bun no mu.

MHB 934
2 . N'enyi hwira m' paapaa adwen
Na nyɛe biara m' kofee;
Sum kebii mu dze mpo da edzi
N'enyim dɛ ewia ketee.

MHB 934
3 . Ahemfo Hen, nyia Ɔwo gya no n',
Mbusu biara nnhaw no;
Wo ntsaban no nwin no ase
Na wɔbɔhom hɔ sɔnn.

MHB 934
4 . W'abɔfoe botwe hɔn mpa ho
Ehyia anweɔn hɔn ndaa m',
Wo gyedzi na nokwar bɔweɔn
Hɔn, 'siandɛ Ɔwo nnda.

MHB 934
5 . Na sɛ ahomgye na adwen papa
Ma yenya foforyɛ a,
Yɛnye adzekyee no tsew hɛn enyi
Na yehyira Siarfo n'.   Amen.

MHB 935
1 . ƆSOR Egya , maba Wo hɔ,
Mohwe W'enyim dɛ daduanyi,
Ama Wo dɔ no aagye me
Wɔ da yi mu adzesoa ase.

MHB 935
2 . Memmba dɛ muruguan m'asodzii,
Memmba dɛ muruguan aperdzi n';
Merebɛgye ahom fofor dze asɔw,
Rohwehwɛ tum fofor abɔ bra.

MHB 935
3 . Pii na wɔhwehwɛ W'enyim pa n'
Dze ekehyiahyia hɔn wu da,
Mbom mihia W'adom wiadze 'i mu,
N-kwasɛm mu yɛ dur kyɛn owu.

MHB 935
4 . Sɛ anapa kan gyegye wimu,
Ne kan yi mo ho fi edzi
Ma mennsɛ bi a, ana nnse dɛ:
Morohoa w' sen sukwankyɛba?

MHB 935
5 . Sɛ ewia ketee hyɛ modo,
Ma nkukubɔ yɛ dzen dodow
Ma nkyɛ meremem a ennka dɛ;
Wo mu na m'ahoɔdzen dzi mu.

MHB 935
6 . Sɛ sum dze wiadze kɔ ndaa mu a,
Kommyɛ a ɔba n' mu yɛ dur ma,
Nkyɛ ɔbɛhaw naaso ese
Kan bɛba 'wimbirbaa mu no.

MHB 935
7 . O ma kan ne ngyegyee hyɛnn no
Ntow nhyɛ m'akwan nyina do daa,
Kesi dɛ gyedzi nnkotua enyi
Na hɛn nda bɛyɛ heaven nda.

MHB 936
1 . ENYIGYE, Kan Nyame
Egya n' N'enyim adom,
Ewuna onnyiewiei ahoɔfɛw;
Ɔsornyi, krɔnn, siarfo,
Hɛn Gyefo Jesus Christ,
Yɛdze dɛw hwɛ Wo mpuei kwan.

MHB 936
2 . Ansaana wimu bomua
Yehu ewimbir kan n',
Yehyia tow hɛn ndowm dɛɛdɛw;
Dze kamfo tum Egya,
Ɔwo Ne Ba a ɔwoo n' n',
Na Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn no so.

MHB 936
3 . Wo nko na ayɛyi ndwom
Krɔnkrɔn nyina yɛ Wodze,
O Nyame Ba, nkwa Mafo,
Dɛm ntsi Ɔwo sorsornyi,
Wiadze hyɛ Wo enyimnyam,
Wobohuhuor Wo daa daa.

MHB 937
1 . WONHUA N'enyimnyam kan a ɔma akomatɔm'!
Ɔno a ɔyɛ bɛkyebo Egya siarfo,
Krɔnkrɔn mu, Krɔnkrɔn Jesus Christ hɛn Wura
Afei yɛaba 'wimbir ahomgye ber mu.

MHB 937
2 . Ewimbir nkandzea hyerɛn hɛn do,
Yɛtow Egya na Ɔba nye Sunsum 
Krɔnkrɔn n' ndwom,
Efata dɛ daa yɛdze gyirama krɔnn
Tow ndwom kamfo Wo',
Ɔwo hɛn Nyankopɔn Ba nkwa Mafo;
Dɛm ntsi W'enyimnyam ahyɛ wiadze nyina ma.

MHB 938
1 . EGYA a etse sorsor wɔ wimu
Ma hɛn ewimbir ndwom a yɛrotow yi
Nyi W' mbɔbɔrhu kɛse n' nkyerɛ:
Wo dɔ n'anyɛn hɛn ndɛ da yi,
Wo nhwɛdo dze sor ayamuyie pii
Edzi hɛn enyim hɛn bra m'.

MHB 938
2 . Gyefo, fa ndɛ bɔn nyina kyɛ,
Adwembɔn, nyɛe basabasa,
Enyiber, ntsɛn na ahantan;
O Ɔwo Calvary Eguambaa,
Yi hɛn fi wiadze na honam m',
Gye hɛn nkwa a sesei na daa.

MHB 938
3 . Yɛ hɛn akokyɛm na hɛn akontar,
Tsia abɔnsam ndaadaa ɔnye
Esunsum bɔn nyina hɔn tum;
Wo tum nwowaw hɛn anafua yi
Na ma sor asomdwee nka hɛn
Na abɔfo so nsian hɛn do.

MHB 938
4 . Anafua bɔw rososɔ yi,
Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, ma Wo kommyɛ n'
Nhyɛ akoma biara mu,
Ma yemmua hɛn enyi bɔkɔɔ,
Na ma hɛn akra nhom Wo nko mu,
Ɔwo Ɔkorsa daa siarfo.  Amen.

MHB 939
1 . EWIA rokɔtɔ ntsɛm,
Adze resa;
Ma dɔ nda no ho edzi
Mbɔ n'ewimbir afɔr.

MHB 939
2 . Christ sɛɛn mbeamudua no do n',
Ɔbɔɔ N' tsir adze,
Na ɔdze Ne kra hyɛɛ
N'Egya Ne nsamu yie.

MHB 939
3 . Dɛm ara na m' kra so
Dze noho nyina
Hyɛ Krɔnkrɔnnyi Ne nsa,
Nyia esunsum nyina tse n' mu.

MHB 939
4 . Afei Egya N'enyim
Na m'bɔhom komm,
Monnkɔdwen hweeara ho,
Ber a meda No bomu n'.

MHB 939
5 . Ne pɛ na ɔnyɛ hɔ,
Mbrɛ obesi bia 'a;
Oewu ama Noho,
Ndzɛmba nyina bɛn No.

MHB 939
6 . Dɛm na m'bɛtsena ase
Na nnyɛ emi a,
No tum no dɔ nyina
Tse ase mo mu ndɛ.

MHB 939
7 . Ɔkorsa Krɔnkrɔn kor,
Ewuradze kor,
Mebɛyɛ Wodze daa,
Wo so yɛ medze daa.   Amen.

MHB 94
1 . Eguambaa bi, nkwagye dzin bi, 
Enyidar bi nnyi sor anaa ase,
Fɔdzi nye fɛr ho guansumabew bi nnyi,
Dɛ Wo nkotoo.

MHB 94
2 . Me gyedzi suar, m' enyidar suar, 
M' akoma ne hia nye no mbusu nko
Na ɔbɔ mu dɛ senaman wɔ mo mu
Kekam' frɛ Wo.

MHB 94
3 . Kaansa muwu a, Ɔwo yɛ nkwa; 
Meyɛ nwim mpo a, mo Wura, dɔ ne gya nye W'
Minnyi etsidaa, minnyi fie biara so
Gyedɛ Woara.

MHB 940
1 . Anapawi hyɛnhyɛnn n' etwam' 
Ɔahwer ne hyɛnhyɛnn nyina ntsɛm
Adzesaa no sunsuma retsen
Prɛko so bio.

MHB 940
2 . Hɛn nkwa tse dɛ ɔpɛber da 
N' enyimnyam wi n' twam' ntsɛmara
Gya hɛn, O Christ, 'Wo a eyɛ nkwa,
Kodu fie sɔnn.

MHB 940
3 . Fa W' adom a ɔhyɛ kra nkuran n' 
Twe hɛn 'koma kɔ sor man ho;
Boa hɛn ma yɛmfa hɛn enyi
Ntsim sor man n' do.

MHB 940
4 . Mbrɛ kan na dɛw na asomdwee 
Bɔ mu yɛ kor dzi hen wɔ hɔ n',
Nna sor abɔfo nngyaa hɔn ndwom
Tow ara da n'.

MHB 940
5 . Mbrɛ ahotsewfo hyɛ ntar fitaa n' 
Na ewimbir sunsuma ngye hɔ da n'
Mbrɛ 'Wo ɔdomankoma Kan mu kan
Yɛ abɔso Hen.

MHB 941
1 . OWURA Jesus, tsetsebaado
Beenu nye W' nantseew 'wimbir bi,
Dɔ nwanwa mapa hyɛɛ hɔn ndam
Ma wɔserɛɛ W' dɛ nye hɔn ntsena.
Adze resa yi hɛn so serɛ W'
Dɛ mma nngyaa hɛn witɔree yi.

MHB 941
2 . Ana hɔn akoma ammfram?
Na kaansa woennhu hɔn Wura mpo a,
Hɔn esunsum ho ammper hɔn?
Woenntum amma Hɔho n' annkɔ.
Hɛn a yenyim Wo sɔr mbordo
Dɛ mma nngyaa hɛn da n'ewiei yi.

MHB 941
3 . Bi a hɛn so mber pii no yennhu
Nyia ɔnye hɛn anantsew kwan do;
Ɔbra ne begyabegyayɛ m'
Yɛanntse dza ewɔ ka kyerɛ hɛn
Anafua kɔnkɔnnkɔn no mu,
Dɔfo Ewuradze, yɛbɛtse W' ndze.

MHB 941
4 . Wi asen, adzesaa abɛn;
Agyenkwa, 'nye hɛn ntsena anafua 'i;
'Nye hɛn nkasa, fa W' nsa ka hɛn,
Gya hɛn kɔ asomdwee na kan mu;
W'enyim a wusoɛr adom wɔ mu n'
Mfa ne hyerɛn no mpam hɛn sum.

MHB 941
5 . Owura siarfo, nnyɛ anafua 'i nko,
Yɛnye Wo bɛnantsew daa daa,
Abɔ namɔn akɔ Emmaus
Eketsie Wo dɔ na tum ndze n',
Na anafua biara yɛatsena
Wo nkyɛn ahwɛ W', enya ahomka.

MHB 942
1 . Gyefo dɔfo, me kra n' ewia, 
Ɔwo 'bɛn a, adze nnsa da;
O mma mununkum biara mmfi fam'
Nn-suma W' mmfi W' akowaa enyiwam'!

MHB 942
2 . Ber a enyikom aka me 
Dɛ bɔsu a ogu asaase do,
N-da refa m' a, m' adwen nyɛ
Dɛ Christ bom' nda n' ɔbɛyɛ dɛw!

MHB 942
3 . Bra begya m' kwan fi ahema, 
Na innyi hɔ a, munntum mmbɔ bra;
Adze sa so a nye me bɛtsena:
Musuro owu sɛ innyi hɔ a.

MHB 942
4 . Wo ba bi a ɔafom kwan wɔ hɔ a 
N-dɛ so oetsia W' asɛm do a,
Adom dwuma n' nhyɛ ase ber yim';
Mma ɔnnda ho ara nnda bɔn mu.

MHB 942
5 . Hwɛ ayarfo do; ma ehiafo 
Nhyira a ofi W' adom mbordo;
Hɔn a awerɛhow atɔ hɔn do,
Wɔnda dɛ mbɔtoaba berɛww.

MHB 942
6 . Yenyan a, bra na behyira hɛn 
Ansaana yeesim' etu kwan,
Ekodu dɛ hɛn nkwa yi ayew
Wɔ sorsor Wo dɔ no bun mu.

MHB 943
1 . 'NYIMNYAM nka Wo, me Nyankopɔn,
Wɔ da yi mu nhyira no ntsi;
Ahemfo Hen, fa m' sie anafua 'i
Wo ntsaban kɛse no ase.

MHB 943
2 . Ewuradze, Wo dɔ Ba no ntsi
Fa da yi mu mo mfom kyɛ me,
Ama meenya asomdwee kɛse 
Ber a morokɔ ndaa mu yi.

MHB 943
3 . Kyerɛ me ma mombɔ bra dɛ
Munnsuro owu kwan biara do;
Kyerɛ me owu pa n'akwan,
Ma ewiei no meenyan dɛw mu.

MHB 943
4 . O ma me kra nhom wɔ Wo mu,
Na ma nda pa ndeda me yie,
Ma onsiesie mo honandua
Ma maasom me Nyankopɔn yie.

MHB 943
5 . Sɛ anafua yi menntum annda a,
Fa adwen pa fi sor dwir me kra;
Mma mma adaaso bɔn bi nnhaw me,
Na sum mu etumfo bi nntsiw me.

MHB 943
6 . O ma menyɛ krado daa daa,
Dɛ me kandzea so dze me nsamu;
Muhu sor a, ma m'enyi ngye,
Ber a m'bɛtse Kumfor n' Ne ndze n'.

MHB 943
7 . Ayɛyi nka Wo, kan Wura,
Ɔwo a ayɛ kan Wo tsenabea;
Ngyegyee hyɛnhyɛn pem fi Wo nkyɛn,
Enyimnyam nyina Nyame Tsir no.

MHB 943
8 . Wonyi Nyame domfo n' ayɛw,
Asaase mba, hom nyi N' ayɛw,
Ɔsor mba hom so nyi Egya,
'Ba na Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn n' ayɛw.

MHB 944
1 . Adze resa ampa 
Ewimbir aba,
Na enyimkan rudum,
Ma wim' reyɛ sum.

MHB 944
2 . Isum rehyɛ ampa, 
Nworaba rupuepue,
Nnoma, mbowa nye nhyiren
Bɛdeda sesei.

MHB 944
3 . Jesus, fa Wo nsa to 
Hɔn a wɔaberɛ do;
Na fa Wo nhyira pa
Dom hɔn ma wɔnda.

MHB 944
4 . Dom mbofra nkakraba 
Ma wonhu Wo daa;
Hɔn a wɔwɔ po do,
Woara hwɛ hɔn do.

MHB 944
5 . Hɔn so a wonntum nnda, 
Hyɛ hɔn dzen daa daa;
Hɔn a wɔdwendwen bɔn,
Dan hɔn na twe hɔn.

MHB 944
6 . W' abɔfo mpa m' mbusu 
Anago yi mu,
Wɔmfa hɔn atsaban
M-bɔ mo ho ban.

MHB 944
7 . Ao, fa mo bɔn kyɛ me, 
Na ma adze nkye me
Dɛ m' akoma mu tsen
Na mo ho yɛ dzen.

MHB 944
8 . Enyimnyam nka Egya, 
Enyimnyam nka Ba,
Nye 'Wo, Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn,
Daa, hɛn Nyankopɔn.   Amen.

MHB 945
1 . ANAFUA a yɛdze da hom n' aba bio,
Nyankopɔn mma ndzɛmba nyina nyɛ yie:
Yɛnda Ne nhyira a suro nnyi m' no ase,
' Siandɛ ɔbɛn hɛn.

MHB 945
2 . Pam adwembɔn na sunsum bɔn kɔ ekyir;
Hɛn Wura, weɔn hɛn kesi adzekyee,
Bɔ honam na kra ho ban tsia mbusu,
Soma W'abɔfoe n'.

MHB 945
3 . Tsew hɛn mpaabɔ na hɛn adwendwen ho,
Ma yennyan dɛw mu dɛ yɛwɔ Wo nkyɛn,
Yɛnsom Wo ndzɛmba nyina mu na adwen m'
Yenyi W' ayɛw.

MHB 945
4 . Ma ayarfo Woara Wo nda pa no,
Dom adaduafo, fua nyinsukyifo;
Hwɛ ekunafo na ngyanka hɔn hia,
Ka tamfo n' gu.

MHB 945
5 . 'Siandɛ yennyi boafo koraa
Ka Wo sor Nyankopɔn hɛn Hwɛfo n' ho;
Ɔwo nnkɛpa W'adɔfo dabiara,
Kan o, sum o.

MHB 945
6 . Han Egya, ayɛyi nka W', W'ahendzi mbra,
Wɔnyɛ Wo pɛ Wɔ ha dɛ sor ara;
Kora hɛn do, fa hɛn bɔn kyɛ hɛn, gye hɛn,
Sesei na daa.   Amen.

MHB 946
1 . AFEI ndua nyina ada
Na sum na fooyɛ repram
Nkurow na mbowa do;
Na 'wo, m'akoma dze, nyan
Na bɔ mpaa yie aber yi,
Yi w' Bɔfo ayɛw ansaana ada.

MHB 946
2 . Ewia kan a aka n' rokɔ,
Na nworaba rupuepue
Wɔ wimu na ekyirkyir;
Na sɛ wɔfrɛ w' kɔ sor a,
Nyame mma w' enyimnyam ma
Innsi nkrum bio wɔ wiadze ha.

MHB 946
3 . Adwendwen na berɛ bɔ adze,
'Siandɛ adzesaa gya abrɛfo
Na ɔma hɔn ahomgye :
M'akoma, ber bi reba a
Ibefi awerɛhow na
Bɔn ho nkowaasom nyina mu.

MHB 946
4 . Me Jesus, tsena me nkyɛn,
Na mma 'tamfo bi mmbɛn me,
Wo ntsaban ase m' wɔ nkwa;
Sɛ 'tamfo no bɔ m' mpuw a,
Mma ɔnnhaw m' kwan biara do,
Ma W'abɔfoe ntow ndwom ntwa m' ho.

MHB 946
5 . M'adɔfo, hom ho ndwe hom,
Hɛn Nyankopɔn bɛgye hom
Efi mbusu nyina m',
Na ɔama hom ahomgye,
Na N'abɔfoe aweɔn hom,
Na wɔabɔ hom ho ban daa daa.

MHB 947
1 . Ansaana m' bɛda n', yie biara 
Me Nyame
Ayɛ m' ndɛ,
M' bɛda m' Agyenkwa ase.

MHB 947
2 . Mo Wura, memfa ndaase bɛn mma 
Wo dzin a
Ɔnnsesa n'
Mbɔbɔrhufo, dɔfo?

MHB 947
3 . M' ekyinkyin nyinam' 'Wo na 'gya m' 
Wɔ Wo kwanm',
Tsiee m' asɔr,
Saan me nyɛe nyina ho.

MHB 947
4 . Mma nndan me nngya na dɔ me daa; 
W' Asomdwee
Nyɛ me nhyira,
Nkodu dɛ 'beyi me ha.

MHB 947
5 . Mo botan, mo weɔmfo, m' aban, 
Kora m' sɔnn,
Ber a mada,
Fa Wo tum nyinara.

MHB 947
6 . Meka m' enyi gu do wum' a, 
Ma monsoɛr
Dɛ meka
Enyansafo no ho.

MHB 948
1 . Enye me ntsena! onwim ano rotɔ; 
Sum regye, Ewuradze, nye me ntsena!
Aboafo pa, na akyekyewerɛfo sa a,
Onnyibi-ne-bi-a-ɔba, enye m' ntsena!

MHB 948
2 . N-kwa da ketseaba yi rotwe kɔ; 
Wiadze dɛw repa; n' enyimnyam resen;
N-sakyer na ɔsɛɛ nko ara na muhu;
Ao, 'Wo a ennsakyer da, enye me ntsena.

MHB 948
3 . Mihia Wo me nkyɛn aber nyinara, 
W' adom n-ko na ɔka siamfo hyɛ;
Gyafo nye Taafo wɔ hen ka Wo ho?
Isum o, ekan o, enye me ntsena.

MHB 948
4 . Sɛ menye Wo nam a, munnsuro hwee; 
Ɔyaw nnyɛ durdur, na nyinsu nnyɛ wen:
Owu, wo bɔr na wo konyim wɔ hen?
Mo konyim wɔ do daa, sɛ 'Wo nye m' tse a.

MHB 948
5 . Murumua m' enyi a, yi Wo mbeamudua n' kyerɛ m'; 
Hyerɛn wɔ sum mu, kyerɛ m' ɔsor do kwan;
Ɔsor rehyerɛn, wiadze kusuww repa;
N-kwam' o, owum' o, enye me ntsena!

MHB 949
1 . EWURADZE, hwɛ, mber tsiabaa bi 
Yefi daa ɔberɛ mu,
Behyia wɔ Wo krɔnkrɔn-bea ha,
Bɔhom kakra, Wo nkyɛn.

MHB 949
2 . Edwuma, ɔberɛ na atseetsee
Twa hɛn ho hyia daa daa,
Na ɔyɛ dzen ma hɛn dodow;
Yennya mber mpo mmbɔ mpaa.

MHB 949
3 . Naaso nnyɛ ha nko nye bea a
Wɔdze hwehwɛ Wo wɔ;
Wo nhyira gu famu famu dwuma a
Wodzi n' nokwar m' so do.

MHB 949
4 . Dwumadze ahorow nyina,
Nsaase pa m' 'gyapadze,
'Bɔdze ho nyimdzee na edwindze
Da Wo nhwɛdo edzi.

MHB 949
5 . Dɛm a yɛnda hɛn sor awoo
Edzi dza yɛyɛ nyina m',
Na yɛmper wiadze ahendzi mma W'
Na nnyɛ W'atamfo no a.

MHB 949
6 . Dwuma a wodzi no Wo pɛ do n'
Bɛyɛ dɛ mpaabɔ daa,
Na mpaabɔ a Woara akyerɛ n'
Nye edwuma yɛ adze kor.

MHB 95
1 . JESUS, eyɛ Ewia na Kyɛm, 
Kyɛm na Ewia afebɔɔ, 
Innkegyaa dɛ ehyerɛn da, 
Innkegyaa hɛn nweɔn da. 
Sɛ yɛrokɔ a pia hɛn, 
Gye hɛn fi atamfo nsamu.

MHB 95
2 . Jesus, 'yɛ Paanoo na Nsa, 
Paanoo na Nsa afebɔɔ,
Innkegyaa dɛ 'nyɛn hɛn daa,
Na ehyɛ hɛn dzen daa.
Kɔ do ma hɛn sor paanoo, 
Yɛnkɔ do nnom sor n-sa.

MHB 95
3 . Jesus eyɛ Dɔ na Nkwa, 
Nkwa na ɔdɔ afebɔɔ.
Innkegyaa dɛ ikenyan hɛn,
Innkegyaa dɛ edɔ hɛn.
N-kwa na ɔdɔ a yehia nyina
Wɔ Wo mu, wɔ Wo mu ampa.

MHB 95
4 . Jesus yɛ Asomdwee na Dɛw,
Dɛw na Asomdwee afebɔɔ.
Dɛw a ɔmmpa, ɔnnsesa,
Asomdwee a onngyaa hɛn.
Yɛwɔ W' mu dɛw na asomdwee, 
Seseiara na afebɔɔ.

MHB 95
5 . Jesus yɛ Ndwom na Ahoɔdzen,
Ndwom na Ahoɔdzen afebɔɔ.
Ahoɔdzen a ɔnnsa da,
Ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze da,
Ma ahoɔdzen na ndwom yi
N-hyɛ hɛn dzen daa nyina.

MHB 950
1 . Nhyira nka akomamutsewfo, 
Wobohu hɛn Nyame;
Nyame esumadze yɛ hɔndze
Hɛn kra yɛ Christ ne fi.

MHB 950
2 . Ewuradze a ofii sor 
Brɛɛ hɛn nkwa na asomdwee,
Nye nyimpa bɛtsenaa botooyɛm',
Yɛɛ Fasusu na Hen-

MHB 950
3 . Ɔda ho dze Noho 
Ma ɔkra brɛfo no;
Na ɔdze N' ahengua no ma
Akoma a no mu tsew.

MHB 950
4 . Ewuradze, yɛrohwehwɛ W' 
Ma nhyira yi nyɛ hɛndze.
Ma hɛn akoma a ɔbotow,
Asɔrfi a ɔsɛ Wo.

MHB 951
1 . NDƐ da yi enya etwa m' kɔ;
Hɛn Wura, yɛda W' ase;
Yɛsɔr dɛ mma yɛnnyɛ bɔn
Biara dɛm sumber yi.
O Jesu, ma yengyina W'enyim,
Na adzesaa yi mu kora hɛn.

MHB 951
2 . Da n' ne dɛw etwa mu kɔ :
Hɛn akoma ba Wo hɔ;
Yɛserɛ W' dɛ mma ɔhaw bi mmba
Dɛm sum ndɔnhwer yi mu.
O Jesu, ma hɔn sum nyɛ kan,
Na adzesaa yi mu kora hɛn.

MHB 951
3 . Da yi mu fona etwa m',
Yɛtow hɛn ndwom ma Wo,
Yɛserɛ W' dɛ mma mbusu bi
Nnsi sum ndɔhwer yi mu;
O Jesu, ma yengyina W'enyim,
Na adzesaa yi mu kora hɛn.

MHB 951
4 . Yɛ hɛn akra korafo,
'Siandɛ Ɔwo na inyim
Mbusu pii a ɔrotweɔn hɛn
Wɔ mfikyir abrɔn mu.
O Jesu dɔyɛfo, tsie hɛn.
Na gye hɛn fi ne nyina mu.  Amen.

MHB 952
1 . NYANKOPƆN Egya, bɛn hɛn,
Gye hɛn ɔhaw m' 'nafua yi;
Yɛ hɛn nyina Wo dɔ mba,
Sum no mu yɛ kan ma hɛn.

MHB 952
2 . Agyenkwa, yɛ hɛn asomdwee,
Yi hɛn bɔn anafua yi;
Ka fahodzi asɛm no
Dan hɛn sum ma ɔnyɛ kan.

MHB 952
3 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, pen na bra
Bɛtsew hɛn ho anafua yi;
Bɛyɛ hɛn akoma Wo fie;
Dan hɛn sum ma ɔnyɛ kan.

MHB 952
4 . Ɔkorsa Krɔnkrɔn, bɛn hɛn;
Dɔ nwanwa a yɛkamfo Wo,
Abrabɔ m' na 'wu m' boafo,
Ewuradze, tsew hɛn sum do!.  Amen.

MHB 953
1 . EWURADZE, Ɔwo a ipue ma dwumadzi m'
Ɔhyew na adzesoa brɛ adze koraa,
Enye mo so ntsena anafua kɔnn yi mu,
Sɛ ewia rokɔtɔ a, nye me ntsena.

MHB 953
2 . Ewimbir dzinn a nhyira ahyɛ n' ma,
Dze ahomgye dɛɛdɛw bi gu mo do;
M'edwuma bɔ adze na eka mo ho a,
M'etsidaa benya edzi mu wɔ Wo mu.

MHB 953
3 . Afei, Ewuradze, bra bɛyɛ m' Hɔhoe,
Dafua mu fona na dede ekyir no;
O ma minnya asomdwee, dɛw nye ahomgye,
Brɛ m' nkwagye, na fa mo bɔn nyina kyɛ me.

MHB 953
4 . Kyekyer epirakur, na dwedwe yaw a
Aka mo bom' wɔ da a etwa m' yi ho n',
Na menda Egya N'bomu dɛ me yaw,
Nyina mo werɛ mfir wɔ nda pa m'.   Amen.

MHB 954
1 . AFE fofor reba bio,
Hɛn Wura pa, ma ɛnyɛ
Afe kor so a wɔdze
Yɛ edwuma, dze tweɔn Wo.

MHB 954
2 . Afe fofor a mbɔbɔrhu,
Gyedzi na adom wɔ mu,
Afe fofor a W'enyim hyerɛn,
Ma dɛw ahyɛ no ma.

MHB 954
3 . M-pontu afe fofor a
Ayɛyi ahyɛ ma, 
Afe a ɔma wohu
Wo daa daa nyina no.

MHB 954
4 . Afe fofor a wodze som,
Dze dzi W' dɔ ho dase;
Afe fofor a wɔdze sua
Sor edwuma krɔnn yɛ.

MHB 954
5 . Afe fofor reba bio,
Hɛn Wura pa, ma ɔnyɛ
Afe fofor mma Wo sor
Na asaase nyina so.   Amen.

MHB 955
1 . YEGYINA afe fofor
Abobow ano,
Yehyia awerɛkyekyer nsɛm a
Otu suro nyina,
Hɛn Egya Ne ndze no
Na ɔka no wɔ
Gyedzi ahoɔdzen mu
Dze ma hɛn enyigye.
    Hom nkɔ kan, mma hom nnsuro
    Adzekyee mba nyina :
    N'asɛm runntwa mu da,
    Orunntwa mu da.

MHB 955
2 . 'Mi Ewuradze nye w' wɔ hɔ,
Mma nnsuro ara da;
Mobɔboa w' ahyɛ w' dzen,
Mma w'abaw nngura!
Medze Me nsa nyimfa
Mubosuo wo mu;
Wɔasan mu eyi wo dɛ
'Begyina M'enyim.

MHB 955
3 . N-dzepa a wɔahyehyɛ
Afe a ɔreba yi m'!
Nkwa nsu bopue ama
'Bɔbɔfo ehiafo;
N'adom bobu do ama
Abɔn abɔbɔfo.
Bahatɔfo benya
Ahoɔdzen mapa.

MHB 955
4 . Ɔremmpa hen ara da
Orinngyaa hɛn so;
N'onnyiewiei ahyɛmu no,
Orummbu do da!
Yɛtwer N'anohoba a,
'Bɛn na yebosuro?
Nyankopɔn so dze ma
Afe a ɔreba 'i.

MHB 956
1 . Hom mbra ma yentu 
Hɛn kwan yi fofor
Yɛnye afe yi nkyin,
Na mma yenngyina kyerɛ hɛn Wura aba.

MHB 956
2 . Hom ma yɛmfa dɛw 
Yɛnyɛ N' apɛdze,
Yɛmfa abotar
Na dɔ dwumadzi nsi hɛn adom no pi.

MHB 956
3 . Hɛn nkwa yɛ adaaso; 
Hɛn mber tse dɛ nsu a
Ɔrepem hwew hwew
Na mber kobɔnyi no nngyina ara pɛn.

MHB 956
4 . Wɔatow egyen no, 
M-ber no ɔkɔ;
Apem afe no
Ɔrobɔto hɛn, na onnyiewiei aba.

MHB 956
5 . Ao, nkyɛ biara aaka 
Da a ɔbɛba n' dɛ,
Mako ɔko pa n'
Dwuma a edze maa me n' mewie ne nyina yɛ.

MHB 956
6 . Ao, nkyɛ biara aatse, 
No Wura reka n' dɛ:
M-bo, ayɛ n' yie
Hɛn me dɛw mu na tsena M' ahengua no do.

MHB 957
1 . EGYA, ma muntu afe yi
Nyina nsi hɔ mma W',
Ɔbra mu gyinabew biara a 
Epɛ dɛ mokɔ m',
Awerɛhow, yaw na haw;
Me mpaabɔ ara nye dɛ
'Nyimnyam nka Wo dzin.

MHB 957
2 . Ana abofra botum akyerɛ
Mbrɛ obesi abɔ bra?
Aso Egya bi n' dɔ bɔpow
Dɛ ɔyɛ dza oye nyina?
Dza yebisa no daa no
Ema ma ɔbor do,
Emmbra hɛn dɛ yɛka dɛ
Enyimnyam nka W' dzin.

MHB 957
3 . Mbɔbɔrhu ntsi sɛ ebɛma
M'enyigye atweɔn;
Sɛ 'kan nserɛmɛn bi bɛhyerɛn
'Bra do asomdwee mu a;
M'enyigye akoma ntow W' ndwom 
Akwan nyina mu;
Na dza ndaamba dze nam nyina,
Nhyɛ W' dzin enyimnyam.

MHB 957
4 . Sɛ efrɛ m' ba mbeamudua n' ho,
Na no sunsuma n' ba,
Na mohwer m'adze nyina,
M'akoma na fie mpo a,
Ma mondwen mbrɛ Wo Ba n' sii
Baa N'enyimnyam mu,
Na mbusu m' monkɔ do nsɔr :
Hyɛ W' dzin enyimnyam.   Amen.

MHB 958
1 . O NYAME, Tsetse Botan,
Ɔwo a ewɔ hɔ daa
Ehumtuber mu nyina
Hɛn asomdwee guandɔbea :
Ansaana erobɔ wiadze
Etse dɛm sesei so,
Mbersantsen nyinara mu,
Bɛkyebo Woara a.

MHB 958
2 . Hɛn mfe tse dɛ esunsum a
Wi tow gu akoko do,
Anaa nkyɛkyɛr mu nsensan a
Onyin prɔmprɔm dze wu :
Nda, adaaso, kodzi bi a
Ahɔho tow no ntsɛm,
Ndzɛmba a ɔyɛ dadaw ntsɛm
N'enyimnyam a ɔnnkye.

MHB 958
3 . O Ɔwo a enntɔ nkom nnda,
Na Wo kan so nnhyɛ sum,
Kyerɛ hɛn, yɛnkan hɛn nda yie 
Ansaana mfe n' ahwer.
Wo mbɔbɔrhu nhyerɛn hɛn do
Wo ayamuyie nye hɛn ntsena
Na ma Wo Sunsum nhyerɛn 
Akoma a ehyira no n' mu.

MHB 958
4 . Hɛn Wura, fa fɛwyɛ na adom
Bɔ hɛn gyedzi abɔtsir,
Kɛpem dɛ kan mu, afebɔɔ
Yebohu W' enyim na enyim:
Enyigye a wonnsusu
Tse dɛ bura a ebu do
Enyigye a ɔpem afebɔɔ
Dɛ po a onnyi mpoano.

MHB 959
1 . HOM ntow Jehovah N'ayɛyi,
Nkamfo nyina dzi wɔ N';
Ɔno a ɔma hɛn nda mu war,
Hɛn ndwom pa no fata N'.

MHB 959
2 . Ɔahwɛ hɛn do dze hɛn etwa
Afe kor so no mu;
Hɛn nyina dzedze ndwom fofor
Befir Nyame N'enyim.

MHB 959
3 . Egya, ehu hɛn mbɔbɔr pɛn;
Na 'da ho hwɛ hɛn;
Mbrɛ yɛtse, dza yɛwɔ biara,
Yedua Christ do dze ma W'.

MHB 959
4 . Hɛn ano na hɛn bra bɛka
Wo dɔ n'anwanwadze;
Yɛnam Jesus N'anamɔn mu
Bohu W'enyim wɔ sor.

MHB 959
5 . Hɛn nda ne nkaase yɛ Wodze,
Ne nyina yɛdze ma W';
Hɛn tum biara yetu si nkyɛn,
Yɛdze bɔ afɔr ma Wo.

MHB 96
1 . KA enyimnyam edzin nyina, 
Nyansa, dɔ na tum bɔ m'.
Dza adasa nyim no,
Dza ɔda abɔfo do;
Iyinom nyina nntum nnkyerɛ 
Dɛ mbrɛ hɛn Agyenkwa no tse.

MHB 96
10 . Sɛ owu ɔnye hɛll,
Na hɔn etumfo nyina
Dze ebufuw kɛse bi
Na enyitan hyia me mpo a,
Christ N'adom na No tum no so
Sen hɔndze ntsi hwee nnkɛyɛ me.

MHB 96
2 . Naaso hɛn Pomfo no
Nam ahobrɛadze kwan
Do na ɔkyerɛ hɛn,
Mbrɛ No sor adom tse;
Me kra dze dɛw na nwanwa hwɛ 
Ɔdɔ a ɔdze dɔ hɛn no!

MHB 96
3 . Ahyɛmu Ɔbɔfo no,
Ɔaba wɔ honam mu,
Okura anohoba
Na fakyɛ wɔ Ne nsamu;
Wɔhyɛɛ N' fii N'Egya ahengua do
Dɛ ɔnka N'adom nkyerɛ adasa.

MHB 96
4 . Nyame No Nkɔnhyɛnyi,
M'ano behyira Wo dzin:
Ɔwo na 'dze nkwagye
Enyigyesɛm no bae;
Bɔnfakyɛ ho enyigyesɛm,
Edzii hɛll do; sor wɔ asomdwee.

MHB 96
5 . Bɛyɛ mo Fotufo,
Mo Nhwɛdo, me Gyefo;
Sar do akwantu yi mu,
Ma membɛn Wo nkyɛn daa:
Mma m'anamɔn mmfom kwan ara da, 
Na memmfa kwan kɔntɔnkye do!

MHB 96
6 . Mo Guanhwɛfo Ne ndze
Na mepɛ dɛ metse;
N'enyi bɔ mo ho aprɔw,
Kora me No nguankuw mu;
Ɔnyɛn No nguan, 'bɔ hɔn edzin, 
Tur No nguambaa wɔ N'abaw mu.

MHB 96
7 . Jesus Sɔfopanyin
Dze N' bɔgyaa bɔgyaa bɔɔ afɔr; 
Me tsibowa fɔdzifo
Nnhwehwɛ afɔrbɔ bio;
No bɔgyaa no pataa prɛko, 
Na ɔserɛ ahengua n' enyim.

MHB 96
8 . Otumfo Ewuradze,
Mo Konyimdzifo, Hen,
Motow W'adom, W'afowa,
Na W'ahempoma ho ndwom;
Ɔwo nye Tumfo, medze m' pɛ 
Tsena Wo nan adze dɛ akowaa.

MHB 96
9 . Afei ma me kra nsoɛr
Ntsia ɔsɔhwɛfo do:
Me Sahen n' dzi m'enyim,
Ma m' Konyim na ahenkyɛw:
Kɔ w'enyim, mma nnsuro, dzi nyim,
Owu na hɛll siw wo kwan mpo a.

MHB 960
1 . ADOM mba a wɔapon hom nyina,
Hom nhur dɛw krɔnkrɔn no,
Hom mbɔ ose nyi Pomfo N' ayɛw,
Ntow dasu mu ndwom krɔnn.

MHB 960
2 . Nhyira, ndaase, ɔdɔ na tum,
Wɔmfa mma hɛn Jesus,
Ɔno na ɔdan hɛn sum yɛ kan,
Na ɔdan hɛn hɛll hɛven.

MHB 960
3 . Hɔ na ogya hɛn gyedzi akra kɔ,
Hɔ na ɔma yɛsoɛr,
Hyɛ hɛn enyigye ahenkyɛw
Dze kehyia No wɔ wimu.

MHB 961
1 . AWƆBER anago fua sum no
Rutwa m' sen wɔ wimu,
Yɛba Wo nkyɛn, N-kwa na Kan,
Behyia wɔ som krɔnkrɔn mu,
Ber a afe n' ewiei reba yi,
Yɛma hɛn ndze do su frɛ Wo,
Totɔ serɛ Wo dɔ n' bio.

MHB 961
2 . Yɛkotow Wo mbeamudua n'enyim,
Yɛdze hɛn mpaabɔ ba W' nkyɛn,
Rekaa W'adom nyina sesei
Na yɛka hɛn bɔn to gua
Reserɛ Wo afe a ɔreba yi
Dɛ yɛntsena Wo gyedzi na suro m'
Na fa Wo nhyira no ma hɛn.

MHB 961
3 . Yeehyia dɔnhwer tsiaba yi mu
Rekaakaa W'ehumbɔbɔr n',
Hɛn ndaase ndwom gye W'ayamuyie
Wo dɔ na W' tum ho dase :
'Siandɛ ayɛ hɛn ahoɔdzen na mboa
Wɔ sum na ɔhaw da no mu,
Ɔhaw na abɛbrɛsɛ nyina m'.

MHB 961
4 . Nyame kɛse, dɛm a, mfe a ɔreba n',
Dza ɔbɔto hɛn biara,
Hɛn fiekɔ akwantu no mu,
Gya hɛn taataa nye hɛn nkɔ
Na mma nngyaa hɛn ɔbra n'ewiei,
Gye hɛn sɔnn wɔ haw na aperdzi m'
Heaven bɛgye hɛn esie.

MHB 962
1 . NDAASEFO nyina, hom mbra,
Hom mfa ndɔbaa ndwom mbra fie:
Ndzɛmba nyina ayɛ krado,
Ansaana ɔpɛber ehum tu n'
Nyame hɛn Bɔfo Noara
Bɛma dza yehia nyina.
Hom mbra Nyame N'asɔrfi m',
Hom nhur ndɔbaa afahyɛ ndwom n'.

MHB 962
2 . Wiadze nyina yɛ Nyame N' kwa a
Ɔsow ayɛyi aba ma N',
'Wifua na nworahaban wɔ m';
Wɔdze enyigye anaa yaw nyin,
Wonyin nkakrankakra ara
Na afei ɔsow aba.
Ewuradze, boa ma yɛnyɛ
Aba pa a no ho tsew.

MHB 962
3 . Ewuradze Nyame bɛba
Dze No ndɔbaa akɔ fie;
Ɔbɛhyew bɔn nyinara
Wɔ Ne haban m' dɛm da no;
Ɔbɛhyɛ N'abɔfoe ma
Wɔahyew nworahaban no nyina;
Na aba pa no nyina dze
Wɔdze bɛhyɛ san do daa.

MHB 962
4 . Dɛm a, Ewuradze, bra ntsɛm;
Fa ewiei ndɔbaa n' bra fie,
Boaboa Wo nkorɔfo ano bra m',
Yi hɔn fi yaw na bɔn mu;
Tsew hɔn ho wɔ hɔ da nyina
Ma wɔntsena Wo siar fie,
Enye W' abɔfoe nyina mbra,
Hom mfa ndɔbaa afahyɛ ndwom n'.   Amen.

MHB 963
1 . YƐDƆW nhaban, yɛpe aba a
Oye gu asaase do,
Na Nyame tumfo Ne nsa
Ɔtɔ nsu gugu do;
Ɔma hɛn nsu wɔ duaber
Ɔma ɔhyew huhur aba n',
Ɔbɔ mframa, ofir ewia
Na ɔtɔ nyankonsu.
    'Kyɛdze pa a etwa hɛn ho n',
    Wɔ dze fi sor ma hɛn:
    Da Ewuradze ase, O da N'ase,
    Wɔ N' dɔ nyina ntsi.

MHB 963
2 . No nko na ɔyɛ ndzɛmba a
Wɔbɛn, wɔ ekyir nyina Yɛfo,
Ogu nhyiren wɔ kwan nkyɛn,
Ɔsɔ anago nworaba;
Mframa na asorɛkye tsie No,
Ɔno na ɔnyɛn nnoma;
Na akantam hɛn, Ne mba,
Ɔma hɛn edziban daa.

MHB 963
3 . Egya, yɛda Wo ase
Wɔ ndzepa nyina ho,
Duaber na buber, hɛn nkwa,
Apɔwmudzen, na edziban;
Gye akyɛdze a yɛdze aba
Wɔ Wo dɔ nyina ntsi,
Na dza ehwehwɛ kɛse a
Ɔyɛ hɛn ndaase akoma.

MHB 964
1 . Yɛma hɛn akoma do tow, 
N-tonton ndwom ma W' Wura,
Yɛdze hɛn dɛw afɔr brɛ Wo
Wɔ dɛw esebɔm' ara;
Harban ahyehyɛ sika ntar
Mbepɔw dze dɛw rowosow
Mbɔnsam' ayɛ eburow ma
Ma hɔn so wɔrotow ndwom.

MHB 964
2 . N-dɛ hɛn afahyɛ da yim', 
Yɛkaa Wo nsaano ayamuyie n',
Wo nhyira ndɔbaa-kan ndaase n',
Nna yɛdze gu W' enyim no
Adom akyɛdze soronko n'
Edze nyɛn hɛn nkorɔfo akra;
'Wo a 'ma hɛn asaase paanoo,
Ma hɛn onnyiewiei paanoo.

MHB 964
3 . Yɛsɔw adzekyee yim' fona, 
Yɛberɛ hɛn dwumadzi mu;
Na wi tɔ a, edwuma sa,
Ma nyia ɔaberɛ n' nya ahomgye
Sɛ abɔfo buber n' wie a,
N-kyɛ ekyir n' yaafata
Christ sika efiefi no a
Wɔdze kɔ asan fɛɛfɛw do n'.

MHB 964
4 . Nyame Ne bea a apapafo 
Tse do no woehyira do,
Mbrɛ sika haban kɛse wɔ,
Na esutsen hyɛnhyɛn pem.
Dɔm krɔnkrɔ nyina hɔn ndwoma no
Ndɛ ɔnye hɛndze asaa;
Buber ndwom a ɔmmbɔ adze n'
Woehyira do m-prɛnsa.

MHB 965
1 . ESUSOW aba bio,
Nkwa fir 'pɛber m' epue;
Mfikyir na kwaamu nyinara
Nhyiren apaa fɛɛfɛw.

MHB 965
2 . O esumasɛm nwanwa,
Dɛ nkwa a osumae no
Bopuei efi asaase mu
Ehyia hɛn n-daase.

MHB 965
3 . 'Napa kan a eyɛ fɛw,
Anago sum apa;
Ma nda pa a enyigye ahyɛ m' ma
Nhyerɛn hɛn akoma mu.

MHB 965
4 . Ewuradze, bue hɛn enyi;
Ma hɛn n-kwa fofor,
Ma yeehu W'esumasɛm wɔ
W'esusuowber nwanwa m'.

MHB 966
1 . FAMU ha asaase ayɛ ma,
Sor so ahyerɛn;
Obiara reserew
Wɔ 'dɔ kan no mu;
Nyimpa nyina dzi dɛw,
'Yɛyi ahyɛ adwen ma;
Dɛw akoma nye ndze
Ma da biara dɛw.

MHB 966
2 . Abran a worutwa ndɔbaa
Wɔ haban mu nyina,
Na wɔtwe eburoguanee
Fi kwa mu kɔ fie,
Suo mu tow ayɛyi ndwom
Wɔ witɔree ber,
Dze ma Nyia daa nyina
Ɔkora hɛn do n'.

MHB 966
3 . Ɔnam ewia na nsu,
Nsutɔree na bɔw
Na esusow na ɔpɛ m'
Dɛw aber no ntsi,
Ɔnam buber no mu
Ndɔbaa bafuu n' ntsi,
Ɔnam dɔ a ɔtwee yinom
Baa hɛn pon ano ntsi.

MHB 966
4 . Wiadze ndɔbaa rinyin
Wɔ ewia kɛse a
Ɔkyɛn dza ɔma hɛn kan
Wiadze nyina mu n' mu;
Egya, ma edwumafo
Nkɔ mbea a edwuma n' wɔ;
Na boaboa aman n' ano,
Boa hɔn ano, gye hɔn.

MHB 967
1 . AFEI woehyira afe no
Ber a yebu eburow no :
Yɛma hɛn enyigye ndwom do.
Dze kyerɛ hɛn ndaase so,
Ɔberɛ nye awerɛhow nda a etwa m'
Runntum nnsɛɛ hɛn asomdwee,
'Siandɛ enyigye ahyɛ akoko do,
Na mbɔnsa tsea mu dzi dɛw.
   Ewuradze No nkorɔfo nyina
   Dze nduaba kan brɛ N' ndaase m';
   Yɛtow ayɛyi ma Egya no
   Wɔ buber mu enyigye ntsi.

MHB 967
2 . M-fuw nyina dzii ehurusi,
Nhaban nyina yɛɛ ahaebun,
Ber a ewia tsiiw sunsuma
Ɔhar do wɔ adandan ber m;
Buber no mu wɔkaa asɛm a
Ɔfa buber enyidar ho :
Afei ɔbɛsɛber mu enyimnyam
Dze sika furaa asaase.

MHB 967
3 . Ana hɛn a hɛn akoma
Da nda a etwa mu no ho n'
Nnkɔtow ayɛyi ndwom akyerɛ
Enyigye a ɔbɛba daakye?
Mununkum ho asomdwee ahyɛmu
Ntsi na nyankontɔn wɔ hɔ,
Mber tsentsen a asaase wɔ hɔ
Yi dze, bubuer runntwa m' da.

MHB 968
1 . Nyew, Nyame ye- wɔ sor na ase 
Epo no bun mu na kwaa mu,
Ndze ɔpedu retsea mu dɛ
Nyame bɔɔ hɛn, na Nyame ye.

MHB 968
2 . Ewia a ɔnam ne kyenan do, 
Na ɔtow ne nserɛmɛn gu ase ha,
Wimu anago dɔm hyɛnhyɛnn n' nyina
Tsea mu dɛ Nyame ye.

MHB 968
3 . Nnoma dze dɛw gye ndwom no do, 
Wɔtow n' fofor afe biara,
Mframa pa a ɔbɔ na nyankom
Wɔsa berɛww dɛ Nyame ye.

MHB 968
4 . Metse n' wɔ mframa a ɔrobɔm', 
Ɔnye tsetse mbepɔw no do,
Sor  a ɔpaapaam', po a ɔwor
Hɔn nyinaa gye do dɛ Nyame ye.

MHB 968
5 . Nyew, Nyame ye, abɔdze ka 
Dɛ mbrɛ Nyame ama kasahom;
Nyimpa mfa ayɛyi mbordo
Ntow ndwom dɛw mu dɛ Nyame ye.

MHB 968
6 . Nyame yɛda W' adom ase, 
Nkanka hɛn sor edziban ho;
W' adom fakyɛ, Wo nkwasɛm no,
Ɔma yɛtow dɛ Nyame ye.

MHB 969
1 . SOR, asaase na po Wura,
Ayɛyi na enyimnyam nka Wo;
Yensi dɛn nyi hɛn dɔ nkyerɛ Wo,
Ɔwo Ɔmafo?

MHB 969
2 . Wo dɔ ma ewia kan, mframa pa
Nhyiren huanhuam na nduaba pii;
Bea a ndɔbaa ber no, hɔ na Ɔwo
Ɔmafo n' wɔ.

MHB 969
3 . Hɛn asomdwee na hɛn apɔwmudzen
Nye asaase do nhyira nyina ntsi
Yɛdze W' ndaase na ayɛyi kaw,
'Wo a ema ne nyina.

MHB 969
4 . Annkam hɛn Wo Ba kortoo no,
Edze No maa wiadze a asɛɛ,
Na edze adze nyina kaa Siarfo
No ho dze mae.

MHB 969
5 . Emaa hɛn Sunsum n' Ne nhyira,
No nkwa, No dɔ, ɔnye No tum;
Ihuee N'adom mbɔho esuon n'
Guu hɛn nyina do.

MHB 969
6 . Akra a wɔapon hɔn, bɔnfakyɛ
Adom kwan na sor enyidar ntsi,
Ayɛyi nyina nka Wo Egya a
Ema ne nyina.

MHB 97
1 . NYAME Dɔyɛfo,
Gye m'abɔdoma sufrɛ,
Hwɛ Wo kra n'aperdzi no,
Agyenkwa, na onnya etsidaa;
Fa me sesei, fa me koraa,
Ɔwo na iwui maa me.

MHB 97
2 . Ɔwo nye nkwa Nsunyiwa,
Minyim, metse nka ndɛ
Wu na bahatɔ mmbɔ m' hu:
Ewɔ mo mu; dza ema n',
Ofifir aber biara,
Kɔ nkwa a onnyiewie mu.

MHB 97
3 . Ɔwo nye Guanhwɛfo n',
Merenndan mmfi Wo ho;
Mo Hwɛfo na me Gyafo,
Kɔ do ara hwɛ mo do;
Gya me bɔkɔɔ wɔ Wo nkyɛn,
Tur m' enyigye m' wɔ Wo bo m'.

MHB 97
4 . Ɔwo nye m' daa Paanoo;
O Christ, Ɔwo nye m' Tsir;
Ma m' ahoɔdzen na ndzepa,
Emi a meyɛ W'akowaa yi;
Enyɛɛn m', maa me edziban,
Ndzɛmba nyina nyin wɔ Wo mu.

MHB 97
5 . Nkɔnhyɛnyi, yi W'Egya
Ne pɛ pa kyerɛ me;
Ɔdasanyi bi nnkasaa
Dɛ Ɔwo a ifi sor yi;
Wɔdze ndze dzendzen tseatea m',
Kumabaa nyina yɛ Wodze.

MHB 97
6 . Mo Sɔfoe, mefrɛ Wo,
Wo bɔgyaa gye obiara;
Eguambaa a wokum Wo,
Igyina ahengua n'enyim,
Edze me mpaabɔ nye Ɔwo
Woara Wodze serɛ ma m'.

MHB 97
7 . Jesus, eyɛ me Hen,
M'ahoɔdzen nyina fir Wo;
Sɛ Wo nsa kata mo do a,
Woana botum ehwim me?
Menam gyedzi do gyina,
Meyɛ dzen wɔ Wo tum n' mu.

MHB 970
1 . Hɛn Wura, fi Wo sor tsenabew do tsie hɛn: 
Dɛ tsetsemba n' hɛn so yɛfona kwa,
Gyesɛ Ɔwo a eyɛ Kan n' nye hɛn kɔ;
Bra, Ewuradze, ama yeehu W' enyim.

MHB 970
2 . Ewuradze 'Wo na 'dzi po a ɔwor do, 
Ber a oetutu ne tsir sgu do n':
W' abaw yɛ dzen, hɛn ahɛn yɛ mberɛw,
Kaa Galilee, na fa Wo mboa ma hɛn.

MHB 970
3 . Yɛdze hɛn fifo nyina hyɛ Wo nsa: 
Hɔn ntsi na yɛdɔw haban, yenu po,
Hɔn ntsi na dabaa yebu eburow pa,
Na 'nafua yebu pom' ndɔbaa fɛɛfɛw n'.

MHB 970
4 .	Yɛda W' ase na ewia, bɔsu, nyankom, 
Wo tum n-sa no dze fir sor petse;-
Nnoma, mbowa, nam, nhaban, aba, nye eburow:
N-kwa horow nyina Farbaa nye 'Wo.

MHB 970
5 . N-kwa Paanoo, aka n' W' asɛm mu dɛ: 
Nyia ɔfa Wo dzi gyedzim' n' onnkowu da!
Fa ehumbɔbɔr tsie Wo mba hɛn sufrɛ:
Ma hɛn ndɛ so hɛn daadaa edziban.

MHB 970
6 . Dua Wo dɔ pa n' n' aba wɔ hɛn 'komam', 
Na yeebu abodwee na akomatɔm'.
Na ndaamba sɛ hɛn dwuma bɔ adze a,
Hɛn so yaaka Wo sor ndɔbaa no ho.   Amen.

MHB 971
1 . YƐDZE dɛw tow ayɛyi ndwom,
Na yɛdze ndaase hyia mu,
Yehyira Nyame dɔ a ɔwɔ sor;
Hɛn domankoma Egya.
     Yɛdze akoma nye ndze dzi dɛw
     Ma Nyia N'enyimnyam mmpa da,
     Nyia Ne nhyehyɛɛ nye hɛn bambɔ,
     Nyia ɔtse ase afebɔɔ.

MHB 971
2 . Na ɔfrɛ kan fi sum kebii mu,
Na nhyiren so fi dɛtse mu;
Ne nhyira fi mununkum m' ba
Wɔ ewia anaa nsutɔ mu.

MHB 971
3 . Ne mba gyinagyina N'enyim,
N'abasa bɔ hɔn ho ban;
Nyia Ne nyansaa hwɛ wiadze do,
Atsentsen hɛn anamɔn.

MHB 971
4 . Biribiara nntɔ famu a onnyim,
Anaa dɛw anaa awerɛhow;
Na Nyia ndeda ohun mbɔbɔr n',
Bɛka hɛn ho ɔkyena.

MHB 971
5 . Hom mma yɛmfa akoma kor
Nyi Ne dzin kɛse n' ayɛw,
Na yɛnka N' dɔ a ɔnnsesa da
Ho anwanwansɛm daa daa.

MHB 972
1 . HƐN Wura, yɛdze dza ɔyɛ fɛw nyina ma Wo,
Hɛn turo m' na hɛn haban mu nhyiren,
Akyɛdze a yɛdze ma ayarfo, yenyin dɛ
Ɔwo dwen dɔ n' ho kyɛn sika a yɛma.

MHB 972
2 . Hɛn wura, fa iyinom kɛma ayarfo nyina
Ka asomdweesɛm gu hɔn akoma mu;
Kyekye hɔn a wɔayɛ mberɛw n' hɔ werɛ
Ma hɔn a woruwu nkɔ asomdwee m'.

MHB 972
3 . Ewuradze, ma hɔn a wɔayar nsoɛr bio,
Ma hɔn abrabɔ nyɛ fɛw dɛ nhyiren;
Fa W'adom ma akra a ama hɔn nkwa nyina
Ma hɔn awerɛhow ndan enyigye.

MHB 973
1 . Wondzi dɛw mma onua a oewu yi, 
No wu yi yɛ no mfaso kɛse,
Woeyi ne kra wɔ efiadze,
Woeyi no honam mpokyerɛ n' mu;
Wɔmma yɛmfa ndwom nka no do,
Yɛnye no sunsum mfow ɔsor,
Oefi nsa kɔ kan man no mu,
Ɔakɛtsena dɔ Eden no mu.

MHB 973
2 . Hɛn nua edu ahɛndwirii hɔ, 
Ɔatsew ehum nye aahow no mu,
Tsiabaa yi ne nsa aka n' ahomgye,
Ɔadan n' afrɛ egya ekyir.
Hɔn wɔda ho da fona pom',
Reper edu siar mpoano hɔ,
Beebi mbrɛ asomdwee nko wɔ,
Na bɔn nye yaw nn-yi hɔ bio.

MHB 973
3 . Hɔ na ahɛn dɔm nyina hyia, 
Hɔn a wɔnye Agyenkwa nantseew ha n',
Wɔbɔ se wokyiakyia hɔnho,
Na wodzi fona nye wu do nyim:
Ɔbra n' akwantu n' abɔ adze;
Honam n' ahohia no etwam';
M-ber a wodzi n' wɔ sor no,
Ɔnnkɔbɔ adze dabiara pɛn.

MHB 974
1 . ATEASEFO Nyame, Ɔwo a
'Bɔdze nyina da W'enyim adagyaw,
Akra nyina yɛ W'dze, yɛnnka dɛ
Hɔn a woewu no ayew koraa;
Woefi hɛn honam wiadze yi m',
Yenyim dɛ wɔtse ase ma Wo.

MHB 974
2 . Woenya asaase do fona m' 'homgye,
Wɔdze hɔn esuma Wo mu;
Hɔn adwendwen, ndwuma, tum, yɛ Wodze,
Wɔyɛ Wodze, hɛn so hɛndze a;
Yenyim dɛ bea a wɔwɔ biara
Hɛn ewufo no tse ase ma Wo.

MHB 974
3 . W'asɛm yɛ nokwar, Wo pɛ tsen,
Yɛdze hɔn hyɛ Wo nsa gyedzi m';
Yehyira Wo wɔ ɔdɔ a ogyaa W'
Ma Wo Ba bɛdaa 'wumaa mu,
Amma obiara ennsuor dɛ
Hɔn nyina tse ase wɔ Wo mu.

MHB 974
4 . Ɔwo a edze ahom ma nyimpa,
Ɔwo a ikitsa owu nsaafee,
Ɔwo a ikenyan nkwa hɛn mu,
Gye hɛn fi owu na bɔn mu :
Na honam, ɔkra na sunsum
Aatsena ama Wo daa nyina.  Amen.

MHB 975
1 . Ber a dwumadzi da asa n', 
Ber a bra 'mpiresi abɔ adze n!
Egya, dom Wo ba fonafo
Ahomgye afebɔɔ.

MHB 975
2 . Ber a bɔn nkodzen abɔ adze n', 
Ber a woeku kra mu tamfo n',
W' adom asɛm no nhyɛ ma-
Asomdwee afebɔɔ.

MHB 975
3 . Ber a sum no enya apa n' 
Ma enyim atsetsew no,
Ma yenhuahua dɛw kan no-
Kan ara afebɔɔ.

MHB 975
4 . Ber a yaw atsɛ akoma 
Ma afei oegyaa tow no,
Fa hɛn kɔ mbrɛ nyinsu nnyi n',
Dɛw ara afebɔɔ.

MHB 975
5 . Ber a yɛrodwen nda a yɛasɛɛ n' ho, 
Nda a ɔrennsan mmba bio n',
Wo dɔm' kyerɛkyerɛ ma yensua
Dɔ ara afebɔɔ.

MHB 975
6 . Ber a nkwahwea etu kɔ n', 
Ber a wumaa regye nedze n',
Nkwa Wura, yɛnsoa W' ahenkyɛw n'-
Nkwa ara afebɔɔ.  Amen.

MHB 976
1 . Ɔsomfo yi apon ndɛ, 
Oewie ɔko pa no ko;
Afei ɔkwantunyi no
Edu esuegya noho: 
Egya, yɛdze Wo ba a ɔada 
Hyɛ W' abaatan dɔ n-sa n' mu.

MHB 976
2 . Hɔ na hɛn nyinsuwa bɔ adze; 
Hɔ na wɔkyerɛ hɛn ase;
Hɔ na ɔsɛndzifo pa n'
Hwɛ hɛn bra nyinara mu:

MHB 976
3 . Hɔ na Guanhwɛfo no dze 
Nguambaa no a wɔayew ba fie,
Ɔkora hɔn wɔ bea a
Pataku n' nnkotum aba:

MHB 976
4 . Hɔn a ɔasakyer wɔ ha, 
Na wɔhwɛ mbeamudua no n',
Wohu Jesus dɔ n' kɛse
Wɔ Ne nkyɛn wɔ Paradise:

MHB 976
5 . Hɔ na sum mu etumfo 
Nsa nnkɛka ara da;
Ewuradze Christ bɔweɔn hɔn,
Ɔno a owui gyee hɔn nkwa:

MHB 976
6 . Fa nkɔ fam', n-so nkɔ nsom'! 
Yɛhyɛ dzen na yɛka yi;
Hɛn so yɛdze enyidar
Yɛhwɛ wusoɛr da no kwan:

MHB 977
1 . YEEDU fie mpoano sɔnn,
Ntaampee homa tsewee,
'Bradaa tsewee, edziban
Sae, naaso hɛn no ammbɔ;
Engyigye a ɔbaa mpoano hɔ a!
Ber a yɛkaa akwantu mu nsɛm.

MHB 977
2 . Yeenya 'mpirenyimadze !
Nkyɛ enguantunyi n' rohwe ase;
Ɔfaa ɔhaw nyina mu,
Ɔammfa n' ho tɔtrɔtɔ :
Nyia ɔbɔ konyim abɔtsir no
Serew ber a ɔhaw etwa m' no.

MHB 977
3 . 'Tamfo n' nntum nnyɛ hwee bio,
Ɔnnkɔtoa hɛn nseraban,
'Nafua ntseam' nnyi hɔ bio,
Yennkehia ɔweɔn kandzea;
Naaso nkyɛ ɔreyɛ ahwe ase,
Nkyɛ ɔtamfo n' reyɛ edzi nyim.

MHB 977
4 . Ndɔmmumnyi n' edu fie:
'Nafua na adzekyee osu a !
Yɛmmpɛ ekyinkyin bio !
Bɔn, 'kyingye, na suro a.
Awerɛhow sum no yɛ ebɛn?
Ɔhen n' apepa nyinsuwa nyina.

MHB 978
1 . Ber a mbusu abrɛ hɛn adze, 
Ber a hɛn nyinsu abor do;
Yerigyam dɔfo a ɔayew n',
Jesu, Mary Ba, tsie hɛn.

MHB 978
2 . Ber a hɛn akoma ridzi yaw, 
Wɔ no bɔn ho adwen ntsi,
Ber a suro ekitsa hɛn n',
Jesu, Mary Ba, tsie hɛn.

MHB 978
3 . 'Wo abyɛ hɛn honam yi bi. 
'Wo asoa hɛn yaw nyina,
'Wo esu dɛ nyimpa pɛn,
Jesu, Mary Ba, tsie hɛn.

MHB 978
4 . 'Wo abɔ Wo tsir adze ewu, 
'Wo ekyi n-kwa bɔgya,
'Wo ada fundaka mu,
Jesu, Mary Ba, tsie hɛn.

MHB 979
1 . HƐN Egya a tsetseber no
W'asomfo sii dan yi,
Ɔwo a Wo nsamu nhyira pii
Dze egu Wo mba do.
W'ehumbɔbɔr a ɔnnsa da n'
Akyerɛ wɔ hɛn kwan do.
Yɛnye hɔn a woedzi hɛn kan
Yi Wo dzin ayɛw ndɛ.

MHB 979
2 . Nsakyer mfe a onngyina da n'
Dze twitwi etwa m' dzinn;
Mfɛfo dze afofor so
Rebɛka fɛkuw n' ho:
Hɛn werɛ efir binom,
Hɔn 'nyidar hɔn suro so,
Ɔwo a ennsesa da no
Wɔrohom wɔ Wo mu.

MHB 979
3 . Wommbu hɔn berɛ mu aba,
Yebu dza woedua no;
Hɛn ndɔbaa dze wobobu n'
Wɔ mfe a yennyae nnhunii m'!
Tsetse mba dze akyɛdze pii a
Yenntum nnkamfo ama hɛn;
Hɛn Egya, ma yɛnsom wɔ nda a
Ɔreba n' nokwar mu.

MHB 979
4 . Hɛn enyim na hɛn nkyɛn nyina
'Da ho kura hɛn Wo nsamu,
Adasefo mununkum a
Yennhu hɔn gyina hɔ :
Yɛyɛ ebusua kortsee,
Yɛbɔ m' dze osebɔ,
Dze akoma kor na ndze kor
Dze yi Wo dzin ayɛw.

MHB 98
1 . ƆWO a ahomgye nyina fir Wo,
Nyame Dɔ a ɔso 'biara do,
Mo mboa na mo guandɔbea nye W',
Meyɛ Wodze a, mowɔ ahotɔ: 
Mifi bɔn, yaw na enyito mu,
Jesus, musuma Wo dzin mu.

MHB 98
2 . Wo dzin kɛse no yɛ nkwagye, 
Ɔma me kra sor enyigye;
Ɔma minya awerɛkyekyer,
Asomdwee, dɛw na onnyiewiei dɔ;
Wo dzin a ɔsom bo no ma me
Fakyɛ na krɔnkrɔn na sor.

MHB 98
3 . Jesus, eyɛ m'adze nyina;
Me berɛ ne yaw mu ahomgye,
M'akoma a ebubu n'edur,
Ɔko mu na minya asomdwee,
Wɔhyɛ mo do a, ema meserew;
M'enyiwu enyimnyam nye Wo.

MHB 98
4 . Me hia mu ema me mbordo,
Me mberɛw mu eyɛ m'ahoɔdzen ,
Mo mpokyerɛ m' ema m' fahodzi;
Satan no sum mu ema m' kan,
Minya dɛw wɔ awerɛhow mu,
Minya nkwa 'wu m', me hɛll dan heaven.

MHB 980
1 . KAN a ifi tsetse 'nnsakyer,
O Asɛm tseasefo,
Yɛatse Wo gy aa asɔ ne nka,
Yɛatse Wo ndze hɛn mu.

MHB 980
2 . Adwen krɔnkrɔn, ndwom nye mpaabɔ
Dze Sunsum tum aba,
Ama fasu yi ayɛ fɛw,
Hɛn na Ɔwo hɛn asɔrfi.

MHB 980
3 . Nyikyerɛ bi a ɔba mfe no mu a!
Nkaakaa pa bi a ɔba a!
Kɛpem dɛ enyiwa dze dɛw su
Ma akoma tow ndwom dɛw m'.

MHB 980
4 . Mber na ntseasee mu bɔw tu kɔ;
Adɔfo a woetwa m' ba;
Na adom kor a etwa hɛn ho ehyia
Kura hɔn nyina m' afebɔɔ.

MHB 980
5 . Hɔn a wɔberɛɛ toow gyedzi fapem
No ammberɛ kwa ara da;
Dɛmara so na hɔn a wɔdze
Dɔ weɔɔn sor ogya n' yɛe!

MHB 980
6 . Ogya krɔnkrɔn dzɛw, kɔ do hyerɛn!
Ber a aman soɛr na wogu,
Gyedzi enyidar nye ɔdɔ wɔ hɔ,
Hɔn nye su nyina mu pɔn.

MHB 981
1 . CHRIST nye ofi yi a
Yesi yi fapem;
N'afasu nyɛ nkwagye
N'apon ayɛyi;
Na ma n'apongua yi
Nsom bo mma Ewuradze;
Ma akoma a wɔsom ha
No mu nyɛ krɔnkrɔn.

MHB 981
2 . Ewuradze, Wo Sunsum
Nsɔw anohoba ano;
'Yarfo mbɔ esu wɔ ha,
Wonhu hɔn a wɔayew;
Ha na akoma a abobɔ
Nnya Wo bɔnfakyɛ;
'Nyɛnkofo a wɔatsetsew m'
Nka mbɔ m' bio wɔ ɔdɔ m'.

MHB 981
3 . Ma Wo ho nsɛnkyerɛdze
Nyina nda edzi;
Ha mpokyerɛ mbubu,
'Daduafo nkɔ kwa;
Ha ma ekan nhyerɛn
Wɔ kra biara do,
Ompegya adasa
Nkɔ Sunsum no mu.

MHB 981
4 . Ha wɔntonton Egya,
Christ, Ɔba, Agyenkwa n',
Ɔnye Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn n';
Dɛ wɔyɛ adze kor;
Kɛpem dɛ abɔdze nyina
Bɔhwe W'ananadze,
Na wɔɔatonton Wo dɛ
Hɔn nyina Ewuradze.   Amen.

MHB 982
1 . EGYA, Wo mu na adasamba a
Wɔwɔ wiadze nyina bɔm' yɛ kor,
Ma dwuma a yɛahyɛ ase Wo mu ntsim.
Sɛ woara ennsi dan no a
Adansifo no berɛ kwa;
Hyɛ hɛn dzen hɛn mberɛwyɛ mu !

MHB 982
2 . Nyimpa nntse ase mma no nko ho,
Ɔwɔ dɛw wɔ nkorɔfo yie ho;
Fɛkuwbɔ m' na yehu ɔbra pa.
Hɛn bra yi mu anyɛnkofo
Hyia dan yi mu ha yɛbɔ mpaa;
Hyira hɛn fɛkuwbɔ do ndɛ.

MHB 982
3 . O Christ, hɛn Nua panyin, Ɔwo a
Esoom nyimpa, yɛɛ Nyame N' pɛ,
Boa ma hɛn so nsom hɛn nuanom.
Gya hɛn ma yentsiw sor ndzɛmba,
Yengyaa adzehun, mpɛ ndzepa.
Yɛntsena ase Wo dɔ mbra mu.

MHB 982
4 . Hɛn dwumadzi na agor nyina m',
Hɛn Wura, hɛn Nyɛnko, yɛ hɛn ahom;
Dzi hɛn enyim kan kɔ da pa n' mu :
Ber n' ma yenhu dɛ ɔbra abɔ adze,
Yɛnye mfɛfo a woedzi hɛn kan,
Nhɛn sor fɛkuwbɔ mu afebɔ.   Amen.

MHB 983
1 . KA hɛn nkyɛn ndɛ, adom Ewuradze;
Yetu ofi yi si hɔ ma Wo;
Tsie Wo nkowaa ber a yɛrosɔr yi,
Na ma W'asowa mbra hɛn do.

MHB 983
2 . Ma wonhu asomdwee krɔnkrɔn,
Dɔ na nokwar wɔ ha daa daa;
Ma akoma berɛfo ahomgye;
Na esiarfo n' soa hɔn ahenkyɛw.

MHB 983
3 . Ma wontsie ebisafo nkrumsi,
Na aberɛfo so nya ahomgye;
Ma abrɛfo nsu mfrɛ Wo wɔ ha,
Na hɔn a wɔtweɔn n' nnya nhyira.

MHB 983
4 . 'Ha, wɔtse asɛmpa n' ne nka
Na wɔbɔ nkwagye dzin no a,
Ma akoma mbɔ hyew nkɔ hɔn kan
Na akra nkyer gya n' ne mframee.

MHB 983
5 . 'Ha wɔmma ewufo nnya nkwa bio,
Mum nkasa, etsitsifo ntse asɛm,
Na mbrɛhoadzefo mma hɔn
Fakyɛ na asomdwee a suro nnyi m'.

MHB 983
6 . Ma iyi nyɛ Woara W'atsenae,
Ma W'enyim no nka abangua yi m',
Ma iyi nyɛ Nyame Ne fie
Na ha nyɛ ɔsor abobow.

MHB 984
1 . O ƆWO a Wo nsa dze hɛn
Aba dɛw da yi mu,
Gye hɛn enyigye ndaase yi,
Tsie hɛn, ber a yɛsɔr no;
Na ma ndɛ da yi som ho
Ahoboa a yɛyɛe no,
Ntu hɛnho nyina, pɛ kor mu,
Mma Wo, O Ewuradze.

MHB 984
2 . Dan a yɛnam W'asɛm do esi
Yi, yeyi W'ayɛw wɔ
Ayamuyie ndzeyɛɛ pa
Na mboa a yenyae nyina ho;
Afei W'asɔrfi yi mu,
Ma yenhu W'enyimnyam,
'Siandɛ Ɔwo nnyi mu a ne fɛw
Na ne kɛse nnyɛ hwee.

MHB 984
3 . Ber a yehyia ha biara,
Na akoma bɔ mu som n',
Ma nokwar nda no tum edzi,
Na mpaa dzendzen mfow sor;
'Ha na ma nkukubɔnyi
Nnyan nhwehwɛ dza ɔkrɔn,
Mbofra, mpanyin nnya ahoɔdzen 
Na nyimpa nsua Wo dɔ.

MHB 984
4 . Ber a mber pem kɔ enyim no,
Na ɔdɔ kyekyer hɛn no,
Na nkaa dɛɛdɛw soɛr dura
Bea krɔnkrɔn yi ho no,
Ma n'enyidzi kɛse no 
Nyɛ n'enyimnyam dabaa,
Dɛ dɔm a wohyia wɔ mu n'
Enya ehu Wo nkyɛn kwan.

MHB 984
5 . Ewuradze, egyaam boafo,
Hɛn dɛw, 'nyidar, na tum,
Ma hɛn nda a ɔreba n' ho
Ndam na nsiyɛ ho adom,
Inyim hɛn akoma apensi;
Yɛtweɔn W'ahengua enyim :
O bra, na ewɔ ha no,
Fa fi yi yɛ Wodze.  Amen.

MHB 985

MHB 986

MHB 986

MHB 987
1 . MEDA Jesus abawm' sɔnn,
Meda No bo mu komm,
No dɔ no kata mo do,
Me kra bɔhom hɔ komm.
Tsie! Abɔfo hɔn ndze a;
Wɔdze rotow ndwom frɛ m',
Fir enyimnyam sar no do,
Fir jasper po n' egya.

      Meda Jesus abawn' sɔnn,
      Motwer No bo mu komm,
      No dɔ no kata mo do,
      Me kra bɔhom hɔ komm.

Aka nyinsu kumaabi,
Ma meefi awerɛhow nsa,
Ma meefi suro nsa.

Wɔ esuegya noho.

MHB 988

MHB 99

MHB 992

MHB 993

MHB 994

Bra, Gyefo kɛse, bra!

      Mabɔ ko nam awɔwim' wɔ akokwaa do,
      Mefi fie abɔ ko akɔ ekyirѐkyir;
      O, nkyɛ gye m' na fa m' kɔ Wo nguambuw mu,
      Bra, Gyefo kɛse, bra.

MHB 994
2 . Minnyi beebi a odu adzeseaà a m'bɛda
Bra, Gyefo kɛse, bra!
Ehwɛ m'prɛko arà a, m'benya kan na nkwa,
Bra, Gyefo kɛse, bra!

MHB 994
3 . Mo kwanm' yɛ kɔnn, m'anan so ebubu,
Bra, Gyefo kɛse, bra!
M'enyi tua sor rohwehwɛ W'enyimtsew,
Bra, Gyefo kɛse, bra!

MHB 994
4 . Akoma a ɔabɔm dze, innkeyi n' edzi,
Bra, Gyefo kɛse, bra!
Hu me mbɔbɔr na tsie mo mbɔbɔr sũ,
Bra, Gyefo kɛse, bra!

MHB 995
1 . Maba W'asɛndua n'ase,
Meyɛ fùrafo mbɔbɔrnyi,
Mebu ne nyina ntwaree,
Morohwehwɛ nkwahosan.

       Ewùradze morotwer Wo,
      Calvàry Eguambaa siarfo;
      Misi W'asɛndua n 'ase:
      Gye me, Jesus, gye m' sesei.

MHB 995
2 . M'akoma afe W' akyɛr,
Bɔn edzi mu hen akyɛr
Jesus kã nsɛm pa kyѐrɛ m' dɛ-
M'bɔhor wo ho bɔn nyina.

MHB 995
3 . Medze m'adze nyina ma Wo,
M'dzѐ a ɔwɔ wiadze nyinaa,
Mo sunsum nye mo honam,
Nyɛ Wodze kὸraa da nyina.

MHB 995
4 . Mo wѐrɛ twer W'anohoba n',
Minyim dɛ bɔgya n' ruguar m';
Medze moho ato daadze,
Menye Christ ewu dua n' do.

MHB 995
5 . Jesus abà abɛhyɛ m' mã!
Medzi mu wɔ No mu;
Mo ho nyinaa asan kὸraa,
Enyimnyam nkã Eguambaa.

MHB 996
1 . MIGYINÀA abow n' ekyir,
Kwantunyi bɔbɔfo;
Ebum a ɔyɛ dzen,
Otuu m'akoma mu;
Suro hyɛɛ me kra do,
Dɛ bѐr yi mber apa ho!
Mo ho popoo dodow,
Na mosɔɔr abow n' ekyir.

MHB 996
2 . Mekaam' dɛ, Ao, adom,
Soa mo bɔn yi ma me!
Na ndze bi buaa dɛ, Nyoo,
Nà adom dze me kɔr danm'.
Ɔkyekyeer m'epirakur,
Na ɔkaa m'akoma toom';
Ɔhoor m'afɔdzi nyinaa,
Na ɔmaa m' ahomgye.

MHB 996
3 . Gyefo n' a memmbu N' bi n',
Ɔno ohun m' mbɔbɔr,
Nyià ɔregye m' akoma
Na mammfa amma N' à, osũi n'.
Aso mo bɔn pii yi,
No ho akatua ny' 'i!-
Migyinàa abow n'ekyir,
Na Jesus dze m' kɔr danm'.

MHB 997
1 . M' egya dɔfo, hyira m' seesei,
Wɔ mbeamudua n' ase ha;
Fa mo mfom na me yaw kɔ,
Tsie na yɛ m' edur sesei.

      Hyira m' sesei, hyira m' sesei,
      M'Egya dɔfo, hyira m' sesei.

MHB 997
2 . Mo Wùra dɔnhwer yim' sesei,
Kyerɛ W'adom ɔnye Wo tum;
Ber a motwer W'anosɛm yi,
Mo Wùra, bra behyira m'sesei.

MHB 997
3 . Sesei onsian Christ n-tsi,
Bɛpa m' sum, botu m' apo;
Ber a morohwɛ W' musu yi,
Fa Wo nsa kã m' san mo ho.

MHB 997
4 . Wo Babanyin Jesus Christ,
Menntetar N' dɛmara pɛn;
Bѐr n' nye ndɛ, na bea n' nye ha,
M'Egya dɔfo, kyerɛ W'adom.

MHB 998
1 . Jesus Christ na ɔresen n'
Bɔnyɛnyi, to w'enyi hwɛ N';
Bѐr a ɔho wɔ na resa,
Kekam' dɛ, Hu me mbɔbɔr.

MHB 998
2 . Jesus Christ na ɔresen n'!
Aso ɔbɛbɛn wo dɛm daa?
Seiseiara nye ɔgye da,
Hwehwɛ nkwa ber a ibenya.

MHB 998
3 . Hwɛ, Ogyina hɔ refrɛ wo.
Ɔse dɛ, 'Rohwɛ bɛn?
Soɛr, ka wo hia nyinaa kyerɛ m'
Soɛr, ɔfrɛ wo ampaara.

MHB 998
4 . Se N' dɛ, Mepɛ W'adom ahwɛ,
Mo Wura, yi Wo dɔ kyerɛ m'
Ma onhwiram' nkitsa me kra,
Ɔnhyɛ 'koma nye bra do.

MHB 999
1 . Mo Wùra Jesus, mo kɔn dɔ dɛ midzi mu!
Morohwehwɛ dɛ etsena mo mu daa.
Dwuruw abosom, yi atamfo edzi,
Guar m' sesei ma monhoa dέ esukwankyɛba.

      Monhoa fitaa, nyew, monhoa fitaa,
      Guar m' sesei ma monhoa dɛ esukwankyɛba.

MHB 999
2 . Jesus, mma efifidze biara nn-ka,
Fa Wo bɔgyaa botu nkekaaba nyina;
Dɛm ahohor ntsi mopow adze nyina,
Guar m' sesei ma monhoa dɛ esukwankyɛba.

MHB 999
3 . Jesus, fi sor ahengua do tὸ enyi hwɛ m',
Boa me ma mombɔ afɔr a odzi mu;
Medze moho nye dza mowɔ nyina ma Wo,
Guar m' sesei ma monhoa dέ esunkwankyɛba.

MHB 999
4 . Jesus, yi ntsi na mokotow mesѐrɛ Wo,
Ewùradze, mokosɔw W'ananadze ha;
Me gyedzi enyi tua dɛ Wo bɔgyaa repem,
Guar m' sesei ma monhoa dέ esukwankyɛba.

MHB 999
5 . Jesus, matɔ mo bo ase morotweɔn,
Bra, bɔbɔ akoma fofor to mo mu;
Hɔn a wɔhwehwɛ W', 'nnse obi Oho da;
Guar m' sesei ma monhoa dέ esukwankyɛba.
